jaina - vividha sāhitya - śāstramālā ( 4 )
śrīlakṣmaṇagaṇiviracitaṁ
supāsanāhacariyaṁ ।
( prathamō bhāgaḥ )
gūrjara dēśāntargata rājadhanya puravāstavyēna śrēṣṭhitrikamacandratanūjēna kalikātāviśvavidyālayē
saṁskr̥ta-prākr̥tādhyāpaka-parīkṣakēṇa nyāya-vyākaraṇatīrthapadavīkēna paṇḍita-
daragōvindadāsēna
saṁśōdhita saṁskr̥tacchāyayā vibhūṣitaṁ ca ।
vīrasaṁvat 2444

śrījaina- vividha-sāhitya-śāstramālā kē paripōṣaka ।
śēṭa śāmacaṁda kēvaḷacaṁda saṁghavī,
taḷēgāṁva ḍhamaḍhērē.=== lakshmangani01output-8-to-8.json ==========================
॥ ōṁ namō vītarāgāya ॥
॥ supāsanāha-cariaṁ ॥
jaya juyāijiṇidō aṁtarariḍavijayanāḍayapabaṁdhē । navaniuṇasuttahārōvva vihiyasuhasaṁghaca upattō ॥ 1 ॥
siyajjhāṇānalapajalira kammarkatāra dhūmalaiucva । rēhati jassa asaṁ saghōlirā cihurakuralīō ||2||
carimaṁ namimō sirivīrajiṇavaraṁ jassa ajjaviya titthaṁ । jayai tilōī kamalāvilāsatilayaṁva supavittaṁ ॥ 3॥
sēsēvi asēsē nikalēvi sayalē'guṇēvi guṇaka liē । namimō am̐garāē nihayaaṇagēvi ajiyāī ॥4॥
paṇamaha phuraṁtapaṇaphaṇakirīḍavararayaṇakiraṇadīvēhiṁ । payataṁ piva sivamaggamaggimaṁ sirisupāsa jiṇaṁ || 5 ||
jāṇaṁ ca tajjagātajjaṇīi laggō uvēmi maṁdapaē । kavyapahē bālō iva tāṇa guruṇa namāmi kamē ॥6॥
sannijjha majjha sayā vimalaṁgōvaṁgaguṇa mahagghaviyā । tijayapiyāmahamuhaka malavāsiṇī kuṇau suyaidēvī ॥7॥
gaṁbhīrapasannapayappavāhiṇi vibuhajaṇamaṇāṇaṁṁ । kavikulagirissa vaṁdē sarassaī iṁdabhūissa || 8 ||
kōna jaṇa harisijjai taraṁgavai - vaiyaraṁ suṇērkēṇa । iyarē pabaṁdha - siṁdhūvi pāviyā jīē mahurataṁ ॥ 9 ॥
bhadaṁ siriharibhadassa sūriṇō jassa bhuvaṇa - raṁgammi । vāṇī visaharasabhāvamaṁtharā naccaē suiraṁ ॥ 10 ॥
maṁdāramaṁjari piva surāvi savaṇāvayaṁ sayaṁ ṇiti । pāgayapabaṁdhakaiṇō vārṇi sirijīvadēvassa ॥11॥
jayati yugādijinēndra āntararipuvijayanāṭakaprabandhē । navanipuṇasūtradhāra iva vihitaśubhasaṁghacatuṣpātraḥ ॥ 1 ॥
sitadhyānānalaprajvalanaśīla karmakāntāradhūmalatā iva । rājanti yasthāṁsē saghūrṇanārśvihurakuralyaḥ ॥2॥
caramaṁ namāmaḥ śrīvīrajinavaraṁ yasyādyāpi ca tīrtham । jayati trilōkīkamalāvilāsa tilakamiva supavitram ॥3॥
śēṣānapyaśēpānniṣkalānapi sakalānaguṇānapi guṇakalitān । namāmō'naṅgarāgānnihatānajñānapyajitādīn ॥ 4 ॥
praṇamata sphuratpañcaphaṇakirīṭavararatna kiraṇadīpaiḥ । prakaṭayantamiva śivamārgamagrimaṁ śrīsupārśvajinam ||5||
yēṣāṁ ca tarjanātarjanyāṁ lagnaḥ sthāpayāmi mandapadāni । kāvyapathē bāla iva tēṣāṁ gurūṇāṁ namāmi kramān ॥6॥
sāṁnidhyaṁ mama sadā vimalāṅgōpāṅgaguṇa maharṣitā । trijagatpitāmaha mukhakamalavāsinī karōtu śrutadēvī ॥7॥
gambhīraprasannapada (yaḥ) pravāhinīṁ vibudhajanamana ānandām । kavikula girērvandē sarasvatīmindrabhūtēḥ ||8||
kō na janō hr̥ṣyēt taraṅgavatīvyatikaraṁ śrutvā । itarē prabandhasindhavō'pi prāpitā yayā madhuratvam ||9||
bhadraṁ śrīharibhadrasya sūrēryasya bhuvanaraṅgē । vāṇī vikasitarasabhāvamantharā nr̥tyati suciram ॥10॥
mandāramañjarīmiva surā api śravaṇapadaṁ svayaṁ nayanti । prākr̥taprabandhakavayō vāṇiṁ śrījīvadēvasya ॥ 11 ॥
1 kha. jugāi । 2 anaṅgē kāmadēvē rāgō yēṣāṁ tāniti virōdhaḥ, nāstyaṅgarāgō yēṣāṁ tāniti parihāraḥ । 3 ka. ga. °yaēvī । 4 ga. 'ūṇaṁ ।
5 kha. niti । 6 cirāṇāṁ kēśānāṁ kuralyaḥ kasāḥ 'karacalī' iti bhāṣāyām ।

For Private & Personal Use Only
www.jainelibrary.org=== lakshmangani01output-9-to-9.json ==========================
supāsanāha-cariammi-
iha suyaṇā kaha maha saṁthavārihā, jē pabaṁdhaguṇalēsaṁ । giṇhati diṭṭhamittaṁpi payaḍaviyaḍēviya na hu dōsē ॥ 12 ॥
tā iha saṁthavivvā paḍhamaṁ ciya dujjaṇā gurujaṇavva । jāṇa vayaṇāṇa bhīō jattēṇa kaī kuṇai kavvaṁ ॥ 13 ॥
ahavā ēyammi samujjayassa maha kiṁ imāē citāē । kō suragiriṇō saraṇi pucchai jalahimmi gaṁtumaṇō ॥ 14 ॥
tā iha supāsacariyaṁ viraiḍakāmassa maha jahāsattiṁ । niyaniyabhāvēṇuvayārakāriṇō hutuṁ tē dōvi ॥ 15 ॥
iha puvva sukaviraiyaṁpabaṁdha savaṇēṇa jaṇiyaguruharisō | kaha lōō amhārisaraiyapabaṁdhēsu ahiramau ? ॥ 16 ॥
katthāhaṁ maṁdamaī katya supāsassa cariyaparikahaṇaṁ । gurutaruphalakhiviyakarō tā isaṇijjō mhi kujjuvva ॥ 17 ॥
tahavi ya jiṇavaraguṇasaṁthavēṇa kammaṁ khavaṁti iha jīvā । ēēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ majjha pavittī imā jāyā ॥ 18 ॥
sukaittaṇakitti puṇa mahēma ēyāu na buhamajjhammi | gaṁdhatthamittha na hu gaṁṭhivannayaṁ carai gaṁdhamaō ॥ 19 ॥
alamittha vittharēṇa, tā saṁpai patthu atthavitthāraṁ । kayamaṁgalōkyārō karēmi bhattīē jahasati ||20||
3
asthi caujalahirasaṇāmaṇahara mahimahiliyāē muhakamalē । suvittamaṁḍaṇaṁ dhāiḍanāmō mahādīvō ॥ 21 ॥
jō nīsanīlavaṁtāyalēhiṁ gayaṇaggalaggasiṁgēhiṁ । rēhai nahasiripariraṁbhaṇatthamukkhiviyabāhuvva ||22||
baihuvannadhannapayapūrapāviyaṁ karisaēhi saṁkiṣṇaṁ । puccavidēhabhidhāṇaṁ tattha ya khittaṁ sukhittaṁva ॥ 23 ॥
jaṁ nīlavaṁtagirisiṁgasariyasīyā sariṣpavāhēṇa । payaḍiyakittipaḍāyaṁva sahaī niyaparamapurisāṇa ||24||
iha sujanāḥ kathaṁ mama saṁstavārhāḥ, yē prabandhaguṇalēśam । gr̥hṇanti dr̥ṣṭamātramapi prakaṭa vikaṭānapi na tu dōṣān॥12॥
tata iha saṁstōtavyāḥ prathamamēva durjanā gurujanā iva । yēṣāṁ vacanēbhyō bhītō yatnēna kaviḥ karōti kāvyam ॥ 13 ॥
arthavaitasmin samudyatasya mama kimanayā cintayā ? । kaḥ suragirēḥ saraṇiṁ pr̥cchati jaladhau gantumanāḥ 1 ॥ 14 ॥
tasmādiha supārśvacaritaṁ viracayitukāmasya mama yathāśakti। nijanijabhāvēnōpakārakāriṇau bhavatāṁ tau dvāvapi ॥ 15 ॥
iha pūrvasukaviviracitaprabandhaśravaṇēna janitaguruharṣaḥ । kathaṁ lōkō'smādr̥śaracitaprabandhēṣvabhiramatām ? ॥16॥
kutrāhaṁ mandamatiḥ kutra supārśvasya caritaparikathanam । gurutaruphalakṣipta karastasmāddhasanīyō'smi kubja iva ॥ 17 ॥
tathāpi ca jinavaraguṇasaṁstavēna karma kṣapayantīha jīvāḥ । ētēna kāraṇēna mama pravr̥ttiriyaṁ jātā ||18||
sukavitvakīrtiṁ punaḥ kāṅkṣāmyētasmād na budhamadhyē | gandhārthamatra na khalu granthivarṇakaṁ carati gandhamr̥gaḥ॥19॥
alamatra vistarēṇa, tasmāt saṁprati prastutārthavistāram । kr̥tamaṅgalōpacāraḥ karōmi bhaktayā yathāśakti ॥ 20॥
asti caturjaladhirasanāmanōharamahī mahilāyā mukhakamalē । supavitramaṇḍanaṁ dhātakīṣaṇḍanāmā mahādvīpaḥ ॥ 21 ॥
yō niṣadhanīlavadacalābhyāṁ gaganāmalagnaśr̥ṅgaiḥ । rājatē namaḥ śrīparirambhaṇārthamutkṣiptabāhuriva ॥22॥
bahuvarṇaṁdha (ghā)nyapada (yaḥ) pūrapāvitaṁ kariśataiḥ ( karṣakaiḥ ) saṁkīrṇam । pūrvavidēhābhidhānaṁ tatra ca kṣētra sukṣētramiva ॥ 23॥
yad nīlavagiriśr̥ṅgasr̥tasītāsaritpravāhēṇa । prakaṭitakīrttipatākamiva rājatē nijaparamapuruṣāṇām ॥24॥
1 ga. hōtu । 2 vidēhapakṣē bahuvarṇakā bhinnajātīyā yē dhanyā bhāgyaśālinaḥ puruṣāstēṣāṁ padānāṁ caraṇānāṁ pūraiḥ samūhaiḥ pāvitaṁ pavitritam,
kṣētrapakṣē bahuvarṇāni dhānyāni yasmāt tādr̥śēna payaḥ pūrēṇa jalapravāhēṇa pāvitamityarthaḥ । 3 ka. kha. kinnaṁ । 4 kha. sāhaḥ ।

puvyabhavatthāvō |
atthi taruṇiyaṇavāraddhavaramaṁgalō maṁgaluggārabahirīkayaṁbaratalō ।
talavarappamuhanivalōyara kkhiyapurō purajaṇāraddhasavisēsadhammujjamō ||25||
jamiyajōgēhiṁ sāhūhiṁ supavittiō tiyasasamarūvaitaruṇayaṇakayavibbhamō ।
bhamaraparikalaṇakhamakamalabhūsiyasarō sarasamallīṇahaṁsāvalīmaṇaharō ||26||
hariyaparikacalaṇā puṭṭagō saṁkulō kulasamuppannanara niyarapayaḍiyanaō ।
naya kayā kalinivōvahayanaramyasuhō suhayarō pavararamaṇijjavijaō tahiṁ ||27|
m
tattha ya jiṇadhammamahāmahivālanivāsagāḍhaduragaṁva । nayarī suhaṁkaricciya asthi jahatthā jayapasiddhā ॥ 28 ॥
jīē visāluṁgō maṇimayaka visīsakaliyapāyārō | gayaṇasirīē rasaṇākalāvalīyaṇṇamuvvahaī ||29||
jīē jalarāsisacchahaparihāsaṁkaṁtaruirara vividhaṁ । jālākalāva piṁgalavaḍavānalalīla muvvahai ||30||
jīē samunnayajiṇabhavaṇasihara saṁṭhaviyakaṇayakalasāṇa । majjhēṇa pailutaṁ na muṇijjai maṁḍala raviṇō ॥ 31 ॥
jīē sarikatamaṇimaṁdirāī nisi sasikarāvapuṭṭhāī । viyaliyavāhalāī rōyaṁtiva taraṇitaviyāī ||32||
gadōsāvi sōsavva jīē pavisaṁti kahavi ravipāyā । kōḍīsaragharasacca viyadhisaṁruddhasaṁcārā ॥ 33 ॥
kamaladalaṭṭhiyajalalavataralāvi na jaṁ kayāvi kayarāyā। muṁcai nivāsijaṇaguṇakalāvasaṁdāṇiyantra sirīrī ॥ 34 ॥
raṁgiratuṁgaturaṁga makhuragganigdhāyavihuriyaṁ dharaṇi । sicaṁti jīē karasīyarēṇa sadayavva karivisarā ॥ 35 ॥
1
asti taruṇījana prārabdhavaramaṅgalō maṅgalōdgārabadhirīkr̥tāmbaratalaḥ ।
purarakṣakapramukha nr̥pa । karakṣitapuraḥ purajanārabdhasaviśēṣadharmōdyamaḥ ||25||
yamitayōgaiḥ sādhubhiḥ supavitritastridaśasamarūpataruṇajanakr̥tavibhramaḥ ।
bhramaraparikalanakṣamakamalabhūṣitasaraḥ saraḥ samālīnahaṁsāvalīmanōharaḥ ॥ 26॥
haritaparikavalanāpuṣṭagōsaṁkulaḥ kulasamutpannanaranikaraprakaṭitanayaḥ ।
naca kadā kalinr̥pōpahatanaramr̥gasukhaḥ sukhakaraḥ pravararamaṇīyavijayastasmin ॥27॥
tatra ca jinadharmamahāmahīpālanivāsagāḍhadurga iva । nagarī śubhakarī khalvasti yathārthī jagatprasiddhā ||28||
yasyā triśālōttuṅgō maṇimayakapiśīrṣakalitaprākāraḥ । gaganaśriyō rasanākalāpalāvaṇyamudvahati ||29||
yasyā ṁ jalarāśisadr̥śaparikhāsaṁkrāntaruciraravibimbam । jvālākalāpapiṅgalavaḍavānalalīlāmudvahati ॥ 30 ॥
yasyāḥ samunnataṁjinabhavanaśikhara saṁsthāpitakanaka kalaśānām । madhyēna paryasyamānaṁ na jñāyatē maṇḍalaṁ ravēḥ ॥31॥
yasyāḥ śaśikāntamaṇimandirāṇi niśi śaśikarāvaspr̥ṣṭāni । vigalitabāppajalāni rudantīva taraṇitaptāni ॥ 32॥
gatadōṣā api sadōṣā iva yasyāṁ praviśanti kathamapi ravipādāḥ | kōṭīśvaragr̥hadr̥ṣṭacihnasaṁruddhasaṁcārāḥ ॥33॥
kamaladalasthitajalalavataralāpi na yāṁ kadāpi kr̥tarāgā । muñcati nivāsijanaguṇakalāpasaṁdānitēva śrīḥ ॥34॥
raṅganaśīlatuṅgaturaṅgamakhurāgranirghātavidhuritāṁ dharaṇim । siñcanti yasyāḥ karasīkarēṇa sadayā iva karivisarāḥ॥ 35 ॥
1 ga. vavarataruṇika । 2 kha. lāvanna0 ga. lāvaṇṇa0 । 3 ga. palōṭaṁ ।

supāsanāhacariammi-
daḍhabhuyadaṁḍālāṇiyakamalākariṇī nivō samarasīhō । cauraṁgacamūsaṁcāraruddhadharaṇīyalō tattha ॥ 36 ॥
maṁḍaliya caṁḍakō daṁḍa mukkakaṁḍōlikhaṁḍiya sirēhiṁ । jō rayai raṇē jayasiriṁ pavēsapaumōvayāraṁ ||37||
vimalakaravāladhārājalēṇa cittāī riucarittāī । jō phusai bhuvaṇabhavaṇaṁtarālabhittīnihittāī ||38|
jassa ya jasajalasittaṁ payāvapāvayapalumavaṇiyalaṁ । navakaṁdalakaliyaṁ piva jayarthabhamisā sayā sahai ॥ 39 ॥
tasta ya sārayacchaṇasasisamavayaṇā mayaṇakaṁdalī daiyā । niyaniruvamasuṁdērima aharī kaya kusumasaraghariṇī ॥40॥
ciracinnapunnapanbhārapariṇayaṁ tīē saha nivō niccaṁ । bhuṁjatō. visayasuha suhēṇa vōlēi bahukālaṁ ॥ 41 ॥
aha annayā ya sēvāsamāgayā sēsamatisāmaṁtē । kayajahuciyasammāṇē saṁjhāvasarē visajjēuṁ ॥ 42 ॥
kayadēvapāyapūyāpahaṇiyanīsēsavigdhasaṁghāō । saṁbhāviūṇa sanbhāvanibbharaṁ kiṁpi niyadaiyaṁ ॥ 43 ॥
vimalacchavētthapacchāiyāē surasariyapulipihulāē । miuhuma haṁsatū lōvahāṇakaliyāē sējjāē || 44 ॥
niddāmuddā miliyacchisaṁpuḍō jāva vāsabhavaṇammi । niviḍīkayadārakavāḍasaṁpuḍō cihna nisī ||45 ||
tāva sahasati niddāsamma duvamadda vihaḍiyacchipuḍō । picchai puraō ramaṇiṁ taṇuppahāpahayatamapaḍalaṁ ॥ 46 ॥
caraṇāraviṁdabhamamiliyamuhalabhasalāvaliva vahamāṇi । maragayamaṇimayamaṁjīra juvalayaṁ maṁjusiṁjaṇayaṁ || 47||
kalayaṁti maṇimayakiraṇakiṁkiṇīkaliyamēhalaṁ ramaṇaṁ । kayatumulatalaba ulasālē rairamaṇanayaraṁva ॥ 48॥
muttāvaliṁ vahati ghaḍimālaṁ piva satahataruṇakaē । gurunāhivāvilāyannarasasamākarisaṇatthaṁva || 49||
dr̥ḍhabhujadaṇḍālānitakamalākariṇīkō nr̥paḥ samarasiṁhaḥ । caturaṅgacamūsaṁcāraruddha dharaṇītalastatra ॥ 36 ॥
maṇḍalitacaṇḍakōdaṇḍamuktakāṇḍālikhaṇḍita śirōbhiḥ । yō racayati raṇē jayaśrīpravēśapadmōpacāramiva ॥ 37॥
vimalakaravāladhārājalēna citrāṇi ripucaritrāṇi । yaḥ spr̥śati bhuvanabhavanāntarālabhittinihitāni ॥ 38॥
yasya ca yaśōjalāsaktaṁ pratāpapāvakaparyastamavanitalam । navakandalakalitamiva jayastambhamiṣātsadā rājati ॥39॥
yasya ca śāradakṣaṇaśaśisamavadanā madanakandalī dayitā । nijanirupama saundaryāgharīkr̥ta kusumaśaragr̥hiṇī ||40॥
ciravīrṇapuṇyaprāgbhārapariṇayaṁ tayā saha nr̥pō nityam । bhuñjānō viṣayasukhaṁ sukhēnātikrāmati bahukālam ॥ 41 ॥
athānyadā ca sēvāsamāgatāśēṣamantrisāmantān । kr̥tayathōcita sammānān sandhyāvasarē visr̥jya ॥ 42 ॥
kr̥tadēvapādapūjāprahataniḥśēṣavighnasaṁghātaḥ । saṁbhāvya sadbhāvanirbharaṁ kimapi nijadayitām ॥43॥
vimalācchavastrapracchāditāyāṁ surasaritpulina pr̥thulāyām । mr̥dusūkṣmahaṁsa tū lōpadhānakalitāyāṁ śayyāyām ||44 ॥
nidrāmudrāmilitākṣisaṁpuṭō yāvad vāsabhavanē । nibiḍīkr̥tadvārakapāṭasaṁpuṭastiṣṭhati niśīthē ॥45॥
tāvat sahasēti nidrāsaṁmardōpamardavighaṭitākṣipuṭaḥ । paśyati puratō ramaṇīṁ tanuprabhā prahatatamaḥ paṭalām ॥ 46 ॥
caraṇāravindabhramamilitamukharabhramarāvalimiva vahantīm । marakatamaṇimayamañjariyugalakaṁ mañjusiñjanakam ॥ 47॥
kalayantīṁ maṇimayakiraṇakiṅkiṇīkalitamēkhalāṁ ramaṇam । kr̥tatumulapurarakṣakā kulasālaṁ ratiramaṇanagaramiva ॥ 48 ॥
muktāvalīṁ vahantīṁ ghaṭīmālāmiva satr̥ṣṇataruṇakr̥tē । gurunābhivāpīlāvaṇyarasasamākarṣaṇārthamiva ॥ 49 ॥
1. ka. ga. paccha । 2 ka. sijāē । 3 ka. kiṁkaṇī । 4 ka. kha. vahiti ।

puvvabhavapatthāvāṁ ।
sīmaṁtanisiyavara paumarāyamaṇikiraṇaraṁjiyaṁ bhālaṁ । kaikēllipallavillaṁ vammahasyaṇaiva vahamāṇi ॥50॥
aha taṁ rioamarasōhiyaṁ picchiūṇa naranāhō । vimhayarasara siyaṁtakaraṇō saparicitiuṁ laggō ॥ 51 ॥
kiṁ kāci kāmiṇī nisiyamayaṇavāṇaṣpahāravihuriyayā । savisēsabhūsiyaṁgī saraṇatthaṁ maṁ samallīṇā ॥ 52 ॥
avā ṭhāṇammi imammi pabalavāyālajāmailammi । payacārīṇa pavēsō kahaṁ nu, tā nūṇamamarīyaṁ ॥ 53 ॥
ava kimimā maha saṁsaēṇa, jā kāvi hōi sā hōu । abbhāgayatti kāuṁ anbhuṭṭāṇārihā tāva ॥54॥
iya citiūṇa paricattasijjasaṁgēṇa tēṇa dharaṇiyalaṁ । mauliyakarakamalēṇaṁ pavittiyaṁ pāpamēhiṁ ॥ 55 ॥
pasaraṁtadaṁtakiraṇāliṁdaliyatimiraṁ payaṁpiyaṁ tayaṇu । suaṇu ! taē niyajammēṇa bhūsiyā kahasu kā jāī ? ॥ 56 ॥
kāya tuha nāmavaṇṇāvalī vibhūsēī lōyavayaṇāī ? | kēṇa va kajjēṇa siṁha pavittiya caraṇaphuṁsēṇa ? ॥57॥
iya bahumāṇapurassaraṇaravaijuttābhibhāsaṇapahiṭṭā । sā pabhaṇai nivapuṁgava ! jai sussā tuha ihatthē || 58 ||
tā hōsu sāvahāṇō khaṇamēgaṁ jēṇa tujjha ahuṇāvi । payaḍēmi puvvapuṭuṁ savittharaṁ, tō imaṁ kahai ॥ 59 ॥
atthi sasikaṁtamaṇisālacaṁgimāsamiyasaggasōhaggaṁ । asaḍhaviyaḍḍhamahiḍhiyanarakaliyaṁ rayaṇasārapuraṁ ॥ 60 ॥
taṁ pālai pōḍhapayāvajalaṇajālāvalīhiṁ sayakālaṁ । jaliyadariyārivaṁsō rāyā saṁgāmasurōti ॥ 61 ॥
tassa ya samaggasōhaggapamuhaguṇagāmagāmaṇī daiyā । rairamaṇagēhiṇī iva nāmēṇaṁ caṁdalēhatti ||32||
avarupparapīiparāyaṇaṁtakaraṇāṇa tāṇa sayakālaṁ । annōnnaamaṁdāṇaṁdamaṁdirā vāsarā jaṁti ॥ 63 ॥
sīmantaniśritavarapadmarāgamaṇikiraṇarañjitaṁ bhālam । kaṅkēllipallavavad manmathasadanamiva vahantīm ॥50॥
atha taṁ nirupamarūpōpaśōbhitāṁ dr̥ṣṭvā naranāthaḥ । vismayarasa rasitāntaḥkaraṇaḥ sa paricintayituṁ lagnaḥ ॥51॥
kiṁ kācit kāminī niśitamadanabāṇaprahāravidhuritā । saviśēṣabhūṣitāṅgī śaraṇārtha māṁ samālīnā ? ॥ 52 ॥
athavā sthānē'smin prabalavācālayāmikē । padacāriṇāṁ pravēśaḥ kathaṁ nu tasmād nūnamamarīyam ॥13॥
athavā kimanēna mama saṁśayēna, yā kāpi bhavati sā bhavatu | abhyāgatēti kr̥tvā'bhyutthānārhā tāvat ॥ 54 ॥
iti cintayitvā parityaktaśayyāsaṅgēna tēna gharaṇitalam । mukulitakarakamalēna pavitritaṁ pādapadmābhyām ॥55॥
prasaraddantakiraṇālidalitatimiraṁ prajalpitaṁ tadanu । sutanu ! tvayā nijajanmanā bhūṣitā kathaya kā jātiḥ ? ॥56॥
kā ca tava nāmavarṇāvalī vibhūṣayati lōkavadanāni ? | kēna vā kāryēṇa gr̥haṁ pavitritaṁ caraṇasparśēna ? || 57 ||
iti bahumāna purassaranarapatiyuktābhibhāṣaṇaprahr̥ṣṭā । sā prabhaṇati nr̥papuṅgava ! yadi śuśrūṣā tavēhārthē ॥ 58॥
tatō bhava sāvadhānaḥ kṣaṇamēkaṁ yēna tavādhunāpi । prakaṭayāmi pūrvapr̥ṣṭaṁ savistaraṁ tata idaṁ kathayati ॥ 19 ॥
asti śaśikāntamāṇasālacaṅgimāśrāmatasvargasaubhāgyam । aśaṭhavidagdhamaharddhikanarakalitaṁ ratnasārapuram ॥60॥
taṁ pālayati prauḍhapratāpajvalanajvālāvalībhiḥ sadākālam । jvalitadr̥ptārivaṁśō rājā saṁgrāmaśūra iti ॥ 61 ॥
tasya samagrasaubhāgyapramukhaguṇagrāmaṇīrdayitā । ratiramaṇagēhinavi nāmnā candralēkhēti ॥62॥
parasparaprītiparāyaṇāntaḥkaraṇayōstayōḥ sadākālam । anyōnyāmandānandamandirāṇi vāsarā yānti ||63 ||
1 ka. ga. kaṁkilli । 2 ka. ga. 'hurahiyā ।

aha annayā ya saha sahayarīhiṁ pāsāyasiharamārūḍhā । jā ciṭṭhā tā picchara kayasiṁgāraṁ nayaralōyaṁ ॥ 64 ॥
aṁkanivēsiyaniyaniyaputtayapaḍiputtanattaputtīyaṁ । vivihaphalaphullaparikaliyapaḍa liyāvāvaḍakara || 65 ॥
kusumāvayaṁsagābhihaujjāṇē'ṇaṁgatērasidiṇammi । gacchaṁtaṁ kusumāuhapayajuyalasamaccaṇanimittaṁ ॥ 66 ॥
tammajjhadviyavahuviharayaṇāharaṇēhiṁ bhrūsiyasarīraṁ । picchai kamalāyara maṁtipaṇaiṇi laḍahalāyaṇaṁ ||37||
sōhaggamaḍappharahēriyakāmagharaṇi suhāsaṇāsīṇaṁ । aṁkanivēsiyaduhiyaṁ lālitaṁ vivihabhaṁgīhiṁ ॥ 68 ॥
taṁ picchiūṇa saṁgāmasuranaranāhapaṇaiṇī sahasā । sasaharakaracuṁbiyakamaliṇivva dīṇāṇaṇā jāyā || 69 ॥
pāubbhavaṁtanimmēramannubharabhāranīsahā tayaṇu । kōvabhavaṇammi jarajinna sikkaḍē paḍai jariyavva ॥ 70 ॥
ciṁtai niyabālāē vibhūsiyāṇaṁgatērasidiṇammi । jā ēvaṁ vilasai maṁtipaṇaiṇī sacciya kayatthā || 71 ॥
vihalō cciya maha mahilājammō kaṁkēllitarulayāēvva । jīē suyapasavaphalaṇēṇa pāviyaṁ nēya jammaphalaṁ ॥72॥
tā kahaṇu salahaṇijjā piyamāṇasaphuraṇarāyahaṁsīvi । hōmi ahaṁ jīucchaṁgalaṁḍaṇaṁ nēya duhiyāvi ॥ 73 ॥
iya tīē niyapasavōvalaṁbhaciṁtāsamuddapaḍiyāē । tadukkhadukkhaō iva divasavasāṇakkhaṇō pattō ॥ 74 ॥
ētthaṁtarammi rōsāruṇacchiasaīkaḍakkhalakkhēhiṁ । vicchuriyaṁ piva raviṇō vivaṁ āryaviraṁ jāyaṁ ॥ 75 ॥
acchōyayaṁtra sēvai khaṇēṇa bhāṇū vilūṇakarapasarō । avarasamuddē puṇaravi diṇalacchīsaṁgamanimittaṁ || 76 ||
atthaṁ gayammi sūrē kamēṇa akkama dasadisācakaṁ । tammaragamagaṇatthaṁva pamuiyaṁ timiranivasiviraṁ ॥ 77 ॥
athānyadā ca saha sahacarībhiḥ prāsādaśikharamārūḍhā । yāvat tiṣṭhati tāvatpaśyati kr̥tagr̥ṅgāraṁ nagara lōkam ॥ 64 ॥
aṅkanivēśitanijanijaputrakapratiputranaptr̥putrīkam । vividhaphalapuṣpaparikalitapaṭalikāvyāpr̥takarāgram ॥ 65 ॥
kusumāvataṁsakābhidhōdyānē'naṅgatrayōdaśīdinē । gacchantaṁ kusumāyudhapadayugalasamarcananimittam ॥66॥
tanmadhyasthitabahuvidharatnābharaṇairbhūṣitaśarīrām । paśyati kamalākaramantripraṇayinīṁ sundaralāvaṇyām ॥67॥
saubhāgyagarvādharitakā magr̥hiṇikāṁ sukhāsanāṁsīnām । aṅkanivēśitaduhitaraṁ lālayantīṁ vividhabhaṅgibhiḥ ॥68॥
tāṁ dr̥ṣṭvā saṁgrāmaśūranaranāthapraṇayinī sahasā । śaśadharakaracumbitakamalinīva dīnānanā jātā || 69 ||
prādurbhavannirmaryādamanyubharabhāra niḥsahā tadanu । kōpabhavanē jarājarṇisītkaṭē patati jvaritēva ||70||
cintayati nijabālayā vibhūṣitā'naṅgatrayōdaśīdinē । yaivaṁ vilasati mantripraṇayinī saiva kr̥tārthā ॥ 71 ॥
viphalamēva mama mahilājanma kaṅkēllitarulatāyā iva । yayā sutaprasavaphalanēna prāptaṁ naiva janmaphalam ॥72॥
tasmātkathaṁ nu ślāghanīyā priyamānasasphuraṇarājahaṁsyapi । bhavāmyahaṁ yasyā utsaṅgalāñchanaṁ naiva duhitāpi ॥ 73 ॥
iti tasyāṁ nijaprasavōpalambhacintāsamudrapatitāyām । tadduḥkhaduḥkhita iva divasāvasānakṣaṇaḥ prāptaḥ ॥74॥
atrāntarē rōṣāruṇākṣyasatīkaṭākṣalakṣaiḥ । vicchuritamiva ravērbimbamātānaṁ jātam ॥75॥
acchōdakamiva sēvatē kṣaṇēna bhānurvilūnakaraprasaraḥ । aparasamudrē punarapi dinalakṣmīsaṅgamanimittam ॥76॥
astaṁ gatē sūrē kramēṇākrāmati daśadikcakram । tanmārgamārgaṇārthamiva pramuditaṁ timiranr̥paśibiram ॥77॥
1 ka. ḍariya । 2 ka, kha, lālaṁtiṁ ।

ēttō ya caṁdalēhāē kōvabhavaṇappavēsavr̥ttaṁtō । saṁgāmasūra rāyassa sāhiō sōviyallīē || 78 ||
sōvi hu niyaavarāhāsaṁkāsaṁbhaṁtamāṇasō ēi । tīsē pasāyaṇatthaṁ kayasaṁjhā vihiyakāyanvō ॥ 79 ॥

।
aḍāṇāivihiṁ kāūṇaṁ sāvi ṭhāi tuṇḍikā । tayabhimuhaṁ sappaṇayaṁ tō rāyā bhaṇiumārō ||80||
kiṁ dēvi ! maē maṇasāvi kāmiṇiṁ kamavi ahilasaṁtēṇa । tuha avaruddhaṁ kiṁcivi vihiyaṁ āharaṇakhūṇaṁbā ॥ 81 ॥
ahavāvi visamadiṭṭhīē niyai tuha pāyapaṁkayaṁ kōvi ? | kiṁvā pariyaṇamajjhammi kōvi avagannaē āṇaṁ ? ॥ 82 ॥
ahavāvi sattusīmaṁtiṇīu samasīsiyaṁ samaṁ tumaē । kammivi atthē kuvrvvati kahasu kamalacchi ! pasiūṇaṁ ॥ 83 ॥
sā jaṁpai avaraddhaṁ na taē khūṇapi katthaviya vihiyaṁ । visamapi kōvi na niyai naya āṇaṁ khaṁḍaē kōvi ॥ 84 ॥
sattukāmiṇīōvi maē samaṁ kaha kuṇaṁtu samasīsiṁ । jaya nihaṇarakkhaṇakhamā jā tuha pabhavaṁti bhuyadaṁḍā || 85 ॥
kiṁpuṇa pahu ! avarajjhai ēttha vihī jēṇa savvasāmamiṁga । vihiūṇa maṁdapunnāē daṁsiyaṁ nēya jāyasuhaṁ ॥ 86 ॥
kiṁca,
piyayama ! tumapi vasaṇāsaṇabhōyaṇamitta punnaparibhōgō । kassa kaē uppāyasi viśvabharaṁ saṁtaīē viṇā ? || 87 ||
rayaṇanihiṇēva jaṇaēṇa jēṇa mahusūyaṇassava suyassa । uppāiūṇa lacchī viyarijjai aivisālāvi ॥ 88 ॥
tiyasapurapatthiyassavi hōhī tuha kahaṇu nivbuī pacchā। jai nō havissai suō kuladhammadhaṇāivuḍa ḍhikarō ॥ 89 ॥
tāki bahuṇā piya ! jaṁpiēṇa taṁ kiṁpi kuṇasu taṁ ihi । gabbhāṇubhāvapaṁḍuragaṁḍayalaṁ niyasi maṁ jēṇaṁ ॥ 90॥
itaśca candralēkhāyāḥ kōpabhavanapravēśavr̥ttāntaḥ । saṁgrāmaśūrarājasya kathitaḥ sauvidallyā ||78 ||
sō'pi khalu nijāparādhāśaṅkāsaṁbhrāntamānasa ēti । tasyāḥ prasādanārthaṁ kr̥tasandhyāvihitakartavyaḥ ॥79॥
abhyutthānādividhiṁ kr̥tvā sāpi tiṣṭhati tūṣṇīkā । tadabhimukhaṁ sapraṇayaṁ tatō rājā bhaṇitumārabdhaḥ ॥80॥
kiṁ dēvi ! mayā manasāpi kāminīṁ kāmapyabhilaṣamāṇēna । tavāparāddhaṁ kiñcidapi vihitamābharaṇakṣūṇaṁ vā ॥ 81 ॥
athavāpi viṣamadr̥ṣṭyā paśyati tava pādapaṅkajaṁ kō'pi । kiṁvā parijanamadhyē kōṣyavagaṇayatyājñām ? ॥ 82 ॥
athavāpi śatrusīmantinyaḥ spardhā samaṁ tvayā । kasminnapyarthē kurvanti kathaya kamalākṣi ! prasīdya ॥ 83 ॥
sā jalpatyaparāddhaṁ na tvayā kṣūṇamapi kutrāpica vihitam । viṣamamati kō'pi na paśyati nacājñāṁ khaṇḍayati kō'pi ॥
śatrukāminyō'pi mayā samaṁ kathaṁ kurvantu spardhām । jagannidhanarakṣaṇakṣamau yāvat tava prabhavatō bhujadaṇḍau ॥ 85 ॥
kintu prabhō ! aparādhyatyatra vidhiyēna sarvasāmagrīm । vidhāya mandapuṇyāyā darśitaṁ naiva jātasukham ॥ 86॥
kiñca,
priyatama ! tvamapi vasanāsanabhōjanamātra pūrṇa paribhōgaḥ । kasya kr̥tē utpādayasi vibhavabharaṁ santatyā vinā ? ॥87॥।
ratnanidhinēva janakēna yēna madhusūdanāyēva sutāya । utpādya lakṣmīrvitīryatē'tiviśālāpi ॥ 88 ॥
tridaśapuraprasthitasyāpi bhaviṣyati tava kathaṁ nu nirvr̥tiḥ paścāt । yadi nō bhaviṣyati sutaḥ kuladharmadhanādivr̥ddhikaraḥ
tasmātkiṁ bahunā priya ! jalpitēna tatkimapi kuru tvamidānīm । garbhānubhāvapāṇḍura gaṇḍatalāṁ paśyasi māṁ yēna ॥ 90॥

supāsanāha-cariammi-
aha - rāyā bhaṇai sayāvi majjha dūmai maṇammi ēsatthō । navaraṁ ihabhavasaṁciṁtaṇāisajjhō na hōi phuḍaṁ ॥ 91 ॥
kiṁtu piē ! puvvabhavāṇucinēhiṁ sijjhaē nūṇaṁ । tāī vihiyāī na hu hōjja, tēṇa na hu saṁtaī amha || 92 ||
tā piyayamē ! visāyaṁ muṁcasu ihi kuṇēsu savisēsaṁ । kuladēvayāi pūyaṁ ittha suōya iyaṁ ca tahā ॥ 93 ॥
iya sōūṇaṁ atōphuraṁtadararōsakaṁpiraharāē । saṁgāmasūranaravaisamuhaṁ dēvīē bhaṇiyamimaṁ ॥ 94 ||
piyayama ! puvvāiṭuṁ savvaṁpi savittharaṁ maē vihiyaṁ । bhattibharaṇibbharāē tahāvina samīhiyaṁ siddhaṁ ॥ 95 ॥
kiṁca,
.?
suhasajyaṁ ciya kajjaṁ kijjai mahilāhiṁ nūṇa lōyammi । dussajyaṁ puṇa kajjaṁ kuṇaṁti purisāṇa bhuyadaṁḍā ॥ 96 ॥
jēṇaṁ sāhasasahiyā gaṇaṁti tē girivaraṁpi girikappaṁ । bhuyagāhivaṁpi rajjuṁ pāyaiālaṁpi hu bilāyāraṁ ॥97॥
tā tubhicciya iha ujjamaṁtu iya nisuṇiūṇa sē vayaṇaṁ । kiṁkāyavvavimūḍhō jā ciṭṭhai naravarō tattha ॥98॥
tāva sahasati picchara ujjōyaṁ kōvabhavaṇamajjhammi । vimhayavasēṇa tō caudisiṁpi sō pēsaē dihiṁ ॥ 99 ॥
pēcchai ya lulaṁtamahaṁtarayaṇamayakuṁḍa lillagaṁḍayalaṁ । dārēṇaṁ pavisaṁtaṁ surajuyalaṁ divvakaṁtillaṁ ॥ 100 ॥
taṁ daddūṇa tahāvihaciṁdhēhiṁ jāṇiūṇa dēvatti । rāyā vimhiyāhiyaō abbhuṭṭhāṇāiyaṁ kuṇai ॥ 101 ॥
bhai ya kē tumbhē ēttha āgayā kēṇa vāvi kajjēṇa ? । iya tumha cariyapīūsapāṇapauṇā imē savaṇā ॥ 102 ॥
aha tammajjhā ēgō dēvō jaṁpai suṇēsu naranāha ! | sōhammē amhē dōvi iṁdasāmāṇiyā dēvā ॥ 103 ॥
atha rājā bhaṇati sadāpi mama dāvayati mana ēṣō'rthaḥ । navaramihabhavasaṁcintanādisādhyō na bhavati sphuṭam ॥ 91 ॥
kintu priyē ! pūrvabhavānucīrṇapuṇyaiḥ sidhyati nūnam । tāni vihitāni na khalu bhavēyuḥ, tēna na saṁtatirāvayōḥ ॥92॥
tasmāt priyatamē ! viṣādaṁ muñcēdānīṁ kuruṣva saviśēṣam । kuladēvatāyāḥ pūjāmatra sutōpayācitaṁ ca tathā ॥93॥
iti śrutvā'ntaḥsphuradīṣadrōṣakampanaśīlādharayā । saṁgrāmaśūranarapatisaṁmukhaṁ dēvyā bhaṇitamidam ||14||
priyatama ! pūrvādiṣṭaṁ sarvamapi savistaraṁ mayā vihitam । bhaktibharanirbharayā tathāpi na samīhitaṁ siddham ॥95॥
kiñca,
sukhasādhyamēva kāryaṁ kriyatē mahilābhirnūnaṁ lōkē । duḥsādhaṁ punaḥ kāryaṁ kurvanti puruṣāṇāṁ bhujadaṇḍāḥ ||96 ॥
yēna sāhasasahitā gaṇayanti tē girivaramapi girikalpam । bhujagādhipamapi rajjūṁ pātālamapi hi bilākāram ॥97॥
tasmād yūyamēvēhōdyacchatēti śrutvā tasyā vacanam । kiṁkartavyavimūḍhō yāvattiṣṭhati naravarastatra ॥98 ॥
tāvat sahasrēti paśyati udyōtaṁ kōpabhavanamadhyē | vismayavaśēna tataścaturdikṣvapi sa prēṣayati dr̥ṣṭim ॥ 99॥
paśyati ca lōlanmahāratnamayakuṇḍalitagaṇḍatalam । dvārēṇa praviśat surayugalaṁ divyakā ntikam ॥100॥
tad dr̥ṣṭvā tathāvidhacinairjñātvā dēvāviti । rājā vismitahr̥dayō'bhyutthānādikaṁ karōti ॥101॥
bhaṇati ca kau yuvāmatrāgatau kēnaṁ vāpi kāryēṇa ? । iti yuvayōścaritapīyūṣapānapraguṇāvimau śravaṇō ॥ 102 ॥
atha tanmadhyādēkō dēvō jalpati śr̥ṇu naranātha ! । saudharma āvāṁ dvāvapandrisāmānikau dēvau ॥103॥
1 ga. ōāi° । 2 °yāraṁ । 3 kha. ga. tubbhēci ।

punvabhavapatthāvō ।
jēṇava kajjēṇa puṇō samāgayā taṁpi saṁparyaṁ suṇasu । kharṇamikamavahiyamaṇō hōha sāhijjaē ittō ॥ 104॥
niyavihavamāhamasarisaṁ cirakālaṁ tattha visuyasuhamaṇahaṁ । aṇuhaviyamamaṁdāṇaṁdajala hiparimajjiraṁgēhiṁ ।। 105 ॥
aha kēiyā nēsaggiyasaggasirīsaṁgabhōgabhaṁgakarā | jāyā amhāṇa imā duṭṭhāridvāṇa richōlī || 106 ॥
kaṁṭhayalakaliyamālā parimalabahulāvi sayā viyāsillā । amhē bhāviradīharapavāsaduhiyā milāē । । 107 ।।
sāsaṇasirīvi niyapariyaṇammi na tahā phurēi amhāṇa । bhāvibhavanayaragamaṇē paḍhamaṁ ciyaṁ kayapayāṇavva ॥ 108 ॥
bhāvibhavagabbhasaṁbhavasaṁbhāviyabhūrisabhamēva । animittaṁ ciya kaṁpai kāō amhāṇa aṇusamayaṁ ॥ 109 ॥
sahagamaṇamaṇō parabhavapatthāṇaṁ jāṇiūṇa amhāṇa | kaṁpatō kappatarū siḍhilai niyamūlajālaṁva ॥ 110 ॥
aṇavarayavihiyabhāsurarayaṇavimāṇāvalōyapahayavva । amhāṇa nayaṇatārā pariciyavatthummivi milāi॥ 111 ॥
aṇavarayaṁ rayaṇavimāṇagamaṇasaṁbhaggagaiyamiva dēhaṁ । amhāṇa niviḍajaḍimāḍaṁbaramāvahai cakamaṇē ॥ 112 ॥
iya daṭṭumaṇiṭṭamariṣṭumaṁḍalaṁ muṇiyacavaṇakhaṇavihurā। avagaṇiyadhīrimaguṇā kēvalipāsaṁ samallīṇā ॥ 113 ॥
āgāmibhavuṣpāyaṁ pucchēḍaṁ jāṇiūṇa tēṇa sayaṁ । hiyayagayābhippīō amhāṇaṁ sīhiō ēvaṁ ।। 114 ॥
jaha bhō dēvāṇupiyā ! tubhē caviūṇa dēvalōgāō । saṁgāmasūrarannō dēvīē caṁdalēhāē ॥ 115 ॥
ēgō puttatā duiō duhiyatti hōhihī, ēyaṁ । sōūṇaṁ amhēhiṁ paryapiyē nāha ! kiṁ sa nivō ? ॥ 116 ॥
sammaṭṭhī ahavā micchadiṭṭhitti tēṇa tō bhaṇiyaṁ । tubbhēhitō sammaṁ pavajjihī bhaō saṁtō ॥ 117 ॥
yēna vā kāryēṇa punaḥ samāgatau tadapi sāṁprataṁ śr̥ṇu । kṣaṇamēkamavahitamanā bhava kathyata itaḥ ॥ 104 ॥
nizavibhavamahimasadr̥śaṁ cirakālaṁ tatra viṣayasukhamakṣatam । anubhūtamamandānandajaladhiparimagnāṅgābhyām ॥ 105 ॥
atha kadācinnaisargika svargaśrīsaṅgabhōgabhaṅgakarā | jātā''vayōriyaṁ duṣṭāriṣṭānāṁ paṅktiḥ ॥ 106 ॥
kaṇṭhatalakalitamālā parimalabahulāpi sadā vikāsavatī । āvayōrbhavanaśīladīrghapravāsaduḥkhitā mlāyati ॥ 107॥
śāsanaśrīrapi nijaparijanē na tathā sphuratyāvayōḥ । bhāvibhavanagaragamanē prathamamēva kr̥taprayāṇēva ॥108॥
bhāvibhavagarbhasaṁbhava saṁbhāvitabhūribhramaṇēva । animittamēva kampatē kāya āvayōranusamayam ॥ 109 ॥
sahagamanamanāḥ parabhavaprasthānaṁ jñātvā''vayōḥ । kampamānaḥ kalpataruḥ śithilayati nijamūlajālamiva ॥ 110 ॥
anavaratavihitabhāsuraratna vimānāvalōkaprahatēva । āvayōrnayanatārā paricitavastunyapi mlāyati ॥ 111॥
anavaraṁtaṁ ratnavimānagamanasaṁbhagnagatika iva dēhaḥ । āvayōrniviḍajaḍimāḍambaramāvahati caṅkramaṇē ॥ 112 ॥
iti dr̥ṣṭvāniṣṭamariṣṭamaṇḍalaṁ jñātacyavanakṣaṇavidhurau । avagaṇitadhīrimaguṇau kēvalipārśvaṁ samālīnau ॥113॥
āgāmibhavōtpādaṁ praṣṭuṁ jñātvā tēna khayam । hr̥dayagatābhiprāya āvayōḥ kathita ēvam ॥ 114॥
yathā bhō dēvānupriyō ! yuvāṁ cyutvā dēvalōkāt । saṁgrāmaśūrarājasya dēvyāścandralēkhāyāḥ ॥ 115 ॥
ēkaḥ putratayā dvitīyō duhitēti bhaviṣyathaḥ, ētat । śrutvā''vābhyāṁ prajalpitaṁ nātha ! kiṁ sa nr̥paḥ ॥ 116॥
samyagdr̥ṣṭirathavā mithyādr̥ṣṭiriti tēna tatō bhaṇitam । yuvābhyāṁ samyaktvaṁ prapatsyatē bhadrakaḥ san ॥ 117॥
1 ka. siḍhalāi | 2 ga. bhamēda । 3 gappāyaṁ । 4 ga. kahiyamiṇamēva

10
supāsanā-riamma-
iya sōūṇaṁ namiḍaṁ ca kēvaliṁ iha samāgayā amhē । tuha sammattapavattaṇahēḍaṁ jēṇamha tujjha kulē ॥ 118 ॥
uppannāṇaṁ na hu hōi dulahō naravariṁda ! jiṇadhammō । samayammi jaṁ imassavi taṁ bhaṇiyaṁ mūlabīyāta ॥ 119॥
aparaṁ ca,
amhāṇaṁ na hu dūmai iṇhiṁ cavarṇapi dēvalōgāō। aviraibahulāō, tuha kulammi jāyāṇa jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 120 ॥
sāvayakulaṁ kulāṇaṁ niggaṁthaṁ pavayaṇaṁ pavayaṇāṇaṁ । dāṇāṇamabhayadāṇaṁ samāhimaraṇaṁ ca maraṇāṇaṁ ॥ 121 ॥
tā tumhakuluppannā sammaṁ paḍivajjiūṇa jiprādhammaṁ । puvvaṁ piva saggasirīē bhāyaṇa hō mha nahu cōjjaṁ ॥ 122 ॥
aha saharisō nariṁdō tayabhimuhaṁ bhaṇai kam̐haha kaha puvviṁ । jiṇadhammāsēvāē pattā dēvattaṇaṁ tubbhē ? || 123 ॥
tēhiṁ niyacariyaṁ jaivi na juttaṁ kahēumamhāṇa । tahavi tuha patthaṇāē sāhijjai, kahai tāṇēgō ॥ 124 ॥
nimmalaphalihasilāyalavisālasālaggabhaggaravimaggaṁ । āsi iha bharahabhūmīē bhūsaṇaṁ kaṇayakūḍapuraṁ ।। 125 ।।
tattha frees siṭṭī uragarihō visidvaguṇajuttō । nāmēṇaṁ jiṇacaṁdō janamāṇasarāyahaṁsōvva ॥ 126 ॥
sīlavaī nāmēṇaṁ sīlālaṁkārasāliṇī tassa । bhajjā niruvamaviṇayappamukkhaguṇajaṇiyajaṇacōjjā ॥ 127॥
tīsē puttattaṇaṁ saṁjāō ha uvāiyasaēhiṁ । ahigayakalākalāvō kamēṇa tāruṇṇamaṇupattō ॥ 128 ॥
aha jiṇacaṁdō siṭṭhī kuṭuṁbasāmittayampi mēṁ ṭhaviḍaṁ । jiṇabhaṇiyadhammamaggāṇusāraō maraṇamāvannō ॥ 129 ॥
tavrahadūmiō haṁ tasiyamaggamaṇucarāmi paraṁ । dhammammi pamāyaṁtō gharaciṁtāvāvaḍattēṇa ॥ 130 ॥
iti śrutvā natvā ca kēvalinamiha samāgatāvāvām । tava samyaktvapravartana hētōryēnāvayōstava kulē ॥118॥
utpannayōrna khalu bhavēd durlabhō naravarēndra ! jinadharmaḥ । samayē yadasyāpi tad bhaṇitaṁ mūla bījamiti ॥ 119॥
aparañca,
āvayōrna khalu dāvayatīdānīṁ cyavanamapi dēvalōkāt | aviratibahulāt, tava kulē jātayōryad bhaṇitam॥ 120 ॥
śrāvakakulaṁ kulānāṁ naigranthaṁ pravacanaṁ pravacanānām । dānānāmabhayadānaṁ samādhimaraṇaṁ ca maraṇānām ॥121॥
tasmādyuṣmatkulōtpannau samyak pratipadya jinadharmam । pūrvamiva svargaśriyā bhājanaṁ bhaviṣyāvō na khalvāścaryam ॥ 122॥
atha saharṣō narēndrastadabhimukhaṁ bhaṇati kathayataṁ kathaṁ pūrvam | jinadharmāsēvayā prāptau dēvatvaṁ yuvām ॥ 123 ॥
tau bhaṇatō nijacaritaṁ yadyapi na yuktaṁ kathayitumāvayōḥ । tathāpi tava prārthanayā kathyatē, kathayati tayōrēkaḥ ॥ 124॥
nirmalasphaṭikaśilātala viśālaśālāgrabhagnaravimārgam । āsīdiha bharatabhūmē bhūṣaṇaṁ kanakakūṭapuram ॥ 129 ॥
tatra nivasati śrēṣṭhī pauragariṣṭhō viśiṣṭaguṇayuktaḥ । nāmnā jinacandrō janamānasarājahaṁsa iva ॥ 126 ॥
śīlavatī nāmnā śīlālaṅkāraśālinī tasya । bhāryā nirupamavinayapramukhaguṇajanitajanāścaryā ॥127॥
tasyāḥ putratvēna saṁjātō'hamupayācitaśataiḥ । adhigatakalākalāpaḥ kramēṇa tāruṇyamanuprāptaḥ ॥ 128 ॥
atha jinacandraḥ śrēṣṭhī kuṭumbasvāmitvē māṁ sthāpayitvā । jinabhaṇitadharmamārgānusāratō maraṇamāpannaḥ ॥129॥
tarihadāvitō'haṁ taddarśitamārgamanucarāmi param । dharmē mādyan gr̥hacintāvyāpr̥tatvēna ॥ 130 ॥
1 ka. humha । 2. kaha kahūṁ । 3 kha bhaṇihiṁ, ga. bhaṇahi । 4ka. ga. saṁṭha° ।

puvyabhavapatthāvō |
11
aha maha māyā haṭṭāgamaṇāvasarammi sigyamēva sayaṁ । varasālidālighayaghayapūrarāiyaṁ rasavaī kuṇai ॥ 131 ॥
navaraṁ parivēsatī mahabhimuhaṁ bhaṇai paidiṇaṁ ēvaṁ । vaccha ! duhāī pāvihisi bhuṁjirō vāsiya bhattaṁ ॥ 132॥
ahamavi bhaṇāmi aṁbē ! kahamēyaṁ bhaṇasi paidiṇaṁpi tumaṁ । sayamavi nivvattiyarasavaīē maha bhōyaṇaṁ ditī ? ।। 133॥
iya puṭṭhā tuṇḍikā hōuṁ sā ciṭṭhaē sayāvi taō । kōūhalakaliēṇaṁ puṇōvi puṭṭhā guruvarōhā || 134 ॥
tō tīē saṁlattaṁ ēvaṁ taṁ vaccha ! puccha gaṁtūṇaṁ । samayāmayanihisūriṁ samōsaḍhaṁ ajja ujjāṇē || 135 ॥
aha tatthavi gaṁtuṁ taṁ namiuṁ pasiṇissamahamimaṁ jāva । tāva sayamēva nāṇēṇa jāṇiuṁ tēṇimaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ।। 136॥
bhō tuha ēyārūvaṁ pasiṇaṁ sāhissaī suhāgapurē । cēḍayasiddhō māyaṁgasaḍhaō thāvarō nāma ॥137॥||
ahaha ahō ! acchariyaṁ savvaṁ nāṇēṇa jāṇamāṇōvi । jaṁ maha na imaṁ sāhai tadavassaṁ kāraṇaṁ kiṁpi ॥ 138 ॥
ēvaṁ vicitamāṇō kamēṇa pattō suhāgapuranayarē । jāva ramaṇīyayāē picchāmi ahaṁ vivaṇimagaṁ ॥ 139 ॥
tāva jarajajjaraṁgō niyasiyaājāṇumaliṇasāḍillō | paṁḍuriyarōmakūvō payaḍasirādhamaṇisaṁṭhāṇō ॥ 140 ॥
harinahakaḍhaṇa mahallirapayanaharaparaṁparāē vikarālō | addhagharaṭṭiyaighuṭaṁ pūgaṁ gaṁṭhīē baṁdhatō ॥ 141 ॥
dūrapalaṁbiranāsā kēsacaō mūlaghaṭṭakararuhaō । bahusēyasinnamalamailakhaṁpaṇayacikkaṇasarīrō ॥ 142 ॥
gahiyakayāṇagauvvariyalabbhadavirṇapi patthamāṇēhiṁ । saha gāhagēhiṁ duvayaṇanibbharaṁ kalahamāṇō ya ॥ 143 ॥
kahakahavi hu sattēṇaṁ rēṇutusāvaṇayaṇatthamanilammi । uppāḍiūṇa piḍagāī taṁdulē ppiṇitō ya ॥ 144 ॥
atha mama mātā haṭṭāgamanāvasarē śīghramēva svayam । varaśālidālighr̥taghr̥tapūrādikāṁ rasavartī karōti ॥ 131 ॥
navaraṁ parivēviṣāṇā madabhimukhaṁ bhaṇati pratidinamēvam । vatsa ! duḥkhāni prāpsyasi bhuñjānō vāsitaṁ bhaktam ॥ 132 ॥
ahamapi bhaṇāmyamba ! kathamētadbhaṇasi pratidinamapi tvam । svayamapi nirvartitarasavatyā mama bhōjanaṁ dadatī || 133 ॥
iti pr̥ṣṭā tūṣṇīkā bhūtvā sā tiṣṭhati sadāpi tataḥ । kautūhalakalitēna punarapi pr̥ṣṭā gurvavarōdhāt ॥ 134॥
tatastayā saṁlaptamētat tvaṁ vatsa ! pr̥ccha gatvā । samayāmr̥tanidhisūriṁ samavasr̥tamadyōdyānē ॥135॥
atha tatrāpi gatvā taṁ natvā prakṣyāmyahamidaṁ yāvat । tāvat svayamēva jñānēna jñātvā tēnēdaṁ bhaṇitam॥136॥
bhōstavaitadrūpaṁ praśnaṁ kathayiṣyati śubhākapurē । cēṭakasiddhō mātaṅgaśrāddhakaḥ sthāvarō nāma ॥ 137॥
ahaha ahō ! āścarya sarvaṁ jñānēna jānannapi । yad māṁ nēdaṁ kathayati tadavaśyaṁ kāraṇaṁ kimapi ॥ 138 ॥
ēvaṁ vicintayan kramēṇa prāptaḥ śubhākapuranagarē । yāvad ramaṇīyatayā paśyāmyahaṁ vipaṇimārgam ॥139॥
tāvajjarājarjarāṅgō nijasitājānumalinaśāṭakaḥ । pāṇḍuritarōmakūpaḥ prakaṭaśirāvamanīsaṁsthānaḥ ॥140॥
harinakhakaṭhinamahāpadainakharaparamparayā vikarālaḥ । ardharaṭṭitaghuṇṭaṁ pūgaṁ granthēnan ॥ 141 ॥
dūrapralambamānanā sākēśacayō mūlaghaṭṭakararuhakaḥ । bahusvēdaśīrṇamalama lina vastracikkaṇaśarīraḥ ॥142॥
gr̥hītakrayāṇakō rvaritalabhyadraviṇamapi prārthayadbhiḥ । saha grāhakairdurvacananirbharaṁ kalahayaṁśca ॥ 143 ॥
kathaṁkathamapi khalu sattvēna rēṇutuṣāpanayanārthamanilē । utpāṭya piṭakādi taṇḍulānutpaṇayaṁśca ॥ 144 ॥

1 ka. saṁtāṇō । 2 ga. °yaghaṁṭaṁ । 3 ga. uppaṇiṁ ।

12
supākhanāha-cariammi-
ēkamma mahāhaṭṭē diṭṭhō dhaṇasāranāmaō siṭṭhī । kiviṇapiyāmaha iya nagaravāsivihiyavarabhihāṇō || 145 ||
puṭṭhō yasō bhaē jaha thāvaranāmā ihatthi māyaṁgō। jiṇavayaṇabhāviyamaī cēḍayasiddhō ya ki kōvi 1 ॥ 146 ॥
ēyaṁ sammamasōūṇa tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kayāṇagaṁ kiṁpi । haṭṭāō āyaḍiya daṁsēmi taō maē puṭṭhē ॥ 147 ॥
mahayā saddēṇa puṇō taṁ ciya, tō tēṇa sāhiya, atthi । dāradviyacicaṇigāē tassa payaḍaṁ ciya gipi ॥ 148 ॥
iya sōūṇa gaō haṁ tassa gihē tattha sōvi saṁpattō । kahiō vāsiyabhattāivaiyarō tassa savvōvi ॥ 149॥
tā jāva sūriṇā haṁ tuha pāsē pēsiutti taṁ sōuṁ । tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kahissaṁ navaraṁ sāhammiō taṁ si || 150 ॥
tākāū pasāyaṁ pāhuṇagō hōsu ajja majjha tumaṁ । bhaṇiyaṁ maē kahaṁpiva jāiviruddhaṁ imaṁ jēṇa ॥ 151 ॥
aha mahaṇicchaṁtassavi sāhammiyavacchalacchapunnaṭṭhā | kiviṇapiyāmaha nirūviyaṁ bhōyaṇaṁ tēṇa ।। 152॥
bhaṇiyaṁ ca bhōyaṇāṇaṁtaraṁpi sigdhaṁ gihammi mahataṇaē । tumaē āgaṁtavvaṁ tuha puḍhaṁ jēṇa sāhēmi || 153॥
i bhaṇiūṇa gaō sō ēttō ya maēvi pabhaṇiō siddhī । jaha taṁdulē payāvasu katthavi bhuṁjāmi jēṇāhaṁ ॥ 154॥
tēṇa niyasiṭṭiṇicciya āhūyā raṁdhaṇatthalōbhēṇa । tīēvi aṇusārēṇa jiṇacaṁda utti vināō || 155।।
bhaṇiyaṁ bhō bhō taṁ maha piubhāyasuutti baṁdhavō hōsi । tā muṁca imaṁ māṁyaṁgadāviyaṁ taṁdulāīyaṁ ॥ 156 ॥
bhuṁjasu niyagēhicciya āgaṁtūṇaṁti tō maē bhaṇiyaṁ । ahamamugakāraṇēṇa samāgaō tassamavammi || 157 ||
tō tāaiyamēyaṁ bhuṁjissaṁ bhōaṇaṁ ahaṁ ajja । ēttō uḍhaṁ jai kiṁpi bhaṇasi tō tujjha maha savahō ॥ 158 ॥
ēkasmin mahāhaṭṭē dr̥ṣṭō dhanasāranāmakaḥ śrēṣṭhī । kr̥paṇapitāmaha iti nagaravāsivihitavarābhidhānaḥ ॥ 145॥
pr̥ṣṭaśca sa mayā yathā sthāvaranāmēhāsti mātaṅgaḥ । jinavacanabhāvitamatiścēṭakasiddhaśca kiṁ kō'pi 1 ॥ 146 ॥
ētat samyagaśrutvā tēna bhaṇitaṁ krayāṇakaṁ kimapi । haṭṭādākr̥ṣya darśayāmi tatō mayā pr̥ṣṭam ॥ 147 ॥
mahatā śabdēna punastadēva, tatastēna kathitaṁ, asti । dvārasthitaghara ṭṭikayā tasya prakaṭamēva gr̥hamapi ॥ 148 ॥
iti śrutvā gatō'haṁ tasya gr̥hē tatra sō'pi saṁprāptaḥ । kathitō vāsitabhaktādivyatikarastasya sarvō'pi ॥ 149 ॥
tāvad yāvatsūriṇā'haṁ tava pārśvē prēṣita iti śrutvā । tēna bhaṇitaṁ kathayiṣyāmi navaraṁ sādharmikastvamasi ॥ 150 ॥
tataḥ kr̥tvā prasādaṁ prāghuṇakō bhavādya mama tvam । bhaṇitaṁ mayā kathamiva jātiviruddhamidaṁ yēna ॥ 151 ॥
atha mamānicchatō'pi sādharmika vātsalyācchapuṇyārtham । kr̥paṇapitāmahahaṭṭē nirūpitaṁ bhōjanaṁ tēna ॥ 152॥
bhaṇitaṁ ca bhōjanānantaramapi śīghraṁ gr̥hē madīyē । tvayā āgantavyaṁ tava pr̥ṣṭaṁ yēna kathayāmi ॥ 153 ॥
-iti bhaṇitvā gataḥ sa itaśca mayāpi prabhaṇitaḥ śrēṣṭhī । yathā taṇḍulān pācaya kutrāpi mujhē yēnāham ॥ 154॥
tēna nijaśrēṣṭhinyēvāhūtā randhanārthalōbhēna । tayāpyanusārēṇa jinacandrasuta iti vijñātaḥ ॥ 155 ॥
bhaṇitaṁ ca bhō bhōstvaṁ mama pitr̥bhrātr̥suta iti bāndhavō bhavasi । tasmānmuñcēdaṁ mātaṅgadāpitaṁ taṇḍulādikam ॥ 156 ॥
bhuṅkṣva nijagēha ēvāgatyēti tatō mayā bhaṇitam । ahamamukakāraṇēna samāgatastatsamīpē ॥ 157 ॥
tatastaddāpitamētad bhōkṣyē bhōjanamahamadya । ita ūrdhvaṁ yadi kimapi bhaṇasi tatastava mama śapathaḥ ॥ 198 ॥
1 ka.
māiṁga । 2 kha. ga. bhōyaṇaṁ ।

puvyabhavapatthācī ।
13
iya gurunibbaṁdhaṇaṁ bhaṇiyā sā raṁdhiūṇa muhigāē । maha dēi bhōyaṇaṁ niyagihammi bhuttattarēya ahaṁ ॥ 159 ॥
jā māyaṁgassa gihaṁ vaccāmi suṇēmi tāva akkaṁdaṁ । tō tassannihiyajaṇā puṭṭhā takkāraṇaṁ tēhiṁ ॥ 160॥
kahiyaṁ, jaha māyaṁgō jassa samīvammi āgaō taṁ si । sō saṁpai mūḍhavisuiyāē paṁcattamaṇupattō ॥ 169 ॥
iya sōuṁ vimaṇamaṇō aṁhayaṁ taṁ siṭṭiṇī ē kahiūṇaṁ । jā niyanayarābhimuhaṁ caliō tō tīē iya bhaṇiō।। 162॥
jaha vīryādiṇaṁ ci iva kāūṇa baṁdhava ! pasāyaṁ । cēiharāī baṁdasu taha pāhuṇagō ya mē hōsu ॥ 163 ॥
iya ainibbaṁdhaparaṁ tīsē vayaṇaṁ nisāmiūṇa maē । paḍivajjiyaṁ tahacciya ēttō duiyammi divasammi॥ 164॥
kiviṇapiyāmaha siṭṭhī tīē gaṁtūṇa haṭṭavaviṭṭhō । bhaṇiō jaha maha baṁdhū bhuṁjihī ajja tuha gēhē ॥ 165 ॥
tā sālidālisasugaṁdhasappipabhīi samappahatti taō । siṭṭī tayabhibhuhaṁ bhaṇai bhuṁjihī kaha ṇu tuha baṁdhū ? ।। 166॥
dēsāgaōvi aidutthiōvi taiyā gihāu mē mukkō । nikālēḍaṁ baṁdhū sahōyarōvi huna kiṁ sarasi ? ॥ 167 ॥
annaṁ ca, kuṇasi vattaṁ sālīdālīṇa taṁ na kiṁ muṇasi ? । jaṁ dēvagihē jaṁtīē tujjha tusaṇī aṇuṇṇāyā ॥ 168 ॥
kiñca,
ja baṁdhusiṇēhaggahagahiyā ciṭṭhasi karhapi na tumaṁ tā । bhuṁjāiyāē maha sōvi jimmau tillēṇa saha vallē ।। 169 ॥
sā bhai niyāgavi hu ghayaghēurabhōyaṇaṁ samākuṇai । maha bhāyā, tā sāmiya ! lajjissamahaṁ imaṁ ditī ॥ 170 ॥
aha sō aṇakkhabhariō pabhaṇai puvvāgayā sirī jassa। vilasaṁtassa jahicchaṁ kā pīḍā tassa kā niṭṭhā ? ॥ 171 ॥
iti gurunirbandhēna bhaṇitā sā randhitvā sudhā । mama dadāti bhōjanaṁ nijagr̥hē, bhuktvā tvarēyāham ॥ 159 ॥
yāvad mātaṅgasya gr̥haṁ vrajāmi śr̥ṇōmi tāvadākrandam । tatastatsaṁnihitajanāḥ pr̥ṣṭāstatkāraṇaṁ taiḥ ॥ 160 ॥
kathitaṁ, yathā mātaṅgō yasya samīpa āgatastvamasi । sa saṁprati mūḍhāvisūcikayā pañcatvamanuprāptaḥ ॥ 161 ॥
iti śrutvā vimanōmanā ahakaṁ tat śrēṣṭhin kathayitvā । yāvannijanagarābhimukhaṁ calitastatastayēti bhaṇitaḥ ॥ 162 ॥
yathā dvitīyādinaṁ tiṣṭhēhaiva kr̥tvā bāndhava ! prasādam । caityagr̥hāṇi vandasva tathā prāghuṇakaśca mama bhava ॥ 163॥
ityatinirbandhaparaṁ tasyā vacanaṁ niśamya mayā । pratipannaṁ tathaivētō dvitīyasmin divasēṁ ॥ 164 ॥
kr̥paṇapitāmahaśrēṣṭhī tayā gayā haṭṭōpaviṣṭaḥ । bhaṇitō yathā mama bandhurbhōkṣyatē'dya tava gēhē ॥ 165 ॥
tasmācchālisūpasusugandhasarpiḥ prabhr̥ti samarpayēti tataḥ । śrēṣṭhī tadabhimukhaṁ bhaṇati bhōkṣyatē kathaṁ nu tava bandhuḥ 1 ॥ 166॥
dēśāgatō'pyatiduḥsthitō'pi tadā gr̥hānmayā muktaḥ । niṣkāśya bandhuḥ sahōdarō'pi khalu na kiṁ smarasi ? ॥167॥
anyacca, karōṣi vārtā śālisūpayōstanna kiṁ jānāsi ? | yad dēvagr̥hē yāntyāstava tūṣṇīmanujñātā ॥ 168 ॥
kiñca,
yadi bandhusnēhagrahagr̥hītā tiṣṭhasi kathamapi na tvaṁ tataḥ । bhōjikayā mama sō'pi bhājyatāṁ tailēna saha vallān ॥ 169 ॥
sā bhaṇati nijagr̥hē'pi khalu ghr̥taghr̥tapūra bhōjanaṁ sadā karōti । mama bhrātā, tasmāt svāmin! lajjiṣyāmyahamidaṁ dadatī ||
atha sa kōpabharitaḥ prabhaṇati pūrvāgatā śrīryasya । vilasatō yathēcchaṁ kā pīḍā tasya kā niṣṭhā ? || 171 ॥
1 ga. sōūṇa । 2 ga ṇammaṇō । 3 ga. ahaṁ si° । 4ka. tusalī ।

14
supāsanāha-cariammi-
kaṭṭhēṇa imēṇa maē lacchī samuvajjiyā na kiṁ muṇasi । jaṁ sisirē himapāēvi carimajāmammi rayaṇīē ॥ 172 ॥
uttari gurusariyaṁ paratīrē kaṭṭabhārayaṁ gahium̐ । jaha navi picchai kōvi hu taha tuha apitaō āsi ॥ 173 ॥
nīraṁpi hu rayaṇīē āṇitō, mā kahiṁpi maha atthō । pāṇañcaēva vacca khaṁḍaṇadalaṇāigihakammē ॥ 174॥
jō mē uvajjiō iha kararuhabasaṇēṇa caraṇaghāsēṇa । gimhumhata viyataṇuṇā tēllakaṇāīṇa vahaṇēṇa ॥ 175 ॥
dhammatthēvi hu jai kahavi kōvi maggai kavaḍḍiyaṁ kāṇaṁ । tō baddhadaṁtasagaḍō maucca ciṭṭhāmi nicciṭṭhō ॥ 176 ॥
tā taṁ kaha maṁ patthasi sālippabhiīṇi iya muṇaṁtīvi । ēvaṁ bālāluṁviṁ kāuṁ siṭṭhī ṭhiō mōṇī ॥ 177॥
parahaṭṭāō aha siṭṭiṇīvi āṇēvi sālimāīyaṁ । jā payai tāva siṭṭīvi bhōyaṇatthaṁ tarhi pattō ॥ 178 ॥
puṭṭhāya tēṇa gihiṇī kiṁ vallā paguṇiyā taē nō vā ? । sā bhaṇai tujjha niyaṁvaṁdhuṇō ya jōgaṁ maē ajja ।। 179॥
varasālidālimāī annaṁ paguṇīkayaṁti sōūṇa । daḍhakōvavasā tēṇaṁ payaṁpiyaṁ dēha maha taṁpi ॥ 180 ॥
tō bhai sāvi siddhiṁ khaṇamēgaṁ ēvamēva ciṭṭhēha । ghēuraghāṇadugaṁ jā paēmi iya nisuṇium̐ sahasā || 181 ॥
nīsahakara pahārēṇa pahaṇiūṇaṁ puṇō puṇō hiyayaṁ । duvvayaṇāī taha jaṁpiūṇa gihiṇīē samuhāī ॥। 182 ॥
citai haddhī atthō ēmēva muhāē galai maha gēhē । tō khēyamuvvahaṁtō suttō gaṁtūṇa gihamajjhē ॥ 183॥
aha davvavvayasaṁjaṇiyahiyayasaṁghaṭṭaghaṭṭiyavivēō । parimukō pāṇēhiṁ sō kiviṇapiyāmahō siṭṭī ||184 ॥
aha siṭṭiṇīvi niṣpāiūṇa vararasavaī samaggapi । bhairiūṇa caukkadugaṁ dāūṇaṁ āsaṇāī ca ॥ 185 ॥
kaṣṭēnānēna mayā lakṣmīḥ samupārjitā na kiṁ jānāsi । yacchiśirē himaprāyēspi caramayāmē rajanyāḥ ॥ 172॥
uttīrya gurusaritaṁ paratīrē kāṣṭhabhārakaṁ gr̥hītvā । yathā nāpi paśyati kōpi khalu tathā tubhyamarpayannāsam ॥173॥
nīramapi khalu rajanyāmānayan, mā kutrāpi mamārthaḥ । prāṇatyāgē'pi vrajatu khaṇḍanadalanādigr̥hakarmaṇi ॥174॥
yō mayōpārjita iha kararuhagharṣaṇēna caraṇagharṣēṇa । grīṣmōṣmataptatanunā tailakṇādīnāṁ vahanēna ॥175॥
dharmārthē'pi khalu yadi kathamapi kōpi mārgayati kapardikāṁ kāṇām । tatō baddhadantaśakaṭō mr̥ta iva tiṣṭhāmi niścēṣṭaḥ ॥
tasmāt tvaṁ kathaṁ māṁ prārthayasi śāliprabhr̥tīnīti jānatyapi । ēvaṁ bālālumbī (?) kr̥tvā śrēṣṭhī sthitō maunī ॥ 177॥
parahaṭṭādatha śrēṣṭhinyapyānīya śālyādikam । yāvat pacati tāvat śrēṣṭhyapi bhōjanārthaṁ tatra prāptaḥ ॥ 178॥
pr̥ṣṭā ca tēna gr̥hiṇī kiṁ vallāḥ praguṇitāstvayā nō vā ? | sā bhaṇati tava nijabandhōśca yōgyaṁ mayādya ॥ 179 ॥
varaśā lisūpādyannaṁ praguṇīkr̥tamiti śrutvā । dr̥ḍhakōpavaśāt tēna prajalpitaṁ datta mahyaṁ tadapi ॥ 180 ॥
tatō bhaṇati sāpi śrēṣṭhinaṁ kṣaṇamēkamēvamēva tiṣṭhata । ghr̥tapūrasaṁghātadvikaṁ pacāmīti śrutvā sahasā ॥ 189 ॥
niḥsahkaraprahārēṇa prahatya punaḥ punarhr̥dayam । durvacanāni tathā jalpitvā gr̥hiṇyāḥ saṁmukhāni ॥182॥ -
cintayati hā dhigartha ēvamēva mudhā galati mama gēhē । tataḥ khēdamudvahan suptō gatvā gr̥hamadhyē ||183 ॥
atha dravyavyayasaṁjanitahr̥dayasaṁghaṭṭaghaṭṭitavivēpaḥ । parimuktaḥ prāṇaiḥ sa kr̥paṇapitāmahaḥ śrēṣṭhī ॥ 184 ॥
atha śrēṣṭhinyapi niṣpādya vararasavatīṁ samagrāmapi । bhr̥tvā catuṣkadvikaṁ dattvā''sanē ca ॥ 185 ॥
1 ka. silla । 2 ga. hāi । 3 ka. bhaṇiū ।

puvvabhavapatthāvāṁ ।
15
bhōyaṇahēḍaṁ kōmalaġirāhiṁ siddhiṁ pabōhiuṁ laggā । jāva na tīsē paccuttaraṁpi sō dēi sāvi taō || 186॥
ruti manamāṇī siṇēhasāraṁ paryapiḍaṁ jāva । saccavai saṁmuhaṁ tāva bhaggaṁ tārāyaṇaṁ niyai || 187॥
•
tō ēsa mautti viṇicchiūṇa pihiūṇa taha gharaduvārē । maha bhōyaṇaṁ viinnaṁ sayuṁca bhuttaṁ taō tīē ॥ 188 ॥
kahiyaṁ mahajaha bhattā ēsō tilatusatibhāgamēttaṁpi । kahavi na kassavi dinōṁ ataṁ paṁtaṁ ca bhuṁjaṁtō ।। 189 ॥
ēttiyakālā iṇhi ukkhuḍiyaṁ sālimāiyaṁ nāuṁ । tuha jōggaṁ tō sahasā puṇō puṇō kuṭṭiyaṁ hiyayaṁ ॥ 190 ॥
suttōcciya sijjāē maō aputtō imō ya iha āsi । caukōḍisāmiō bhāya ! tā jahā jāi nō davvaṁ ॥ 191 ॥
rāyaulē, tamuvāyaṁ ciṁtēmō kiṁpi sō imō cēva । gharamajjhicciya siṭṭhī khippara uṁḍāē khaḍḍāē || 192॥
kāūṇa kiṁpi kavarḍa na muṇijjai jahavahiṁ imō atthō । iya nicchiūṇa tīē maē ya jahaciṁtiyaṁ vihiyaṁ ॥ 193॥
aha tīē mahabhimuhaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ jaha ajja nisi pasuttāē । jaṁ dinaṁ sumiṇaṁ tayaṇusāraō haṁ muṇēmi imaṁ ॥ 194 ॥
jēha hōhī maha puttō tā bhāya ! tumaṁ ihēva haṭṭammi । vavaharamāṇō ciṭṭhasu jāhaṁ pasavāmi, iya sōuṁ ॥ 195॥
tīsē uvarōhēṇaṁ tahatti paḍivajjiyaṁ maē savvaṁ । sāvi hu kayasiṁgārā sahīṇa puraō imaṁ kahai || 196॥
vaddhāvijjaha tubhē siṁghaladīvammi jāī vahāṇāī । tumhāṇa bhaiṇivaiṇō avatitthagayāī nisuyāī ॥ 197॥
mahapaipunnavasēṇaṁ vēlākūlammi tāī pattāī । tō tayabhimuō siṭṭī harisēṇa sa gaō ihi || 198 ॥
iya paḍatī savvaṁ gamēi diyahāī siṭṭiṇī hiṭṭhā | ahamavi gharavāvāraṁ savvaṁ ciṁtēmi ēttau ya ॥ 199॥
bhōjanahētōḥ kōmalagīrbhiḥ śrēṣṭhinaṁ prabōdhayituṁ lagnā । yāvanna tasyai pratyuttaramapi sa dadāti sāpi tataḥ ॥ 186॥
ruṣṭa iti manyamānā snēhasāraṁ prajalpya yāvat । paśyati saṁmukhaṁ tāvad bhagnaṁ tārākaṇaṁ paśyati ॥ 187॥
tata ēṣa mr̥ta iti viniścitya pidhāya tathā gr̥hadvāram । mahyaṁ bhōjanaṁ vitīrṇa svayaṁ ca bhuktaṁ tatastayā ॥ 188॥
kathitaṁ mama yathā bhartaiṣa tilatuṣatribhāgamātramapi । kathamapi na kasyāpi dadadantaṁ prāntaṁ ca bhuñjānaḥ ॥ 189 ॥
ētāvatkālādidānī randhitaṁ śālyādikaṁ jñātvā । tava yōgyaṁ tataḥ sahasā punaḥ punaḥ kuṭṭitaṁ hr̥dayam ॥ 190 ॥
supta ēva śayyāyāṁ mr̥tō'putrō'yaṁ cēhāsīt । catuṣkōṭisvāmī bhrātaḥ ! tasmādyathā yāti nō dravyam ॥191॥
rājakulē, tamupāyaṁ cintayāmaḥ kamapi sō'yamēva । gr̥hamadhya ēva śrēṣṭhī kṣipyatāṁ gabhīrē gartē ॥ 192॥
kr̥tvā kimapikapaṭaṁ na jñāyatē yathāvadhyayamarthaḥ । iti niścitya tayā mayā ca yathācintitaṁ vihitam ॥193॥
atha tayā madabhimukhaṁ bhaṇitaṁ yathā''yai ! niśi prasuptayā । yō dr̥ṣṭaḥ svapnastadanusāratō'haṁ jānāmīdam ॥ 194॥
'yathā bhaviṣyati mama putrastasmād bhrātastvamihaiva haṭṭē । vyavaharaṁstiṣṭha yāvadahaṁ prasūyē iti śrutvā ॥ 195 ॥
tasyā uparōdhēna tathēti pratipannaṁ mayā sarvam । sāpi khalu kr̥taśr̥ṅgārā sakhīnāṁ purata idaṁ kathayati ॥ 196 ॥
vardhāpyadhvē yūyaṁ siṁhaladvīpē yāni yānāni । yuṣmākaṁ bhaginīpatērapatīrthagatāni śrutāni ॥ 197॥
matpatipuṇyavaśēna vēlākulē tāni prāptāni । tatastadabhimukhaḥ śrēṣṭhī harṣēṇa svayaṁ gata idānīm ॥ 198॥
iti prakaṭayantī sarvaṁ gamayati divasāni śrēṣṭhinī hr̥ṣṭā । ahamapi gr̥havyāpāraṁ sarvaṁ cintayāmi itaśca ॥ 199 ॥
་
1 ka. jai ।

16
supāsanāha-caritryammi-
I
I
sā samayammi pasūyā paramamuhuttammi dārayaṁ pavaraṁ । bhō sāma māma lahu ēhi ēhi punaruttamiya bhaṇiraṁ ॥ 200 ॥
tō tīē sahijhīē vihiyahiyayāē lahu samāgaṁtuṁ । āhūō haṁ gēhē gaṁō ya jā tassa diṭṭhipahaṁ ॥ 201 ||
tō bhaṇiō tēṇāhaṁ bhō māmagu ! ajja dāhiṇa disāē । ciṁcaṇīgāē samīvē māyaṁgī pasaviyā asthi || 202 ||
jāō ya tīē taṇaō ahuṇā sā ṭhivviūṇa tassa muṁhaṁ | paṁcataṁ pāvēhī bahuḍiṁbhaduhēhiṁ saṁtattā ॥ 203 ॥
tā tī dammapaṁcagamappasu taṁ jhatti tattha gaṁtūṇa । bhaṇiyavvā ya taē sā ghayataṁdulamāiyaṁ kuṇasu ॥ 204॥
pālasu ḍiṁbhaṁ mā mārasutti ēvaṁ tahatti kāūṇa । puṇaravi gihāgaō haṁ sappaṇayaṁ tēṇēmaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 205 ॥
paccabhijāṇasi nō vā māmaga ! maṁsō ahaṁ khu māyaṁgō । vāsiyabhattāīvaiyarassa saṁpucchaṇa nimittaṁ ॥ 206॥
samayāmaya nihiguruṇā jassa samīvammi pēsiō si tumaṁ । sāhammiutti kāuṁ tuha bhōyaṇadāṇaō taiyā || 207
cirapunnaprabhāvēṇa yaṁ ummūḍhavisūiyāē mariūṇa । ahamihamupapannō baddhapuvvamaṇuyāuyattēṇa ॥ 208 ॥
jō puṇa mārijjatō davvapayāṇēṇa rakkhiō tumaē । sō dhaṇasārō siṭṭhī mariuṁ mēiṇisuō jāō ॥ 209 ॥
navapunnaṇajjaṇaṁ vāsiyapunnakkhaēṇa tā māma ! | dhammammi pamāyaṁtō diṭṭhō tuha aṁbayā tumaṁ ॥210 ॥
iya kāraṇēṇa tajhyā bhaṇiō taṁ tīē paidiṇaṁpi imaṁ । 'vaccha ! duhāī pāvihisi bhuṁjirō vāsiṁyaṁ bhattaṁ' ॥211।
taha sūriṇāvi dhaṇasārapaccaēṇa tujjha muṇivi paḍivōhaṁ । taṁ iha pahiō māmaga! tādhaṇasārō duhaṁ pattō || 212 ।
jaha vāsiya pugnuvabhuṁjaṇēṇa taha māma ! taṁpi pāvihisi । jai dhammapamāyaparō uvarbhujasi vāsiyaṁ punnaṁ ॥ 213 ।
sā samayē prasūtā paramamuhūrtē dārakaṁ pravaram । bhō mātula mātula laghvēhi ēhi bhr̥śamiti bhaṇitāram ||200॥
tatastayā prātivēśmikyā bismitahr̥dayayā laghu samāgatya । āhūtō'haṁ gēhē gataśca jātasya dr̥ṣṭipatham ॥ 201 ॥
tatō bhaṇitastēnāhaṁ bhō mātula ! adya dakṣiṇadiśi । gharaṭṭikāyāḥ samīpē mātaṅgī prasūtāsti ॥ 202॥
jātaśca tasyāstanayō'dhunā sā vighaṭya tasya mukham । pañcatvaṁ prāpayiṣyati bahuḍimbhaduḥkhaiḥ saṁtaptā ॥203॥
tasmāttasyai drammapañcakamarpaya tvaṁ jhaṭiti tatra galā । bhaṇitavyā ca tvayā sā ghr̥tataṇḍulādikaṁ kuruṣva ॥ 204 |
pālaya ḍimbhaṁ mā mārayētyētat tathāta kr̥tvā । punarapi gr̥hāgatō'haṁ sapraṇayaṁ tēnēdaṁ bhaṇitam ॥ 205 ॥
pratyabhijānāṁsi nō vā mātula ! māṁ sō'haṁ khalu mātaṅgaḥ । vāsitabhaktādivyatikarasya saṁpraśnanimittam ॥ 206।
samayāmr̥tanidhiguruṇā yasya samīpē prēṣitō'si tvam | sādharmika iti kr̥tvā tubhyaṁ bhōjanadānatastadā ॥207॥
cirapuṇyaprabhāvēṇa cōnmūḍhavisūcikayā mr̥tvā । ahamihōtpannō baddhapūrvamanujāyuṣkatvēna ॥ 208 ॥
yaḥ punarmāryamāṇō dravyapradānēna rakṣitastvayā । sa dhanasāraḥ śrēṣṭhī mr̥tvā mēdinīsutō jātaḥ ॥ 209 ॥
navapuṇyānarjanēna vāsitapuṇyakṣayēṇa tasmānmātula ! । dharmē pramādyaṁn dr̥ṣṭastavāmbayā tvam || 210 ॥
iti kāraṇēna tadā bhaṇitastvaṁ tayā pratidinamapīdam । 'vatsa ! duḥkhāni prāpsyasi bhuñjānō vāsitaṁ bhaktam ॥211
tathā sūriṇāpi dhanasārapratyayēna tava jñātvā pratibōdham । tvamiha prahitō mātula! tasmād dhanasārō duḥkhaṁ prāptaḥ ॥ 212
yathā vāsitapuṇyōpabhōgēna tathā mātula ! tvamapi prāpsyasi । yadi dharmapramādapara upabhuṅgē vāsitaṁ puṇyam ॥ 213 ।
1 kha dijjīē । 2 ka, tēṇa bhaṇiō haṁ ।

punvabhavatthāvō ।
17
iya suṇivi vimhiyamaṇō ciṁtēmi ahō imaṁ mahacchariyaṁ । jaṁ tadahajāyassavi imassa iya vayaṇavinnāsō ॥ 214॥
tā kiṁ saccamasaccaṁ iti pr̥cchāmi kiṁpi aisaiṇaṁ । iya saṁkaṣpaparō haṁ jā saṁciṭṭhāmi tā tattha ॥ 215 ॥
samayāmayanihisūrī sō caitra samāgautti lōāō । nisuyaṁ tassa samīvē gaō ō tē imaṁ puṭṭhā ॥ 296॥
puvvuttavaiyaraṁ, tēhiṁ jaṁpiyaṁ bhadda savvamavi saccaṁ । jaṁ tuha bhaiṇisuēṇaṁ payaṁpiyaṁ, tō maē bhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 217॥
kiṁ pahu māyaṁgēṇaṁ punaṁ samuvajjiyaṁ jaō jāō । caukōḍīṇaṁ sāmī ēsō, tō tēṇa iya kahiyē || 218 ||
caurūvagē vaūṇa tēṇa kēṇāvi suddhabhāvēṇa | sāhammiutti kāuṁ dinaṁ tuha bhōyaṇaṁ taiyā || 219॥
tē jēṇa tassa caukōḍidaviṇabhāvēṇa pariṇayā, ēttō। bhaṇiyaṁ maē kaham̐ pahu tassiṇhiṁ vayaṇasattīvi ? ।। 220 ।
tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ imapi hu nisuṇasu, taiyā ġayassa gēhampi । divasassa paḍhamajāmē sē mūḍhavisūiyā jāyā || 221॥
saṁyuddhamāṇasēṇaṁ sariō tō siddhacēḍaō tēṇa । tatthāgaō ya puṭṭhō ki maha saṁpai carimasamaō ? || 222॥
jō ēvaṁ saṁjāyā vimūiyā majjha, sō bhaṇai ēvaṁ । tō puḍhaṁ mariūṇaṁ uppajjissaṁ ahaṁ kattha ? || 223 ||
tēṇavi sammaṁ avahiṁ pauṁjiuṁ sāhiyaṁ imaṁ tassa । jaha dhaṇasārasuō taṁ hōhisi tō tēṇimaṁ puḍhaṁ ||224॥
jaha kaha jāṇatēviṁ nāṇēṇaṁ sūriṇā maha samīvē । vāsiya bhattāīvaiyarassa saṁpucchaṇanimittaṁ ॥ 225॥
ēsō saḍḍhō iha pēsiutti sōūṇa jaṁpiyaṁ tēṇa । jaha ēyassavabōhō sūrīhiṁ ihēva vinnāō || 226 ॥
sō uṇa dhaṇasāragihammi jāyamittassa tuha muhē hōuṁ । jaṁpissāmi jayā haṁ tajhyā hōhitti jaṁpēuṁ ॥ 227॥
iti śrutvā vismitamanāścintayāmyahō idaṁ mahāścaryam । yat tadaharjātasyāpyasyēti vacanavinyāsaḥ || 214 ||
tasmāt kiṁ satyamasatyamidamiti pr̥cchāmi kamapyatiśayinam । iti saṁkalpaparō'haṁ yāvatsaṁtiṣṭhē tāvattatra ॥215॥
samayāmr̥tanidhisūriḥ sa ēva samāgata iti lōkāt । śrutaṁ tasya samīpē gatastatastē imaṁ pr̥ṣṭāḥ ॥ 216॥
pūrvōktavyatikaraṁ, tairjalpitaṁ bhadra sarvamapi satyam । yattava bhaginīsutēna prajalpitaṁ, tatō mayā bhaṇitam ॥217॥
kiṁ prabhō mātaṅgēna puṇyaṁ samupārjitaṁ yatō jātaḥ । catuṣkōṭīnāṁ svāmyēṣaḥ, tatastēnēti kathitam ॥218॥
catūrūpakān vīt tēna kēnāpi śuddhabhāvēna । sādharmika iti kr̥tvā dattaṁ tubhyaṁ bhōjanaṁ tadā ॥ 219॥
tē yēna tasya catuṣkōṭidraviṇabhāvēna pariṇatāḥ, itaḥ । bhaṇitaṁ mayā kathaṁ prabhō tasyēdānīṁ vacanaśaktirapi ? ॥220॥
tēna bhaṇitamidamapi khalu śr̥ṇu, tadā gatasya gr̥hē । divasasya prathamayāmē tasya mūḍhavisūcikā jātā ||221॥
saṁkṣubdhamānasēna smr̥tastataḥ siddhacēṭakastēna । tatrāgataśca pr̥ṣṭaḥ kiṁ mama saṁprati caramasamayaḥ ? || 222॥
yata ēvaṁ saṁjātā visūcikā mama, sa bhaṇatyēvam । tataḥ pr̥ṣṭaṁ mr̥tvōtpatsyē'haṁ kutra ? ॥223 ॥
tēnāpi samyagavadhiṁ prayujya kathitamidaṁ tasmai । yathā dhanasārasutastvaṁ bhaviṣyasi tatastēnēdaṁ pr̥ṣṭam ॥ 224॥
yathā kathaṁ jānatāpi jñānēna sūriṇā mama samīpē । vāsitabhaktādivyatikarasya saṁpraśnanimittam ॥229॥
ēṣa śrāddha iha prēṣita iti śrutvā jalpitaṁ tēna । yathaitasyāvabōdhaḥ sūribhirihaiva vijñātaḥ ॥ 226 ॥
saṁ punardhanasāragr̥hē jātamātrasya tava mukhē bhūtvā । jalpiṣyāmi yadā'haṁ tadā bhaviṣyatīti jalpitvā ॥ 227॥
1 vyayaṁ kr̥tvā । 2 avabōdhaḥ ।

।

18
supāsanāha- cariammi-
niyaṭhāṇammi gaō sō taiyā iṇhi tu avasaraṁ nāuṁ । avainnō tassa muhē sōcciya tō jaṁpai imōti ॥ 228 ॥
iya sōuṁ bhavavāsuvviggēṇaṁ tassa caiva pāsammi । navapunnajjaṇahēḍaṁ paḍivannā savvaō viraī || 229||
ēkkārasa aṁgāī ahijjiūṇa kamēṇa saṁpattō । gīyatthō viharatō bahuvarisēhi suhāgapurē ॥ 230 ॥
tō sō maha bhaiṇisuō samāgaō majjha vaṁdaṇanimittaṁ । tappuraō āraddhā maēvi sadēsaṇā ēvaṁ ||231 |
bhō savvā asārē saṁsārē sayaladukkhanilayammi । taṁ kīsa vasasi ujjamaparammuhō dhammavisayammi ? ।। 232 ॥
kiṁ ēttha caugaī suvisutthaṁ dinaṁ taē kahi, ahavā । maraṇammi abhayavattaṁ pattaṁ tumaē kayaṁtāō ? ।। 233 |
kiṁvājarāmara dēvēṇaṁ dāṇavēṇava vinnō । tujjha varō, iha ahavā maṇimaṁtōsahibalaṁ kiṁpi ? || 234 ||
kiṁ nō picchasi sayalaṁ jiyalōyaṁ visarisaṁ pakuvvatī । jararakkhasī hadvēṇaṁ sujhīriyapamuhaharaṇēṇa ? || 235 |
tā cayasu pamāyaṁ savvahāvi aṁgīkarēsu jaidhammaṁ । jai siddhivahūpariraṁbhavinbhamaṁ mahasi bhō bhadda || 236 ॥
iya sōuṁ paḍivō paḍhamavaē caiva tēṇa jaidhammō । paripāliō ya suciraṁ pajjaṁtē aṇasaṇaṁ kāuṁ ||237 ॥
saṁpattō sōhammē tatthāhaṁ paḍhamaō samuppannō । iya jaha jiṇadhammāō pattō saggō tahā kahiyaṁ ॥ 238 ॥
iya sōuṁ viṇayapurassarēṇa saṁgāmasūrarāēṇa । dēvīē caṁdalēhāē saṁjuraṇaṁ surasamīvē ॥ 239॥
sammattēṇaṁ juttō gahiō bārasavihōvi giridhammō । surajayalapi hu ēttō vaccai sōhammakappammi || 240 ॥
kālakamēṇa tattō caviṁḍaṁ dēvīē caṁdalēhāē । samagaṁ ganbhattāē utpannaṁ punnasamayammi || 241 ||
sāvi pasūyā puttaṁ kannaṁ ca taō ya naravaridēṇa । bārasa diṇāī vihiaṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ pamōēṇa ॥242॥
nijasthānē gataḥ sa tadēdānīṁ tvavasaraṁ jñātvā | avatīrṇastasya mukhē sa ēva tatō jalpatyayamiti ॥228॥
iti śrutvā bhavavāsōdvignēna tasyaiva pārśvē । navapuṇyārjana hētōḥ pratipannā sarvatō viratiḥ ॥229॥
ēkādaśāṅgānyadhītya kramēṇa saṁprāptaḥ । gītārthō viharan bahuvarṣēḥ śubhākapurē ॥ 230॥
tataḥ sa mama bhaginīsutaḥ samāgatō mama vandananimittam । tatpurata ārabdhā mayāpi sadēśanaivam || 231॥
bhōḥ sarvathā'sārē saṁsārē sakaladuḥkhanilayē | tvaṁ kasmād vasasyudyamaparāṅmukhō dharmaviṣayē ? ॥ 232 ॥
kimatra caturgatiṣvapi sausthyaṁ dr̥ṣṭaṁ tvayā kvāthavā । maraṇē'bhayavattvaṁ prāptaṁ tvayā kr̥tāntāt ? || 233 ||
kiṁvā'jarāmaratvē dēvēna dānavēna vā vitīrṇaḥ । tubhyaṁ varaḥ, ihāthavā maṇimantrauṣadhivalaṁ kimapi ? ॥ 234 ॥
kiṁ nō paśyasi sakalaṁ jīvalōkaṁ visadr̥śaṁ prakurvatī । jarārākṣasī haṭhēna smr̥tivīryapramukhaharaṇēna ॥ 235 ॥
tasmāttyaja pramādaṁ sarvathāpyaṅgīkuru yatidharmam । yadi siddhivadhū parirambhavibhramaṁ kāṅkṣasi bhō bhadra ||236 ॥
iti
śrutvā pratipannaḥ prathamavayasyēva tēna yatidharmaḥ । paripālitaśca suciraṁ paryantē'naśanaṁ kr̥tvā ॥ 237॥
saṁprāptaḥ saudharmē tatrāhaṁ prathamataḥ samutpannaḥ । iti yathā jinadharmāt prāptaḥ svargastathā kathitam ||238 ॥
iti śrutvā vinayapurassaraṁ saṁgrāmaśūrarājēna | dēvyā candralēkhayā saṁyutēna surasamīpē ॥239॥
samyaktvēna yuktō gr̥hītō dvādaśavidhō'pi gr̥hidharmaḥ । surayugalamapi khalvitō vrajati saudharmakalpa || 240॥
kālakramēṇa tataścyutvā dēvyāṁ candralēkhāyām । samakaṁ garbhatayōtpanna pūrṇasamayē ॥ 249 ॥

uciyasamayammi nāma vihiyaṁ jayasuṁdarōtti puttassa । duhiyāē puṇō jayasuṁdaritti aitō ya tāīpi ॥ 243 ॥
bahuvija hicchakīlāvilāsa suhagahiyaviggahabalāī । jāyāī aṭuvacchara pariyāyāī kamēṇa taō || 244 ||
sayalakalākalaṇakara lēhāyariyassa tāī vihipuvvaṁ । uvaṇīyāī rannā gahiyāu kalāvi kamēṇa ॥ 245 ॥
aha annayā ya jayasuṁdarīvi samavayasahīhiṁ pariyariyā । ujjāṇavaṇē sirivīyarāyabhavaṇammi gaṁtūṇa ॥ 246 ॥
namiūṇa jiṇaṁ puraō uvavisiya bhattinibbharā tayaṇu । kahavi hu laggā vīṇāvāyaṇavāvāra māyariṁjaṁ ॥247॥
ētyaṁtarē jahicchāvihāravāvāraparavasaṁ kiṁpi । kinnara mihuṇaṁ gayaṇē vaccataṁ taṁ nisāmē ॥ 248 ॥
Mahuratṇusārēṇa jaṇiyagayaṇayalatara lagaibhaṁgaṁ । jayasuṁdarīsamīvē pattaṁ kōūhalāuliyē || 249||
tīsē sāgayavayaṇamukkhapaḍivattipayaḍaṇapaṭṭhiṁ । uciyāsaṇammirammē tō taṁ mihuṇaṁ samāsīṇaṁ || 250 ॥
sāhiyaāgamaṇapaōyaṇassa puraō ya tassa kumarīē । vihiyaṁ vīṇāvāyaṇakalāē kōsallasavvassaṁ || 251 ॥
tattō kī kalā tumhēṁ kōsallasaṁpayā phurai ? | iya sabahumāṇavayaṇāē pasiṇiyaṁ tīē taṁ mihuṇaṁ ॥ 252 ॥
tēvi gīyakalākō sallē sāhiyammi tayabhimuhaṁ । jayasuṁdarīē bhaṇiyaṁ taṁ daṁsaha majjha, tō tēhiṁ ॥ 253 ॥
kalakaṁṭhakaṁdalīghōlamāṇamimahuramuṁddiyasarēṇaṁ । jayasuṁdarisavaṇāmayavāṇasamō dhīhiō vihiō || 254 ॥
tālāṇukūlasulaliyapayapēsalamullasaṁtasuṁharāyaṁ । sapiyāē samaṁ ciya kinnarēṇa tō gāiyaṁ gīyaṁ ॥ 255 ॥
।
sāpi prasūtā putraṁ kanyāṁ ca tataśca naravarēndrēṇa । dvādaśa dināni vihitaṁ vardhāpanakaṁ pramōdēna ॥ 242 ॥
ucitasamayē nāma vihitaṁ jayasundara iti putrasya । duhituḥ punarjayasundarītītaśca tāvapi ॥243॥
bahuvidhayathēcchakrīḍāvilāsasukhagr̥hītavigrahabalau । jātāvaṣṭavatsaraparyāyau kramēṇa tataḥ ॥ 244॥
sakalakalākalanakr̥tē lēkhācāryasya tau vidhipūrvam । upanītau rājñā, gr̥hītāḥ kalā api kramēṇa || 245 ॥
athānyadā ca jayasundaryapi samavayaḥ sakhībhiḥ parikaritā | udyānavanē śrīvītarāgabhavanē gatvā ॥ 246॥
natvā jinaṁ purata upaviśya bhaktinirbharā tadanu । kathamapi khalu lagnā vīṇāvādanavyāpāramācaritum ॥247॥
annāntarē yadr̥cchāvihāravyāpāraparavaśaṁ kimapi । kinnara mithunaṁ gaganē vrajat taṁ niśamya ॥ 248 ॥
vīṇāravānusārēṇa janitagaganatalataralagatibhaṅgam । jayasundarīsamīpē prāptaṁ kautūhalākulitam ॥249॥
tasyāḥ svāgatavacanapramukhyapratipattiprakaṭanaprahr̥ṣṭam । ucitāsanē ramyē tatastanmithunaṁ samāsīnam ॥250॥
kathitāgamanaprayōjanasya purataśca tasya kumāryā । vihitaṁ vīṇāvādana kalāyāḥ kauśalasarvasvam ॥ 299 ॥
tataḥ kasyāṁ kalāyāṁ yuṣmākaṁ kauśalasaṁpat sphurati ? । iti sabahumānavacanayā praśnitaṁ (pr̥ṣṭaṁ ) tayā tanmithunam॥ 252 ॥
tēnāpi gītakalākauśalē kathitē tadabhimukham । jayasundaryā bhaṇitaṁ tad darśaya mama tatastābhyām ॥ 253॥
kalakaṇṭhakandalī ghūrṇamānamr̥dumadhuramudritasvarēṇa । jayasundarīśravaṇāmr̥tapānasama ālāpō ( ? ) vihitaḥ ॥ 254 ॥
tālānukūla sulalitapadapēśala mullasacchubharāgam । svapriyayā samamēva kinnarēṇa tatō gīta gītam ॥259॥
tatra ca vismayavaśavikasannayanēna tēna saṁgītaḥ । tavaiva guṇagrāmastathā kathamapi khalu yēna tadbalam || 256॥

supāsanāha-cariasmi
tattha ya vimyavasaviyaṁsamāṇanayaṇēṇa tēṇa saṁgīō। tuha caiva guṇaragāmō taha kahavi hu jēṇa tavvēlaṁ || 256 |
rairamaṇasarā saṇavāṇavarisaṇajjhāsaṭhāṇamaṇupattā । jayasuṁdarī suṇaṁtī tamasarisaṁ tuha guṇaggāmaṁ || 257 |
tō takkhaṇēṇa mucchā nimīliyacchimahīyalucchaṁgē । acchukkutthariyamahallavāha bharanīsahā paḍiyā || 258 ॥
tō sē sahīō kāōvihiyaṁ maddati kāōvi kuṇaṁti । sirikhaṁḍara sanisēyaṁ kā ōvi vīyaṁti viyaṇēhiṁ ।। 259 ।
pariyaṇakaruṇāiva tō kapi vivihōvayāravihavēṇa । paccāgayacēyannā saṁjāyā sā sasaṁkamuhī ॥ 260 ॥
ētthaṁtarammi bahanē samāgayā vēyarā tahiṁ bhavaṇē । jiṇapaḍimaṁ paṇamēuṁ ēyāvatthā ya sā tattha ।। 261 ||
diṭṭhā uttara sēḍhīvaiṇō taṇaēṇa kaṇayacūḍēṇa । tō sō tavvēlaṁ ciya gahiō mayaṇaggaṇa darda || 262 ||
ki bahuṇā,
phuṭṭaṁti hāramuttāmaṇīu lāyavva jammi sayakhaṁḍaṁ । sō dāhajarō sahasā viyaṁbhiō tassa dēhammi || 263 ॥
jayasuṁdarīvi pattō kahavi hu saṁvāhium̐ sahiyaṇēṇa । niyapiugihammi nīyā tatthavi tumamēva citaṁtī || 264|
na rasaṁ rasēi na ravaṁ suṇēi na hu gaṁdhayaṁ ca gēṇhēi । naya rūvaṁpi nirūvai na kiṁpiphāsaṁpi sā muṇai || 266 ॥
ētthaṁtarammi saṁgāmasūra rāyassa pāsamallīṇō । sirikaṇayacūḍapiyarēṇa pēsiō mahuyarō dūō || 266 ||
abbhāgayajaṇapaḍivattiniuṇarannāvi dāviyaṁ viulaṁ । kaṇayamayamāsaṇaṁ tassa sōvi namiūṇa uvaviṭṭō || 267/
tō dūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ jaha ēvaṁ bhaṇai kaṇayacūḍapiyā | viyarijjau jayasuṁdarikannā sirikaṇayacūḍassa ॥ 268 ॥
ratiramaṇaśarāsanabāṇavarṣaṇādhyāsasthānamanuprāptā । jayasundarī śr̥ṇvatī tamasadr̥śaṁ tava guṇagrāmam ॥257॥
tatastatkṣaṇēna mūrcchānimīlitākṣimahītalōtsaṅgē । akṣikūpa tulōtsr̥tamahābāṣpabharaniḥ sahā patitā ||258 ||
tatastasyāḥ sakhyaḥ kā api hr̥dayaṁ mardayanti kā api kurvanti । śrīkhaṇḍarasaniṣēkaṁ kā api vījanti vyajanaiḥ । 259 |
parijanakaruṇayēva tataḥ kathamapi vividhōpacāravibhavēna । pratyāgatacaitanyā saṁjātā sā śaśāṅkamukhī ॥ 260॥
atrāntarē bahavaḥ samāgatāḥ khēcarāstasmim bhuvanē । jinapratimāṁ praṇantumētadavasthā ca sā tatra ॥261॥
dr̥ṣṭōttaraśrēṇīpatēstanayēna kanakacūḍēna । tataḥ sa tadvēlamēva gr̥hītō madanagrahēṇa dr̥ḍham ॥262॥
kiṁ bahunā,
sphuṭanti hāramuktāmaṇayō lātā iva yasmiṁśatakhaṇḍam । sa dāhajvaraḥ sahasā vijr̥mbhitastasya dēhē ॥ 263 ॥
jayasundaryaipītaḥ kathamapi kila saṁvāhya sakhījanēna । nijapitr̥gr̥hē nītā tatrāpi tvāmēva cintayantī ॥ 264॥
na rasaṁ rasati na ravaṁ śr̥ṇōti na khalu gandhaṁ ca gr̥hṇāti । naca rūpamapi nirūpayati na kamapi sparśa ca sā jānāti ॥ 265॥
atrāntarē saṁgrāmaśūrarājasya pārśvamālīnaḥ । śrīkanakacūḍapitrā prēṣitō madhukarō dūtaḥ || 266 ॥
abhyāgatajanapratipattinipuṇarājēnāpi dāpitaṁ vipulam । kanakamayamāsanaṁ tasmai sō'pi natvōpaviṣṭaḥ ॥ 267 ॥
tatō dūtēna bhaṇitaṁ yathaivaṁ bhaṇati kanakacūḍapitā । vitīryatāṁ jayasundarī kanyā śrīkanakacūḍāya ॥ 268 ॥
tatō naravarēṇa bhaṇitaṁ ratimadanayōrivānayōḥ saṁbandham । kō na bahu manyatē kintu tasyā jananīha pramāṇam || 269 ॥

।
21
tō naravarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ raimayaṇāṇava imāṇa saṁbaṁdhaṁ । kō nabahu mannaē kiṁtu tīē jaṇaṇī iha pamāṇaṁ ॥ 269 ॥
iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ sammāṇiuṁ ca rāyā visajjiraṁ dūyaṁ । caṁdalēhāē puvyuttavaśyaraṁ sāhaē sāvi ॥ 270 ॥
pucchissamahaṁ dhūyaṁti jaṁpiūṇaṁ taō samuṭṭhēuṁ । jā jayasuṁdaripāsē samāgayā tō tayaṁ niyai || 271 ||
parihariyakēlikamalaṁ karakisalayaganbhasaṁṭhiyakavōlaṁ । uvarinivaḍaṁtaasuppahārathara hariyasi hiṇajuyaṁ ॥ 272॥
mimahurāla | vaparāyaṇāē dēvīē caṁdalēhāē । jayasuṁdarī sappaṇayaṁ pāraddhā pucchiuṁ ēvaṁ ॥ 273 ॥
yāvatthāē tuha kō putti ! nibaṁdhaṇaṁ phuḍaṁ kahasu । maha savvakajjaciṁtāyagāē mā khēyamuvha || 274 ||
taṁ natthi kiṁpi bhuvaṇattayammi sayalammi jaṁ na maha sajyaṁ jaṁ phurai vatthujāyaṁ maha hatthagayaṁtra savvaṁpi ।। 275॥
iya puṭṭhā sā nahu kiṁpi dēi paccuttaraṁ taō tīē । kahiyaṁ jaha tuha varaṇatthamāgaō saṁpayaṁ dūō || 276 ||
sirikaṇaya cūḍahēḍaṁ taviṇā pēsiutti sōūṇa । bāḍhaṁ nīsasiūṇa ya puṇōvi dharaṇīyalē paḍiyā || 277 ॥
aha tīē sahayarīē vibbhamalēhāē kumarijaṇaṇīē । kahiyaṁ jaha rāīē kinnara mihuṇēṇa gijjatō || 278 ||
sirisamarasīharāyā nisāmiō nūṇa tā imā tammi । aṇuratā, tā jaha kahavi tēṇa saha saṁgamō hōi ।। 279 ॥
taha ujjamēu dēvī, iya sōūṇaṁ nivēiyaṁ tīē । niyapiyayamassa, tēṇavi āhūō sō kharadūō || 280 ||
kahiyē jahaṭṭiyaṁ ciyatapuraō naravarēṇa, sō bhaṇai । jai kahavi kōvi annō pariṇēhī tuha imaṁ dhūyaṁ ।। 281 ॥
tā nūṇa tujjha tassavi nō kusalaṁ tā tumaṁ imaṁ nāuṁ । dēhi niyakannayaṁ kaṇayacūḍakhayarassa ahavāvi || 282||
raṇasajjō hōsu lahuṁ, ēhī jēṇaṁ pabhāyasamayammi । sirikaṇayacūḍakhayarō balāvi kumariṁ pagivhēuṁ ॥ 283 ॥
iti bhaṇitvā sammānyaca rājā visr̥jya dūtam । candralēkhāyai pūrvōktavyatikaraṁ kathayati sāpi ॥ 270 ॥
prakṣyāmyahaṁ duhitaramiti jalpitvā tataḥ samutthāya । yāvajjayasundarīpārśvē samāgatā tatastāṁ paśyati || 271॥
parihr̥takēlikamalāṁ karakiśalaya garbhasaṁsthitakapōlām । uparinipatadaśruprahārakampitastanayugām ॥ 272॥
mr̥dumadhurālāpaparāyaṇayā dēvyā candralēkhayā । jayasundarī sapraṇayaṁ prārabdhā praṣṭumēvam ॥ 273॥
ētadavasthāyāstava kaḥ putri ! nibandhanaṁ sphuṭaṁ kathaya । mayi sarvakāryacintikāyāṁ mā khēdamudvaha || 274॥
tannāsti kimapi bhuvanatrayē sakalē yanna mama sādhyam । yat sphurati vastujātaṁ mama hastagatamiva sarvam ॥ 275 ॥
iti pr̥ṣṭā sā na khalu kimapi dadāti pratyuttaraṁ tatastayā । kathitaṁ yathā tava varaṇārthamāgataḥ saṁprati dūtaḥ ॥ 276 ॥
śrīkanaka cūḍa hētōstatpitrā prēṣita iti śrutvā । bāḍhaṁ niḥśvasya ca punarapi dharaṇītalē patitā ॥ 277॥
atha tasyāḥ sahacaryā vibhramalēkhayā kumārījananyai । kathitaṁ yathaitayā kinnaramithunēna gīyamānaḥ ॥ 278॥
śrīsamarasiṁharājō niśamitō nūnaṁ tata iyaṁ tasmin । anuraktā, tasmādyathā kathamapi tēna saha saṁgamō bhavēt ॥ 279॥
tathōdyacchatu dēvīti śrutvā nivēditaṁ tathā । nijapriyatamāya, tēnāpyāhūtaḥ sa khacaradūtaḥ ॥ 280 ॥
kathitaṁ yathāsthitamēva tatpuratō naravarēṇa sa bhaṇati । yadi kathamapi kō'pyanyaḥ pariṇēṣyati tavēmāṁ duhitaram॥ 281 ॥
tatō nūnaṁ tava tasyāpi nō kuśalaṁ tasmāttvamidaṁ jñātvā । dēhi nijakanyakāṁ kanakacūḍakhacarāyāthavāpi ॥ 282 ॥
raṇasajjō bhava laghu, ēvyati yēna prabhātasamayē । śrī kanakacūḍakhacarō balādapi kumārī pragrahītum ||283 ||

supāsanāha-cariasmi-
iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ ruṭṭhō dapiṭṭhō nigaō khayaradūō । kahiyē jaha vittaṁ taha sapiuṇō kaṇayacūḍassa ॥ 284॥
raṇasāmaggiṁ kāuṁ samujjaō sōvi, tammi samayammi । maha savisēsaṁ pūyā vihiyā saṁgāmasūrēṇa ॥ 285 ॥
tarasa kuladēvayā haṁ khaṇēṇa pattammi samavaiṇṇamhi । maha puraō viṇṇattaṁ tēṇa imaṁ dēvi jaha kahavi || 286 |
amhāṇaṁ kusalēṇaṁ kumari pariṇēi samarasīha nivō | akkamiḍaṁ vijjāhara sinnaṁ taha kuṇasu lahu dēvi || 287
paḍivajjiūṇa ēyaṁ tujjha samīvammi āgayā ahayaṁ । kahiyaṁ paōyaṇaṁ tuha saṁpai saha siviraniyarēṇa ॥ 288
hō payāgapavaṇō baddhō paṇayaṁjalī maē tujjha । iya nisamiūṇa sirisamarasūrarāyāvi lahumēva || 289
cauraṁgacamūē sēmaṁ dēvīē prabhāvaō nahapahēṇa । pattō khaṇēṇa sirirayaṇasāranayarassa bāhimmi ॥ 290 ॥
ētthaṁtarammi niyabhuyabala gavcuggāravaddharaṇavaṁchō । pattō saha piuṇā tattha khēyarō kaṇayacūḍōvi ॥ 299 ॥
saṁnēhiyasavvasuhaḍaṁ kayavahupaharaṇapariggahaṁ laggaṁ । avaśēpparēṇa sinaṁ varisēuṁ visiha bhāraṁ ||292 ||
jā samarasīhakhayarāṇa tāva kuladēvayāē māyāē । sahasacciya tallōyassa daṁsiṁyaṁ samararaṁgammi || 293॥
paḍiyaṁ sirakamalaṁ kaṇayacūḍakhayarasta tassa tō sinaṁ । dūraṁ dūra palāṇaṁ appāṇamanāyagaṁ nāuṁ ||294 ||
ary balēṇaṁ rahiō gāgī kaṇayacūḍakhayarōvi । tabhayabhīō nahō savvaṁ sutthaṁ taō jāyaṁ ||295 ||
aha sōhaṇē muhuttē amaṁda āṇaṁdaguṁdalapuṁruvvaṁ । piyarēhiṁ pairidinaṁ pariṇai jayasuṁdarīkannaṁ ॥ 296 ॥
sirisamarasīharāyā tīē samaṁ ciya puṇōvi niyanayarē । āgaṁtuṁ visayasuhaṁ uvabhuṁjai jaṇiyajaṇacōjjaṁ ॥ 29
iti bhaṇitvā ruṣṭō darpiṣṭhō nirgataḥ khacaradūtaḥ । kathitaṁ yathā vr̥ttaṁ tathā sapitr̥kāya kanakacūḍāya ॥ 284॥
raṇasāmagra kr̥tvā samudyataḥ sō'pi tasmin samayē । mama saviśēṣaṁ pūjā vihitā saṁgrāmaśūrēṇa ॥ 285 ॥
tasya kuladēvatā'haṁ kṣaṇēna pātrē samavatīrṇāsssam । mama puratō vijñaptaṁ tēnēdaṁ dēvi ! yathā kathamapi || 286।
asmākaṁ kuśalēna kumārīṁ pariṇayēt samarasiṁhanr̥paḥ । ākramya vidyādharasainya tathā kuruṣva laghu dēvi ! ||28
pratipadyaitat taba samīpa āgatā'hakam । kathitaṁ prayōjanaṁ tē saṁprati saha śibiranikaraṇa || 288 ||
bhava prayāṇakapravaṇō baddhaḥ praṇayāñjalirmayā tubhyam । iti niśamya śrīsamaraśūrarājō'pi laghvēva || 289 ॥
caturaṅgacambā samaṁ dēvyāḥ prabhāvatō nabhaḥ pathēna । prāptaḥ kṣaṇēna śrīratnasāranagarād bahiḥ || 290 ||
atrāntarē nijabhujabalagarvēīddvārabaddharaṇavāñchaḥ । prāptaḥ saha pitrā tatra khēcaraḥ kanakacūḍō'pi ॥ 299 ॥
saṁnaddhasarvasubhaṭaṁ kr̥tabahupraharaṇaparigrahaṁ lagnam | parasparaṁ sainyaṁ varṣituṁ viśikhaprāgbhāram ॥ 292॥
yāvatsamarasiṁhakhacarāṇāṁ tāvatkuladēvatayā māyayā । sahasaiva tallōkasya darśitaṁ samararaṅgē ॥293॥
patitaṁ śiraḥkamalaṁ kanakacūḍakhacarasya tasya tataḥ sainyam । dūraṁ dūraṁ palāyitamātmānamanāyakaṁ jñātvā ||294
tadanu balēna rahita ēkākī kanakacūḍakhacarō'pi । tadbhayabhītō naṣṭaḥ sarvaṁ susthaṁ tatō jātam ॥ 295॥
atha śōbhanē muhūrtē'mandānandasandōha pūrvam । pitr̥bhyāṁ parittāṁ pariṇayati jayasundarīkanyām ||296॥
śrīsamarasiṁharājastayā samamēva punarapi nijanagarē | āgamya viṣayasukhamupabhuṅktē janitajanāścaryam ||297|
1 ka. kha. sayaṁ । 2 ka. kha. saṁnihi । 3 kha puruvña, ga. pura3° । 4ka. °pi di° ।

23
aha annayā ya jayasuṁdarīvi rayaṇīē carimajāmammi । ciṭṭhai suhaṇasuttā jā tā picchai imaṁ sumiṇaṁ ॥ 298 ॥
kēvi pahāṇapurisēṇa divvālaṁkāraka liya dēhēṇaṁ । niyasiyadivvadvēgūlajuyala ḍihaṇiyatimirēṇa ॥ 299 ॥
kila majjha mahārayaṇaṁ pāṇippaṇayīkayaṁti taṁ daddhuṁ । vimhayapavāhabuḍuṁtamāṇasā uṭṭhiyā tayaṇu ॥ 300 ॥
sāhaipiyassa sōvi hu taya bhimuhaṁ bhaṇai dēvi ! ēēṇa | sumiṇēṇa visuṇiyā tuha nūṇaṁ puttassa saṁpattī ॥ 309 ॥
harisaviyasaṁtanayaṇāē pulayaparikaliyakā yalaiyāē । ēvaṁti hōu tīē paiṇō bahu manniyaṁ vayaṇaṁ ॥ 302 ॥
aha dhammakammanimpavaṇaujjayā duguṇajaṇiyasuhavihavā । jayasuṁdarīvi gandhaṁ mahagghasōhaggamuvvahaṁi ||303 ||
niruvamagarimālaṁ kiyapaōharāṇaṁ siriṁ samakamiuṁ । sāmarisaṁ uyarasirī paivaḍhaē tīē aṇudiyahaṁ ॥ 304 ॥
damadāṇā pahā tīē sarīrē visēsaō vasiyā । gabbhagaya su anihālaṇakōū halata ra liyavva guṇā ।। 305 ।।
aha amhaṇiya muhaṁ mahūsavaṁ aṇihavitta niyasamaē । paḍipunnaḍōhalā sā suhaṁ pasūyā pasannamuṁhī ॥ 306 ॥
puttaṁ taṇuṣpahā pahayasūibhavaṇaṁtarālatamapasaraṁ । navadiṇamaṇiva puvvā āṇaṁdiyajaṇaṇimuhakamalaṁ ॥ 307 ॥
itthaṁtarammi turiyāgamaṇavisaṁṭhuladukūlakaliyāē । baddhāviō saharisaṁ cēḍīē samarasūranivō || 308 ||
suyajampanisāmaṇajaṇiyaduguṇaharisēṇa naravarēṇāvi | dāliduvamaddakarō mahāpasāō kaō tīsē ॥ 309 ॥
vr̥ddhāvaṇayaṁ niyavivamahimagarimāṇurūvayaṁ tayaṇu । sirisamarasīharannā paṭṭiyaṁ aimahāraṁbhaṁ ॥ 310 ॥
priya samajhatē mahāvibhūīē māsapajjaṁtē । naṁdisētti nāmaṁ rannā vihiyaṁ niyasuyassa || 311 ||
athānyadā ca jayasundaryapi rajanyāścaramayāmē । tiṣṭhati sukhaprasuptā yāvattāvat paśyatīmaṁ svapnam ||298।।
kēnāpi pradhānapuruṣēṇa divyālaṅkārakalitadēhēna । nijasitadivyadukūlayugala pratihatatimirēṇa ॥ 299 ॥
kila mahyaṁ mahāratnaṁ pāṇipraṇayakr̥tamiti tad dr̥ṣṭā । vismayapravāha majjanmānasōtthitā tadanu ॥ 300 ॥
kathayati priyāya sō'pi ca tadabhimukhaṁ bhaṇati dēvi ! ētēna । svapnēna kathitā tavaṁ nūnaṁ putrasya saṁprāptiḥ ॥ 301 ॥
harṣavikasannayanayā pulakaparikalitakāyalatikayā । ēvamiti bhavatu tathā patyurbahumataṁ vacanam ॥ 302 ॥
atha dharmakarmanirmāpanōdyatā dviguṇajanitasukha (śubha) vibhavā । jayasundaryapi garbhamaharghyasaubhāgyamudvahati ॥ 303 ॥
nirupamagarimālaṅkr̥tapayōdharayōḥ śriyaṁ samākramya । sāmarṣamudaraśrīḥ pravardhatē tasyā anudivasam ||304||
damadānadayāpramukhāstasyāḥ śarīrē viśēṣata uṣitāḥ । garbhagatasutanibhālaṁna kautūhalaṁtaralitā iva guṇāḥ || 305 ॥
athāgrāhnikapramukhaṁ mahōtsavamanubhūya nijasamayē । paripūrṇadōhadā sā sukhaṁ prasūtā prasannamukhī ॥ 306 ॥
putraṁ tanuprabhā prahataṁsūtibhavanāntarālatamaḥprasaram । navadinamaṇimiva pūrvānanditajananī mukhakamalam ॥307॥
atrāntarē tvaritāgamanavisaṁsthuladukūkalitayā । vardhāpitaḥ saharṣaṁ cēṭyā samaraśūranr̥paḥ ||308॥
sutajanmaniśamanajanitadviguṇaharṣēṇa naravarēṇāpi । dāridrayōpamardakarō mahāprasādaḥ kr̥tastasyāḥ ||309 ||
vardhāpanakaṁ nijavibhavamahimagarimānurūpakaṁ tadanu । śrīsamarasiṁharājēna pravartitamatimahāramyam ||310 ||
tasmiṁśca samatikrāntē mahāvibhūtyā māsaparyantē । nandiṣēṇa iti nāma rājñā vihitaṁ nijasutasya ॥ 311॥
1 kha dukūla । 2 ka. pavaḍiyā, kha. paṭṭaē । 3 kha suha, ga, suya । 4 ka, ētthaṁ । 5 ka aha naṁ 6 ka. sēṇanā' |

supāsanāha-cariammi-
lālijjatō mahaṇaṇhāṇāiparāhi paṁcadhāīhiṁ । manē. piyaramaṇōra īsāiva sōvi vaḍḍēi ||312 ||
tassa ya vayaṇaṁtaravāsiṇīē vāṇīē muttiyalayavva । jaṁpaṁtassa sahēlaṁ suhumā dasaṇāvalī sahai || 313||
kuralakuralīhi kaliō tamāladalaśāmalō aisaṇiddhō । ma ulikamalē pahōlai cihuracaō kōmalō tassa ।। 314
aha sō jahicchakīlā vilāsa suhagahiyaviggahōvacaō। jāō ya aṭṭhavacchara parivāō jaṇiyajaṇaya suhō ।। 315 ।
tō vijjāgaraṇakhama ēsō iya nicchiuṁ naridēṇa । uvaṇīō vihipuvvaṁ lēhāyariyassa paḍhaṇatthaṁ ॥ 396 ॥
asarisabuddhisamiddhīē sugurubhattīra ujjamēṇaṁ ca । sō thōvadiṇēhiṁ samatya satyaparamatyaviū jāō ।। 317 ॥
niyavayapayārapūyaṁ kuṇamāṇō mahiyalē samaṇupattō । sō varjuvvaṇalacchi savvaṁgama kittimāharaṇaṁ ॥ 318 ॥
miusumā rōmalayā kavōlapālīsu sē samullasiyā | muhakamalaparimaluggāralōlalīṇālimālavva ॥ 319
kaṁcaṇasilā visāla bacchayalaṁ pihusamunnayaṁ tassa | aṁtōphuraṁta guṇagaṇapaṇulliyaṁ pitra samuha || 320||
aha sō sayaṁvarāgayapahāṇapasthivasuyāō'ṇēgāō । pariṇāviō nariṁdēṇa naṁdisēṇō vibhūīē || 321 |
kaiyāvi phāraphēṇānilāṇaṇaṁ damai duddamaturaṁgaṁ । guruvēyavidvattaṁ niyajasaṁva lōyāṇa darisaṁtaṁ ॥ 322 ॥
bahuhāvabhāvalaḍahaṁ kaiyāvi vilāsiṇīṇa savilāsaṁ । lāsavihiṁ sa palōyai gēyarasāyannaṇasayaṇhō || 323॥
kararuhakiraṇamisēṇaṁ dālidajalaṁjaliva viyaraṁtō । kaiyāvi kuṇai maggaṇajaṇāṇa sakarēṇa dāṇavihiṁ || 324 |
muttāhalāṇa vāhi aṁtō puṇa niyaguṇāṇa mālāē । kuṇai savibhūsaṇāī kayāvi sukaīṇa hiyayāī || 325 |
lālyamānō mardanasnānādiparābhiḥ pañcadhātrībhiḥ । manyē pitr̥manōrathēyayēva sōpi pravardhatē ॥ 212 ॥
tasya ca vadanāntaravāsinyā vāṇyā mauktikalatēva । jalpataḥ sahēlaṁ sūkṣmā daśanāvalī rājatē ||313 ||
kuralakuralībhiḥ kalitastamāladalaśyāmalō'tisnigdhaḥ । maulikamalē praghūrṇatē cihuracayaḥ kōmalastasya || 314 ॥
atha sa yathēcchakrīḍāvilāsasukhagr̥hītavigrahōpacayaḥ । jātaścāṣṭavatsaraparyāyō janitajanakasukhaḥ || 315॥
tatō vidyāgrahaṇakṣama ēṣa iti niścitya narēndrēṇa । upanītō vidhipūrva lēkhācāryasya paṭhanārtham ॥ 396 ॥
asadr̥śabuddhisamr̥ddhayā sugurubhaktyōdyamēna ca । sa stōkadinaiḥ samastaśāstraparamārthavijjātaḥ || 317 ||
nijapadapracārapūtaṁ kurvan mahītalaṁ samanuprāptaḥ । sa navayauvanalakṣmīṁ sarvāṅgīṇamakr̥ttrimābharaṇam ।। 318 ।।
mr̥dusūkṣmā rōmalatā kapōlapālyāstasya samullasitā । mukhakamalaparimalōdgāralālalīnālimālēva ॥ 319 ||
kāñcanaśilāviśālaṁ vakṣastalaṁ pr̥thusamunnataṁ tasya । antaḥsphuradguṇagaṇapraṇōditamiva samudvahati ॥ 320॥
atha sa svayaṁvarāgatapradhānapārthivasutā anēkāḥ । pariṇāyitō narēndrēṇa nandiṣēṇō vibhūtyā || 321 ॥
kadācidapi sphāraphēnāvilānanaṁ dāmyati durdamaturaṅgam । guruvēgārjitaṁ nijayuśa iva lōkān darśayantam ॥322
bahuhāvabhāvaramyaṁ kadācidapi vilāsinīnāṁ savilāsam । lāsyavidhiṁ sa pralōkatē gēyarasākarṇanasatr̥ṣṇaḥ ॥ 323 ॥
kararuha kiraṇamiṣēṇa dāridryajalāñjalimiva vitaran । kadācidāpē karōti mārgaṇajanānāṁ svakarēṇa dānavidhim || 326
muktāphalānāṁ bahirantaḥ punarnijaguṇānāṁ mālayā । karōti savibhūṣaṇāni kadāpi sukavīnāṁ hr̥dayāni ॥ 325 ॥
1 ka. ga. nava । 2 ka. jōvaṇa, kha. jīvvaṇa |

punvabhavapatthāyō ।

baccaṁ kālē niyarajjē ṭhāviō vibhūīē । sō naṁdisēṇakumarō rannā sirisamarasīhēṇa ॥ 326 ॥
ēkkārasa paḍimāō sayamavi paḍivajjiūṇa vihipuvvaṁ । pālēḍaṁ kālēṇa ya jaidhammadhuraṁdharō hōuṁ || 327||
savvattha apaḍibaddhō kāuṁ chaṭṭaṭṭamāitavacaraṇaṁ । pajjaṁtakayāṇasaṇō laṁtayakappē surō jāō || 328 ||
ēttō ya naṁdisēō narāhivō nihayasayalapaḍivakkhaṁ । paripālai taṁ rajjaṁ sāhiyanīsēsagaḍhaduggaṁ ॥ 329॥
nivapuṁgavāṇa maulīsu jassa sāsaṇasirī sayā vasai । cūḍāmaṇikara maṁjarimisēṇa kayapa umapēyarēsu ।। 330 ॥
tassa ya māṇasaviphuraṇarāyahaṁsī sasaṁkasamavayaṇā । sayalaṁtē urapamuhā sasippahā piyayamā āsi ॥ 332 ॥
sīē samaṁ cirasaṁciyapunnacayaṁ naṁdisēṇanaravaiṇō । visayasuhaṁ sēvaṁtassa paidiṇaṁ vōlaē kālō ।। 332॥
aha dēvayā kapiyavivihōvāiyasaēhi saṁjāō । tīsē puttō sē nāma ṭhāviyaṁ dhaṇakumārōti ॥ 333॥
kālē yasayala kalākalākalaṇakkhamō ya saṁjāō। tō vihipuvvaṁ rannā samappiō sō kalāguruṇō ।। 334॥
nēṇāvi tassa aisuhumabuddhiviṇaēhiṁ ujjamēṇa ca । raṁjiyahiyaēṇa kaō sō sayalakalākalāvaviū।। 335 ।।
jaya jīva naṁda iccāikōmalālā vapēsalaṁ vayaṇaṁ । na tahā harisēi maṇaṁ tassa jahā sugurusikkhaviyaṁ ॥ 336 ॥
ahannayā ya ajjhāvaraṇa saha naṁdisēṇanaravaiṇō । pāyavaḍiyānimittaṁ saṁpattō dhaṇakumārōvi ||337||
aha sō kayapaṇāma samucipaṭhāṇē suhāsaṇāsīṇō । harisiyahiyaēṇa narāhivēṇa bhaṇiō imaṁ vayaṇaṁ ।। 338 ॥
jīīē vaccha ! bhaṇiyaṁ payāṇa paripālaṇaṁ naravaīṇaṁ । tāvacciya jāna havai niyarajjadhuraṁdharō putō ।। 339 ॥
iti vrajati kālē nijarājyē sthāpitō vibhūtyā । sa nandiṣēṇakumārō rājñā śrīsamarasiṁhēna || 326॥
ēkādaśa pratimāḥ svayamapi pratipadya vidhipūrvam । pālayitvā kālēna ca yatidharmadhurandharō bhūtvā ॥ 327॥
sarvatrāpratibaddhaḥ kr̥tvā ṣaṣṭhāṣṭama । ditapaścaraṇam । paryantakr̥tānaśanō lāntakakalpē surō jātaḥ || 328 ॥
itaśca nandiṣēṇō narādhipō nihatasakalapratipakṣam । paripālayati tadrājyaṁ sādhitaniḥ śēṣaprākāradurgam ॥ 329॥
nr̥papuṅgavānāṁ mauliṣu yasya śāsanaśrīḥ sadā vasati । cūḍāmaṇikaramañjarīmiṣēṇa kr̥tapadmaprakarēṣu ॥ 330 ॥
tasya ca mānasavisphuraṇarājahaṁsī śaśāṅkasamavadanā । sakalāntaḥpurapramukhā śaśiprabhā priyatamā''sīt ॥ 131 ॥
tayā samaṁ cirasaṁcitapuṇyacayaṁ nandiṣēṇanarapatēḥ । viṣayasukhaṁ sēvamānasya pratidinaṁ gacchati kālaḥ ॥ 332 ॥
atha dēvatāyāḥ kalpitavividhōpayācitaśataiḥ saṁjātaḥ । tasyāḥ putrastasya nāma sthāpitaṁ dhanakumāra iti ॥ 333 ॥
kālēna ca sakalakalākalāpakalanakṣamaśca saṁjātaḥ । tatō vidhipūrvaṁ rājñā samarpitaḥ sa kalāguravē ॥ 334 ॥
tēnāpi tasyātisūkṣmabuddhivinayābhyāmudyamēna ca । rañjitahr̥dayēna kr̥taḥ sa sakalakalākalāpavit ॥335॥
jaya jīva nandētyādikōmalālāpapēśalaṁ vacanam । na tathā harṣayati manastasya yathā suguruśikṣitam ॥ 336 ॥
athānyadā cādhyāpakēna saha nandiṣēṇanarapatēḥ । pādapatananimittaṁ saṁprāptō dhanakumārō'pi ॥ 337 ॥
atha sa kr̥tapraṇāmaḥ samucitasthānē sukhāsanāsīnaḥ । harṣitahr̥dayēna narādhipēna bhaṇita idaṁ vacanam ॥ 338 ॥
nītau vatsa ! bhaṇitaṁ prajānāṁ paripālanaṁ narapatīnām । tāvadēva yāvanna bhavati nijarājyadhurandharaḥ putraḥ ||339|
1 ka. paurē ।

supāsanāha-cariammi-
tāvaccha ! tumaṁ mahabhuyakayaciravāsa karēsu rajjasiriṁ । niyabāhuvajjapaṁjara nivāsasuhiyaṁ lahu ihi || 340 ।
aṇumannasu aviyaṣpaṁ ca majjha saṁjamamahārahāruhaṇaṁ । siddhipuraṁdhīsarahasapariraṁbhaṇara siyahiyayassa || 341 ॥
iya piuvayaṇa sō nisamiūṇa tāḍijjamāṇagalasaraṇī । gaggaya girāē laggō vinnavium̐ dhaṇakumārōvi ।। 342
tāya ! na kiṁpi hu picchāmi kāraṇaṁ tujjha tārisaṁ ahayaṁ । tā kaha dukkarakammammi maṁ niuṁjēsi iṇhipi ।। 343 |
parivakvapakkakvaṁtarēsu khittō na tāya ! maṇayaṁpi । uvasamiō pajalatō payāvadāvānalō tujjha ॥ 344 |
tihuyaṇajaṇana yaṇamahārasāyaṇaṁ rūvasaṁpayā tujjha । ajjavi kaṁdappamaḍappakhaṁḍaṇē vahai paṁḍicaṁ || 345 ||
tristisalō bhuvi na atthi tārisōṁ kōvi । jō tuha laṁghai maṇayapi bhūlayāpallavavilāsaṁ ॥ 346
ajjavi samatthasupasatthavatyuvittharavibhūsiō tujjha । bhaṁḍāgārōvi hu dhaṇayajakkhavihavaṁ viḍaṁbē ||347 ||
ajjavi ya mahāraṇa kēlikammakusalō samujjamō tāya!। sō kōvi sahai tuha jaṁ sahiuṁ sakkōvi na hu sakō ।। 348
tattō ya pasīya tumaṁ pālasu cirapāliyaṁ niyaṁ rajjaṁ । samayammi puṇa kuṇatō dhammaṁ nāhaṁ nivārissaṁ ॥ 349
ēvaṁ dhaṇakumarēṇaṁ vinnattō naṁdisēṇanaranāhō । dhammujjamabaddharaī puṇōvi aṇusāsiuṁ laggō ॥ 350 ॥
jaha bajjhō riuvaggō samaggasāmaggiyāē rahiē hiṁ । na tarijjai niggahiuṁ taha aṁtarasattusaṁghōvi ॥ 351॥
nigahammiya puṇō sāmaggī sayalakaraṇagāmassa । pauṇattaṁ taṁ taralaṁ jarakaḍapūyaṇi uttatthaṁ ।। 352 ।
jamhā tī kaṁtō karaṇaggāmō jahadviyaṁ vatyuṁ । paricchidium̐ na pārai bāḍhaṁ parivattiyasarūvō || 353॥
tasmādvatsa ! tvaṁ madbhujakr̥taciravāsāṁ kuru rājyaśriyam । nijabāhuvajrapañjara nivāsa sukhitāṁ ladhvidānīm ॥ 340
anumanyasvāvikalpaṁ ca mama saṁyamamahārathārōhaṇam । siddhipurandhrīsarabhasaparirambhaṇarasikahr̥dayasya ॥ 349 ॥
iti pitr̥vacanaṁ sa niśamya tāḍyamānagalasaraṇiḥ । gaṅgadagirā lagnō vijñapayituṁ dhanakumārō'pi ॥342॥
tāta ! na kimapi khalu paśyāmi kāraṇaṁ tava tādr̥śamahakam । tasmātkathaṁ duṣkarakarmaṇi māṁ niyuṅgē idānīmapi ।। 343
pratipakṣapakṣakakṣāntarēṣu kṣiptō na tāta ! manāgapi । upaśāntaḥ prajvalan pratāpadāvānalastava ॥ 344॥
tribhuvanajananayana mahā rasāyanaṁ rūpasaṁpat tava । adyāpi kandarpagarvakhaṇḍanē vahati pāṇḍityam || 345॥
bhujadaṇḍapracaṇḍabalō bhuvanē'pi nāsti tādr̥śaḥ kō'pi । yastava laṅghatē manāgapi bhrūlatāpallavavilāsam ||346 ॥
adyāpi samasta supraśastavastuvistāravibhūṣitastava । bhāṇḍāgārō'pi dhanadayakṣavibhavaṁ viḍambayati ॥ 347॥
adyāpi ca mahāraṇakēli karmakuśalaḥ samudyamastāta ! । sa kō'pi śōbhatē tava yaṁ sōḍhuṁ śakrō'pi na hi śaktaḥ ॥ 348
tataśca prasīda tvaṁ pālaya cirapālitaṁ nijaṁ rājyam । samayē punaḥ kurvan ( ? ntaṁ ) dharma nāhaṁ nivārayiṣyē ॥ 349 ॥
ēvaṁ dhanakumārēṇa vijñatō nandiṣēṇanaranāthaḥ । dharmōdyamabaddharatiḥ punarapyanuśāsituṁ lagnaḥ || 350||
yathā bāhyō ripuvargaḥ samaprasāmagryā rahitaiḥ । na śakyatē nigrahītuṁ tathā''ntaraśatrutrō'pi ॥ 359 ॥
tannigrahē ca punaḥ sāmagrī sakalakaraṇaprāmasya । praguṇatvaṁ tattaralaṁ jarākr̥tapiśācamiyāttrastam || 352॥
'yasmāttayā''krāntaḥ karaṇayāmō yathāsthitaṁ vastu । paricchēttuṁ na śaknōti bāḍhaṁ parivartitasvarūpaḥ ॥ 393॥
1 kha tatthaṁ । 2 ka. tīyavakaṁ ।
