tājā pauṇattaṁ iṁdiyāṇa jāvājyaṁ taha balaṁ ca । tā juttō mahakāuṁ dhammō samayammi jaha bhaṇiyaṁ || 354 |
"jāva na jarakaḍapūyaṇi savvaṁgayaṁ gasai, jāva na rōyabhuyaṁgu ugu niddau ḍasai ।
tāva dhamma maṇu dijjau kijjau appahiu, ajja ki kali payāṇau jiu nicappa hiu || 355 | 1
tāvaccha ! tumaṁ giṇhasu rajja siriṁ majjha nivviyappamaṇō । gurusāsaṇaparipālaṇamarihaṁ sukulappasūyāṇa ॥ 356 ॥
iya bahuvivayaṇēhiṁ jāva aṇusāsaē dhaṇakumāraṁ । sirinaṁdisēṇarāyā dhammujjamadaḍhanivaddhamaī ॥ 357 ||
tā muhamēliyakara kōsapihiyapasaraṁ tadaṁta karapasaraṁ । ujjāṇapāliyāē vinnattō naṁdisēṇanivō || 358 ||
dēva ! mayaraṁdamaṁdiraārāmē surasamūhanayacalaṇō । muṇimaṁḍalapariyariō sirinaṁdaṇajiṇavarī pattō ॥ 359 ॥
iya nisamiūṇa tī sē dāūṇaṁ pāritōsiyaṁ dāṇaṁ । kahakahavi aṇicchaṁtaṁpi ṭhavai - rajjammi dhaṇakumaraṁ ॥ 360 ॥
sirinaṁdisēṇarāyā samaggasāmaggiyāē parikaliō । ārāmaṁ pai caliō muṇipahupayapaṇamaṇanimittaṁ ।। 361 ।।
pattō ya kamēṇa samullasaṁtasuhabhāvabhāviyamaṇō sō | paṁcavihābhigamēṇa jiṇuggahē saṁpaviṭṭhō ya ॥ 362 ॥
ti payāhiṇīkarēḍaṁ bhattibharulasiravahalapulayabharō । cūḍāmaṇicuṁbiyadharaṇimaṁḍalō jiṇapaē namiḍaṁ । । 363 ॥
āṇaṁdavisēsa visappamāṇabāhulalōyaṇō tayaṇu । pisuṇiyasuhamaṇapariṇāmapēsalaṁ ṇiumāraddhō || 364||
saviṇayanamirasurēsaracūḍāmaṇimasiṇavihiyakamavīḍha ! । tujjha namō sacarācarajīvōvarividdiyanirukaruṇa ! ।।
ajja ci ki jāō haṁ ajja suciracinnāī । punnāīvi uiyāī tuha daṁsaṇamāgaō jamahaṁ | | 366 ||
pahu vaṁciō mhi tamahaṁ ēttiyakālaṁ khu mōharāēṇa । jaṁ tuha payakamalajuē nahu ramiō majjha maṇabhamarō ॥ 367॥
tasmādyāvatpraguṇatvamindriyāṇāṁ yāvadāyustathā balaṁ ca । tāvadyuktō mama kartuṁ dharmaḥ samayē yathā bhaṇitam ॥ 354 ॥
yāvanna jarākr̥tapiśācī sarvāṅgakaṁ grasati, yāvanna rōgabhujaṅga ugrō nirdayō daśati ।
tāvaddharmē manō dīyatāṁ kriyatāmātmahitamadya vā kalyē prayāṇakaṁ jīva ! nityaprathitam ||399||
tasmādvatsa ! tvaṁ gr̥hāṇa rājyaśriyaṁ mama nirvikalpamanāḥ । guruśāsanaparipālanamarhaṁ sukulaprasūtānām ॥ 356॥
iti bahuvidagdhavacanairyāvadanuśāsti dhanakumāram । śrīnandiṣēṇarājō dharmōdyamadr̥ḍhanibaddhamatiḥ ॥357॥
tāvanmukhamēlita karakō śapihitaprasaraddantakaraprasaram । udyānapālikayā vijñaptō nandiṣēṇanr̥paḥ || 358 ।।
dēva ! makarandamandirārāmē surasamūhanatacaraṇaḥ । munimaṇḍalaparikaritaḥ śrīnandanajinavaraḥ prāptaḥ ॥ 359 ॥
iti niśamya tasyai dattvā pāritōṣikaṁ dānam । kathaṁkathamapyanicchantamapi sthāpayati rājyē dhanakumāram || 360 ||
śrīnandiṣēṇarājaḥ samagrasāmagrikayā parikalitaḥ । ārāmaṁ prati calitō muniprabhupādapraṇamananimittam ॥ 369 ॥
prāptaśca kramēṇa samullasacchubhabhāvabhāvitamanāḥ saḥ । pañcavidhābhigamēna jināvagrahē saṁpraviṣṭaśca ॥ 362 ||
triḥ pradakṣiṇīkr̥tya bhaktibharōllasamānabahalapulakabharaḥ । cūḍāmaṇicumbitadharaṇimaṇḍalō jinapādān natvā ॥ 363॥
ānandaviśēṣavisarpadbāhulyalōcanastadanu । kathitaśubhamanaḥ pariṇāmapēśalaṁ stōtumārabdhaḥ || 364 ॥
savinayanamrasurēśvara cūḍāmaṇimasr̥ṇa vihitakramapīṭha ! । tubhyaṁ namaḥ sacarācarajīvōparivihitaniścitakaruṇa ! || 365॥
adyaiva kr̥takr̥tyō jātō'hamadya suciracīrṇāni । puṇyānyapyuditāni tava darśanamāgatō yadaham ॥ 366 ॥

supāsanāha-variammi-
taī sōmasamē diṭṭhē rahasulasiyassa sāyarassa mahaṁ । pulayabharō maṇinivahuvva sahai bāhiṁ viṇikkhittō ।। 368
kaha pahu ! sivasirisaṁgō maha dulahō kahasu saṁpayē hōhī । vararāyahaṁsakappē maṇakamalē tai saṇāhammi ? ।। 369
kiṁpuṇa sivasirisaṁgēvi māṇasaṁ majjha saṁpayaṁ vimuhaṁ । tuhaguṇagaṇāṇurattaṁ sayāvi saraṇaṁ tumaṁ mahai || 370
iya jiṇapahuṇō kāuṁ saṁthavaṇaṁ naṁdisēṇamahināhō । bhūmaṁḍalamiliyaniḍālamaṁḍalō kuṇai paṇivāyaṁ । । 371 ।
karajuyalamiliyakōsō viyasiyamuhakamalajāyasaṁtōtrō । jiṇavayaṇalīṇana yaṇō jahēṭhāṇaṁ tayaṇu uvaviṭṭhō ॥
dasaṇakiraṇāvalīhiṁ ṭiviḍikatōvva disivahumuhāī । sirisirinaṁdaṇajiṇapuṁgavōvi dhammaṁ kahai ēvaṁ ॥ 373
bhō bhō bhavabhamirāṇaṁ aṁtarariugasiya suddhabuddhīṇaṁ । dukkammagalacchaṇadutthiyāṇa jīvāṇa sayakālaṁ ॥ 374 ॥
pāyaṁ savvaṁpi hu kahavi kiṁpi saṁpaḍai na uṇa maṇuyattaṁ । ciṁtārayaṇava samīhiyattha saṁpāyaṇapavīṇaṁ ।। 375 ।।
kahakahavi divvavasaō laddhassavi maṇuyajammarayaṇassa | jiṇavaravayaṇani sāmaṇanisāṇasaṁgō havai dulahō । 376
na hu viṇā imiṇā malamaliṇamimaṁ tirōhiyasaruvaṁ । sugurukalāyapasaṁsārahiyaṁ jīvāṇa paramatthaṁ ॥ 377
tā naravariṁda ! tuma samaggasāmaggiyāē saṁpannaṁ । narabhavarayaṇaṁ pattaṁ paramatthaṁ giṇhasa imēṇaṁ || 378 ||
iya sirinaṁdaṇajiṇapahupaṇīyasuviyaḍḍhadēsaṇaṁ sōuṁ । sirinaṁdisēṇarāyā tayabhimuha jaṁpaē ēvaṁ ।। 379 ।।
'jayapahu kuṇasu pasāyaṁ niyadikkhādāṇaō maha iyāṇi । jai atthi jōggayā jiṇavarēṇa tō jaṁpiyaṁ ēvaṁ ।। 380
naravara ciṁtārayaṇassa jahamiha mahagghassa kaṇayamēva payaṁ । taha dikkhārayaṇassavi ṭhāṇaṁ tumhārisā caiva ॥ 381
prabhō ! vañcitō'smi tadaha mētāvatkālaṁ hi mōharājēna । yattava pādakamalayugē na khalu ratō mama manōbhramaraḥ || 367 ||
tvayi sōmasamē dr̥ṣṭē rabhasōllasitasya sāgarasya mama । pulakabharō maṇinivaha iva rājatē bahirviniṣkrāntaḥ ॥ 368
kathaṁ prabhō ! śivaśrīsaṅgō mama durlabhaḥ kathaya sāṁprataṁ bhaviṣyati । vararājahaṁsakalpē manaḥkamalē tvayā sanāthē ? ॥ 369
kintu śivaśrīsaṅgē'pi mānasaṁ mama sāṁprataṁ vimukham । tvadguṇagaṇānuraktaṁ sadāpi śaraṇaṁ tvāṁ kāṅkṣati ॥ 370 ॥
iti jinaprabhōḥ kr̥tvā saṁstavanaṁ nandiṣēṇa mahīnāthaḥ । bhūmaṇḍalamilitalalāṭamaṇḍalaḥ karōti praṇipātam ॥ 371 |
karayugalamilitakōśō vikasita mukhakamalajātasaṁtōṣaḥ । jinavadanalīnanayaṁnō yathāsthānaṁ tadanūpaviṣṭaḥ || 372।।
daśana kiraṇāvalībhirmaṇḍayanniva digvadhūmukhāni । śrīśrīnandanajinapuṅgavō'pi dharmaṁ kathayatyēvam ॥ 373 ॥
bhō bhō bhavabhramaṇaśīlānāmāntararipugrasita śuddhabuddhīnām । duṣkarma kalakṣaṇaduḥ sthitānāṁ jīvānāṁ sadākālam ॥ 374
prāyaḥ sarvamapi hi kathamapi kimapi saṁpatati na punarmanujatvam । cintāratnamiva samīhitārthasaṁpādanapravīṇam ॥375 |
kathaṁ kathamapi daivavaśatō labdhasyāpi manujajanmaratnasya । jinavaravacananiśamananiśāṇasaṅgō bhavati durlabhaḥ || 376
na hi dadāti vinā'nēna malama linamidaṁ tirōhitasvarūpam । sugurumaṇikārapraśaṁsārahitaṁ jīvēbhyaḥ paramārtham ॥ 377
tasmād naravarēndra ! tvayā samagrasāmagrikayā saṁpannam । narabhavaratnaṁ prāptaṁ paramārtha gr̥hāṇānēna ॥ 378 ॥
iti śrīnandanajinaprabhupraṇītasuvidagdhadēśanāṁ śrutvā । śrīnandiṣēṇarājastadabhimukhaṁ jalpatyēvam ||379||
jagatprabhō ! kuruṣva prasādaṁ nijadīkṣādānatō mamēdānīm । yadyasti yōgyatā, jinavarēṇa tatō jalpitamēvam ॥ 380
1 ga, hathāmaṁ । 2 kha. ga. ēyaṁ ।

tā nivvigdhaṁ tuha havau ēsa atyōti jaṁpiūṇa jiṇō । ōṇayasiraṁ sahatthēṇa dikkhaē naṁdisēṇanivaṁ ॥ 382॥
aha naṁdisēṇasāhū tiguttiguttō samiīhi juttō ya । hayapaṁcidiyapasarō dujjayanijjiṇiyakusumasarō ।। 383 ।।
paḍhiēkārasaaṁgō duppaḍikaṁtāṇa duṭṭhakammāṇa । khavaṇatthamuggatavasā appāṇaṁ jhōsamāṇō ya ।। 384 ।।

tahāhi ;-
siddhipurīpahapatthiyasatthāhasamāṇatitthanāhāṇa । taha ēgaṁtiya sivasuhariddhisamiddhāṇa siddhāṇa || 386||
taha saṁghassavi nimma hiyasayaladhammiyaṇavigghasaṁghassa । taha pasamāmayanihiṇō guruṇō vacchalakaraṇēṇa ।। 387 ।।
taha siṁḍhilīkayasaddhammakammacittāṇa sattasaṁghāṇa । thirakaraṇēṇaṁ pariyāyathērajvahaṇēṇa ca ॥ 388 ॥
taha sussāē bahussuyāṇa saṁsayasahassamahaṇāṇa । paḍiyaraṇēṇaṁ ca tahā tavanirayāṇa tavassīṇaṁ ॥ 389॥
sasarīrēvi hu amamattabuddhikaraṇēṇa tahaya paisamayaṁ । paribhāvaṇēṇa saṁvēgapamuhasuhabhāvaṇāṇaṁ ca ॥ 390 ॥
taha bārasabhēyassavi tavassa āsēvaṇāvihāṇēṇa । abdhiṁtarasattūṇaṁ nicaṁ ciya cāyakaraṇēṇa ॥ 399 ॥
iccē māhiṁ ṭhāṇēhiṁ naṁdisēṇamuṇivasa hō । titthayaranāmagōyaṁ kammaṁ baṁdhēi vihiputraṁ ॥ 392 ॥
ēttō ya carimasamaē ālōiyaniyayaduccariyavaggō । ucca riyavaō sammaṁ khāmiyanīsēsasattugaṇō ॥ 393॥

naravara ! cintāratnasya yathēha mahārghasya kanakamēva padam । tathā dīkṣāratnasyāpi sthānaṁ yuṣmādr̥śā ēva ॥ 381॥
tasmānnirvighnaṁ tava bhavattrēṣō'rtha iti jalpitvā jinaḥ । avanataśiraskaṁ svahastēna dīkṣatē nandiṣēṇanr̥pam ॥ 382॥
atha nandiṣēṇasādhustriguptiguptaḥ samitibhiryuktaśca । hatapañcēndriyaprasarō nirjitadurjaya kusumaśaraḥ || 383 ||
paṭhitaikādaśāṅgō duṣpratikrāntānāṁ duṣṭakarmaṇām । kṣapaṇārtha mugratapasā''tmānaṁ kṣapayaśca ॥ 384 ॥
apratibaddhavihārēṇa viharan vidhinā spr̥śati । tīrthakaratvanibandhana bhūtānīmāni sthānāni ॥385॥
tathāhi ;-
|
siddhipurīpathaprasthitasārthavāhasamānatīrthanāthānām। tathaikāntikaśivasukharddhisamr̥ddhānāṁ siddhānām ॥ 386 ॥
tathā saṁghasyāpi nirmathitasakaladharmijana vighna saṁghasya । tathā praśamāmr̥tanidhērgurāvātsalyakaraṇēna ||387 ॥
tathā śithilīkr̥tasaddharmakarmacittānāṁ sattvasaṁghānām । sthirakaraṇēna paryāya sthavirōpabr̥ṁhaṇēna ca ॥ 388 ॥
tathā śuśrūṣayā bahuśrutānāṁ saṁśaya sahasramathanānām । pratikaraṇēna ca tathā tapōniratānāṁ tapasvinām || 389 ||
svaśarīrē'pi mamatvabuddhikaraṇēna tathā ca pratisamayam । paribhāvanēna saṁvēgapramukhaśubhabhāvanānāṁ ca ॥ 390॥
tathā dvādaśabhēdasyāpi tapasa āsēvanāvidhānēna । ābhyantaraśatrūṇāṁ nityamēva tyāga karaṇēna ॥ 399 ॥

majjhima uvarimagēvijjagammi dēvō mahiḍiō jāō । dōhatthapamāṇataṇū rāyarisinaṁdisēṇutti ।। 395 ।।
tattō ahamiṁdasuralacchisacchavacchatthalammi hārōvva । vilasai aṭṭhāvīsaṁ airāī suhanimaggaṁgō || 396
iya sirisupāsacariē samatthiō ēsa paḍhamapatthāvō । titthayaranāmakammō vāyaparirsṁaṇāganbhō ||397|
aha sō āuyavigamē tattō caviūṇa jammi ṭhāṇammi । uppajjihī tamēttō vōcchaṁ samayānusārēṇa । । 398
॥ iya sirisupāsanāhacariē paḍhamō bhavō bīō surabhavō ya samattō ॥
vidhinā māsikasaṁlēkhanayā saṁlikhitanijaśarīraśca । pañcanamaskāraparāyaṇaśca mr̥tvā samādhinā ॥ 394 ॥
madhyamōparimagraivēyakē dēvō maharddhikō jātaḥ । dvihastapramāṇatanū rājarṣirnandiṣēṇa iti ॥ 395 ॥
tatō'hamindrasuralakṣmīsvaccha vakṣaḥsthalē hāra iva । vilasatyaṣṭāviṁśatiṁ sāgarān sukhanimagnāṅgaḥ ।। 396॥
iti śrīsupārśvacaritē samarthita ēṣa prathamaprastāvaḥ । tīrthakara nāmakarmōpapātaparisūcanāgarbhaḥ ॥ 397 ॥
atha sa āyurvigamē tataścyutvā yasmin sthānē । utpatsyatē taditō vakṣyē samayānusārēṇa ॥ 398 ॥
॥ iti śrīsupārśvanāthacaritē prathamō bhavaḥ, dvitīyaḥ surabhavaśca samāptaḥ ॥

suragirikūvakkhaṁbhaṁ jiṇamajjaṇasalila siyavaḍāḍōvaṁ । bhavajalahijāṇavattaṁ jayai jaē māṇusa khēttaṁ ॥ 1 ॥
tattha ya jaṁbuddīvō varakēvalanāṇarayaṇakōḍīhiṁ । lōyālōyavvaiyaramujjōyatō sayā sahai ||2||
tattha ya khēttaṁ bharahaṁ tatthavi laṅghaṇaṁ jattha dāhiṇayaṁ । majjhimakhaṁḍaṁ kaṁḍaṁva jaṁti bhaviyā javēṇa sivaṁ ॥ 3 ॥
tattha tthi dhannadhaṇakaṇayakaliyagurugāmanayarasaṁ kinnō । kāsitti jaṇavaō jaṇamaṇāṇa saṁjaṇiyaguruha risō | 4 |
tammiya maṁgalanilayā guruvittā sūrabuhakavisamēyā । aṁbarasirivva navaraṁ aṇēyarisibhūsiyā ēsā ||5||
vihiēkkakōsiyapayaṁ paḍimaṁdira kēlihaṁsaramaṇīyā । pāsāyapahā paḍalacchalēṇa jā hasai amarapuraṁ || 6 ||
phaṇivaikamā hivabhuvaṇavāsidēvēhiṁ jīi sayakālaṁ । pikkhijjai parihāvivarakkhittadiṭṭhīhi varasōhā ॥7॥
jattha ya gayaṇagaṇalagga vimalapāyārasihara niyarēhiṁ । sakalakōtti niruddhō na lahai caṁdōvi hu pavēsaṁ ||8||
hu
sātigacaccaragōuracakadhavalahara jaṇiyavarasōhā । vāṇārasitti nayarī vitthinnā asthi bhuvaṇayalē ||9||
jammi visayāṇurāō nivassa sajaṅattaṇaṁ pasuvaissa । paralacchī ahilāsō harista paikkhisu viruvattaṁ ॥ 10 ॥
aha navari tattha dōsō jaṁ kira gōsammi taruṇa mihuṇāṇaṁ । kēlīsuō payaṁpai rayaṇīvīsaṁbhabhaṇiyāī ॥11॥
tatyatthi sayaladariyāriniyararamaṇīṇa aṁsujalahimmi । haviyajasarāyahaṁsō supaiṭṭhō nāma naranāhō ॥ 12॥
jassa samarēsu rēhai hayagayamaya miliyaparimaluggārā । daiḍhapariyaṭṭhiyajayasirikēsakalāvōcva khaggalayā ||13|
jassa ya cāitaṁ saiṁuṇasaṁkulē raṇabharammivi gihēvi । paralōyasāhaṇaṭṭā rēhai payaḍaṁ ciya jayammi ॥ 14॥
1
suragirikūpastambhaṁ jinamajjanasalilasitapaṭāṭōpam । bhavajaladhiyānapātraṁ jayati jagati mānuṣaṁ kṣētram ॥1॥
tatra ca jambūdvīpō barakēvalajñānaratnakōṭībhi: । lōkālōkavyatikaramudyōtayan sadā rājatē ||2||
tatra ca kṣētraṁ bhārataṁ tatrāpi labdhvā yatra dakṣiṇakam । madhyamakhaṇḍaṁ kāṇḍamiva yānti bhavikā javēna śivam ॥ 3॥
tatrāsti dhānyadhanakanakakalitagurugrāmanagara saṁkīrṇaḥ । kāśīti janapadō janamanasāṁ saṁjanitaguruharṣaḥ || 4 |
tasmiṁśca maṅgalanilayā guruvittā śūrabudhakavisamētā । ambara śrīriva navaramanē karṣibhūṣitapradēśā ||5||
vihitaikakauśikapadaṁ pratimandirakēlihaṁsaramaṇīyā । prāsādaprabhāpaṭalacchalēna yā hasatyamarapurīm ||6||
phaṇipatikamaṭhādhipabhuvanavāsidēvairyasyāḥ sadākālam । prēkṣyatē parikhāvivarakṣiptadr̥ṣṭibhirvaraśōbhā ||7||
yatra ca gaganāṅgaṇalagnavimalaprākāra śikharanikaraiḥ । sakalaṅka iti niruddhō na labhatē candrōpi hi pravēśam ॥8॥
sātrikacatvaragōpuracakradhavalagr̥hajanitavaraśōbhā । vāṇārasīti nagarī vistīrṇāsti bhuvanatalē ||9॥
yasyāṁ viṣayānurāgō nr̥pasya sajaḍatvaṁ paśupatēḥ । paralakṣmyabhilāṣō harēḥ pakṣiṣu virūpatvam ॥ 10॥
asau navaraṁ tatra dōṣō yatkila prabhātē taruṇamithunānām । kēliśukaḥ prajalpati rajaniviśrambhabhaṇitāni ॥ 11॥
tantrāsti sakaladr̥ptārinikararamaṇīnāmaśrujaladhau । snapitayaśōrājahaṁsaḥ supratiṣṭhō nāma naranāthaḥ ॥ 12 ॥
yasya samarēṣu rājati hatagajamadamilitaparimalōdvārā । dr̥ḍhaparikr̥ṣṭajaya śrī kēśakalāpa iva khaṅgalatā ॥13॥
yasya ca tyāgitvaṁ śakunasaṁkulē raṇabharēpi gr̥hēpi । paralōkasādhanārthaṁ rājati prakaṭamēva jagati ॥ 14 ॥

jō vipaṇacaraṇōvi gōttabhēī na, mēiṇipaīvi । na hu māyaṁgō, pajjunnaōvi paḍipunnasayalaṁgō ॥15
mittāṇaṁ udayagirī vibuhacaōrāṇa sasaharasamāṇō । jō sūrō riutamasaṁtaīē pahavō viggassa || 16 ||
kēlikulaṁba kalāṇaṁ guṇarayaṇāṇaṁ ca rōhaṇagirivva । jō dappaṇuñca chaddaṁsaṇāṇa lacchīē jalahivva ॥ 17
jassāriniyararamaṇīō luṭiē bhūmaṇē aṇuprayāō । vacchatthalammi payaḍaṁti avirayaṁ nayaṇajalahāraṁ ||18
tassa ya puhaī puhaivya pavarāvattā suvannakaliyā ya । supaōharā surayaṇā ya paṇaiṇī asthi bahussā ||19
kuḍilāṇaṁ cihurāṇaṁ jīē sīmaṁtayasya saralassa । pacchāpurakaraṇēṇaṁ nīivva padaṁsiyā paiṇō ||20||
kaliyaṁ varālaēhiṁ naravaibhavaṇaṁva jīē bhālayalaṁ । vijiyaṭṭamīsa saṁkaṁ nīsaṁkaṁ harai hiyayāī ॥ 21 ॥
viyasiyakuvalayadaladīhavibbhamaṁ jīē nayaṇajuyalaṁpi । alipaḍalēhiṁ bhamuhānihēṇa sēvijjaē niccaṁ || 22 |
jīsē nāsāvaṁsō saralō rēhēi kittithaṁbhōvva । vihiṇō anannasamarūvapayaḍaṇuppannagavvassa ||23||
raipīīṇa parupparaīsā saṁjaṇiyakalaha bhīēṇa । jīsē ya savaṇadōlājuyaṁva mayaṇēṇa nimmaviyaṁ ||24||
sōhēi muhaṁ jalahijva jīē lāyannasalilapaḍipuna । surayaṇakaliyaṁ vidumalayāharaṁ sassirīyaṁ ca || 25 |
jīsē ya kaṁbusama kaṁṭhakaṁdalē sāhaivva lōyāṇaṁ । rēhātiyaṁ jayattayaramaṇīyaṇavijaya parisaṁkhaṁ ||26||
jīē taṇummi ārūḍhamayaṇajōhassa jubvaṇagayassa | kuṁbhatthalaṁva rēhai pīṇunnayaka ḍhiṇasihiṇajuyaṁ ||27||
kōmalamuṇālanālē jīē rēhaṁti bāhujuyalammi । kamalāīva kōmalakara yalāī saralaṁgulidalāī ॥ 28 ॥
yō vibudhapraṇatacaraṇōpa gōtrabhēdī na, mēdinīpatirapi । na hi mātaṅgaḥ, pradyumnakōpi paripūrṇasakalāṅgaḥ ॥ 15 ॥
mitrāṇāmudayagirirvibudhacakōrāṇāṁ śaśadharasamānaḥ । yaḥ sūrō riputamaḥ saṁtatēḥ prabhavahnivargasya ॥ 16 ॥
kēlikulamiva kalānāṁ guṇaratnānāṁ ca rōhaṇagiririva । yō darpaṇa iva ṣaḍdarśanānāṁ lakṣmyā jaladhiriva ||17|
yasyārinikararamaṇyō luṇṭitē bhūṣaṇē'nuśayāt । vakṣaḥsthalē prakaṭayantyavirataṁ nayanajaladhārām ॥ 18 ॥
tasya ca pr̥thivī pr̥thivīva pravarāvarttā suvarṇakalitā ca । supayōdharā suratnā ca praṇayinyasti bahuśasyā ||19|
kuṭilānāṁ cihurāṇāṁ yasyāḥ sīmantakasya saralasya । paścātpuraḥkaraṇēna nītiriva pradarśitā patyuḥ ||20||
kalitaṁ varā (varajā) lakairnarapatibhavanamiva yasyā bhālatalam । vijitāṣṭamīśaśāṅkaṁ niḥśaṅkaṁ harati hr̥dayāni ||21|
vikasitakuvalayadaladīrghavibhramaṁ yasyā nayanayugalamapi । alipaṭalairr̥nibhēna sēvyatē nityam ॥22॥
yasyā nāsāvaṁśaḥ saralō rājatē kīrtistambha iva । vidhērananyasamarūpa prakaṭanōtpannagarvasya ||23||
ratiprītyōḥ parasparērṣyāsaṁjanitakalahabhītēna । yasyāśca śravaṇadōlāyugamiva madanēna nirmārpitam ॥ 24॥
śōbhatē mukhaṁ jaladhiriva yasyā lāvaṇyasalilaparipūrṇam । suratnakalitaṁ vidrumalatādharaṁ saśrīkaṁ ca ॥ 25॥
yasyāśca kambusamakaṇṭhakandalē kathayatīva lōkānām । rēkhātrikaṁ jagattraya ramaṇījanavijaya parisaṁkhyām ||26||
yasyāstanāvārūḍhamadanayōdhasya yauvanagajasya । kumbhasthalamiva rājatē pīnōnnatakaṭhinastanayugam ॥27॥
kōmalamr̥ṇālanālē yasyā rājanti bāhuyugalē । kamalānīva kōmalakaratalāni saralāṅgulidalāni ॥28॥
1 vibudhāḥ = dēvāḥ parvatāśca । 2 gōtraḥ = parvataḥ, vaṁśaśca । 3 mēdinī - pr̥thivī, mātaṅgī ca । 4 pradyumnakaḥ = anaṅgaḥ, prakr̥ṣṭaṁ dyumnaṁ dhanaṁ yasya sa ca ।

jammāpatthāvō ।
33
taha nāhida hō juvvaṇaghaṇēṇa lāyannavāriṇā bhariō । na huṁ niṭṭhai jaha uliṁciōvi piyanayaṇakalasēhiṁ ॥ 29॥
jīsē niyaṁvibassa kāmakīlāyalassa siharaṁva । sahai sayā taṇumajjhaṁ parigijjha muṭṭhimajjhēṇa ॥ 30 ॥
horanasi fatei lacchīē jīē sacchāyaṁ । kamajuyalē laliyaṁgulikaliyaṁ nahakēsarasaṇāhaṁ ॥ 31 ॥
sukaivva suttauttīē rayaṇināhōcca punnajōṇhāē । rayaṇanihivva suhāē sahai nivō tīē daiyāē ॥ 32 ॥
jiha natri kharṇapi mayaṇō raīē parivajjiō raī lahai । sasisēharōvi gōrīē taha viṇā tīē naranāhō ॥ 33 ॥
tīē samaṁ bhuṁjatō paṁcapayāraṁpi visayasuhamaṇahaṁ । suiraṁpi gayaṁ kālaṁ na muṇai dōguduyasurōvva ॥ 34॥
aha annayāya bhadavaya asiyapakkhaḍamīē rayaṇīē । līlāē kaṁci vēlaṁ daiēṇa samaṁ gamēūṇa ॥ 35॥
surasari puṇivisālē palakē haṁsatūliyasaṇāhē । paramasuhēṇa pattā jā ciṭṭhā syaṇicarimammi ||36||
majjhimauvarimagēvijjaṁgāu tō caviya naṁdisēṇanivō। avayariō tagganbhē tō sā caudasa niyai sumiṇē ॥ 37 ॥
dippaṁtadaṁtamusalaṁ kavōlaviyalaṁtamayajalapavāhaṁ । himagiridhavaluttuṁgaṁ picchai sugayaṁ gayaṁ paḍhamaṁ ॥ 38 ॥
sihigalasāmalasasisayalaku ḍilasiṁgaṁ tusārakaradhavalaṁ । unnayakhaṁdhavararayaṇamāliyaṁ niyai vasahavaraṁ ॥ 39 ॥
dīhara kaḍāra kē sarabhāsurakhayaṁ chaṇidukaradhavalaṁ । paṁcāṇaṇaṁ niyacchai guṁjāruṇanayaṇatēilaṁ ॥ 40 ॥
varakarikaraggasaṁṭhiyā suvannakalasēhi taha havijjataṁ । picchai kamaladalacchi lacchi kamalāsaṇanisannaṁ ॥41॥
mayaraṁdabiṁdusaṁdōhaluddhabhasalāvalīhi saṁvaliyaṁ । asamasiyakusumadāmaṁ maṇōbhirāmaṁ palōi ॥ 42 ॥
tathā nābhidrō yauvanaghanēna lāvaṇyavāriṇā bhr̥taḥ । nahi nistiṣṭhati yathōdriktō'pi priyanayanakalaśaiḥ ॥29॥
prasyā nitambabimbasya kāmakrīḍācalasya śikharamiva । rājatē sadā tanumadhyaṁ parigrāhyaṁ muṣṭimadhyēna ॥ 30॥
līlākamalayugamiva rājatē lakṣmyā yasyāḥ sacchāyam । kramayugalaṁ lalitāṅgulikalitaṁ nakhakēsarasanātham॥ 31 ॥
sukaviriva sūktōktyā rajaninātha iva pūrṇajyōtsnayā । ratnanidhiriva sudhayā rājati nr̥pastayā dayitayā ॥32॥
'yathā naiva kṣaṇamapi madanō ratyā parivarjitō ratiṁ labhatē । śaśiśēkharō'pi gauryā tathā vinā tayā naranāthaḥ ॥ 33 ॥
tayā samaṁ bhuñjānaḥ pañcaprakāramapi viṣayasukhamakṣatam । suciramapi gataṁ kālaṁ na jānāti daugundukasura iva ॥34॥
athānyadā ca bhādrapadāsitapakṣāṣṭamyā rajanyām । līlayā kāñcidvēlāṁ dayitēna samaṁ gamayitvā ॥35॥
surasaritpulina viśālē palyaṅkē haṁsatūlikāsanāthē । paramasukhēna prasuptā yāvat tiṣṭhati rajanicara mē || 36॥
madhyamōparimagraivēyakāttataścyutvā nandiṣēṇanr̥paḥ । avatīrṇastadgarbhē tataḥ sā caturdaśa paśyati svapnān ॥ 37॥
dīpyaddantamuśalaṁ kapōlavēigalanmadajalapravāham । himagiridhavalōttuṅgaṁ paśyati sugataṁ gajaṁ prathamam ||38 ! |
śikhigalaśyāmalaśaśiśakalakuṭilaśr̥ṅgaṁ tuṣārakara dhavalam । unnataskandhavararatnamālikaṁ paśyati vr̥ṣabhavaram ||39||
dīrghakaḍārakēsarabhāsuraskandhaṁ kṣaṇēndukaradhavalam । pañcānanaṁ paśyati gujāruṇanayana tējaskam ॥40॥
varakarikarāgrasaṁsthitasuvarṇakalaśaistathā snapyamānām । paśyati kamaladalākṣī lakṣmī kamalāsananiṣaṇṇām ॥ 41 ॥
makarandabindusandōhalubdhabhramarāvalībhiḥ saṁvalitam । asamasitakusumadāma manōbhirāmaṁ pralōkatē ॥ 42 ॥
1 ga. ullibbijjatōvi hi nipi । 2 niṣṭhām = antaṁ yātīti । 3 suṣṭhu gataṁ = gatiryasya tam ।

juṇhujjōiyabhuvaṇaṁtarālamabhira miyakumuyavaṇasaṁḍaṁ । sasimaṁḍala palōyai pavisaṁtaṁ vayaṇakamalammi ||43|| 3
cakaṁga mihuṇa saṁghaḍaṇapañcalaṁ daliyatimirariupasaraṁ । paviyāsiya kamalavaṇaṁ khaṇaṁ nihālēi diṇanāhaṁ ॥46
kaṇayakamaṇīyakiṁkiṇiravamuhalaṁ siyaṁsuyapaḍāyaṁ । bahurayaṇakaliyadaṁḍē mahādhayaṁ picchaē tattō ॥ 45 ॥
amalāmayapaḍipunnaṁ kuvalayamālōkmāliyamuhaṁ ca । kaṇayamayapuṣṇakalasaṁ vilasataṁ pāsa puraō || 46 ||
vararāya haṁsarāī virāiyaṁ pavaramīṇakayasōhaṁ । piyapayatalava picchara sirikaliṁga paramasaramamalaṁ ||47 || ।
halaṁtamahalluvvillalaharimālāviinnarayaṇēhiṁ । diṣpaṁtataḍasaṇāhaṁ surasarināhaṁ taō niyai ||48 ||
cīrṇasamūdhiyavirāiyaṁ kaṇirakiṁkiṇīmāla । muttāhalajālavilāsabhāsuraṁ pikkha vimāṇaṁ ॥ 49 ॥
viṣphuriyaphāra ravikara karaṁbiyāsēsadisimuhaṁ tattō । rayaṇucayaṁ visālaṁ viṇiyacchai mayasiliṁbacchī ||50
niddhūmatē yapasaraṁ supayāhiṇajalirataralajālāhiṁ | ujjōiyabhuvaṇayalaṁ jalaṇaṁ sakkhaṁ nirikkhēi ||51||
ētyaṁtara mmi savvaivi vāsavā avahināṇabhāvēṇa । caliyāsaṇā muṇēuṁ jiṇavaraganbhāvayāramahaṁ ॥ 52॥
sattaṭṭhapayāī uūṇa katthaēṇa tayabhimuhaṁ । dharaṇiyalamiliyavaramaulimaṁḍalā tattha vadati || 53 ॥
paṁcasu kallāsuṁ gaṁtavyamavasa jiṇavariṁdāṇaṁ । tiyasāhivēhiṁ iya nicchiūṇa savvaivi saṁcaliyā ||24|
pihuvacchatthalavila saṁtapavaramuttākalāvakamaṇīyā । ramaṇīyakaṇaya kuṁḍalamaṁḍiyagaṁṭhatthalābhōgā || 55 ||
maṇirayaṇakiraṇabhāsura kirīḍaparikaliyamaulimālā ya। niyapaṇaiṇīhiṁ sahiyā pattā supaṭṭanibhavaṇaṁ ॥ 56
tattha ya harisavasubbhavarōmaṁcacyā payāhiṇīkāuṁ । dēvi viṇaṇayā tattō saṁdhuṇimāḍhattā ||27||
jyōtsnā dyōtitabhuvanāntarālamabhiramitakumudavanaṣaṇḍam | śaśimaṇḍalaṁ pralōkatē praviśad vadanakamalē ||43
cakrāṅgamithunasaṁghaṭanapratyalaṁ dalitatimiraripuprasaram । pravikāsita kamalavanaṁ kṣaṇaṁ nibhālayati dinanātham ||44
kanakakamanīyakiṅkiṇīravamukharaṁ sitāṁśukapatākam । bahuratnakalitadaṇḍaṁ mahādhvajaṁ paśyati tataḥ ॥45॥
amalāmr̥taparipūrṇaṁ kuvalayamālōpamālitamukhaṁ ca । kanakamayapūrṇakalaśaṁ vilasantaṁ paśyati purataḥ ॥ 46 ॥
vararājahaṁsarājivirājitaṁ pravaramīnakr̥taśōbham । priyapādatalamiva paśyati śrīkalitaṁ padmasarō'malam ||47 ||
calanmahōdvēllitalaharīmālāvitīrṇaratnaiḥ । dīpyattaysanāthaṁ surasarinnāthaṁ tataḥ paśyati ॥ 48 ॥
cīnāṁśusamucchritadhvajavirājitaṁ kvaṇanaśīla kiṅkiṇī mālam । muktāphalajālavilāsabhāsuraṁ prēkṣatē vimānam ||49
visphuritasphāraravikarakarambitāśēṣadiṅmukhaṁ tataḥ । ratnōccayaṁ viśālaṁ paśyati mr̥gaśāvākṣī ||10||
nirdhūmatējaḥ prasaraṁ supradakṣiṇajvalanaśīlataralajvālābhiḥ | udyōtitabhuvanatalaṁ jvalanaṁ sākṣād nirīkṣatē ॥ 51
atrāntarē sarvē'pi vāsavā avadhijñānabhāvēna । calitāsanā jñātvā jinavaragarbhāvatāramaham ||52॥
saptāṣṭapadānyutthāya śakrastavēna tadabhimukham । gharaṇitalāmilitamaulimaṇḍalāsta vandantē || 13 ॥
pañcasu kalyāṇēṣu gantavyamavaśya jinavarēndrāṇām । tridaśādhipairiti niścitya sarvē'pi saṁcalitāḥ ||14||

35
mōhaṁdharāya dūmiyasa maggatailōyaḍaṇapayaṁḍē । jiganavadiṇayaramuyarēṇa uvvahaṁtīē tuha namimō ॥ 58 ॥
sayarēṇa dharatīē nararayaṇamimaṁ mahamyahaṁ dēvi ! | aharībhūyamasēsa jayaṁpi tuha raṇagabhāē ॥ 69 ॥
tucchatāi pasiddhaṁ kalaṁka miha nūṇamajjamavaṇīyaṁ । annāṇavi mahilāṇaṁ tumaē jiṇaganbhadharaṇēṇaṁ ||30||
dēvi! tumaṁ ciya aggēsarā si bhuvaṇammi puttavaṁtīṇaṁ । bhavajalahijāṇavattaṁ jiṇavaramuyarēṇa vahamāṇī ॥ 61 ॥
vivarā viviha saṁdhuṇiūṇaṁ jiṇidavarajaṇaṇi । jiṇanāhaṁ gabhaṭṭhiyaṁ dhuṇaṁti tattō ya bhattīē ॥ 62 ॥
sayalasurāsura kinnara vijjāharaniyaranaravariṁdā | sāmiya ! sāmiyabhuvaṇōvasaggaggassa tujjha namō ॥ 63॥
taṁ nikāraṇakaruṇāyarō si jiṇanāha ! jamiha avayariō । majjhima uvarimagēvijjagāō bhavvāṇa bōhatthaṁ ॥ 64 ॥
tā ajjamajjhimōvi hu ukkidvayarō imō maṇuyalōō । jāō jiṇa ! tuha gabbhāvayāraō natthi saṁdēhō || 65 ||
iya vayaṇēhiṁ thōūṇa jiṇavaraṁ bhattinibbharā iṁdā | naṁdīsarammi kāuṁ jiṇamahamamarālayaṁ pattā ॥ 66 ॥
ēyāī daṇaṁ savvattamacitiyatthajaṇagāīṁ 1 varadhēṇukappapāyavaciṁtāmaṇiguṇamahagghāī || 67 ॥
pāhāya tūraravapaḍibuddhā sumiṇadaṁsaṇasamutthaṁ । harisaṁva amāyataṁ viyarai pulayacchalēṇa bahiṁ ॥ 68 ॥
tō namō jiṇāṇaṁ iya bhaṇirī syaṇiviramasamayammi । paurayaraharisakaliyā līlāē muyai pallaṁkaṁ ॥ 69 ॥
aūṇa jidipaḍimamappaḍimabhattisaṁjuttā । saṁdhuṇiūṇa ya suvisuddhapavara muddātiyā gayā ||70 ||
yaha sāi kamēṇaṁ asumiṇāṇa vaiyaraṁ paiṇō । āyannia sōvi taō pamuiyacittō bhai ēvaṁ ॥ 71 ॥
natra ca harṣavaśōdbhava rōmāñcacayāḥ pradakṣiṇīkr̥tya । dēvīṁ vinayapraṇatāstataḥ saṁstōtumārabdhāḥ ||17||
pōhāndhakāradāvitasamagratrailōkyaprakaṭanapracaṇḍam | jinanavadinakaramudarēṇōdvahantyai tubhyaṁ namaḥ || 18 ||
udarēṇa dharantyā nararatnamidaṁ mahāprabhaṁ dēvi ! | adharībhūtamaśēṣaṁ jagadapi tvayā ratnagarbhayā ॥ 59 ॥
tucchatāyā: prasiddhaḥ kalaṅka iha nūnamadyāpanītaḥ । anyāsāmapi mahilānāṁ tvayā jinagarbhadharaṇēna ॥ 60 ॥
dēvi ! tvamēvāgrēsarāsi bhuvanē putravatīnām । bhavajalāviyānapātraṁ jinavaramudarēṇa vahantī ॥ 61 ॥
iti vinayapravarā vividhaṁ saṁstutya jinēndravarajananīm । jinanāthaṁ garbhasthitaṁ stuvanti tataśca bhaktyā ॥ 62॥
sakalasurāsurakinnaravidyādharanikaranaravarēndrāṇām । svāmin ! śamitabhuvanēāpasargavargāya tubhyaṁ namaḥ ||63 ||
'vaṁ niṣkāraṇakaruṇākarō'si jinanātha ! yadihāvatīrṇaḥ । madhyamōparimayaivēyakādū bhavyānāṁ bōdhārtham ॥64॥
tasmādadya madhyamō'pi khalūtkr̥ṣṭatarō'yaṁ manujalōkaḥ । jātō jina ! tava garbhāvatāratō nāsti sandēhaḥ ॥ 65 ॥
iti vacanaiḥ stutvā jinavaraṁ bhaktinirbharā indrāḥ । nandīśvarē kr̥tvā jinamahamamarālayaṁ prāptāḥ ॥ 66 ॥
ētāni dr̥ṣṭrā sarvōttama cintitārthajanakāni । varadhēnukalpapādapacintāmaṇiguṇa mahārghāṇi ॥ 67 ॥
prābhātikatūryaravapratibuddhā svapnadarśanasamuttham । harṣamivāmāntaṁ vitarati pulakacchalēna bahiḥ ॥ 68 ॥
aal 'namō jinēbhyaḥ' iti bhaṇitrī rajanivirāmasamayē । pracurataraharṣakalitā līlayā muñcati palyaṅkam ॥69॥
tatō'citvā jinēndrapratimāmapratimabhaktisaṁyuktā । saṁstutya ca suviśuddhapravaramudrātrikānugatā || 70 ॥
1 kha.ga. "mya ! 2 kha. ēyaṁ ।

hōhī ēyārisasumiṇadaṁsaṇē tujjha dēvi ! varaputtō । niyaniruvakkavikkamaakkaṁtasamaggariucakkō॥7
ia bhaṇiē bhaṇai taō viasiasayavattasarisavayaṇēṇaṁ । ēvaṁ hōutti jiṁ ṇiṁdasāhupāyappasa ēṇa || 73
tō aṇumayā nivēṇaṁ harisavasuppannapulayakaliaṁgī । mayagalamaṁtharagamaṇā vaccai niyavāsabhavaṇammi ||74

vāhara siṁddhaputtē ahaṁganimittasatthasuviaṭṭhē । muṇiyajiṇavayaṇasārē visāraē suviṇasatthēsu || 76 ||
tō tē viasiya sayavatta kusumamālāvalaṁvivacchathalā | ghaṇasāramīsacaṁdaṇavilittagattā kaṇayaruṇō ॥77

tō āsaṇēsu vimalacchavatthapacchāiēsa. nivasati । bhūvaiṇāṇunnāyā, paḍivattipurassaraṁ saccē ।। 79 ।।
sammāṇiūṇa taṁbōlapupphavatthāiēhiṁ rāyāvi । asamacaudasasumiṇāṇa vaiyaraṁ sāhuē tēsiṁ ॥ 80 ॥
tēvi ya vimhiyāhiyayā bhaṇati ēēsimikkamikkaṁpi । bahupumēhiṁ dīsai kiṁpuna savvēsivalabhō ||8|
jaṁ ēyāī jiṇavarajaṇaṇī aha cakkavaṭṭijaṇaṇī vā । saṁpunnāī picchai iya bhaṇiyaṁ savvadasīhi ॥ 82 ॥
ētyaṁtara mmi nāṇī cāraṇasamaṇō samāgaō tattha । vihiṇā puṭṭhō rannā sumiṇāṇa phalaṁ kahai ēvaṁ ॥ 83
tahāhi ;-
aviralagalaṁtamaya salilamaliṇagaṁḍayaladaṁtidaṁsaṇaō । bahudāṇapavittakarō gayagāmī tuha suō hōhī || 8
atha kathayati kramēṇādbhutasvanānāṁ vyatikaraṁ patyē । ākarṇya sō'pi tataḥ pramuditacittō bhaṇatyēvam ॥ 71
bhaviṣyatyētādr̥śasvapnadarśanēna tava dēvi ! varaputraḥ । nijanirupakramavikramākrāntasamagrariputrakraḥ ॥ 72 ॥
iti bhaṇitē bhaṇati tatō vikasitaśatapatrasadr̥śavadanēna । ēvaṁ bhavatviti jinēndrasādhupādaprasādēna ॥ 73 ॥
tatō'numatā nr̥pēṇa harṣavaśōtpannapulakakalitāṅgī । madakalamantharagamanā vrajati nijavāsabhavanē ॥74॥
rājā ca prabhātē sakalaprabhātakaraṇīyajātakr̥takr̥tyaḥ । āsthānaṁ dattvā bahuvidhanr̥pamantriparikaritaḥ ॥75 ||
āhvayati siddhaputrānaṣṭāṅganimittaśāstrasuvidagdhān । jñātajinavacanasārān viśāradān svapnaśāstrēṣu ||76||
tatastē vikasitaśatapatrakusumamālāvalambivakṣaḥsthalāḥ । ghanasāramiśracandanaviliptagātrāḥ kanakarucayaḥ ॥ 7
akṣataharitālīkalitamaulaya ārdrācchasitavastrāḥ । pratihārasūcitā jalpitvā kalyāṇavacanāni ॥ 78 ॥
tata āsanēṣu vimalācchavastrapracchāditēṣu nivasanti । bhūpatinā'nujñātāḥ, pratipattipurassaraṁ sarvān ॥79॥
sammānya tambōlapuṣpavastrādikai rājāpi । asamacaturdaśasvapnānāṁ vyatikaraṁ kathayati tēbhyaḥ ||80||
tē'pi ca vismitahr̥dayā bhaṇantyētēṣāmēkaikamapi । bahupuṇyairddaśyatē kiṁ punaḥ sarvēṣāmupalambhaḥ ॥ 81 ॥
yadētān jinavarajananyatha cakravartijananī vā । saṁpūrṇān paśyatīti bhaṇitaṁ sarvadarśibhiḥ ॥82॥
atrāntarē jñānī cāraṇaśramaṇaḥ samāgatastatra । vidhinā pr̥ṣṭō rājñā svapnānāṁ phalaṁ kathayatyēvam ॥83॥

jammāpatthāvō ।

37
savarabalasālisuṁdara vasa hunnayakhaṁdhabaṁdhurō dhīrō । sayalasurāsuravasahō vasahō taha vasahadaṁsaṇaō ॥ 85 ॥
bhayarahiō tēyassī duddharisō riugaiṁdaviṁdāṇaṁ । bhavihī kisōyarōvi ya paṁcāṇaṇadaṁsaṇāhitō ॥ 86 ॥
suravaravihiyaṁ suragiri sirammi khīrōyajala hisalilēhiṁ । majjaṇayamaṇubhavissai siriahilēyāvalōēṇaṁ || 87 ॥
hika malubbhava uvaēsa gaṁdhaluddhēhiṁ bhavibhamarēhiṁ । niccaṁ nisēvaṇijjō sumaṇasamālāpalōyaṇaō ॥ 88 ॥
sārayacchaṇasa sivayaṇō bhaviyacaōrāṇa jaṇiyamaṇaharisō। sasidaṁsaṇēṇa hōhī bhaviyaṇakumuyaṣpahāsayarō ।।89
yaṇa sujāla nimma hiyasayalajaṇahiyayamōha timirabharō। kumayagahatēyaharaṇō sahassakiraṇassa pāsaṇaō ॥ 90 ॥
hōyaggapavarapāsāyasiha ra saṁjaṇiyaasamasaṁsōhō । kittipaḍāyākaliō dhauvva sudhayassa pēcchaṇaō ॥91॥
sēvapura patthiyaba hujaṁtusatthapatthāṇamaṁgalaghaḍōvva । maṇavaṁchiyasiddhikarō saccaviē punakalasammi ॥ 92 ॥
hadāhapivāsiyasayalabhaviyanivvuipayāṇadullaliō । paumālaō visālō paumataḍāyassa sumiṇēṇa ॥ 93 ॥
guṇagaṇarayaṇāhārō gabhīrō pavarasattasaṁjuttō । karuṇāmayarasakaliō rayaṇāyaradaṁsaṇē nūṇaṁ ॥ 94 ॥
māṇiyasurathuṇaṇārihō vimāṇāō ittha avayarai । uttattakaṇayavanō pavaravimāṇammi saccavi || 95||
|ilōēva mahagghō dulahō lōyāṇa punnarahiyāṇaṁ । saṁjaṇiyabhuvaṇabhūsō ya rayaṇarāsissa daṁsaṇaō || 96 ||
hiūṇa kammavaṇaṁ sukkajjhāṇānalēṇa sayalaṁpi । bhaviyāṇa niviḍajaḍimaṁ avaṇēi sihimmi diṭṭammi ॥97॥
kē bahuṇā tā hōhī sattamatitthaṁkarō su tumha | dhammavaracakavaṭṭī lōyālōyappayāsayarō ॥ 98 ॥
taviralagalanmadasalilamalinagaṇḍataladantidarśanataḥ । bahudānapavitrakarō gajagāmī tava sutō bhaviṣyati ॥ 84 ॥
[varabalaśālisundaravr̥ṣabhōnnataskandhabandhurō dhīraḥ । sakalasurāsuravr̥ṣabhō vr̥ṣabhastathā vr̥ṣabhadarśanataḥ ॥ 85 ॥
yarahitastējasvī durdharṣō ripugajēndravr̥ndānām । bhaviṣyati kr̥śōdarō'pi ca pañcānanadarśanāt ॥ 86 ॥
suravaravihitaṁ suragiriśirāsē kṣīrōdajalādhisalilaiḥ । majjanakamanubhaviṣyati śrayabhiṣēkāvalōkēna ||27||
dukhakamalōdbhavōpadēśa gandhalubdhairbhavika bhramaraiḥ । nityaṁ niṣēvaṇīyaḥ sumanōmālāpralōkanataḥ ॥ 88 ॥
prāradakṣaṇaśaśivadanō bhavikacakōrāṇāṁ janitamanōharṣaḥ । śaśidarśanēna bhaviṣyati bhavijana kumudaprahāsakaraḥ ॥89॥
cināṁśujālanirmathitasakalajana hr̥dayamōha timirabharaḥ । kumatagrahatē jōharaṇaḥ sahasrakiraṇasya darśanataḥ ॥ 90 ॥
hōkā grapravara prāsādaśikhara saṁjanitāsamasaṁśōbhaḥ । kīrtipatākākalitō dhvaja iva sudhvajasya darśanataḥ ॥ 91 ॥
śivapuraprasthitabahujantusārthaprasthānamaṅgalaghaṭa iva । manōvāñchitasiddhikarō dr̥ṣṭē puṇyakalaśē ॥ 92 ॥
duḥkhadāhapipāsitasakalabhavikanirvr̥tipradānadurlalitaḥ । padmālayō viśālaḥ padmataḍāgasya svapnēna ॥ 93 ॥
guṇagaṇaratnādhārō gambhīraḥ pravarasattvasaṁyuktaḥ । karuṇāmr̥tarasakalitō ratnākaradarśanē nūnam ॥ 94 ॥
mānikasurastavanā vimānādatrāvatarati । uttaptakanakavarṇaḥ pravaravimānē dr̥ṣṭē ॥ 95 ॥
trailōkyē'pi mahārghē durlabhō lōkānāṁ puṇyarahitānām । saṁjanitabhuvanabhūṣaśca ratnarāśērdarśanataḥ ॥ 96 ॥
dagdhvā karmavanaṁ śukladhyānānalēna sakalamapi । bhavikānāṁ nibiḍajīḍamānamapanayati śikhini dr̥ṣṭē ॥97॥
1 ga. pabala ।

38
supāsanāha-cariammi-
āyanniūṇamēvaṁ harisēṇa visajji namasittā । naravaiṇā muṇināhō gaō ya hiyaicchiyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ ॥ 99 ॥
tēsiṁ ca siddhaputtāṇa dāviyaṁ pāritōsiyaṁ daviṇaṁ । āsattapurisasaṁtaidā lida vimadasaṁjaṇayaṁ ॥ 100 ॥
ētō dēvībhavaṇaṁ gaṁtūṇaṁ sāhiyaṁ mahīvaiṇā । caudasasumiṇāṇa phalaṁ jaha kahiyaṁ tēhiṁ savisēsa ॥ 101 ॥
sōūṇa sumiṇavivaraṇamullasiyāsamapamōyajuttāē । suraramaṇisarisavāṁtavivbhamāē taō tīsē ॥ 102 ॥
titthayarapabhāvēṇaṁ dūrayaravilīṇarōyaniyarāē । parivaḍhi umārō ganbhō saha dēhakaṁtī ॥ 103 ॥
aha sōhi pattā dēvī gavbhappabhāvaō ahiyaṁ । khīrōyajala hivēlavya pavaramuttāhalasaṇāhā ॥ 104॥
aṁtasthaḍiviviyaugamaṁtanavataraṇikiraṇavicchuriyā । tiyasāyalanimmalakaṇayasāṇubhittivva airui ।। 105
anyaṁtarapāunbhuyaasamasa simaṁḍalā nahasirivva । phalihadharaṇīva aṁtaranihittavara rayaṇapavbhārā ॥ 106 ॥
sughaṇapayōhara maṁḍala parimaṁḍiyagayaṇa vimalavacchayalā । ullasiyālāyāvalayahāsirī pāusasirivva ।। 107 ।।
iya gabhaṭṭhiyajiṇavarapabhāvavarddhata kaṁtasavvaṁgā । rēhai navakampa malaiyavva maṇōharā • dēvī || 108 ||
ae ausget fre iṁdā ēsēṇa dhaṇavaiṣpamuhā | muṁcati jakkhaniyarā maṇirayaṇasuvannadaviṇabharaṁ ॥ 109 ॥
bahuvihamaṇunnabhōgaṁgasaṁcayaṁ taha pasatthavatthāṇi । vivihābharaṇāṇi ya kiraṇajālaka liyāṇi vikiraṁti ।। 110 ।।
avaṇiti vāudēvī kayacaraṁ tattha tammi samayammi । gaṁdhōyayadhārādhōraṇīē varisaṁti taha mēhā ॥ 111॥
savvāvi riusirīō muṁcati samaṁtaō kusumabuddhiṁ । āyarisaṁ daṁsaṁti ya jōisiyāṇaṁ puraṁdhīō ||112||
kiṁ bahunā tasmādbhaviṣyati saptamatīrthaṅkaraḥ sutastava । dharmavaracakravartī lōkālōkaprakāśakaraḥ ॥ 98 ॥
ākaṇyaivaṁ harṣēṇa visr̥jya namasthitvā । narapatinā munināthō gataśca hr̥dayēpsitaṁ sthānam ॥ 99 ॥
tēbhyaśca siddhaputrēbhyō dāpitaṁ pāritōṣikaṁ draviṇam । āsaptapuruṣasaṁtatidāridryavimardasaṁjanakam ॥100॥
itō dēvībhavanaṁ gatvā kathitaṁ mahīpatinā । caturdaśasvapnānāṁ phalaṁ yathā kathitaṁ taiḥ saviśēṣam ॥101॥
śrutvā svapnavivaraṇamullasitāsamapramōdayuktāyāḥ । suraramaṇīsadr̥śavardhamānavibhramāyāstatastasyāḥ ॥102॥
tīrthakaraprabhāvēṇa dūrataravilīnarōganikarāyāḥ । parivardhitumārabdhō garbhaḥ saha dēhakāntyā ॥ 103 ॥
atha śōbhituṁ pravr̥ttā dēvī garbhaprabhāvatō'dhikam । kṣīrōdajaladhivēlēva pravaramuktāphalasanāthā ॥ 104 ॥
antaḥpratibimbitōdgacchannavataraṇikiraṇavicchuritā । tridaśācalanirmalakanakasānubhittirivātirucirā ॥ 105॥
ābhyantaraprādurbhūtāsamaśaśimaṇḍalā namaḥ śrīriva । sphaṭikavaraṇirivāntarnihitavararatnaprāgbhārā ॥ 106 ॥
sughanapayōdhara maṇḍalaparimaṇḍitagaganavimalavakṣastalā | ullasitabalākāvalyahrāsavatī prāvr̥vi ॥ 107॥
iti garbhasthitajinavaraprabhāvavardhamāna kāntasarvāṅgā । rājatē navakalpadrumalatikēva manōharā dēvī ॥ 108 ॥
atha supratiṣṭhasya gr̥hē indrādēśēna dhanapatipramukhāḥ । muñcanti yakṣanikarā maṇiratnasuvarṇa draviṇabharam ॥ 109 ॥
bahuvidhamanōjñabhōgāṅgasaṁcayaṁ tathā praśastavastrāṇi । vividhābharaṇāni ca kiraṇajāla kalitāni vikiranti ॥ 110 ॥
apanayanti vāyudēvyastr̥ṇādyutkaraṁ tatra tasmin samayē । gandhōdakadhārāghōraṇyā varṣanti tathā mēghāḥ ॥ 111 ॥
1 ga. mēyaṁ ।

jammāipatthāvō |
36
vaṁtaravēmāṇiyabhuvaṇavāsidēvāṇa pavararamaṇīō । dēviṁ dhuṇaṁti bhattīē sāsaṇaṁ taha paḍicchaṁti ।। 113 ।।
jiṇajaṇaṇīē puraō disidēvīō dasāvi gāyaṁti । vīṇāvēṇumuyaṁga | imahurajhuṇi maṇaharaṁ gēyaṁ ॥ 114 ॥
kiṁ bahuṇā;
jaya-jīva-naṁda - iccāikōmalālāvapēsalāhiṁ sayā । sēvijjai cēḍīhiṁva suraramaṇīhiṁ puidēvī ।। 115 ॥
picchaṁtī naḍanāḍayapicchaṇayāī kayāi, karuṇāē । viyaraṁtī dutthiyāṇaṁ kayāvi tavaṇijjapuṁjāī ॥ 116 ॥
āyanaṁtīya purāṇapurisacariyāī savaṇasuhāī । kaiyāvi nayarasōhaṁ picchaṁtī sahiyaṇāṇugayā | 117॥
kuṇamāṇī kaśyāvi ya niyabaṁdhuvahūjaṇassa parihāsaṁ । kaiyāvi dhammasaṁbaddha kahā viyāraṁ nisāmitī ॥ 118 ॥
parivālai taṁ garbhaṁ nō aiuṇhēhiṁ nāimahurēhiṁ । nō aitittēhiṁ nāiaṁbilēhiṁ na kahiṁ ॥ 119 ॥
nō sāhiṁ na yāisī ēhiṁ nāilavaṇēhiṁ । savvōuyasuhaēhiṁ āhārēhiṁ puhaidēvī ॥ 120 ॥
saṁpunnammiya samaē supaṭṭamahānivassa rajjammi । jaṇayaṁtī kallāṇaṁ paripūriyasayaladōhēlayā ॥ 121 ॥
jisa vārasīē siyāē rayaṇīē duiyajāmammi । sattamatularāṁsīē supavittammiya muhuttammi || 122॥
uccāṭiēsa ravimaṁgalasukkabuhara visurasu । sōmammi visāhatthē kiṁdiyaṭhāṇaṭṭhiyagurummi ॥ 123 ॥
bīyantra navasakaṁ ahiṇavamuttāhalaṁ sumuttivva । suragiridharavva navakappapāyanaṁ pasaviyā putaṁ ॥ 124॥
taṁ daṇaṁ tihuyaṇadivāyaraṁ tēyakaṁtiparikaliyaṁ । puvvadisā viva viyasiyamuhakamalā rēhaē dēvī ।। 125
sarvā api r̥tuśriyō muñcanti samantataḥ kusumavr̥ṣṭim । ādarśa darśayanti ca jyōtiṣkāṇāṁ purandhrayaḥ ॥ 112 ॥
vyantaravaimānikabhuvanavāsidēvānāṁ pravararamaṇyaḥ । dēvīṁ stuvanti bhaktyā śāsanaṁ tathā pratīcchanti ॥ 113 ॥
jinajananyāḥ puratō digdēvyō daśāpi gāyanti । vīṇāvēṇumr̥daṅgādimadhuradhvani manōharaṁ gēyam ॥ 114 ॥
kiṁ bahunā;
"
jaya-jīva-nandētyādikōmalālāpapēśalābhiḥ sadā । sēvyatē cēṭībhiriva suraramaṇībhiḥ pr̥thivīdēvī ॥115॥
paśyantī naṭanāṭaka prēkṣaṇakāni kadācit karuṇayā । vitarantī duḥkhitēbhyaḥ kadāpi tapanīyapuñjān ॥ 116 ॥
ākarṇayantī ca purāṇapuruṣacaritāni śravaṇasukhadāni । kadāpi nagaraśōbhāṁ paśyantī sakhījanānugatā ॥ 117 ॥
kurvāṇā kadāpi ca nijabandhuvadhūjanasya parihāsam । kadāpi dharmasaṁbaddhakathāvicāraṁ niśāmyantī ॥118॥
paripālayati taṁ garbhaṁ nō atyuṣṇairnātimadhuraiḥ । nō atitiktairnātyānē kaṭukaiḥ ॥ 119॥
nō atikaṣāyakairna cātiśītairnātilavaṇaiḥ । sarvartuka sukhadairāhāraiḥ pr̥thivīdēvī ॥ 120॥
saṁpūrṇē ca samayē supratiṣṭhamahānr̥pasya rājyē । janayantī kalyāṇaṁ paripūritasakaladōhadā ॥ 121 ॥
jyēṣṭhasya dvādaśyāṁ sitāyā rajanyā dvitīyayāmē । saptamatulārāśau supavitrē ca muhūrtē ॥122॥
uccasthānasthitēṣu ravimaṅgalaśukrabudharavisutēṣu । sōmē viśākhāstha kēndrasthānasthitagurau ॥ 123 ॥
dvitīyēva navaśaśāṅkamabhinavamuktāphalaṁ khuśuktiriva । suragiridharēva navakalpapādapaṁ prasūtā putram ॥ 124॥
2 ga. ḍōha । 2 ya, rāsimmi ।

supāsanāha - cariammi-
aitthaṁtarammi sahasā ānaṁdiyasayala tihuaṇābhōyaṁ । maṁdō sisirō surahī gayaṇē paviyaṁbhiō pavaṇō ॥ 126 ॥
sacarācarajaṁtūṇaṁ aisuhaō garuyavimhayakarō ya । saṁbhūō naraēsuvi khaṇamitrōṇaṁ samujjōō || 127||
pamajjiyaṁva dharaṇīē maṁḍalaṁ taha pahaṁjaṇasurēhiṁ । uvasaṁtarēṇuniyaraṁ ghaṇēhiṁ gaṁdhōdayaṁ buddhaṁ ॥ 128 ॥
uudēvīō kusumāṇa paṁcavannāṇa paramuvaṇiti । samakālamaggidēvīō dīvaē tattha dīvaṁti ॥ 129॥
suparaṭṭhanivaibhavaṇē dhaṇayāē sēṇa jaṁbhagasurāvi । vararayaṇakaṇayavasaṇābharaṇasamūhaṁ ca varisaṁti ॥ 130 ॥
dēvēhi dēvīhi iṁtēhi paḍiniyattamāṇēhiṁ । vāṇārasīvi jāyā tavvēlaṁ amaranayarivva ॥ 131 ॥
ētō ya sūikammāvasaraṁ muṇiūṇa ōhināṇēṇaṁ । aṭṭha disākumarīō ahalōgāō tahiṁ iṁti ॥ 132॥
pavaravimāṇārūḍhā causāmāṇiyasahassa pariyariyā | aṇiāhivēhi sattahiṁ sattahiṁ aṇiēhiṁ saṁjuttā ॥ 133॥
amarakarikuṁbhavibbhramapaōharābharaṇabhūsiyasarīrā । jiṇajaṇaṇisamīvaṁ takkhaṇēṇa ēyāō saṁpattā ॥ 134 ॥
taṁ jahā;--
1
bhōgakarā bhōgavaī subhōgā bhōgamāliṇī । tōyadhārā vicittā ya puṣpamālā aṇidiyā ॥ 135 ॥
ti payāhiṇīkarēḍaṁ jiṇavarajaṇaṇi parāē bhattīē । savvāōvi samakālaṁ dhuṇaṁti kalakōilaravēṇaṁ ।। 136 ॥
kahaṁ viya;
namimō tihuyaṇaramaṇīsirabhūsaṇarayaṇavibhamē dēvi । payakamalaṁ kōmalalaliya aṁgulīpavaradalakaliyaṁ ॥ 137॥
taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā tribhuvanadivākaraṁ tējaḥ kāntiparikalitam । pūrvadigiva vikasitamukhakamalā rājatē dēvī || 125 ॥
atrāntarē sahasā''nanditasakala tribhuvanābhāgam । mandaḥ śiśiraḥ surabhirgaganē pravijr̥mbhitaḥ pavanaḥ ॥ 126॥
sacarācarajantūnāmatisukhadō guruvismayakaraśca । saṁbhūtō narakēṣvapi kṣaṇamātrēṇa samudyōtaḥ ॥ 127॥
pramārjitamiva dharaṇyā maṇḍalaṁ tathā prabhañjanasuraiḥ । upaśāntarēṇunikaraṁ dhanairgandhōdakaṁ vr̥ṣṭam ॥128॥
r̥tudēvyaḥ kusumānāṁ pañcavarṇānāṁ prakaramupanayanti । samakālamagnidēvyō dīpakāṁstatra dīpayanti ॥ 129॥
supratiṣṭhanr̥patibhavanē dhanapādēśēna jr̥mbhakasurā api । vararatnakanakavasanābharaṇasamūhaṁ ca varṣanti ॥ 130 ॥
dēvairdēvībhirāyadbhiḥ pratinivartamānaiḥ । vāṇārasyapi jātā tadvēlamamaranagarīva ॥ 131 ॥
•
itaśca sūtikarmāvasaraṁ jñātvāvadhijñānēna । aṣṭa dikkumāryō'dhōlōkāt tatrāyanti ॥ 132 ॥
pravara vimānārūḍhāścatuḥ sāmānikasaha rūparikaritāḥ । anīkādhipaiḥ saptabhiḥ saptabhiranīkaiḥ saṁyuktāḥ ॥ 133॥
amarakarikumbhavibhramapayōdharābharaṇabhūṣitaśarīrāḥ । jinajananīsamīpaṁ tatkṣaṇēnaitāḥ saṁprāptāḥ ॥ 134 ॥
tadyathā;-
.
bhōgakarā bhōgavatī subhōgā bhōgamālinī । tōyadhārā vicitrā ca puṣpamālā'ninditā ॥ 135 ॥
triḥ pradakṣiṇīkr̥tya jinavarajananīṁ parayā bhaktyā । sarvā api samakālaṁ stuvanti kalakōkilaravēṇa ॥ 136 ॥
kathamiva;

jammāpatthāyō ।
41
bhāsaṁsāraṁ dasa suvidisāsu paribhrama nirbharaṁ dēvi । sarayanisāyara hara hasiyahāradhavalō jasō tujjha ॥ 138 ॥
tumacciya saṁpattā rēhā majjhammi puttavaṁtīṇa । jīē niyauyarēṇa ubbūḍhō sattamajirṇō ॥ 139 ॥
iya muiraṁ jiṇajaṇaṇi namiuṁ jaṁpati gurupamōēṇa । na hu dēvi ! bhāiyavtraṁ jaṁ amhē disikumārīō ॥ 140 ॥
ēyassa sayalabhuvaṇikkasāmiṇō jiṇavarassa bhattīē । niyaahigāraṇurūvaṁ jammaṇamahimaṁ vihissāmō || 141 ॥
iya aṇujāṇāvēḍaṁ jiṇajammaṇabhavaṇacaudisiṁ vihiyaṁ । jōyaṇamittaṁ khittaṁ vavagayataṇakaṭṭharayapattaṁ ॥ 142॥
takkhaṇaviubviṇaṁ saṁvagavāuṇā samaggapi । duggaṁdhaṁ avaṇēuṁ jiṇajaṇaṇīē adūrammi || 143 ।।
gāyaṁtīu guruharisaviyasiyacchīō tattha cidvaṁti । ēvaṁ uḍhadisā ōvi dēvīō iti ēyāō ।। 144 ।।
1
mērā mēhavaī sumēhā mēhamāliṇī । suvacchā vacchamittā ya vārisēṇā balāhagā || 145 ।।
tō vēḍabbiyamēṇa mahiyalaṁ nihayarēṇuyaṁ kāuṁ । sōrabbhaguṇāyadviyabhamaraulaṁ pupphavarisaṁ ca ।। 146 ॥ -
titthayaraguṇasamūhaṁ aimahurasarēṇa savaṇasuharaṇa । āsannammi ṭhiyāō gāyaṁti guruppamōēṇaṁ ॥ 147 ॥
aha pōra cchimaruyagāō aha dēvīu disikumārīō । niyapariyaṇasahiyāō ēyāō āgayā tattha ॥ 148 ॥
naṁduttarā yē naṁdā ānaṁdā naṁdivarddhaṇā । vijayā ya vējayaṁtī jayaṁtī cāparājiyā ॥ 149 ॥
diṇahara vivasaricchaṁ karē karēūṇadapaṇaṁ vimalaṁ । puvvadisi saṁṭhiyāō gāyaṁti guṇē jiṇidassa ॥ 150 ॥
aha dāhiṇaruyagāō ēvaṁciya aṭṭha disikumārīō । muṇiyajiṇajammaṇāō ēyāu samāgayāu tarhi ।। 151 ॥
namā māstribhuvana ramaṇī śirōbhūṣaṇaratnavibhramē ! dēvi ! । pādakamalaṁ kōmalalālitāṅgulipravaradalakalitam ||37||
āsaṁsāraṁ daśasvapi dikṣu paribhrāmyatu nirbharaṁ dēvi ! । śaranniśākaraharahasitahāraghavalaṁ yaśastava ॥ 138 ॥
tvayaiva saṁprāptā rēkhā madhyē putravatīnām । yayā nijōdarēṇōdvayūḍhaḥ saptamajinēndraḥ ॥ 139 ॥
iti suciraṁ jinajananīṁ natvā jalpanti gurupramōdēna । na khalu dēvi ! bhētavyaṁ yad vayaṁ dikkumāryaḥ ॥ 140 ॥
ētasya sakalabhuvanaikasvāminō jinavarasya bhaktyā | nijādhikārānurūpaṁ janmamahaṁ vidhāsyāmaḥ ॥ 141 ॥
ityanujñāpya jinajanmabhavanacaturdikṣu vihitam | yōjanamātraṁ kṣētraṁ vyapagatatr̥ṇakāṣṭharajaḥ patram ॥142॥
tatkṣaṇa vikurvitēna saṁvartakavāyunā samagramapi । durgandhamapanīya jinajananyā adūrē || 143 ||
gāyantyō guruharṣavikasitākṣyastatra tiṣṭhanti । ēvamūrdhvadiśō'pi dēvya āyantyētāḥ ॥ 144 ॥
mērā mēghavatī sumēdhā mēghamālinī । suvatsā vatsamātrā ca vāriṣēṇā balāhakā ॥ 145॥
tatō vikurvitamēghēna mahītalaṁ nihatarēṇukaṁ kr̥tvā । saurabhyaguṇa kr̥ṣṭabhramarakulaṁ puṣpavarṣē ca ॥146॥
tīrthakara guṇasamūhamatimadhurasvarēṇa śravaṇasukhadēna । āsanē sthitā gāyanti gurupramōdēna ॥ 147 ॥
atha paurastyacakādaṣṭa dēvyō dikkumāryaḥ । nijaparijanasahitā ētā āgaṁtāstatra ॥148॥
nandōttarā ca nandā''nandā nandivardhanā । vijayā ca vaijayantī jayantī cāparājitā ॥ 149 ॥

samāhārā pannā ya suppabuddhā jasōharā । lacchīvaī bhōgavaī cittaguttā vasuṁdharā ।। 152 ।।
karakamalē kaliūṇaṁ bhiṁgāraṁ sura hisa lilapaḍipunaṁ । pahuṇō dāhiṇāsē ṭhiyāō gāyaṁti guṇaniyaraṁ ।। 153 ॥

dēvī surādēvī puhaī umāvaī ( tahā ? ) । ēganāsā'navamiyā bhaddā'sōyā ya aṭṭamā || 155 ॥

aha vidisiruyagaparivāsiṇīō cattāri disikumārīō । cittā ya cittakaṇayā sutērasōyāmaṇīnāmā 16
namiūṇa puhaidēvi ṭhāuṁ vidisāsu causuvi kamēṇa । suṁdara paī vahatthā gāyaṁti jiṇassa guṇanivahaṁ ॥ 169॥
majjhimaruyagaṭṭiīō disākumārīō iṁti cattāri । taṁ jaha rūm̐yā ruyaṁsā sukhyā ruyagāvaīnāmā ॥ 162॥
tatthāgatuṁ nāhīnālaṁ kappaṁti jiṇavariṁdassa । cauraṁgulāu uddhaṁ khaṇaṁti tattō ya varavivaraṁ ।। 163 ॥
taṁ tattha nāhinālē ṭhaviūṇa paṁcavaṇṇarayaṇēhiṁ । pūriti taduvariṁ tō syaṁti hariyālagurupīṭhaṁ || 164 ||

"samāhārā pradattā ca suprabuddhā yaśōdharā । lakṣmīvatī bhōgavatī citraguptā vasundharā ॥152॥
karakamalē kalayitvā bhr̥ṅgāraṁ surabhisalilaparipūrṇam । prabhōdakṣiṇapārśvē sthitā gāyanti guṇanikaram ॥ 153॥
atha paścimarucakasthitāḥ pravaravimānēna dikkumāryaḥ । aṣṭaiva bhaktibharanirbharā ētāḥ praviśanti ॥ 154 ॥
ilādēvī surādēvī pr̥thivī padmāvatī । ēkanāsā'navamikā bhadrā'śōkā cāṣṭamī ॥ 155 ॥
karakamalakalitasuviśālatālavr̥ntā dīrghākṣyaḥ । paścimadiksthitāḥ stuvanti tīrthakaraguṇanivaham ॥156॥
athauttarāharucakē vāstavyā dikkumāryaḥ । aṣṭaivāgatāstasṇa pragalbhā ētāḥ ॥ 197॥
vāruṇī puṇḍarīkā ca miśrakēśā'lambukā । āśā sarvaprabhā caiva hrīdēvī śrīstathā ॥ 158॥
karakamalakalitasitacāmarā uttaradiśi dēvasya । natvā pr̥thivīdēvī pūrvakramēṇa ca tiṣṭhanti ॥ 199॥
atha vidigurucakaparivāsinyaścatasrō dikkumāryaḥ । citrā ca citrakanakā sutērā-saudāmanīnāmānau ॥ 160 ॥
natvā pr̥thivīdēva sthitvā vidikṣu catasr̥ṣvavi kramēṇa । sundarapradīpahastā gāyanti jinasya guṇanivaham ॥ 169॥
madhyamarucakasthitayō dikkumārya āyanti catasraḥ । tadyathā rucā rucāṁśā surucā rucakāvatīnāmā || 162 ||
tatrāgatya nābhinālaṁ kalpayanti jinavarēndrasya । caturaṅgulādūrdhvaṁ khananti tataśca caravivaram ॥ 163 ॥
tat tatra nābhinālaṁ sthāpayitvā pañcavarṇaratnaiḥ । pūrayanti tadupari tatō racayanti haritālagurupīṭham ॥ 164 ॥
tadanantaraṁ cātimanōharāṇi kadalīgr̥hāṇi trīṇyēva । vikurvya tēṣāṁ ca madhyabhāgē ramyāṇi ॥ 169॥

paṁcappayāra maṇirayaṇara iyakuṭṭimatalāī viulāī । dārappaēsasaṁṭhaviyakaṇayamayapunnakalasāī || 166 ||
uddāmakhvavarasālahaṁ jiyārēhirāī viśyaṁti । uttaradāhiṇapuvvāsu tinni causālabhavaṇāī || 167॥
tēsiṁ ca majjhabhāgē mahamyamaṇikhaṁḍamaṁḍiyatalāī । niyakiraṇajālaviraiyasuriṁdakōdaṁḍa daṁḍāī ॥ 168 ॥
varakaṇayapavvayasilāvitthinnāī ṭhavaṁti tibhēva । sīhāsaṇāī tattō titthayaraṁ garuyabhattīē || 169 ॥
karayala puḍēṇa dhittuṁ jiṇavarajaṇaṇiṁ ca dāhiṇadisimmi । nisiyāvitiya varacā usālasīhāsaṇē tattō ।। 170
abbhaṁgaṁti sarīraṁ sayapāgasahassapāgatēllēhiṁ । tēsiṁ pahāṇagaṁdhuddharēhiṁ paramaṇyamōēṇa || 171 ॥
uvvaṭṭiūṇa ubhayaṁ sugaṁdhaubvaṇēṇa ēmēva । puvvābhimuhē causālapavarasīhāsaṇē viḍaṁ ॥ 172 ॥
gaṁdhōdaraṇa puṣphōdaēṇa suddhōdaēṇa hāviṁti । pavaramaṇirayaṇakaṇayābharaṇēhiṁ taō vibhūsiṁti || 173 ||
uttaradisimmi causāla vijala siṁhāsaṇē nivēsēuṁ । saṁtinimittaṁ hōmaṁ karaṁti gōsīsadārūhiṁ ॥। 174 ॥
niyaya pabhāvaparirakkhiyassavi jiṇassa jīyamēyaṁti । kāūṇa pavararakkhāpuṭṭaliyaṁ baṁdhayaṁti taō।। 175 ।।
tārḍiti savaṇamūlē rayaṇutralē ērisaṁ vayaṁtīō । sattakulapavvayāū appaḍihayasāsaṇō havasu ।। 176 ।।
paṇayajaṇa pūriyāsō dūrayarapalīṇarōyasōgō ya । iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ jammaṇagēhammi ṭhaviṁti jiṇajaṇaṇi ॥177॥
tattō mahurasarēṇa gāyaṁti jidibhūriguṇanivahaṁ । harisēṇa samalliyaṁti puhaidēvīsamīvammi || 178 ॥
iya jassa jammakiccaṁ jiṇassa chappannadisikumārīhiṁ | lahumēva samatthijjai bhattīē paramaharisēṇaṁ ॥ 179 ॥
pañcaprakāramaṇiratnaracitakuṭṭimatalāni vipulāni । dvārapradēśasaṁsthāpitakanakamaya puṇyakalaśāni ॥ 166॥ -
uddāmarūpavaraśālabhañjikārājamānāni viracayanti । uttaradakṣiṇapūrvāsu trīṇi catuḥśālabhavanāni ॥ 167॥
tēṣāṁ ca madhyabhāgē mahārghamaṇikhaṇḍamaṇḍitatalāni । nijakiraṇajālaviracitasurēndrakōdaṇḍadaṇḍāni ॥ 168॥
varakanakaparvataśilāvistīrṇāni sthāpayanti trīṇyēva । siṁhāsanāni tatastīrthakaraṁ gurubhaktyā ॥ 169 ॥
karatalapuṭēna gr̥hītvā jinavarajananīṁ ca dakṣiṇadiśi । niṣādayanti ca varacatuḥśāla siṁhāsanē tataḥ ॥ 170 ॥
abhyaṅganti śarīraṁ śatapākasahasrapākatailaiḥ । tayōḥ pradhānagandhōddhuraiḥ paramapramōdēna ॥ 171 ॥
udvr̥tyōbhayaṁ sugandhōdvartanēnaivamēva । pūrvābhimukhaṁ catuḥśālapravarasiṁhāsanē sthāpayitvā ॥ 172॥
gandhōdakēna puṣpōdakēna śuddhōdakēna snapayanti । pravaramaṇiratna kana kābharaṇaistatō vibhūṣayanti ॥ 173 ॥
uttaradiśi catuḥśāla vipula siṁhāsanē nivēśya । śāntinimittaṁ hōmaṁ kurvanti gōśīrṣadārubhiḥ ॥ 174॥
nijaka prabhāparirakṣitasyāpi jinasya jītamētaditi । kr̥tvā pravararakṣāpōṭṭalikāṁ badhnanti tataḥ ॥ 175 ॥
tāḍayanti śravaṇamūlē ratnōpalānīdr̥śaṁ vadantyaḥ । saptakulaparvatāyurapratihataśāsanō bhavatāt ॥176॥
praṇatajanapūritāśō dūratarapralīnarōgaśōkaśca । iti bhaṇitvā janmagēhē sthāpayanti jinajananīm ॥ 177॥
tatō madhurasvarēṇa gāyanti jinēndrabhūriguṇanivaham । harṣēṇa samupasarpanti pr̥thivīdēvīsamīpē || 178 ॥
iti yasya janmakr̥tyaṁ jinasya ṣaṭpañcāśaddikkumārābhiḥ । ladhvēva samarthyatē bhaktyā paramaharṣēṇa ॥ 179 ॥

ētyaṁtara mmi sōhammaṣpa sāmissa suravariṁdassa | sīhāsaṇaṁ pakaṁpai takkaṁpēṇaṁ taō sahasā || 180 ॥
aivihiō suriṁdō rōsāruṇalōyaṇō vicitē । naṇu kassa saggalacchī paraṁmuhī saṁpayaṁ jāyā । ॥ 189 ॥
kō vā kayaṁ tadujjayakaḍakkhavikkhēva gōyaraṁ pattō । gamaṇamaṇō vā salahuvva vajjajālāsu kō majjha ।। 182 ॥
kō vā nimajjaṇamaṇō agāhavasaṇōpahimmi dubbuddhī | saṁcāliyaṁ thiraṁpi hu jēṇa sīhāsaṇaṁ majjha ।। 183 ||
iya ciṁtāku liyamaṇō disidasayaṁ jā palōyamāṇōvi । na hu kiṁpi niyai puraō puṇōvi tā citaē sakkō । 184।
kiṁ majjha catraṇakālō aha sōvi na saṁpayaṁ ghaḍai jamhā | kaṁpēi nāmaratarū na parimilāyaṁti kusumāṇi 185
ajjavi ya na hu viraccai sacījaṇō nēya phurai dīṇattaṁ । na nimēsiṇī ya diṭṭī vatthāṇi ya nēya maliṇāṇi 186
iya jā aṇappakku viyappasaṁkulō niyai avahināṇēṇa । tā sīhāsaṇakaṁpikakāraṇaṁ muṇai jiṇa jammaṁ ।। 187 ||
tā uṭṭhēuṁ sīhāsaṇāu gaṁtuṁ payāī sattaṭṭa । tattha ṭhiōvi hu sakatthaēṇa harisēṇa thuṇai jiṇaṁ ॥ 188 ||
siṁhāsanē niṇṇō puṇōvi ciṁtēi suravaī ēvaṁ | haddhī aciṁtaṇīyaṁ picchasu paricitiyaṁ pāvaṁ ॥ 189 ॥
tō āṇavē harisēṇa suracamūsāmiyaṁ tiyasanāhō । bhō sōhammasabhāē gaṁtūṇa lahuṁpi tikhuttō ॥ 190 ॥
mēhōhagahiraghōsa jōyaṇaivittaṁ sughōsavaraghaṁṭaṁ । tāḍēūṇaṁ mahayā ravēṇa ghōsēha taha ēvaṁ ॥ 19 ॥
bhārahakhittē sattamatitthayarō saṁpayaṁ samuppannō । vāṇārasīē sakkō caliō sē jammamahimatthaṁ ॥ 192॥
tō bhō dēvā ! tunbhē savvālaṁkārabhūsiyā savvē । savvēhiṁ nāḍaēhiṁ savvavalēṇaṁ ca saṁjuttā ॥ 193 ||
atrāntarē saudharmakalpasvāminaḥ suravarēndrasya । siṁhāsanaṁ prakampatē tatkampēna tataḥ sahasā ॥ 180 ॥
ativismitaḥ surēndrō rōṣāruṇalōcanō vicintayati । nanu kasya svargalakṣmīḥ parāṅmukhī sāṁprataṁ jātā ? ।। 181 ॥
kō vā kr̥tāntadurjayakaṭākṣavikṣēpagōcaraṁ prāptaḥ । gamanamanā vā śalabha iva vajrajvālāsu kō mama ? || 182 ॥
kō vā nimajjanamanā agādhavyasanōdadhau durbuddhiḥ । saṁcālitaṁ sthiramapi hi yēna siṁhāsanaṁ mama ? || 183॥
iti cintākulitamanā digdaśakaṁ yāvat pralōkamānō'pi । na hi kimapi paśyati purataḥ punarapi tataścintayati śakraḥ ।।
kiṁ mama yavanakālō'tha sō'pi na sāṁprataṁ ghaṭatē yasmāt । kampatē nāmaratarurna parimlāyanti kusumāni ॥185॥
adyāpi ca na hi virajyatē śacījanō naiva sphurati dīnatvam । na nimēṣiṇī ca dr̥āṣṭarvastrāṇi ca naiva malināni ॥ 186॥
iti yāvadanalpakuvikalpasaṁkulaḥ paśyatyavadhijñānēna । tāvatsiṁhāsanakampaikakāraṇaṁ jānāti jinajanma ॥ 187 ॥
tata utthāya siṁhāsanād gatvā padāni saptāṣṭa । tatra sthitō'pi hi śakrastavēna harṣēṇa stīti jinam ॥ 188॥
siṁhāsanē niṣaṇṇaḥ punarapi cintayati surapatirēvam। hā dhigacintanīyaṁ paśya paricintitaṁ pāpam ॥ 189 ॥
tata ājñapayati harṣēṇa suracamūsvāminaṁ tridaśanāthaḥ । bhōḥ saudharmasabhāyāṁ gatvā ladhvapi triḥ ॥ 190॥
mēghaughagabhīraghōṣāṁ yōjanavr̥ttāṁ sughōṣāvaraghaṇṭām । tāḍayitvā mahatā ravēṇa ghōṣayata tathaivam ॥191॥
bhāratakṣētrē saptamatīrthakaraḥ sāṁprataṁ samutpannaḥ । vārāṇasyāṁ śakraścalitastasya janmamahimārtham ॥ 192॥
tatō bhō dēvāḥ ! yūyaṁ sarvālaṅkārabhūṣitāḥ sarvē । sarvainārṭakai: sarvabalēna ca saṁyuktāḥ ॥193॥

taha savvavibhūīē āruhiuṁ pavaraniyarimāṇāī । divvaccharāhiṁ sahiyā sēkasayāsa lahu ēha ॥ 194 ॥
iyaṁ tiyasanāhavayaṇaṁ sōuṁ viṇaēṇa suracamūsāmī । turiyagaī gaṁtūṇaṁ sōhammasabhāē tikhuttō ॥ 195॥
tāḍa sughōraṁ tīsē ghaṇaghōsapaḍiravavasēṇaṁ । annāṇavi ghaṁṭā battīsa sayasahassāī ॥ 196 ॥
ēguṇagāī samakālamēva kāuṁ raṇajjhaṇārāvaṁ । pāraddhāraṁ tappaḍiravōvi samagaṁ samucchaliō ॥197॥
ētthaṁtaram paṁcavihavisayasēvāpamatta cittāvi । dēvā tamēgakālaṁ vajjiraghaṁṭāsaraṁ sōuṁ ॥ 198 ॥
ciṁtaṁti kiṁ viṭṭaṁta caṁḍavaṁ bhaṁḍabhaṁḍayasa rakhō । rayaṇamayavimāṇāvalipaḍiphalaṇēṇaṁ pavitthari ॥ 199 ॥
niṇijjaṁtō saṁbuddhamuddhahiyayāhiṁ amararamaṇīhiṁ । hā nāha ! rakkha rakkhatti jaṁpirīhiṁ bhayavasēṇaṁ ॥ 200 ॥
daṇuyavavahaharisiyatiyasasuhaḍagalagajjibhīsaṇō bhuvaṇē । savvattōvi viyaṁbhai ghaṁṭāṇaṁ raṇaraṇārāvō ॥ 201 ॥
iya ciṁtāē siḍhiliyamāṇiṇigādāvagūḍhakaṁṭhammi । saṁjāē suranivahē savvattō mūḍhahiyayammi || 202॥
uvasaṁtē ya khaṇēṇaṁ samaggagaṁbhīraghaṁṭanigghōsē । avahiyasurāṇa surarāyasāsaṇaṁ kahai ēsa taō || 203॥
iya nāuṁ hariṇagavēsivayaṇaō jammamajjaṇaṁ pahuṇō । viṣphuriyapamōyabharā tō saṁvihiuṁ samāraddhā ॥ 204॥
gaṁtū majjaṇakēlidīhiyaṁ aha kuṇaṁti majjaṇayaṁ । kappūramīsacaṁdaṇarasēṇa dēhaṁ vilipaṁti ॥ 205 ||
dūsajuyaṁ nimmalakōmalaṁ ca parihaṁti kaṁtikamaṇīyaṁ । kaṁṭhapaiṭṭiyahārā durujjhiyakāmuyaviyārā ॥ 206 ॥
varakaḍayatuḍiyamaṇimauḍa kiraṇavicchuriyasayalagayaṇayalā । niyarūtramaḍappharahasiyakusumabāṇā taō caliyā।।
tathā sarvavibhūtyā''ruhya pravara nijāvamānāni । divyāpsarōbhiḥ sahitāḥ śakrasakāśaṁ ladhvēta ॥ 194॥
iti tridaśanāthavacanaṁ śrutvā vinayēna suracamūsvāmī । tvaritagatirgatvā saudharmasabhāyāṁ triḥ ॥195॥
tāḍayati sughōṣāghaṇṭāṁ tasyā ghanaghōṣapratiravavaśēna । anyāsāmapi ghaṇṭānāṁ dvātriṁśacchatasahasrāṇi ॥ 196॥
ēkōnakāni samakālamēva kr̥tvā rēṇajjhaṇārāvam । prārabdhāni tatpratiravō'pi samakaṁ samucchālitaḥ ॥197॥
atrāntarē pañcavidhaviṣayasēvāpramattacittā api । dēvāstamēkakālaṁ vādyamānaghaṇṭāsvaraṁ śrutvā ॥ 198 ॥
cintayanti kiṁ visphuṭaccaṇḍabrahmāṇḍabhāṇḍakasya ravaḥ । ratnamayavimānā vālapratiphalanēna pravistīrṇaḥ ॥ 199॥
śrūyamāṇaḥ saṁkṣubdhamugdhahr̥dayābhiramararamaṇībhiḥ । hā nātha ! rakṣa rakṣēti jalpitrībhirbhayavaśēna ॥ 200 ॥
danujapativadhaharṣita tridaśasubhaṭagala garjibhīṣaṇō bhuvanē | sarvatō'pi vijr̥mbhatē ghaṇṭānāṁ raṇaraṇārāvaḥ ॥ 201 ॥
iti cintayā śithilitamāninīgāḍhāva gūḍhakaṇṭhē । saṁjātē suranivahē sarvatō mūḍhahr̥dayē ॥ 202 ॥
upaśāntē ca kṣaṇēna samagra gambhīraghaṇṭā nirghōṣē । avahitasurān surarājaśāsanaṁ kathayatyēṣa tataḥ ॥ 203॥
iti jñātvā hariṇagamēṣivacanatō janmamajjanaṁ prabhōḥ । visphuritapramōdamarāstataḥ saṁvidhātuṁ samārabdhāḥ ॥204॥
gatvā majjanakēlidīrghikāmatha kurvanti majjanakam । karpūramiśracandanarasēna dēhaṁ vilimpanti ॥205॥
dūṣyayugaṁ nirmala kōmalaṁ ca paridadhati kāntikamanīyam । kaṇṭhapratiṣṭhitahārā dūrōjjhitakāmukavikārāḥ ॥ 206॥
varakaṭakatruṭitamaṇimukuṭa kiraṇavicchuritasakala gaganatalāḥ । nijarūpagarvahasitakusumabāṇāstataścalitāḥ ॥ 207॥
1 kha. ga. majjha sa° । 2 anukaraṇaśabda iti tathaivānudyamānō yuktaḥ, ēvamutaratrāpi ।

iya savvavalasamēyā sahiyā niyēpaṇaiṇīhiṁ vēgēṇa । savvēvi harisēṇa āgayā suravaisamīvaṁ ॥ 210॥
ētthaṁtarammi lavaṁtavimalamuttāhalāvacūlilaṁ । phālihamaṇinimmiyasālabhaṁjiyāghaḍiyavaradāraṁ ॥ 219 ॥
khaṁbhasahasanibaddhaṁ raṇaṁtaghaṁṭāvalīhiṁ suisuhayaṁ । ubhaḍapavaṇapakaṁpirajayappaḍāgāi aipayaḍaṁ ||212 ||
sōlasabhēyāmalarayaṇanimpriyaṁ majjhimassa bhuvaṇassa । siharaṁva puvtrakayasuṁkayasi hariṇō nimmalaphalaṁ ।। 213॥
tihuyaṇapahāṇaparamāṇuniyaranivvattiyaṁva vicchaḍē । jōyaṇalakkhapamāṇaṁ jōyaṇapaṇa sahassassēhaṁ ||214 ||
suravaravayaṇa sasaṁbhamapālayasurasaṁciyaṁ varavimāṇaṁ । āruhiūṇaṁ caliō sakō saha dēvakōḍīhiṁ ॥ 215॥
tatō siīē tiriyaṁ dīvāṇa majjhayārēṇa । nandīsaravaradīvē dāhiṇapōracchimammi nagē ॥ 216 ॥
raikaranāmammi samāgatūṇa taō kamēṇa dēvaiṭiṁ । taṁ divvaṁ dēvajuī divvaṁ dēvāṇubhāvaṁ ca ॥ 217||
tattō vimārṇava saṁharēvi jēṇēva bhārahaṁ khittaṁ । vārāṇasī ya jēṇaṁ jēṇa ya jiṇajammabhavaṇaṁ ca ॥218॥
tēṇēva ya maggēṇaṁ āgaṁtūṇaṁ kamēṇa saṁpattō । supaṭṭanivaibhavaṇē sakkō saha dēvadēvīhiṁ ॥ 219 ॥
āyāhiṇāpayāhiṇamaha kāuṁ divvavaravimāṇēṇaṁ । tikkhuttaṁ jiṇajammaṇa bhuvaṇassa taō niyavimāṇaṁ || 220॥
saṁṭhaviūṇaṁ uttarapuracchimē suhadisāvibhāgammi । aggamahisīhiṁ ahiṁ sāmāṇiyasahassaculasīhiṁ ॥ 221||
uttuṅgaturagakuñjaravarāhavarahariṇamakarayānaiḥ । ārūḍhāścīnāṁśukacihnasahasōpaśōbhaiḥ ॥ 208॥
kē'pi vimānārūḍhāḥ kiṅkiṇīraṇajhaṇitabadhiritadigantāḥ । kē'pi hi mahāśārdūlaśara bhaha rihaṁ savr̥ṣabhagatāḥ ॥ 209 ॥
iti sarvabalasamētāḥ sahitā nijapraṇayinībhivēṁgēna । sarvē'pi surā harṣēṇāgatāḥ surapatisamīpam ॥ 210 ॥
atrāntarē lambamānavimalamuktāphalāvacūlikam । sphāṭikamaṇinirmitaśālabhañjikāghaṭitavaradvāram ॥ 211॥
stambhasaha sūnibaddhaṁ raṇadghaṇṭāvalībhiḥ śrutisukhadam । udbhaṭapavanaprakampamānajayapatākādyatiprakaṭam ॥ 212॥
ṣōḍaśabhēdāmalaratnanirmitaṁ madhyamasya bhuvanasya । śikharamiva pūrvakr̥tasukr̥taśikhariṇō nirmalaphalamiva || 213॥
tribhuvanapradhānaparamāṇunikaranirvartitamiva vistārē | yōjanalakṣapramāṇaṁ yōjanapañcasaha sōtsēdham ॥ 214॥
surapativacanasasaṁbhramapālakasurasaṁcitaṁ varavimānam । āruhya calitaḥ śakraḥ saha dēvakōṭibhiḥ || 215||
tataḥ śīghragatyā tiryadvīpānāṁ madhyēna । nandīśvaravaradvīpē dakṣiṇapaurastyē nagē ॥ 216 ॥
ratikaranāmni samāgatya tataḥ kramēṇa dēvarddhim । tāṁ divyāṁ dēvadyutiṁ divyaṁ dēvānubhāvaṁ ca ॥ 217 ||
tatō vimānamupasaṁhr̥tya yēnaiva bhārataṁ kṣētram । vārāṇasī ca yēna yēna ca jinajanmabhavanaṁ ca ॥218॥
tēnaiva ca mārgēṇāgatya kramēṇa saṁprāptaḥ । supratiṣṭhanr̥pabhavanē śakraḥ saha dēvadēvībhiḥ ॥ 219 ॥
ādakṣiṇapradakṣiṇāmatha kr̥tvā divyavaravimānēna । trirjina janmabhavanasya tatō nijavimānam ॥ 220 ॥
saṁsthāmyōttarapaurastyē śubhadigvibhāgē । agramahiṣībhiraṣṭābhiḥ caturaśītisāmānikasahasraiḥ ॥229॥

saṁjuttō tiyasapa pavisai tatthēva jattha titthayarō | jaṇaṇī ya, diṭṭivisaē puṇō paṇāmaṁ karēmāṇō ॥ 222॥

kahaṁ aiya ?
jayasi tumaṁ niyakulagayaṇasayala saṁpuna caṁdavararjuṇhē ! । tihuyaṇapahāṇasīlāiguṇagaṇāhāravaradharaṇi ! ||224 ||
vararayaṇaniyara paripuriaṁtarō lahuiō taē jalahī । tihuaṇapasaṁsaṇijjaṁ jiṇavararayaṇaṁ dharatīē ॥ 225॥
jaṇiuṁ jiniṁdamaṁtaratamapasaraniraṁbhaṇikadipanāhaṁ । khajjōyapasaciṇī iva kayā taē saṁvayaṁ puvvā ॥ 226॥
paramamuṇīṇapi tumaṁ jāyā āsīsabhāyaṇa dēvi ! । ēēṇaṁ ciya tumaē bhavajalahī duttarō tariō || 227||
ahariyatihuyaṇaciṁtāmaṇijiṇavara kucchidhāriṇīē dhuvaṁ । tuha caiva maṇuyajammō pasaṁsaṇijjō buhāṇaṁpi॥ 228॥
iya thōḍaṁ jiṇajaṇaṇi avasōvaṇidāṇapuvvayaṁ sakkō । ṭhaviūṇaṁ vēucciyajirṇapaḍirūvaṁ jaṇaṇipāsē ॥229॥
sayamavi paṁca sarīrē viubviraṁ dharai chattamēgēṇa । dōhiṁ ca ubhayapāsēsu ḍhālaē sēyavaracamarē || 230॥
ēkkēṇaṁ dharai purō sārayaravimaṁḍalaṁva disivalayaṁ । ujjōyaṁtaṁ vajjaṁ asaṁkhapaḍivakkha vikkhavaṇaṁ ॥231॥
ēgēṇa surahigōsīsacaṁdaṇuṣpaṁkapaṁḍurē sugaṁdhē । dharai jiṇaṁ karakaimalē harisavasullasiyarōmaṁcō || 232 ||

appāṇaṁ mannatō samatthasupasatthatitthajalaṇhāyaṁ । maṁdara sēlābhimuhaṁ caliō ākhaṁḍalō tattō ॥ 234॥

supāsanāha-cariammi-
paramēṇa pamāṇaṁ divbagaīē kamēṇa saṁpattō । tuṁgattaṇēṇa jōyaṇalakkhapamāṇaṁ suragiriṁdaṁ ||235 ||
jō tes ēkapaōharōvva dharaṇīē kaṇayakaṁtillō । rayaṇāvalīramaṇīō paṁḍagavaṇakasiṇasiharō ya || 236 ||
amiyaramaṇīyaguṇagaṇasaṁkhārēhavva suravarēhiṁ kayā । rēhaṁti jattha disidaṁtidaṁtara lihaṇarāīō || 237॥
pihulaniyēvō saṁsōhikaṇayama yamēhalāi parikaliō । supayōharō virāyai ruirō ramaṇīyaṇōvva sayā ॥ 238 ॥
uttuṁga siharasaṁṭhiyasāsayajiṇabhavaṇadhayapaḍāgāē । viyariyapattavva sayā jassa sirī rēhai divassa ॥ 239 ॥
savvattō gurunivbharasalilapayaṭṭāhiṁ gahirasariyāhiṁ । niruvamamahimasamubbhavakittīhiṁva sahai parikaliō240
iya garuyaguṇanihāṇaṁ taṁ jāva surāhivō samāruhai । tō picchai ramaṇīyaṁ mahāvaṇaṁ paṁḍagabhihāṇaṁ || 241॥
katthavi unnayanavajalayagajjipamujhyakalā vikulakaliyaṁ । katthavi ya kinnarīgēyasavaṇata licchahariṇakulaṁ । 242 ।
tō tattha paṁḍukaṁbalasilāē nīhārahāradhavalāē । maṇirayaṇakiraṇajalakhāliyammi tavaṇīyamaiyapi ॥ 243॥
nivasaibhisēyasiṁhāsaṇammi ucchaṁgaṭhaviyajiṇanāhō । puvvābhimuhō sakō harisavasupphullanayaṇajuō ॥ 244 ॥
jiṇavarapabhāvapaya liyaniyāsaṇā ōhiṇā viyāṇēuṁ । jiṇajammamajjaṇamahaṁ īsāṇāīvi suravaiṇō ॥ 245 ॥
savvēvi samāgatuṁ niyayasamiddhīi tiyasasēlammi । kayajiṇapayadhvaṇāmā harisēṇa ṭhiā niaṭṭhāṇē ॥ 246॥
tattō paḍhamaṁ bhaṇiyā accuyasurasāmiṇā niyā dēvā । bhō sigghaṁ titthayarābhisēyamuvaṇēha supasatyaṁ || 247॥
anuttaraṁ sahassaṁ tō tē kalasāṇa kaṇayamaiyāṇaṁ । kalahōyamayāṇa tahā aṭṭasahassaṁ maṇimayāṇaṁ ॥ 248 ॥
kaṁcaṇarupamayāṇaṁ varatārayamaṇimayāṇa ēmēva । maṇikaṇayarupamaiyāṇa taha ya bhōmēyagāṇaṁ ca ॥ 249॥
paramēṇa pramōdēna divyagatyā kramēṇa saṁprāptaḥ । tuṅgatvēna yōjanalakṣapramāṇaṁ suragirīndram ॥ 235 ॥
yō rājatyēkapayōdhara iva dharaṇyāḥ kanakakāntikaḥ । ratnāvalīramaṇīyaḥ pāṇḍukavanakr̥ṣṇaśikharaśca ॥ 236 ॥
amitaramaṇīyaguṇagaṇasaṁkhyārēkhā iva suravaraiḥ kr̥tāḥ । rājanti yatra digdantidantōllikhanarājayaḥ ॥ 237॥
pr̥thunitambaḥ saṁśōbhikanakamayamēkhalayā parikalitaḥ । supayōdharō virājatē rucirō ramaṇījana iva sadā ॥ 238 ॥
‘uttuṅgaśikhara saṁsthitaśāśvatajinabhavanadhvajapatākayā । vitīrṇapatrēva sadā yasya śrī rājatē divaḥ ||239 ॥
sarvataḥ pravr̥ttagurunirbharasalilābhirgambhīrasaridbhiḥ । nirupamamahimasamudbhava kīrttibhiriva rājatē parikalitaḥ ॥ 240॥
iti guruguṇanidhānaṁ taṁ yāvat surādhipaḥ samārōhati । tataḥ paśyati ramaṇīyaṁ mahāvanaṁ pāṇḍukābhidhānam || 241 ॥
kutrāpyunnatanava jaladgarjipramuditakalāpikulakalitam । kutrāpi ca kinnarīgēyaśravaṇatatpara hariṇakulam ॥242॥
tatastatra pāṇḍukambalaśilāyāṁ nīhārahāradhavalāyām । maṇiratnakiraṇajalakṣālitē tapanīyamayē ॥ 243॥
nivasatyabhiṣēkasiṁhāsana utsaṅgasthāpita jinanāthaḥ । pūrvābhimukhaḥ śakrō harṣavaśōtphullanayanayugaḥ ॥ 244॥
jinavaraprabhāvapracalitanijāsanā avadhinā vijñāya । jinajanmamajjanamahamīśānādayō'pi surapatayaḥ ॥ 245 ॥
sarvē'pi samāgatya nijakasamr̥ddhyā tridaśaśailē । kr̥tajinapādapraṇāmā harṣēṇa sthitā nijasthānē ॥ 246॥
tataḥ prathamaṁ bhaṇitā acyutasurasvāminā nijñā dēvāḥ । bhōḥ śīghraṁ tīrthakarābhiṣēkamupanayata supraśastam ॥ 247॥
aṣṭōttaraṁ sahasraṁ tatastē kalaśānāṁ kanakamayānām । kaladhautamayānāṁ tathā'sahasraṁ maṇimayānām || 248 ||

ēvaṁ rayaṇamayāṇaṁ bhaṁgārāīṇa pavaravatthūṇaṁ । pattēyaṁ pattēyaṁ aṭṭhasahassaṁ viḍēvvittā || 250॥
gaṁtuṁ khīrasamudaṁ kala sē bhariūṇa khīrasalilēṇaṁ । gahiyāī kamalakēravasyavattasahasvattāī ॥ 259॥
ēvaṁ mahaṁtamupasatthatitthasatthāṇa māgahāīṇaṁ । pavaranaīṇaṁ ca jalaṁ tahōsahīmaṭṭiyāō ya ॥ 252 ॥
uttarakurumāīsuvi kulagirivakvāranaṁdaṇavaṇēsu । aṁtaranaīdahēsu ya jāṇi ya kusumōsahiphalāī || 253 ||
iya savvaṁ ciya tiyasā turiyaṁ saṁgahiumāgayā tattha । viṇayappaṇayā accuyasurāhivaiṇō samaprpati ॥ 254॥
aha sō accuyasakō daṭṭaṇamabhisēyasayalasāmaggiṁ । jāyaharisō ya sigghaṁ uṭṭai niyaāsaṇāu taō ।। 255 ॥
sāmāṇiyasahassēhiṁ dasa hiṁ tahā cauhiṁ lōgapālēhiṁ । tihiṁ parisāhiṁ sattahi aṇiyāhivaīhiṁ aṇiēhiṁ ॥ 256 ॥
taha tāyattīsāē tāyattīsēhi āyarakkhāṇa । cattālīsasahassēhiṁ parivuḍō accuyasuriṁdō || 257 ॥
tattō ya vimalatitthāṇa khīrajalahīṇa salilapunnēhiṁ । gōsīsacaṁdaṇappamuhasāravatthūhi kalihiṁ || 258 ॥
vimalakamalapihāṇēhiṁ pavarasavvōsahīsaṇāhēhiṁ । sāhāviyavē uvtriyakalasēhiṁ mahappamāṇēhiṁ ॥ 259 ॥
sattamajiṇassa tihuyaṇanikkāraṇabaṁdhavasta bhattīē । jammāhisēyamahimaṁ accuyakappāhivō kuṇai ॥ 260 ॥
itthaṁtara mmi jugavaṁ palōikalasāṇa jiṁgasiraggāō । jaladhōraṇīō rēhiṁti siharisiharāō sariyanva | 261 ।
paharisaparavasāhiṁ disiramaṇīhiṁva ahava khittāō । muttāvalīō sōhaṁti nimmalāviralakaṁtīō ॥ 262॥
ahavāvi kugainivaḍirajaṇamuddhariḍaṁva punarajjūō । aha khuhiyajiṇajasōjala hiṇōvvaṁ kallōlamālāō 263
kāñcanarūpyamayānāṁ varatārakamaṇimayānāmēvamēva । maṇikanakarūpyamayānāṁ tathā ca bhaumēyakānāṁ ca ॥249॥
ēvaṁ ratnamayānāṁ bhr̥ṅkārādīnāṁ pravaravastūnām । pratyēkaṁ pratyēkamaṣṭasahasraṁ vikurvya ॥ 290॥
gatvā kṣīrasamudraṁ kalaśān bhr̥tvā kṣīrasalilēna । gr̥hītāni kapala kairavaśatapatrasahastrāṇi ॥ 259 ॥
ēvaṁ mahāsupraśastatīrthasārthānāṁ māgadhādīnām । pravaranadīnāṁ ca jalaṁ tathaiauṣadhimr̥ttikāśca ॥ 252 ॥
uttarakurvādiṣvapi kulagirivakṣaskārai nandanavanēṣu । antarnadīdrahēṣu ca yāni ca kusumaupadhiphalāni ॥253॥
iti sarvamēva tridaśāstvaritaṁ saṁgr̥hyā gatāstatra । vinayapraṇatā acyutasurādhipatayē samarpayanti ॥ 254 ॥
atha sō'cyutaśakō dr̥ṣṭvā'bhiṣēkasakala sāmagrīm । jātaharṣaśca śīghramuttiṣṭhati nijāsanāt tataḥ ॥ 255॥
sāmānikasaha sairdaśabhistathā caturbhirlēaukapālaiḥ । tisr̥bhiḥ parṣadbhiḥ saptabhiranīkādhipatibhiranīkaiḥ ॥ 256 ॥
tathā trayastriṁśatā trayastriṁśairātmarakṣāṇām । catvāriṁśatsahasrūcyā parighr̥tō 'cyutasurēndraḥ ॥ 257 ॥
tataśca vimalatīrthānāṁ kṣīrajaladhīnāṁ salilapūrṇaiḥ । gōśīrṣacandanapramukhasāravastubhiḥ kalitaiḥ ॥218॥
vimalakamalapidhānaiḥ pravarasarvauṣadhisanāthaiḥ । svābhāvika vaikrayikakalaśairmahāpramāṇaiḥ ॥259॥
saptamajinasya tribhuvananiṣkāraṇabāndhavasya bhaktyā | janmābhiṣēkamahimānamacyutakalpādhipaḥ karōti ॥ 260॥
atrāntarē yugapat paryastakalaśānāṁ jinaśirō'yāt । jaladhōraṇyō rājanti śikhariśikharāt sr̥tā iva ॥ 269 ॥
praharṣaparavaśābhirdigramaṇībhirivāthavā kṣiptāḥ । muktāvalyaḥ śōbhantē nirmalāviralakāntayaḥ ॥ 262॥
1. viōvittā ।

ēvaṁ jiṇābhisēgē paṭṭiē suravaīhiṁ harisēṇa । tāḍijjaṁti cauvvihaāujjāī surēhiṁ taō ॥ 264 ॥ -
1
saghaṇaghaṇaghōsaduṁduhininā uddharaṁ karaḍiraḍaraḍiyapaḍupaḍa haravabaṁdhuraṁ ।
sarasasiṁjaṁtaḍhakkā huḍukā ulaṁ mahuragaṁbhīra ghumaghumiyavaramadalaṁ ॥ 265 ॥
bukataṁbuka saṁbukasadukkaḍaṁ tālaṁjhaṇajhaṇiyavara talimaghōsunbhaḍaṁ ।
muhalakaṁsālachalachalaravāḍaṁbaraṁ bhēribhaṁbhāravāraṁbhabhariyaṁbaraṁ ॥ 266 ॥
vēṇuvīṇā samālavaṇiravasuṁdaraṁ jhallarighōsa samīsakharamuhisaraṁ ।
palayakālivvasajalaghaṇagajjiyaṁ tattha vajjēi cāuvhivajjayaṁ ॥ 267॥
garuyabhattinbharugbhinnarōmaṁcayā dhuṇahi titthēsaraṁ tattha naccaṁtayā ।
kēvi muṁcati maṁdāra sumanōharaṁ gaṁdhavasamiliyabhasalōha sumanōharaṁ ॥ 268 ॥
kēvi mallavva sajjati kamadaduraṁ avari gāyaṁti suhakaṁṭharavasuṁdaraṁ ।
kēvi uttālatālāulaṁ rāsayaṁ kuṇahiṁ karanacciyaṁ avari varahāsayaṁ ॥ 269॥
kēvi harisuddharā tiyasagaladaduraṁ kuṇahiṁ hayahēsiyaṁ kēvi subaṁdhuraṁ ।
afa gayagajjiyaṁ kuṇahiṁ mayabhibhala ani muṭṭhīhi paharaṁti dharaṇīyalaṁ ॥ 270 ॥
kēvi phōṁḍiṁti vakkariyaukērayaṁ kēvi kuvvaṁti kaṁṭhīravunnāyayaṁ ।
athavāpi kugatinipatanaśīlajanamuddhartumiva puṇyarajjvaḥ । atha kṣubvajinayaśōjaladhēriva kallōlamālāḥ ॥ 263 ॥
ēvaṁ jinābhiṣēkē pravartitē surapatibhirharṣēṇa । tāḍyantē caturvidhātōdyāni suraistataḥ ॥ 264 ॥
saghanaghanaghōṣadundubhininādōddhuraṁ karaṭiraṭaraṭitapaṭupaṭaharavabandhuram ।
sarasasiaḍḍhakkā huḍukkākulaṁ madhura gambhīra ghumaghumitavaramurajam ||26||
bukkatambukka sambukkaśabdōtkaraṁ tālajhaṇajhaṇitavara talimaghēōṣōdbhaṭam ।
mukharakāsālacchalacchalaravāḍambaraṁ bhērībhambhāravārambhabhr̥tāmbaram ||266॥
vēṇuvīṇāsamālapanīravasundaraṁ jhalarīghōṣasaṁmiśrakharamukhīsvaram ।
pralayakālikasajalaghanagarjitaṁ tatra vādyatē caturvidhavādyakam ॥267॥
gurubhaktibharōdbhinnarōmāñcakāḥ stuvanti tīrthēśvaraṁ tatra nr̥tyantaḥ ।
kēpi muñcanti mandārasumanōbharaṁ gandhavaśamilitabhramarautrasumanōharam ॥ 268 ॥
kē'pi mallā iva sajjanti kramadarduramaparē gāyanti śubhakaṇṭharavasundaram ।
kē'pyuttālatālākulaṁ rāsakaṁ kurvanti karanartitamaparē varahāsakam || 269॥
kē'pi harṣōddhurāstridaśagaladarduraṁ kurvanti hayahēṣitaṁ kēspi śrutibandhuram ।
kē'pi gajagarjitaṁ kurvanti mayabhimbhalamanyē muṣṭibhiḥ praharanti dharaṇītalam ॥ 270 ॥
kēspi sphōṭayanti durdinōtkaraṁ kēspi kurvanti kaṇṭhīravōnnādakam ।

51
iya va sattamatitthēsarajammamajjaṇamahammi । savvēvi suriṁdā paramaharisabharapulaiyasarīrā ||273 ||
dhūvakaḍucchayahatthā siyacamaravisālachattasaṁjuttā । suhapuṣpagaṁdha vāvaḍahatthā ya purō ṭhiyā tattō || 274 ||
ēvaṁ accuyasakē virayammi jiṇēsaraṁ havēūṇa । niyaparivārāṇugayā āṇayapamuhā suriṁdāvi || 275 ||
ahisicaṁti jiṇidaṁ mahāvibhūīē accuyavaivva । tīsaṁpi niyakamēṇaṁ muttuṁ sōhammakappapahuṁ || 276 ||

caurō cauddisiṁpi ha himakaraharahāsasaṁkhadaladhavalē । taruṇavasahē viuvvai ramaṇijjasarīrakaṁtilē ॥278॥
hu
tēsiṁca aṭṭhasiṁgaggabhāyaō aṭṭha saliladhārāō । uṭaṁgamāō dhaṇiyaṁ aha paḍaṇē ēgibhūyāō ।। 279 ॥
kāuṁ jiṇuttamaṁ khivēi āṇaṁda viyasiyacchijuō । annēhivi taha khīrōyakalasasahassēhiṁ bahuēhiṁ ॥ 280 ॥
ahisiṁcai ya kamēṇaṁ aha vihiē paramamajjaṇamahammi | sōhammavaī sukumālagaṁdhakāsā yavatthēhi ||281||
titthēsarassa dēhaṁ jayaṇāē lūhiūṇa savvattō । accai ya surahigōsīsacaṁdaṇasaṁmīsa ghusiṇēṇaṁ ॥ 282॥
maṁdāra sura hisiyakusumadāmanivahēhi rayai varapūyaṁ । savvālaṁkārēhiṁ vibhūsiūṇaṁ taō puraō || 283 ||
sārayasa sikaravalēhiṁ akkhaēhi imē samālihai । dappaṇabhadāsaṇavaddhamāṇasirivacchamacchē ya ॥ 284॥

iti surapatisaṁvēna pratihatavighnēna yasmin vr̥tyata ādarēṇa ।
saptamajinamajjanē tasmin bhavabhañjanē kiṁ kīrtyatē mādr̥śēna ? ॥ 272 ॥

dhūpadavahastāḥ sitacāmaraviśālacchatrasaṁyuktāḥ । śubhapuṣpagandhavyāpr̥tahastāśca puraḥ sthitāstataḥ ॥ 274 ॥

abhiṣiñcanti jinēndraṁ mahāvibhūtyā'cyutapatiriva । triṁśadapi nijakramēṇa muktvā saudharmakalpaprabhum ॥276॥
tadanantaraṁ sthāpayitvēśānēndrō jinaṁ nijāṅkē । siṁhāsanē niṣīdati tataḥ saudharmasvāmyapi ॥ 277॥
caturaścaturdikṣvapi hi himakaraharahāsaśaṅkhadalaghavalān । taruṇavr̥ṣabhān vikurvati ramaṇīyaśarīrakāntikān ॥278॥
tēṣāṁ cāṣṭaśr̥ṅgāgrabhāgatō'ṣṭa saliladhārāḥ । ūrdhvaṅgamā gāḍhamatha patanē ēkībhūtāḥ ॥ 279 ॥
kr̥tvā jinēōttamāṅgē kṣipatyānandavikasitākṣiyugaḥ । anyairapi tathā kṣīrōdakalaśa sahasairbahubhiḥ ॥ 280 ॥
abhiṣiñcati ca kramēṇātha vihitē paramamajjanamahē । saudharmapatiḥ sukumālagandhakāṣāyavastraiḥ || 281 ॥
tīrthēśvarasya dēhaṁ yatanayā pramārṇya sarvataḥ । arcati ca surabhigōśīrṣacandanasaṁmiśra ghusr̥ṇēna ॥ 282॥
mandārasurabhisitakusumadāmaniva hai racayati varapūjām । sarvālaṅkārairvibhūṣya tataḥ purataḥ ॥ 283 ॥

taha satthiyanaṁdāvattakalasapajjaṁtamaṁgalē arddha । muyai taō bahuvihakusumaniyaramājāṇumittaṁ ca || 285॥ .
tattō nāṇāmaṇibhatticittadaṁḍēṇa vairamaiēṇa | sukaḍacchuēṇa gaṁdhābhirāmamukkhivai varadhūyaṁ ॥ 286 ॥
pajalaṁtadīviyā cakavālamārattiyaṁ maṇabhirāmaṁ । uttārai varamaṁgalanilayaṁ taha maṁgalapaīva || 287 ||
ēvaṁ ca savvāyavvavittharē vittayammi tavvēlaṁ । jaya jaya jayāiyammi cāraṇamunipuṁgavagaṇēṇa ॥ 288 ॥
harisuttālanamira sira viyaliyakusumacciyadharāyalaṁ । naccirakara muṇālavalayāvalikalayalaravara mājalaṁ ||289 ।
ubbhaḍabharahabhāvabharanaccaṇaviyaliyahāra acciyaṁ । bhattibharēṇa tayaṇu jiṇamajjaṇi sayalasurēhiṁ nacciyaṁ ॥ 290॥
iya nacciūṇa paramappamōyabhara nivbharāē bhattīē । bhayavaṁtaṁ saṁthōuṁ ēvaṁ savvē samāraddhā ॥ 299 ॥
jaya nīsēsa aṇōrapārabhavasāyaratāraṇa ! | tihuyaṇapaṇamiyapāyakamala ! niruvamasuhakāraṇa ! || 292||
mayaṇahariṇa saṁharaṇa taruṇahariṇāriparakkama ! | muṇimāṇasaparisaraṇahaṁsa ! tailōyanayakkama ! ॥ 293॥
sirivēllahalavisaṭṭakamalakō malapayakarayala ! । himakaṇahimakara kiraṇasarisajasadhavaliyamahīyala ! ।। 294 ॥
saralanayaṇajya pasaratuliyaviyasiyapaṁkayadala ! | bhavabhayatāviyahiyayanavajalaharasīyala ! ॥ 295 ॥
tamabhara pasara niraṁbhaṇikadivasayarasamappaha ! | saraṇāgayadaḍhagūḍhavajjapaṁjara ! hayakuppaha ! ।। 296 ।।
ujjōiyabhuvaṇayala ! mōhakarikuṁbhaviyāraṇa ! | jaya jiṇanāha ! samatthavatthuparamatthaviyāraṇa ! ॥ 297॥
bhāraha khittu pavittu taṁ ji jahi tuhuṁ uppannau । sā jaṇaṇī. sakayattha jīē tuhuṁ uruppanna || 298 ||
śāradaśaśikaradhavalairakṣatairimān samālikhati । darpaṇabhadrāsana vadhamānaśrīvatsamatsyāṁśca ॥ 284 ॥
tathā svastikanandāvartakalaśaparyantamaṅgalānyaṣṭa । muñcati tatō bahuvidhakusumanikaramājānumātraṁ ca ॥285॥
tatō nānāvidhamaṇibhakticitradaṇḍayā vajramayyā | sudarvyā gandhābhirāmamutkṣipati varadhūpam ॥ 286 ॥
prajvaladdīpikā cakravālamārātrikaṁ manō'bhirāmam । uttārayati varamaṅgalanilayaṁ tathā maṅgalapradīpam ॥ 287॥
ēvaṁ ca sarvakartatryavistārē vr̥ttē tadvēlam । jaya jaya jayādikē cāraṇamunipuṅgavagaṇēna ॥288॥
harṣōttālanamraśirōvigalitakusumārcitadharātalam । nartanaśīlakara mr̥ṇālavalyāvālakalakalaravaramākulam ॥ 289॥
udbhaṭabharatabhāvabharanartanavicalitahārācitam । bhaktibharēṇa tadanu jinamajjanē sakalasurairnartitam ॥ 290॥
iti nartitvā paramapramōdabharanirbharayā bhaktyā । bhagavantaṁ saṁstōtumēvaṁ sarvē samārabdhāḥ || 291 ॥
jaya niḥśēṣānādipārabhavasāgaratāraṇa ! । tribhuvanapraṇatapādakamala ! nirupama sukhakāraṇa ! ॥ 292 ॥
madanahariṇa saṁharaṇataruṇahariṇāriparākrama ! | munimānasaparisaraṇahaṁsa ! trailōkyanatakrama ! ॥ 293 ॥
śrīvilāsivikasitakamalakōmalapādakaratala ! । himakaṇahimakarakiraṇasadr̥śayaśōdhavalitamahītala ! ||294 ॥
saralanayanayugaprasaratulita vikasitapaṅkajadala ! | bhavabhayatāpitabhavikahr̥daya navajaladharaśītala ! ॥ 295॥

'jammāipatthāvō ।
53
I
sacca sōjji jahattha hōi supaṭṭanarēsaru । jasu ghari ciṁtāmaṇisaricchu tuhuṁ jāu jiṇēsaru ॥ 299 ॥
iya thōūṇa jiṇidaṁ iṁdā naṁdīsarē jiṇē namiuṁ । niyaniyaṭhāṇēsa gayā sōhammavaīvi puṇa ittō ॥ 300 ॥
uttattakaṁcaṇaruiṁ gahiuṁ karasaṁpuṁḍēṇa jiṇanāhaṁ । vaccai jiṇavarajammaṇagharammi paramappamōēṇa ॥ 301 ॥ .
tattha ya paḍirūvaṁ taha avasōvaṇimavaṇiūṇa vēgēṇa । puhaijaṇaṇīsamīvē suyarayaṇaṁ muyai namiūṇa ॥ 302 ॥
ēgaṁ kuṁḍalajuyalaṁ pavaraṁ taha dēvadūtajuyalaṁ ca । ūsīsagamūlammi ṭhavēi puraō jiṇidassa || 303 ||
tidusagaṁ ca ēgaṁ paṇavanniyarayaṇakiraṇaramaṇijjaṁ । laṁbaṁtapavaramuttāhalāvacūlaṁ kaṇayamaiyaṁ ॥ 304 ||
muṁcai dipihammi abhiramaṇaṭṭhāi jamavalōyaṁtō । titthēsarō suhēṇaṁ sacakkhuvikkhēvaṇaṁ kuṇai ॥ 305 ॥
āṇavas taō sakkō vēsamaṇaṁ bhadda ! jaha lahuṁcēva । uvaiṇaya jiṇajammaharē battīsaṁ suvannakōḍīō || 306 ।।
taha caiva hirannassavi kōḍīō taha ya naṁdabhadāṇaṁ । pattēyaṁ battīsaṁ annāṇi ya vivihavatthūṇi ॥307॥
sōvi ha tahatti sigghaṁ jaṁbhagadēvēhiṁ savvamuvaṇēi । tattō puṇōvi sakkō umghōsāvēi savvattha ||308॥
hu
jaha bhō dēvā savvē dēvīōvi hu suṇaṁtu ēkamaṇā। jō kira jiṇassa jiṇavarajaṇaṇīē vāvi niyacittē ॥ 309 ॥
asivamaṇi kāuṁ ciṁtēhī tassa uttamaṁgaṁ ca । phuḍihī sahassahā ciya ajjagatarumaṁjarivva lahuṁ ||310॥
ēvaṁ kāūṇa vihiṁ bhayavaṁta paṇamiūṇa bhattīē । uppaiuṁ sō naṁdīsarammi gaṁtu gaō saggaṁ ॥ 311 ॥
aha uggayammi sūrē viyaliyatimirāsu sayalaāsāsu । taha vajjiēsa maṁgalatūrēsu ya gahirasaddēsu ॥ 312 ॥
satyaṁ sō'dya yathārthī bhavati supratiṣṭhanarēśvaraḥ । yasya gr̥hē cintāmaṇisadr̥kṣastvaṁ jātō jinēśvaraḥ ॥ 299 ॥
iti stutvā jinēndramindrā nandīśvarē jinān natvā । nijanijasthānēṣu gatāḥ saudharmapatirapi punaritaḥ ॥ 300 ॥
uttaptakāñcanaruciṁ gr̥hītvā karasaṁpuṭēna jinanātham । vrajati jinavara janmagr̥hē paramapramōdēna ॥ 302 ॥
tatra ca pratirūpaṁ tathā'vasvāpanīmapanīya vēgēna । pr̥thivījananīsamīpē sutaratnaṁ muñcati natvā ॥ 302 ॥
ēkaṁ kuṇḍalayugalaṁ pravaraṁ tathā dēvadūṣyayugalaṁ ca । uccharṣikamūlē sthāpayati puratō jinēndrasya || 303 ||
śrīdāmagaṇḍaṁ caikaṁ pañcavarṇikaratna kiraṇaramaṇīyam । lambamānapravaramuktāphalāvacūlaṁ kanakamayam ॥304॥
muñcati dr̥ṣṭipathē'bhiramaṇārthē yadavalōkamānaḥ । tīrthēśvaraḥ sukhēna svacakṣurvikṣēpaṇaṁ karōti ॥ 305 ॥
ājñapayati tataḥ śakrō vaiśramaṇaṁ bhadra ! yathā ladhvēva । upanaya jinajanmagr̥hē dvātriṁśataṁ suvarṇakōṭīḥ ॥ 206॥
tathaiva hiraṇyasyāpi kōṭastathā ca nandabhadrāṇām । pratyēkaṁ dvātriṁśatamanyāni ca vividhavastūni ॥307॥
sō'pi hi tathēti śīghraṁ jr̥mbhakadēvaiḥ sarvamupanayati । tataḥ punarapi śakra udghōṣayati sarvatra ॥ 308 ॥
yathā bhō dēvāḥ sarvē dēvyō'pi khalu śr̥ṇvantvēkamanasaḥ । yaḥ kila jinasya jinavarajananyā vāpi nijacittē॥ 309॥
aśivamaniṣṭaṁ kartuṁ cintayiṣyati tasyōttamāṅgaṁ ca । sphuṭiṣyati sahasravaivārjakatarumañjarīva laghu ॥310॥
ēvaṁ kr̥tvā vidhiṁ bhagavantaṁ praṇamya bhaktyā । utpatya sa nandīśvaraṁ gatvā gataḥ svargam ॥319॥
athōdgatē sūrē vigalitatimirāsu sakalāśāsu । tathā vāditēṣu maṅgalatūrēṣu ca gabhīraśabdēṣu ॥312॥
1 ka. kha. ḍāya । 2 ga. vaṇiya ।

mucaṁti cāragāō dhaṇiyaṁ avarāhakāriṇōvi jaṇā । kīraṁti visaṁṭhulavibbhamāō taha chaṇapavittīō ॥ 326 ॥
taddāhi; -
naccatamayāurataruṇigaliyasārasaṇalhasiyaparihāṇā । parihāṇalhasaṇa hasiraviḍajaṇakōlāhalāuliyā 327
āuliyaghaṇākaṁkhira maggaṇagaṇadijjamāṇaviḍaladhaṇā । dhaṇaviyara ṇaritanihāṇakhittavēsa maṇataivaṇīyā ॥ 328
tavaṇīyadaṁḍaūsiyacīṇaṁsuyadhayasahastraramaṇīyā । ramaṇīyaramaṇisahari sapāraṁbhiyacaccarīgīyā ॥ 329 ॥
gīyaguṇaniuṇagāyaṇamahurassara pūriyākhiladisōhā | sōhaṁtapa urabahuyaṇasāyara kī raṁ tamaṁgalā ||330||

iya vāṇārasinayarī savāhiraṁbhaṁtarā surapurīva । jāyā samuciyapaḍivattī suṁdarā suiraramaṇīyā ||332 ||
aha navaframaṇuciyamaṇaṁ jamiha karā jaṇavayāṇa chijjēti । avisēsiyabhiccanarēsaraṁva taha havai nivabhavaṇaṁ ।।
ēvaṁ paṭṭamāṇē nayarīē mahūsavammi naranāhō । suparaṭṭō kayaṇhāṇō pavarālaṁkāralaṁkariō ||334||
niyasiyamahagghavatthō gaṁtūṇatthāṇabhūmimuvavihō । ētthaṁtarasmi sāmaṁtamaṁtipamuhā visijaṇā ॥ 335 ॥
āgaṁtūṇa namiūṇa pāyapaumāī bhaṇiumāraddhā | dēva ! sarīrārōgattaṇēṇa sattūṇa vijapaṇaṁ ॥ 336 ॥
taha rajjavittharēṇa dhaṇāgamēṇaṁ ca savvahā tubbhē । vaddhāvijjaha jēsi tihuyaṇacūḍāmaṇisaricchō ||337||
niyakulanahayalasaṁ punnapunnimācaṁda maṁḍalasamāṇō । ērisaputtō jāō iya bhaṇiūṇa taō savvē ||338॥
mucyantē cārakād bāḍhamaparādhakāriṇō'pi janāḥ । kriyantē visaṁsthula vibhramāstathā kṣaṇa pravr̥ttayaḥ ॥ 326 ॥
tathāhi;-

tathā rājyavistarēṇa dhanāgamēna ca sarvathā yūyam । vardhāpyadhvē yēṣāṁ tribhuvanacūḍāmaṇisadr̥kṣaḥ ॥ 337 ॥

pavara kariturayabhūsaṇamaṇivasaṇāīṇi nivaiṇō puraō । uvaḍhōiti sahēla sammāṇēuṁ nivaiṇāvi ।। 339 ॥
taṁbōlavatthakusumālaṁkārapayāṇapuñvayaṁ savvē । bahuvihavihiyapasāyā visajjiyā niyayaṭhāṇēsu || 340 ॥
tattō niyasuyadaṁsaṇasamr̥suō samuvalabbha patthāvaṁ । supaṭṭō atthāṇāṁ samuṭṭhiō garuyaharisēṇa ॥ 349 ॥
pattō kamēṇa maṇimayakuṭṭimatala lihiyasaṁtthiyaṁ viulaṁ । ubbhiyahiraṇṇamusalaṁ suvihiyarakkhāparikkhēvaṁ ॥
dārapaēsanivēsiyasiyakamalapahāṇapunnajalakalasaṁ । jiṇavarajammaṇabhavaṇaṁ tattha ya diṭṭhō ya jiṇanā hō । 343॥
sārayasahassa kiraṇōvva rayaṇarāsivva tēyapuṁjōvva । ujjōyaṁtō bhavaṇaṁ dēhapahāē samagaṁpi || 344 ||
taṁ daddūṇa citimāḍhattō naravaī ahō apuvvā । ēyassa paḍhamajāyassa kāvi kaṁtī sarīrassa || 345 ||
taha ya avibhāvaṇijjaṁ lāyannaṁ rūvasaṁpayā asamā । nimmēraṁ sudēraṁ taha ya abhaggaṁ ca sōhaggaṁ ॥ 346॥
tā sayalapunnapabbhārasāyaraṁ mama kulaṁ, jahiṁ ēyaṁ । saṁpunnalakkhaṇadharaṁ pāunbhūyaṁ taṇayarayaṇaṁ ॥ 347॥
iya ēvamāi saṁcitiūṇa supaṭṭanaravaī tattō । paḍhamadiṇē ṭhiivaḍiyaṁ karēi titthāhivassa taō || 348 ||
taiyammi dinē daṁsaṁti ummuhaṁ maṁḍalāī ravisasiṇō । saṁpattō ya kamēṇa paramapamōēṇa chaṭṭhadiṇō ||349॥
aviṇalaṭṭhapaṁciṁdiyāhiṁ jīvaṁtapāṇanāhāhiṁ । nīrōgaaṁguvaṁgāhiṁ rāyā kulavuṭṭiyāhiṁ ca ॥ 350 ॥
ghaṇakuṁkumapaṁkalittavayaṇakamalāhiṁ khvavaṁtīhi । kaṁbusamakaṁṭha kaṁdala avalaṁviyasurahimālāhiṁ ॥ 359 ॥
accaṁta jāyamāṇasasaṁtōsō naravariṁdasuparaṭṭhō । kulavilayāhiṁ jāgaramahūsavaṁ tō paṭṭē ||352 ||
pravarakarituragabhūṣaṇamaṇivasanādīni nr̥patēḥ purataḥ । upaḍhōkantē sahēlaṁ, sammānya nr̥patināpi ॥ 339॥
tāmbūlavastrakusumālaṅkārapradānapūrvakaṁ sarvē । bahuvidhavihitaprasādāḥ visarjitā nijakasthānēṣu ॥ 340 ॥
tatō nijasutadarśanasamutsukaḥ samupalabhya prastāvam । supratiṣṭha āsthānātsamutthitō guruharṣēṇa ॥ 341 ॥
prāptaḥ kramēṇa maṇimaya kuṭṭimatala likhitasvastikaṁ vipulam । ūrdhvakr̥ta hiraṇyamuśalaṁ suvihitarakṣāparikṣēpam ॥
dvārapradēśanivēśitasitakamalapradhānapūrṇa jalakalaśam । jinavarajanmabhavanaṁ tatra ca dr̥ṣṭaśca jinanāthaḥ ॥ 343॥
śāradasahasrakiraṇa iva ratnarāśiriva tējaḥpuñja iva । uddyōtayan bhavanaṁ dēhaprabhayā samagramapi ॥ 344॥
ਰ dr̥ṣṭrā cintayitumārabdhō narapatirahō ! apūrvā । ētasya prathamajātasya kāpi kāntiḥ śarīrasya || 345 ||
tathā cāvibhāvanīyaṁ lāvaṇyaṁ rūpasaṁpadasamā । nirmaryādaṁ saundaryaṁ tathā cābhagnaṁ ca saubhāgyam ॥ 346॥
tasmātsakalapuṇyaprāgbhārasāgarō mama kulaṁ, yasminnētat । saṁpūrṇalakṣaṇavaraṁ prādurbhūtaṁ tanayaratnam ||347||
ityēvamādi saṁcintya supratiṣṭhanarapatistataḥ । prathama dinē sthitipatikāṁ karōti tīrthādhipasya tataḥ ॥ 348॥
tr̥tīyasmindinē darśayantyunmukhaṁ maṇḍalē raviśaśinōḥ । saṁprāptaśca kramēṇa paramapramōdēna ṣaṣṭhadinaḥ || 349 ॥
avinaṣṭamanōharapañcēndriyābhirjīvatprāṇanāthābhiḥ । nīrōgāṅgōpāṅgābhī rājā kulavr̥ddhikābhiśca ॥ 350 ॥
ghanakuṅkumapaṅkālaptavadanakamalābhī rūpavatībhiḥ । kambusamakaṇṭhakandalāvalambitasurabhimālābhiḥ || 351॥
atyantajātamānasasaṁtōṣō naravarēndrasupratiṣṭhaḥ । kulavanitābhirjāgara mahōtsavaṁ tataḥ pravartayati ॥ 392 ॥
1 kha 'ṇāu uhi । 2 ka. ga. sutthi ।
