jammāpatthāvō ।
૭
ēkkārasamma divasē samāgaē sūikammamuvarṇiti । jahabhaṇiyavihāṇēṇaṁ, pattē vārasamadiyahammi || 353 ॥
nāṇāvihavaṁjaṇakhaṁḍakhajjakhajjūrapāṇayasamēyaṁ । bahusālisyasahiyaṁ nivvattāvēi rasavaiyaṁ || 354 ||
tayaṇataraṁ ca niyakhattiyāṇa taha purapahāṇalōyāṇaṁ । taṁ bhōyaṇaṁ paṇāmai bahumāṇapurassaraṁ tattō || 355 ||
āyaṁtāṇa khaṇēṇaṁ vīsatyāṇaṁ suhāsaṇagayāṇaṁ । sammāṇiyāṇa tēsiṁ puraō supaṭṭanaranāhō ॥ 356 ॥
bhai ya bhō bhō khattiyapahāṇapurisā ! mamēsa saṁkappō । āsī puvrvvapi jahā jadivasa ēsa gavbhammi | | 357 |
puhaīdēvīē susaṁkatō taddiṇāō ahiyayaraṁ । saṁjāyā suhapāsā tattō ēyassa juttamiṇaṁ ॥ 358 ॥
nāmaṁ supāsakumārō tumhāṇavi saṁgaī jai gamēi । tō uvalakkhiyabhāvēhi tēhi iya naravaī bhaṇiō || 359 /
ēyaṁ ciya khalu juttaṁ, guṇaniṣpannammi vijjamāṇammi | nāmammi kīsa kīrai ajahaṭṭhiyakappaṇaṁ tattō ॥ 360 ॥
iya jaṁpirēhi tēhi jayaguruṇō sirisupāsanāmaṁti । parituṭṭhēhiṁ paṭṭiyamaha vittē nāmakaraṇammi || 361॥
surasaṁkāmiyakāmiyarasāē niyayaṁgulīē pāṇēṇa । kayabhōyaṇakāyavvō paṁcahiṁ dhāīhiṁ pariyariō || 362|
sārijjatō aṁtēurēṇa hatthāu hatthakamalammi । ammāpiyarēhiṁ tahā kārijjutō ya caṁkaimaṇaṁ ॥ 363 ॥
hāsijjatō bahukhujjavāmaṇāīhiṁ kayaviyārēhiṁ । saggāhivāsasarisaṁ tiyēṁsēhi ya uvayarijjaṁtō।। 364।।
jōijjatō vihiyaṁjasāhi harisāu purapuraṁdhīhiṁ । iya sō lālijjatō paḍhamillubbhinnada saṇajuō ॥ 368
parivaḍhiumārō kulagirikuharuggauvva kappatarū । paḍipunnasayaladēhāvayavō ya kamēṇa saṁjāō ॥ 366॥
ēkādaśē divasē samāgatē sūtikarmōpanayanti । yathābhaṇitavidhānēna, prāptē dvādaśadivasē ॥ 353 ॥
nānāvidhavyañjanakhaṇḍakhādyakharjūrapānakasamētām । bahuśālisūpasahitāṁ nirvartayati rasavatikā (tī) m ॥354॥
tadanantaraṁ ca nijakṣatriyēbhyastathā purapradhānalōkēbhyaḥ । tad bhōjanamarpayati bahumānapurassaraṁ tataḥ ॥ 355॥
āgacchatāṁ kṣaṇēna viśvastānāṁ sukhāsanagatānām । saṁmānitānāṁ tēṣāṁ purataḥ supratiṣṭhanaranāthaḥ || 356॥
bhaṇati ca bhō bhōḥ kṣatriyapradhānapuruṣāḥ ! mamaiṣa saṁkalpaḥ । āsītpūrvamapi yathā yadivasa ēṣa garbhē || 397॥
pr̥thivīdēvyāḥ sutaḥ saṁkrāntastaddinādadhikataram । saṁjātāḥ śubhapārśvāstata ētasya yuktamidam ||318 ||
nāma supārśvakumārō yuṣmākamapi saṁgatiṁ yadi gamayati । tata upalakṣitabhāvaistairiti narapatirbhaṇitaḥ ॥ 359 ॥
ētadēva khalu yuktaṁ guṇaniṣpannē vidyamānē । nāmni kasmāt kriyatē'yathāsthitakalpanaṁ tataḥ ॥ 360 ॥
iti jalpitr̥bhistairjagadgurōḥ śrīsupārśvanāmēti । parituṣṭaiḥ pratiṣṭhitamatha vr̥ttē nāmakaraṇē ॥ 361 ||
surasaṁkrāmitakāmitarasāyā nijakāṅgulyāḥ pānēna । kr̥tabhōjanakartavyaḥ pañcabhirghātrībhiḥ parikaritaḥ॥362॥
sāryamāṇō'ntaḥpurēṇa hastāddhastakamalē । mātāpitr̥bhyāṁ tathā kāryamāṇaśca caṁkramaṇam || 363॥
hāsyamānō bahukuñjavāmanādibhiḥ kr̥tavikārai: । svargādhivāsasadr̥śaṁ tridaśaiścōpacaryamāṇaḥ || 364 ॥
dr̥śyamānō vihitāñjasābhirharṣāt purapurandhrībhiḥ । iti sa lālyamānaḥ prāthamikōdbhinnadaśanayutaḥ ।।365॥
parivardhitumārabdhaḥ kulagirikuharōdgata iva kalpataruḥ । paripūrṇa sakaladēhāvayavaśca kramēṇa saṁjātaḥ ॥ 366 ॥
1 ka gayaṁ, ga. gamaṁ । 2 kha. nēva karē3 । 3 ka. kamiṇaṁ । 4ka. sēhiṁ ।

tāvicchaguccha sacchaha kuṁciyakēsēhiṁ sahai tassa muhaṁ । viyasiyanravāraviṁda līṇēhiṁ va bhamara vidēhi ॥ 368|

aha sahai visālaṁ satthalasamubbhavaṁ bhuyaasōyalayajuyalaṁ । naha kiraṇapuṣphiyaṁ pāṇipallavāruṇimaramaṇīyaṁ 372

kiṁbahunā savvāvayavasuṁdarī suyalalakkhaṇajuō ya । kassa na nayaṇāṇaṁdaṁ jaṇēi suhaō sa divi ।। 376।

tāpicchaguccha sadr̥śa kuñcita kēśai rājatē tasya mukham । vikasitanavāravindaṁ līnairiva bhramaravr̥ndaiḥ || 368 ||

atha rājatē viśālaṁ satsthala samudbhavaṁ bhujāśōkalatāyugalam । nakhakiraṇapuṣpitaṁ pāṇipallavāruṇimaramaṇīyam ||372॥

kiṁ bahunā sarvāvayavasundaraḥ sakalalakṣaṇayutaśca । kasya na nayanānandaṁ janayati subhagaḥ sa dr̥ṣṭō'pi ॥ 376 ॥

bālō'pi khala sukavīnāṁ yō gurumanōvismayaṁ sadā janayati । rasabhāvasundarāṇi viracayalalitakāvyāni ॥ 379 |

uvaṇīyataruṇimaṇanayaṇavibbhamaṁ saṁbhavaṁtanavasōhaṁ । aṁtariyakumārattaṁ tattō pattō sa tāruṇaṁ ॥ 389 ॥

pōḍhapurasuṁdarīṇaṁ guṇagaṇasaṁdāṇiyāṇiva maṇāṇi । tasmi vayaṁtē aṇudhāvirāī valirāī valamāṇē ||383 ||

iya kēlīē kālaṁ gamēi jasapasaradhavaliyadisōhō । nissīmathāmamaivasa vibhāviyāsēsavinnāṇō ।। 392 ।।
aha tassa ṭiinimittaṁ surēhiṁ raiō siraiggalihiyanahō । kaṇayamaṇiviḍḍurillō mēruvva mahaṁtapāsāō ||

kadāpi pādaprakaṭanasthirāsanō durdamānāṁ dantinām । kumbhasthalaśāṇaniśāṇitāṅkuśaḥ skhalayati madaprasaram ॥
ēvamēva kathamapi līlāvaśēna yaḥ kō'pi tasya guṇanidhēḥ । paramārthamiva śikṣatē caritalavaṁ tamapi vidvajjanaḥ ॥

atha tasya sthitinimittaṁ surai racitaḥ śirō'gralikhitanakhaḥ । kanakamaṇivaiḍūryavān mēruriva mahāprāsādaḥ ॥ 393॥

tatthēva ṭhiōjaṁ kiṁpi suṁdaraṁ sō vibhāvaē hiaē । taṁ kiṁkaravva dēvā savvaṁpi hu tassa uvarṇiti ।। 395॥

āgamaṇakāraṇaṁ puṇa rūṇabharasōṁḍīra ! nisuṇasu mamēyaṁ । jēṇaṁ tumha sayāsē niyapahuṇā pēsiō ahayaṁ ॥ 402 ॥

sau cadakalāō cuniūṇa ālōḍiūṇa amaēṇa । mannē aṇaṁgasaṁjīvaṇōsahī nimmiyā vihiṇā ||407॥
ēyaṁ maṇunaṁ ēyaṁ ca suṁdaraṁ salahaṇijjamēyaṁti । iya bhāvintō tattiṁ na lahai lōō tayaṁgē || 408 ||
bhōjanavilāsamajjanamaṇḍapa parimaṇḍitō manō'bhirāmaḥ । yaḥ prakaṭamā khaṇḍalavimānamānamapi khaṇḍayati ॥ 394 ॥
tatraiva sthita yatkimapi sundaraṁ sa vibhāvayati hr̥dayē । tat kiṅkarā iva dēvāḥ sarvamapi hi tasyōpanayanti ॥ 395 ॥

dēva ! dvārē'marāvatītō ripumardanasya varadūtaḥ । naranāthaṁ draṣṭumana |stasmātkaraṇīyaṁ samādiśa ॥ 397 ॥

sō'pi mahītalagatamaulimaṇḍalaḥ praṇamya naranātham । tatkṣaṇumupanītē viṣṭarē sānandamupaviṣṭaḥ ॥399॥

vinayāvanatēna śirōracitāñjalyatha narēṇa pratibhaṇitam । dēvaprasādēna sadā kuśalamēva svāmiśālasya ( ? ) ॥ 401 ॥

kaṁcīvisayāō kuṁtalamma tattō ya majjhadēsammi । juvadiṭṭhīō tayaṁgē pahiyanva ciraṁ payati ॥ 409 ॥
aha annayā ya sā sahayarīhiṁ sahiyā gayā niujjāṇaṁ । nisuṇai gijjaṁta kiṁnarīhiṁ gāhājuyaṁ ēyaṁ । । 410॥
sirisupaṭṭanara। hivavisālakulagayaṇa bhūmaṇasaṁsakō। sayalakalākalahaṁsīlīla(kamalāyarō kumarō || 411 ॥
nāmēṇa supāsō sayalasuhayasirasēharō guṇāṇuyahī । taruṇiyaṇahiyayaharaṇō dhannāē imō varō hōhī ॥ 492 ॥
sā ēvaṁ nisutī kumāra guṇakittaṇaṁ tahiṁ bālā । īsāiēṇa nūṇaṁ mayaṇēṇa sarēhiṁ saṁviddhā ||413 ||
tattō ya hiṁsā kīliyavva suttavva ahava mattavva । gāḍhaṁ nimīliyanayaṇā mucchāvihalaṁghalā jāyā414
gayacēyannā na sahīṇaṁ uttaraṁ dēi kiṁpi puṭṭhāvi । tāōvi saṁbhaṁtāō ciṁtaṁti ahō kimēti ||415 ॥
asisāsēhiṁ dēhē dāhōtti mannamāṇīō । kamaliṇidalēhiṁ sējjaṁ virayaṁti kahaṁtiya piūṇaṁ ॥ 416 ॥
hā divva ! kahamakaṁḍē maha daṁḍō pāḍiō taē sahasā । iccāi palavamāṇī samāgayā caṁdavayaṇāvi ॥ 417॥
tatō ya dēhadāhassa kāraṇa pucchiō sahīggō । savvōvi jā na sāhai tā nimgaṁtūṇa ēgaṁtē ॥ 418॥
puṭṭhā vikkhaṇā nāma sahayarī, tīi sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ । jaha sirisupāsakumarē'ṇurattacittā imā nūṇaṁ ॥ 419 ॥
jaṁ ujjāṇē aiyāē nisuṇiō kiṁnarīē gijjaṁtō । sō sirisupāsakumarō ēyāvasthā taō jāyā ।। 420॥
tō dēvī gaṁtūṇaṁ sāhai savvaṁpi vaiyaraṁ rannō । tēṇatri pahihiyaēṇa jaṁpiyaṁ vayaṇamēti ॥ 421 ॥
jaha puvrvvapi mamēsō saṁkaṣpō āsi jaha imā dhūyā । dēyā supāsakumarassa saṁpayaṁ laṭṭhayaṁ vihiṇā ||422 ||
kāñcīviṣayātkuntalē tataśca madhyadēśē । yuvadr̥ṣṭayastadaṅgē pathikā iva ciraṁ pravartantē ॥ 409 ॥
athānyadā ca sā sahacarībhiḥ sahitā gatā nijōdyānē । śr̥ṇōti gīyamānaṁ kinnarībhirgāthāyugamētat ॥ 410 ॥
śrīsupratiṣṭhanarādhipaviśāla kulagagana bhūṣaṇa śaśāṅkaḥ । sakalakalākalahaṁsīlīlā kamalākaraḥ kumāraḥ ॥ 411॥
nāmnā supārśvaḥ sakalasubhagaśiraḥ śēkharō guṇānāmudadhiḥ । taruṇī janahr̥dayaharaṇō dhanyāyā ayaṁ varō bhaviṣyati ।। 412 ॥
saitacchr̥ṇvatī kumāraguṇakīrtanaṁ tasmin bālā । īṣyāyitēna nūnaṁ madanēna śaraiḥ saṁviddhā ||413॥
tataśca taiḥ sā kīlitēva suptēvāthavā mattēva । gāḍhanimīlitanayanā mūrcchāviśr̥ṅkhalā jātā ॥414 ॥
gatacaitanyā nasakhīnāmuttaraṁ dadāti kimapi pr̥ṣṭāpi । tā api saṁbhrāntāścintayanti ahō kimētaditi ? || 415॥
atyuṣṇōcchvāsairdēhē dāha iti manyamānāḥ । kamalinīdalaiḥ śayyāṁ viracayanti kathayanti ca pitarau ॥ 416॥
hā daiva ! kathamakāṇḍē mama daṇḍaḥ pātitastvayā sahasā । ityādi pralapantī samāgatā candravadanāpi ||4 17 ॥
tataśca dēhadāhasya kāraṇaṁ pr̥ṣṭaḥ sakhīvargaḥ । sarvē'pi yāvanna kathayati tāvannirgatyaikāntē ॥418॥
pr̥ṣṭā vicakṣaṇā nāma sahacarī, tathā kathitaṁ sarvam । yathā śrīsupārśvakumārē'nurakta cittēyaṁ nūnam ॥ 419 ॥
dudhānē tayā śrutaḥ kinnaryā gīyamānaḥ । sa śrīsupārśvakumāra ētadavasthā tatō jātā ॥420॥
tatō dēvī gatvā kathayati sarvamapi vyatikaraṁ rājñē । tēnāpi prahr̥ṣṭahr̥dayēna jalpitaṁ vacanamētaditi ॥421 ॥
yathā pūrvamapi mamaiṣa saṁkalpa āsīdyathēyaṁ duhitā । dēyā supārśvakumārāya sāṁprataṁ manōharaṁ vidhinā ॥ 422॥

sayamēva kathaṁ, tā ēttha ujjamaṁ sigghamēva kāhāmō । iya gaṁtūṇaṁ sāhasu duhiyāē dēvi ! duhiyāē || 423 ||
"

taṁ caiva puṇō paramakkharaṁca gāhājuyaṁ vicitaṁtī । ētaṭhiyā ciṭṭhai lajjai divi sahi
avaraṁ ca;
||425 ||
bhuṁjai naya āhāraṁ na kuṇai pahāṇaṁ nayāvi siṁgāraṁ। taṁbūlaṁpi na giṇhai na ya niyasai cāruvatyāṇi ॥ 426॥
nō diṭṭhīivi picchai ruvāī mahānariṁdakumarāṇaṁ । dūyāṇīyāī citta paṭṭiyāsuṁpi lihiyāī ॥427||
kiṁ bahuṇā;
ēvaṁ taṇuaṁgī bhinnāē nisiyamayaṇabāṇēhiṁ । saraṇaṁ supāsakumarō maraṇaṁ vā daiva ! na hu annaṁ ||428||
ēyāvatthaṁ taṁ pāsiūṇa taha maṁtiūṇa maṁtiyaṇaṁ । riumadaṇēṇa raṇṇā maisāyaramaṁtiṇā sahiyā || 429 ||
sōmā nāmēṇa suyā sayaṁvarā sirisupāsakumarassa | saṁpēsiyā tahā hūṁ maisāyaramaṁtiṇā puraō ||430 ॥
kahiuṁ tumha samīvē vaiyaramēvaṁ nirūviō dēva ! । ētō tuma pamāṇaṁ iya bhaṇiuṁ ṭhāi tuhakō || 431 ॥
tō bhaṇiyaṁ naravaṇā sammaṁ ālōiūṇa sāhissaṁ । vaccasu niyayāvā sē tumaṁti sammāṇiō raṇṇā ॥ 432 ॥
baccai niyaāvāsē sō, ēttō naravaīvi sāhēi । puhavīpiyāē savvaṁ tō pabhaṇai sāvi parituṭṭhā || 433 ||
dēva ! maē pattāī suhāī savvāī aṇaṇubhūyāī । tuha pāyapasāēṇaṁ ēttiyamēttēṇa hīṇāī || 434 ||
svayamēva kr̥taṁ, tasmādatrōdyamaṁ śīghramēva kariṣyāmaḥ । iti gatvā kathaya duḥkhitāṁ dēvi ! duhitaram ॥423॥
tataśca harṣitayā''gatyāsmin vr̥ttāntē । kathitē dēvyā tataḥ sā kiñcit sacētanā jātā ||424॥

aparaca;
bhuṅgē na cāhāraṁ na karōti snānaṁ na cāpi śr̥ṅgāram । tāmbūlamapi na gr̥hṇāti na ca nivasati cāruvastrāṇi ॥426 ॥
nō dr̥ṣṭyāpi paśyati rūpāṇi mahānarēndrakumārāṇām । dūtānītāni citrapaṭṭikāsvapi likhitāni ॥ 427॥
kiṁ bahunā;

ētadavasthāṁ tāṁ dr̥ṣṭvā tathā mantrayitvā mantrijanēna । ripumardanēna rājñā matisāgaramantriṇā sahitā ॥ 429॥
sōmā nāmbā sutā svayaṁvarā śrī supārśvakumārāya | saṁprēṣitā tathā'haṁ matisāgaramantriṇā purataḥ ॥ 430 ॥
kathayituṁ yuṣmākaṁ samīpē vyatikaramēvaṁ nirūpitō dēva ! । itō yūyaṁ pramāṇamiti bhaṇitvā tiṣṭhati tūṣṇīkaḥ॥ 431।.
tatō bhaṇitaṁ narapatinā samyagālōcya kathayiṣyāmi । vraja nijakāvāsē tvamiti saṁmānitō rājñā ॥ 432 ॥
vrajati nijakāvāsē saḥ, itō narapatirapi kathayati । pr̥thivīpriyāṁ sarvaṁ tataḥ prabhaṇati sāpi parituṣṭā || 433॥
dēva ! mayā prāptāni sukhāni sarvāṇyananubhūtāni । tvatpādaprasādēnaitāvanmātrēṇa hīnāni ॥ 434 ॥

63
jara puṇa kapi ēyaṁ vīvāhamahūsavaṁpi picchāmi । saṁpai supāsakumarassa dēva ! tā hōmi kayakiccā ॥ 435॥
tō naravaṇā bhaṇiyaṁ jai ēvaṁ dēvi ! tā tumaṁ sigghaṁ । vaccasu kumarasamīvaṁ vīvāhatthaṁ ca pannavasu ॥ 436 ॥
tattō ya puhaidēvī vaccara kaṁcuijaṇēṇa pariyariyā । pāsē supāsakumarassa sōvi daṭṭūṇa taṁ iti ॥437॥
aṇugamai abhimuhaṁ ciya satta payāī tahaya kāravara । āsaṇadāṇappamuhaṁ paḍivattiṁ taha ya namiūṇaṁ ॥ 438॥
bhālayalamiliyakarakamalasaṁpuḍō vinnavēi kumarōvi । saṁpai tumhāgamaṇē ammō ! kiṁ kāraṇaṁ -kahasu ? || 439 ॥
puijaṇaṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ puttāhaṁ pēsiyamhi dēvēṇa । tuha vīvāhamahūsavadaṁsaṇaukaṁṭhiō jamhā ||440||
dēvō iyarajaṇōvi ya, taha majjhavi ēttiyaṁ ca dūmēi । saṁpai apattapruvvaṁ pattāī suhāī annāī ||441 ||
tujjha pasāēṇanē paḍipunnā jaṁ maṇōrahā savvē । tā paḍivajjau kumarō vīvāhamahūsavaṁ kāuṁ || 442 ||
taṁ succā kumarōvi hu pabhaṇai ammō ! na muṇaha maha cittaṁ । navi yāṇaha visayasuhaṁ gihavāsaṁpi hu sadukkhaphalaṁ ॥
jēṇaṁ vivāhavisaē ēvaṁ ullavaha, tīē tō bhaṇiyaṁ । muṇimō savvaṁ kiṁpuṇa alaṁghaṇijjaṁ ca piuvayaṇaṁ ॥ 444॥
na hu tumhāṇaṁ pacchimavaēvi dulahō hu gihaparicāō । paḍikūlissai dēvō paḍipunnamaṇōrahō na tumaṁ ॥ 445 ॥
tō bhaṇiyaṁ kumarēṇa paḍivajjijjai kahaṁ imaṁ ammō ! | paḍhamaṁ ciya payaḍijjai vivāhasamaē jahiṁ ēyaṁ || 446 |
caumaṁḍalagāvattaṇajchalēṇa saṁsāraca ugaibhamaṇaṁ । ghayamahuhuṇaṇamisēṇaṁ kārijjai sayalaguṇadahaṇaṁ ॥ 447॥
kiṇaṇatthaṁ kampakayāṇagassa paḍhamaṁpi hatthasannavva । kannāpāṇiggahakaiyavēṇa dāvijjaē tattha || 448॥
tatō narapatinā bhaṇitaṁ yadyēvaṁ dēvi ! tatastvaṁ śīghram । vraja kumārasamīpaṁ vīvāhārthaṁ ca prajñapaya ॥ 436॥
tataśca pr̥thivīdēvī vrajati kañcukijanēna parikaritā | pārśvē supārśvakumārasya sō'pi dr̥ṣṭā tāmāyatīm ॥437॥
anugacchatyabhimukhamēva saptāṣṭa padāni tathā ca kārayati | āsanadānapramukhāṁ pratipattiṁ tathā ca natvā ||438॥
bhālatalamilitakarakamalasaṁpuṭō vijñapayati kumārō'pi । saṁprati tavāgamanē'mba ! kiṁ kāraṇaṁ kathaya ॥439॥
pr̥thivījananyā bhaṇitaṁ putrāhaṁ prēṣitāsmi dēvēna । tava vīvāha mahōtsavadarśanōtkaṇṭhitō yasmāt ॥ 440 ॥
dēva itarajanō'pi ca, tathā mamāpyētāvacca dāvayati । saṁpratyaprāptapūrvaṁ prāptāni sukhānyanyāni ॥ 441 ॥
tava prasādēnānyē paripūrṇāṁ yanmanōrathāḥ sarvē । tataḥ pratipadyatāṁ kumārō vīvāha mahōtsavaṁ kartum ॥442॥
tat śrutvā kumārō'pi hi prabhaṇatya hō na jānītha mama cittam । nāpi jānītha viṣayasukhaṁ gr̥havāsamapi ca saduḥkhaphalam ॥
yēna vīvāhaviṣaya ēvamullapatha, tayā tatō bhaṇitam । jānīmaḥ sarvē kiṁpunaralaṅghanīyaṁ ca pitr̥vacanam ॥444॥
na khalu yuṣmākaṁ paścimavayasyapi durlabhō hi gr̥haparityāgaḥ । pratikūlayipyati dēvaḥ paripūrṇamanōrathō na tvām ॥445॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ kumārēṇa pratipadyēta kathamidamamba ! | prathamamēva prakaṭyatē vivāhasamayē yasminnētat ||446॥
caturmaṇḍalakāvartanacchalēna saṁsāracaturgatibhramaṇam । ghr̥tamadhuhavanamiṣēṇa kāryatē sakalaguṇadahanam ||447॥
krayārthaṁ karmar̥yāṇakasya prathamamapi hastasaṁjñēva । kanyāpāṇigrahakaitavēna dāpyatē tatra ॥ 448 ॥
caturdikṣvapyayaśastaruṇīgīyamānamaṅgalacchalēna । bhāvyatē kiṁ bahunā yadyadiha sūkṣmabucyā ॥449॥

cāuddisiṁpi ajasō taruṇīgijjaṁtamaṁgalacchalēṇaṁ । bhāvijjai kiṁbahuṇā jaṁ jaṁ iha suhumabuddhī ||449||
citijjai taṁ savvaṁ rōmuddhōsaṁ jaṇēi maha ammō ! | tā muṁcasu paḍibaṁdha aṇujāṇaha maṁ vayaggahaṇē ॥ 450 ॥
ēvaṁ bhaṇiē pahuṇā jaṁpai dēvī kumāra ! kiṁ juttō | tumhārisāṇa kāuṁ ammāpiupatthaṇābhaṁgō ? ।।451 ॥
iya bhaṇiē dēvīē mahōvarōhēṇa nirahilāsōvi । paḍivajjai kahakahavi hu kumarō kāuṁ vivāhamahaṁ ॥ 452 ॥
tō parituṭṭhā dēvī sāhai gaṁtūṇa niyayanāharusa । ētthaṁtarammi supaiharāyamatthāṇamuvavihaṁ ॥ 453 ||
karakaliyakamaladaṁḍā bhālayalanilīṇaaṁjalipuḍā ya । paḍihārī sukkarisaṁ namiuṁ vinnaviumāraddhā || 454 ||
riumaddaṇassa rannō maṁtī maisāarōtti vikkhāō | cihna tumhāṇaṁ daṁsaṇūsuō dārasamma ||455 ||
tattha ya kō āēsō tō bhaṇiyaṁ rāiṇā pavēsēhiṁ । sigdhaṁ ciya jaṁ dēvō samāṇavēitti bhaṇiūṇa ॥ 456 ॥
sō desynāō pavisēuṁ paṇamiūṇa naranāhaṁ । dināsaṇī niviṭṭhō puṭṭhō sō uciyapatthāvē ॥ 457॥
sāgayavayaṇaṁ tēṇavi saṁlattaṁ taṁ tuha pasāēṇa । tattō ya sōvi sāhai jaha tuha mittēṇa naravaiṇā || 458॥
riumaddaṇēṇa rannā niyakannā sirisupāsakumarassa | sōmā nāmēṇa varāya sayaṁvarā pēsiyā dēva ! ।।459 ॥
ētō tuma pamāṇaṁti jaṁpiē nivaraṇāvi tō tīsē । dāvāviō visālō nivāsa hēu supāsāō || 460 ॥
taha pēsiyā rasavaī sayalā takkālauciyapaḍivattī । kāraviyā tō maṁtī visajjiō niyayaāvāsē ||461 ॥
tō tēṇa samārō kāuṁ vīvāhuvakamō tattha । baṁdhāviyā ya maṁcā dinnāī āsaṇāī taha || 462 ||
vivihēsu kammēsuṁ nirūviyā kiṁkarā taō vihiyaṁ । varavēigāvimāṇaṁ raṁbhāraṁbhubbhiyapaḍāyaṁ ॥ 463॥
cintyatē tat sarvaṁ rōmōddharṣē janayati mamāmba ! । tasmānmuñca pratibandhamanujānīhi māṁ vratagrahaṇē ॥ 450 ॥
ēvaṁ bhaṇitē prabhuṇā jalpati dēvī kumāra ! kiṁ yuktaḥ । yuṣmādr̥śānāṁ kartuṁ mātāpitr̥prārthanābhaṅgaḥ 1 ॥ 411 ॥
iti bhaṇitē dēvyā mahōparōdhēna nirabhilāṣō'pi । pratipadyatē kathaṁ kathamapi hi kumāraḥ kartuṁ vivāha maham ॥ 492 ॥
tataḥ parituṣṭā dēvī kathayati gatvā nijakanātham । atrāntarē supratiṣṭharājamāsthānamupaviṣṭam ||453॥
karakalitakamaladaṇḍā bhālatalanilīnāñjalipuṭā ca । pratīhārī sōtkarṣa natvā vijñapayitumārabdhā ||454॥
ripumardanasya rājñō mantrī matisāgara iti vikhyātaḥ । tiṣṭhati yuṣmākaṁ darśanōtsukō dvāradē ||455॥
tatra ca ka ādēśastatō bhaṇitaṁ rājñā pravēśaya । śīghramēva yad dēvaḥ samājñapayatīti bhāṇatvā ॥ 456 ॥
sa tayā'nujñātaḥ praviśya praṇamya naranātham । dattāsanō niviṣṭaḥ pr̥ṣṭaḥ sa ucitaprastāvē || 457॥
svāgatavacanaṁ tēnāpi saṁlaptaṁ tat tava prasādēna । tataśca sō'pi kathayati yathā tava mitrēṇa narapatinā ॥ 458 ॥
ripumardanēna rājñā nijakanyā śrīsupārśvakumārāya । sōmā nāmnā varāya svayaṁvarā prēṣitā dēva ! || 459 ||
itō yūyaṁ pramāṇamiti jalpitē nr̥patināpi tatastasmai । dāpitō viśālō nivāsa hētōḥ suprāsādaḥ ॥ 460॥
tathā prēṣitā rasavatī sakalā tatkālōcitapratipattiḥ । kāritā tatō mantrī visarjitō nijakāvāsē ॥ 461॥
tatastēna samārabdhaḥ kartu vīvāhōpakramastatra । bandhitāśca mañccā dattānyāsanāni tatra ॥ 462 ॥
vividhēṣu karmasu nirūpitāḥ kiṅkarāstatō vihitam । varavēdikā vimānaṁ rambhāstanbhōvakr̥tapatākam ||463 ॥

maragayamaṇiparimaṁḍiyavarakaṁcaṇakalasavirayaṇākaliyaṁ । savvattha nivēsiyarayaṇa kiraṇapāḍahaṇiyatamapasaraṁ ||
ēvaṁ kālōciyamannaṁpi hu savvahāvi kāūṇa । maisāyarēṇa tattō kahāviaṁ nivaiṇō ē || 465॥
jaha saṁpai supasatthaṁ hatthagrahaṇē muhuttamainiyaḍaṁ | tō kumaraṁ ghittūṇaṁ tubbhē āgacchaha ihaṁti ॥ 466 ॥
rannāvi puidēvī bhaṇiyā sigdhaṁ karēha kumarassa । puṁkhaṇagāivihāṇaṁ saṁpai sumuhuttamāsannaṁ ॥467॥
tō savvā dēvīu guruppamōēṇa bahuppayārēhiṁ । puṁkhēūṇaṁ maṁgalapurassaraṁ havahiṁ rakumaraṁ ||468 ||
tattō ya niyaṁsāhi mahagghamullāī siyadugullāī । kāyavyavihiṁ savvaṁ kārāvahiṁ taha ya sēsaṁpi ।।469 ।।
taṁ jahā;
gōsīsacaṁdaṇuṣpaṁkalittagattō virāyaē kumarō । sārayasasaṁkajōṇhāē dhavaliō kaṇayasēlōvva ॥ 470 ॥
maṁdārakusumagucchēhiṁ chāiō jassa kuṁtalakalāvō । kasiṇō rēhai tārāvirāiō nahavibhāgōvva ॥ 471 ॥
savvatthārōviyara yaṇaruira āharaṇabhūmipasarīrō । dēvō rōhaṇasēlō jaṁgamattaṁ gaō sahai ||472 ||
ki bahuṇā;
sahāviyapi rūvaṁ na jassa sakkōvi sāhiu tarai । kiṁ puṇa kaṇayavibhūsaṇabhūsiva dēhassa tassa tayā ? || 473 ||
ēvaṁ kayakācvē kumarammi nivēśyaṁ nariṁdassa । tēṇavi niyayā purisā nirūviyā jaha lahuṁ tubbhē ||474 ||
mēlēha nāyakhattiyavaggaṁ sayalaṁpi taha payaṭṭēha । nayarīmahūsavaṁ taha kumarassa samappaha pahāṇaṁ || 475 ||
1
marakatamaṇiparimaṇḍitavarakāñcanakalaśaviracanākalitam । sarvatra nivēśitaratna kiraṇapratihatatamaḥ prasaram ॥ 464 ॥
ēvaṁ tatkālōcitamanyadapi khalu sarvathāpi kr̥tvā । matisāgarēṇa tataḥ kathitaṁ nr̥patērēvam ||469 ॥
yathā saṁprati supraśastaṁ hastagrahaṇē muhūrtamatinikaṭam । tataḥ kumāraṁ gr̥hītvā yūyamāgacchatēti ॥ 466॥
rājñāpi pr̥thivīdēvī bhaṇitā śīghraṁ kuruta kumārasya । puṅkhanakādividhānaṁ saṁprati sumuhūrtamāsannam ||467 ॥
tataḥ sarvā dēvyō gurupramōdēna bahuprakāraiḥ । puṅkhayitvā maṅgalapurassaraṁ snapayanti varakumāram ||468 ||
tataśca nivāsayanti mahārghamūlyāni sitadukūlāni । kartavyavidhiṁ sarvaṁ kārayanti tathā ca śēṣamapi ||469 ||

niṁdas niyaṁvabissa attaṇō kāvi aimahaṁtaṁpi । turiyaṁ kumārakhvassa daṁsaṇē gaṁtumataraṁtī || 204 |

annā pabhaṇai muddhē ! mā jaṁpaha ērisa jaō tattha । aṁgaṁ piīsarēṇa dēddhaṁ kaṁtī puṇō dūrē || 509 ॥
tō bhai halē ! sakkō ēsō ēsā. saī ya tassa piyā । iyarāvi bhaṇai vālē ! nūṇaṁ maivibbhamō tujjha ॥ 510 ॥
jaṁ tassa lōyaṇēhiṁ savvatō dūsiyaṁ sarīraṁpi । nūṇaṁ supāsakumarō ēsō, sōmā puṇō ēsā ॥ 511 ॥

ēvaṁ ca kumāradarśanōtkaṇṭhātyaktagēhakarmaṇām । rājantītthamālāpavibhramāḥ purapurandhrīṇām ॥903॥

sukumālapādakaratalanirupamarūpōpaśōbhitaśarīram । tanukāntiprasaradhavalitajanmabhavanaṁ sukhaṁ prāptam ॥ 127॥
ucitasamayē ca śrīśēkhara iti nāma mahāvibhūtyā । tasya kr̥taṁ tataḥ sō'pi hi pañcabhirdhātrībhiḥ parikaritaḥ ॥ 128॥
parivardhitumārabdhaḥ svayaṁvarābhiḥ kalābhiḥ sakalābhiḥ । āgatya vr̥tō vinā prayatnamapi, itaśca ॥ 129॥
yāvat śrīsupārśvarājastiṣṭhati bhavanasyōparyupaviṣṭaḥ । tāvat paśyati vicchāyaṁ gaganē ravimaṇḍalaṁ sahasā ॥ 130 ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
karavattasarisadādākaḍappaduṣpiccha rāhuṇā ghatthaṁ । thērīṇavi uḍḍhamuhāṇa kāmamavalōyaṇijjaṁ ca ॥ 531 ॥
taha saharisaparidhāviratimira mahārakkhasēṇa duṭṭhēṇa । kavalijjataṁ picchara gayaṇapaēsaṁ samapi || 532 ||
ētthaṁtarammi māhaṇakuṭuṁbiṇīṇaṁ saputtagahiyāṇaṁ । muṁcasu sūraṁ rāhuti pukaraṁtīṇa halavalaṁ ||533||
sōūṇa aiss diṭṭhi dharaṇīyalē tāva cakamihuṇāī । dōsaṁdhayārasaṁkāē vihaḍamāṇāī picchē || 534 ||
taha ya viḍaṁbiṁjjaṁtāī kōsiēhiṁ vaṇēsu līṇāī । saṁkuiya aṁguvaṁgāī vāyasīṇaṁ sarāī ||535 ||
taha aggihōttiēhiṁ maṁtaravittē hi mahughayāīhiṁ । tammōyaṇānimittaṁ huṇijjamāṇassa jalaṇassa || 536 |
dhūmapaḍalēṇa saṁchāiyammi gayaṇammi mēhasakāē । dhuyapakkhaurḍa picchai haṁsaulaṁ māṇasē caliyaṁ ॥ 537||
taha mēhāgamasaṁsiyaāgamaṇāṇaṁ paṇa muddhāō । maggamavalōyamāṇīu niyai pāusiyadaiyāō || 538 || -
tattō khaṇamēttēṇaṁ dhūmēṇa mī uvva uvvamai । rāhū raviṇō biṁbaṁ samuttichēyammi tattō ya ॥ 539॥
sutthāvatthaṁ jāyaṁ bhuvaṇaṁ sacarācaraṁpi jā niyai । tā vivai puṇō diṭṭhi rāyā gayaṇaṁgaṇā bhimu || 540 ||
tattha ya viyaliyatimiraṁ disāṇa cakaṁ samaggalapayāvaṁ । acchīhi duṣpicchaṁ tēēṇaṁ niyai ravirvivaṁ ॥ 541 ॥
tō takkhaṇapaṇa takhadiṭṭhē ca pāsiuṁ rāyā । khaṇigattabhāvaṇaṁ ciya bhāvēuṁ sō samārō || 542 ||
jaṁha ēsō sūrōbihu gasijjaē rāhuṇā haṭēṇāvi । taha pāṇiṇō gasijjaṁti maccuṇā nūṇa saṁsārē || 543 ॥
taha ēyammivi sōkkhaṁ jaṁ kiṁpi hu taṁpi dukkhaparikaliyaṁ । causuvi gaīsu, lōyā tahavi hu ēyammi vāmūḍhā । 2 44 ।
karapatrasadr̥śadaṁṣṭrā nikara durdarśarāhuṇā grastam | sthavirāṇāmapyūrdhvamukhānāṁ kāmamavalōkanīyaṁ ca ॥131॥
tathā saharṣaparidhāvanaśīlatimiramahārākṣasēna duṣṭēna । kavalyamānaṁ paśyati gaganapradēśaṁ samagramapi ॥ 532॥
atrāntarē brāhmaṇakuṭumbinīnāṁ svaputragr̥hītānām । muñca sūraṁ rāhō ! iti pūtkurvatīnāṁ tumulam ॥133॥
śrutvā kṣipati dr̥ṣṭiṁ dharaṇītalē tāvaccakramithunāni । dōṣāndhakāraśaṅkayā vighaṭamānāni paśyati ||1.34 ||
tathā ca viḍambyamānāni kauśikairvanēṣu līnāni । saṁkucitāṅgōpāṅgāni vāyasīnāṁ śarīrāṇi ॥ 939 ॥
tathāgnihōtrikairmantrapavitrairmadhughr̥tādibhiḥ । tanmōcanānimittaṁ hūyamānasya jvalanasya ॥136॥
dhūmapaṭalēna saṁchāditē gaganē mēghaśaṅkayā । dhutapakṣapuṭaṁ paśyati haṁsakulaṁ mānasē calitam ॥137॥
tathā mēghāgamaśaṁsitāgamanānāṁ patīnāṁ mugdhāḥ । mārgamavalōkamānāḥ paśyati prātivēśmikadayitāḥ ||538 |
tataḥ kṣaṇamātrēṇa dhūmēna manika ivōdvamati । rāhū ravērbimbaṁ svabhukticchēdē tataśca ॥ 139 ॥
susthānasthaṁ jātaṁ bhuvanaṁ sacarācaramapi yāvat paśyati । tāvat kṣipati punardr̥ṣṭiṁ rājā gaganāṅgaṇābhimukham ||540||
tatra ca vigalitatimiraṁ diśāṁ cakraṁ samargalapratām । akṣibhyāṁ durdarśa tējasā paśyati ravivimbam ॥541॥
tatastatkṣaṇapranaṣṭaṁ tatkṣaṇadr̥ṣṭaṁ ca dr̥ṣṭvā rājā । kṣaṇaikatvabhāvanāmēva bhāvayituṁ sa samārabdhaḥ ॥142॥
yathaiṣa sūrō'pi khalu grasyatē rāhuṇā haṭhēnāpi । tathā prāṇinō grasyantē mr̥tyunā nūnaṁ saṁsārē ॥ 143 ॥
tathaitasminnapi saukhyaṁ yat kimapi hi tadapi duḥkhaparikalitam । catasr̥ṣvapi gatiṣu, lōkāstathāpyētasmintryāmūḍhāḥ ॥

dukkhaṁ sahati pattā taruṇīṇaṁ nayaṇavāgurāvisayaṁ । mayaṇamahāpāra ddhiyanisāyabāṇāvalīviddhā ॥ 545 ॥
tattō apārasaṁsāra dukkhadāvānalammi tē nūṇaṁ । aparittāṇā puṇaravi iṁdhaṇaka pacciya havaṁti ॥ 246 ॥

ētyaṁtara mmi kaṁpiyasiṁhāsanā ōhināyaniyakiccā । naravarasupāsapāsaṁ samāgayā lahū imē tiyasā । 548 |
sārasyamāiccā vahiṁvaruṇā ya gaddatōyā ya । tusiyāṁ avvābāhā aggiccā cēvariṭṭhā ya ॥549 ॥
namirutta maṁgaviyalaṁtasura himaṁdārakusumasaṁghāyā । viṇaēṇaṁ jiṇanāhaṁ thōḍaṁ ēvaṁ samāraddhā ॥ 550 ॥
jayasi tumaṁ bhuvaṇāvalisarōjavaṇasaṁḍacaṁḍamāyaṁḍa ! | vammahamayaṁdha siṁdhurakuṁbhayaḍaviyāraṇamayaṁda ! || 551 ॥
muttivahūkaṁṭhaggahaukkaṁṭhiya! maliyamōhamāhappa ! | tujjha namō tihuyaṇara kkhaṇakkhaṇiya ! paramakāruṇiya ।। 552 ।
iya thōūṇaṁ pabhaṇati tuha purō dēva ! amha kā gaṇaṇā । khajjōyāṇava sūrassa rurddhadhayārassa ? ।। 553 ॥
tahavi niyayāhigārāṇurūvamamhēvi kiṁpi vinnavimō । sumaraṇamittanimittaṁ tuha puraō na uṇa uvaēsō ।। 554 ॥
pabvajjaṁ paḍivajjasu bhavaduhavaṇadahaṇajalaṇajālōliṁ । taha ya payaṭṭasu sigdhaṁ aṇatthanimmaṁthaṇaṁ tithaṁ ॥ 555 ॥
taha pahu ! payaṁḍapāsaṁḍidēsaṇātimira niyara aṁtariyaṁ । payaḍasu sivamaggaṁ vimalanāṇarayaṇapaīvēṇa || 556 ||
iya lōgaṁtiyadēvōvaēsadguṇappavaḍhiullāsō । savisēsaṁ saṁjāō siddhibahūsaṁgamāsaṁsī ॥ 557 ॥
ēvaṁ vinavaṇaṁ gaēsu tēsuṁ supāsanaranāhō । vārasiyamahādāṇaṁ dāum̐ paricitaē jāva ।। 558||
duḥkhaṁ sahantē prāptāstaruṇīnāṁ nayanavāgurāviṣayam । madanamahāvyādhiniśātabāṇāvalī viddhāḥ ॥945॥
tatō'pārasaṁsāraduḥkhadāvānalē tē nūnam । aparitrāṇāḥ punarapīndhanakalpā ēva bhavanti ॥146॥
tasmādētasmāt kārāgarādiva yujyatē palāyitum । bhaktvēdānīṁ putravadhūsnēha nigaḍān ॥547॥
atrāntarē kampitasiṁhāsanā avadhijñātanijakr̥tyāḥ । naravarasupārśvapārśvaṁ samāgatā ladhvimē tridaśāḥ ।। 548॥
sārasvatādityā vahnivaruṇāśca gardatōyāṁśca । tuṣitā avyābādhā āgnēyāścaivāriṣṭāśca ॥ 149 ॥
namrōttamāṅgavigalatsurabhimandārakusumasaṁghātāḥ । vinayēna jinanāthaṁ stōtumēvaṁ samārabdhāḥ ||150 ॥
jayasi tvaṁ bhuvanāvalisarōjavanapaṇḍacaṇḍamārtaṇḍa ! | manmathamadāndhasindhurakumbhataṭa vidāraṇamr̥gēndra ! ॥ 151 ॥
muktivadhū kaṇṭhagrahōtkaṇṭhita ! marditamōha māhātmya || tubhyaṁ namastribhuvana rakṣaṇākṣaṇika ! paramakāruṇika ! | 552॥
iti stutvā prabhaṇanti tava purō dēva ! asmākaṁ kā gaṇanā । khadyōtānāmiva sūrasya dūraruddhāndhakārasya ? ||553॥
tathāpi nijakādhikārānurūpaṁ vayamapiṁ kimapi vijñapayāmaḥ । smaraṇamātranimittaṁ tava puratō na punarupadēśaḥ || 554 ॥
pravrajyāṁ pratipadyasva bhavaduḥkhavanadahanajvalanajvālālim । tathā ca pravartaya śīghramanarthanirmanthanaṁ tīrtham ||555॥
tathā prabhō ! pracaṇḍapāṣaṇḍidēśanātimiranikarāntaritam । prakaṭaya śivamārga vimalajñānaratnapradīpēna ॥ 5.56 ॥
iti lōkāntikadēvōpadēśadviguṇapravardhitōllāsaḥ । saviśēṣaṁ saṁjātaḥ siddhivadhūsaṁgamāśaṁsī ॥157॥
ēvaṁ vijñapya gatēṣu tēṣu supāśvanaranāthaḥ । vārṣikamahādānaṁ dātuṁ paricintayati yāvat ॥198॥

supāsanāha-cariammi-
tā takkhapi caliyaṁ sīhāsaṇamamalarayaṇapahapayaḍaṁ । sōhammadēvalōē suhāsaṇatthassa sakkssa ।। 559 ॥
taccalaṇāṇaṁtara avahiṇā ya nāūṇa jiṇamaṇaviyaṣpaṁ । sō sattaha, payāī uṭṭiya gaṁtūṇa tayabhimuṁha || 560 ॥
thōūṇa jiṇaṁ ciṁtimāraddhō jaha supāsajiṇanā hō । icchai dāṇaṁ dāum̐ āvarisaṁ tassa tō majjha ॥ 561॥
jujjai dhaṇasaṁpatti kāuṁ, iya takkhaṇaṁpi vēsamaṇaṁ । āṇavai jahā nikkhamaṇadāṇajōggaṁ jiṇagihammi ॥ 562॥
vivasu pabhūyaṁ kaṇagaṁ, iya sōuṁ sakkasāsaṇaṁ sōviṁ । āṇavai jaṁbhagasurē paḍicchiuṁ tēvi viṇaṇa || 563 ॥
jiṇa maṁdirammi varisaṁti kaṇayarāsiṁ taō ya bhayavapi । caccaraca ukkaca umuhamahāpahappamuhaṭhāṇēsu || 564 ||
aṇavikkhiyamuhamaṇitrāriyaṁ ca varavariyaghōsaṇāpuvvaṁ । savvāṇa viēgatthaṁ patthaṇauttāṇiyakarāṇaṁ ।। 265 ।। .
aṇudiyahaṁ dāvāvara kaṇayaṁ, tassāvi dijjamāṇassa । divasē divasē dijjai aḍalakkhahiyā kaṇayakōḍī ॥566॥
aha navapariṇayalavalīphalabharathavalāē dhavaliyā tassa । aṇavaśyakaṇayadāṇubbhavāē kittīē disinivahāṁ ॥
tattōya dūradēsā kē iṁtēsu maggaṇagaṇēsuṁ । annēsuṁ ca hiraṇṇaṁ gahiūṇa niyattamāṇēsu || 568 ||
ruṁdāsurityā vāṇārasipuravarī majjhami । dukkhēṇa bhamai lōō niddayaniddaliyavacchayalō ||669 ॥
ēttha tavaṇijjapuṁjē ēttha ya vatthē pavittharaha sigyaṁ । ēttha ya rayaṇukēraṁ maggaṇajōgaṁ nivēsēha || 570 ॥
iha kariturarrahāī ṭhāvaha viraha ēttha vilāō | bhōaṇasālāu tahā āhāratthaṁ vidēsīṇaṁ ॥ 571 ॥
ēvaṁ dāṇanimittaṁ niuttapurisāṇa vaccharaṁ jāva | aṇisaṁ samāisaṁtāṇa kiṁ karē havai ullāvō || 572 ।।
tāvat tatkṣaṇamapi calitaṁ siṁhāsanamamalaratnaprabhāprakaṭam । saudharmadēvalōkē sukhāsanasthasya śakrasya ॥159॥
taccalanānantaramavadhinā ca jñālā jinamanōvikalpam । sa saptāṣṭa padāni utthāya gatvā tadabhimukham ॥ 960 ॥
stutvā jinaṁ cintayitumārabdhō yathā supārśvajinanāthaḥ । icchati dānaṁ dātumāvarṣaṁ tasya tatō mama ॥ 561 ||
yujyatē dhanasaṁpattiṁ kartumiti tatkṣaṇamapi vaiśramaṇam । ājñapayati yathā niṣkramaṇadānayōgyaṁ jinagr̥hē ॥ 962 ॥
kṣipa prabhūtaṁ kanakam, iti śrutvā śakraśāsanaṁ sō'pi । ājñapayati jr̥mbhakasurān pratyēṣṭuṁ tē'pi vinayēna ॥563॥
jinamandirē varṣanti kanakarāśiṁ tataśca bhagavānapi । catvara catuṣkacaturmukhamahāpathapramukhasthānēṣu ||564 ॥
anavēkṣitamukhamanivāritaṁ ca varavarikāghōṣaṇāpūrvam । sarvēbhyō vivēkārtha prārthanōttānitakarēbhyaḥ || 165॥
anudivasaṁ dāpyatē kanakaṁ, tasyāpi dīyamānasya । divasē divasē dīyatē'ṣṭalakṣādhikā kanakakōṭiḥ ॥ 166 ॥
atha navapariṇayalavalīphalabharadhaṁvalayā dhavalitāstasya । anavaratakanakadānōdbhavayā kīrttyā diṅnivahāḥ ।। 567॥
tataśca dūradēśāt kēṣvapyāyatsu mārgaṇagaṇēṣu । anyēṣu ca hiraṇyaṁ gr̥hītvā nivartamānēṣu ॥ 968 ॥
viśālāsvapi rathyāsu vārāṇasī puravarāyā madhyē | duḥkhēna bhramati lōkō nirdaya nirdalitavakṣastalaḥ ॥ 169॥
atra tapanīyapuñjānatra ca vastrāṇi pravistr̥ṇīta śīghram । atra ca ratnōtkaraṁ mārgaṇayōgyaṁ nivēśayata ॥ 970॥
iha karituragarathādīn sthāpayata viracayatātra vipulāḥ । bhōjanaśālāstathā''hārārthaṁ vidēśinām ||571 ॥
ēvaṁ dānanimittaṁ niyuktapuruṣāṇāṁ vatsaraṁ yāvat । aniśaṁ samādiśatāṁ kiṁ kurvē bhavatyullāpaḥ || 572॥

73
tinnēva ya. kōḍisayā aṭṭhāsīyaṁ ca huti kōḍīō । asiyaṁ ca sayasahassā savvaṁkō vaiyakaṇayassa॥573 ॥
iya āvarisaṁ kaṁcaṇavarisēṇaṁ tapiūṇa bhavaṇaṁpi । nimmaragaṇaṁ vihēḍaṁ saddāvara maṁtiṇō rāyā ॥ 574 ||
taha talavarasēṇā hivakō sāhivamaṁḍalīyasāmaṁtē । nayarīpahāṇalōēṇa saṁjuē, tāṇa pañcakkhaṁ ||575 ||
viḍaṁ savvaṁpi hu kumārē sirisēharammi niyarajjaṁ । nīitti daṁtakaṁti virayaṁtō bhaṇai vayaṇamiṇaṁ ॥ 576 ।।
tumhāṇa ēsa sāmī dēvāṇupiyāṇumannaha iyāṇi । maṁ savvaviraiggahaṇē, tēvi husōūṇa vimhaiyā || 577 ||
jaṁpati vajjamaiyā savaṇā amhāṇa nūṇa jē ajja । bahirattaṇaṁ na pattā imāē vayaṇāsaṇī lahuṁ ॥ 578 ||
iya ēvamāisakaluṇavayaṇāṇi paraṁparā kahakahaṁpi । aṇumannati nariṁdaṁ gurunibbaṁdhēṇa jaṁpataṁ ॥ 579 ॥
aha sirisēhararāyā nayaṇaṁ sunivāyamaiiliyakavōlō । calaṇēsu nivaḍiūṇaṁ vinnavai kahaṁpi jayaguruṇō ॥ 580 ॥
jaivi parivīṇamōhā tubbhē viraiyā ya savvaviraīē। tahavi hu nikkhamaṇamahaṁ paḍivajjaha majjha pasiūṇa || 581 ॥
tassuvarōhēṇa imaṁ paḍisuṇai supāsajiṇavarō tattō । sirisēhara nivaāṇāpavattiyā vēttiā turiyaṁ ॥ 582॥
aṭṭuttaraṁ sahassaṁ suvannakalasāṇu tattha āṇiti । suprasatthatitthasalilaṁ divvāō tahōsahīō ya ।। 583 ॥
ghaṇasāramīsacaṁdaṇapamuhāī vilēvaṇāī surahīṇi । jiṇamajjaṇatthamuvaṇiti tattha, ētthantarē tāva ॥ 584 |
battīsaṁpi suriṁdā kaṁpiyasīhāsaṇā muṇēūṇa । ōhīē paramatthaṁ pavaravimāṇēsu ārūḍhā || 585||
viyasiyasayavattāvisālalōyaṇā jōvvaṇubbhaḍavilāsā । bahudēvakōḍikōḍīhi parivuḍā cārurūvadharā।।586॥
trīṇyēva ca kōṭiśatānyaṣṭāśītiśca bhavanti kōṭayaḥ । aśītiśca śatasahasrāṇi sarvāṅkō vyayitakanakasya ॥573॥
ityāvarṣī kāñcanavarṣēṇa tarpayitvā bhavanamapi । nirmāṇaṁ vidhāya śabdāyayati mantriṇō rājā ॥ 974 ॥
tathā talavarasēnādhipakōśādhipamaṇḍalika sāmantān । nagarīpradhāna lōkēna saṁyutān tēṣāṁ pratyakṣam ॥ 175 ॥
sthāpayitvā sarvāṅgamapi hi kumārē śrīśēkharē nijarājyam । nītiriti dantakānti viracayanbhaṇati vacanamidam ॥
yuṣmākamēva svāmī dēvānupriyāḥ ! anumanyadhvamidānīm । māṁ sarvaviratigrahaṇē, tē'pi khalu śrutvā vismitāḥ ॥
jalpanti vajramayāḥ śravaṇā asmākaṁ nūnaṁ yē'dya । badhiratvaṁ na prāptā anēna vacanāśaninā laghu ॥ 578 ॥
ityēvamādisakaruṇavacanāni prajalpitāraḥ kathaṁkathamapi । anumanyantē narēndraṁ gurunibandhēna jalpantam ॥579 ॥
atha śrīśēkhararājō nayanāśrunipātamalinitakapōlaḥ । caraṇayōrnipatya vijñapayati kathamapi jagadgurūn ॥ 580 ॥
yadyapi, parikṣīṇamōhā yūyaṁ viratāśca sarvavaratyāḥ । tathāpi khalu niṣkramaṇamahaṁ pratipadyadhvaṁ mama prasīdya ॥ 181॥
tasyōparōdhēnēmaṁ pratiśr̥ṇōti supārśvajinavarastataḥ । śrīśēkharanr̥pājñāpravartitā vaitrikāstvaritam ॥182॥
aṣṭōttaraṁ sahasraṁ suvarṇa kalaśānāṁ tatrānayanti । supraśastatīrthasalilaṁ divyāstathaiauṣadhīśca ॥ 183 ॥
ghanasāra miśracandanapramukhāni vilēpanāni surabhīṇi । jinamajjanārthamupanayanti tatra, atrāntarē tāvat ॥ 584 ॥
dvātriṁśadapi surēndrāḥ kampitasiṁhāsanā jñātvā ! avadhinā paramārthaṁ pravaravimānēṣvārūḍhāḥ ||585||
vikasitaśatapatraviśālalōcanā yauvanōdbhaṭa vilāsāḥ । bahudēva kōṭi kōṭibhiḥ parivr̥tāścārurūpadhasaḥ ||586॥

paḍupaiḍahasaṁkhakāhalamuiṁgatalimāitūraghōsēṇa । bahiriyabaṁbhaṁḍā jiṇavariṁdapāsaṁ samallīṇā || 587 ||
jayapahuṇō payapamaṁ tipayāhiṇapuvvagaṁ paṇamiūṇa । bhavaṇaṁgaṇē nisannā jiṇapayacinnāsasupaitē || 1588 ॥
aha accuyasakēṇaṁ niyadēvā paraṇiyā jahā sigdhaṁ । nivvattēha samaggaṁ nikkhamaṇa bhisēyasāmaggiṁ ॥ 589 ॥
jiṇavara dikkhāsamautti ēyamāyanniḍaṁ kayapaṇāmā । pavarakaṇayāikala sē khīrōyajalēṇa paḍinē ॥ 590 ॥
susugaṁdhapupphapaḍalāī tahaya annaṁ ca jaṁpi pāu । supahāṇavatthunivahaṁ accuyasakkassa uvarṇiti ।। 591 ॥
tattō accuyatiyasāhivōvi dēvēhiṁ parigaō tēhiṁ । kaṇayāimahākuṁbhēhiṁ advasāhassasaṁkhēhiṁ ॥ 592 ॥
divvōsa himīsēhiṁ maṁdiramaṁdaraṭṭhiyaṁ jiṇavariṁdaṁ । harisullasaṁtadēhō ahisiṁcai garuyabhattīē ॥ 593 ॥
ēvaṁ surāhivaraṇa sēsāvi hu caṁdasūrapajjaṁtā । majjaṁti jiṇaṁ tō tēsu saṁṭhiēsuṁ saṭhāṇammi || 594 ||
sirisēharanaranāhō viṇayaparō appamattacittō ya । bhattīē dukūlaṁcalanimmiyamuhakōsa vinnāsō ॥ 596 ॥
puvvaṇīhi tēhi kaṇayāimarahiṁ kalasasahassēhiṁ । titthajalapūriēhiṁ majjēi jiṇaṁ jaēkapahuṁ ॥ 596 ॥
ēvaṁ ca vaṭṭamāṇē jiṇavaramajjaṇamahūsavē tattha । kēvi suriṁdā cāliti ubhayapakkhēsu siyacamarē || 597 ||
kēvi hu dhavalimanijjiyasiyasayavattāī āyavattāī । dhāriti vvaṁti purō akhaṁpaṇaṁ dappaṇaṁ kēvi ॥ 598 ॥
uppāḍiti ya ḍajāṁtaagurughaṇasāradhūvadhūmēṇa । aṁdhāriyadisivalayaṁ varadhūvakaḍacchrayaṁ kēvi ॥599 ॥
paṇavannakusumamālāu parimalā miliyabhasalamālāō । kēvi pêyaraṁti annē ya pajjuvāsiṁti bhayavaṁtaṁ ॥ 600॥
aha nivvattē majjaṇamahammi sirisēharēṇa naravaiṇā । sīhāsaṇamannayaraṁ ṭhāviyamaha uttarābhimuhaṁ || 601 ॥

paṭupaṭahaśaṅkhakāhalamr̥daṅgatalimāditūraghōṣēṇa । badhiritabrahmāṇḍā jinavarēndrapārśvaṁ samālīnāḥ ||587 ||
jagatprabhōḥ pādapadmaṁ tripradakṣiṇā pūrvakaṁ praṇamya । bhavanāṅgaṇē niṣaṇṇā jinapādavinyāsasupavitrē ॥ 588 ॥
athācyutaśakrēṇa nijadēvāḥ prabhaṇitā yathā śīghram । nirvartayata samagrāṁ niṣkramaṇābhiṣēkasāmagrīm ||589 ॥
jinavaradīkṣāsamaya ityēvamākarṇya kr̥tapraṇāmāḥ । pravarakanakādikalaśān kṣīrōdajalēna paripūrṇān ॥ 990 ॥
susugandhapuṣpapaṭalāni tathānyaṁ ca yadapi prāyōgyam । supradhānavastunivahamacyutaśakramupanayanti ॥591॥
tatō 'cyutatridaśādhipō'pi dēvaiḥ parigatastaiḥ । kanakādimahākumbhairaṣṭasaha susaṁkhyaiḥ || 592 ||

śrī śēkharanaranāthō vinayaparō'pramattacittaśca । bhaktyā dukūlāñcalanirmitamukhakōśavinyāsaḥ ||995 ॥
pūrvōpanītaistaiḥ kanakādimayaiḥ kalaśasahasraiḥ । tīrthajalapūritairmajjayati jinaṁ jagadēkaprabhum ॥ 596 ॥
ēvaṁ ca vartamānē jinavaramajjanamahōtsavē tatra । kē'pi surēndrāścālayantyubhayapakṣayōḥ sitacāmarān ॥197॥

tattha ṭhiyaṁ ca jiṇidaṁ vhaviūṇaṁ sēyapīyakalasēhiṁ । puvvābhimuhē sīhāsaṇammi nisiyāvaē tattō ॥ 602॥
tatthaṭṭhiyassa suumālāṁdhakāsāila hiyaṁgassa । gōsīsasura hicaṁdaṇacacciyadēhassa dēvassa || 603 ||
parihiyaphalihujjaladēvadūsajuyalassa vacchadē sammi । ghōlaṁtavimalaniccalanavamuttāhalakalāssa ||604||
maṇimaṁḍiyakuṁḍalajualakiraṇakabburiyagaṁḍabhāyassa । rayaṇamayamauḍamaṁḍiyamuddhassa supāsanāhassa || 605 ||
namiūṇa calaṇajuyalaṁ puṇōvi dharaṇiyalanihiyasirakamalā । āsīsāhi thuṇiu : surāsuriṁdā samāraddhā ॥
kahaṁ viya ?
vijayasu kutitthasatthaṁ dalasu mahāmōhamallamāha । ucchiṁdasu micchataṁ muttipahaṁ payaḍasa jaṇāṇa || 607 ॥
pālasu susamaṇadhammaṁ sayalaṁtarasattūsinnanimmahaṇaṁ । kuṇasu jayassavi ajayaṁ raippiyaṁ jayasu taṁ nāha ! ॥ 608 ॥
iya thōḍaṁ bhuvaṇaguruṁ harisiyahiyaēhiṁ savvasahiṁ । sasurāsuramaṇuēhiṁ puraō ya paṭṭiyaṁ na || 609 ॥
ētthaṁtarammi bhāviraniya piuguruvirahaggidūmiyamaṇēṇa । sirisēharēṇa bhaṇiyā niyapurisā bhō jahā sigdhaṁ ।।
tijayapahuṇō nimittaṁ caṁdaṇarasa lihiyasatthiyapasatthaṁ । majjhanivēsiyamaṇimayasapāyavīḍhāsaṇasaṇāhaṁ ॥ 611 ॥
raṁgata vivihacidhaṁ maṇōramānāmiyaṁ mahāsiviyaṁ । nivvattahatti tēvi hu sōūṇaṁ sāmiṇō vayaṇa ||612||
nivvattaṁti tahacciya savvaṁ itthaṁtarammi sakēṇa । harisullasaṁtahiyaēṇa niyasurā ēvamāṇattā ॥ 613 ॥
bhō bhō mahagghamaṇikhaṁḍamaṁḍiyaṁ mukkasuttiōcūlaṁ । tulaṁ maṇōramāē sahassanaravāhiṇi siviyaṁ ॥ 614 ||
atha nirvr̥ttē majjanamahē śrī śēkharēṇa narapatinā । siṁhāsanamanyatarat sthāpitamathōttarābhimukham || 601 ॥
tatra sthitaṁ ca jinēndraṁ napayitvā śvētapītakalaśaiḥ । pūrvābhimukhē siṁhāsanē niṣādayati tataḥ ॥ 602 ||
tatra sthitasya sukumālagandhakāṣā yirūkṣitāṅgasya । gōśīrṣasurabhicandanacarcitadēhasya dēvasya ||603 ॥
parihitasphaṭikōjjvaladēvadūṣyayugalasya vakṣōdēśē । ghūrṇamānavimalaniścalanavamuktāphalakalāpasya ॥ 604 ॥
maṇimaṇḍitakuṇḍalayugala kiraṇarburitagaṇḍabhāgasya । ratnamayamukuṭamaṇḍitamūrdhnaḥ supārśvanāthasya || 605 ॥
natvā caraṇayugalaṁ punarapi dharaṇītala nihitaśiraḥ kamalāḥ । āśīrbhiḥ stōtuṁ surāsurēndrāḥ samārabdhāḥ || 60 6 ॥

kathamiva ?
vijayasva kutīrthasārtha dalaya mahāmōha malamāhātmyam । ucchintsva mithyātvaṁ muktipathaṁ prakaṭaya janānām ॥ 607 ॥
pālaya suśramaṇadharma sakalāntaraśatrusainyanirmanthanam । kuruṣva jagatō'pyajayyaṁ ratipriyaṁ jaya tvaṁ nātha ! || 608 ||
iti stutvā bhuvanaguruṁ harṣitahr̥dayaiḥ sarvaśakraḥ । sasurāsuramanujaiḥ purataśca pravartitaṁ nāṭyam ||609 ॥
atrāntarē bhāvinija pitr̥guruvirahāgnidāvitamanasā । śrīśēkharēṇa bhaṇitā nijapuruṣā bhō yathā śīghram ॥ 61-0 ॥
trijagatprabhōrnimittaṁ candanarasa likhitasvastikapraśastam । madhyanivēśitamaṇimayasapādapīṭhāsana sanātham ||611 ॥
raṅgadvividhacihnāṁ manōramānāmikāṁ mahāśibikām । nirvartayatēti tē'pi hi śrutvā svāminō vacanam || 612 ॥
nirvartayanti tathaiva sarvamatrāntarē śakrēṇa । harṣōllasaddhr̥dayēna nijasurā ēvamājñaptāḥ ॥ 613 ॥ -

supāsanāha cariammi-
raiūṇaṁ vivaha lahuṁ majjhammi maṇōramāē siviyāē । tēvi hu sakkāēsaṁ tahatti kuvvaṁti saṁtuṭṭā || 615॥
aha sirisupāsanāhō sayalālaṁkāralaṁkiyasarīrō । kayachaṭṭatavōkammō tiyasāhiīhi vinnō || 616 ॥
uūṇaṁ sīhāsaṇāō tamaṇuppayāhiṇīkāuṁ । āruhai mahāsiviyaṁ maṇōramaṁ tīē majjhammi ||617॥
puvvābhimuhē maṇirayaṇamaiyasīhā saṇammi uvavihō । tattōvi ammadhāīvi vāmapāsaṁ nisaṇṇā sē || 618 ||
kulamayahariyāvi tahā suibhūyā gahiyapavaranēvatthā | gahiūṇa sāḍayaṁ haṁsalakkhaṇaṁ dāhiṇē pāsē || 619 |
bhāsaṇē nisannā tahā ya sāmissa pacchimadisāē । vara taruṇī siyacchattaṁ dharamāṇī ṭha|i annikā।। 620 ॥
taha caliracavalacāmarajuyalaṁ gahiūṇa dōsu pāsēsuṁ । varavārasuṁdarīō havaṁti siṁgārapavarāō || 621 ॥
uttarapuratthimammi bhāgammi vilāsiṇī havai annā । gahiūṇaṁ bhiṁgāraṁ surakarikaranā lagāgāraṁ ||622॥
ēvaṁ dāhiṇapōratthimammi bhāgammi suṁdarī ēgā । gahiūṇa tālaviṭaṁ karakamalē ṭhāi harisēṇa || 623॥
taha piō ya vēruliyamaiyadaṁḍāī āyavattāī । dhāriti suriṁdā sarayapunnacaṁdappāsāī ||624 ||
taha dōsuvi pāsēsuṁ siviyāē ṭhiyā siēhiṁ camarēhiṁ | sōhammīsāṇiṁdā vīti supāsajiṇayēdaṁ ।। 625 ॥
ētyaṁtara mmi niyasiyasiyavatthā samavayā pavarakhvā । niruvahayaṁgā balasāliṇō ya kayasavvakāyavvā ॥ 626||
rōmaṁcaciyadēhā sahastasaṁkhā narā mahāsiviyaṁ । taṁ sirisēhara naravaravayaṇēṇa ukkhivaṁti huṁ ||627||
vaccatīra tīē sōhammīsāṇanāyagā dōvi । dāhiṇauttarabāhuṁ giṇhaṁti guruppamōēṇa || 628 ||
siviyāē dāhiṇuttarahiṭṭimabāhāō dōvi asurridā । camarabalināmadhēyā harisēṇa samuvvahaṁti taō ॥ 629॥
racayitvā kṣipata laghu madhyē manōramāyāḥ śivikāyāḥ । tē'pi khalu śakrādēśaṁ tathēti kurvanti saṁtuṣṭaḥ ॥ 615॥
atha śrīsupārśvanāthaḥ sakalālaṁkārālaṁkr̥taśarīraḥ । kr̥taṣaṣṭhatapaḥkarmā tridaśādhipatibhirvijñaptaḥ || 6 16॥
utthāya siṁhāsanāt tāmanupradakṣiṇīkr̥tya । ārōhati mahāśibikāṁ manōramāṁ tasyā madhyē || 617॥
pūrvābhimukhē maṇiratnamayasiṁhāsana upaviṣṭaḥ । tatō'pyambādhātryapi vāmapārśvē niṣaṇṇā tasya ॥ 618 ॥
kulamahattarāpi tathā śucibhūtā gr̥hītapravaranēpathyā । gr̥hītvā śāṭakaṁ haṁsalakṣaṇaṁ dakṣiṇē pārśvē ॥ 19 ॥
bhadrāsanē niṣaṇṇā tathā ca svāminaḥ paścimadiśi । varataruṇī sitacchatraṁ dharamāṇā tiṣṭhatyanyaikā ॥ 620 ॥
tathā calanaśīlacapalacāmarayugalaṁ gr̥hītvā dvayōḥ pārśvayōḥ । varavārasundaryō bhavanti śr̥ṅgārapravarāḥ ॥ 621॥
uttarapaurastyē bhāgē vilāsinī bhavatyanyā । gr̥hītvā bhr̥ṅgāraṁ surakarikaranālakākāram ||622||
ēvaṁ dakṣiṇapaurastyē bhāgē sundayēkā । gr̥hītvā tālavr̥ntaṁ karakamalē tiṣṭhati harṣēṇa ॥ 623||
tathā pr̥ṣṭhataśca vaiḍūryamadaṇḍānyātapatrāṇi । dhārayanti surēndrāḥ śaratpūrṇacandraprakāśāni ॥ 624 ॥
tathā dvayōrapi pārśvayōḥ śivikāyāḥ sthitāḥ sitaiścāmaraiḥ । saudharmēśānēndrau vījayataḥ supārśvajinacandram ॥ 625 ॥
atrāntarē nivasitasitavastrāḥ samavayasaḥ pravararūpāḥ । nirupahatāṅgā balaśālinaśca kr̥tasarvakartavyāḥ || 626 ॥
rōmāñcāñcitadēhāḥ sahasrasaṁkhyā narā mahāśibikām । tāṁ śrīśēkharanaravaravacanēnātkṣipanti laghu ॥ 627॥
vrajantyāstasyāḥ saudharmēśānanāyakau dvāvapi । dakṣiṇōttarabāhuṁ gr̥hītō gurupramōdēna ॥ 628 ||

bhavaṇavaivāṇamaṁtara jōisavēmāṇiyā surasamūhā। avasēsāvi hu siviyaṁ jahārihaṁ ukkhiviṁti tahā ॥ 630 ॥
kiṁbahunā ?
puvaṁ ukttiā naravarēhiṁ pulaūsasaṁtagattēhiṁ । pacchā varhati siviyaṁ asuriṁda suriṁdanā giṁdā ॥ 631 ॥
bhavaṇāō nīharaṁtē jiṇammi cāuvvihēhi dēvēhiṁ । iṁtēhiya jaṁtēhiya kahamiva ubbhāsayaṁ gayaṇaṁ ॥ 632॥
siddhatthacūyacaṁ payakēsara kaṇiyāra kuruvagavarṇava । kusumabharēhiṁva sōhai nahaṁgaṇaṁ tiyasarvidēhiṁ ॥ 633||
varapaḍa bhērijhallariduṁduhi saṁkhāitūranigghōsō । dharaṇiyalē gayaṇayalē payaṭṭaō maṇuyadēvēhiṁ ॥ 634 ||
ēvaṁ ca vaccamāṇassa tijayabaṁdhussa āṇupubbīē । satthiyapamuhā avi maṁgalagā paṭṭiyā puraō || 635॥
tattō saṁpuna kalasā bhiṁgārā taha ya vējayaṁtīō | taha divvamāyavattaṁ palaṁbakō riṭamālillaṁ ||636॥
sīhāsaṇaṁ ca nimmalamaṇimayapayapīḍhasaṁjuyaṁ vijalaṁ । saṁcaliyaṁ taha puraō nēradhariyaṁ pāuyājuyalaṁ ||637॥
ravirahaturayasamāṇaṁ cāmīyaramayakhalīṇajuttāṇaṁ । narakhittāṇaṁ paṭṭiyamamayaṁ jaccaturayāṇaṁ || 638 ||
taha ya pagiṭṭhāṇa purō aṭṭhasayaṁ kuṁjarāṇa mattāṇaṁ । ārōhapauttāṇaṁ sattaṁgapaṭṭhiyāṇaṁ ca ॥639॥
juttiyaturaṁgamāṇa rahāṇa karakaliyaāuhāṇaṁ ca । suhaḍāṇaṁ asayaṁ pattēyaṁ paṭṭiyaṁ tattō ॥ 640 ॥
rahagayahayaaṇiyāī puraō saṁpaṭṭiyāiṁ vēgēṇa । taha pāyattāṇīyaṁ amuṇiyasaṁkhaṁ asaṁkhabalaṁ ||641 ॥
tayaṇaṁtaraṁ ca garuyattaṇēṇa gayaṇaṁpi parimiṇatōvva । surapāṇipariggahiō māhidajhaō aivilōlō ॥ 642 ॥
śivikāyā dakṣiṇōttarādhastanabāhū dvāvapyasurēndrau । camarabalināmadhēyau harṣēṇa samudrahr̥tastataḥ ॥ 629॥
bhavanapativānavyantarajyautiṣavaimānikāḥ surasamūhāḥ । avaśēṣā api hi śibikāṁ yathārha mutkṣipanti tathā ॥ 630 ॥
kiṁ bahunā ?
pūrvamutkṣiptā naravaraiḥ pulakō cchrasadgātraiḥ । paścād vahanti śibikāmasurēndrasurēndranāgēndrāḥ ॥ 631 ॥
bhavanād niḥsarati jinē caturvidhairdēvaiḥ | āyadbhiśca yādbhiśca kathamivōdbhāsitaṁ gaganam ||632 ||
siddhārthacūtacampakakēśarakarṇikārakurubakavanamiva । kusumabharaikhi śōbhatē nabhō'ṅgaṇaṁ tridaśavr̥ndaiḥ ॥633॥
varapaṭahabhērījhallarīdundubhiśaṅkhāditūranirghōṣaḥ । dharaṇītalē gaganatalē pravartitō manujadēvaiḥ ||634 ॥
ēvaṁ ca vrajatastrijagadbandhōrānupūrvyā । svastikapramukhānyaṣṭāpi maṅgalakāni prasthitāni purataḥ ॥ 635||
tataḥ saṁpūrṇa kalaśā bhr̥ṅgārāstathā ca vaijayantyaḥ । tathā divyamātapatraṁ pralambakuraṇṭamālāvat ॥ 636 ॥
siṁhāsanaṁ ca nirmalamaṇimayapādapīṭhasaṁyutaṁ vipulam । saṁcalitaṁ tathā puratō naradhr̥taṁ pādukāyugalam ||637॥
ravirathaturagasamānāṁ cāmīkaramayakhalīnayuktānām । narakṣiptānāṁ prasthitamaṣṭaśataṁ jātyaturagāṇām ||638||
tathā ca prakr̥ṣṭānāṁ purō'ṣṭaśataṁ kuñjarāṇāṁ mattānām । ārōhaprayuktānāṁ saptāṅgapratiṣṭhitānāṁ ca ॥639॥
yauktrikaturaṅgamāṇāṁ sthānāṁ karakalitāyudhānāṁ ca । subhaṭānāmaṣṭaśataṁ pratyēkaṁ prasthitaṁ tataḥ ॥ 640 ॥
rathagajahayānīkāni purataḥ saṁprasthitāni vēgēna । tathā pādātānīkamajñātasaṁkhyamasaṁkhyabalam ॥ 641 ॥
1 ga. naravaīyaṁ ।

supāsanāha cariammi-
1
tattō ya daṁḍiṇō muṁḍiṇō ya hāsaṁkarā ya khiḍḍakarā । gāyaṁtā vāyaṁtā naccaṁtā taha pasaṁsaṁtā || 643 ॥
jaya jayaravaṁ kuṇaṁtā paḍatā maṁgalīya sahasāī । jiṇaguṇagaṇaṁ dhuṇaṁtā savvēvi hu paṭṭiyā turiyaṁ ॥ 644॥
sēṇāvaimaṁtimahaṁtakhattiṇō siṭṭiṇō ya satthāhā । saṁpaṭṭiyā ya puraō niyaniyajāṇēsu ārūḍhā || 645 ||
sirisēhara naranāhō suibhūō gaṁdhasiṁdhurārūḍhō । dhuvvaṁtadhavalacamarō jiṇavaramaṇugaṁtumārō ॥ 646 ॥
ēvaṁ suranaraniyarāṇugammamāṇō supāsajiṇanāhō | dhaṇusayadugataṇumāṇō samāṇacauraṁsaṭhāṇō ||647||
accijjatō pamhalavisālanayaṇuppalēhi ramaṇīhi । ānaṁdanivbharaṁ vitruhaviṁdagijjaṁ jasō ||648 ||
paricattapāṇabhōyaṇapāsāyārūḍha picchirajaṇēhiṁ । muccaṁta kusumavarisō thuvvaṁtō baṁdivaṁ dēhi ||649 ॥
nūrṇa ēsa asārō saṁsārō ērisēhiṁ jaṁ cattō । iya cittē jaṇayaṁtō sasurāsuramaṇuyanāhāṇaṁ ||650 ॥
salahijjatō maṁgalamuhalāhiṁ galata sudhārāhi । vāravilayāvalīhi attāṇaṁ sōmāṇīhiṁ ॥ 651 ॥
ēgattō sirisēhara muhēhiṁ khattiēhiṁ āvariō । annattō sōmābhihapamuhaṁtēurapuraṁdhīhiṁ ||652 ||
pattō supāsanā hō sahasaṁbavaṇābhihāṇamujjāṇaṁ । kayasadaṁ piva ucchaliyakōilā kōmalaravēhiṁ ॥653 ||
naccataṁ piva pavaṇaṁdōlirakaṁkēllipallava karēhiṁ । gāyataṁ piva bahuvihavihaṁga kulatumulasa dēhi ||654 ||
paṇamaṁtaṁ piva miupavaṇanamiratarusihara uttamaṁgēhiṁ । hāsaṁ piva payaḍaṁtaṁ viyasiyakusumaṭṭahāsēhiṁ || 665॥
saviyāsakusumaviyaliyamayaraṁdāṇaṁda asubiṁdūhiṁ । ukkhittavahaladhūyaṁva parimalumpīsapavaṇēhiṁ ॥ 656 ॥
।
tadanantaraṁ ca gurutvēna gaganamapi parimimāṇa iva । surapāṇiparigr̥hītō māhēndradhvajō'tivilōlaḥ ॥642॥
tataśca daṇḍinō muṇḍinaśca hāsyakarāśca khiṅgakarāḥ । gāyantō vādayantō nr̥tyantastathā praśaṁsantaḥ ॥ 643 ॥
jayajayaravaṁ kurvantaḥ prakaṭayantō maṅgalikasahasrāṇi । jinaguṇagaṇaṁ stuvantaḥ sarvē'pi khalu prasthitāstvaritam ॥
sēnāpatimantrimahākṣatriyāḥ śrēṣṭhinaśca sārthavāhāḥ । saṁprasthitāśca puratō nijanijayānēṣvārūḍhāḥ || 645॥
śrīśēkharanaranāthaḥ śucibhūtō gandhasindhurārūḍhaḥ । dhūyamānadhavalacāmarō jinavaramanugantumārabdhaḥ ॥ 646 ॥
ēvaṁ suranarānikarānugamyamānaḥ supārśvajinanāthaḥ । dhanuḥ śatadvikatanumānaḥ samānacaturasrasaṁsthā naḥ || 647॥
arcyamānaḥ pakṣmalaviśālanayanōtpalai ramaṇībhiḥ । ānandanirbharaṁ vibudhavr̥ndagīyamānajayaśabdaḥ || 648॥
parityaktapānabhōjanaprāsādārūḍha draṣṭr̥janaiḥ । mucyamānakusumavarṣaḥ stūyamānō bandivr̥ndaiḥ ॥649॥
nūnamēṣō'sāra : saṁsāra īdr̥śairyat tyaktaḥ । iti cittē janayan sasurāsuramanujanāthānām ॥650 ॥
ślāghyabhānō maṅgalamukharābhirgaladaśrudhārābhiḥ । vāravanitāvalībhirātmānaṁ śōcayantībhiḥ ||651 ॥
ēkataḥ śrī śēkharapramukhaiḥ kṣatriyairāvr̥taḥ । anyataḥ sōmābhidhapramukhāntaḥpurapurandhrībhiḥ ॥ 652 ॥
prāptaḥ supārśvanāthaḥ sahasrāmravaṇābhidhānamudyānam । kr̥taśabdāmivōcchalita kōkilā kōmalaravaiḥ ॥ 653 ॥
nr̥tyadiva pavanāndōlanaśīla kaṅkēllipallavakaraiḥ । gāyadiva bahuvidhavihaṁgakula tumulaśabdaiḥ ॥ 654 ॥
praṇamadiva mr̥dupavananamrataruśikharōttamāṅgaiḥ । hāsyamiva prakaṭayad vikasitakusumāṭṭahāsaiḥ ||655 ||
savikāśakusumavigalitamakarandānandāśrubindubhiḥ । utkṣiptabaha laghupamiva parimalōnmiśrapavanaiḥ ॥ 656 ॥

76
dinnagdhaṁva marudayataruvara nivaḍata kusuma niyarēhiṁ । sāgayamiva pucchaṁtaṁ kalā vikēkāiyaravēhi ||657 ||
tattha ya kaṁkēllimahātarussa mūlammi sīyalacchāē । suravaikarāvalaṁbī siviyāē avayarēūṇa || 658 |
siddhāṇa namōti bhaṇitu muyai āharaṇakusumavatthāī । tāī ca tiyasanāhō gahiūṇaṁ niyayakarakamalē ||
sirisēhara naravaiṇō samappaē tayaṇu garuyaharisēṇa । sēṇā hivamāisiuṁ ruṁbhai suratūranigdhō ||660 ||
ittō muttāhalavigbhamāī dhūlaṁsuyāī muyamāṇī | kulamayahariyā gaggaya girāē bhaṇiuṁ samāraddhā ||661 ॥
dēva ! jayattayanimmalakā savasupavittagōttajāō si । supaiṭṭhapatthivāmalakulajalanihipāriyāō si ।। 662 ॥
vimalōbhayapakkhāē puhaīdēvīē kucchibhūō si । sārayasasaṁka jōṇhānimmalajasadhavaliyadharō si ॥ 663 ॥
amiyaaṇōvamalāyannarūvasōhaggakaliyadēhō si । tā taha kahavi payaṭṭasu jaha sivasōkkhaṁ lahuṁ lahasi । 664॥
iya kulamayahariyāē vayaṇaṁ sōḍaṁ supāsa jiṇanāhō । uppāḍiumāraddhō kēsakalāvaṁ samuṭṭhīhi ||665 ||
jā tāva aṁtaracciya vajjēṇaṁ chiṁdiūṇa suranāhō । jiṇakarayalapalhatthiyakēsabharaṁ garuyabhattīē ||666 ||
īsīsinamiyadēhō dēvadukūlaṁcalēṇa niyaēṇa । giṇhai kamēṇa ittō nivvattiē lōyakammammi ||667 ||
jiṇavaramaṇunnavēḍaṁ kuḍilaṁ kasiṇaṁ ca dujjaṇamaṇaṁva । kēsakalāvaṁ khīrōyajala himajjhammi pakkhivai ||668 ॥
aha jēsuddhapakammi tērasīē'varaṇhasamayammi । bhayavaṁ supāsanāhō sayamēva samujjaō sahasā ||669 ॥
kāūṇa namōkāraṁ siddhāṇamabhiggahaṁ ca giṇhēi । savvaṁ mē'karaṇijjaṁ pāvaṁti caritamāruḍhō ॥ 670 ॥
dattārdhamiva maruddhatataruvaranipatatkusumanikaraiḥ । svāgatamiva pr̥cchat kalāpikē kāyitaravaiḥ ॥ 667 ॥
tatra ca kalimahātarōrmūlē śītalacchāyē । surapatikarāvalambī śivikāyā avatīrya ॥ 658 ॥
siddhēbhyō nama iti bhaṇitvā muñcatyābharaṇakusumavastrāṇi । tāni ca tridaśanātha gr̥hītvā nijakarakamalē ||659 ॥
śrīśēkharanarapatēḥ samarpayati tadanu guruharṣēṇa । sēnādhipamādiśya ruṇaddhi suratūranirghōṣam ॥660 ॥
itō muktāphalavibhramāṇi sthūlāṁśukāni muñcantī । kulamahattarā gadgadagirā bhaṇituṁ samārabdhā ॥ 661 ॥
dēva ! jagattrayanirmalakāśyapasupavitra gōtrajātō'si । supratiṣṭhapārthivāmalakulajalanidhipārijātō'si ॥ 662॥
vimalōbhayapakṣāyāḥ pr̥thivīdēvyāḥ kukṣibhūtō'si । śāradaśaśāṅkajyōtsnānirmala yaśōdhavalitadharō'si ॥ 663 ॥
amitānupamalāvaṇyarūpasaubhāgya kalitadēhō'si । tasmāttathā kathamapi prayatasva yathā śivasaiaukhyaṁ laghu labhasē ||664॥
iti kulamahattarāyā vacanaṁ śrutvā supārśvajinanāthaḥ । utpāṭayitumārabdhaḥ kēśakalāpaṁ svamuṣṭibhyām ॥665 ॥
yāvat tāvadantaraiva vajrēṇa cchittvā suranāthaḥ । jinakaratalaparyasta kēśabharaṁ gurubhaktayā ॥666॥
īṣadīṣannamitadēhō dēvadukūlāñcalēna nijakēna । gr̥hṇāti kramēṇētō nirvartitē lōcakarmaṇi ॥ 667 ॥
jinavaramanujñāpya kuṭilaṁ kr̥ṣṇaṁ ca durjanaṁmana iva । kēśakalāpaṁ kṣīrōdajaladhimadhyē prakṣipati ||668 ||
atha jyēṣṭhaśuddhapakṣē trayōdaśyāmaparāṇhasamayē । bhagavān supārśvanāthaḥ svayamēva samudyataḥ sahasā ॥ 669 ॥ .
kr̥tvā namaskāraṁ siddhēbhyō'bhigrahaṁ ca gr̥hṇāti । sarvaṁ mē'karaṇīyaṁ pāpamiti cāritramārūḍhaḥ ||670 ॥
atrāntarē dēvēndravr̥ndanarakhacara kinnaragaṇēna । ambaratalasthitēna bhūmisthitēna ca jinēndrasya ॥ 679 ॥

I
ētthaṁtarammi dēviṁdaviṁdanarakhayara kinnaragaṇēṇaṁ । aṁbaratalaṭṭhiēṇaṁ bhūmiṭṭhiēṇa ya jiṇidassa ||671 ||
uvari vimukō suhagaṁdhaluddhabhasalāvalīviluppatō । suhagaṁdhavāsacannō piṁgaliyasamaggagayaṇayalō || 672 ||
pahayāō dēvaduṁduhiḍhakahuḍukāmuiṁgatalimāō । taha bahiriyabaṁbhaṁḍō ucchaliō jayajayārāvō ||673 ||
Fat savahiraṁtarapariga jiṇavarēṇa paricatē । khivai varadēvadasaṁ vāmaṁsatalē tiyasanāhō || 674 |
aha aṭṭhārasasīlaṁgasahassabhārē jiṇēṇa ukkhittē । sāhijjaṁ piva kāuṁ maṇapajjavanāṇamutpannaṁ || 675॥
ētthaṁtarammi sāmaṁtamaṁtimaṁḍaliyapauralōēhiṁ । mittēhiṁ ya samakālaṁ sahassasaṁkhēhiṁ namiū ||676 ||
bhaṇiyamiṇaṁ jayapuṁgava ! jaha ihalōyammi tuha pasāēṇa । asarisasuhamaṇubhuttaṁ amhēhiṁ ēttiyaṁ kālaṁ || 677॥
taha pahu ! parōyamivi taha payasēvāē sāsayaṁ sukkhaṁ । icchāmō aṇuttuṁ iya bhaṇiuṁ tēhiṁ dhīrēhiṁ ॥ 678 ॥
saṁviggamāṇasēhiṁ paṁcahiṁ muṭṭhīhiṁ kuṁtalakalāvā । ullaṁciyā sayaṁ ciya savvēhivi cattamōhēhiṁ ॥ 679॥
aha dēvayā tāṇaṁ liṁgāī samapiyāī savvēsiṁ । dēvēhiṁ tappasaṁsāhiṁ vahiriyaṁ sayaladisivalayaṁ । । 680 ॥
aha sirisēhararāyā amaṁda āṇaṁdagaggayagirāē । vimhaiyamaṇō tāṇaṁ abhimumēyaṁ payam̐pē || 681 ॥
bhō bhō mahāṇubhāvā kittīē dhavaliyaṁ tihuyapi । taha bhavabhamaṇaduhāṇaṁ tubbhēhiṁ jalaṁjalī dinnō || 682 ॥
taha dullavaṁ mayaṇassa sāsaṇaṁ laṁghiyaṁ ca hēlāē । tubhēhiṁ muttikaṁtākaḍakkhapattaṁ kaō appā ||683॥
jēhiṁ duddharavayabhāradharaṇadhavalēhiṁ sāmiō ēsō । iṇhipi hu paḍivannō nikāraṇabaṁdhavō bhayavaṁ ॥ 684 ॥
ēvaṁ kāūṇa dhukaṁ viraē sirisēharē nivē iṁdā । namiya jiṇidaṁ naṁdīsarammi gaṁtuṁ gayā saggē ।। 685 ।।
upari vimuktaṁ śubhagandhalubdhabhramarāvalīvilupyamānam । śubhagandhavāsacūrṇaṁ piṅgalitasamagragaganatalam ||672 ॥
prahatā dēvadundubhiḍhakkā huḍukkāmr̥daṅgatalimāḥ । tathā badhiritabrahmāṇḍa ucchalitō jayajayārāvaḥ ॥ 673॥
itaḥ sabāhyābhyantaraparigrahē jinavarēṇa parityaktē । kṣipati varadēvadūṣyaṁ vāmāṁśatalē tridaśanāthaḥ ॥ 674 ||
athāṣṭādaśaśīlāṅgasahasrabhārē jinēnōtkṣiptē । sāhāyyamiva kartuṁ manaḥ paryavajñānamutpannam ॥675॥
atrāntarē sāmantamantrimaṇḍalika pauralōkaiḥ । mittraiśca samakālaṁ sahasūsaṁkhyairnatvā ||676॥
।
bhaṇitamidaṁ jagatpuṅgava ! yathēhalōkē tava prasādēna । asadr̥śasukhamanumuktamasmābhirētāvantaṁ kālam || 677॥
tathā prabhō ! paralōkē'pi tava pādasēvayā śāśvataṁ saukhyam । icchāmō'nubhōktumiti bhaṇitvā taidhīraiḥ ।। 678 ।।
saṁvignamānasaiḥ pañcabhirmuṣṭibhiḥ kuntalakalāpāḥ । ulluñcitāḥ svayamēva sarvairapi tyaktamōhaiḥ || 679 ॥
atha dēvatayā tēbhyō liṅgāni samarpitāni sarvēbhyaḥ । dēvaistatpraśaṁsābhirbādhiritaṁ sakaladigvalayam ||680॥
atha śrīśēkhararājō'mandānandgadgadagirā । vismitamanāstēṣāmabhimukhamēvaṁ prajalpati ॥ 681 ॥
bhō bhō mahānubhāvāḥ ! kīrtyā dhavalitaṁ tribhuvanamapi । tathā bhavabhramaṇaduḥkhānāṁ yuṣmābhirjalāñjalirdattaḥ ॥ 682॥
tathā durlaṅgha madanasya śāsanaṁ lāṅghataṁ ca hēlayā । yuṣmābhirmuktikāntākaṭākṣapātraṁ kr̥ta ātmā ॥ 683 ॥
yairdurdharavratabhāradharaṇadhavalaiḥ svāmyēṣaḥ । idānīmapi khalu pratipannō niṣkāraṇabāndhavō bhagavān ||684||
ēvaṁ kr̥tvā stutiṁ viratē śrīśēkharē nr̥pa indrāḥ । natthā jinēndra nandīśvarē gatvā gatāḥ svargē || 685 ॥

sirisēharōvi rāyā sahiō jaṇaṇīē namivi bhattīē । titthēsarassa calaṇa tāṇaṁ ca samuha sahasā ॥ 686 ॥
pujjō surāsurāṇaṁ majjha piyā iya pamōyasaṁjuttō । caiūṇa rajjaraṭṭhē ṭhiō aranē iya sasōō || 687 |
niyanayarīē pōi dūsaha piyavirahasōyasaṁtattaṁ । saṁṭhāvara kahakahavi hu dēvi sōmābhihaṁ tattha || 688 ||
iya jammaṇanikkhamaṇābhihāṇakallāṇakahaṇapaḍibaddhō । jiṇavara supāsacariē samatthiō duiyapatthāvō ।। 689 ।।
śrīśēkharō'pi rājā sahitō jananyā natvā bhaktyā । tīrthēśvarasya caraṇau tēṣāṁ ca samutthitaḥ sahasā ||686 ॥
pūjyaḥ surāsurāṇāṁ mama pitēti pramōdasaṁyuktaḥ । tyaktvā rājyarāṣṭrē sthitō'raṇya iti saśōkaḥ ||687 ||
nijanagaryāṁ praviṣṭō duḥsaha priyavirahaśōkasaṁtaptām । saṁsthāpayati kathaṁkathamapi hi dēvīṁ sōmābhidhāṁ tatra ॥ 688 ॥
janmaniṣkramaṇābhidhānakalyāṇakathanapratibaddhaḥ । jinavarasupārśvacaritē samarthitō dvitīyaprastāvaḥ ॥ 689 ॥

aha sirisupāsanāhō caunāṇī savvasattahiyaniraō । kāussagammi ṭhiō nikaṁpō mērusiharaṁva ॥ 1 ॥
taṁ tattha gamai diyahaṁ pasaṁtamuṇimaṁḍalēṇa pariyariō | jaṇayaṁtō āṇadaṁ bhaviyacaōrāṇa jimacaṁdō ||2||
aha duiyadi bhayavaṁ mayabhibhalatiyasasiṁdhuragaīē । pāraṇagatthaṁ pattō pāḍalisam̐ḍammi nayarammi ||3||
tattha ya mahuyaravittiṁ aṇusaramāṇō mahiṁdagēhammi | saṁpattō sōvi taō harisabhalasiyarōmaṁcō ||4||
jiṇanāhassābhimuhaṁ vaccai niyayāsaṇāō uṭṭhēuṁ । namiuṁ ca niruvamāṇaṁdagaggayaṁ bhaṇiumārō ॥5॥ -
kēhipa ajja cirasaṁciēhiṁ phaliyamha tavavisēsēhiṁ । kappatarūhiṁva nūṇaṁ saimahurapacēlimaphalēhi ||6||
jēṇēyaṁ maha bhavaṇaṁ suravisaranamaṁsaṇijjamajjēva । jāyaṁ jiṇa ! tuhapayapaumapaṁtivicchittiramaṇīyaṁ ॥ 7॥
tē tihuyaṇasirisiṁgārabhāyaṇa jē jiṇidamuhakamalē । viṣphārayanayaṇauḍā piyati lāyannamayaraṁdaṁ ॥8॥
kitti kuṇēi uvaṇē saṁpayaṁ paḍihai malapaḍalaṁ । dēva ! duhāvi amōhaṁ sāhai tuha daṁsaṇaṁ kiṁ nō ? ॥ 9 ॥
bhuvaṇayalāsāsakaraṁ tuha pahu । iṇamō aciṁtiyāgamaṇaṁ । cattaghaṇasamayavaṭṭīē saṁnihaṁ harai saṁtāvaṁ ॥ 10 ॥
pēkkhati paramajōīsarāvi jaṁ jhāṇacakkhuṇā kahavi । sō paramappasarūvā tumaṁ gaō diṭṭivisamma || 11 ||
ahibhōgē viya bhōgē nihaṇaṁva dhaṇaṁ malaṁva kamalaṁpi । mannaṁtā bhavavimuhā bhavārisā kassa iṁti hi 12 ||
iya thōūṇa saharisaṁ bahumāṇaparō bhai niyaṁ gihiṇi । kallāṇāṇaṁ paṇaiṇi ! ēgacciya bhāyaṇa taṁsi ॥
jīē jaēkanāhō saṁpattaṁ dāṇapattamēsa taē । jiṇanāhō sacarācarajaṁtūṇamakattimō baṁdhū || 14 ||
tō pāraṇayaṁ kārāviūṇa ēvaṁ visuddhadavvēṇa । gahiraṁpi bhavasamudaṁ gōpayamittaṁva laṁghēsuṁ ॥ 15 ॥
atha śrīsupārśvanāthaścaturjñānaḥ sarvasattvahitanirataḥ । kāyōtsargē sthitō niṣkampō mēruśikharamiva ॥ 1 ॥
taṁ tatra gamayati divasa praśāntamunimaṇḍalēna parikaritaḥ । janayannānandaṁ bhavikacakōrāṇāṁ jinacandraḥ ॥2॥
atha dvitīyadinē bhagavān madamattadiśasindhuragatyā | pāraṇakārtha prāptaḥ pāṭaliṣaṇḍē nagarē ||3||
tatra ca madhukaravr̥ttimanusaran mahēndra gēhē । saṁprāptaḥ sō'pi tatō harṣabharōllasita rōmāñcaḥ || 4 ||
jinanāthasyābhimukhaṁ vrajati nijakāsanādutthāya । natvā ca nirupamā nandagadgadaṁ bhaṇitumārabdhaḥ ॥ 5 ॥
kairapyadya cirasaṁcitaiḥ phalitaṁ mama tapōviśēṣaiḥ । kalpatarubhiriva nanaṁ sadāmadhurapacēlimaphalaiḥ || 6 ||
yēnēdaṁ mama bhavanaṁ suravisaranamasyanīyamadyaiva । jātaṁ jina ! tvatpādapadmapaṅktivicchittiramaṇīyam ॥7॥
tē tribhuvanaśrīśr̥ṅgārabhājanaṁ yē jinēndramukhakamalē । visphāritanayanapuṭāḥ pibanti lāvaṇyamakarandam ॥8॥
kīrttiṁ karōtyupanayati saṁpadaṁ pratihantilam । dēva ! dvidhāpyamōghaṁ (haṁ ) sādhayati tava darśanaṁ kiṁ nō ? ॥
bhuvanatalāśvāsakaraṁ tava pramā । idamacintitāgamanam । tyaktaghana samayavr̥ṣṭyāḥ saṁnibhaṁ harati saṁtāpam ॥ 10 ॥
prēkṣantē paramayōgīśvarā api dhyānacakṣuṣā kathamapi । sa paramātmasvarūpastvaṁ gatō dr̥ṣṭiviṣayē ॥ 11 ॥
ahibhōgāniva bhōgān nidhanamiva dhanaṁ malamiva kamalamapi । manyamānā bhavavimukhā bhavādr̥śāḥ kasyāyanti gr̥ham ? ॥
iti stutvā saharṣaṁ bahumānaparō bhaṇati nijāṁ gr̥hiṇīm । kalyāṇānāṁ praṇayiṇi ! ēkaiva bhājanaṁ tvamasi ॥ 13 ॥
yayā jagadēkanāthaḥ saṁprāptaṁ dānapātramēṣa tvayā । jinanāthaḥ sacarācarajantūnāmakr̥trimō bandhuḥ || 14 ||

supāsanāha- cariammi-
iya sōuṁ aviralapulayajālakaliyāē tīē bhattīē । attāṇaṁ kayakiccaṁ manaṁtī pamōēṇaṁ ॥ 16 ॥
kalahōyama thālē khiviraṁ paraṁ mannaparamannaṁ । ghayasakarasaṁmīsaṁ pakappiyaṁ jiṇavariṁdassa || 17||
davvāisu uvaōgaṁ sammaṁ dāūṇa bhayavayā tāhē । taṁ savvaguṇavisuddhaṁ paḍicchiyaṁ pāṇipuḍaṇaṁ ॥ 18 ॥
ētyaṁtara mmi duṁduhiravavahiriyadisimuhēhiṁ dēvēhiṁ । ugghuṭṭamahō ! dāṇaṁ pamuiyacitcēhiṁ gayaṇayalē ||19||
addhattērasakaṁ caṇakōḍīhi mahiṁdamaṁdiratalammi | buddhaṁ gaṁdhajalēṇa ya kusumēhi ya paṁcavannēhiṁ ||20||
tō bhaṇiyamahō sattī bhattī ya ahō supattaāgamaṇaṁ । dhannō tamēva punnassa bhāyaṇaṁ taṁ ciya mahiṁda ! ॥ 21
iha tāva māṇusataṁ bhavannavē dulahaṁ khu jīvāṇaṁ । tatthavi samatthapurisatyasāhagaṁ nūṇa purisataṁ ||22||
tattha ya vivō sārō jēṇa viṇā nimmalāvi guṇakuralī | vāyāhayasiṁbhalitūlalīlamuvvahai lōyasmi ॥
taṁ ciya kiviṇā tattha ya giddhā muddhāvi kahavi laddhūṇa । vihalaṁ kuṇaṁti ucchukusumaṁ piva dāṇamaira hiyā ||
dāṇamaīvi jāṇaṁ ūsarakhittammi mēḍiva । vihalacciya guṇagarūyaṁ viṇāvi suhapatta saṁpatti ॥25॥
pattaṁ ca taṁ jahatthaṁ rakkhai jaṁ duggaīē nivaḍataṁ । attāṇaṁ ca paraṁ ciya taṁ puṇa tivihaṁ viṇihiṁ ||26||
cārittanāṇadaṁsaṇasaṁjuttaṁ havai uttamaṁ pattaṁ । dōhiṁ ca majjhamaṁ taha jahannamēgēṇa nāyavvaṁ ||27||
tā ēttha bhavasamuddē uttamapattaṁ sujāṇavattaṁva । jiṇanāhōcciya punnēhiṁ āṇiō tujjha gēhammi ||28||
iccāinahatthēhiṁ mahiṁda mahisa lihiūṇa vayaṇēhiṁ । namiūṇa ya jiṇanāhaṁ sahāṇaṁ paḍigayā dēvā || 29॥
।
tataḥ pāraṇakaṁ kārayitvaitaṁ viśuddhadravyēṇa । gabhīramapi bhavasamudraṁ gōṣpadamātramiva laṅghasva ||15||
iti śrutvā'viralapulakajālakalitayā tayā bhaktyā । ātmānaṁ kr̥takr̥tyaṁ manyamānayā pramōdēna ॥ 16 ॥
kaladhautamayē sthālē kṣiptvā pracuraṁ manōjñaparamānnam । ghr̥taśarkarāsaṁmiśraṁ prakalpitaṁ jinavarēndrāya ॥ 17 ॥
dravyādiṣūpayōgaṁ samyag dattvā bhagavatā tadā । tat sarvaguṇaviśuddha pratīṣṭaṁ pāṇipuṭakēna ॥ 12 ॥
atrāntarē dundubhiravabadhiritadiṅmukhairdēvaiḥ । uddr̥ṣṭamahō ! dānaṁ pramuditacittairgaganatalē ॥ 19 ॥
ardhatrayōdaśakāñcanakōṭibhirmahēndramandiratalē । vr̥ṣṭaṁ gandhajalēna ca kusumaiśca pañcavarṇaiḥ ॥20॥
tatō bhaṇitamahō ! śaktirbhaktiścāhō ! supātrāgamanam । dhanyastvamēva puṇyasya bhājanaṁ tvamēva mahēndra ! ॥ 21॥
iha tāvanmanuṣyatvaṁ bhavārṇavē durlabhaṁ khalu jīvānām । tatrāpi samartha puruṣārthasādhakaṁ nūnaṁ puruṣatvam ॥22॥
tatra ca vibhavaḥ sārō yēna vinā nirmalāpi guṇakuralī । vātāhataśālmalītalalīlāmudvahati lōkē ॥ 23 ॥
tadēva kr̥paṇāstatra ca gr̥ddhā mugdhā api kathamapi labdhvā । viphala kuvantīkṣukusumamiva dānamatirahitāḥ ॥ 24 ॥
dvānamatirapi janānāmūṣarakṣētrē mētravr̥ṣṭiriva । viphalaiva guṇagurukāṁ vināpi śubhapātrasaṁprāptim ॥25॥
pātraṁ ca tad yathārthaṁ rakṣati yad durgatau nipatantam । ātmānaṁ ca paraṁ caiva tatpunastrividhaṁ vinirdiṣṭam ||26|
cāritrajñānadarśanasaṁyuktaṁ bhavatyuttamaṁ pātram । dvābhyāṁ ca madhyamaṁ tathā jaghanyamēkēna jñātavyam ||27||
tasmādatra bhavasamudra uttamapātraṁ suyānapātramiva । jinanātha ēva puṇyairānītastava gēhē ||28||
ityādiyathārthairmahēndramabhiślāghya vacanaiḥ । natvā ca jinanāthaṁ svasthānaṁ pratigatā dēvāḥ ||29||

kēvalapatthāvāṁ |
85
uddhava bhayavaṁ pārai tatthēva pāṇitalakaliyaṁ । taṁ suddhanna pāsati nēya lōyāvi jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 30॥
paramāisayajuyāṇaṁ havaṁti titthēsarāṇa sayakāla । āhārā nīhārā ahissā cammaca khūṇaṁ ॥ 31 ॥
sāvi muṇivariṁdā sammanimmūlaṇammi ujjuttā । jahavihiṇā jē pattaṁ kuṇaṁti pāraṇayamittōya || 32 ॥
bhayakaṁpi gahiyavahuvihaabhiggahō niṣpariggahō dhīrō । gāmāgaranayarāimu vihara samasattu mittamaṇō ॥ 33॥
katthavi nicalacittō paḍiruddhaasē sakaraṇavāvārō । suddhajjhāṇadadvēṇa pāvavaṇaṁ dahai sēyalaṁpi ॥ 34 ॥
katthavi ya lagaṁḍāsaṇagaruḍāsaṇapamuhaṭhāṇa karaṇēṇa । uvalapaḍibiṁbasakaṁ jaṇai jaṁṇāṇaṁ payāsēvi ॥ 35 ॥
katthavi navanīluppalasaṁḍava himēṇa ujjhamāṇōvi । niñcalataṇū maṇapi hu nacalai niyajhāṇasarasīō ॥ 36 ॥
nagar atō vāhiṁ ca sahassakarapayāvēṇa । ōlaṁviyayaparihō vāḍhaṁ sōhēi dēhamalaṁ ||37||
chaṭṭaṭṭamadasamaduvālasāimāsaddhamāsakhamaṇāī | bhadamahābhadāī kuṇamāṇō uggatavakammaṁ ॥ 38 ॥
bāvīsa parīsaha sahaṇapaccalō daliya mōhamāhappō । tuḍiyadaḍhaviyaḍanēhāyasaniyaḍō khaṁliyamayapasarō || 39॥
niyapayakamalaraēṇaṁ pavittayatō mahīyalaṁ sayalaṁ । nimmūlaṁ dalamāṇō sayalaṁtara sattusinnavalaṁ ||40||
attāṇaṁ bhāviṁtō muhuṁ muhuṁ bhāvaṇāhiṁ suddhāhiṁ । kammamalēṇa ya maliṇaṁ dhōyatō samasalilēṇaṁ ॥ 41 ॥
kalayaṁtō gahiraṁpi hu jāṇupamāṇaṁ bhavannavaṁ dēvō । chaumatthō nava māsē gamēi paricattasāvajjō || 42 ॥
aha annayā ya ukkaṁṭhiuvva dēsēsu vihariḍaṁ pattō । vārāṇasīē īsāṇadisiṭṭiē sahasavaṇē ||43||
ūrdhvasthitō'pi bhagavānpārayati tatraiva pāṇitalakalitam । tacchuddhānnaṁ paśyanti naiva lōkā api yadbhaṇitam॥ 30 ॥
paramātiśayayutānāṁ bhavanti tīrthēśvarāṇāṁ sadākālam । āhārā nīhārā adr̥śyāścarmacakṣuṣām ||31||
śēṣā api munivarēndrāḥ svakarmanirmūlana udyuktāḥ । yathāvidhi yat prāptaṁ kurvanti pāraṇakamitaśca ||32||
bhagavānapi gr̥hītabahuvidhābhigrahō niṣparigrahō dhīraḥ । grāmākaranagarādiṣu viharati samaśatru mittramanāḥ || 33॥
kutrāpi niścalacittaḥ pratiruddhāśēṣakaraṇavyāpāraḥ । śuddhadhyānadēvēna pāpavanaṁ dahati sukalamapi ॥34॥
kutrāpi ca lakuṭāsanagaruḍāsanapramukhasthānakaraṇēna । upalaprativimbaśaṅkāṁ janayati janānāṁ prakāśē'pi ||35||
kutrāpi navanīlōtpalapaṇḍamiva himēna dadyamānō'pi । niścalatanurmanāgapi khalu na calati nijadhyānasarasītaḥ ।।
tapōhutavahē nāntarbahiśca sahasakara pratāpēna । avalambitabhujaparighō bāḍhaṁ śōdhayati dēhamalam ||37||
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamadaśamadvādaśādimāsārdhamā sakṣapaṇādi । bhadrā mahābhadrādi kurvāṇa ugratapaḥ karma ॥ 38 ॥
dvāviṁśatiparīṣahasahanapratyalō dalitamōhamāhātmyaḥ । truṭitadr̥ḍhavikaṭa snēhāyasa nigaḍa : skhalitamadaprasaraḥ ॥39॥
nijapādakamalarajasāṁ pavitrayan mahītalaṁ sakalam । nirmūlaṁ dalayan sakalāntaraśatrusainyabalam ॥40॥
ātmānaṁ bhāvayan muhurmuhurbhāvanābhiḥ śuddhābhiḥ । karmamalēna ca malinaṁ dhāvan praśamasalilēna ॥41॥
kalayan gabhīramapi hi jānupramāṇaṁ bhavārṇavaṁ dēvaḥ । chadmasthō nava māsān gamayati parityaktasāvadyaḥ ॥ 42 ॥
athānyadā cōtkaṇṭhita iva dēśēṣu vihr̥tya prāptaḥ । vārāṇasyāmīśānadisthitē sahasāvaṇē ॥ 43 ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
tattha ya ummilirapaḍhamapallavāruṇiyasayalasāhassa । amarapurassava maṇahara sumaṇasaniyarābhirāmassa || 44 ॥
I
naranāhassava bahupattaniyatpariyariyabhūmibhāyassa । sirisassa mahātaruṇō mūlammi avaḍiō bhayavaṁ ॥ 45 ॥
tattha ya carittadaṁsaṇanāṇēhiṁ aṇuttarappabhāvēhiṁ । ālayavihāramadava ajjavalāhavapahāṇēhiṁ ॥ 46 ॥||
ākiṁcaṇasaccatiguttimuttikhaṁtipamukkhacariēhiṁ । sammaṁ muhuṁ muhuṁ ciya bhāvēmāṇassa appāṇaṁ ॥47॥
jahavaṭṭiyabhāvabhāvaṇabhāviyahiyayassa karuṇajalanihiṇō । sayalaṁpi hu jiyalōyaṁ ataṁva pōyamāṇassa ॥ 48 ॥
vāhiravikvavivajjiērhi karaṇēhiṁ saha samāhīē । ēgībhūyaṁva maṇaṁ kāuṁ tattammi līṇassa || 49||
gayalēvassa nahastava mērussava suiraniṣpakaṁpassa | pavamāṇassava katthavi paḍivaṁdhaṁ akuṇamāṇassa ॥ 50 ॥
sukkajjhāṇānaladr̥ḍḍhasayalaghaṇaghāikammagahaṇassa । nivvāyathimiyajalarāsivigbhamaṁ niru vatassa ॥ 51 ॥
sukkajjhāṇassavi carimabhēyajuyalaṁ apattaputrassa । phagguṇavaichaṭṭīē muhē muhuttammi pu ॥ 52 ॥
caṁdammi visāhatthē supāsatitthēsarassa jayapahuṇō । anvāhayaṁ anaṁtaṁ paḍipunnaṁ taha nirāvaraṇaṁ ॥ 53 ॥
bhāvissa bhūyapabhavaṁtabhāva ālōyalōyaṇaṁ vimalaṁ । lōyālōyapayāsaṁ uppannaṁ kēvalaṁ nāṇaṁ ॥ 54 ॥
ētthaṁtarammi āsaṇapakaṁpa saṁbōhiō tiyasanāhō । avahīē jāṇiūṇaṁ jiṇassa jāyē jahā nāṇē ॥ 55 ॥
uṭṭiya sataha para gaṁtuṁ bhaktibharōṇamiyasīsō । pabhaṇai namōtthu titthaṁkarassa bhayavaṁsupāsassa || 56 ॥
āṇavara tahā sēṇāvaī ca bhō bhada ! jaha lahuṁ gaṁtu । sōhammasahāē tumaṁ apphālasu sāsayaṁ ghaṁṭaṁ ॥ 57॥
taha tikkhutō ghōsaha jaha bharahē sattamassa jiṇavaiṇō । kēvalanāṇaṁ jāyaṁti tattha sakkēṇa gaṁtavvaṁ ॥ 58॥
tatra cōnmīlanaśīla prathamapallavāruṇitasakalaśākhasya । amarapurasyēva manōharasumanōnikarābhirāmasya ॥44॥
naranāthasyēva bahupa(pā)tranikarapa rikaritabhūmibhāgasya । śirīṣasya mahātarōrmūlē'vasthitō bhagavān ॥45॥
tatra ca cāritradarśanajñānairanuttaraprabhāvaiḥ । ālayavihāra mārdavārjavalāghavapradhānaḥ ॥ 46 ॥
ākiñcanyasatyatriguptimuktikṣāntipramukhyacaritaiḥ । samyag muhurmuhurēva bhāvayata ātmānam ||47॥
yathāvasthitabhāvabhāvanābhāvitahr̥dayasya karuṇājalanidhēḥ । sakalamapi jīvalōkamātmānamiva pralōkamānasya ॥48॥
bāhyavikṣēpavivarjitaiḥ karaṇaiḥ saha samādhinā । ēkībhūtamiva manaḥ kr̥tvā tattvē līnasya ॥ 49 ॥
gatalēpasya nabhasa iva mērōriva suciraniṣprakampasya । pavamānasyēva kutrāpi pratibandhamakurvāṇasya ॥50॥
śukladhyānānaladagvasakalaghanaghātikarmagahanasya । nirvātastimitajalarāśivibhramaṁ niścitaṁ vahataḥ ॥ 51 ॥
śukladhyānasyāpi caramabhēdayugalamaprāptapūrvasya । phālgunāsitaṣaṭyāṁ śubha muhūrtē pūrvāhnē ॥12॥
candrē viśākhāsthē supārśvatīrthēśvarasya jagatprabhōḥ । avyāhatamanantaṁ paripūrṇa tathā nirāvaraṇam ||13||
bhaviṣyadbhūtaprabhavadbhāvālōkalōcanaṁ vimalam । lōkālōkaprakāśamutpannaṁ kēvalaṁ jñānam ॥54॥
atrāntarē āsanaprakampasaṁbōdhitastridaśanāthaḥ । avadhinā jñātvā jinasya jātaṁ yathā jñānam ॥55॥
utthāya saptāṣṭa padāni gatvā bhaktimarāvanataśīrṣaḥ । prabhaṇati namō'stu tīrthaṅkarāya bhagavatsupārśvāya ॥ 56 ॥
ājñapayati tathā sēnāpatiṁ ca bhō bhadra ! yathā laghu gatvā । saudharmasabhāyāṁ tvamāsphālaya śāśvatīṁ ghaṇṭām ॥

kēvalapatthāvō |
tā bhō dēvā tumbhē āgacchaha pariyaṇēṇa pariyariyā । iya sakkasāsaṇaṁ sō paḍicchiuṁ taṁ tahā kuṇai ॥ 59 ॥
tattō ya gahiraghaṁṭā apphālaṇaucchalaṁtapaḍisadaṁ । paḍisaddapaḍipphalaṇāvajjiranīsēsasuraghaṁṭaṁ ॥60॥
suraghaṁṭaraṇaṁjjhaṇāravavasavajjiyatiyasacauvihāujjaṁ । āujjasahasaṁsagabhaggagaṁdhavvagīyara || 61||
gīyaravabhaṁga parigaliyatālalayacukkana ciraccharasaṁ । accharasakalayalārava akaṁtasamaggadisicakkaṁ ॥62॥
ēvaṁ suralōē savvēsuvi suravarāṇa bhavaṇēsu । kiṁkiṁtisaddamīsō ucchaliō bahalahalabōlō ||63 ||
uvasaṁtē ya khaṇēṇa sāhai sēṇāvaīvi tiyasāṇa । jiṇakēvalamahimatthaṁ jaha suravaiṇā samāi || 64 ||
sōūṇa taṁ ca samagaṁ savvaivi hu suravarā suriṁdēṇa । saha saṁcaliyā niyaniyajāṇavimāṇēsu ārūḍhā || 65 ||
harisukarisamayaṁ kiṁ kiṁvā jayajayaja ēkaravamaiyaṁ । rayaṇujjōyamayaṁ kiṁ kiṁ lacchīvigbhamamayaṁ vā ? ॥66॥
ēvaṁ gayaṇayalaṁ pai hiyaē lōyāṇa vimhayaṁ garuyaṁ । jaṇayaṁtā saṁpattā sahasaṁbavaṇammi ujjāṇē || 67॥
tattha ya savvēhiṁ suravaīhiṁ āṇaṁdagaggayagirāē । cauvihadēvanikāyā, vayaṇamimaṁ saharisaṁ bhaṇiyā ||68 ॥
bhō bhō supāsanāhassa samavasaraṇammi jassa jaṁ kiccaṁ । taṁ kāūṇa kayatthā havaha surā, tēvi taṁ sōuṁ ॥ 69॥
vākumārā avaṇiti rēṇutiṇakayavarāīyaṁ savvaṁ । jōyaṇamittē khittē tarukuvāiyaṁ tirōhaṁti || 70 ||
mēhakumārā puṇa pavaṇacaliyarayaniyaranāsaṇaṁ surahiṁ । tammi ya kuṇaṁti tuṭṭhā gaṁdhōdaya sīyarakkhēvaṁ ॥ 71 ॥
kēvi hu amaṁdamaya raṁdabiṁdunīsaṁdaluddhaalipaḍalaṁ । hariyaṁdaṇamaṁdārayakusumakēraṁ ca varisaṁti ॥ 72 ॥
tathā triṣaya yathā bharatē saptamasya jinapatēḥ । kēvalajñānaṁ jātamiti tatra śakrēṇa gantavyam ॥ 58 ॥ .
tasmād bhō dēvā yūyamāgacchata parikarēṇa parikaritāḥ । iti śakraśāsana sa pratīṣya tattathā karōti ॥59॥
tataśca gabhīraghaṇṭāsphālanōcchalatpratiśabdam । pratiśabdapratisphālanāvādanaśīla niḥśēṣasuraghaṇṭam ॥ 60 ॥
suraghaṇṭā raṇajjhaṇā ravavaśavāditatridaśacaturvidhātōdyam । ātōdyaśabdasaṁsargabhagnagāndharvagītaravam ॥ 61 ॥
gītaravabhaṅgaparigalitatālalaya bhraṣṭa nartanaśīlāpsarasam । apsaraḥ kalakalāravākrāntasamagradikcakram ॥62॥
ēvaṁ suralōkēṣu sarvēṣvapi suravarāṇāṁ bhavanēṣu । kiṁkimitiśabdamiśra ucchalitō bahalakōlāhalaḥ ||63 ||
upaśāntē ca kṣaṇēna kathayati sēnāpatirapi tridaśān । jinakēvalamahimārthē yathā surapatinā samādiṣṭam || 64॥
śrutvā taca samakaṁ sarvē'pi hi suravarāḥ surēndrēṇa । saha saṁcalitā nijanijayānavimānēṣvārūḍhāḥ ॥65॥
harṣōtkarṣamayaṁ kiṁ kiṁvā jayajayajayaikara vamayam । ratnōdyōtamayaṁ kiṁ kiṁ lakṣmīvibhramamayaṁ vā ? ॥ 66 ॥
ēvaṁ gaganatalaṁ prati hr̥dayē lōkānāṁ vismayaṁ gurum । janayantaḥ saṁprāptāḥ sahasrāmravaṇa udyānē ॥ 67 ॥
tatra ca sarvaiḥ surapatibhirānandgadgadagirā । caturvidhadēvanikāyā vacanamidaṁ saharṣa bhaṇitāḥ ॥ 68 ॥
bhō bhōḥ supārśvanāthasya samavasaraṇē yasya yat kr̥tyam । tatkr̥tvā kr̥tārthā bhavata surāḥ, tē'pi tat śrutvā ॥ 69 ॥
vāyukumārā apanayanti rēṇutr̥ṇakaccarādikaṁ sarvam | yōjanamātrē kṣētrē tarukūpādikaṁ tirōdadhati ॥ 70 ॥
mētrakumārāḥ punaḥ pavanaḥcalitarajōnikaranāśanaṁ surabhim । tasmiṁśca kurvanti tuṣṭā gandhōdakasīkarākṣēpam ॥ 71 ॥
kē'pi mandamakarandabinduniḥ syandalubdhālipaṭalam । haricandanamandārakakusumōtkaraṁ ca varṣanti ॥ 72 ॥

35
supāsanāha cariammi----
tattō paḍhamō kappōvavaṇṇadēvēhiṁ rayaṇapāyārō । nimmaviō jō rēhai rōhaṇagirituṁgasiṁgasamō ॥ 73 ॥
duiō jōisiēhiṁ varakaṇayamaō viuvviō jhatti । jō suragirivva rēhai samāgaō jiṇasiriṁ daddhuṁ ॥ 74 ॥
taiō bhavaṇavaīhiṁ kalahōyamaō viṇimmiō sālō । jō caṁdakuṁdadhavalō tuhiṇāyala līlamumbaī || 75 ॥
ēmma ṭiō sāmī cavihasaṁghasta cauvihaṁ dhammaṁ । sāhissai iya tēhiṁ kayāī cattāri dārāī ॥ 76 ॥
taha suvi dārēsuṁ phālihasōvāṇamālaka liyāō । vāvīō raiyāō visadr̥kaṁdōhavaṁdāō ॥77॥
taha vihiyāī vaṇāī caṁpayapunnāyanāyaviḍavīṇaṁ । pavaṇuvvallirapallavakarasaṇṇiyasayalalōyāī ॥78॥
sīhāsaṇaṁ ca majjhē hēmamayaṁ nimmiyaṁ aivisālaṁ । udayāyalasiharaṁ piva tihuyaṇa ra visaṁgamītaṁ ॥ 79 ॥
taha uvari bārasaguṇō pavaṇuccilaṁtagucchasaṁchannō | kōmalakisalayakaliō asōyavarapāyavō raiō ॥ 80 ॥
ēsō tiguttiguttō nijjiyadaṁḍattaō tikālaviū । tihuyaṇagurutti raiyaṁ vimalaṁ chattattayaṁ uvariṁ ॥ 81 ॥
ēgōściya jiṇanāhō pōō bhavasāyarampi ii kahiḍēṁ । dharaṇīē aṁgulī viya samubbhiyā dhammadhayamisaō ॥ 82 ॥
bhāmaṁḍala ca paṭṭhīē nimmiyaṁ rayaṇakiraṇacicaṁiyaṁ । varaduṁduhī ya taha tattha tāḍiyā saharisasurēhiṁ || 83 ||
sakīsāṇidāvi hu dōsuvi pāsēsu caṁdakarathavalaṁ । cālaṁti cāmarajuyaṁ taha buṭṭī havai kusumāṇa || 84॥
puraōvi dhammacakkaṁ paṭṭiyaṁ ghaḍiyamamalarayaṇēhiṁ । jaṁ sēvāgayataraṇivva sahai vijiutti jayaraviṇā ॥85॥
ētyaṁtarē jiṇidō suraviraiyakaṇayapa umapaṁtīē । ṭhāvitō kamajuyalaṁ thuvvaṁtō cāraṇamuṇīhi ॥ 86 ॥
paṇamijjaṁtō sāyaranara kinnara khayara surasamūhēhiṁ । suravaisiyamaggō puvvaduvārēṇa pavisēi ||87||
tataḥ prathamaḥ kalpōpapannadēvai ratnaprākāraḥ । nirmārpitō yō rājati rōhaṇagirituṅgaśr̥ṅgasamaḥ ||73 ||
dvitīyō jyautipikairvarakanakamayō vikurvitō jhaṭiti । yaḥ suragirivi rājati samāgatō jinaśriyaṁ draṣṭum || 74 ॥
tr̥tīyō bhavanapatibhiḥ kaladhautamayō vinirmitaḥ śālaḥ । yaścandrakundradhavalastuhinācalalīlāmudvahati ॥75॥
ētasmin sthitaḥ svāmī caturvivasaṁghasya caturvidhaṁ dharmam । kathayiṣyatīti taiḥ kr̥tāni catvāri dvārāṇi ॥76॥
tathā catuṣvapi dvārēṣu sphāṭikasōpānamālākalitāḥ । vāpyō citā vikasitanīlōtpalavr̥ndāḥ ॥77॥
tathā vihitāni vanāni campakapunnāganāgaviṭapinām । pavanōdvēlanaśīla pallavakara saṁjñitasakalalōkāni ॥78॥
siṁhāsanaṁ ca madhyē hēmamayaṁ nirmitamativiśālam । udayācalaśikharamiva tribhuvanaravisaṅgamīhamānam ॥79॥
tathōpari dvādaśaguṇaḥ pavanōdvēladgucchasaṁchannaḥ । kōmalakiśalayakalitō'śōkavara pādapō racitaḥ ॥ 80 ॥
ēṣa triguptiguptō nirjitadaṇḍacayastrikālavit । tribhuvanagururiti racitaṁ vimalaṁ chatratrayamupari ॥ 81 ॥
ēka ēva jinanāthaḥ pōtō bhavasāgara iti kathayitum । dharaṇyā'ṅgulīva samūvitā dharmadhvajamiṣataḥ ॥82॥
bhāmaṇḍalaṁ ca pr̥ṣṭhē nirmitaṁ ratnakiraṇamaṇḍitam । varadundubhiśca tathā tatra tāḍitā saharṣasuraiḥ ॥ 83 ॥
śakrēśānēndrāvapi hi dvayōrapi pārśvayōścandrakaradhavalam । cālayanti cāmarayugaṁ tathā vr̥ṣṭirbhavati kusumānām ॥ 84 ॥
puratō'pi dharmacakraṁ pratiṣṭhitaṁ ghaṭitamamalaratnaiḥ । yat sēvāgatataraṇiriva rājatē vijita iti jagadraviṇā ॥ 85 ॥
atrāntarē jinēndraḥ suraviracitakanakapadmapaṅgau । sthāpayan kramayugalaṁ stūyamānaścāraṇamunibhiḥ ॥ 86 ॥

kēvalapatthāvāṁ |
majjhavi taṁ namaṇijjaṁ titthaṁ lōyāṇa iya nidasatō । kayakiccāvi hu bhayavaṁ 'namōtthu titthassa' iya bhaṇa3 ||88 ॥
aha samavasaraṇa sīhāsaṇaṁ saruvakhaṁ payāhiṇīkāuṁ । puvvābhimuhō bhayavaṁ uvavisara tilōyahiyakārī ॥ 89 ॥
annāivi jiṇapaḍirūvagāī tinnēva tisuvidisāsu । ṭhāviṁti surā sīhāsaṇammi akaliyapahāvāṇi ।।
90 ।।
tāī ca tappabhāvēṇa tayaṇurūvāī caiva sōhaṁti । aha caurūvō jāō ēgōvi supāsajiṇanāhō || 91 ॥
taṁ ca namiūṇa dēvā kēvi hu gāyati kēvi naccati । phōrḍiti kēvi tivaī kuṇaṁti taha saṁbhavaṁ kēvi ॥ 92 ॥
jiṇavarapayapaumōvari amaṁdamayaraṁdabiṁdusaṁvaliyaṁ । muṁcati kēvi dēvā paṇavannaṁ jalaruhasamūhaṁ ॥ 93||
cēlaca lēhiṁ vīyaṁti kēvi kēvi hu kuṇaṁti bhattīē । ubbhiyabhuvadaṁḍā caṁḍataṁḍavāḍaṁbaraṁ puraō || 14 ||
raṁbhāpamuhāō vilāsiṇīō saṁgīyakaraṇaniuṇāō । payaḍiyabhāvābhiṇayaṁ harisiyahiyayāō naccati ॥95॥
ētthaṁtarasmi sirikaliyama uḍa maṇikiraṇakavisiyadasāsā। savvē surāsuriṁdā tipayāhiṇa puvvagaṁ namiḍaṁ । 96 ।
niyaniyasamuciyaṭhāṇētu saṁnisannā, sahassanayaṇēṇa । ētyaṁtarē nisiddhō surayaṇakōlāhalō sahasā ॥97॥
bhayakaṁpi daṇamālāmaūhasalilēṇa dhōiyāivva । vimalāē ēgāivi aṇēgajaṇasaṁsayaharāē || 98॥
suranara tirikkhasāhāraṇāē jalavāhagajjigahirāē । saṁsāradukkhasaṁtattasattasaṁtāvahariṇī ॥99॥
jōyaṇamittapaḍiphalaṇapañcalāē girāē mahurāē । aha parisāē supāsō sāhēuṁ dhammamārō ॥ 100 ॥
ētthaṁtarammi vaṇapāliyāē acabhūyaṁ bhuvaṇaguruṇō । riddhiṁ palōiūṇaṁ sasaṁbhramaṁ vimhiyamaṇāē || 101 ॥
praṇamyamānaḥ sādaranara kinnara khacarasurasamūhaiḥ । surapatidarśitamārgaḥ pūrvadvārēṇa praviśati ॥ 87 ॥
mamāpi tannamanīyaṁ tīrthaṁ lōkānāmiti nidarśayan । kr̥takr̥tyō'pi hi bhagavān 'namō'stu tīrthāya' iti bhaṇati ॥ 88 ॥
atha samavasaraṇasiṁhāsanaṁ savr̥kṣaṁ pradakṣiṇīkr̥tya । pūrvābhimukhō bhagavānupaviśati trilōkīhitakārī ॥ 89 ॥
anyānyapi jinapratirūpakāṇi trīṇyēva tisr̥ṣvapi dikṣu । sthāpayanti surāḥ siṁhāsanē'ka litaprabhāvāṇi ॥90॥
tāni ca tatprabhāvēṇa tadanurūpāṇyēva śōbhantē । atha catūrūpō jāta ēkō'pi supārśvajinanāthaḥ ॥ 91 ॥
taṁ ca natvā dēvāḥ kē'pi khalu gāyanti kē'pi nr̥tyanti । sphōṭayanti kē'pi tripadīṁ kurvanti tathā saṁstavaṁ kē'pi ॥92॥
jinaparapādapadmōparyamandamakarandabindusaṁvalitam । muñcanti kēspi dēvāḥ pañcavarṇaṁ jalaruhasamūham ॥93॥
cēlāca vījayanti kēspi kē'pi hi kurvanti bhaktyā । ūdhvitabhujadaṇḍā caṇḍatāṇḍavāḍambaraṁ purataḥ ॥94॥
rambhāpramukhā vilāsinyaḥ saṁgītakaraṇanipuṇāḥ । prakaṭitabhāvābhinayaṁ harṣitahr̥dayā nr̥tyanti ॥ 95 ॥
atrāntarē śrīkalitamukuṭamaṇikiraṇakapiśitadaśāśāḥ । sarvē surāsurēndrāstripradakṣiṇāpūrvakaṁ natvā ॥96॥
nijanijasamucitasthānēṣu saṁniṣaṇṇāḥ, sahasūnayanēna । atrāntarē niṣiddhaḥ surajanakōlāhalaḥ sahasā ||97॥
bhagavānapi daśanamālāmayūkhasalilēna dhautayēva । vimalayaikayāpyanēka janasaṁśayaharayā ॥98॥
suranaratiryaksādhāraṇayā jalavāhagajiṁgabhīrayā । saṁsāraduḥkhasaṁtaptasattvasaṁtāpahāriṇyā ॥99॥
yōjanamātrapratiphalanapratyalayā girā madhurayā । atha parṣadi supārśvaḥ kathayituṁ dharmamārabdhaḥ ॥ 100॥
atrāntarē vanapālikayāstyadbhutāṁ suvanagurōḥ । r̥ddhiṁ pralōkya sasaṁgha vipitamanasā ॥ 101 ॥

60
supāsanāha cariammi-
āgaṁtūṇaṁ taha paṇamiṇa sirisēharaṁ naravariṁdaṁ । vinnattamamaṁdāṇaṁdagaggayaṁ sassimaṁ puraō ॥ 102 ॥
diṭṭhī dēva ! vaddhasi dēviṁdanariṁdavaṁdiō ajja । tuha ujjāṇē saṁjhāē āgaō jiṇavara supāsō ॥103॥
tassa ya kēvalanāṇaṁ utpannaṁ saṁpayaṁ aṇāvāhaṁ । lōyālōyabbhaṁtara samatthavatthuppayāsakaraṁ ॥ 104 ॥
ēgaṁ tu kāsavakulaṁ na kēvalaṁ dhavaliyaṁ niyajasēṇa । tihuyaṇamavi nīsēsaṁ supāsanā hēṇa nūṇamiṇaṁ ॥ 105 ॥
piccha savvatthavisāmi ! sālapuraō cauvihasurāṇaṁ । rayaṇamayavimāṇēhiṁ rēhai nayaraṁ surapurivva ।। 106 ।।
aha bhattibharōṇayama ulimiliyakarasaṁ puḍō paṇamiūṇa । harisēṇa jiṇavariṁdaṁ thōḍaṁ sakkatthaēṇa taō ।। 107 ॥
dāu ghaṇaddhatērasalakkhē dāṇammi tīē, paḍihāraṁ । āṇaviḍaṁ nayarīē kāravara mahūsavaṁ rāyā ॥ 108 ॥
taha paḍapaḍahapayāṇēṇa pauralōyaṁ pavaṭṭaē savvaṁ । samuciyasiṁgārēṇaṁ jiṇanāhanamasaṇāhēuṁ ॥ 109 ॥
sayamavi ya mattamayagala uttuṁgaturaṁga rahavaraṭhiēhiṁ । aṁtēra suya sāmaṁtamaṁtirvidēhiṁ paripariō ॥110॥
saṁcaliō jāva tarhi tāva yathaṇa sihara luliyahāralayā । karakaliyakaṇayadaṁḍā pavisēuṁ bhaṇai paḍihārī ॥ 111 ॥
dēva ! purā tubbhēhiṁ cauramaī nāma pēsiō ō । jō āsi mayaṇamaṁjarikannāē sayaṁvaranimittaṁ ॥ 112 ॥
aṁgāhivavaṁgāhivamagahāhivanaravaīṇa kumarāṇaṁ । āmaṁtaṇatthamihiṁ sō cihai dāradēsamma ॥ 113 ॥
tō muṁcatti bhaṇiē naravaiṇā sō pavēsiō tīē । gharaṇiyalaṁviluliyāsirō vinnavai sarūtramaha pahuṇō ॥ 114 ॥
ahamāsa gaō tuha sāsaṇāō aṁgāinivapasūyāṇaṁ । āhavaṇatthaṁ kannāsayaṁvarē dēva ! kumarāṇaṁ ॥ 115 ॥
āgatya tathā praṇamya śrīśēkharaṁ naravarēndram | vijñaptamamandānandgadgadaṁ tasyēdaṁ purataḥ ॥ 102 ॥
diṣṭyā dēva ! vardhyasē dēvēndranarēndravanditō'dya । tavōdyānē saṁdhyāyāmāgatō jinavara supārśvaḥ ॥ 103 ॥
tasya ca kēvalajñānamuspannaṁ sāṁpratamanābādham । lōkālōkābhyantarasamasta vastuprakāśakaram ॥104॥
ēkaṁ tu kāśyapakulaṁ na kēvalaṁ dhavalitaṁ nijayaśasā । tribhuvanamapi niḥśēṣaṁ supārśvanāthēna nūnamidam ॥ 105
paśya sarvatrāpi svāmin ! śālapurataścaturvidhasurāṇām । ratnamayavimānai rājati nagaraṁ surapurīva ॥ 106 ॥
atha bhaktibharāvanatamaulimilitakarasaṁpuṭaḥ praṇamya । harṣēṇa jinavarēndraṁ stutvā śakrastavēna tataḥ ॥ 107॥
dattvā dhanārdha trayōdaśalakṣāṇi dānē tasyai, pratihāram । ājñapya nagaryāṁ kārayati mahōtsavaṁ rājā ॥ 108 ॥
tathā paṭupaṭahapradānēna pauralōkaṁ vartayati sarvam । samucitaśr̥ṅgārēṇa jinanāthanamasyanahētōḥ ॥ 109 ॥
svayamapi ca mattamadakalōttuṅgaturaṅgarathavara sthitaiḥ । antaḥpurasutasāmantamantrivr̥ndaiḥ parikaritaḥ ॥ 110 ॥
saṁcalitō yāvattatra tāvacca stana śikharaluṭhitahāralatā । karakalitakanakadaṇḍā praviśya bhaṇati pratihārī ॥ 111 ॥
dēva ! purā yuṣmābhiścaturamatirnāma prēṣitō dūtaḥ । ya āsīd madanamañjarīkanyāyāḥ svayaṁvaranimittam ।। 112॥
aṅgādhipabaṅgādhipamagadhādhipanarapatīnāṁ kumārāṇām । āmantraṇārthamidānīṁ sa tiṣṭhati dvāradēśē ॥ 113॥
tatō muñcēti bhaṇitē narapatinā sa pravēśitastayā । gharaṇitalaviluṭhitaśirā vijñapayati svarūpamasau prabhavē ॥ 114 ॥
ahamāsaṁ gatastava śāsanādaṅgādinr̥paprasūtānām । āhvānārthaṁ kanyāsvayaṁvarē dēva ! kumārāṇām ॥ 115 ॥
1 ga. raputtamahaṁta maṁtisāmaṁta pari° ।
