kēvalapatthāvō ।.
61
uciyapaḍivattipuvvaṁ maēvi savvē kamēṇa saccaviyā । nīsēsaguṇijaṇāulapuhaī acchērayanbhūyā ॥ 116 ॥
jaṁ jaṁ saṁbaṁdhaviū varēsu jōaṁti kiṁpi taṁ tāṇaṁ । kularūvavivapabhiī nīsāmannapi sāmannaṁ ॥ 117||
aha jōggayaṁ muṇē savvāṇavi sāsaṇaṁ tuha nariṁda ! | saṁpāḍiyaṁ ca tēhivi paḍicchiyaṁ namiramaulīhiṁ ।। 118 ॥
tō takkhaṇa dinnapayāṇabhēribhaṁkāratumuliya diyaṁtā | sajjiyaca uraṁgavalā āucchiyagurujaṇā caliyā | 119 ।
lōbhijjaṁtā guṇakittaṇēṇa kumarīē visamaṭhāṇāī | laṁghittu paṁcanavasaṁkhā kumarā ihaṁ pattā || 120 ॥
tā āisa lahuṁ ciya dīsantudaṁḍapuṁḍarīēhiṁ । ṭiviḍikkijjai tuha nayariparisarō tāṇa sinnēhiṁ ॥ 121 ॥
iya suṇiūṇaṁ ciṁtai naravarōvi ēēvi jaha pasaṁgāō । daṭṭṇa bhuvaṇasāmiṁ lahaṁtu jayalacchipariraṁbhaṁ ॥ 122 ॥
iya tāṇa pavētthaṁ pacōṇīē balē samāisai । tēvi vihiōvayārā pavisaṁti mahāvibhūīē || 123 ||
pattā ya rāyamaṁdiramamaṁdamānaṁdiyā nariṁdēṇa । pariraṁbhiūṇa paṇamaṁtamaṁḍaliṇō niddhavayaṇēhiṁ ॥ 124 ॥
tō kahiyajiṇāgamavaiyarēhiṁ tērhipi parigaō rāyā । niyaaṁvāēya samaṁ sōmāē karēṇuyārūhō ॥ 125॥
jiṇanādasamavasaraṇē saṁcaliō bhattinirucchāhō । pattō kamēṇa tattō kariṇīē lahuṁ samōara ।। 126॥
jāva vihīē parisara ujjāṇavaṇassa majjhabhāgammi । tā jiṇavarassa lacchīvitthāraṁ pāsiuṁ bhaṇai ।। 127॥
ammō ! picchasu puraō kiṁkaraāyāradhārayasurēhiṁ । jiṇanāhaṁ muttūrṇa sēvijjai kassa kamakamalaṁ ॥ 128 ॥
chattattayaṁ ca tihuyaṇasāmitvalakkhaṇaṁ imaṁ kassa । annassōvari suiraṁ dharaṁti sasipaṁḍuraṁ tiyasā ? ॥ 129 ॥
rayaṇāsaṇē nisannō vīijjai suravarēhiṁ kō annō । ammō ! mōttūṇa jiṇaṁ camaruppīlēhiṁ dhavalēhiṁ ॥ 130 ॥
ucitapratipattipūrvaṁ mayāpi sarvē kramēṇa dr̥ṣṭāḥ । niḥśēṣaguṇijanākulapr̥thivyāścaryabhūtāḥ ॥ 116 ॥
yadyat saṁbandhavidō varēṣu paśyanti kimapi tattēṣām । kularūpavibhavaprabhr̥ti niḥsāmānyamapi sāmānyam ॥117॥
atha yōgyatāṁ jñātvā sarvēṣāmapi śāsanaṁ tava narēndra ! | saṁpāditaṁ ca tairapi pratīṣṭaṁ namramaulibhiḥ ॥118॥
tatastatkṣaṇadattaprayāṇabhērībhāṅkāratu mulitadigantāḥ । sajjitacaturaṅgabalā āpr̥ṣṭagurujanāścalitāḥ ॥ 119॥
lōbhyamānā guṇakīrtanēna kumāryā viṣamasthānāni । laṅghitvā pañcanavatisaṁkhyāḥ kumārā iha prāptāḥ ॥ 120॥
tasmādādiśa ladhvēva dr̥śyamānōddaṇḍapuṇḍarīkaiḥ । maṇḍyatē tava nagaraparisarastēṣāṁ sainyaiḥ ॥ 121 ॥
iti śrutvā cintayati naravarō'pyētē 'pi yathā prasaṅgāt । dr̥ṣṭrā bhuvanasvāminaṁ labhantāṁ jayalakṣmīparirambham ॥ 122 ॥
iti tēṣāṁ pravēśārthaṁ pratyunnītaṁ balaṁ samādiśati । tē'pi vihitōpacārāḥ praviśanti mahāvibhūtyā ॥ 123॥
prāptāśca rājamandiramamandamānanditā narēndrēṇa । parirabhya praṇamanmaulayaḥ snigdhavacanaiḥ ॥ 124॥
tataḥ kathitajināgamatryatikaraistairapi parigatō rājā । nijāmbayā ca samaṁ sōmayā karēṇukārūḍhaḥ ॥ 125 ॥
jinanāthasamavasaraṇē saṁcalitō bhaktinirmarōtsāhaḥ । prāptaḥ kramēṇa tataḥ kariṇyā laghu samavatarati ॥ 126॥
yāvad vidhinā praviśatyudyānavanasya madhyabhāgē । tāvajjinavarasya lakṣmīvistāraṁ dr̥ṣṭvā bhaṇati ॥ 127॥
amba' ! paśya purataḥ kiṅkarā kāradhārakasuraiḥ । jinanāthaṁ muktvā sēvyatē kasya karakamalam ॥ 128 ॥
chatratrayaṁ ca tribhuvanasvāmitvōpalakṣaṇamidaṁ kasya । anyasyōpari suciraṁ gharanti śaśipāṇḍuraṁ tridaśāḥ ? ॥ 129॥

62
supāsanāda- cariammi-
I
maṇimaiyadhammacakkacchalēṇa bhāṇūvi kaṁ samaliyai ? | surā kamalāṇi va kassa ya payavināsa paḍicchaṁti ? ||
bhamirabhamaraulamuhalā kassa purō paḍai kusumabuṭṭīvi । gayaṇāu muttiramaṇīkaḍakkhamālavva aitaralā ॥132॥
iya sāhitō jaṇaṇīē savvaō harisanibharō rāyā । paḍhamaṁ pāyāramaikamittu duiyaṁ samāruhai ॥ 133॥
tattha ya piccha bahubhavaparibhramaṇajjiyamahaṁtavērāṇaṁ । jīvāṇaṁ mihuṇāī annōnapasannacittā ॥ 134 ॥
tattō puṇōvi pabhaṇai aṁba ! mahacchērayaṁ imaṁ jayahaṁ । jiṇanāhasahāē jaha milati ēkammi vērigaṇā ।। 135 ॥
majjārassa sirammiya nahaggabhāgēhi mūsaō kaha ṇu | kaṁḍuyamāṇō nisuṇai jiṇavayaṇaṁ mukaāryakō ।। 136 ।।
aiuggavisabhuyaṁgama phaṇākaḍappammi niyasi uvavihō । sālūrō gayavērō jaṇai jaṇāṇaṁ mahacchariyaṁ ।। 137|
cattapaōsassa ciraṁ maō mayaṁdassa kēsarakalāvaṁ । īsummīliyanayaṇassa aggasiṁgēṇa vivarēi ॥ 138॥
vaṇamahisō gavalaggēṇa niyaha turayassa lōyaṇarddhataṁ । kaṁḍuyamāṇō na kuṇai jiṇavayaṇaparassa viharataṁ ॥
niccalasāmalasihikaṁṭhakaṁdalē kōmalē kisalayanna । uyaha ahī jiṇavayaṇa kuṁḍaliyakalēvarō suṇaḥ ।। 140 ॥
picchasu kaḍāra kēsarakaḍappaduṣpicchapaṁcatrayaṇāṇa | majjhē saṁvaliyakarō vasaī karī jivāvēṇa ॥149॥
iya ēvamāiaccunbhuyāī vimhayakarāī aṁvāē । daṁsiṁtō naranāhō pattō taiyammi pāyārē ॥ 142 ॥
tattha ya niruvamabhattīparavvasō vahalapulayakaliyaṁgō । ānaṁdapurassara surasamūhapicchijjamāṇō ya ॥ 143 ॥
niyaparivārēṇa juō piyāhiṇadāṇapucvagaṁ rāyā । rayaṇamayapāyapīḍhaggabhāyaviṇihittabhālayalō।। 144॥
ratnāsanē niṣaṇṇī vījyatē suravaraiḥ kō'nyaḥ । amba ! muktvā jinaṁ cāmarasaṁghātairvavalaiḥ 1 ॥ 130 ॥
maṇimayadharmacakracchalēna bhānurapi kē samupasarpati ? | surāḥ kamalānīva kasya ca pādavinyāsaṁ pratīcchanti ॥ 131 ॥
bhramaṇaśīlabhramarakulamukharā kasya puraḥ patati kusumavr̥ṣṭirapi । gaganānmukti ramaṇīkaṭākṣamālē vātitaralā ? ॥ 132 ॥
iti kathayañjananīṁ sarvatō harṣanirbharō rājā । prathamaṁ prākāramatikramya dvitīyaṁ samārōhati ॥ 133 ॥
tatra ca paśyati bahubhavaparibhramaṇārjitamahāvairāṇām । jīvānāṁ mithunāni anyōnyaprasannacittāni ॥ 134॥
tataḥ punarapi prabhaṇati amba ! mahāścaryamidaṁ paśya । jinanāthasabhāyāṁ yathā milanti ēkatra vairiṁgaṇāḥ ॥ 135 ॥
mārjārasya śirasi ca namō'grabhāgairmūṣakaḥ kathaṁ nu । kaṇḍūyamānaḥ śr̥ṇōti jinavacanaṁ muktātaṅkaḥ ॥ 136॥
atyugraviṣabhujaṅgamaphaṇānikarē paśyasyupaviṣṭaḥ । śālūrō gatavairō janayati janānāṁ mahāścaryam ॥ 137॥
tyaktapradvēṣasya ciraṁ mr̥gō mr̥gēndrasya kēsarākalāpam । īṣadunmīlitanayanasyāgraśr̥ṅgēṇa vivr̥ṇōti ॥138॥
vanamahiṣō gavalāyēṇa paśya turagasya lōcanaparyantam । kaṇḍūyamānō na karōti jinavacanaparasya vidhuratvam ।।
niścalaśyāṁmalaśikhikaṇṭhakandalē kōmalē kiśalayamiva । paśyāhirjinavacanaṁ kuṇḍalitakalēvara: śr̥ṇōti ॥ 140 ॥
paśya kaḍāra kē tarā nikara durdarśapañcavadanānām । madhyē saṁvalitakarō vasati karī jinaprabhāvēṇa ॥149॥
ityēvamādyatyadbhutāni vismayakarāṇyambāyai । darśayan naranāthaḥ prāptastr̥tīyē prākārē ॥ 142 ॥
tatra ca nirupamabhaktiparavaśō bahulapulakakalitāṅgaḥ । ānandapurassara surasamūhadr̥śyamānaśca ॥ 143॥
nijaparivārēṇa yutastripradakṣiṇādānapūrvakaṁ rājā । ratnamayapādapīṭhāgrabhāgavinihitabhālatalaḥ ॥ 144 ॥

kēvalatthāvā |
63
namiūṇa jiṇavariṁdaṁ paṇanavaikumarēhiṁ parigaō saṇiyaṁ । puñyuttara disibhāgē nivasai suddhammi mahivīḍē ॥
tajjaṇaṇīva hu naravaiavarōhavahūhiṁ parigayā tattha । puraōṁ kāūṇa nivaṁ ubaṭṭiyā ciṭa pahihā ॥ 146 ॥
aha tēsu nividvēsuṁ bhālayalālīṇaaṁjalipuḍēsu । bhayavaṁ supāsanāhō ēvaṁ dhamakkahaṁ kahai || 147॥
bhō bhō dēvāṇupiyā ! saṁsārē māṇusattaṇaṁ sāraṁ । taṁ puṇa dasahiṁ culagapamuhāharaṇēhiṁ aidulahaṁ ।। 148 ||
tathāhi;
1
mōhāikammaainiviḍavipaḍaniyaḍēhiṁ niyaḍiyā kēvi । jīvā aṇaṁtakāyābhihāṇaguttīē nivasati ॥ 149 ॥
tēsiṁ ca mōhamōhiyamaīṇa kahakahavi didviviyammi । pattēyavaṇassaibhūmiyāvi saṁjāyaē nūṇaṁ ॥ 150॥
tatthavi pattā kēvi hū tilapīsayagōṇauntra cirakālaṁ । cihnati paribhamaṁtā puṇōvi tatthēva tatthēva ॥ 151 ॥
tattō ō vimukkā kahakahavi ahāpavattakaraṇēṇa । sēsēgiṁdiyajaṁtusu varayā vañcati tē jīvā ॥ 152 ॥
tatthavi kukammavujhyā ṇagāṇa saṁtāḍaṇēṇa cirakālaṁ । tatthēva jaha tahacciya girivva khittā sahati duhaṁ ॥
vasiūṇōsappiṇisappiṇīutāu tatthēva tē jīvā । vigalidiēsu kahakahavi divvajōēṇa jāyati ।। 154 ।।
tatthavi tamapaḍalaṁtariyalōyaṇā tēsu cēva aṇavarayaṁ । taruvarasāhāsuva aṁdhavāyasā paribhamaṁti ciraṁ ।। 155 ।।
tāṇaṁ ca taō sulahaṁ kahaṁ nu paṁcidiyattaṇaṁ haṁta ! | jāṇaṁ na tippēi vihī vigaliṁdiyapabhavadukkhēhiṁ ।। 156 ।।
aha kavi kammapariṇaivasēṇa aṇukūlabhāvamāvannō । jai sōvi dugghaḍaṁ ghaḍai kahavi paṁcidiē jammaṁ ॥
tahavi hu dūsahanārayaviḍaṁbaṇāhi viḍaṁbai bhavasmi । taha kahavi jaha na vīrai vayaṇasahassēhiṁvi kahēuṁ ॥
natvā jinavarēndraṁ pañcanavatikumāraiḥ parigataḥ śanaiḥ । pūrvōttaradigbhāgē nivasati śuddhē mahīpīṭhē ॥ 145 ॥
tajjananyapi khalu narapatyavarōdha vadhūbhiḥ parigatā tatra । purataḥ kr̥tvā nr̥pamupasthitā tiṣṭhati prahr̥ṣṭā ॥ 146॥
atha tēṣu niviṣṭēṣu bhālatalālīnāñjalipuṭēṣu । bhagavān supārśvanātha ēvaṁ dharmakathāṁ kathayati ॥ 147 ॥
bhō bhō dēvānupriyāḥ ! saṁsārē manuṣyatvaṁ sāraḥ । tat punardaśabhiśculakapramukhōdāharaṇairatidurlabham ॥148॥
mōhādikarmātinibiḍavikaṭa nigaḍairnigaḍitāḥ kē'pi । jīvā anantakāyābhidhānaguptau nivasanti ॥ 149॥
tēṣāṁ ca mōhamōhitamatīnāṁ kathaṁ kathamapi dr̥ṣṭiviṣayē । pratyēkavanaspatibhūmikāpi saṁjāyatē nūnam ॥ 150॥
tatrāpi prāptāḥ kē'pi khalu tilapēpakagava iva cirakālam । tiṣṭhanti paribhramantaḥ punarapi tatraiva tatraiva ॥ 151 ॥
tatastatō vimuktāḥ kathaṁkathamapi yathāpravr̥ttakaraṇēna । śēṣaikēndriyajantuṣu varākā vrajanti tē jīvāḥ ॥ 152 ॥
tatrāpi kukarmavr̥tā nagānāṁ saṁtāḍanēna cirakālam । tatraiva yathā tathaiva giraya iva kṣiptāḥ sahantē duḥkham ।। 153॥
uṣitvāvasarpiṇyutsarpiṇīranantāstatraiva tē jīvāḥ । vikalēndriyēṣu kathaṁkathamapi daivayōgēna jāyantē ॥ 154॥
tatrāpi tamaḥpaṭalāntaritalōcanāstēṣvēvānavaratam । taruvaraśākhāsvivāndhavāyasāḥ paribhramanti ciram ॥ 156 ॥
?
tēṣāṁ ca tataḥ sulabhaṁ kathaṁ nu pañcēndriyatvaṁ hanta ! । yēṣāṁ na tr̥pyati vidhirvika lōndrayaprabhavaduḥ khaiḥ 1 ॥ 156 ॥
atha kathamapi karmapariṇativaśēnānukūlabhāvamāpannaḥ । yadi sō'pi durghaṭaṁ ghaṭayati kathamapi pañcēndriyē janma ||
tathāpi hi duḥsahanārakaviḍambanābhirviḍambayati bhavē । tathā kathamapi yathā na śakyatē vadanasahasrairapi kayitum ॥

supāsanāha cariambhi -
ēvaṁ kili kammammi dhummiyāṇaṁ iō taō tāṇaṁ । bahupōggalapariyaṭṭāvaṭṭavivaṭṭīṇa aṇavarayaṁ ॥ 159 ॥
ghaṇajōṇilakkhakacchavaga lacchaṇātikkhadukkha duhiyāṇa । kiṇhapamukkhālēsāabālasēvālakaliyāṇa ॥ 160॥
kōhamahāvaḍavānalatattāṇaṁ rāyapaṁkakhuttāṇaṁ । micchattamacchabhīyāṇa kalisasalilammi buḍḍāṇaṁ || 161॥
jīvāṇa bhavasamuddē aṇōrapārammi dullahaṁ ēyaṁ । maṇuyattajāṇavattaṁ visālakulajāidalakaliyaṁ ॥ 162॥
taṁ
puṇa
pattaṁpi hu kahakahaṁpi rahiyaṁ sukannadhārēṇa । tatthēva nimajjaṁtaṁ puṇōvi kō dhāriḍaṁ tarai ? ।। 163 ||
tē ya puṇa kandhārā duvihā cidvaṁti bhavasamudammi । ēgē kutitthapatthāṇapatthiyā maggamūḍhāya ॥ 164 ॥
annē uṇa sayalaavāyarakkhaṇakhamā bhavasamudamaggammi । dīvaṁtarēsu saṁbalasaṁpāḍaṇāppā ||165||
tā jai samma aparikkhiūṇa puvyuttakannadhārāṇaṁ । vayaṇēṇa paripillai jīvō maṇuyattavōhitthaṁ ॥ 166॥
tā māṇamīṇakhaliyē maccharamayarāṇaṇammi paḍiphaliyam । māyāvittalayāvaṇagahaṇē gāḍhaṁ nigūḍhaṁva ।। 167।।
lōhamaha। girigurusihara ghaṭṭaṇājajjarijjamāṇaṁtra | abalakāmakallōlamālaāvattapaḍiyaṁva || 168 ||
mōhamahāgirikuharaṁtarālavāsīhi laddhalakkhēhiṁ । lūḍijjataṁ iṁdiyacōrēhiṁ sudunnivārēhiṁ ॥ 169 ॥
kōhamahāvaḍavānalakarālajālāvalīkalijjataṁ । ruddajjhāṇabhihāṇēṇa savararāēṇa hīraṁtaṁ ॥ 170 ॥
rāyaggāhapasāriyauyāra siṁgāradāḍhauragāḍhaṁ । visayamahāvisavisaharasaēhi vēṭijjamānaṁ ॥ 171 ॥
iya ēvama bahuvihaavāyapaḍiyaṁ taḍatti phutaṁ । kiṁkāyavyavimūḍhā na hu tē pāraṁti taṁ dhariu || 172 ||
tampiya phuṭṭē jīvō puṇōvi saṁsārajalahimajjhammi | nivaḍai anaṁtakāyāiēsa dukkhāī ya sahē || 173 ||
ēvaṁ kliṣṭakarmaṇā ghūrṇitānāmitastatastēṣām । bahupudgalaparāvartāvartavivartinā manavaratam ॥159॥
ghanayōnilakṣakacchapakalakṣaṇatīkṣṇaduḥkhaduḥkhitānām । kr̥ṣṇapramukhya lēśyā'bālaśaivālakalitānām ॥ 160 ॥
krōdhamahāvaḍavānalataptānāṁ rāgapaṅkamagnānām । mithyātvamatsyabhītānāṁ klēśasalilē magnānām । || 161॥
jīvānāṁ bhavasamudrē'nādipārē durlabhamētat । manujatvayānapātraṁ viśāla kulajātidalakalitam ॥ 162॥
tat punaḥ prāptamapi hi kathaṁ kathamapi rahitaṁ sukarṇadhārēṇa । tatraiva nimajjat punarapi kō dhārayituṁ śaknōti ?||
tē ca punaḥ karṇadhārā dvividhāstiṣṭhanti bhavasamudrē । ēkē kutīrthaprasthānaprasthitā mārgamūḍhāśca ॥ 164॥
anyē punaḥ sakalāpāyarakṣaṇakṣamā bhavasamudramārgē । dvīpāntarēṣu śambalasaṁpādanaprakaṭamāhātmyāḥ ॥ 165॥
tasmād yadi samyagaparīkṣya pūrvōktakarṇadhārāṇām । vacanēna paripīḍayati jīvō manujatvayānapātram ॥ 166॥
tatō mānamīnaskhalitaṁ matsaramakarānanē pratiphalitam । māyāvr̥ttalatāvr̥nagahanē gāḍhaṁ nigūḍhamiva ॥ 167 ॥
lōbhamahāgiriguruśikhara ghaṭṭanā jarjaryamāṇamiva । atiprabalakāma kallōlamālāvartapatitamiva ॥ 168 ॥
mōhamahāgirikuharāntarālavāsibhirlabdhalakṣyaiḥ । luṇṭyamānamindriyacauraiḥ sudurnivāraiḥ ॥ 169॥
krōdhamahāvaḍavānalakarālajvālāvalīkalyamānam । raudradhyānābhidhānēna śavararājēna hiyamāṇam ॥ 170 ॥
rāgagrāhaprasāritōdāraśr̥ṅgāradaṁṣṭrōdgāḍham | viṣayamahāviṣaviṣadharaśatairvēṣṭyamānamiva ॥ 171 ॥
ityēvamādibahuvidhāpāyapatitaṁ taditi sphuṭyamānam । kiṁkartavyavimūḍhā na khalu tē pārayanti tad dhartum ॥

kēvalapatthācō |
65
tā iha kutitthapatthiyakukannahārē lahuṁ vimōttr̥ṇa । sammaṁ parikkhiūṇaṁ sukannadhārē ya aṇusaraha || 174 |
tē puṇa saṁsāramahāsamudataraṇammi kannadhārasamā । paṁca paramiṭṭiṇō cciya jayattaē payaḍamāhappā ॥ 175 ॥
jēṇaṁ tē cciya ummaggamaggirāṇaṁ nivāraṇasamatthā | jahavadviyaparibhāviyasaṁsa | rōdahisarūvā ya ।।176।।
ticciya puvvapasāhiyaavāyaniyarāu rakkhiūṇa imaṁ । avvāvāhapaṇaṁ niṁti sucāritadīvapi ॥ 177॥
tatthavi ya savvasāvajjaviraināmammi tuṁgasēlammi | nēūṇa vara mahavvayarayaṇāī khivaṁti ēyammi || 178 ||
jēhi karayalakaliērhi natthi bhuvaṇēvi kiṁpi hu asajyaṁ । nivbuipurīvi paramā niyaḍacciya havai lahumēva ||
tasa ya giriṇī uvariṁ dasavihamuṇidhammanāmarukkhāō । asamahārasa sīliṁgasahasaphalaniyaramuvarṇiti ।।
tassaviya aggabhāgē kēvalanāṇābhihāṇasiharammi । vīsāmiūṇa kaivayadiṇāī tō tassa aggammi181
nivvāṇapurī fear bhavapārāvāraparamatīrasamā | tammi ya ṭhavaṁti jīvaṁ mōttuṁ maṇuyattavōhityaṁ ॥ 182 ॥
jīēna jammō na jarā naya maraṇaṁ nēha chuhapivāsāvi । naya rāyarōsarōyā na bhayaṁ naya sōyalēsōvi ॥
navyāmōhō na maō navi ciṁtā nēya khēyasōyāvi । na visāō navi niddā kayāi araī naya kharṇapi ॥
kēvalamamaṁdaāṇaṁdaamayasēēṇa akkhayasarūvō । niraṁjaṇō thirappā jīvō rayaṇa pavōcca ॥ 185 ॥
lōyālōyabbhaṁtara samatthasupasatthavatyuvitthāraṁ । ujjōyaṁtō ciṭṭhai sayāvi akhaṁḍiyappasarō ॥ 186॥
ētyaṁtarasmi paṇanavaikumarēhiṁ pucchiō jiṇavariṁdō । bhayavaṁ ! jē tubbhēhi kahiyā iha kannadhārasamā । 187|
tasmiṁśca sphuṭitē jīvaḥ punarapi saṁsārajaladhimadhyē । nipatatyanantakāyādikēṣu duḥkhāni ca sahatē ॥ 173 ॥
tasmādiha kutīrthaprasthitakukarṇadhārāllaghu vimucya । samyak parīkṣya sukarṇadhārāṁścānusarata ॥ 174॥
tē
punaḥ saṁsāramahāsamudrataraṇē karṇadhārasamāḥ । pañca paramēṣṭhina ēva jagattrayē prakaṭamāhātmyāḥ ॥175॥
yēna ta ēvōnmārgamārgikāṇāṁ nivāraṇasamarthāḥ । yathāvasthitaparibhāvitasaṁsārōdadhisvarūpāśca ॥ 176 ॥
taēva pūrvaprakathitāpāyanikarād rakṣitvēdam । avyābādhapathēna nayanti sucāritradvīpam ॥ 177॥
tatrāpi ca sarvasāvadyaviratināmni tuṅgaśailē । nītvā varamahāvrataratnāni kṣipantyētasmin ॥178॥
yaiḥ karatalakalitairnāsti bhuvanē'pi kimapi sādhyam । nirvr̥tipuryapi paramā nikaṭaiva bhavati ladhvēva ॥ 179॥
tasya ca girērupari daśavidhamunidharmanāmavr̥kṣāt । asamāṣṭādaśaśīlāṅgasahasraphalanikaramupanayanti ॥ 180॥
tasyāpi cāgrabhāgē kēvalajñānābhidhānaśikharē । viśramya katipayadināni tatastasyāyē ॥ 181 ॥
nirvāṇapurī tiṣṭhati bhavapārāvāraparamatīrasamā । tasyāṁ ca sthāpayanti jīvaṁ mōktuṁ manujatvayānapātram ॥ 182॥
yasyāṁ na janma na jarā naca maraṇaṁ nēha kṣutpipāsē api । naca rāgarōṣarōgā na bhayaṁ naca śōkalēśō'pi ।। 183 ॥
na vyāmōhōna madō nāpi cintā naca khēdaśōkāvapi । na viṣādō nāpi nidrā kadāpyaratirnaca kṣaṇamapi ॥
kēvalamamandānandāmr̥ta sēkēnākṣayasvarūpaḥ । nirañjanaḥ sthirātmā jīvō ratnapradīpa iva ॥ 185 ॥
lōkālōkābhyantarasamasta supraśastavastuvistāram । udyōtayaṁstiṣṭhati sadāpyakhaṇḍitaprasaraḥ ॥ 186॥
atrāntarē pañcanavatikumāraiḥ pr̥ṣṭō jinavarēndraḥ । bhagavan ! yē yuṣmābhiḥ kathitā iha karṇadhārasamāḥ ॥ 187॥

paṁca para miṭṭaṇa tē pattēyaṁ kahaha amha pasiūṇa । tō kahai jiṇō tāṇaṁ pattēya paṇa jiṇāīē || 188 ॥
aha paṇanauī kumarā calaṇēsuṁ nivaḍiūṇa jayaguruṇō । saṁsāravirattamaṇā ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samāraddhā॥189॥
bhayavaṁ ! paḍhamā tubbhē paṇaparamidvīṇa bhavajalanihissa | pāragayā, tā iṇhi amhēvi hu tuha pasāēṇa ॥ 190 ॥
tumēhiṁ kannavāmēhi maṇuyatta jāṇavattambhi | kahakahavi hu ārūḍhā duttarabhavajalahimajjhāōṁ ॥ 191 ॥
tuha parikahiyapaṇaṁ nivvāṇapurammi gaṁtumicchāmō । tō bhayavayāvi bhaṇiyaṁ juttaṁ tumhārisāṇa imaṁ । । 192॥
ēvamutrabūhiṇaṁ jayaguruṇā dikkhiyā sahatthēṇa | piṁgalakumāra muhā kajhvayalōgēṇa pariyariyā || 193 ॥
aat freandisōhiyā cittasattisaṁjuttā । vōcchinnanēhaniyaḍā visiddhakulajā saṁpannā ||194||
paricattasavvasaṁgā samatyasupasatthasatthapāragayā । suravisaravaṁdaṇijjā tē paṇana mahāmuṇiṇō || 195||
jaidhammabhāraduddharadhuraṁdharā guṇakalāvaparikaliyā । rēhaṁti sissakalahēhiṁ parivuḍā disigadavva ॥ 196 ॥
ētyaṁtarammi anē rāīsara siṭṭhisatthavāhasuyā । sāmaṁtamaṁtiṇō taha avi visiḍakulaputtā ॥197॥
bhavavāsuvviggamaṇā kayāhilāsā ya savvaviraīē । jiṇavarasupāsapāsa allīṇā bhayavayā tāhē ।। 198 ।.
puttē kamēṇaṁ tēvi sahatthēṇa dikkhiyā tattō । sōmāvi samaṁ sāmaṁtamaṁtidārēhiṁ sārēhiṁ ॥ 199 ॥
savvaviraī pavajji umahilasamāṇī ubaṭṭiyā puraō । tō tīsēvi mahavvayadā pahuṇā sayaṁ vihiaṁ॥ 200 ॥
jē pavvajjaṁ kāuṁ asamatthā kēvi tē sanārīyā । sāvayadhammē ṭhaviyā ēvaṁ ca supāsanāhassa ॥ 209 ॥
paḍhamammi samōsaraṇē samaggaguṇarayaṇarōhaṇāgiriṁdō । saṁghō caubvihōva ya jāō, aha bhayatrayā tāṇaṁ ॥ 202 ॥
pañca paramēṣṭhinastān pratyēkaṁ kathayāsmān prasadya । tataḥ kathayati jinastēṣāṁ pratyēkaṁ pañca jinādikān ॥ 188 ॥
atha pañcanavatiḥ kumārāścaraṇayōrnipatya jagadgurōḥ । saṁsāraviraktamanasa ēvaṁ bhaṇituṁ samārabdhāḥ ॥ 189 ॥
bhagavan ! prathamā yūyaṁ pañcaparamēṣṭhināṁ bhavajalanidhēḥ । pāragatāḥ, tasmādidānīṁ vayamapi khalu tava prasādēna ॥ 190॥
yuṣmābhiḥ karṇadhārōpamai manujatvayānapātrē । kathaṁkathamapi khalvārūḍhā dustarabhavajalavimadhyāt ॥ 199॥
tava parikathitapathēna nirvāṇapurē gantumicchāmaḥ । tatō bhagavatāpi bhaṇitaṁ yuktaṁ yuṣmādr̥śāmidam ॥192॥
ēvamupabr̥ṁhya jagadguruṇā dīkṣitā svahastēna । piṅgalakumārapramukhāḥ katipayalōkēna parikaritāḥ ॥ 193॥
tatō nirupamarūpōpaśōbhitāścitraśaktisaṁyuktāḥ । vyucchinnasnēha nigaḍā viśiṣṭakulajātisaṁpannāḥ ॥ 194 ॥ .
parityaktasarvasaṅgāḥ samastasupraśastaśāstrapāragatāḥ । suravisaravandanīyāstē pañcanavatirmahāmunayaḥ ॥ 199॥
yatidharmadurdharabhāraghurandharā guṇakalāpaparikalitāḥ । rājanti śiṣyakalabhaiḥ parivr̥tā diggajēndrā iva ॥ 196॥
atrāntarē'nyē rājēśvaraśrēṣṭhisārthavāhasutāḥ । sāmantamantriṇastathā'nyē'pi viśiṣṭakulaputrāḥ ॥ 197॥
bhavavāsōdvignamanasaḥ kr̥tābhilāṣāśca sarvavaratyām । jinavarasupārśvapārśvamālīnāḥ, bhagavatā tadā ॥ 198 ॥
pūrvōktēna kramēṇa tē'pi svahastēna dīkṣitāstataḥ । sōmāpi samaṁ sāmantamantridāraiḥ sāraiḥ ॥ 199॥
sarvaviratiṁ prapattumabhilapamāṇōpasthitā purataḥ । tatastasyā api mahātratadānaṁ prabhuṇā svayaṁ vihitam ॥ 200॥
yē pravrajyāṁ kartumasamarthāḥ kē'pi tē sanārīkāḥ । śrāvakadharmē sthāpitāḥ ēvaṁ ca supārśvanāthasya || 201 ||

paṇanuvaisaṁkhamuṇipuṁgavāṇaṁ sayalatthasaṁgaharāī । upapannavigamadhuvalakkhaṇāī tinnēva ya payāī ।।203 ||
kahiyāī taō aṁtōmuhuttamēttēṇa tayaṇusārēṇa । takālulasiyaaubvabuddhivihavappabhāvēṇaṁ ॥ 204 ||
puvvabhavabbhatthasamatthasatthaparamatthavittharavasēṇaṁ । savvēhiṁ viraiyāī duvālasaṁgāī, ēvaṁ ca ॥ 205 ॥
sayamēva jā jiniṁdō ēē ṭhāvēi gaṇaharapayammi । tā gaṁdhavāsacunna thālē vittr̥̄ṇa sakkōvi ॥ 206 ॥
puraō turiyayaraṁ ciya uvaḍiō avasaraṁti kaliūṇa । tō udviūṇa sāmī minhai cunnaṁ samuṭṭīē || 207॥
tāṇaṁ ca avaṇayāṇaṁ sirammi pakkhivai iya payapatō | tumhāṇamaṇunnāyaṁ titthamimaṁ pajjavaguṇēhiṁ ॥ 208 ॥
ētthaṁtarammi bhamaraulamuhaliyaṁ tāṇamuttimaṁgammi | paṇavannavāsavāsaṁ vihiyaṁ tōsāu tiyasēhiṁ ॥ 209 ॥
sōmajjāva ajāṇa saṁjamujjōyasāsaṇanimittaṁ । ṭhaviyā pavittiṇipaē nimmalasīlēkkakulabhavaṇaṁ ॥
ētthaṁtarammi ughāḍapōrisīsūyagō balī pattō । kāraviō sirisēharanivēṇa varakalamasālimaō॥ 211 ॥
āḍhagamittō ucchāliō ya gahiō surāsuranarēhiṁ । tō savvē suravaiṇō pattā naṁdīsarē dīvē ॥ 212॥
kāū jiṇidāṇaṁ aṭṭhāhiyamaha sadvāṇamaṇupattā | iya kāuṁ bakkhāṇaṁ kavi diṇē tayaṇu jiṇanāhō ॥ 213॥
savvēhiṁ gaṇaharērhi tahaṇēgamuṇīhiṁ sāhuṇīhiṁ ca । pariyariō nikkhatō navakaṁcaṇakamalakayacaraṇō ॥ 214॥
tō āgāsagaēṇaṁ laṁbiyabhuttāvacūlaka liēṇaṁ । chattēṇa tahā sārayasasaṁkadhavalēhiṁ camarēhiṁ ॥ 215 ॥
gayaṇayalāla biyapāyavīḍhasīhāsaṇēṇa viulēṇa । taha māhidajhaēṇaṁ nahamaggagaēṇa rātō ॥ 216 ॥
hu
prathamē samavasaraṇē samagraguṇaratna rōhaṇagirīndraḥ । saṁvaścaturvidhō'pi ca jātaḥ, atha bhagavatā tēṣām ॥ 202 ॥
pañcanavatisaṁkhyamunipuṅgavānāṁ sakalārthasaṁgraha parāṇi । utpannaviṁgamadhruvalakṣaṇāni trīṇyēva ca padāni ॥ 203 ॥
kathitāni tatō'ntarmuhūrtamātrēṇa tadanusārēṇa । tatkālōllasitā pūrvabuddhivibhavaprabhāvēṇa ॥ 204 ॥
pūrvabhavābhyastasamastaśāstraparamārthavistaravaśēna । sarvē viracitāni dvādaśāṅgāni ēvaṁ ca ॥ 205 ॥
svayamēva yāvajñjinēndra ētān sthāpayati gaṇavarapadē । tāvad gandhavāsacūrṇaṁ sthālē gr̥hītvā śakrō'pi ॥ 206॥
puratastvaritatara mēvōpasthitō'vasara iti kalayitvā । tata utthāya svāmī gr̥hṇāti cūrṇa svamuṣṭayā ॥207॥
tēṣāṁ cāvanatānāṁ śirasi prakṣipatīti prajalpan । yuṣmākamanujñātaṁ tīrthamidaṁ paryavaguṇaiḥ ॥ 208 ॥
atrāntarē bhramarakulamukharitastēṣāmuttamāṅgē । pañcavarṇavāsavāsō vihitastōpāt tridaśaiḥ ॥ 209॥
sōmāryāpi khalvāryāṇāṁ saṁyamōdyōtaśāsananimittam । sthāpitā pravartinīpadē nirmalaśīlaikakulabhavanam ॥210॥
atrāntarē udghāṭaparupī sūcakō valiḥ prāptaḥ । kāritaḥ śrīśēkharanr̥pēṇa varakalamaśālimayaḥ ॥ 219 ॥
āḍhakamātra ucchālitaśca gr̥hītaḥ surāsuranaraiḥ । tataḥ sarvē surapatyaḥ prāptā nandīśvarē dvīpē ॥ 212 ॥
kr̥tvā jinēndrāṇāmaṣṭāhikāmatha svasthānamanuprāptāḥ । iti kr̥tvā vyākhyānaṁ katyapi dināni tadanu jinanāthaḥ ॥
sarvairgaṇa dhēraistathānēkamunibhiḥ sādhvībhiśca । parikaritō niṣkrāntō navakāñcanakamalakr̥tacaraṇaḥ ॥ 214॥
tata ākāśagatēna lambitamuktāvacūlakalitēna । chatrēṇa tathā śāradaśaśāṅkaghavalaiścāmaraiḥ ॥ 215 ॥
gaganatalālambitapādapīṭhāsiṁhāsanēna vipulēna । tathā māhēndradhvajēna nabhōmārgagatēna rājan ॥ 216 ॥

sāyaramaṇugacchaṁtīsu bhattiparikaliyatiyasakōḍīsu । vāyaṁtēsu ya aṇukūlasisirasusugaṁdhapavaṇēsu ॥ 217॥

tathāhi-
muṇivēmāṇiyadēvīsāhuṇīō ḍhaṁti aggikōṇammi । jōisiyabhavaṇavaṁtara dēvīō hōṁti nēraīē || 224 ||
bhavaṇavaṇa jōisadēvā vāyavyē, kappavāsiṇō amarā । naranārīō īsāṇē punvāisa pavisiuṁ ṭhaṁti।।225॥
ētyaṁtarē pasiddhī vitthariyā naṁdivaddhaṇapurapi । jaha sirisupāsanāhō ujjāṇē iha samōsariō ||226 ॥
tattō suibhūyataṇū nayarajaṇō jāi jiṇavaraṁ dahuṁ । pūōnagaraṇapaḍalayahatthō supasatthavēsadharō || 227॥
taṁ taha vaccataṁ picchiūṇa sirivijayavaddhaṇō rāyā । pāsāyagavakkhagaō puccha maisāyaramamacaṁ ॥ 228॥
jaha iṁdamahamuha kiṁ kōvi mahasavō nayaramajjhē । pupphakaraṁḍayahatthō jaṁ vaccai ēsa sayalajaṇō ? || 229॥
sādaramanugacchantīṣu bhaktiparikalitatridaśakōṭiṣu । vātsu cānukūlaśiśirasusugandhapavanēṣu ॥ 217॥
adhōmukhaṁ parisaṁsthitēṣu mārgē kaṇṭakagaṇēṣu । bhaktatyēva namantīṣu mārgataruvisaraśrēṇīṣu ॥218॥
anugr̥hṇastathā sarvaviratidānēna bhavya sattvajanam । grāmākaranagara maḍambakhēṭapurakarbaṭādiṣu ॥ 219 ॥
viharan saṁprāptaḥ kramēṇa śrīnandivardhanapurē । pūrvōttaradigvibhāgē kusumakaraṇḍa udyānē ॥ 220॥
pūrvōktēna kramēṇa racitaṁ dēvairvarasamavasaraṇam । ratnamayaprākārābhyantarē siṁhāsanaṁ sthāpitam ॥ 229 ॥
pūrvābhimukhaṁ maṇimayasupādapīṭhēna saṁyutaṁ tataḥ । bhagavān supārśvanāthastrijagatprabhustatrōpaviśati ॥ 222॥
pādapīṭhādūra ēva bhagavantō gaṇadharādikāḥ sarvē । nijanijasthānēṣu sthitāstiryañcō dvitīyē prākārē ॥223॥
munivaimānikadēvī sādhyastiṣṭhantyagnikōṇē । jyautiṣikabhavanavyantaradēvyō bhavanti nairr̥tē ॥ 224 ॥
bhavanavanajyōtipadēvā vāyavyē, kalpavāsinō'marāḥ । naranārya īśānē pūrvādiṣu praviśya tiṣṭhanti ॥ 225 ॥
atrāntarē prasiddhirvistr̥tā nandivardhanapurē । yathā śrīsupārśvanātha udyāna iha samavasr̥taḥ ॥ 296॥
tataḥ śucibhūtatanurnagarajanō yāti jinavaraṁ ṭum । pūjōpakaraṇapaṭalakahastaḥ supraśastavēṣadharaḥ ||227॥
taṁ tathā vrajantaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā śrīvijayavardhanō rājā । prāsādagavākṣagataḥ pr̥cchati matisāgaramamartyam ॥228॥
yathēndramahapramukhaḥ kiṁ kō'pi mahōtsavō nagaramadhyē | puṣpakaraṇḍakahastō yad vrajatyēṣa sakalajanaḥ 1 ॥ 229॥
tataḥ saṁnihitajanājjināgamanaṁ vijñāya sō'pi । jalpati na kō'pyanyō mahōtsavaḥ kintu bahiḥ ||230 ॥

kēvalapatthāvō ।
88
tō saṁnihiyajaṇāō jiṇaāgamaṇaṁ viyāṇiuṁ sōvi । javai na kōvi amnō mahūsavō kiṁtu vāhimmi ॥
ujjāṇavaṇē summai samōsaḍhō sirisupāsatitthayarō | tavvaṁdaṇatthamēsō nayarajaṇō vaccai samaggō ॥231॥
taṁ sōūṇaṁ paṇai naranāhō jaha amacca ! amhēvi । tavvaṁdaṇānimittaṁ vaccisāmō kimantrēṇa ? ॥232॥
bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa tadaṁsaṇaṁpi kallāṇakāraṇaṁ dēva ! । kiṁ puṇa gamaṇanamaṁsaṇapayasēvāpamuhapaḍivattī ॥233॥
tā kuṇasu sayaṁ tadaṁsaṇēṇa maṇuyattassa saphalattaṁ । iya buttē sacivēṇaṁ vijayanariṁdō taō turiyaṁ ||234||
saṁcaliō jiṇavarapāyamūlamaha sō kamēṇa saṁpattō । paṁcavihābhigamēṇaṁ ullasiyāviralarōmaṁcō ||235||
tikkhuttō dāūṇaṁ payāhiṇaṁ paṇamiuṁ ca jiṇanāhaṁ । bhattibharanivbharaṁgō ēvaṁ thuṇiuṁ samārō || 236 ||
dēva ! tuha caraṇanahamaṇimaūhadīvā jayaṁtu jē raviṇō । khaṁḍaṁti caṁḍimaṁ mōhatimiraharaṇēṇa bhuvaṇammi ॥ 237॥
pahu ! bahupayaṁḍapāsaṁḍimaṁḍiē mahiyalammi jīvāṇa । tuha daṁsaṇaṁpi jāyai aṇaṁ bhavacinnapunnēhiṁ ॥ 238 ॥
ajjaṁ ciya maha maṇavaṁchiyāī jāvāī ajja jāō haṁ । cirakālaōvi jaṁ diṭṭigōyarē nāha! taṁ jāō ॥ 239 ॥
tā lahu iṇhi sārayasaṁ punnasa saṁka kiraṇasisirāē । avaharasu niyagirāē jiṇamha bhavagimhasaṁtānaṁ ॥ 240 ॥
iya saṁthōuṁ rāyā uvaciṭṭhā ṭhāviūṇa niyadiṭṭhi । jiṇavaravayaṇē, ēttō bhayavaṁ dhammaka kahai ॥ 249 ॥
kahaṁ viya ?
1
jōṇīlakkhāṇi ya paribhamittu laḍhūṇa kavi maṇuyattaṁ । jē nāyaraṁti dhammaṁ nariṁda ! tē appaṇō ahiyā ॥ 242 ॥
jēṇaṁ karayalaparikaliyasalilabiṁduva galai aṇusamayaṁ । jīyaṁ, jarāirōgā dēhaṁ dūti taha nica ॥ 243॥
udyānavanē śrūyatē samavasr̥taḥ śrīsupārśvatīrthakaraḥ । tadvandanārthamēṣa nagarajanō vrajati samagraḥ ॥231॥
tat śrutvā prabhati naranāthō yathā'martya ! vayamapi । tadvandanānimittaṁ vrajiṣyāmaḥ kimanyēna ? ॥232॥
bhaṇitaṁ ca tēna taddarśanamapi kalyāṇakāraṇaṁ dēva ! । kiṁ punargamananamasyana padasēvāpramukhapratipattiḥ ॥ 233 ॥
tasmāt kuruṣva svayaṁ taddarśanēna manujatvasya saphalatvam । ityuktē sacivēna vijayanarēndrastatastvaritam ॥ 234॥
saṁcalitō jinavarapādamūlamatha sa kramēṇa saṁprāptaḥ । pañcavidhābhigamēnōllasitāviralarōmāñcaḥ ||235॥
tridattvā pradakṣiṇāṁ praṇamya ca jinanātham । bhaktibharanirbharāṅga ēvaṁ stōtuṁ samārabdhaḥ ॥ 236 ॥
dēva ! tava caraṇanakhamaṇimayūkhadīpā jayantu, yē ravēḥ । khaṇḍayanti caṇḍimānaṁ mōha timiraharaṇēna bhuvanē ॥ 237॥
prabhō ! bahupracaṇḍapākhaṇḍimaṇḍitē mahītalē jīvānām । tava darśanamapi jāyatē'nantabhavacīrṇa puṇyaiḥ ॥ 238 ॥
adyaiva mama manōvāñchitāni jātānyadya jātō'ham । cirakālatō'pi yad dr̥ṣṭigōcarē nātha ! tvaṁ jātaḥ ॥ 239॥
tasmāladhvidānīṁ śāradasaṁpūrṇa śaśāṅkakiraṇa śiśirayā । apahara nijagirayā jināsmākaṁ bhavagrīṣmasaṁtāpam ॥ 240॥
iti saṁstutyaṁ rājōpatiṣṭhatē sthāpayitvā nijadr̥ṣṭim । jinavaravadanē, itō bhagavāna dharmakathāṁ kathayati ॥241॥
kathamiva ?
yōnilakṣāṇi ca paribhramya labdhvā kathamapi manujatvam । yē nācaranti dharmaṁ narēndra ! ta ātmanō'hitāḥ॥242॥
yēna karatalaparikalitasalilabinduriva galatyanusamayam । jīvitam, jvarādirōgā dēhaṁ dāvayanti tathā nityam ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
aibahukilēsasamuvajjiyāvi cōrāiharaṇakavaḍēhiṁ । lacchī khaṇēṇa nāsai vijjulayācaṁcalā nūṇaṁ || 244॥
piumāimittasukalatta puttasayaṇāiōvi saṁjōgō । khadiṭṭhanaharūvō jalanihikallōlasaṁkāsō || 245॥
visayahaṁ puṇa virasaṁ khaṇaramaṇīyaṁ ca jōvvaṇaṁ nr̥ṇaṁ । kiṁ bahuṇā iha naravara ! mōtuṁ jiṇadēsiyaṁ dhammaṁ ॥
na hu kiṁpi sāsayaṁ iya muṇittu taṁ caiva kuṇasu aviyaṣpaṁ । jēṇa lahumēva sāsayasivasuhaṭhāṇaṁ tumaṁ lahasi ।।
iya sōuṁ saṁviggō dāṇavirayassa niyakumārassa | kāuṁ rajjabhisēyaṁ vijayanariṁdō pamōēṇa || 248 ॥
pavvajjaṁ paḍivajjai mahāvibhūīē jiṇavarasamīvē । ēttō ya dāṇaviraō naranāhō bhāi namiūṇa || 249||
jiṇanāha ! rajjakajjē samujjayāṇaṁ gihē vasaṁtāṇa । jaṁ kiṁpi hu karaṇijjaṁ amhāṇa tamihimāisasu ॥
tō bhai jiṇō sāvayadhammō naranāha ! tumha kāyavvō । sō ya dubālasabhēō tē puṇa bhēyā imē nēyā ||
pāṇihamusāvā adinnamēhuṇapariggahē cēva । disibhōgadaṁḍa samaiyadē sē taha pōsahavibhāgē ।। 252 ।।
ēyassa sabhēyassavi pattēya paṁca paṁca aiyārā । mūlaṁ puṇa sammattaṁ sabhēyaminnassavi imassa || 253॥
tassa ya paṁca aiyārā tā taṁ paḍivajjiūṇa naranāha ! | niraīyāra, sāvayadhammaṁ vīrasahi kuṇasu ॥ 254 ॥
iya sōūṇaṁ pabhaṇai dāṇaviraō jiniṁda! jē kēvi । pālaṁti niraiyāraṁ sammattaṁ jaṁ phalaṁ tāṇaṁ ॥ 255॥
jē puṇa sāīyāraṁ kēvi hu pālaṁti jaṁ ca tāṇa phalaṁ । taha bārasabhēyaṁpi hu sāvayadhammaṁ niraiyāraṁ ।। 256॥
jē āyaraṁti kēvi hu tāṇa phalaṁ, jē ya sāiyāraṁ tu । pālaṁti tāṇa ya phalaṁ savittharaṁ sōḍamicchāmi ॥
hu
।
atiba huklēśasamupārjitāpi caurādiharaṇakapaṭaiḥ । lakṣmī: kṣaṇēna naśyati vidyullatācañcalā nūnam ॥244 ॥
pitr̥mātr̥mittra suklatraputrasvajanādikō'pi saṁyōgaḥ । kṣaṇadr̥ṣṭanaṣṭarūpō jalanidhikallōlasaṁkāśaḥ ॥ 245॥
viṣayasukhaṁ punarvirasaṁ kṣaṇaramaṇīyaṁ ca yauvanaṁ nūnam । kiṁ bahunēha naravara ! muktvā jinadēśitaṁ dharmam ॥ 246॥
• na khalu kimapi śāśvatamiti jñātvā tadēva kuruṣvā vikalpam । yēna laghvēva śāśvataśivasukhasthānaṁ tvaṁ labhasē ॥
iti śrutvā saṁvignō dānaviratasya nijakumārasya । kr̥tvā rājyābhiṣēkaṁ vijayanarēndraḥ pramōdēna || 248 ।।
pravrajyāṁ pratipadyatē mahāvibhūtyā jinavarasamīpē । itaśca dānaviratō naranāthō bhaṇati natvā || 249॥
jinanātha ! rājyakāryē samudyatānāṁ gr̥hē vasatām । yat kimapi hi karaṇīyamasmākaṁ tadidānīmādiśa ॥ 250 ॥
tatō bhaṇati jinaḥ śrāvakadharmō naranātha ! tvayā kartavyaḥ । sa ca dvādaśabhēdastē punarbhēdā imē jñēyāḥ ॥251॥
prāṇivadhamr̥ṣāvādāva dattamaithunaparigrahāścaiva । digbhōga - daṇḍa- sāmāyika - dēśāstathā pauṣadha - vibhāgau ॥ 252 ॥
ētasya sabhēdasyāpi pratyēkaṁ pañca pañcāticārāḥ । mūlaṁ punaḥ samyaktvaṁ sabhēdabhinnasyāpyasya || 253॥
tasya ca pañcāticārāstasmāt tatpratipadya naranātha ! | niratīcāraṁ śrāvakadharmaṁ dvādaśavidhaṁ kuruṣva ॥ 254॥
iti śrutvā prabhaṇati dānaviratō jinēndra ! yē kēspi । pālayanti niraticāraṁ samyakttatvaṁ yat phalaṁ tēṣām ॥255॥
punaḥ sātīcāraṁ kē'pi khalu pālayanti yacca tēṣāṁ phalam । tathā dvādaśabhēdamapi khalu śrāvakadharmaṁ niraticāram
ya ācarantikē'pi khalu tēṣāṁ phalaṁ, yē ca sāticāraṁ tu । pālayanti tēṣāṁ ca phalaṁ savistaraṁ śrōtumicchāmi ॥

tā pasiūṇaṁ sāhasu sōyāharaṇaṁ jiṇiṁda ! jaṁ jāṇaṁ । jāyaṁ phalaṁti, ēttō bhayavaṁpi hu kahiumārō ||

1
sammatta thiracittā sattā jē patrayaṇa pabhāviti । caṁpayamālavva lahaṁti tē sivaṁ tabbhavēṇēva ॥ 1 ॥
tāhi;
jīvē dīvē bhārahavāsa majjhayārammi | asthi nayarī visālā tihāvi nāmēṇa ya visālā ||2||
jatthuvasaggō gurulāghavaṁ ca guṇavāhiyā ya taha buḍḍhī । vannanivāyaviyārā vāgaraṇē na uṇa lōyasmi ॥3॥
tatyatthi asthimaṇavaṁchiyatthasaṁpāḍa ṇikkadullaliō । laliyaṁgautti rāyā rāyā jaṇakumuyasaṁḍassa || 4 |
nijjiyavipakkhalakkhō kamaladalakkhō kalāsu nirudakkhō । jiṇadhammabaddhalakkhō jō niśca vihiyahiyarakkhō
tassatthi piyā bhajjā vimalajjā susīlakayacōjjā | saddhammammi susajjā pīimaī nāma niravajjā |
tāṇaṁ ca parōppara pīinivbharaṁ visayasōkkhanirayāṇaṁ । paṁcasuyāṇaṁ uvariṁ jāyā dhūyā pavararūvā ||7||
girikaṁdaraṁtaragayā dēhōvacaraṇa guṇakalāvēṇa । caṁpayalayavtra vaḍḍhai caṁpayamālatti kayanāmā ॥ 8 ॥
aha jōggattaṁ pattā ajjhāvaya kumuyacaṁdapāsammi । lakkhaṇasāhittapamāṇajōisāīṇi sā paḍhai ||9||
sāmaṁtamaṁtibhaḍasaṁkaḍammi aha annayā nariṁdassa । atthāṇammi paviṭṭō paḍihāranirūvisarūvō ॥10॥
rāyāhirāyaarikēsarissa pahuṇō kuṇālanayarīē । nāgēṇaṁ amaragurū rāyaguruttaṇaguṇagdhaviō ॥11॥
abbhuṭṭhiūṇa rannā sāyaramavagūhiuṁ uciyaṭhāṇē । uvavēsiūṇa puṭṭhō arikēsarinivaiṇō kusalaṁ ||12||
tammiya khaṇammi vālā caṁpayamālā sahīhiṁ pariyariyā । niyaajjhāvayajuttā saṁpattā rāyapāsamma || 13 ||
I
samyaktvē sthiracittāḥ sattvā yē pravacanaṁ prabhāvayanti । campakamālēva labhantē tē śivaṁ tadbhavēnaiva ॥ 1 ॥
tathāhi ;-
jambūdvīpē dvīpē bhāratavarṣasya madhyē । asti nagarī viśālā tridhāpi nāmnā ca viśālā ॥2॥
yatrōpasargē gurulāghavaṁ ca guṇabādhitā ca tathā vr̥ddhiḥ । varṇanipātavikārā vyākaraṇē na punarlōkē ॥3॥
tatrāstyarthimanōvāñchitārthasaṁpādanaikadurlalitaḥ । lalitāṅgaka iti rājā rājā janakumudaṇḍasya ॥ 4 ॥
nirjitavipakṣalakṣaḥ kamaladalākṣaḥ kalāsu niścitadakṣaḥ | jinadharmabaddhalakṣyō yō nityaṁ vihitahitarakṣaḥ ||5||
tasyāsti priyā bhāryā nirupamalajjā suśīlakr̥tāścaryā । saddharmē susajjā prītimatī nāma niravadyā ॥ 6 ॥
tayōśca parasparaprītinirbharaṁ viṣayasaukhyaniratayōḥ । pañcasutānāmupari jātā duhitā pravararūpā ॥7॥
girikandarāntargatā dēhōpacayēna guṇakalāpēna । campakalatēva vardhatē campakamālēti kr̥tanāmā ॥8॥
atha yōgyatāṁ prāptā'dhyāpakakumudacandrapārśvē । lakṣaṇasāhityapramāṇa jyautiṣādīni sā paṭhati ॥9॥
sāmantamantribhaṭa saṁkaṭē'thānyadā narēndrasya । āsthānē praviṣṭaḥ pratihāranirūpitasvarūpaḥ ॥ 10 ॥
rājādhirājārikēsariṇaḥ prabhōḥ kuṇālānagaryāḥ । nāmnā'maragurū rājagurutvaguṇaparipūrṇaḥ ॥ 11 ॥
abhyutthāya rājñā sādaramavaguhyō citasthānē । upavēśya pr̥ṣṭō'rikēsarinr̥patēḥ kuśalam ॥12॥
tasmiṁśca kṣaṇē bālā campakamālā sakhībhiḥ parikaritā | nijādhyāpakayuktā saṁprāptā rājapārśvē ॥ 13 ॥
1 vistīrṇa, viśiṣṭa: śālaḥ prākārō yasyām, viśiṣṭāḥ śālā: = drumāśca yasyāṁ mā vidhā viśālētyarthaḥ ।

supāsanāha cariasmi -
pāyavaḍiyā niṣēṇa ucchaṁgē ṭhāviūṇa sāpuṭṭhā । kiṁ paḍhiyaṁ putti ! taē kahēhi mūlāō ārambha ? ॥ 14 ॥
sā kiṁpi jā na jaṁpai tā bhaṇiyaṁ kumuyacaṁda vibuhēga । apaḍhiyamavi muṇai imā naravara ! bahusatthaparamatthaṁ ॥
taṁ sōuṁ amaragurū arikēsariṇō mahānariṁdassa । jai gihiṇī havai imā tō laṭhṭhē iya 'vicitē ॥ 16 ॥
pucchai kiṁ tuha vacchē cūḍāmaṇisatthaāgamō asthi ? । sā bhāi atthi kiṁcivi, jai asthi kam̐hē ha tā ēyaṁ ॥
hōhī kō tujjha paī kayā ya kaha vaṭṭihī ya saha tumaē । saṁtasaṁpattīē kai puttā kai va puttīō ? ॥ 18 ॥
lajjāē jā na jaṁpai taṁ para paccuttaraṁ, taō bhaṇiyā । ujjhāēṇa kahijjau mā vijjāhīlaṇaṁ hōhī ॥ 19 ॥
tō paricitiya jaṁpai mauyaṁ mahurakkharēhiṁ sā bālā । arikēsarinaranāhō varisaṁtē maha paī hōhī ||20||
bāraha varisē rattō chammāsē viraciūṇa raccēhī । suyajuyalaṁ ēkkā kannagā u taha saṁtaī hōhī ||21||
iya tuha
i kahiyē tu puḍhaṁ iṇmipuṭuṁpi kiṁpi sāhēmi । tuha puttō pattō paralōyagaīya dasamadiṇē ||22||
are far taṇī carimē jāmammi paṇaiṇī tumha । puttarayaṇaṁ pasūyā varalaṁchaṇalaṁchiyasarīraṁ ||23 ॥
aha sō visāyasaṁtōsaparavasō pucchara naridayaṁ । kō hēū saṁjāō paralōyagamē maha suyassa ! ||24||
tō savisēsaṁ paribhāviūṇa cūḍāmaṇīē paramatthaṁ । sammaṁ nāuṁ sāhai jahaṭṭhiyaṁ vaiyaraṁ ēvaṁ ||25||
taṁ patthiō si jayā rāyāēsēṇa tāyamuddisiṁu । tajhyā kila tuha puttō tara samaṁ āsi saṁcaliō ॥ 26॥
thakkō tara vimukō samuvvahatō maṇammi avamāṇaṁ । suhapaṁsukīliēhiṁ kīlatō saha vayaṁsēhi ||27||
pādapatitā nr̥pēṇōtsaṅgē sthāpayitvā sā pr̥ṣṭā । kiṁ paṭhitaṁ putri ! tvayā kathaya mūlādāramya ? ॥ 14 ॥
sā kimapi yāvanna jalpati tāvadbhaṇitaṁ kumudacandravibudhēna । apaṭhitamapi jānātiīyaṁ naravara ! bahuśāstraparamārtham | 15|
tat śrutvā'maragururarikēsariṇō mahānarēndrasya । yadi gr̥hiṇī bhavēdiyaṁ tataḥ sundaramiti vicintya ॥ 16 ॥
pr̥cchati kiṁ tava vatsē ! cūḍāmaṇiśāstrāgamō'sti ? | sā bhaṇatyasti kiñcidapi, yadyasti kathaya tata ētat ॥
bhaviṣyati kastava patiḥ kadā ca kathaṁ vartsyati ca saha tvayā । saṁtatisaṁpattau kati putrāḥ kati vā putryaḥ 1 । 18 ।
lajjayā yāvanna jalpati taṁ prati pratyuttaraṁ, tatō bhaṇitā । upādhyāyēna kathyatāṁ mā vidyāhēlanaṁ bhūt ॥ 19 ॥
tataḥ paricintya jalpati mr̥dukaṁ madhurākṣaraiḥ sā bālā । arikēsarinaranāthō varṣāntē mama patirbhaviṣyati ॥20॥
dvādaśa varṣāṇi raktō ṣaṇmāsān virajya rakṣyati । sutayugalamēkā kanyakā tu tathā saṁtatirbhaviṣyati ॥21॥
iti kathitaṁ tava pr̥ṣṭamidānīmapr̥ṣṭamapi kimapi kathayāmi । tava putraḥ saṁprāptaḥ paralōkagatau daśamadinē ॥22॥
tasyāmēva rajanyāṁ caramē yāmē praṇayinī tava । putraratnaṁ prasūtā varalāñchanalāñchitaśarīram ॥23॥
atha sa viṣādasaṁtōṣaparavaśaḥ pr̥cchati narēndrasutām । kō hētuḥ saṁjātaḥ paralōkagamē mama sutasya ? ॥24॥
tataḥ saviśēṣaṁ paribhāvya cūḍāmaṇēḥ paramārtham । samyag jñātvā kathayati yathāsthitaṁ vyatikaramēvam ||29||
tvaṁ prasthitō'si yadā rājādēśēna tātamuddiśya । tadā kila tava putrastvayā samamāsīt saṁcalitaḥ ॥ 26 ॥
avasarē tvayā vimuktaḥ samudvahan manasyapamānam । sukhapāṁśukrīḍitaiḥ krīḍan saha vayasyaiḥ ॥27॥

caṁpayamālākahā ।
105
aha annayā kayāī ujjāṇamahūsavammi gamaṇatthaṁ । tuhapuṣvapurisakhaggaṁ karē karēūṇa jā caliō ॥ 28 ॥
tō jaṇaṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ pūijjai cēva khaggarayaṇamiṇaṁ । na hu cālijjai tāvaccha ! gaccha ēvaṁ trimōttūṇa ॥ 29 ॥
avamāṇayamappāṇaṁ mannatō sōvi puvvakammavasā । rayaṇīē pasuttāē sapariyaṇāēva jaṇaṇīē ॥30॥
saṇiyaṁ saṇiyaṁ sayaṇīyayāu gaṁtūṇa uvavaṇassaṁtō । vāvīē nivaḍiō vihaḍiō ya sē pāṇasaṁbaṁdhō ||
sanvattha gaviṭṭhō sō alahaṁtēṇaṁ pauttimittaṁpi । jaṇaṇīpamuhajaṇēṇa tō tuha pāsammi dhāvaṇaō ॥ 32॥
saṁpēsiō kuraṁgō ēhī sō saṁpayammi ētthēva । takkhaṇamaha paḍihārēṇa mūiō sōvi saṁpattō ||33||
naranāhaṁ amaraguruṁ ca namiya taṁ taha kahēi sō savvaṁ । jaha kumarīē bhaṇiyaṁ amaragurū aha papē || 34 ॥
annāṇatimiraharaṇī aladdhakaraṇīya jayattayavahūhiṁ । tumha gihē avainnā pañcakkhasara saī ēsā ||35||
iya sēsēvi saṁsārasiē atthāṇasaṁṭhiē lōē । āpucchiūṇa jaṇayaṁ samuṭṭiyā jāva kira kumarī ॥ 36 ॥
tā aṁgavilaggaṁ naravarēṇa anēṇa tayaṇu lōēṇa । dinnamasēsāharaṇaṁ, rannā taha kumuyacaṁdassa ||37|
dinaṁ suvaṇṇalakkhassa sāsaṇaṁ nāsaṇaṁ daridassa । caṁpayamālāṇugaō gaō taō sōvi niyaṭhāṇaṁ ॥ 38॥
naranāhō amaraṁ guruṁ para jaṁpara tumha saṁpai kuṇālaṁ । gaṁtuṁ juttaṁ turiyaṁ niyapariyaṇāvaṇāē ||39||
tā saṁkhēvēṇa ciya kahēhi rāyāhirāyaāēsaṁ । tō jaṁpai amaragurū tumha gaḍhō atthi sīmāē ॥ 40॥
sō ahaṁ ciya dijjau lijjau atthēṇa saha gaḍhō uciō । iya āēsō rāyāhivassa, tō jaṁpaē rāyā ॥
athānyadā kadācidudyānamahōtsavē gamanārtham । tvatpūrvapuruṣakhaṅgaṁ karē kr̥tvā yāvaccalitaḥ ||28||
tatō jananyā bhaṇitaṁ pūjyata ēva khaḍgaratnamidam । na ca cālyatē tasmād vatsa ! gacchainaṁ vimucya || 29॥
avamānitamātmānaṁ manyamānaḥ sō'pi pūrvakarmavaśāt । rajanyāṁ prasuptāyāṁ saparijanāyāmapi jananyām ॥30॥
śanaiḥ śanaiḥ śayanīyād gatvōpavanasyāntaḥ । vāpyāṁ nipatitō vighaṭitaśca tasya prāṇasaṁbandhaḥ ||31||
sarvatra gavēṣitaḥ sō'labhamānēna pravr̥ttimātramapi । jananīpramukhajanēna tatastava pārśvē dhāvanakaḥ ॥ 32॥
saṁprēṣitaḥ kuraṅga ēṣyati sa sāṁpratamatraiva । tatkṣagamatha pratihārēṇa sūcitaḥ sō'pi saṁprāptaḥ ||33||
naranāthamamaraguruṁ ca natvā tat tathā kathayati sa sarvam । yathā kumāryā bhaṇitamamaragururatha prajalpati ॥34॥
ajñānatimiraharaṇī alabdharūpā ca jagattrayavadhūbhiḥ । yuṣmākaṁ gr̥hē'vatīrṇā pratyakṣasarasvatyēṣā ॥ 35॥
iti śēṣē'pi praśaṁsārasikē āsthānasaṁsthitē lōkē । āpr̥cchaya janakaṁ samutthitā yāvatkila kumārī ||36||
tāvadaṅgavilagnaṁ naravarēṇānyēna tadanu lōkēna । dattamaśēṣābharaṇaṁ rājñā tathā kumudacandrīya || 37॥
dattaṁ suvarṇalakṣasya śāsanaṁ nāśanaṁ dāridryasya । campakamālānugatō gatastataḥ sō'pi nijasthānam ॥ 38॥
naranāthō'maraguruṁ prati jalpati tava saṁprati kuṇālām । gantuṁ yuktaṁ tvaritaṁ nijaparijanasthāpanārtham ||39|
tataḥ saṁkṣēpēṇaiva kathaya rājādhirājādēśam । tatō jalpatyamaraguruyuṣmākaṁ durgō'sti sīni ॥40॥
sō'smabhyaṁ dīyatāṁ lāyatāmarthēna saha durga ucitaḥ । ityādēśō rājādhipasya, tatō jalpati rājā ॥41॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
arikēsarinaravaṇō rajjamiṇaṁ kiṁ gaḍhēṇa ēkkēṇa ? | tō amaragurū jaṁpai suyaṇatē tujjha kō tullō ? ॥ 42 ॥
appāviṁḍa gaḍhaṁ sō rannā saṁmāṇiō bahupayāraṁ । niyanayari saṁcaliō citai vimhayavasaṁ pattō ॥ 43 ॥
bālāē avalāē sārayavāliṁdunimmalakalāē । kalikālakaluttinnāē tinni accanbhuyāṁī sē ॥ 44 ॥
tathāhi ;-
iha dēsakālavavahiyabāyarasuhumatthapayaḍaṇaṁ nāṇaṁ । rūvaṁ avayavasamudayasōhaṁ muṇimaṇaviṇōyakhamaṁ ॥ 45 ॥ .
itthiyaṇatucchayāvisayasatyaavahēlaō phuḍaṁ viṇaō । abbhāsāō kammammi kōsalaṁ taṁ imaṁ vihiṇō ||
saṁpattō ya kuṇālā pahuṇō arikēsarissa pāsammi । laliyaṁgarāyapēsiyamuvaṇīyamuvāyaṇaṁ tattō ॥ 47॥
uciyapaḍivattipuvvaṁ uvavisiuṁ kahai tumha āēsō । laliyaṁgaēṇa rannā sīsēṇa paḍicchiō ēvaṁ ॥ 48 ॥
aha jahavat sāhai jaṁpēi avaccatraṁ ca sō cēva । jēṇa pasūyā bhuvaṇikkabhūsaṇaṁ ērisā kannā ॥ 49 ॥
tathāhi; -
rūvēṇa raī varaī gaurī gaṁgāvi jīē na hu caṁgā । sōhaggēṇa sabhā raṁbhāvi hu taṁ niyaṁtāṇaṁ ॥ 50 ॥
sayalakalākusalattaṁ tīē pāēṇa, kiṁtu naranāha ! | cūḍāmaṇīi sō kōci pagarisō jō na annassa ॥51॥
kaha jāṇaha iya bhaṇiē savittharō puttamaraṇavr̥ttatō । tīē jaha parikahiō taha kahiō tēṇa niyaranō ।
kiṁ bahuṇā aṇurūvō saṁjōō jāyaē jayappavarō । jai tumhāṇaṁ karaphaṁsasuhalaṁbhaṁ lahai sā bālā ॥53॥
ēvaṁ nisutēṇaṁ naravaiṇā vammahō tahagghaviō । jaha garimīrimāhiṁ cattō īsāiva khaṇēṇa || 54 ||
tō pabhaṇai amaraguruṁ buddhīē amara gurusamassāvi । jāō tujjha pamāō jaṁsā na hu maggiyā taiyā । । 55 ।
arikēsarinarapatē rājyamidaṁ kiṁ durgēṇaikēna ? । tatō'maragururjalpati sujanatvē tava kastulyaḥ 1 ॥42॥
arpayitvā durga sa rājñā saṁmānitō bahuprakāram । nijanagarī saṁcalitaścintayati vismayavaśaṁ prāptaḥ || 423॥
bālāyā abalāyāḥ śāradabālēndunirmala kalāyāḥ । kalikālakalōttīrṇāyāstrīṇyatyadbhutāni tasyāḥ ॥44॥
iha dēśakālavyavahitavādara sūkṣmārthaprakaṭanaṁ jñānam । rūpamavayavasamudayaśōbhaṁ munimanōvinōdakṣamam ||45॥
strījanatucchatāviṣayaśāstrāvahēlakaḥ sphuṭaṁ vinayaḥ । abhyāsāt karmaṇi kauśalaṁ tadidaṁ vidhēḥ ॥ 46 ॥
saṁprāptaśca kuṇālāprabhōrarikēsariṇaḥ pārśvē । lalitāṅgarājaprēṣitamupanītamupāyanaṁ tataḥ ॥ 47 ॥
ucitapratipattipūrvamupaviśya kathayati yuṣmākamādēśaḥ । lalitāṅgakēna rājñā śīrṣēṇa pratīṣṭa ēvam ॥48॥
atha yathāvr̥ttaṁ kathayati jalpatyapatyavāṁśca sa ēva । yēna prasūtā bhuvanakabhūṣaṇamīdr̥śī kanyā ॥ 49 ॥
rūpēṇa ratirvarākī gaurī gaṅgāpi yasyā na hi caṅgā । saubhāgyēna sadambhā rambhāpi khalu tāṁ paśyatām ॥50॥
sakalakalākuśalatvaṁ tasyāḥ prāyēṇa, kintu naranātha ! । cūḍāmaṇau sa kō'pi prakarṣō yō nānyasya ॥51॥
kathaṁ jānīthēti bhaṇitē savistaraḥ putramaraṇavr̥ttāntaḥ । tayā yathā parikathitastathā kathitastēna nijarājasya ॥ 52 ॥
kiṁ bahunāsnurūpaḥ saṁyōgō jāyēta jagatpravaraḥ । yadi yuṣmākaṁ karasparśasukhalābhaṁ labhatē sā bālā || 13 ||
ēvaṁ śr̥ṇvatā narapatinā manmathastathā pūrṇaḥ । yathā marimadhīrimabhyāṁ tyakta īṣyēyēva kṣaṇēna ||24||

payamālā kahā |
107
taṁ jai kannārayaṇaṁ saṁpāḍai naravarōsa annassa । rayaṇanihiṁ daṁsiya ukkhayāṇi tā amha nayaṇāṇi ॥56॥
tō jaṁpai amaragurū hōina annassa sā nariṁda ! jaō । varisassaṁtē taṁ ciya tīē varō apaṇō kahiō ।। 57॥
bhai nivō tahavi raī na diti ēyāī majjha nayaṇāīṁ । tadaṁsaṇapīūsāsāyaṇaailaṁpaḍattēṇa || 58 ||
tā patthaṇāmisēṇaṁ tīē taṁ gaccha tattha sigdhaṁpi । vēsaṁtaraṁ karēḍaṁ tumhaṁ thaiyādharō hōuṁ ॥ 59 ॥
ahamavi saha tubbhēhiṁ alakkhiō ēmi tō tahā vihiē । saṁpatthiō visālaṁ amaragurū pavaravalakaliō ॥60॥
sīhaduvārammi ṭhiō paḍihāranivēiō nivasahāē । saṁpattō naravaiṇā nēhēṇavagr̥hiō vāḍhaṁ ॥ 61 ॥
uciyāsaṇē nivēsiya puṭṭhō arikēsarissa taṇukusalaṁ । laliyaṁgaēṇa rannā taha sigyāgamaṇahēḍaṁ ca ॥ 62॥
tō pabhaṇai amaragurū majjha sayāsāu rāyaputtīē । sōuṁ guṇasāmaggiṁ appāṇaṁ tavvara tēṇaṁ ॥ 63 ॥
varisaṁtē•vinnāuṁ aiūsuyamāṇasō nivō jāō । diṭṭimapattāē imāē nūṇa pāṇē paricaya || 64 ||
tā ēvaṁ vahṷ̄tē jaṁ jujjai kiṁpi kuṇaha taṁ tubbhē । kahiumimaṁ tuha suhiṇō vasaṇaṁ parinivyā amhē || 65 ॥
ēvaṁ ciya japatāṇa tāṇa sahasā samāgayā bālā । piupāyavaṁdaṇatthaṁ juttā samavayavayaṁsīhi ||66 ||
niyaaṁkaśmi nivēsiya vr̥ttā puhaīsarēṇa sā bālā । vacchē ! ēsō viusō samāgaō kassa kajjēṇa ? ||67 ||
sā pabhaṇai thaiyāvāhayassa ēyassa cēva, tō rāyā । vimhaiyamaṇō ciṁtai jujjai ēyaṁ jamē ēṇa ॥ 68 ॥
maha nāmiyaṁ na sīsaṁ uvaviṭṭhō āsaṇēvi na hu nīē । muttīvi kahai ēyassa niyamaō rāyarāyattaṁ ॥ 69 ॥
tataḥ prabhaṇatyamaraguruṁ buddhyā'maragurusamasyāpi । jātastava pramādō yat sā na khalu mārgitā tadā ॥ 55॥
tadyadi kanyāratnaṁ saṁpādayati naravaraḥ sō'nyasmai । ratnanidhiṁ darśayitvōtkhātāni tatō'smākaṁ nayanāni ॥ 56 ॥
tatō jalpatyamaragururbhavati nānyasya sā narēndra ! yataḥ । varṣasyāntē samēva tayā vara ātmanaḥ kathitaḥ ॥ 57 ॥
bhaṇati nr̥pastathāpi ratiṁ na datta ētē mama nayanē । taddarśanapīyūṣāsvādanātilampaṭatvēna ॥58॥
tasmāt prārthanāmiṣēṇa tasyāstvaṁ gaccha tatra śīghramapi । vēṣāntaraṁ kr̥tvā tava sthagikāgharō bhūtvā ॥59॥
ahamapi saha yuṣmābhiralakṣita ēmi tatastathā vihitē । saṁprasthitō viśālāmamaraguruḥ pravarabalakalitaḥ ॥60॥
siṁhadvārē sthitaḥ pratīhāranivēditō nr̥pasabhāyām । saṁprāptō narapatinā snēhēnāvagūḍhō bāḍham ॥ 61॥
ucitāsanē nivēśya pr̥ṣṭō'rikēsariṇastanukuśalam । lalitāṅgakēna rājñā tathā śīghrāgamanahētuṁ ca ॥ 62 ॥
tataḥ prabhaṇatyamaragururmama sakāśād rājaputryāḥ । śrutvā guṇasāmagrīmātmānaṁ tadvaratvēna ॥63॥
varṣāntē vijñāyātyutsukamānasō nr̥pō jātaḥ । dr̥ṣṭimaprāptāyāmasyāṁ nūnaṁ prāṇān parityajēt ॥64॥
tasmādēvaṁ vartamānē yad yujyatē kimapi kurutha tad yūyam । kathayit vēdaṁ tava suhr̥dō vyasanaṁ parinirvr̥tā vayam ॥ 65 ॥
ēvamēva jalpatāstayōḥ sahasā samāgatā bālā । pitr̥pādavandanārthaṁ yuktā samavayōvayasyābhiḥ ||66 ॥
nijāṅkē nivēśayōktā pr̥thivīśvarēṇa sā bālā । vatsa ! ēṣa vidvān samāgataḥ kasya kāryēṇa ? ||67॥
sā prabhaṇati sthagikāvāhakasyaitasyaiva tatō rājā । vismitamanāścintayati yujyata ētad yadētēna ॥68॥
mahyaṁ namitaṁ na śvarṣimupaviṣṭa āsanē'pi na hi nīcē । mūrtirapi kathayatyētasya niyamatō rājarājatvam ||69 ॥

supāsanāha cariamma-
tō uṭṭhaūṇa sīhāsaṇammi taṁ ṭhāviuṁ paṇasiuṁ ca । avarāsaṇē niviṭṭō caṁpayamāṁlaṁ paryapēī || 70 ॥
naravarapāṇiggahaṇē varisavilaṁbammi tujjha kō hēū ? । niyapāyaguhaṁ para nivēsa sā taō diṭṭhi || 71 ||
jaṁpara na kiṁpi jā tāva naravarō saddiūṇa jōisiyaṁ । bhagai kumarīē pāṇiggahaṇē laggaṁ nivēha ॥ 72 ॥
bhaṇai huṁti na imammi vaccharē sōhaṇāī lamgāī । jaṁ bhāṇukhittasaṁṭhiyajīvēṇaṁ dūsigaṁ ēvaṁ || 73 ||
yata uktam ;
""
"
gurukṣētragatē bhānau bhānukṣētragatē gurau । vivāhādi na kurvīta vāñchan śubhaparamparām ॥
tērasamāsē ahiē gurusta ēkkammi hōi rāsimmi । jaṁ bhuttī tō varisē gayammi vaisāhamāsassa ॥ 74 ॥
uttaraphagguṇapāra paḍhamē ēkārasīē suddhāē । mukkē harisaṇajōgē ravirikkhā dasamarikkhammi ॥75॥
udayāō gaē ghaḍiyāpaṇagē ghaḍiyātibhāgaūṇammiṁ । visalaggē vavuttamaasē udaya iddhijayaṁ । 76 ॥
paṁcaggahabalajuttaṁ ravisukēsucaṭhāṇavattēsu । lāyāidōsamukaṁ naravara ! aisōhaṇaṁ laggaṁ ॥77॥
tattō ya taṁ lihāviya apāvēḍaṁ purōhiyassa taō । saṁmāṇiuṁ visajjai jōisiyaṁ mēiṇīnāhō || 78 |
nēūṇa rāyarāyaṁ majjagasālāē aṁgamadēhiṁ । tō lakkhapāgatillēṇa abhaṁgāvēi majjēi ||79 ||
kārēi samālihaṇaṁ parihāvai taha ya varadugūlāī । dēvālayasmi nēuṁ appēi ya pupphagaṁdhāī ॥ 80 ॥
sōvi vavahāraucciya pūyai paṇamai taō saparivāraṁ । nēuṁ bhōgaṇasālāē bhōiuṁ vaha palaṁkē ॥ 81 ॥
bhai ya tapacakhaṁ gōttīmukkhaṁ jahā iha jaṇassa । punnēhiṁ ihāgamaṇaṁ ēvaṁvipurisarayaṇassa || 82 ॥
tata utthāya siṁhāsanē taṁ sthāpayitvā praṇamya ca । aparāsanē niviṣṭaścampakamālāṁ prajalpati ॥ 70 ॥
naravarapāṇigrahaṇē varṣavilambē tava kō hētuḥ ? । nijapādāṅguṣṭhaṁ prati nivēśayati sā tatō dr̥ṣṭim ॥ 71 ॥
jalpati na kimapi yāvattāvannaravara : śabdayitvā jyautipikam । bhaṇati kumāryāḥ pāṇigrahaṇē lagnaṁ nivēdayata ।
sa bhaṇati bhavanti nāsmin varṣē śōbhanāni lagnāni । yad bhānukṣētrasaṁsthitajīvēna dūṣitamētat ॥ 73 ॥
trayōdaśamāsē'dhikē gurōrēkasmin bhavati rāśau । yadbhaktistatō varṣē gatē vaiśākhamāsasya ||74 ||
uttaraphālgunapādē prathamē ēkādaśyāṁ śuddhāyām । śukrē harṣaṇayōgē ravir̥kṣād daśamarkṣē ||721|
udayād gatē ghaṭikāpañcakē ghaṭikātribhāgōnē । vr̥ṣalagnē bavōttamāṁśa udayādiśuddhiyutam ॥ 76 ॥
pañcagrahanalayuktaṁ raviśukrayōrucca sthānaprāptayōḥ । lātādidōṣamuktaṁ naravara ! atiśōbhanaṁ lagnam ॥77॥
tataśca tallēkhayitvā'rpayitvā purōhitāya tataḥ । saṁmānya visr̥jati jyautiṣikaṁ mēdinīnāthaḥ ||78 ||
nītvā rājarājaṁ majjanaśālāyāmaṅgamadaiḥ । tatō lakṣapākatailēnābhyaṅgayati majjayati ॥ 79 ॥
kārayati samālēpanaṁ paridhāpayati tathā ca varadukūlāni । dēvālayaṁ nītvā'rpayati ca puṣpagandhādi ॥ 80 ॥
sō'pi vyavahārata ēva pūjayati praṇamati tataḥ saparivāram । nītvā bhōjanaśālāyāṁ bhōjayitvā sthāpayati palyaṅkē।।
bhaṇati ca tatpratyakṣaṁ gōtrimukhyaṁ yathā'sya janasya । puṇyairihāgamanamēvaṁvidhapuruṣaratnasya ॥82॥

106.
tā gōttinihittāṇavi saṁpajjau suṁdarā dasā ihi । bhuṁjāvēu pārahāāvauṁ ca muccati tē savvē ॥ 83 ॥
sammāṇiuṁ nariṁdō hayagayaraharayaṇabhūsaṇāīrhi । bhaṇiō suhāsaṇatthō laliyaṁgayapuhainā hēṇa ॥ 84॥
yasu tumha daṁsaṇa amarasāsāyaparavasēsuṁpi । paricita maha hiyayaṁ ēyāṇadvāṇapaṭibaṁdhō ॥ 85 ॥
kavi marutthali haṁsō pattō pāmara gihammi karināhō । na pahuppai tāṇa imaṁ jēṇa ciraṁ tattha vāsaṁti (?) || 86 ॥
tāniyanayarābhimuhaṁ karai payāṇaṁ jayā naravariṁdōṁ । caṁpayamālāvi tathā kannacciya tattha āgamihī ॥87॥
saha majjha amaccēhi, pāṇibhgahaūsavammi kannāē । hōhiṁti tē nimittaṁ, bhaṇai ō naravarāhivaī ।। 88 ।।
uciyannuēsa kālannuē dhīrēsu garuyahiyaēsu । suyaṇadhuraṁdhara ! kō dharai tujjha līhaṁ tihuyaṇēvi ? ॥ 89 ॥
bhāvanē paripēlāṇa niccaṁ rasāyaṇārṇava । tuha viṇayālāvāṇaṁ naravara ! tittiṁ na vaccāmō ॥ 90 ॥
tahavi maṇōrasālā caṁpayamālā na ṭhāi jā puraō । tā siḍhiliyagurukajjaṁtarāṇa iha ṭhāṇamamhāṇa॥ 91 ॥
tō sō caṁpayamālāē saha lahuṁ naravaraṁ visajjēi । kaivayapayāṇayāī aṇugaṁtuṁ valaiṣṇunnāō ॥ 92 ॥
rāyāvi tayaṇu paṁcappāṇacitijjamāṇanivakajjaṁ । niyanayaraṁ saṁpattō kamēṇa ūsiyadhayapaḍāyaṁ ॥93॥
tō caṁpayamālāē pāsāō apiō naridēṇa । jattha ṭhiyā niyāṇadviyassa nayaṇūsa kuṇai || 94 ॥
divasa jāi tarhi, ahannayā naravarēṇa amaragurū । saha nīō sō jaṁvai kalāviyārē bhagaha kiṁpi ।। 95॥
sā bhaṇai vivihapāsaṁḍivihiadhammāṇa tumha kō'bhipaō ? । tō sō bhaṇai kimēvaṁ appatthuyamullavēha tumaṁ ? ॥ 96 ॥
sā jaṁpa kimapatyamiha ki dhammō kalā na tumha mayā । ihalōyapāralōiyasivasuhasaṁpāḍaṇappavarā ? ॥97॥
tasmād gōtrinihitānāmapi saṁpadyatāṁ sundarā daśēdānīm । bhōjayitvā paribhrāpya ca mucyantē tē sarvai ॥83॥
I
saṁmānya narēndrō hayagajaratharatnabhūṣaṇādibhiḥ । bhaṇitaḥ sukhāsanasthō lalitāṅgakapr̥thivīnāthēna ॥ 84 ॥
nayanayōstava darśanāmr̥tarasāsvādaparavaśayōrapi । paricintayati mama hr̥dayamētēṣāṁ sthānapratibandham ॥8॥
kathamapi marusthalē haṁsaḥ prāptaḥ pāmaragr̥hē karināthaḥ । na prabhavati tayōridaṁ yēna ciraṁ tatra vāsayati ॥ 86 ॥
tasmād nijanagarābhimukhaṁ karōti prayāṇaṁ yadā naravarēndraḥ । campakamālāpi tadā kanyaiva taṁtrāgamiṣyati ॥87॥
saha mamāmātyaiḥ, pāṇigrahōtsavē kanyāyāḥ । bhaviṣyanti tē nimittaṁ, bhaṇati tatō naravarādhipatiḥ ॥ 88 ॥
ucitajñēṣu kālajñēṣu dhīrēṣu guruhr̥dayēṣu । sujanadhurandhara ! kō dharati tava rēkhāṁ tribhuvanē'pi ? ॥89॥
sadbhāva snēhaparipēśalānāṁ nityaṁ rasāyanānāmiva । tava vinayālāpānāṁ naravara ! tr̥ptiṁ na vrajāmaḥ ॥90॥
tathāpi manōrathaśālā campakamālā na tiṣṭhati yāvatpurataḥ । tāvacchithilitagurukāryāntarāṇāmiha sthānamasmākam ॥
tataḥ sa campakamālayā saha laghu naravaraṁ visr̥jati । katipayaprayāṇakānyanugamya valatē'nujñātaḥ ॥92॥
rājāpi tadanu pañcapradhānacintyamānanr̥pakāryam । nijanagaraṁ saṁprāptaḥ kramēṇōcchritadhvajapatākam ॥93॥ -
sa campakamālāyai prāsādō'rpitō narēndrēṇa । yatra sthitā nijasthānasthitasya nayanōtsavaṁ karōti ॥94॥
pratidivasaṁ yāti tatra, athānyadā naravarēṇāmaraguruḥ । saha nītaḥ sa jalpati kalāvicārē bhaṇata kimapi ॥99॥
sā bhaṇati vividhapāskhaṇḍivihitadharmāṇāṁ tava kō'bhimataḥ ? । tataḥ sa bhaṇati kimēvamaprastutamullapatha yūyam ? ||

yataḥ,
supāsanāha cariammi-
I
bāvattarī kalāpaṁḍiyāvi purisā apaṁḍiyā caiva । savvakalā pavaraṁ jē dhammakalaṁ na yāti ॥ 98 ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ ca amaraguruṇā na viyārō ēttha saṁgaō kōvi । jō jassa puvvapurisēhi sēviō tassa sō dhammō ॥
kiñca;
sussīlā dussīlā va hōu jaṇaṇīē ki viyārēṇa । annaṁ vijjuvaēsō ōsahavisaē jaha pamāṇaṁ ॥ 100 ॥
taha niyagurūhi jēsiṁ jō kahiō jannapabhiiō dhammō । sō cciya tēsiṁ pamāṇaṁ kimimīē aṇatthaciṁtāē ? ॥
iya bhaṇijaṁ amaragurū dhammavidhārammi uvaraō jāvaṁ । tāva kalayaṁṭhikaṁṭhā bhagai laṭhṭhē taē bhaṇiyaṁ । । 102 ॥
kiṁtu na ēvaṁ japaṁti paṁḍiyā hōṁti tujjha jē sarisā । paramapurisatthabhūpa dhammē juttō cciya viyārō ॥ 103 ॥
paramattaṁ purisatthēsimassa jaṁ ēsa atthakāmāṇaṁ । payaḍaṁ nibaṁdhaṇaṁ bahujaṇassa bhaṇiyaṁ ca nīīē || 104 ||
" dharmādarthō'rthataḥ kāmaḥ kāmāt sukhaphalōdayaḥ । ātmānaṁ hanti tau hatvā yō yuktayā na niṣēvatē ॥ "
punnassa ya pāvarasa ya jaivi abhāvō bhaṇijjaē mōkkhō । sōvi hu punnappagaī vivāgakējjaṁ tu supasiddhaṁ ॥
jaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ tara buha ! kamāgaō jō ya jēsiṁ kila dhammō । sō ya pamāṇō tēsiṁ ēyaṁpi na saṁgaī lahaṛa ।
puvvapurisakamēṇa jai dāliṁda havēi vāhī vā । tā kiṁ kulajāēhiṁ tāī nō vajjaṇijjāī ? || 107॥
taha jaṇaṇīditō na hu laṭṭhō jēṇa suppasiddhamigaṁ । jagaṇīvi galiyasīlā aparicattā haṇai taṇayaṁ ||
ōsahaditēvi gurūvaēsō pamāṇiō tumaē । rāyōsavittō paramatthaviū ya hōi guru ॥ 109 ॥
॥
sā jalpati kimaprastutamiha kiṁ dharmaḥ kalā na tava matā । aihalōkika pāralōkika śiva sukhasaṁpādanapravarā ? ॥ 97 ॥
dvāsaptatikalāpaṇḍitā api puruṣā apaṇḍitā ēva । sarvakalānāṁ pravarāṁ yē dharmakalāṁ na jānanti ॥98॥
bhaṇitaṁ cāmaraguruṇā na vicārō'tra saṁgataḥ kō'pi । yō yasya pūrvapuruṣaiḥ sēvitastasya sa dharmaḥ ॥99॥
khuśīlā duḥśīlā vā bhavatu jananyāḥ kiṁ vicārēṇa । anyad vaidyōpadēśa auṣadhaviṣayē yathā pramāṇam ||100
tathā nijagurubhiryēṣāṁ yaḥ kathitō yajñaprabhr̥tikō dharmaḥ । sa ēva tēṣāṁ pramāṇaṁ kimanayā'narthacintayā ? ॥ 101 ॥
iti bhaṇitvā'maragururdharmavicāra uparatō yāvat । tāvatkalakaṇṭhīkaṇṭhā bhaṇati sundaraṁ tvayā bhaṇitam ॥ 102॥
kintu naivaṁ jalpanti paṇḍitā bhavanti tava yē sadr̥śāḥ । paramapuruṣārthabhūtē dharmē yukta ēva vicāraḥ ॥ 103 ॥
paramatvaṁ puruṣārthēṣvasya, yadēṣō'rthakāmayōḥ । prakaṭaṁ nibandhanaṁ bahujanasya bhaṇitaṁ ca nītau ॥ 104 ॥
puṇyasya ca pāpasya ca yadyapyabhāvō bhaṇyatē mōkṣaḥ । sō'pi hi puṇyaprakr̥tirvipākakāryē tu suprasiddham ॥105॥
yajjalpitaṁ tvayā budha ! kramāgatō yaśca yēṣāṁ kila dharmaḥ । sa ca pramāṇaṁ tēṣāmētadapi na saṁgatiṁ labhatē ॥ 106॥
pūrvapuruṣakramēṇa yadi dāridryaṁ bhavati vyādhirvā । tataḥ kiṁ kulajātaistau nō varjanīyau ? ॥ 107 ॥
tathā jananīdr̥ṣṭāntō na khalu sundarō yēna suprasiddhamidam । jananyapi galitaśīlā'parityaktā hanti tanayam ॥
auṣadhadr̥ṣṭāntēnāpi gurūpadēśaḥ pramāṇitastvayā । rāgadvēṣaviyuktaḥ paramārthavicca bhavati guruḥ ॥ 109 ॥

sō sayamarihaṁtō tavvayaṇaviū vā ṭiō ya āṇāē । kālē ciya jayaṇāē vahatō maccharavimukō ॥ 110॥
rāgāī feat arahaṁtō annadēvayā na tahā । kimiha pamāṇaṁ iya gurubhaṇiē pabhaṇēi rāyasuyā ॥ 111 ॥
ēyaṁ ittha pamāṇaṁ jaṁ tēsiṁ tēsu tēsu satthēsu । suvvai tahā sarūvaṁ jaha rāgāīṇa uvalaṁbhō ॥192॥
saṁhāra siṭṭhipālaṇa kāraṇabhāvēṇaṁ jaṁ jahā bhaṇiyaṁ । akuṇaṁtāṇa saṁyaṁ ciya akahaṁtāṇaṁ ca lōyāṇaṁ ॥ 113॥
kiñca tatpratikr̥tayō'pi darśayantyanyadēvānāmarhataścāntaram; -
0.66
iha hi ramaṇīśastrākṣālīdharāḥ suramūrttayō, nipuṇasugamān rāgadvēṣabhramān gamayantyalam ।
tava punariyaṁ tyaktāsaṅgā tanuḥ kr̥takr̥tyatāṁ, prasabhamuśatī svāmin ! satyaṁ pravakti tadatyayam ।। "
iccāisujuttīhi sō tīē niruttarō tahā vihiō । jaha arikēsarisahiō jiṇadhammē niccalō jāō ||
tō pabhaṇai amaragurū bhavajalahitarī tumamha saṁpēttā । jaṁ ummaggapayaṭṭā ṭhaviyā jiṇadhammaggami | | 115॥
iya tēṇa kahavi gamiō varisō kaṭṭēṇa jugasamāṇō sō । pattē ya laggasamaē rannā vīdāhiyā vālā ||
tīē samaṁ visayahaṁ paṁcapayāraṁ taō aṇuhavaṁtō | iṁduvva dēvalōē gayaṁpi kālaṁ na yāṇēi ॥ 117 ॥
appāṇaṁ amaragurū ahannayā sumiṇayammi syaṇimuhē । karahārūḍhaṁ piccha gacchaṁtaṁ dāhiṇadisāē | | 118 ||
citai jaṛa saccamiṇaṁ tō maha āukkhaō samāsannō । dhāukkhōhāīhi ya kiṁpuṇa sumiṇāī dīsaṁti ||
iya sō bhai naridaṁ pucchaha dēvi mamāuṇō sēsaṁ । dēvisayāsē nēuṁ taṁ bhaṇai nivō sayaṁ puccha ॥ 120॥
appuṭṭhā sā sāhai savvaṁ sē sumiṇavaiyaraṁ dēvī । bhāi ya tuhadasa māsā sēsō āussa tō sōvi॥ 121 ॥
bhaṇai maha dhammajaṇaṇī ! dhammagurū saṁti saṁpayaṁ kattha ? | jaṁpai dēvī jōyaṇasaē divaḍhē purāṇapurē ॥ 122 ॥
sa svayamarhan tadvacanavidvā sthitaścājñāyām । kāla ēva yatanāyāṁ vartamānō mātsaryavimuktaḥ ॥ 110 ॥
rāgādibhirvimuktō'rhannanyadēvatā na thā । kimiha pramāṇamiti gurubhaṇitē prabhaṇati rājasutā ॥ 111 ॥
ētadatra pramāṇaṁ yat tēṣāṁ tēṣu tēṣu śāstrēṣu । śrūyatē tathā svarūpa yathā rāgādīnāmupalambhaḥ ॥ 112 ॥
saṁhārasr̥ṣṭipālana kāraṇabhāvēna yadyathā bhaṇitam । akurvatāṁ svayamēvākathayatāṁ ca lōkānām ॥ 113 ॥
ityādisuyuktibhiḥ sa tathā niruttarastathā vihitaḥ । yathā'rikēsarisahitō jinadharmē niścalō jātaḥ ॥ 114 ॥
tataḥ prabhaṇatyamaragururbhavajjaladhitarī lamasmākaṁ saṁprāptā । yadunmārgapravr̥ttāḥ sthāpitā jinadharmamārgē ॥ 115 ॥
iti tēna kathamapi gamitō varṣaḥ kaṣṭēna yugasamānaḥ saḥ । prāptē ca lagnasamayē rājñā vivāhitā bālā ॥ 116 ॥
tayā samaṁ viṣayasukhaṁ pañcaprakāraṁ tatō'nubhavan । indra iva dēvalōkē gatamapi kālaṁ na jānāti ॥ 117 ॥
ātmānamamaragururathānyadā svapnē rajanīmukhē । karabhārūḍhaṁ paśyati gacchantaṁ dakṣiṇadiśi ॥ 118 ॥
cintayati yadi satyamidaṁ tatō mamāyuḥ kṣayaḥ samāsannaḥ । dhātukṣōbhādibhiśca kintu svapnā dr̥śyantē ॥ 119॥
iti sa bhaṇati narēndraṁ pr̥cchata dēvīṁ mamāyuṣaḥ śēṣam । dēvīsakāśē nītvā taṁ bhaṇati nr̥paḥ svayaṁ pr̥ccha ॥ 120॥
apr̥ṣṭā sā kathayati sarvaṁ tasya svapnavyatikaraṁ dēvī । bhaṇati ca tava daśa māsāḥ śēṣa āyuṣastataḥ sō'pi ॥

supāsanāha-cariammi-
tō amaragurū jaṁpara rāyaṁ dēvi ca khamaha avaruddhaṁ । jaṁ kiṁpi maē, saṁpai maha saraṇaṁ tāṇa payakamalaṁ ॥
bhaṇai sagaggayavayaṇaṁ naranāhōvi buha ! tujjha avarāhā । tīraṁti kēvi sahiuṁ ikō puṇa dukkaraṁ khamiḍaṁ ||
dahalōyapāralōiyasuhasya saṁpattikāraṇaṁ dēvī । caṁpayamālā dēstarāō jaṁ āṇiyā tuma || 125 ||
saddāviya tassa suyaṁ tassa para ṭhāvara naravariṁdō । sammāṇiūṇa vivihaṁ paṁccakkhaṁ rāyalōyassa || 126 ॥
kārai kārāgāraṁ sunnaṁ ghōsāvaē amāriṁ ca । dāvēi amaraguruṇā dāṇaṁ adhāidīṇāṇaṁ ॥ 127 ॥
sammāṇai sāhammiyavaggaṁ savvaṁpi taha ya kāravai । jiṇamaṁdirēsu maṇanayaṇasuhaya aṭṭāhiyāmahimaṁ ॥ 128 ॥
iya ēvamāi takāladhammakiccaṁ kaṁrāviṁḍa sayalaṁ । dhammāikajjajōgaṁ paraṁ appāviḍaṁ daviṇaṁ ॥ 129॥
aijaviṇavāhaṇāī appāvēuṁ tahēba varasuhaḍē । maggasahāē dāuṁ kāuṁ annaṁpi jaṁ kiñca ॥ 130॥
āpucchiūṇa bahuyāī rajjakajjāī dhammakajjāī । aṇurūvammi ya laggē aṇukūlēsuṁ ca sauṇēsuṁ ॥ 131 ॥
aṇugaṁtūṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ payājayaṁ naravarēṇa amaragurū । pavvajjāgahaṇatthaṁ visajjiō sa vahumāṇēṇa ॥ 132 ॥
maggajiṇabhavaṇamahimāidhammakamyāī agaō caiva । apiyadavvēhiṁ dhammiēhiṁ sayalāī kāritō ॥ 133॥
sirisamayajalahikēvalipayamūlē turiyamava gatr̥̄ṇaṁ । paḍivajjivi pavvajjaṁ sāsayasōkkhaṁ gaō mōkkhaṁ ||
aha rāyapuvvaladuladēvī dūramuvayariḍaṁ । bahuḍakavaḍabhariyā bhaṇiyā pavvāiyā sulasā ॥ 135॥
bhayavai ! kiṁpi kalaṁkaṁ caṁpayamālāē ṭhavasu jēṇa imaṁ । visamīsattaṇasaṁ ki yamahubhōyaṇamitra nivō cayai ||
bhaṇati mama dharmajanani ! dharmaguravaḥ santi sāṁprataṁ kutra ? | jalpati dēvī yōjanaśatē divāḍhyē purāṇapurē ॥ 122 ॥
tatō'maragururjalpati rājānaṁ dēvīṁ ca kṣamadhvamaparāddham । yat kimapi mayā, saṁprati mamaṁ śaraṇaṁ tēṣāṁ pādakamalam ॥
bhaṇati sagadgadavacanaṁ naranāthō'pi budha ! tavāparādhāḥ । śakyantē kē'pi sōḍhumēkaḥ punarduṣkaraḥ kṣamitam ॥ 124 ॥
aihalōkikapāralōkikasukhaśatasaṁpattikāraṇaṁ dēvī । campakamālā dēśāntarāda yadānītā tvayā ॥ 125 ॥
śabdayitvā tasya sutaṁ tasya padē sthāpayati naravarēndraḥ । sammānya vividhaṁ pratyakṣaṁ rājalōkasya ॥ 126॥
kāsyati kārāgāraṁ śūnyaṁ ghōṣayatyamāriṁ ca । dāpayatyamaraguruṇā dānamandhādidīnēbhyaḥ ॥127॥
sammānayati sādharmikavarga sarvamapi tathā ca kārayati । jinamandirēṣu manōnayana sukhadāṣṭā hi kāmahimānam ॥ 128 ॥
ityēvamādi tatkāladharmakr̥tyaṁ kārayitvā sakalam । dharmādikārya yōgyaṁ pracuramarpayitvā praviṇam ॥129॥
atijavivāhanānyarpayitvā tathaiva varasubhaṭān । mārgasahāyān dattvā kr̥tvā'nyadapi yatkr̥tyam ॥130॥
āpr̥cchya bahukāni rājyakāryāṇi dharmakāryāṇi । anurūpē ca lagnē'nukūlēṣu ca śakunēṣu ॥131॥
anugamya prathamaṁ prayāṇakaṁ naravarēṇāmaraguruḥ । pratrajyāgrahaṇārthaṁ visr̥ṣṭaḥ sa bahumānēna ॥132॥
mārgajinabhavanamahimādidharmakarmāṇyagrata ēva । arpitadravyairdhārmikaiḥ sakalāni kārayan ॥ 133 ॥
śrīsamayajaladhikēvalipādamūlē tvaritamēva gatvā । pratipadya pratrajyāṁ śāśvatasaukhyaṁ gatō mōkṣam ॥134॥
atha rājapūrvavallabhadurlabhadēvyā dūramupacarya । bahukūṭakapaṭabhr̥tā bhaṇitā pravājikā mulasā ॥135॥
bhagavati ! kamapi kalaṅkaṁ campakamālāyāṁ sthāpaya yēnēmām । viṣamiśratvaśaṅkitamadhubhōjanamiva nr̥pastyajati ॥ 136 ॥

113
pavtrāiyā paryavai imīē ramaṇīguṇēhiṁ pavarēhiṁ । bahumāṇavayaṁ appā na ṭhāviō naravariṁdassa || 137||
kiṁpuṇa sō mr̥ḍhappā i manna ṭhāviō hamēyāē । jiṇadēsiyamma dhammē paramappayaparamahēmi ॥ 138 ॥
tā tī dhamma sē kayammi rāyāvi citihī ēsā । jaha bhaṇai tahā na kuṇai iya vāyālattamittamiṇaṁ ।
tā tatthēva jaissaṁ vacchē ! pacchā kalaṁkadāṇēvi । tujjha maṇōraharukkhō hōhī saṁpunnaphulaphalō ॥ 140 ॥
iya nicchaya vihē pattā pavvāiyā niyamaḍhīē । dullahadēvīvi tayaṁ paidiṇamuvayarai savisēsaṁ ॥ 141 ॥
tattō paidiyahaṁ sā uvāyasayasaṁkulā vicitē । kō ṇu uvāō jiṇadhammabhaṁsaṇē hōja ēīē ? || 142 ॥
huṁ nāyaṁ jaha ēsā apattaputtā taō pabhāyammi । gaṁtuṁ tīē sayāsē āsīvāēṇa tōsēuṁ ॥ 143 ॥
putta uvāyaṁ sāhēmi tīi pakarēmi rakkhaṇhavaṇāī | ōvāiyamāīyaṁ icchāvāvēmi kālīē || 144||
iya ciṁti pabhāē pattā dēvīē vāsabhavaṇammi । paḍihārīē sā puvvasaṁgayā bhaṇai taṁ ēvaṁ ॥ 145॥
sāhasu maṁ dēvī, sāvihu taṁ kuṇai bhaṇai ēvaṁ ca । kō āēsō tīē jhatti visajjēhi dārāō || 146 ॥
dēvīē iya bhaṇiē paḍihārī vinnavē jaha ēsā । dēvīē daṭṭavyā majjha pasāyaṁ vihēūṇa || 147 |
ēvaṁ hōutti ta bhaṇiē dēvīi, taṁ pavēsēi । uvavidvā āsīsaṁ dāu sā bhai ētē || 148 ||
dēvīē natthi putō puttaviṇāsu vallahāsuṁpi । kālēṇa galai pimmaṁ taha ya aputtāṇa na hu sugaī ॥ 149 ॥
tā kuṇa maha bhaṇiyaṁ giṇha mūliyē rakkhakaṁḍayasamēyaṁ । maṁtapavittaṁ ṇhavaṇāiyaṁ ca kārēha maha hatthā || 150 ॥
taha kālīdēvīē pūyaṁ kāūṇa tappaṇāpucvaṁ । suyavisayaṁ ōvāiyamicchasu tuha jēṇa hōi suō ॥ 151 ॥
pravrājikā prajalpatyanayā ramaṇīguṇaiḥ pravaraiḥ । bahumānapadamātmā na sthāpitō naravarēndrasya ॥ 137 ॥
kintu sa mūḍhātmēti manyatē sthāpitō'hamētayā । jinadēśitē dharmē paramapadaparamahētau ॥ 138 ॥
tasmāttasyā dharmabhraṁśē kr̥tē rājāpi cintayiṣyatyēṣā । yathā bhaṇati tathā na karōtīti vācālatvamātramidam ॥
tasmāttatraiva yatiṣyē vatsē ! paścāt kalaṅkadānēnāpi । tava manōrathavr̥kṣō bhaviṣyati saṁpūrṇaphullaphalaḥ ॥ 140 ॥
iti niśvayaṁ vidhāya prāptā pravājikā nijamaṭhikāyām । durlabhadēvyapi tāṁ pratidinamupacarati saviśēṣam ॥ 141 ॥
tataḥ pratidivasaṁ sōpāyaśatasaṁkulā vicintayati ! kō nūpāyō jinadharmabhraṁśanē bhavēdētasyāḥ 1 ॥ 142 ॥
jñātaṁ yathaiṣā'prāptaputrā tataḥ prabhātē । gatvā tasyāḥ sakāśa āśīrvādēna tōṣayitvā || 143॥
putrēōpāyaṁ kathayāmi tasyā: prakarōmi rakṣāsnapanādi । upayācitādikamēṣayāmi kālyāḥ ॥ 144 ॥
iti cintayitvā prabhātē prāptā dēvyā vāsabhavanē । pratihāryā sā pūrvasaṁgatā bhaṇati tāmēvam ॥ 145 ॥
kathaya māṁ dēvyai, sāpi hi tat karōti bhaṇatyēvaṁ ca । ka ādēśastasyā jhaṭiti visr̥ja dvārāt ॥ 146 ॥
dēvyēti bhaṇitē pratihārī vijñapayati yathaiṣā । dēvyā draṣṭavyā mayi prasādaṁ vidhāya ॥ 147 ॥
ēvaṁ bhavatviti tatō bhaṇitē dēvyā, tāṁ pravēśayati । upaviṣṭā''śiṣaṁ dattvā sā bhaṇatyēkāntē ॥ 148॥
dēvyā nāsti putraḥ putravihīnāsu vallabhāsvapi । kālēna galati prēma tathā cāputrāṇāṁ na hi sugatiḥ ॥ 149 ॥
tasmātkuru mama bhaṇitaṁ gr̥hāṇa mūlikāṁ rakṣākāṇḍakasamētām । mantrapavitrāṁ snapanādikaṁ ca kāraya mama hastēna ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
iyattā sampattē akhōhaṇijjā saīda vidēhiṁ । dēvēhi sā jaṁpara vr̥ttārasi jai jaṇaṁ annaṁ ॥ 152 ॥
jiṇavayaṇabhāviyāṇaṁ avagayaduharūvabhava sarūvāṇaṁ । tumhārisīṇa vayaṇaṁ na kamēi visaṁgha amayapi ।। 153 |
puttavihūṇā siccāi palaviyaṁ jaṁ taē aiviyaḍḍhē ! । itthīrayaṇāṇa huṁti kai suyā jēṇa cakkīṇaṁ ? ।। 154 |
jammaṁtarapattāṇavi puvvabhakanbhatya pēmavasagāṇaṁ । sahasā ullāvā tadabhihāṇagandhā payati ॥ 155 ॥
hōi iha aputtāṇaṁ na ya sugaī, mōhavilasiyamimaṁpi । puttā avabhahēū vaṁbhē dhammō taō sugaī || 156 ॥
putēhi jai saggō hōi taō gaḍḍa suyarī paḍhamaṁ । sāṇī vā sauṇīvā kamaḍhī vā gacchihī sagaṁ ॥ 157 ॥
jai rakkhakaṁḍayāī puttaṁ jaṇayaṁti tō na hu aputtō । jāyai jayammi kōvi hu, jaṇaṁ muhā mā bhamāḍēsu || 158 ।
pi palattaṁ kālī pūyamiccāi, tattha kā kālī । kiṁva suramaṁsagiddhāisāiṇīēvi dēvattaṁ ? ॥ 159 ॥
mōttūṇa jiṇaṁ jiṇamaṭṭhiēya annaṁ ahaṁ na vaṁdāmi । varakarivarampi caḍiuṁ kō khara karakhaṁdhaṁ samāruhai ? । 160 ।
iya ēvaṁ ttīhi vr̥ttī sunivāriyāvi nōḍāi | paḍihārīē bāhāhiṁ dhariya nivvāsiyā tattō ॥ 169 ॥
kōvēṇa dhamamaṁtī sumara sā puvvasāhiyaṁ vijjaṁ । sumariyamittā pattā kiṁ kāyavvaṁti sā bhai || 162 ||
pavvāiyā papaī ēsā niyanāṇagavtriyā pāvā । majjhavi kuṇai avannaṁ tā jīvaṁtī jahā ēsā ॥ 163॥
sārī māṇasāī duhāī aṇuhavai rāyaparicattā । sīlavisayaṁ kalaṁka taha ēīē payāsēha || 164 ||
tō vijjādēvīē rayaṇīi samāgayarasa naravaiṇō । vāsabhavaṇē ramatō saha tīē daṁsiō purisa || 165 |
tathā kālīdēvyāḥ pūjāṁ kr̥tvā tarpaṇāpūrvam । sutaviṣayamupayācitāmiccha tava yēna bhavati sutaḥ ॥ 151 ॥
ityuktā samyaktvē'kṣōbhaṇīyā sēndravr̥ndaiḥ । dēvaiḥ sā jalpati pratārayasi yadi janamanyam ॥192॥
jinavacanabhāvitēṣvavagataduḥ kharūpabhavasvarūpēṣu । yuṣmādr̥śīnāṁ vacanaṁ na krāmēd viṣamivāmr̥tē ॥ 113 ॥
putravihīnā'sītyādi pralapitaṁ yat tvayā'tividagdhē ! strīratnānāṁ bhavanti kati sutā yēna cakriṇām ? ।। 154 |
janmāntaraprāptānāmapi pūrvabhavābhyastaprēmavaśagānām । sahasōlāpāstadabhidhānagarbhāḥ pravartantē ॥ 159 ॥
bhavatīhāputrāṇāṁ na ca sugatiḥ, mōhavilasitamidamapi । putrā abrahmahētavō brahmaṇi dharmastataḥ sugatiḥ ॥ 156॥
putrairyadi svargō bhavati tataśchāgī śaikarī prathamam । śunī vā śakunirvā kamaṭī vā gacchēt svargam ॥157॥
yadi rakṣākāṇḍakādayaḥ putraṁ janayanti tatō na khalvaputraḥ । jāyatē jagati kō'pi hi janaṁ mudhā mā bhramaya ॥ 158 ॥
yadapi pralaptaṁ kālyāḥ pūjāmityādi, tatra kā kālī । kiṁvā surāmāṁsagr̥ddhātiśāyinyā api dēvatvam ? ॥
muktavā jinaṁ jinamatasthitāṁścānyamahaṁ na vandē । varakarivarē caṭitvā kaḥ kharaskandhaṁ samārōhati ? ॥ 160 ॥
ityēvaṁ yuktibhirvr̥rtā sunivāritāpi nōttiṣṭhati । pratihāryā bāhubhyāṁ dhr̥tvā nirvāsitā tataḥ ॥ 169 ॥
kōpēnōddhamantī smarati sā pūrvasādhitāṁ vidyām । smr̥tamātrā prāptā kiṁ kartavyamiti sā bhaṇati ॥ 162 ॥
patrājikā prajalpatyēpā nijajñānagarvitā pāpā । mama pi karōtyavajñāṁ tasmājjīvantī yathaiṣā ॥ 163 ॥
śārīramānasāni duḥkhānyanubhavati rājaparityaktā । śīlāvaṣayaṁ kalaṅka tathaitasyāḥ prakāśaya ॥ 164 ॥
tatō vidyādēvyā rajanyāṁ samāgatāya narapatayē । vāsabhavanē ramamāṇaḥ saha tayā darśitaḥ puruṣaḥ ॥ 165 ॥

rāyā jā avalōyai savisēsaṁ tā adaṁsaṇaṁ pattō । sō sahasā, tō rāyā vimhaiyamaṇō vicitē || 166 ||
ēīē rūvamōhiyahiō vijjāharō imō kōvi । pacchannō paḍivannō viddhī ! itthīsahāvassa ॥ 167॥
naya pii susaṇēhi na hu viṇaihi guṇihi, nahu lajjaha naya māṇiṇa naya cāḍuyasaihiṁ ।
naya kharakōmalavaṇina vihavi na jōvvaṇiṇa, duggējjhauṁ maṇu mahilahaṁ citaha āyariṇa || 168 ||
jō jāi jubaivaggē sambhāvaṁ mayaṇamōhiō purisō । duttaradukkhasamuddē nivaḍai sō natthi saṁdēhō ॥ 169 ॥
jiṇavayaṇabhāviyāvi hu nimmalakulasaṁbhavāvi dhīrāvi । jai ēsrāvi kusīlā kā gaṇaṇā iyaranārīṇaṁ ? ॥
iya tīē vittamaṇō rāyā ciṁtēi majjha bhōgakhamā । nūṇaṁ na hōi ēsā tahāvi saṁbhāsaṇīyā mē ॥ 171 ॥
jēṇutrayārō sō kōi tīē jiṇadhammadāṇaō vihiō । bhavasayaparaṁparā suvi paḍiuvayārē na jassa khamō ॥
kiñca ।
vāyasa vidyālayabhōyaṇaṁ tu kō bhuṁjiuṁ samahilasai ? | amayaṁva chipachittaṁ na bhōgamarihēi viusāṇa ||
iya tīē aṁgasaṁgē saṁgōviūṇa appaṇō cittaṁ । saṁvari āgāraṁ tīē sayāsammi saṁpattō ॥ 974 ॥
puvvaṭiīē tattō tīē ambhuṭṭiō ṭiō sijjaṁ । sabhā sivi khaṇamēgaṁ puṇōvi uṭṭhēi naranāhō ॥ 175 ॥
iya padvipi ēvaṁ sabhāsāī karēi naranāhō । nō puṇa taṇusaṁbhōga tō sā ēvaṁ vicitē ॥ 176 ॥
kiṁ kāraṇaṁ nariṁdō maṁdasiṇēhō paīva iva dāum̐ । khagamēgaṁ darisāvaṁ puṇōvi asaṇī hōi ? || 177 ||
tō ōgiṇya sadaṁ karēi cūḍāmaṇīi uvaōgaṁ । pañcāiyavijjāē picchara vilasiyamasēpi ॥ 178 ॥
rājā yāvadavalōkatē saviśēṣaṁ tāvadadarśanaṁ prāptaḥ । sa sahasā, tatō rājā vismitamanā vicintayati ॥ 166॥
ētayā rūpamōhitahr̥dayō vidyādharō'yaṁ kō'pi । pracchannaḥ pratipannō dhig dhik strīsvabhāvam ॥167॥
naca gr̥hyatē susnēhairna ca vinayairguṇaiḥ, na hi lajjābhirnaca mānēna natra cāṭukaśataiḥ ।
naca kharakōmalavacanēna na vibhavēna va yauvanēna, dugrahaṁ manō mahilānāṁ cintayatādarēṇa ॥ 168 ॥
yō yāti yuvativargē sadbhāvaṁ madanamōhitaḥ puruṣaḥ । dustara duḥkhasamudrē nipatati sa nāsti saṁdēhaḥ ॥ 169 ॥
jinavacanabhāvitāpi hi nirmalakulasaṁbhavāpi dhīrāpi । yadyēṣāpi kuśīlā kā gaṇanētaranārīṇām ॥ 170 ॥
iti tasyāṁ viraktamanā rājā cintayati mama bhōgakṣamā । nūnaṁ na bhavatyēṣā tathāpi saṁbhāṣaṇīyā mē ॥ 171 ॥
yēnōpakāraḥ sa kō'pi tathā jinadharmadānatō vihitaḥ । bhavaśataparamparāsvapi pratyupakārē na yasya kṣamaḥ ॥ 172 ॥
vāyasavidālitabhōjanaṁ tu kō bhōktuṁ samabhilaṣatē ? | amr̥taṁ vā bhikṣāspr̥ṣṭaṁ na bhōgamarhati viduṣām ॥173॥
iti tasyā aṅgasaṅgē saṁgōpyātmanaścittam । saṁvr̥tyākāraṁ tasyāḥ sakāśē saṁprāptaḥ ॥ 174 ॥
pūrvasthityā tatastayābhyutthitaḥ sthitaḥ śayyāyām । saṁbhāṣya kṣaṇamēkaṁ punarapyuttiṣṭhati naranāthaḥ ॥ 175 ॥
iti pratidinamapyēvaṁ saṁbhāṣādīn karōti naranāthaḥ । nō punastanusaṁbhōgaṁ tataḥ saivaṁ vicintayati ॥ 176॥
kiṁ kāraṇaṁ narēndrō mandasnēha : pradīpa iva dattvā । kṣaṇamēkaṁ darśanaṁ punarapyadarśanībhavati ॥ 177 ॥
tatōsvagr̥hya śabdaṁ karōti cūḍāmaṇērupayōgam । pratrājikāvidyāyāḥ paśyati vilasitamaśēṣamapi ॥ 178 ॥

narasiracūḍāmaṇiṇō tuha tarai na kōī guṇagaṇaṁ gaṇiuṁ । paccakkhadiṭṭhadōsēvi pariyaṇē jassa iya karuṇā ||
ucchibhōyaṇassava cattē bhōgē tara maha taṇussa । cūḍāmaṇīē dāum̐ uvaōgē iya maē nāyaṁ ॥ 193 ॥
jaha sijāē purisō piēṇa diṭṭhō maē saha lulaṁtō । lōēvi iya akittī dinnuvaōgē puṇō nāyā ॥
jaṇapaccakkhaṁ tā kiṁci dēha maha nāha dāruṇaṁ divvaṁ । jēṇēsa ayasapaḍahō vajjatō virama majjha ॥ 195 ॥
divyuttinnā jatti taha niyanāhassa parika hissāmi । parapurisadaṁsaṇaṁ iṁdiyālatulaṁ jahā muṇai || 196 ||
bhai nivō kaiyā taṁ kāyavvaṁ, bhaṇai sā pabhāyampi । kiṁ puṇa taṁ, pauramahallayāṇaṁ jaṁ samayaṁ hōhī ||
ēvaṁ hōutti ta bhaṇi āpucchiuṁ ca taṁ dēviṁ । vihiyatassamayakiccō suttō annattha gaṁtūṇaṁ ।। 198 ।।
aha paribuddhō cita nisāvasāṇammi kahavi divvavasā । jai ēsā na visujjhai tā duttaramamha vasaṇamiṇaṁ ||
iya puṇaruttaṁ ciṁtāurassa dōlāyamāṇahiyayassa । sūiyamaha kālanivēyaēṇa sūruggamasarūvaṁ ॥ 200 ॥
tadyathā;
“āsīstvaṁ niśi rājabhakta hr̥dayē tīrṣyālunā vajriṇā, prātaḥ śaṅkita ēva divyapadavīṁ gatvātmanaḥ śuddhayē ।
ūrvōttāpitavārdhitāpakatatyādākr̥ṣya muktō bahiḥ, prācyāsau nr̥pa ! taptamāṣaka iva pradyōtanō dyōtatē ॥”
iya sōuṁ paricita sujjhai ēsā sunicchiyaṁ divvē । divvaṁpi divvavāṇīē sūiyaṁ hōu imamēva || 201 ||
tō vihiyagōsa kicca sadāviya parijaṇaṁ purajaṇaṁ ca । dhammāhigaraṇiē taha pabhaṇai ēvaṁ jahā bhō bhō ! ॥
caṁpayamālā dēvī dussīlā ērisō jaṇapavāō। dēvīē suō sā bhaṇai divvasuddhacciya jimissaṁ ॥ 203 ॥
nicchiō maṁ taṁ puṇa tattamāsaō tā karēha sāmaggiṁ । bhāi jaṇō pāmaravayaṇamittaō ki imaṁ juttaṁ ? ॥
nara śiraścūḍāmaṇēstava śaknōti na kō'pi guṇagaṇaṁ gaṇayitum । pratyakṣadr̥ṣṭadōṣē'pi parijanē yasyēyaṁ karuṇā ॥
ucchiṣṭabhōjanasyēva tyaktē bhōgē tvayā mama tanōḥ । cūḍāmaṇau dattvōpayōgamiti mayā jñātam ॥193॥
yathā śayyāyāṁ puruṣaḥ priyēṇa dr̥ṣṭō mayā saha lōṭhan । lōkē'pītyakīrttirdattōpayōgē punarjñātā ॥ 194 ॥
janapratyakṣaṁ tasmātkiñcid dēhi mama nātha ! dāruṇaṁ divyam । yēnaiṣō'yaśaḥ paṭahō vādyamānō viramati mama ॥ 195॥
divyatīrṇā yukti tathā nijanāthaṁ parikathayiṣyāmi । " parapuruṣadarśanamindrajālatulyaṁ yathā jānāti ॥ 196 ॥
bhaṇati nr̥paḥ kadā tatkartavyam, bhaṇati sā prabhātē । kiṁ punastat, pauramahatāṁ yat saṁmataṁ bhavēt ॥ 197॥
ēvaṁ bhavatviti sakō bhaṇitvā''pr̥cchya ca tāṁ dēvīm । vihitatatsamayakr̥tyaḥ suptō'nyatra gatvā ॥ 198 ॥
atha pratibuddhaścintayati niśāvasānē kathamapi divyavaśāt । yadyēṣā na viśuddhyati tadā dustaramasmākaṁ vyasanārmidam
iti bhr̥śaṁ cintāturasya dōlāyamānahr̥dayasya । sūcitamatha kālanivēdakēna sūrōdgamasvarūpam ॥200॥

1॥
iti śrutvā paricintayati śudhyatyēṣā suniścitaṁ divyē । divyamapi divyavāṇyā sūcitaṁ bhavatvidamēva ॥ 209 ॥ .
tatō vihitaprātaḥkr̥tyaḥ śabdayitvā parijanaṁ purajanaṁ ca । dharmādhikaraṇikāṁstathā prabhaṇatyēvaṁ yathā bhō bhōḥ ! ||
campakamālā dēvī duḥśīlēdr̥śō janapravādaḥ । dēvyā śrutaḥ, sā bhaṇati divyaśuddhaiva jēmiṣyē ॥ 203॥
niścitō mē tatpunastaptamāṣakastasmātkuruta sāmagrīm । bhaṇati janaḥ pāmaravacanamātrataḥ kimidaṁ yuktam ? ॥ 204 ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
bhai nariṁdō juttaṁ avanavāō jahā tahā lōē । jēṇa payaṭṭō nūṇaṁ garuyāṇavi hara māha || 205 ॥
uktaṁ ca-
"viruddhastathyō vā bhavatu vitathō vā kimaparaṁ pratītaḥ sarvasmin harati mahimānaṁ janaravaḥ ।
"
tulōttīrṇasyāpi prakaṭanihatāśēṣatamasō, vēstādr̥k tējō na hi bhavati kanyāṁ gata iti ॥ "
dēvō jāṇai ēvaṁ jaṇēṇa bhaṇiyammi divvaṭhāṇammi | gaṁtuṁ hakkārāvara mahaliyē pēsiḍaṁ dēvi || 206 ||
pārēvi pōsaha sā pūēvi vihīē jinavariṁdēvi । siviyaṁ samāruhēḍaṁ saṁpattā divvabhūmī || 207||
aṁtērapi dulahadēvī muhaṁ mahalliyāmuhaō । vinnaviḍaṁ naranāhaṁ, avalōya javaṇiyaṁtariyaṁ ||208 ||
jāō nayarakhōhō miliō lōō vibhiō sahō । caṁpayamālādēvīē sōhaṇaṁ ajja hōutti ॥ 209 ॥
aha pajjaliō jalaṇō taviyaṁ tavayammi tillamaiparaṁ । kāraṇiyaniuttēhiṁ purisēhiṁ purō ya dēvīē ॥
jaha jaha pajalai sihī tillaṁ ullasai bahalalaharīhi । taha taha jagahiyayāī tannihiyāīva ḍajjhati ॥ 211 ॥
dhammāhigaraṇiēhiṁ pakkhittō jāva māsaō tattha । tāva sahasatti amhā palayānalasaṁnibhō analō ॥
pajjaliō savvattō taḍayaḍarāvēhiṁ bhariyanahavivarō । khaḍahaḍakhuḍaṁ tapāsāyasihara tuṭṭaṁtakōṭṭō || 213 ॥
māyāvi pi puttaṁ putō jaṇaṇipi miliḍaṁ jhatti । pāsāyasēlasālaggalaggaō gadhāhāhiṁ ॥ 214 ||
pukkarai ruyai vilavara hā hā hā putta ! māi ! jaṇasadō | vitthariō taha gayaṇē sāsaṇadēvīē iya bhaṇiyaṁ ॥
kittiyamittaṁ ēvaṁ caṁdakalānimmalāē dēvīē । ārōvaṁtāṇayasaṁ tumhāṇaṁ appavērīṇaṁ ? ॥ 216 ॥
iya suṇiuṁ nayarajaṇō bhayabhīō nivaḍiūṇa calaṇēsu । caṁpayamālābhimuhaṁ ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samārō || 217||
bhaṇati narēndrō yuktamavarṇavādō yathā tathā lōkē । yēna pravr̥ttō nūnaṁ gurūṇāmapi harati māhātmyam ॥205॥
dēvō jānātyēvaṁ janēna bhaṇitē divyasthānē । gatvā hakkārayati vr̥ddhāṁ prēpya dēvīm ॥ 206 ॥
pārayitvā pauṣadhaṁ sā pūjayitvā vidhinā jinavarēndrānapi । śivikāṁ samāsya saṁprāptā divyabhūmau ॥ 207 ॥
antaḥpuramapi dularbhadēvīpramukhaṁ vr̥ddhāmukhataḥ । vijñapya naranātham, avalōkatē yavanikāntaritam ॥208॥
jātō nagarakṣōbhō militō lōkō vijr̥mbhitaḥ śabdaḥ । campakamālādēvyāḥ śōbhanamadya bhavatviti ॥ 209 ॥
atha prajvalitō jvalanastāpitaṁ kaṭāhē tailamatipracuram । kāraṇika niyuktaiḥ puruṣaiḥ puraśca dēvyāḥ || 210॥
yathā yathā prajvalati śikhī tailamullasati bahalalaharībhiḥ । tathā tathā janahr̥dayāni tannihitānīva dahyantē ॥ 219 ॥
dharmādhikaraṇikaiḥ prakṣiptō yāvanmāṣakastatra । tāvat sahasētyakasmātpralayānalasaṁnibhō'nalaḥ ॥ 212 ॥
prajvalitaḥ sarvatastaṭataṭarāvairbhr̥tanabhōvivaraḥ । khaṭakhaṭakhaṭatprāsādaśikhara truṭyatkōṭṭataṭaḥ ॥ 293 ॥
mātāpi priyaṁ putraṁ putrō jananīmapi muktvā jhaṭiti । prāsādaśailaśālāgralagnō gurusvaraiḥ ॥ 214 ॥
pūtkarōti sōdati vilapati hā hā hā putra ! mātaḥ ! janaśabdaḥ । vistīrṇastathā gaganē śāsanadēvyēti bhaṇitam ॥
kiyanmātramētaccandrakalā nirmalāyāṁ dēvyām । ārōpayatāmayaśō yuṣmākamātmavairiṇām ॥ 216 ॥
iti śrutvā nagarajanō bhayabhītō nipatya caraṇayōḥ । campakamālābhimukhamēvaṁ bhaṇituṁ samārabdhaḥ ॥217॥

ō dēvi ! rakkha rakkhaha nayaramanāhaṁva ujjhamāṇamiṇaṁ । aviṇīēsuvi uvajīvagēsu na parammuhā garuyā ।।
yataḥ;
"upajīvakēṣu vimukhāḥ sujanā na bhavanti durvinītēṣu । vatsavyathitē'pyūdhasi surabhinōṁ śēmayati kṣīram " ॥
rāyāvi papaī tujha dēvi ! phalihujjalambhi sīlammi । ārōviyaṁ kalaṁkaṁ jamimēhiṁ jaṇēhiṁ mūḍhēhiṁ ||
tassēva pāvavasaviḍō kusumamaṇuhavaṁti iha ēē । tujjha pasāyaṁ mōttuṁ saraṇaṁ annō na āṇaṁ ॥ 220 ॥
caṁpayamālā pabhaṇai jai maha arikēsariṁ vimōttaṇaṁ । vasai maṇēvi na annō tō aggī ēsa vijjhāu ||
sutthāvatthaṁ sayalaṁpi hōu ḍīpa ḍajjhamāṇaṁpi । tavvayaṇānaṁtaraō sāsaṇadēvīē taha vihiyaṁ ॥ 222 ॥
kōhalabhattīhiṁ jē tattha surā samāgayā tēhiṁ । ghuṭuṁ jayai susīla taha mukkā kusumabuṭṭīvi ॥ 223॥
jayajayaravasaṁmissō ucchaliō dēvaduduhīsahō । gayaṇayalē ya salīlaṁ paṇacciyaṁ dēvanārīhi ॥ 224 ॥
dharaṇiyalē savvattō nayarē dijjaṁti kuṁkumachaḍāō । vaṁdaṇamālasaṇāhāī tōraṇāī raijaṁti || 225||
akkhuḍiō pakkhuḍiō chikkatōva ya sabālavuḍaḍhajaṇō । jīvau caṁpayamālatti pirō viyara tattha ।।
iya accanbhuyamavalōiūṇa pavvāiyā bhayattattathā । ciṁtēi ahamaṇatthassa mūlabhūyamhi ēyassa ||227||
tāmaha maraṇaṁ saraṇaṁ sahiyavvāī ca dukkhalakkhāī । pāvāi maē pāvāī jēṇa vihiyāīgāī || 228 ॥
ēyaṁ tu mahāpāvaṁ mannē jai nittharāmi tattha gayā । apaiṭṭhāṇaṁ narayaṁ bhaṇati jaṁ jiṇamaē niuṇā ॥ 229॥
tahavi hu niyaduccariyaṁ payāsi sayalalōyapaccakkhaṁ । paṇamāmi mahāsaipāya paṁkayāiṁ tahiṁ gaṁtuṁ ॥ 230 ॥
hē dēvi ! rakṣa rakṣa nagaramanāthamiva dahyamānamidam । avinītēṣvapyupajīvakēṣu na parāṅmukhā guravaḥ ॥218॥
rājāpi prajalpati tava dēvi ! sphaṭikōjjvalē śīlē। ārōpitaḥ kalaṅkō yadēbhirjanairmūḍhaiḥ ॥ 219 ॥
tasyaiva pāpaviṣaviṭapinaḥ kusumamanubhavantīhaitē । tava prasādaṁ muktvā śaraṇamanyō naitēpām ॥220॥
campakamālā prabhaṇati yadi mamārikēsariṇaṁ vimucya । vasati manasyapi nānyastatō'gnirēṣa vidhyāyatu ॥221॥
susthāvasthaṁ sakalamapi bhavatu dagdhamapi dahyamānamapi । tadvacanānantarataḥ śāsanadēvyā tathā vihitam ॥ 222 ॥
kautūhalabhaktibhyāṁ yē tatra surāḥ samāgatāstaiḥ । ghuṣṭaṁ jayati suśīlaṁ tathā muktā kusumavr̥ṣṭirapi ॥ 223॥
jayajayaravasaṁmiśra ucchalitō dēvadundubhiśabdaḥ । gaganatalē ca salīlaṁ pranartitaṁ dēvanāśībhiḥ ॥224॥
dharaṇītalē sarvatō nagarē dīyantē kuṅkumacchaṭāḥ । vandanamālāsanāthāni tōraṇāni racyantē ॥225॥
kuṣṭō vikāśitaḥ kṣutayannapi sabālavr̥ddhajanaḥ । jīvatu campakamālēti jalpanaśīlō vicarati tatra ॥226॥
ityatyadbhutamavalōkya pratrājikā bhayatrastā । cintayatyahamanarthasya mūlabhūtā'smyētasya ॥ 227 ॥
tasmād mama maraṇaṁ śaraṇaṁ sōḍhavyāni ca duḥkhalakṣāṇi । pāpayā bhayā pāpāni yēna vihitānyanēkāhi ॥ 228 ॥
ētattu mahāpāpaṁ manyē yadi nistarāmi tatra gatā । apratiṣṭhānaṁ narakaṁ bhaṇanti yaṁ jinamatē nipuṇāḥ || 229||
tathāpi hi nijaduścaritaṁ prakāśayitvā sakalalōkapratyakṣam । praṇamāmi mahāsatīpādapaṅkajāni tatra gatvā ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
ēyaṁ tu karaṁtīē saṁpajjai kahavi jaivi maha maraṇaṁ । pāvabharabhāralahuyattakāraṇaṁ taṁpi na yaṇihaṁ ॥ 239 ॥
iya sāhasamavalaṁbiya turiyaṁ gaṁtr̥̄ṇa divvabhūmīē । dūrujjhiyabhuyadaṁḍā sahāsamakkhaṁ bhai ēvaṁ ||232||
jayau jiṇasāsaṇamiṇaṁ mahāsaīō mahappabhāvāō । iya pāḍihēravaḍāō jattha dīsaṁti ajjavi ya ॥
iya jaṁpiūṇa camayamālāpāsu paṇamiuṁ bhaṇai । jayai tuha dēvi ! sīlaṁ nicalacittāē sammattē ॥ 234 ॥
ajjappabhiī mamāvi hu sammattaṁ havau tuha pasāēṇa | dēvaguruṇōya jē tuha tē majjhavi hōṁtu jājīvaṁ ॥ 235 ॥
iya paḍivaijjivi sammaṁ capayamālā kalaṁkamavaṇēuṁ । nicaduccariyaṁ payaḍai dukkammāvagamaō ēvaṁ ॥ 236॥
jaha dēvīē saīṇaṁ sirōmaṇīē samaṁ abhiramaṁtō । vijjāsāmatthā daṁsiō maē nivaiṇō purisō ||237||
nivapariyaṇammi taha purajaṇammi sayalammi vaiyarō ēsō । gamiō paraṁ pasiddhiṁ vijjāsāmatyaō caiva ॥
aha taṁ pucchai rāyā hēū kō ēttha tujjha, sā bhaṇai । maha kūḍakavaḍaduḍakuḍīē hēū kimanōvi ? ॥ 239 ॥
rāyā jaṁpara jaha avitahaṁ taē dukkaḍaṁ niyaṁ kahiyaṁ । hēūvi taha kahijjau annaha nūṇaṁ viṇassihisi ।।
kittiyamittaṁ ēvaṁ sā jaṁpara dukkaḍassa ēyassa ? | aṇuhaviyavvāī maē ajjavi naraēsa dukkhāī | | 241 ॥
rāyā japai ēyaṁ siṁha rē rē kadaṁtatillēṇa । dhiṭṭimajavamuddā galai jēṇa maṇabhavaṇadārāō || 242॥
jāva tahacciya kāuṁ samuṭṭiyā kiṁkarā nivāēsaṁ । caṁpayamālā jaṁpai saṁsaṁbhamā tāva naranāhaṁ ॥ 243 ॥
vāraha bāraha sāmiya ! ēē jā kiṁpi vinnavēma ahaṁ । rannā tahēva vihiē cēpamālā imaṁ bhaṇai || 244॥
ētattu kurvatyāḥ saṁpadyatē kathamapi yadyapi mama maraṇam । pāpabharabhāralaghutvakāraṇaṁ tadapi na cāniṣṭam ॥ 239 ॥
iti sāhasamavalambya tvaritaṁ gatvā divyabhūmau । dūrōjjhitabhujadaṇḍā sabhāsamakṣaṁ bhaṇatyēvam ॥ 232 ॥
jayatu jinaśāsanamidaṁ mahāsatyō mahāprabhāvāḥ । iti prātihāryaprakaṭā yatra dr̥śyantē'dyāpi ca ॥233॥
iti jalpitvā campakamālāpādau praṇamya bhaṇati । jayati tava dēvi ! śīlaṁ niścalacittāyāḥ samyaktvē ||234 ||
adyaprabhr̥ti mamāpi khalu samyaktvaṁ bhavatu tava prasādēna । dēvaguravaśca yē tava tē mamāpi bhavantu yāvajjīvam ॥
iti pratipadya samyaktvaṁ campakamālākalaṅkamapanētum । nijaduścaritaṁ prakaṭayati duṣkarmāvigamata ēvam ॥236॥
yathā dēvyā satīnāṁ śirōmaṇinā samamabhiramamāṇaḥ । vidyāsāmarthyād darśitō mayā nr̥patayē puruṣaḥ ॥ 237॥
nr̥paparijanē tathā purajanē sakalē vyatikara ēṣaḥ । gamitaḥ parāṁ prasiddhi vidyāsāmarthyata ēva || 238॥
atha tāṁ pr̥cchati rājā hētuḥ kō'tra tava, sā bhaṇati । mama kūṭakapaṭaduṣkr̥takuṭyā hētuḥ kimanyō'pi ? ॥
rājā jalpati yathā'vitathaṁ tvayā duṣkr̥taṁ nijaṁ kathitam । hēturapi tathā kathyatāmanyathā nūnaṁ vinaṅkṣkṣyasi ||
kiyanmātramētat sā jalpati duṣkr̥tasyaitasya ! | anubhavitavyāni mayā'dyāpi narakēṣu duḥkhāni ॥ 241॥
rājā jalātyētāṁ siñcata rē rē tapyamānatailēna । ghr̥ṣṭatājapamudrā galati yēna manōbhavanadvārāt ॥ 242॥
yāvattathaiva kartuṁ samutthitāḥ kiṅkarā nr̥pādēśam । campakamālā jalpati sasaṁbhramā tāvad naranātham ॥ 243॥
vāraya vāraya svāmin ! ētān yāvatkimapi vijñapayāmyaham । rājñā tathaiva vihitē campakamālēdaṁ bhaṇati ॥ 244 ॥
