tumhārisāṇa sāmiya ! vivēśvararayaṇarōhaṇagirīṇa । karuṇārasasarasīē kimimī juttamiya kāuṁ ? |
nipāṇacāṇavi parapāṇē rakkhiuṁ mahai ēsā । kō kuṇai jīvalōē piya ! ēvaṁ maraṇabhīrummi ? |
annaṁ ca--
niyaduccariyaṁ iya saṁkaḍammi kō payaḍiḍaṁ taraha ēvaṁ । jiṇavayaṇaṁ jassa maṇē na bhāvaō pariṇayaṁ hōi ? ॥
vōlīṇā sāvatthā jīē visakaṁdalī imā āsi । tā vacchalamimīē juttaṁ ēttō na duhadāṇaṁ || 248॥
uktaṁ ca--
" sādharmikavatsalatā kalpalatā sakalasaṁpadāṁ prasavē । yasmāttasmāttatraiva kr̥tadhiyaḥ kurvatē yatnam ॥”
juttājuttaṁ jāṇai dēvicciya jēpiḍaṁ iya naridō | caṁpayamālāra samaṁ saṁpattī niyaṁyabhavaṇami || 249||
pavvāiyāvinivyahiyayā nisuṇēi paidiṇaṁ dhammaṁ । dēvīi saṁnihāṇē kuṇai ya jahasati gihiuciyaṁ ॥
pacchāyāvadavānalakavaliyahiyayā visōvaōgēṇa । aha dullahadēvīvi hu icchai niyajīviyaṁ ca || 251 ||
iya tīē vavasiyaṁ nāumittha cūḍāmaṇīē lahumēva । tattō caṁpayamālā saṁpattā tassamītrammi || 252 ||
pucchai kiṁ 'tumha karē pāsu nivaḍiūṇa sā bhaṇai । jaṁ kiṁpi muṇaha tubbhē, kō hēū, muṇaha jaṁ tubbhē ॥ 253॥
jaṁpara caṁpayamālā ēyassa na hōi ēsa paḍiyārō । vajjai ya ayasapaḍahō tiṇha juṇḍujjalakulā ||254||
ēvaṁ ēvaṁ dhammaṁ kuṇamāṇā gamaha kavi diyahāī । paḍiyārammi uvāyaṁ imassa samaē kahissāmi || 255॥
avayārauvayāraparāyaṇāē para chidapihaṇavasaṇāē । tujjha namō tujjha namō saphalīkaya sukulajammāē ॥ 256॥
yuṣmādr̥śāṁ svāmin ! vivēkavararatnarōhaṇagirīṇām । karuṇārasasarasyāḥ kimasyā yuktamiti kartum ॥ 245॥
nijaprāṇatyāgēnāpi paraprāṇān rakṣituṁ kāṅkṣatyēṣā । kaḥ karōti jīvalōkē priya ! ēvaṁ maraṇabhīrau ! || 246 ॥
anyacca,
I
nijaduścaritamiti saṁkaṭē kaḥ prakaṭayituṁ śaknōtyēvam । jinavacanaṁ yasya manasi na bhāvataḥ pariṇataṁ bhavati ? ॥247॥
atikrāntā sāvasthā yasyāṁ viṣakandalīyamāsīt । tasmād vātsalyamasyā yuktamitō na duḥkhadānam ॥ 248 ॥
yuktāyuktaṁ jānāti dēvyēva jalpitvēti narēndraḥ । campakamālayā samaṁ saṁprāptō nijakabhavanē || 249||
pravrājikāpi nirvr̥tahr̥dayā śr̥ṇōti pratidinaṁ dharmam । dēvyāḥ saṁnidhānē karōti ca yathāśakti gr̥hayucitam ॥ 290॥
paścāttāpadavānalakavalitahr̥dayā viṣōpayōgēna । atha durlabhadēvyapi khalvicchati nijajīvitaṁ tyaktum ॥259॥
iti tasyā vyavasitaṁ jñātvā'tra cūḍāmaṇinā ladhyēva । tataścampakamālā saṁprāptā tatsamīpē || 252 ॥
pr̥cchati kiṁ tava karē pādayōrnipatya sā bhaṇati । yat kimapi jānīta yūyaṁ kō hētu:, jānīta yaṁ yūyam ॥ 253॥
jalpati campakamālaitasya na bhavatyēṣa pratikāraḥ । vādyatē cāyaśaḥ paṭahastrayāṇāṁ jyōtsnōjjvalakulānām ॥254॥
ēvamēvaṁ dharmaṁ kurvāṇā gamaya katyapi divasāni । pratikāra upāyamasya samayē kathayiṣyāmi ॥295॥
mapakārōpakāraparāyaṇāyai paracchidrapidhānavyasanāyai । tubhyaṁ namastubhyaṁ namaḥ saphalīkr̥tasukulajanmāyai ॥ 256 ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
iya dharaṇinihittasirā dullahadēvī puṇō paṇamiūṇa । maha ēē ciya caraṇā saraṇaṁ iya bhaṇiya puṇaruttaṁ ॥ 257॥
bhāi taicciya vayaṇaṁ kassavi suyaṇassa suyaṇu ! saccaviyaṁ । jaṁ aguṇēsuvi sattēsu hōṁti uvayāriṇō suyaṇā ||
yataḥ;-
" nirguṇēṣvapi sattvēṣu dayāṁ kurvanti sādhavaḥ । nahi saṁharati jyōtsnāṁ candraścāṇḍālavēśmasu ॥”
iya caṁpayamālāē saha gurupīīē vaḍḍhamāṇīē | dullahadēvīē nivō camakkiō citaē ēvaṁ || 259 ||
sukuluppattī ya guṇannuyā ya sammaṁ imīē nivvaḍiyā । vayagassa imassa tahā atthōvi ya pariṇaō bāḍhaṁ ॥
" varaṁ jvālākulē vahāvahāya nihitaṁ vapuḥ । na punarguṇasaṁpannē kr̥taḥ svalpō'pi matsaraḥ |"
iya ēvaṁ savvatthavi samuvvahaṁtō guṇēsu bahumāṇaṁ । savisēsaṁ jiṇadhammē kuṇai pavittiṁ punāhō ॥ 269 ॥
tathāhi; -
painagaraṁ paigāmaṁ savvattha jiṇēsarāṇa bhavaṇāī । kārēi niyayadēsē visēsaō suvihiyajaṇassa ॥ 262॥
bhattivahumāṇapavvaṁ vasa hipayāṇāiēsa kicēsu । niyaahigāriyalōyaṁ payaṭṭaē samayanīīē ॥ 263 ॥
sāhammiyavacchalaṁ paramaṁgaṁ sivasuhassa taṁ kuṇai । suṇai siddhaṁtasāraṁ dhariyassa na maraṇamāṇavara ॥ 264 ॥
savvatthavi ghōsāvara paḍahayapucvaṁ amārisadaṁ ca । ummukkakadaṁḍaṁ sāvayalōyaṁ karāvē || 265 ||
iya dēvīē samēō dhamrō pālaē sunīīē । rajjamaṇavajjakajjē sajjamaī sayayamujjamaī ॥ 266 ॥
aha annayā kayāī pasavai puttaṁ pavittasumuhuttē । caṁpayamālā puvyacca diṇayaraṁ aruṇakaracaraṇaṁ || 267 ||
vaddhāviō nariṁdō pivaīyā ē puttajammēṇa । sē dinamaṁgalaggaṁ ābharaṇaṁ mauḍaparivajjaṁ ॥ 268 ॥
taha sā dāsattāō mukkāṇattō ya taha paḍīhārō । jaha jiṇapūyāpuvvaṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ karāvēha || 269 ||
iti dharaṇanihitaśirā durlabhadēvī punaḥ praṇamya । mamaitāvēva caraṇau śaraṇamiti bhaṇitvā bhūyaḥ ॥ 257 ॥
bhaṇati tvayaiva vacanaṁ kasyāpi sujanasya sutanu ! satyāpitam । yadaguṇēṣvapi sattvēṣu bhavantyupakāriṇaḥ sujanāḥ ॥ 258।
iti campakamālayā saha guruprītau vardhamānāyām । durlabhadēvyā nr̥paścamatkr̥taścintayatyēvam ॥259
sukulōtpattiśca guṇajñatā ca samyagasyā niṣpatitā । vacanasyāsya tathā'rthō'pi ca pariṇatō bāḍham ॥260 ॥
ityēvaṁ sarvatrāpi samudvahan guṇēṣu bahumānam । saviśēṣaṁ jinadharmē karōti pravr̥ttiṁ pr̥thivīnāthaḥ ॥ 269॥
pratinagaraṁ pratigrāmaṁ sarvatra jinēśvarāṇāṁ bhavanāni । kārayati nijadēśē viśēṣataḥ suvihitajanasya ॥262॥
bhaktibahumānapūrvaṁ vasatipradānādikēṣu kr̥tyēṣu । nijādhikārilōkaṁ pravartayati samayanītyā ॥ 263 ॥
sādharmika vātsalyaṁ paramāṅgaṁ śivasukhasya tatkarōti । śr̥ṇōti siddhāntasāraṁ dhr̥tasya na maraṇamājñapayati ॥ 264 ।
sarvatrāpi ghōṣayati paṭahapūrvamamāriśabdaṁ ca । unmuktaśulkadaṇḍaṁ śrāvakalōkaṁ kārayati ॥ 265 ॥
iti dēvyā samētō dharmaparaḥ pālayati sunītyā । rājyamanavadyakāryē sajjamatiḥ satatamudyacchati ॥ 266॥
athānyadā kadācitprasūtē putraṁ pavitraṁ sumuhūrtē । campakamālā pūrvēva dinakaramaruṇakaracaraṇam ॥ 267 ॥
vardhitō narēndraḥ priyaṁvadayā putrajanmanā । tasyai dattamaṅgalagnamābharaṇaṁ mukuṭaparivarjam || 268 ||

caṁpayamālākahā ।
123
tēvi tahatti vihiyaṁ purisē saṁpēsiūṇa savvattha । dhayaciṁdhahaṭṭasōhāē sōhiyaṁ taṁ puraṁpi kayaṁ ॥ 270 ॥
māsamma aikkaṁtē nāmaṁ puttassa sumuhuttammi । bhuvaṇāṇaṁdōtti kayaṁ mahāvibhūīē bhūvaiṇā ||271 ||
saṁgayakalākalāvō vittajuō sayalalōyamaṇaharaṇō । juvarāyapaē rāyavva ṭhāviō sō naridēṇa || 272॥
tatō kamēṇa puttō jāō bīōvi kumarakarisīhō । duhiyāvi tahā ēkkā jayasuṁdarināmiyā jāyā ||
iya vaccatē kālē caṁpayamālāē niyapaī bhaṇiō । samaō ēsa narēsara ! vayamaggē garuyapurisāṇaṁ ॥ 274 ॥
tō bhai nivō juttaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ tumhēhiṁ kiṁtu kammavasā । tuhamuhakamalavilōyaṇatisiōcciya ajjavi mayacchi ! ।।
tō paitaṁ sā jaṁpai mā jaṁpasu nāha ! ērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ । aṇusāsasu appāṇaṁ imēṇa aṇusāsaṇakamēṇa || 276 ।।
tadyathā;
hī hī nihīṇa rē jīva ! pāviḍaṁ maṇuyajammamavi dulahaṁ । hārasi ramaṇīṇa kaē jāṇa kā caṁgimā tāṇa ? ॥
tathāhi :-
jaṁ majjhē taṁ bāhiṁ jaṁ bāhi taṁ havijja jaha majjhē । ramaṇītaṇussa tā hōjja dunnivārā suṇayakāyā ||278 ॥
kiṁ ramaṇīyaṁ ramaṇītaṇussa cammaṭṭhiruhira maiyassa । muttaṁtapurīsanasāvasāvisappaṁtagaṁdhassa ! || 279॥
mayaṇaabhullira dullaliyabhillasumahallatikkhabhallī hiṁ । sō vijjhai jō gijjhai ramaṇīramaṇīyataṇuphāsē ॥ 280 ॥
jaha aṇurajjasi taruṇīyaṇammi taha jaṛa jiṇidadhammammi । tō tēṇēva bhavēṇaṁ bhavakkhaō tuha bhavē jīva ! ।।
kō aṇurāō kā tamma bhallimā vallahammi rē jīva ! । jammi calō sambhāvō gayaṇamiva taḍitaḍakārō! ॥
tathā sā dāsatvād muktā''jñaptaśca tathā pratīhāraḥ । yathā jinapūjāpūrva vardhanakaṁ kāraya ॥ 269 ॥
tēnāpi tathēti vihitaṁ puruṣān saṁprēṣya sarvatra । dhvajacihahaṭṭaśōbhayā śōbhitaṁ tatpuramapi kr̥tam ॥270॥
māsē'tikrāntē nāma putrasya śubhamuhūrtē । bhuvanānanda iti kr̥taṁ mahāvibhūtyā bhūpatinā ॥ 279 ॥
saṁgatakalākalāpō vr̥ttayutaḥ sakalalōkamanōharaṇaḥ । yuvarājapadē rājēva sthāpitaḥ sa narēndrēṇa || 272॥
tataḥ kramēṇa putrō jātō dvitīyō'pi kumārakarisiṁhaḥ । duhitāpi tathaikā jayasundarīnāmikā jātā ॥ 273॥
iti vrajati kālē campakamālayā nijapatirbhaṇitaḥ । samaya ēṣa narēśvara ! vratamārgē gurupuruṣāṇām ॥ 274॥
tatō bhaṇati nr̥ṣō yuktaṁ bhaṇitaṁ yuṣmābhiḥ kintu karmavaśāt । tvanmukhakamalavilōknatr̥ṣita ēvādyāpi mr̥gākṣi ! ॥
tataḥ prati taṁ sā jalpati mā jalpīnātha ! īdr̥śaṁ vacanam । anuśādhyātmānamanēnānuśāsanakramēṇa ॥276॥
hī hī nihīna rē jīva ! prāpya manujajanmāpi durlabham । hārayasi ramaṇīnāṁ kr̥tē yāsāṁ kā caṅgimā tāsām ॥
yad madhyē tad bahiryad bahistad bhavēdyadi madhyē । ramaṇītanōstatō bhavēyurdunirvārāḥ śunakakāyāḥ || 278 ॥
kiṁ ramaṇīyaṁ ramaṇītanōścarmāsthirudhiramayasya । mūtrāntrapurīṣanasāvasāvisarpagandhasya 1 ॥ 279 ॥
madanābhraṁśanaśīladurlalitabhillasumahātīkṣṇabhalībhiḥ । sa vidhyati yō gr̥dhyati ramaṇīramaṇīyatanusparśē ॥280॥
yathā'nurajasi taruṇījanē tathā yadi jinēndradharmē । tatastēnaiva bhavēna bhavakṣayastava bhavajjīva ! ॥ 281॥

supāsanāha-variammi-
addhacchipicchirīhiṁ avalāhiṁ vicalavivēyanēhāhiṁ । asuigurukuṭṭiyāhivi jē bhaṁsijjaṁti sattāō ||
tāṇa fasijjau līhā jīhā viusāṇa dhuṇau kiṁ tāṇa । purisāyāradharāṇaṁ cicāpurisāṇava narāṇaṁ ॥
hī hī ! aṇajjakajjajjayassa rē jīva ! tujjha, kiṁ bhaṇiyō । jiṇasāsaṇaṁpi kahamavi laddhaṁ hārēsi muhiyāē ? |
jaṁ visaēsu pasajjasi bhaṁjasi suhasīlagaruyavaṇa rāī । mattakarivva na cēyasi dēsaṇatikkhaṁ kusapahāraṁ ||286॥
tarammi bhulaṁ hē hiyaya ! hayāsa ! jiṇamayaṁ ladhuṁ । visayasuhāī vaṁchasi jīyaṭṭā piyasi hālahalaṁ ||
visaghāriō sattūriō si mōhēṇa kiṁva ṭhagiō si । visaēsuvi jaṁ sukkhaṁ maggasi rē jīva ! jāṇatō ॥
ghī ! tujjha caṁgimā tuṁgimāvi dhī ! dhī! guṇāṇa māhappaṁ । jaṁ kira laddhavivēōvi vavasasē bhuṁjiraṁ visaē ।
visayā visaṁva visayā asibba visayā masivva mantrēsu । maighāraṇalēyaṇakāraṇāu jasamayalaṇāō ya ॥
tā khaṇamavina khamaṁ tē visaēsa maṇō karitu rē jīva ! | suracāvacaṁcalē jīviyammi visaēsa kā tahā ? ॥
iya lakkhamaṇaṁ kāuṁ sayāvi jhājja bhavasarūvaṁ tu । jēṇa jaramaraṇaharaṇaṁ saṁvēgarasāyaṇaṁ lahaha || 292॥
iya tavayaṇāyannaṇasaṁvēyavasucchalaṁtaghaṇapulaō | caṁpayamā sappaṇayanitrbharaṁ bhaṇai naranāhō ||293 ||
micchattakaddamāō taha uddhariḍaṁ paṭṭiō pubviṁ । jaha ihaparabhavasuhakāraṇēsu aha ujjaō jāō ।। 294 ॥
rajjadhurādharaṇakhamē saṁpai pattēvi puttarayaṇammi । puvvabhavanbhāsāō rāgānaladāhaviharassa ||295 ||
niyama hasuvaṇṇakala suddhasaṁta saṁvēyarasajaluppīlō । palhatthiō mamōvari rāyapayāvaṁva avaṇēuṁ ॥ 296 ॥
kō'nurāgaḥ kiṁ tasmin bhadratvaṁ vāllabhyē rē jīva ! । yasmiṁścalaḥ sadbhāvō gagana iva taḍittaṭatkāraḥ ॥ 282॥
ardhā kṣidraṣṭrī bhirabalābhirvicalavivēkasnēhābhiḥ । aśucigurukōṣṭhikābhirapi yē bhraṁśyantē sattvāt ॥ 283॥
tēṣāṁ mr̥jyatāṁ rēkhā jihvā viduṣāṁ stōtu kiṁ tēṣām । puruṣākāragharāṇāṁ cañcāpuruṣāṇāmiva narāṇām ||284॥
hī hī ! anāryakāryārjakasya rē jīva ! tava kiṁ bhaṇāmaḥ । jinaśāsanamapi kathamapi labdhvā hārayasi mudhā ||
yad viṣayēṣu prasīdasi bhanakṣi śubhaśīlaguruvanarājīḥ । mattakarīva na cētasi dēśanā tīkṣṇāṅkuśaprahāram ॥ 286 ॥
mārgīntarē bhraṣṭaṁ hē hr̥daya ! hatāśa ! jinamataṁ labdhvā । viṣayasukhāni vāñchasi jīvitārthaṁ pibasi halāhalam ॥
viṣaghātitō'si dhattūritō'si mōhēna kiṁvā vañcitō'si । viṣayēṣvapi yatsaukhyaṁ mārgayasi rē jīva ! jānan ||
dhiktava caṅgimānaṁ tuṅgimānaṁ dhigdhig guṇānāṁ māhātmyam । yatkila labdhavivēkō'pi vyavasyasi bhōktuṁ viṣayān ॥
viṣayānviṣamiva vivayāna simiva viṣayānmaṣimiva manyasva । matighātanacchēdanakāraṇādyaśōmalinakaraṇācca ॥ 290 ॥
tasmātkṣaṇamapi na kṣamaṁ tē viṣayēṣu manaḥ kartuṁ rē jīva ! | suracāpacañcalē jīvitē viṣayaṣu kā tr̥ṣṇā ? ॥291॥
iti lakṣyamanaḥ kr̥tvā sadāpi dhyāyēta bhavasvarūpaṁ tu । yēna jarāmaraṇaharaṇaṁ saṁvēgarasāyanaṁ labhadhvam ॥ 292 ॥
iti tadvacanā karṇanasaṁvēgavaśōcchaladvana pulakaḥ । campakamālāṁ sapraṇayanirbharaṁ bhaṇati naranāthaḥ ॥ 293 ॥
mithyātva kardamāt tathōddhr̥tya pravartitaḥ pūrvam । yathēha parabhava sukhakāraṇēṣvasāvudyatō jātaḥ ||294 ||
rājyadhurādharaṇakṣamē saṁprati prāptē'pi putraratnē । pūrvabhavābhyāsād rāgānaladāha vidhurasya || 299||

payamālākahā।
125
tā sigyaṁ ciya kijjau appahiaṁ jā na ēi appahiyē । maraṇamasaraṇaparāṇaṁ amhāṇaṁ akayasukayāṇa ॥
samautti iyaviyāṇi varanāṇī bahumuṇīhi pariyariō । suyajala hināmasūrī samāgaō naṁdaṇujjāṇē ॥
ujjāṇapālaēṇaṁ kahiē dāūṇa pīidāṇaṁ sē। sattadrupayā ī gaṁtuṁ tadabhimuhaṁ daṇaṁ kuṇai ||299 ||
dēvī kumarēṇa ya anēvi maṁtipamuhalōēṇa । parivariō dēvēhi iṁdōvva gaīdamāruhō ||300 ||
ullasiyaamaṁda।ṇaṁdapulayajālēṇa jaḍiliyasarīrō | paṁcavihābhigamēṇaṁ saṁpattī sūripāsamma || 301 ||
caṁpayapālādulahadēvīpamuhāvarōhaparivariō | sūricaraṇāraviṁdaṁ namiuṁ bhūmīē uvavi ॥ 302 ॥
tō sajalajala gajjiyagahirasarēṇa pasāhaē sūrī । savvaṁpi bhavasarūvaṁ savittharaṁ taṁ nisāmē || 303 ॥
bhālayalamiliyakara kamala saṁpuḍō vinnavēi naranāhō । pahu ! dikkhānāvāē uttārahi maṁ bhavasamuddā || 304 ||
hōu avighaṁ tuha naravariṁda ! mā kuṇasu kamavi paḍivaidhaṁ । tō rāyā muṇiugaha āsannē ucchuvāḍampi ||
gaṁtuṁ saha kumarēṇa dēvīhivi tahaya maṁtilōēṇa । siṁhāsanammi kumaraṁ ṭhaviūṇaṁ bhaṇai saṁtiyaṇaṁ ॥ 306 ॥
ēsō bhuvāṇaṁdō tumha samakkhaṁ maē niyapayasmi । uviō taha daṭṭhavvō jahā ahaṁ ēttiyaṁ kālaṁ ||307 ||
iya bōtuṁ takkaṁṭhē ṭhaviō hārō niyāō kaṁṭāō । niyamauḍōvi piṇō tassa sirē rayaṇacicaiō ||
kāuṁ caṁdagatilayaṁ sapariyaṇō paṇamiūṇa taṁ bhaṇai । ēsa jaṇō daṭuvvō taha jaha diṭṭō maē puvviṁ ॥ 309 ॥
jaha maha āṇā sirasā paḍicchiyā taha imassa naravaimō । sammaṁ paḍicchiyacvāiya bhaṇiō pariyaṇō tattō ॥
nijamukhasuvarṇakalaśōllasatsaṁvēgarasajalasaṁghātaḥ । paryastō mamōpari rāgapratāpamivāpanētum ॥296॥
tasmācchīghramēva kriyatāmātmahitaṁ yāvannaityāprathitam । maraṇamaśaraṇaparāṇāmasmākamakr̥tasukr̥tānām ||297॥
samaya itīti vijñāya varajñānī bahumunibhiḥ parikaritaḥ । śrutajaladhināmasūriḥ samāgatō nandanōdyānē ॥ 298 ॥
udyānapālakēna kathitē dattvā prītidānaṁ tasmai । saptāṣṭapadāni gatvā tadabhimukhaṁ vandanaṁ karōti ॥ 299 ॥
dēvībhiḥ kumārēṇa cānyēnāpi mantripramukhalōkēna । parivr̥tō dēvairindra iva gajēndramārūḍhaḥ ॥300
ullasitāmandānandapulakajālēna jaṭilataśarīraḥ । pañcavidhābhigamēna saṁprāptaḥ sūripārśvē ॥ 301 ||
campakamālādurlabhadēvīpramukhāvarōdhaparivr̥taḥ । sūricaraṇāravindaṁ natvā bhūmyāmupaviṣṭaḥ ॥302॥
tataḥ sajalajaladagarjitagabhīrasvarēṇa prakathayati sūriḥ । sarvamapi bhavasvarūpaṁ savistaraṁ tanniśamya ॥ 303 ॥
bhālatalamilitakarakamalasaṁpuṭō vijñapayati naranāthaḥ । prabhō ! dīkṣānāvōttāraya māṁ bhavasamudrāt ॥ 304 ॥
bhavatvavighnaṁ tava naravarēndra ! mā kuruṣva kamapi pratibandham । tatō rājā munyavagrahāsanna ikṣuvārē ॥ 305 ॥
gatvā saha kumārēṇa dēvībhirapi tathā ca mantrilōkēna । siṁhāsanē kumāraṁ sthāpayitvā bhaṇati mantrijanam ॥ 306॥
ēṣa bhuvanānandō yuṣmākaṁ samakṣaṁ mayā nijapadē । sthāpitastathā draṣṭavyō yathāhamētāvantaṁ kālam ||307॥
ityuktvā tatkaṇṭhē sthāpitō hārō nijātkaṇṭhāt । nijamukuṭō'pi pinaddhastasya śirasi ratnamaṇḍitaḥ ॥ 308 ॥
kr̥tvā candanatilakaṁ saparijanaḥ praṇamya taṁ bhaṇati । ēṣa janō draṣṭavyastathā yathā dr̥ṣṭā mayā pūrvam ||309 ॥
yathā mamājñā śirasā pratīṣṭā tathāsya narapatēḥ । samyak pratyēpratyēti bhaṇitaḥ parijanastataḥ ॥ 310 ||

supāsanāha-riammi-
dulladēvīca payamālāpamuhāhiṁ sayaladēvīhiṁ । āsīsāmuhalāhi tassa kaō akkhayakkhēvō ॥ 311॥
bhai ya caṁpayamālā kamāgayaṁ jāya ! rajjariṇamēyaṁ । tai saṁkamiyaṁ piuṇā nitthariyavvaṁ payattēṇa ॥ 312॥
puttaya ! lōē bhannaṁti atthasatthēsu tini purisatthā । tēsuṁpi atthakāyā dhammāucciya lahijjaṁti ॥ 313 ॥
paramatthammi u succiya mōkkhassavi kāraṇaṁ na uṇa iyarē । jaṁ tē nisēviyā bhavaduhikahēuṁ bhavaṁti taō || 314 ||
purisatthattaṁ kiṁ tēsu, hōi dhammōvi vaccha ! purisatthō । sōcciya jō khalu bhaṇiō jiṇēhiṁ gayarāya dōsēhi ||
tāvaccha ! tara appā paṭṭiyanvō'pamattacittēṇaṁ । taha niyavaccasamāṇō lōōvi jiṇidadhammammi ||316॥
naya rāyadhammabāhāē hōi ēsōvi, tatthavi paiyattō । nō mōtavvō rēhaṛa jēṇa avatthōciyaṁ savvaṁ ||317||
savvakalā kusala savi pattahastavi jiṇidadhammammi । jā tuha sikkhā saccaṁ avaccanēhassa taṁ laliyaṁ ॥
iya tīsē uvaēsē pāuṁ savaṇaṁjalīhiṁ amayaṁva। bhuvaṇāṇaṁdanariṁdō uṭṭhēuṁ paṇamai naridaṁ ॥ 319 ॥
taha dēvīōvi, tattō tēṇāṇugaō'rikēsarinariṁdō । dēvīhiṁ pariyaṇēṇa ya vaṁdai gaṁtu mudipa ॥ 320 ॥
taha giṇhai akkhēvēṇa mōkkhasōkkhābhikaṁkhirō dikkhaṁ । caṁpayamālāpamuhāvarōharamaṇīhiṁ pariyariō ।। 321 ॥
pavvāiyā sulasāvi hu tīē gurū saṁkarōvi sayalēṇa । saha pariyaṇēṇa givha dikkhaṁ gurupāyamūlammi || 322||
caṁpayamālāpabhiī ajjāu samadhiyāu mayaharīē । siriāṇaṁda sirīē saṁjaya sirī ēvva paccakkhaṁ ॥ 323 ॥
bhuvaṇādanivōvi hu vaṁdēuṁ jiṇavaraṁ muṇidē ya । saṁvr̥ttō niyabhavaṇaṁ harisavisāyāulō dhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 324॥
durlabhadēvīcampakamālāpramukhābhiḥ sakaladēvībhiḥ | āśarmukharābhistasya kr̥tō'kṣatākṣēpaḥ ॥ 311 ॥
bhaṇati ca campakamālā kramāgataṁ jāta ! rājyarṇamētat । tvayi saṁkramitaṁ pitrā nistarītavyaṁ prayatnēna ॥ 312 ॥
putraka ! lōkē bhaṇyantē'rthaśāstrēṣu trayaḥ puruṣārthāḥ । tēṣvapyarthakāmau dharmādēva labhyētē ||313 ||
paramārthatastu sa ēva mōkṣasyāpi kāraṇaṁ na punaritarau । yattau niṣēvitau bhavaduḥkhēkahētū bhavatastataḥ ॥ 214॥
puruṣārthatvaṁ kiṁ tayōḥ, bhavati dharmō'pi vatsa ! puruṣārthaḥ । sa ēva yaḥ khalu bhaṇitō jinairgatarāgadvēpaiḥ ॥ 215 ॥
tasmād vatsa ! tvayātmā pravartitavyō'pramattacittēna । tathā nijāpatyasamānō lōkō'pi jinēndradharmē ॥ 396 ॥
na ca rājadharmabādhayā bhavatyēṣō'pi tatrāpi prayatnaḥ । nō mōktavyō rājatē yēnāvasthōcitaṁ sarvam ॥317॥
sarvakalākuśalasyāpi bahuśikṣitasyāpi jinadharmē । yā tava śikṣā satyamapatyasnēhasya tallalitam ॥318॥
iti tasyā upadēśān pītvā śravaṇāñjalibhyāmamr̥tamiva । bhuvanānandanarēndra utthāya praṇamati narēndram ॥319॥
tathā dēvīrapi, tatastēnānugatō'rikēsarinarēndraḥ । dēvībhiḥ parijanēna ca vandatē gatvā munīndrapādān ॥320॥
tathā gr̥hṇātyakṣēpēṇa mōkṣasaukhyābhikāṅkṣanaśīlō dīkṣām । campakamālāpramukhāvarōdharamaṇībhiḥ parikaritaḥ ।। 321 ॥
pravājikā sulasāpi hi tasyā guruḥ śaṅkarō'pi sakalēna । saha parijanēna gr̥hṇāti dīkṣāṁ gurupādamūlē ॥ 322 ॥
campakamālāprabhr̥taya āryāḥ samarpitā mahattarāyai । śrīānanda śriyai saṁyamaśriyā iva pratyakṣam ॥323॥
muvanānandanr̥pō'pi khalu vanditvā jinavaraṁ munīndrāṁśca । saṁprāptō nijabhavanaṁ harṣaviṣādākulō bāḍham ॥ 324॥

citai taō kimēsā nayarī annā gipi annayaraṁ । annē ya tē parasā jē piuṇā bhūsiyā huṁtā ॥ 325॥
jaha gayaṇaṁ rayaṇīē rahiyaṁ rayaṇīyarēṇa na hu sōhaṁ । dharai tahā nagaramiṇaṁ ahiyaṁ tāēṇa paricattaṁ ॥ 326 ॥
kālē galiyasōgō pālai rajjaṁ jaṇāṇa kayacōjjaṁ । siribhuvaṇāṇaṁda nivō akkamiyāsēsa riucakkō ।। 327||

aha sā gurusmr̥savisōhiyakammamala, vēyāvaccasamujjamarrubhiyatamapaḍala |

॥ iti samyaktyapraśaṁsāyāṁ campakamālākathānakaṁ samāptam ॥

yathā gaganaṁ rajanyāṁ rahitaṁ rajanīkarēṇa na hi śōbhām । dharati tathā nagaramidamadhikaṁ tātēna parityaktam ॥ 326॥
kālēna galitaśōkaḥ pālayati rājyaṁ janānāṁ kr̥tāścaryam । śrībhuvanānandanr̥pa ākrāntāśēṣaripucakraḥ ॥327॥

sūripadē gurubhiḥ sthāpitaḥ saha dīkṣitaśca sarvaḥ saḥ । munisādhvīnāṁ vargaḥ parivāratvēnānujñātaḥ ॥229॥
viharatō'ṇi ca tataḥ kṣīṇaghātikarmatamōnikarē । saddhyānaśailaśikhara uditō varakēvala dinēndraḥ ||330॥
pratibōdhya bhavikajanaṁ suciram, āyuḥ kṣayē śailēśīm । āruhyārikēsarisūriḥ paramapadaṁ prāptaḥ ॥ 339 ॥
durlabha dēvī sulasāpramukhābhiḥ sādhvībhiḥ parikaritā । ēkādaśāṅgāni campakamālāpi paripaṭhati ॥ 332॥

jaha gahagaṇāṇa gayaṇaṁ āhārō rōhaṇī ya rayaṇāṇaṁ । siṁdhūṇaṁ jaha jalahī taha sammattaṁ sivasuhāṇaṁ ॥ 1 ॥
jaha uvasamō muṇīṇaṁ cāō vihavīṇa sīlāmitthīṇa । taha sampattaṁ gihiṇō jaiṇō yavi bhūsaṇaṁ paramaṁ ||2||
saṁkāē jimmē savvē dēsē ya mailiē tammi | jāyai vihalaṁ sayalaṁḍāṇaṁ maṇirahassēva || 3 ||
tathāhi;
mahurā nāmēṇa purī asthi pasiddhā jayampi bhamarahiyā । vittasupavittapattā lacchīnivāsā kamaliṇinca ॥4॥
tatthasthi asthimaṇavaṁchiyatthasaṁpūraṇēkkavēsamaṇō । vēsamaṇō varasiṭṭī sammāṭṭhī purarō ||5||
rūvēṇa rūtriṇī itra rūviṇināmēṇa rōhiṇī tassa | micchattamōhiyamaī tahāvi sā bhattaṇō iṭṭā || 6 ||
tāṇaṁ ca dunni puttā jāyā samayammi suṁdarataraṁgā । maṇisiṁhanāmō paḍhamō vīō uṇa maṇirahō nāma ॥7॥
tāṇaṁ ca parōpparapīipagarasō vaḍhiō tahā kahavi । jaha rāmalakkhaṇāṇa nisuṇijjai samayasatthēṣu ||8||
aha annayā kayāi jugavaṁ jamuṇānaīē kūlammi । kīlaṁtāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ cāraṇasamaṇō tahiṁ pattō ॥ 9 ॥
mayaṇaṁva muttimataṁ taṁ jaṇiyalōyaṇāṇaṁdā | gurubhattipagarisēṇaṁ namasiuṁ dōvi uvi ॥ 10 ॥
tō dhampalābha putraṁ muṇiṇā saṁbhāsiō visēsēṇa । pāraddhā dhammakā tēsiṁ hiyaṭṭhāē jiṇabhaṇiyā ॥ 11 ॥
iha bhō bhaddā ! bhavasāgarammi tumbhērhiṇōrapārammi । jugasamilānā ēṇa kahavi bhamatē hiṁ maṇuyattaṁ ॥ 12 ॥
pattaṁ āriyakhitē jāikulāīhiṁ saṁgayaṁ inhi । savaṇuggahōvi ēsō saṁpatō tumha punnēhiṁ ||13||
annapi hu kallāṇaṁ savvaṁ saṁsāravāsijīvāṇaṁ । saṁpāḍijjaī punēṇa cēva kēṇāvi bhaṇiyaṁ ca ॥ 14 ॥
hu
yathā grahagaṇānāṁ gaganamādhārō rōhaṇaśca ratnānām । sindhūnāṁ yathā jalādhistathā samyaktvaṁ śivasukhānām ||
yathōpaśamō munīnāṁ tyāgō vibhavināṁ śīlaṁ strīṇām । tathā samyaktvē gr̥hiṇī yatinaścāpi bhūṣaṇaṁ paramam ॥2॥
śaṅkayā jinamēṁ sarvatō dēśataśca malinitē tasmin । jāyatē viphalaṁ sakalamanuṣṭhānaṁ maṇirathasyēva ॥2॥
mathurā nāmnā puryasti prasiddhā jagati bhrama-ra-hitā । vr̥ttasupavitrapā ( pa ) trā lakṣmīnivāsā kamalinīva ॥4॥
tatrāstyarthimanōvāñchitārthasaṁpūraṇaika vaiśramaṇaḥ । vaiśramaṇō varaśrēṣṭhī samyagdr̥ṣṭiḥ puragariṣṭhaḥ ||5||
rūpēṇa rūpiṇīva rūpiṇīnāmnā gēhinī tasya । mithyātvamōhitamatistathāpi sā bharturiṣṭā ॥ 6 ॥
tayōśca dvau putrau jātau samayē sundaratarāṅgau । maṇisiṁhanāmā prathamō dvitīyaḥ punarmaṇirathō nāma ||7||
tayōśca parasparaprītiprakarṣō vardhitastathā kathamapi । yathā rāmalakṣmaṇayōḥ śrūyatē samayaśāstrēṣu ||8||
athānyadā kadācidyugapad yamunānadyāḥ kūlē । krīḍatōstayōścāraṇaśramaṇastasmin prāptaḥ ॥9॥
madanamiva mūrttimantaṁ taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā janitalōcanānandau । gurubhaktiprakarṣēṇa namasthitvā dvāvapyupaviṣṭau ॥10॥
tatō dharmalābhapūrva muninā saṁbhāṣitō viśēṣēṇa ! prārabdhā dharmakathā tayōrhitārtha jinabhaṇitā ॥ 11 ॥
iha bhō bhadrāḥ ! bhavasāgarē yuṣmābhiranādipārē । yugasamijjñātēna kathamapi bhramadbhirmanujatvam ॥12॥
prāptamāryakṣētrē jātikulādibhiḥ saṁgatamidānīm । śravaṇāvagrahō'pyēṣa saṁprāptō yuṣmākaṁ puṇyaiḥ ॥ 13 ॥
anyadapi khalu kalyāṇaṁ sarva saṁsārabāsijīvānām ! saṁpādyatē puṇyanaiva, kēnāpi bhaṇitaṁ ca ॥ 14॥

maṇisiṁhakā ।

" yadvapuratiramaṇīyaṁ strījanakamanīyamanabhibhavanīyam । yatsāmrājyamakhaṇḍaṁ tatkhaṇḍaṁ dharmalābhēkṣōḥ ।"
ēyaṁca kisīē kaḍaṁgaraṁva, paramatthaō phalaṁ mōkkhō | dhammassa sucinnassēha avitahō sō ya jiṇabhaṇiō ||
tattō pattapuvvē jidhammē sammamāyaraṁ kuṇaha । jēṇa duhalaharirudaṁ bhavasamuddē lahuṁ taraha ॥ 16 ॥
sō duvigappō kahiō jiṇēhiṁ jiyarāgadōsamōhēhiṁ । sāhugihibhēyabhinnō paḍhamō ya mahavvayāiō ॥ 17 ॥
bīō bārasabhēō mūlaṁ duṇhapi tēsiṁ sammataṁ । taṁ saṁkāivimukkaṁ jīvāitattasadahaṇaṁ ॥ 18 ॥
suranaravarakayasēvō arihaṁ dēvō susāhuṇō guruṇō । iya sammattaṁ vr̥ttaṁ tavvivarīyaṁ tu micchattaṁ ॥ 19 ॥
bhālayalamiliyakarakamalasapuḍō vinnavēi taṁ sāhuṁ । maṇisihanāmā namiu bhayavaṁ ! paḍhamassa asamatthā ||20||
bīyassavi asamatthā tahāvi tuha daṁsaṇaṁ amōhati । pasiya sammattamittō dijjau amhāṇa jiṇadhammō ||
jara jōggayā muṇīsara ! amhāṇaṁ asthi, tō muṇī bhaṇai । rayaṇāṇa mahagghāṇavi rayaṇanihīvi huna kiṁ ṭhāṇaṁ ? ॥
iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ muṇiṇā karuṇārasavāsiyaṁtakaraṇēṇa । ārōviyaṁ vihīē sammattaṁ tāṇa dōhaṁpi ॥ 23 ॥
taha kahiyā tassa guṇā savittharaṁ sāhiyā ya dōsāvi । takārayāṇa kahium̐ suranārayasukkhadukkhāī ||24||
uppaiō muṇivasahō tēvi ya pattā niyammi gēhammi । piuṇō kahaṁti jaha ajja tāya ! jamuṇānaīkūlē ||
sammattamūlapasariya suṁddhamahanvayavisālakhaṁdhālō । sappasara samiiguttīmahalasāhō damapavālō || 26 ॥
suranara suhakusumaḍḍhō guṇagaṁdhaḍḍhō na rāyadavadaḍūḍhō । sauṇajaṇajaṇiyasakō mōkkhaphalaḍḍhō khamāruḍhō ॥27॥
bhavagimhataviyajaṇakayanivbujhdēsaṇa susīyalacchāō । paṇayajaṇakaṣpaviḍavī amhēhiṁ muṇivarō diṭṭhō ||28||
ētacca kr̥ṣyāstr̥ṇamiva, paramārthataḥ phalaṁ mōkṣaḥ । dharmasya sucīrṇasyēhāvitathaḥ sa ca jinabhaṇitaḥ ॥ 15॥
tatō'prāptapūrvē jinadharmē samyagādaraṁ kuruta । yēna duḥkhalaharīrudraṁ bhavasamudraṁ laghu tarata ॥ 16 ॥
sa dvivikalpaḥ kathitō jinairjitarāgadvēṣamōhaiḥ । sādhugr̥hi bhēdabhinnaḥ prathamaśca mahātratādikaḥ ॥17॥
dvitīyō dvādaśabhēdō mūlaṁ dvayōrapi tayōḥ samyaktvam । tacchaṅkādivimuktaṁ jīvāditattvaśraddhānam ॥ 18॥
suranaravarakr̥tasēvō'rhan dēvaḥ susādhavō guravaḥ । iti samyaktvamuktaṁ tadviparītaṁ tu mithyātvam ||19||
bhālatalamilitakarakamalasaṁpuṭō vijñapayati taṁ sādhum । maṇisiṁhanāmā natvā bhagavan ! prathamāyāsamarthau ॥20॥
dvitīyāyāpyasamarthau tathāpi tava darśanamamōghamiti । prasadya samyaktvamātrō dīyatāmāvābhyāṁ jinadharmaḥ ||21||
yadi yōgyatā munīśvara ! āvayōrasti, tatō munirbhaṇati । ratnānāṁ mahārvāṇāmapi ratnanidhirapi hi na kiṁ sthānam ? ॥
iti bhaṇitvā muninā karuṇārasavāsitāntaḥ karaṇēna । ārōpitaṁ vidhinā samyaktvaṁ tayōrdvayōrapi ॥ 23 ॥
tathā kathitāstasya guṇāḥ savistaraṁ kathitāśca dōṣā api । tatkārakāṇāṁ kathayitvā suranārakasukhaduḥkhāni ॥
utpatitō munivr̥ṣabhastāvapi ca prāptau nijē gēhē । pitaraṁ kathayatō yathā'dya tāta ! yamunānadīkūlē ॥25॥
samyaktvamūlaprasr̥ta śuddhamahāvrataviśālaskandhaḥ । saprasarasamiti guptimahāśākhō damapravālaḥ ॥ 26 ॥
puranarasukhakusumāḍhyō guṇagandhāḍhyō na rāgadavadagdhaḥ । śakuna (rūḍha ) janajanitaśabda | mōkṣaphalāḍhyō kṣamārūḍhaḥ ॥27॥

supāsanāha cariammi
mōkkha mahātaruvīyaṁ tēṇaṁ amhāṇa hiyayakhittēsu । sammattaṁ nihiūṇaṁ sittaṁ saddhāmuhajalēṇa ||29||
tō sēṭṭhī vēsamaṇō mammi tuṭṭhōvi pabhaṇaē ēvaṁ । juttaṁ tumhēhiṁ kathaṁ jai jaṇaṇībahumayaṁ hōhī ||30||
tō tāṇaṁ jaṇaṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ bhō ḍimbhagā ! jahicchāē । purapauraparisarāī sarāī sariyāṇa puliṇāī || 31॥
ityāgayā gayā iva niraṁkusā bhamaḍiūṇa sacchaṁda । nikkhaṇiyā niyahaṭṭē kiṁ nō ciṭṭhēha rē duṭṭā ! ||32||
kōsvasarō tumhāṇaṁ saṁpai dhammassa savaṇagahaṇēsu ? | mōttuṁ niyavāṇijjaṁ annaṁ nō kiṁpi kāyavvaṁ ||33|
tō jē jaṇaṇīē suṇiuṁ vayaṇāṇi japaē ēvaṁ । na puṇōvi imaṁ kāhaṁ khamasu mahaṁ mahapasāēṇa || 34॥
bīō puṇō vicitas karammi ciṁtāmaṇi kahavi pattaṁ । kiṁ cayai kōviō kōvi kahavi niyajīyavigamēvi ?
hura kāruṇiṇaṁ amayarasaṁ pāiō mahārōgī । sō ya paikhaṇamaṇuhavai lāghavaṁ tēṇa rōgassa ॥36॥
tō tamaṇakkhaparāyaṇapiyajaṇavayaṇēṇa vamau kiṁ rōgī ? । tō bhaṇau kiṁpi jaṇaṇī dhammaṁ ma caēmi jīvaṁtō ॥
pattaṁ apattapuvvaṁ sammattaṁ jaṁ maē imaṁ tassa । ciṭṭhara jaṇaṇī iṇhiṁ vahabaṁdhaṇamāraṇakarāvi ||38||
annōva kō sakkai jakkhō rakkhō na ahava sahasakkhō । maṁ cālēuṁ caliōvi palayapavaṇōvva surasēlaṁ ॥ 39 ॥
iya tīē nibhaō sō gacchai jiṇabhavaṇasāhuvasahīsu । pūyai vaṁdai gihajiṇapaḍimā tijhamuvauttō 40
jiṭṭhō bhagai jaṇaṇīē ṇiṭṭamēyaṁ karēsu mā vaccha ! । gharajiṇapaḍimāpūyā tāēṇa kayāvi sā na kayā ॥। 41॥
taṁ maṇirahō rammī pabhaṇai ēvaṁ kayammi kira jaṇaṇī । aṇuyattiyā bhavissai iyaṁ tuha bhāvō na sō juttō ॥
bhavagrīṣma taptajanakr̥tanirvr̥tidēśanasuśītalacchāyaḥ । praṇatajanakalpaviṭapī āvābhyāṁ munivarō dr̥ṣṭaḥ ॥ 28 ॥
mōkṣamahātarubījaṁ tēnāvayōrhadayakṣētrayōḥ । samyaktvaṁ nidhāya siktaṁ śraddhāśubhajalēna ॥ 29 ॥
tataḥ śrēṣṭhī vaiśramaṇō manasi tuṣṭō'pi prabhaṇatyēvam । yuktaṁ yuvābhyāṁ kr̥taṁ yadi jananībahumataṁ bhavēt ॥ 30 ॥
tatastayōrjananyā bhaṇitaṁ bhō ḍimbhakau ! yadr̥cchayā । purapracuraparisarēṣu sarassu saritāṁ pulinēṣu ॥ 31॥
atrāgatau gajāviva niraṁkuśa bhrāntvā svacchandam । niṣkhātau nijahaṭṭē kiṁ nō tiṣṭhataṁ rē duṣṭau ? || 32॥
kō'vasarō yuvayōḥ saṁprati dharmasya śravaṇagrahaṇayōḥ । muktvā nijavāṇijyamamyannō kimapi kartavyam ||33||
tatō jyēṣṭhō jananyāḥ śrutvā vacanāni jalpatyēvam । na punarapīdaṁ kariṣyē kṣamasva māṁ mahāprasādēna ॥34॥
dvitīyaḥ punarvicintayati karē cintāmaṇi kathamapi prāptam। kiṁ tyajati kōvidaḥ kō'pi kathamapi nijajīvitavigamēpi
kēnāpi kāruṇikēnāmr̥tarasaṁ pāyitō mahārōgī । sa ca pratikṣaṇamanubhavati lāghavaṁ tēna rōgasya ॥ 36 ॥
tatastaṁ rōṣaparāyaṇapriyajanavacanēna vamatu kiṁ rōgī ? । tatō bhaṇatu kimapi jananī dharma na tyajāmi jīvan ||37|
prāptamaprāptapūrvaṁ samyaktvaṁ yanmayēdaṁ tasya । tiṣṭhatu jananīdānīṁ vadhabandhanamāraṇakarāpi ॥ 38 ॥
anyō'pi kō'pi śaknōti yakṣō rakṣō nāthavā sahasrākṣaḥ । māṁ cālayituṁ calitō'pi pralayapavana iva suraśailam ।
iti tasyā nirbhayaḥ sa gacchati jinabhavanasādhuvasatiṣu । pūjayati vandatē gr̥ha jinapratimāstrisaṁdhyamupayuktaḥ ॥ 40 ॥
jyēṣṭhō bhaṇati jananyā aniṣṭamētat kāma vatsa ! । gr̥hajinapratimāpūjā tātēna kadāpi sā na kr̥tā ॥ 41 ॥

ēvaṁ ca karatēṇaṁ ēīē durāsayammi bahumāṇō । saṁjaṇiō hōjja maē nibaṁdhaṇaṁ dukkha lakkhāṇaṁ ||43||
jaṁpi tumhēhiṁ cattā sudhammakiriyā imīē vayaṇēṇaṁ । taṁpi na juttaṁ jamhā imīē ēsō na uvayārō ||44 ||
kiṁtu imō uvayārō jaṁ jiṇadhammē ṭhavijjaē ēsā । taṁ tu sayaṁ acayaṁtāṇa cēva saṁgacchaē nūṇaṁ ||45 ||
kiñca ।
na hu jidhammō labbhai paijammaṁ nēya tārisī sugurū । tamhā nissaṁkaṁ ciya kuṇa dhammaṁ kiṁ ca jaṇaṇīē ? ॥
kiṁca jaṇaṇī na jaṇaṇī piyāvi na piyā na baṁdhavō baṁdhū । naya taṁ mittaṁ mittaṁ jaṁ jiṇadhammā sē ||
dhammō na khalu annō rammō paramatthaō imaṁ mōttuṁ । jaṁ jīvadayāmr̥lō sā jīvadayā ya nannattha || 48 ॥
dēvavi jiṇavarōcciya jō vibbhamasaṁbhamēhiṁ parimukō । annē tayāgamēsuvi vibbhamasahiyā jaō bhaṇiyā ||49 ॥
kiñca ।
•
jaṇaṇī jaṇaō jāyā bhāyāmabhiīṇi bhavaparāvattē । na hi samagarmiti ētō aīyabhavasaṁbhavāṇīva ||50 ॥
dhammādhammāṇa phalaṁ jammaṁtarasaṁciyāṇa puṇa payaḍaṁ । riddhisamuddharaniddhaṇakulasaṁbhavaō jahāsaṁkhaṁ ॥ 51 ॥
jiṭṭhō pabhaṇai kō baccha ! paccaō, jaṁ jiṇēvi saṁdēhō । ciṭṭhau tā taddhammō na hu kajjaṁ kāraṇābhāvā ॥
iya saṁkāghaṇapaṁkē khuttaṁ taṁ nāuṁ maṇirahō bhaṇai । tuha khayaravisēṇassava bahuduharāhaṇaṁ bhavē hōhī ॥ 53॥
tathāhi;
atitha supasiddhavijjā vijjāsāhagasahassanayacalaṇā | maṁtasarōruhasarasī dēvī paumāvaī nāma ||24||
jiṇabhavaṇavahi bahuruvaruramī saragiva rayaṇaḍhaṁ । aṭṭhāvayagirisiharē tabbhavaṇaṁ asthi ramaṇīyaṁ ॥ 55 ॥
taṁ maṇiratha rahasi praṇatyēvaṁ kr̥tē kila jananī । anuvr̥ttā bhaviṣyatīti tava bhāvō na sa yuktaḥ ॥ 42॥
ēvaṁ ca kurvataitasyā durāśayē bahumānaḥ । saṁjanitō bhavēd mayā nibadhanaṁ duḥkhalakṣāṇām ॥43॥
yadapi yuṣmābhistyaktā sudharmakriyā'syā vacanēna । tadapi na yuktaṁ yasmādasyā ēṣa nōpacāraḥ ॥ 44 ॥
kintvayamupacārō yajjinadharmē sthāpyata ēṣā । tat tu svayamatyajatāmēva saṁgacchatē nūnam ॥45॥
na khalu jinadharmō labhyatē pratijanma naiva tādr̥śaḥ suguruḥ । tasmānniḥśaṅkamēva kuru dharma kiṁ ca jananyā ! ॥ 46 ॥
kiñca jananī na jananī pitāpina pitā na bāndhavō bandhuḥ । naca tanmittraṁ mittraṁ yajjinadharmād bhraṁśayati ॥47॥
dharmō'pi na khalvanyō ramyaḥ paramārthata imaṁ muktvā । yajjīvadayāmūlaḥ sā jīvadayā ca nānyatra ॥ 48 ॥
dēvō'pi jinavara ēva yō vibhramasaṁbhramaiḥ parimuktaḥ । anyē tadāgamēṣvapi vibhramasahitā yatō bhaṇitāḥ ॥ 49 ॥
nanī janakō jāyā bhrātr̥prabhr̥tīni bhavaparāvartē । nahi samakaṁ yantītō'tītabhavasaṁbhavānīva ॥50॥
dharmādharmayōḥ phalaṁ janmāntarasaṁcitayōḥ punaḥ prakaṭam । r̥ddhisamuddharanirdhanakulasaṁbhavatō yathāsaṁkhyam ॥ 11 ॥
jyēṣṭhaḥ prabhaṇati kō vatsa ! pratyayō, yajjinē'pi saṁdēhaḥ । tiṣṭhatu tāvattaddharmō na hi kārya kāraṇābhāvāt ॥ 12 ॥
iti śaṅkāghanapaṅkē magnaṁ taṁ jñātvā maṇirathō bhaṇati । tava khacaraviṣēṇasyēva bahuduḥ khasahanaṁ bhavē bhaviṣyati ॥53॥
asti suprasiddhavidyā vidyāsādhaka sahasunatacaraṇā । mantrasarōruhasarasī dēvī padmāvatī nāma ॥ 54 ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
aha annayā kayāī vēyaḍḍhanagāu kamalavimalāṇa । vijjāharīṇa jayalaṁ saṁpattaṁ tattha jiṇabhavaṇē ॥ 56 ॥
pūiya jiṇapaḍimāō bhattīē vaṁdiūṇa vihisāraṁ । sāraṁgīgayagēyajjhaṇīē gāyaṁti gīyāī ॥ 57 ॥
jiṇanāhaguṇapagarisasaṁbaddhāī visuddhabaṁdhāī । savvattō tā sahasā ucchaliō bahalahalavōlō || 58||
jaya jayasaddammīsō ahamahamigayāē pavisamāṇāṇaṁ । vijjāharāṇa cēiyaharammi jiṇarvivapūyā ॥ 59 ॥
tō tēṇa kalayalēṇa sāraṁgiravammi avalavijjaṁtē । paumāvaīya bhavaṇē gaṁtūṇaṁ tāu gāyaṁti ॥ 60 ॥
jaha gōyarīē hariṇā āgarisijjaṁti mahurasadēṇa । taha taggīyaravēṇaṁ sēṇavisēṇā duvē khayarā || 61 ॥
pacchannaṭhiyā nisuṇaṁti tāṇa gēyajyuṇīō mahurāō । jāṇērisā jhuṇīō hōjjā naṇu tāṇa rūvaṁpi । 62|
iya buddhīē gaṁtu pāsaṁtā tāṇa ruvariddhīō | īsāiva mayaṇēṇa samāhayā tikkhabāṇēhiṁ ॥ 63 ॥
tāōvi tāṇa rūvaṁ picchaṁtīō tahāhayā tēṇa । sāraṁgīō karāō paḍiyāuvi jaha na cēyaṁti ॥ 64 ॥
aha tē niyajaṇaṇaṁ vāhariyā dēvi jaṁti sahāṇaṁ । niyahiyayāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ hiyaēhiṁ viṇimayaṁ kāuṁ ॥ 65 ॥
tāōvi tēsu gaēsuṁ sahasā mucchānimīliyacchīō । dharaṇīē nivaḍiyāō tō aṇukaṁpāē dēvīē ॥ 66॥
kāūṇaṁ pauṇāō bhaṇiyāō jaha imāṇa tumhēkō । thōvadiyaēhiṁ bhattā hōhī tā muṁha visāyaṁ || 67 ||
tōtā mahāpasāutti jaṁpiḍaṁ harisapulaiyasarīrā । pattā jaṇayagihammī maṇēsu tēcciya vahaṁtīō || 68 ॥
tē ya chaumēṇa kēvi valiyā jā tattha tā apicchaṁtā । gayasavvassā iva ṭhaṁti tāva dēvī imaṁ bhaṇai ॥ 69 ॥
jinabhavanād bahirbahurūparuciramīśvaragr̥hamiva ratnāḍhyam । aṣṭāpadagiriśikharē tadbhavanamasti ramaṇīyam ॥55॥
athānyadā kadācid vaitāḍhyanagāt kamalāvimalayōḥ । vidyādharyōryugalaṁ saṁprāptaṁ tatra jinabhavanē ॥ 56 ॥
pūjayitvā jinapratimā bhaktyā vanditvā vidhisāram । sāraṅgīgatagēyadhvaninā gāyatō gītāni ॥ 57 ॥
jinanāthaguṇaprakarṣasaṁbaddhāni viśuddhabandhāni । sarvatastāvatsahasōcchalitō bahalakalakalaḥ ||18||
jaya jayaśabdōnmiśrō'hamahamikayā praviśatām । vidyādharāṇāṁ caityagr̥hē jinabimbapūjārtham ॥19॥
tatastēna kalakalēna sāraṅgīravē'palapyamānē । padmāvatyā bhavanē gatvā tē gāyataḥ ||60 ||
yathā gōcaryāṁ hariṇā ākr̥ṣyantē madhuraśabdēna । tathā tadgītaravēṇa sēnaviṣēṇō dvau khacarau ॥ 61 ॥
pracchannasthitau śr̥ṇutastayōrgēyadhvanīn madhurān । yayōrīdr̥śā dhvanayō, bhavēnnanu tayō rūpamapi ॥ 62 ॥
iti buddhayā gatvā paśyantau tayō rūpaddhaḥ । īrṣyayēva madanēna samāhatau tīkṣṇa bāṇaiḥ ॥63॥
tē api tayō rūpaṁ paśyantyau tathāhatē tēna । sāraṅgyau karāt patitē api yathā na tataḥ ॥ 64 ॥
atha tau nijajanakēna vyāhr̥tau dvāvapi yātaḥ svasthānam । nijahr̥dayayōstayōrhr̥dayābhyāṁ vinimayaṁ kr̥tvā ॥ 65 ॥
tē api tayōrgatayōḥ sahasā mūrcchānimīlitākṣyau । gharaṇyāṁ nipatitē tatō'nukampayā dēvyā ||66 ||
kr̥tvā praguṇē bhāṇatē yathānayōryuvayōrēkaḥ । stōkadivasairbhartā bhaviṣyati tatō muñcataṁ viṣādam ॥67॥
tatastē mahāprasāda iti jalpitvā harṣapulakitaśarīrē । prāptē janakagr̥hē manasōstāvēva vahantyau ॥ 68 ॥
tau ca chadmanā kēnāpi valitau yāvattatra tē apaśyantau । gatasarvasvāviva tiṣṭhatastāvadēvī bhaṇati ॥ 69 ॥

ahamistha vasāmicciya na tattaā maha maṇammi jiṇadhammō । tā jai tadasaggāhaṁ muṁha pāvēmi tō tāō ॥
tattha visēṇō citiyaki jiṇadhammēṇa maha parukkhēṇa । saṁdiddhēṇaṁ, jaṁpara paricattō sō maē dēvi ! ॥71॥
sēṇō puṇō paryaṁpai susaṁniviṭṭhammi juttilakkhēhiṁ । ahariyaciṁtāmaṇikāmadhēṇukappahumasarūvē ॥72॥
jaṁ jiṇadhammē cattē saṁpajjai tēṇa natthi maha kajjaṁ । tumhārisāṇa jai puṇa iya cittaṁ jayai tā mōhō 73
tuṭṭā mammi bāhiṁ bhiuḍiṁ kāūṇa jaṁpaē dēvī । rē mūḍha ! mamaṁ mūḍhaṁ jaṁpasi tā marasi rē duṭṭha ! ||74 ||
sō bhai tumaṁ maraṇaṁ ēkaṁ dāum̐ khamā va na khamā vā । jiṇadhammē puṇa cattē bhavaṁti maraṇāītāī ॥75॥
tō sākira akuddhā sēṇaṁ ghittūṇa uppayai gayaṇē । vijayapurārāmē taṁ viḍaṁ sīhāsaṇē bhāi ॥ 76 ॥
bhadaṁ tujha mahāyasa ! supurisasayapattapaḍhamalīhasta । taṁ khamasu kavaḍavayaṇēhiṁ dūmiō jaṁ khaṇaṁ ēkaṁ ॥ 77 ॥
jāō laddhavayāsāō tujjha hiyayambhitāō kannāō । iha nayarē vijjāhararāyasudādassa taṇayāō ॥78॥
tāhi ca tujjha saṁpāḍaṇammi putraṁ maē pavanammi । bhaṇiyaṁ mahāpasāutti tō ahaṁ jāmi iya bhaṇiuṁ ॥ 79 ॥
tāṇa gihē sā vacca picchara tāō ya mayaṇavihurāō । piyarērhi sadukkhēhiṁ dhaṇiyaṁ aṇusōyamāṇīō ||
tappa kayapaḍivattī dēvī jaṁpēṛa kaha ṇu vacchāō ! । taṁ maha vayaṇaṁ vīsariya imamavatthaṁ pavannāō ? ॥ 81 ॥
sō iha āṇiō tumha hō bhaṇai khētharō kō sō । dāhiṇasēḍhīrahacakavālapahuṇō susēṇassa ॥ 82 ॥
sugahīyanāmadhēō sēṇō nāmēṇa puttavararayaṇaṁ । ēyāsu sāṇurāō ujjāṇē ciṭṭha ihēba || 83 ||
tō nagarūsavamāṇavi naravarō saharisaṁ savicchaḍō । dēvīē saha gaṁtuṁ āṇai taṁ karivarārūḍhaṁ ॥ 84 ॥
ahamatra vasāmyēva na tattvatō mama manasi jinadharmaḥ । tasmādyadi tadasadgrahaṁ muñcataṁ prāpayāmi tatastē ॥ 70 ॥
tatra viṣēṇaścintayitvā kiṁ jinadharmēṇa mama parōkṣēṇa । saṁdigdhēna, jalpati parityaktaḥ sa mayā dēvi ! ॥ 71 ॥
sēnaḥ punaḥ prajalpati susaṁniviṣṭē yuktilakṣaḥ । adharitacintāmaṇikāmadhēnukalpadrumasvarūpē ॥72॥
yajjinadharmē tyaktē saṁpadyatē tēna nāsti mama kāryam । yuṣmādr̥śāṁ yadi punariti cittaṁ jayati tatō mōhaḥ ॥ 73 ॥
tuṣṭā manasi bahibhr̥kuṭiṁ kr̥tvā jalpati dēvī । rē mūḍha ! māṁ mūḍhāṁ jalpasi tatōtriyasē rē duṣṭa ! || 74॥
sa bhaṇati tvaṁ maraṇamēkaṁ dātuṁ kṣamā vā na kṣamā vā । jinadharmē punastyaktē bhavanti maraṇānyanantāni ॥75॥
tataḥ sā kilātikruddhā sēnaṁ gr̥hītvōtpatati gaganē । vijayapurārāmē taṁ sthāpayitvā siṁhāsanē bhaṇati ॥ 76 ॥
bhadraṁ tava mahāyaśaḥ ! supuruṣaśatapatraprathama rēkhasya । tat kṣamasva kapaṭavacanaidavitō ( dūnaḥ ) yatkṣaṇamēkam ॥77॥
yē labdhāvakāśē tava hr̥dayē tē kanyē । iha nagarē vidyādhararāja sudaṁṣṭrasya tanayē ॥78॥
tābhyāṁ ca tava saṁpādanē pūrva mayā prapannē । bhaṇitaṁ mahāprasāda iti tatō'haṁ yāmīti bhāṇatvā ॥79॥
tayōgr̥hē sā vrajati paśyati tē ca madanavidhurē । pitr̥bhyāṁ saduḥkhābhyāṁ gāḍhamanuśōcantyau ॥80॥
tatpitr̥kr̥tapratipattirdēvī jalpati kathaṁ nu vatsē ! । tad mama vacanaṁ vismr̥tyēmāmavasthāṁ prapannē ? ॥81॥
sa ihānītō yuvayōrvallabhaḥ, bhaṇati khēcaraḥ kaḥ saḥ । dakṣiṇaśrēṇīrathacakravālaprabhōḥ suṣēṇasya ॥82॥
sugr̥hītanāmadhēyaḥ sēnō nāmnā putravararatnam । ētayōḥ sānurāga udyānē tiṣṭhatīhaiva ॥ 83 ॥

tāō tayavasthāō taṁ daddhuṁ amayasiṁcapāuvva । uvaladdhacēyaṇāō tiriyacchīō palōyaṁti ॥ 85 ॥
dēvī bhaṇai narēsara ! imassa lahubaṁdhuṇā visēṇēṇa । gaṁtr̥̄ṇaṁ niyanayarē sēṇassaidāruṇaṁ vasaṇaṁ ॥ 86 ॥
kahiuṁ jaṇaō jaṇaṇī sayaṇō taha pariyaṇō purajaṇō ya । duhasāyarammi chūḍhō niyamaiukarisa hiṭṭēṇa ॥

i bhaṇiūṇaṁ dēvī susēṇakhayarassa sēṇataṇukusalaṁ । kahium̐ savittharaṁ tō sahasā adaṁsaṇī jāyā ॥ 89 ॥
ētōya susēṇōvi hu puttassa amaṁgala paḍihaṇēuṁ । jiṇabhavaṇapūyaputraṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ pavaṭṭē ॥ 90 ॥
nayarajaṇōvi samaggō accaṁtavisappamāṇaāṇaṁdō | naccara gāyai hasaī ya parōpparaṁ punāī ॥ 91 ॥

avasaṭṭō saṁtō kālaṁ kālaṁtarammi kāūṇa । bhamai ciraṁ saṁsārē pāēṇaṁ dukkhaō dīṇō ॥ 94 ॥
sēṇōvi susēṇēṇaṁ jaṇaēṇaṁ ṭhāviō niyapayammi । vittavivāhō niyanayaramāgaō carimasamayammi || 95||
sēṇakhayarōvi samagaṁ vimalākamalāhi vilasiuṁ suciraṁ । samaē punaṁ paripāliūṇa taha khayararāyattaṁ ॥96॥
ūsapiūṇa jiṇanāhasāsaṇaṁ nāsaṇaṁ bhavaduhāṇaṁ । rajjadhurādharaṇakhamaṁ ṭhaviṁḍaṁ kamalāsuyaṁ rajjē ॥ 97 ॥
vimalākamalāhiṁ samaṁ anēṇaṁ pariyaṇēṇa parēṇa । dikkhaṁ pāliya pattō sāsayasōkkhammi mōkkhammi ॥ 98 ॥
tatō nagarōtsarvamājñapya naravaraḥ saharṣa savistāraḥ । dēvyā saha gatvā''nayati taṁ karivarārūḍham ॥84॥
tē tadavasthē taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā'mr̥tasikkē iva । upalabdhacētanē tiryagayau pralōkātē ॥ 85 ॥

kathayitvā janakō jananī svajanastathā parijanaḥ purajanaśca । duḥkhasāgarē kṣiptō nijamatyutkarṣahr̥ṣṭēna ॥ 87 ॥
jinavaramatē dr̥ḍhatvaṁ sēnasyā sadgrahaṁ matibhraṁśam । prakaṭayatā, tasmādyāmi tatra tēṣāṁ janayāmi dhr̥tim ॥88॥
iti bhāṇatvā dēvī suṣēṇakhacarasya sēnatanukuśalam । kathayitvā savistaraṁ tataḥ sahasā'darśanā jātā ॥89॥
itaśca suṣēṇō'pi khalu putrasyāmaṅgalaṁ pratihantum | jinabhavanapūjāpūrvaṁ vardhāpanakaṁ pravartayati ॥90॥
nagarajanō'pi samagrō'tyantavisarpadānandaḥ । nr̥tyati gāyati hasati ca parasparaṁ pūrṇapātrādiḥ ॥91॥

kamalasaraṁva virāya rāyasiṁha rāyahaṁsakayasōhaṁ । sacchapayaṁ suvisālaṁ lacchinivāsaṁ salakkhaṇiyaṁ ॥2॥
tatthatthidariyariukara ḍikaraḍataḍapāḍaṇikakharanaharō । narakēsarinaranāhō arivahuvē havvadikkha gurū ॥3॥
tattha nivasaṁti vaṇiṇō dhaṇiṇō kariṇōvva dāṇadullaliyā | unnayarvasappabhavā bhaddamahābhadanāmāṇō ||4||
jayavijayāō bhajjā tāṇaṁ paḍhamasta suṁdarō puttō । bīyassa khēmacaṁdō vissassavi vissuō jāō || 5 ॥
viṇaēṇa naēṇa pōrisēṇa, sō annayā saparivārō । suṁdarasahiō pattō ujjāṇē jaṇamaṇāṇadō || 6 ||
āṇaṁdaguṁdalēṇaṁ lalai līlāvaīhiṁ parikaliō । naṁdaṇavaṇammi iṁdōvva accharāviṁdapariyariō ||7||
aha tassa - bālamitō suṁdaranāmā adūradēsammi । abhiramamāṇō ahiṇā daṭṭhō caraṇaṁgulīdēsē ||8||
tō takkhaṇēṇa khaliyā tassa gaī nivaḍiō mahīvaḍē । maulipalōyaṇajuyalō jhaḍatti nīlacchavī jāō ||
hāhāvē paṭṭē pattō tassaṁtiyaṁ saparivārō । sō khēmacaṁda mittō kiṁkiti payaṁpirō sahasā ||10|
tō taṁ taha dahūṇaṁ kēūramaṇi jalēṇa ōhalihī । jā tassa chaṁṭaṇatthaṁ tā kēūrō ahī jāō || 11||
tō dabbhaṁ gahiūṇaṁ jā uṁjissai sayaṁ sarēūṇa | gāruḍamaṁta tāva ya taṇasaṁkhā vichiyā jāyā ॥ 12॥
tā khuhiyamaṇō ciṁtā jāva uvāya taō ya kēṇāvi । kahiyē jahā pasiddhō gāruḍiō ēsa maha mittaṁ ॥
dō bhāyarō ya ēē puvvi dēsatarammi paḍhiūṇa । gāruḍamaṁtāīyē vāliyā niyadē sagamaṇatthaṁ ॥ 14 ॥
anyānyadarśanākāṅkṣā naṭita hr̥dayasya sundarasyēva । jāyatē dharmabhraṁśastatpratyayitaśca saṁsāraḥ ||1||
kamalasara iva virājati rājagr̥haṁ rājahaṁsakr̥taśēōbham । svaccha prajaṁ (payaḥ) suviśālaṁ lakṣmīnivāsaṁ salākṣaṇikam ॥
tatrāsti dr̥ptaripukaraṭikaraṭataṭapāṭanai kakharanakharaḥ । narakēsarinaranāthō'rivadhūvaidhavyadīkṣāguruḥ ॥ 3 ॥
tatra nivasatō vaṇijau dhaninau kariṇāviva dānadurlalitau । unnatavaṁśaprabhavau bhadramahābhadrānāmānau ||4||
jayāvijayē bhāyēṁ tayōḥ prathamasya sundaraḥ putraḥ । dvitīyasya kṣēmacandrō viśvasyāpi viśrutō jātaḥ || 5 ||
vinayēna nayēna pauruṣēṇa, sō'nyadā saparivāraḥ । sundarasahitaḥ prāpta udyānē janamanaānandaḥ ||6||
ānandagundalēna lalati līlāvatībhiḥ parikalitaḥ । nandanavana indra ivāpsarōvr̥ndaparikaritaḥ ||7||
atha tasya bālamitraṁ sundaranāmā'dūradēśē । abhiramamāṇamahinā daṣṭaṁ caraṇāṅgulīdēśē ॥ 8 ॥
tatastatkṣaṇēna skhalitā tasya gatirnipatitō mahīṣpr̥ṣṭhē । mukulitalōcanayugalō jhaṭiti nīlacchavijatiḥ ॥9॥
hāhāvē pravr̥ttē prāptaṁ tasyāntikaṁ saparivāram । tatkṣēmacandramitvaṁ kiṁ kimiti prajalpitr̥ sahasā ॥ 10 ॥
tatastat tathā dr̥ṣṭvā kēyūramaṇi jalēnāvagharṣiṣyatē । yāvattasya sēcanārthaṁ tāvatkēyūrō'hirjātaḥ ॥ 11 ॥
tatō darbha gr̥hītvā yāvad yōkṣyati svayaṁ smr̥tvā । gāruḍamantraṁ tāvacca tr̥ṇasaṁkhyā vr̥ścikā jātāḥ ॥ 12 ॥
tadā kṣubdhamanāścintayati yāvadupāyaṁ tataśca kēnāpi । kathitaṁ yathā prasiddhō gāruḍika ēṣa mama mitram ॥ 13 ॥
dvau bhrātarau tau pūrva dēśāntarē paṭhitvā । gāruḍamantrādikaṁ valitau nijadēśagamanārtham ॥ 14 ॥

pattā mahāaranē jalapāṇaḍhā naīdahaṁ caliyā । diṭṭhō tammajjhāō vāha vayaṁtō mahāsappō ॥ 15 ॥
tasya uvari diṭṭhō kasiṇataṇū maṇimaūhapiṁjariō । gurudappō lahusappō tō taṁ picchēvi lahubhāyā ||
bhaṇai imāṇaṁ baṁdhava ! gamaṇaṁ khillēmi kaṭṭiuṁ rēhaṁ । tō bhaṇiō jidvēṇaṁ na ēsa tuha mannaē āṇaṁ ॥ 17 ॥
lahuō aippayaṁḍō tālauḍassāvi garuyavisavēō । khattiyajāī ēsō na kamai ēyassa tā maṁtō ॥ 18 ॥
iya tannivāriēṇavi āṇaṁ dāūṇa kaḍhiyā rēhā । tō jō garuō sappōṁ sō na calai tēppaēsāō ॥ 19 ॥
tō tappaṭṭīō lahuō uttara pamhusēi taṁ rēhaṁ । niyadēhaṁ lōlēuṁ puṇōvi tappaṭṭhimāruhiō ॥ 20 ॥
caliō ya tapabhāvā vāhaṇasappō, iō ya hatthīṇaṁ । galagajjigaruyasakō ucchaliō bhariyanahavivarō ॥
tō bhaṇiō jiṭṭēṇaṁ vaccha ! samāgaccha rukkhamāruhiuṁ । rakkhāmō appāṇaṁ ēyāō hatthizahāō ||22||
annaṁ ca visēṇa imassa bhāviyaṁ salilamimamahaṁ mannē । jaṁ jalavannaviruddhā imammi ainīlimā bhāi || 23॥
tā picchāmō ēyaṁ karizaha ki imaṁ jalaṁ piyaṛa । taha pīyammivi kiṁ hōi, tē taō rukkhamārūḍhā ||24||
tō siṁhuta karijū piō karēūṇa | kalahāimukkaladiṁ ṭhāvaṁtō niyayakuṁbhammi ||25||
siṁhābhimuhaṁ dhāvara jūhavaī jāva tāva ucchalium̐ । sajjiyakamō sa sīhō caḍiō kuṁbhatthalē tassa ||26||
dhūṇiō ya tēṇa tattō paḍiō dharaṇīē caṁpiō kariṇā । pāēṇa gayappāṇō tattō harisēṇa gulaguliyaṁ ॥27॥
kāraṇīhi kalahēhiṁ ya khaṇamēkkaṁ harisaguṁdalaṁ kāuṁ । tattō aitisiēhiṁ sariō sariyādahō jāva ||28||
prāptau mahāraṇyē jalapānārthaṁ nadīdrahaṁ calitau । dr̥ṣṭastanmadhyād bahitrajan mahāsarpaḥ ॥ 15॥
tasya cōpari dr̥ṣṭaḥ kr̥ṣṇatanurmaṇimayūkhapiñjaritaḥ । gurudapōṁ laghusarpastatastaṁ dr̥ṣṭrā laghubhrātā ॥ 16 ॥
bhaṇatyanayōrbāndhava ! gamanaṁ skhalayāmi kr̥ṣṭā rēkhām । tatō bhaṇitō jyēṣṭhēna naiṣa tava manyata ājñām ॥ 17 ॥
laghukō'tipracaṇḍastālapuṭādapi guruviṣavēgaḥ । kṣattriyajātirēṣa na krāmatyētasya tasmānmantraḥ ॥ 18 ॥
iti tannivāritēnāpyājñāṁ dattvā kr̥ṣṭā rēkhā । tatō yō guruḥ sarpaḥ sa na calati tatpradēśāt ॥ 19 ॥
tatastatpr̥ṣṭhatō laghuruttīrya pramuṣṇāti tāṁ rēkhām । nijadēhaṁ lōṭhayitvā punarapi tatpr̥ṣṭhamārūḍhaḥ ॥20॥
calitaśca tatprabhāvād vāhanasarpaḥ, itaśca hastinām । galagarjiguruśabda ucchalitō bhr̥tanabhōvivaraḥ ॥21॥
tatō bhaṇitō jyēṣṭhēna vatsa ! samāgaccha vr̥kṣamāruhya | rakṣāva ātmānamētasmād hastiyūthāt ॥22॥
anyacca viṣēṇāsya bhāvitaṁ salilamidamahaṁ manyē । yajjalavarṇaviruddhō'sminnatinīlimā bhāti ||23||
tasmātpaśyāva ētatkariyūthaṁ kimidaṁ jalaṁ pibati । tathā pītē'pi kiṁ bhavati, tau tatō vr̥kṣamārūḍhau ॥ 24 ॥
tataḥ siṁhōttrastaṁ kariyūthaṁ pr̥ṣṭhataḥ kr̥tvā । kalabhādimuktapurīṣaṁ sthāpayannijakumbhē ॥25॥

dhūnitaśca tēna tataḥ patitō dharaṇyāṁ campitaḥ kariṇā । pādēna gataprāṇastatō harṣēṇa gulagulitam ||27||

supāsanāha - cariśrammi-
tō jūhavaī aggē hōūṇaṁ pāṇiyaṁ parikkhēi । tō tiṇayaṇagalanīlaṁ taṁ dadrūṇaṁ nivārēi 1129 ।।
savrvvapi taō jūha, sayaṁ tu gacchēi vaṇaniguṁjammi | taddahapaccāsanē mōḍēuṁ viḍaviṇō ḍālaṁ ||30||
kassavi, visaghāyatthaṁ vivēi nīrammi takkhaṇādēva । harahāsahāradhavalaṁ jāyaṁ tō nivvisa nīraṁ ॥ 31 ॥
tō taṁ nivasannāē āhūyaṁ hatthiṇā niyaṁ jūhaṁ । sicchāē piyai jalaṁ takkīlāē pakīlēuṁ ॥ 32॥
nīhariḍaṁ nīrāō gayaṁ gaiṁdāṇaṁ jr̥hamannattha । uttariya taruvarāō tīrē nīrassa saṁpattā ||33||
sajjagahiyayasaricchaṁ sacchamaucchaṁ jalaṁ piēūṇa । taṁ ōsahīē valayaṁ vittaṇaṁ patthiyā ēttha ॥ 34॥
āgacchaṁtēhi pahē gāruḍiyā ṇijjiyā tahāṇēgē । visavāriyāvi bahavē uṭṭhaviyā ōsahivasēṇa ॥ 35 ॥
tampajjhāō jiṭṭō ēsa iha āgaō maha sagāsē । kālaḍasipi mannē jīvāvēuṁ samatthōti ॥ 36॥
tō sēṭṭhimaō paṇa nariṁda! sajjīkarēsu maha mittaṁ । kāūṇa maha pasāyaṁ, lakkhaṁ kaṇayassa dāvissaṁ ॥ 37॥
tō tēṇōsahivalayaṁ ōhaliḍaṁ sīyalēṇa salilēṇa । sō suṁdarō suhatthaṁ jhaḍatti jā chaṁṭiō tāva || 38 ॥
lōhamayatavayatāviyatillachaḍāhiva nīraviṁdrahiṁ । savvasarīrē jāyā phuḍiyāō vidusaṁkhāō ||39||
naya kavi sē visēsō jāō jāyā ya navari gurupīḍā । tō sōvi asajjhō majjha ēsa iya bhaṇiya nīhariō॥
tō annēṇaṁ kēṇavi kappaḍiō kōvi āṇiō tattha । kahiyā ya khēmacaṁdassa maṁtasattīvi tassa imā ॥ 41 ॥
niyayāō nagarāō gāmaṁtarapatthiyassa majjha suō। avayariō turayāō sarīracitānimittēṇa ॥ 42 ॥
tō caraṇacapiēṇaṁ ḍasiō sappēṇa garuyadappēṇa । maha picchaṁtassa taō paḍiō dharaṇīē adharō sō ॥ 43 ॥
tatō yūthapatiragrē bhūtvā pānīyaṁ parīkṣatē । tatastrinayanagalanīlaṁ tad dr̥ṣṭvā nivārayati ||29||
sarvamapi tatō yūthaṁ, svayaṁ tu gacchati vananikujē । tadrahapratyāsannē marditvā viṭapinaḥ śākhām ॥30॥
kasyāpi, viṣaghātārthaṁ kṣipati nīrē tatkṣaṇādēva । harahāsahāradhavalaṁ jātaṁ tatō nirviṣaṁ nīram ॥31॥
tatastad nijasaṁjñayā''hr̥taṁ hastinā nijaṁ yūtham । svēcchayā pibati jalaṁ tatkrīḍayā prakrīḍya ॥32॥
niḥsr̥tya nīrād gataṁ gajēndrāṇāṁ yūthamanyatra | uttīrya taruvarāt tīrē nīrasya saṁprāptau ॥ 33 ॥
sajjanahr̥dayasadr̥śaṁ svacchamatucchaṁ jalaṁ pītvā । tadōṣadhēvalayaṁ gr̥hītvā prasthitāvatra ||34||
āgacchadbhayāṁ pārtha gāruḍakā nirjitāstathā'nēkē । viṣaghāritā api bahava utthāpitā ōṣadhivaśēna ॥ 35 ॥
tanmadhyājjyēṣṭha ēṣa ihāgatō mama sakāśē । kāladr̥ṣṭamapi manyē jīvayituṁ samartha iti ॥ 36 ॥
tataḥ śrēṣṭhitaḥ prabhaṇati narēndra ! sajjīkuruṣva mama mitram । kr̥tvā mayi prasādaṁ, lakṣaṁ kanakasya dāpayiṣyē ॥
tatastēnauṣadhivalayamavanr̥ṣya śītalēna salilēna । sa sundaraḥ sukhārthaṁ jhaṭiti yāvat siktastāvat ॥38॥
lōhamaya kaṭāhatāpitatailacchābhiriva nīrabindubhiḥ । sarvaśarīrē jātāḥ sphōṭikā bindusaṁkhyāḥ ॥ 39॥
na ca kō'pi tasya viśēṣō jātō jātā ca kēvalaṁ gurupīḍā । tataḥ sō'pyasādhyō mamaiṣa iti bhaṇitvā niḥsr̥taḥ ॥
tatō'nyēna kēnāpi kārpaṭikaḥ kō'pyānītastatra । kathitā ca kṣēmacandrāya mantraśaktirapi tasyēyam ॥ 41 ॥
nijāda nagarād grāmāntaraprasthitasya mama sutaḥ । avatīrṇasturagāccharīra cintānimittēna ॥ 42 ॥

136
vāhariyaṁ ca maē tō na kōvi āgacchaī jaṇābhāvā । tō niyaguruāṇāē maēvi sō uṁjiō tahavi ॥ 44॥
anicēṭṭhō diṭṭhō mautti sō manniḍaṁ maē nayarā । āhūō sayalajaṇō samāgaō garuyasāmaggiṁ ॥ 45 ॥
kāū siviyāē vihiyā niggamaṇapamuhasōhāvi । titthābhimuhaṁ nīō' ghaṇatūraravēṇa taṁ sōuṁ ॥ 46 ॥
kappaḍiō pahiyajuō muṇiuṁ tūrassa saravisēsēṇa । pabhaṇai ahō ! aṇāhō jīvaṁtō ḍajjhihī varaō ||
tō taṁ vayaṇaṁ sōuṁ pahiēṇaṁ pēsiō niō purisō । amha sayāsē ajjavi pajjālēmō na jāva ciyaṁ ॥ 48॥
tō tēṇaṁ gaṁtūṇaṁ tavvayaṇaṁ vimhayāvahaṁ amha । kahiyē, bhaṇiyā ya tahā ēmēva paḍikkhaha muhutaṁ ॥ 49 ॥
ēvaṁ ṭhiyāṇa tumhēṁ kira paḍiyāraṁ karissara kōvi । ēttō kappaḍiēṇaṁ bhaṇiō pahiō jahā tumha || 50 ॥
saṁvalayamatthi, sō bhai asthi dahisāliōyaṇakaraṁbō । bhuttō sō tēṇa taō suttavivva uṭṭhē ॥ 51 ॥
majjha suō kaṭṭhēhiṁ udvaviōvi hu taō ya amhēhiṁ । tassa sayāsa nīō vajjaṁtaṇavajjatūrēhiṁ ॥ 52 ॥
pārasu pāḍiō tassa taha ya sayalēṇa sayaṇavaggēṇa । jaṁ jassa āsi pāsē ābharaṇaṁ tēṇa taṁ dinaṁ ॥53॥
pahiraṇa taō bhaṇiō kappaḍiō pasiya kahasu maha ēyaṁ । bhuttō taē karaṁbō ēyassa viṁsa kahaṁ nahaṁ ? ॥
savvōvi vimyāulahiyaō pāsaṭṭhiō jaṇō bhaṇai । juttamimēṇaṁ puḍhaṁ tā tēṇuvvakkiuṁ vamiō ॥55॥
hālāhalapuṁjō iva karaṁbaō nīlavannaduppicchō । tō jaṁpara savvajaṇō arcitamāhappa ! tujha namō ॥ 56 ॥
para muvayārī ēsō pahiōvi ya iya ṭhavivi niyacittē । aigauravēṇa nīyā dōvi maē niyayagēhammi ॥57॥
tataścaraṇacampitēna daṣṭō sarpēṇa gurudarpaṇa । mayi paśyati tataḥ patitō dharaṇyāmadharaḥ saḥ ॥ 43 ॥
vyāhr̥taṁ ca mayā tatō na kō'pyāgacchati janābhāvāt । tatō nijagurvājñayā mayāpi sa yōjitastathāpi ॥ 44॥
atiniśrēṣṭō dr̥ṣṭō mr̥ta iti sa matvā mayā nagarāt । āhūtaḥ sakalajanaḥ samāgatō gurusāmagrīm ॥ 49 ॥
kr̥tvā śivikāyāṁ vihitā nirgamanapramukhaśōbhāpi । tīrthābhimukhaṁ nītō ghanatūraravēṇa taṁ śrutvā ॥ 46 ॥
kāpaṭikaḥ pathikayutō jñātvā tūrasya svaraviśēṣēṇa । prabhaṇatyahō ! anāthō jīvan dhakṣyatē varākaḥ || 47॥
tatastadvacanaṁ śrutvā pathikēna prēṣitō nijaḥ puruṣaḥ । asmākaṁ sakāśē'dyāpi prajvālayāmō na yāvaccitām॥48॥
tatastēnaṁ gatvā tadvacanaṁ vismayāvahamasmākam । kathitaṁ bhaṇitāśca tathaivamēva pratīkṣadhvaṁ muhūrtam ॥49॥
ēvaṁ sthitēṣu yuṣmāsu kila pratikāraṁ kariṣyati kō'pi । itaḥ kāryaṭikēna bhaṇitaḥ pathikō yathā tava ॥ 50॥
śambalamasti, sa bhaṇatyasti dadhiśālyōdanakarambaḥ । muktaḥ sa tēna tataḥ suptavyuttha ivōttiṣṭhati ॥51॥
mama sutaḥ kaṣṭhairutthāpitō'pi khalu tataścāsmābhiḥ । tasya sakāśaṁ nītō vādyamānānavadyatūraiḥ ||12||
pādayōḥ pātitastasya tathā ca sakalēna svajanavargēṇa । yad yasyāsīt pārśvē ābharaṇaṁ tēna tad dattam ॥53॥
pathikēna tatō bhaṇita: kārpaṭikaḥ prasadya kathaya mamaitat । bhuktastvayā karamba ētasya viṣaṁ kathaṁ naṣṭam ? ॥54॥
sarvō'pi vismayākulahr̥dayaḥ pārśvasthitō janō bhaṇati । yuktamanēna pr̥ṣṭaṁ tatastēnōdgīrya vamitaḥ ॥55॥
hālāhalapuñja iva karambakō nīlavarṇadurdarśaḥ । tatō jalpati sarvajanō'cintyamāhātmya ! tubhyaṁ namaḥ || 56 ॥
paramōpakāryēṣa pathikō'pi cēti sthāpayitvā nijacittē । atigauravēṇa nītau dvāvapi mayā nijagēhē ||17||

supāsanāha cariammi-
saṁmāṇiūṇa bahuyaṁ suvannavatthāiēhiṁ vatthūhiṁ । mōkaliō sō pahiō kappaḍiō puṇa niyammi gihē ॥ 58 ॥
dhariō kavi diṇāī saṁpaṛa puṇa paṭṭiō sadēsamma । bōlāviḍaṁ ya ēēṇa saha ahaṁ ēttha saṁpattō ॥ 59 ॥
ētthavi nisuyā vattā jaha daṭṭhō suṁdarō visaharēṇa । tō ēsa ihāṇīō maēti sō bhaṇai suṭṭu kayaṁ । । 60॥
kappaḍiēṇa tava ya pauṁjiō puvvavanniyapaōgō । nahu thēvōvi visēsō saṁjāō tassa visavisaē ||
iya jaṁ visasamā kijjai annaṁpi tassa taṁ savvaṁ । hōi aṇatthaphalaṁ ciya aphalaṁ vā jāyaē kiṁpi ॥
tā ādinnō phunō jā ciṭṭhā khēmacaṁdavaṇippavarō । tā kēṇavi āgaṁtuṁ nivēiyaṁ ērisaṁ tassa ॥ 63 ॥
jaha cūyarukkhahiṭṭā diṭṭhō muṇipuṁgavō maē ēkō । nāsagganisiyadiṭṭhī aidhammiṭṭhō paramajōgī || 64 ॥
tō tassa pāyamūlē khippaḍa ēsō bhaṇijjau ēvaṁ । jaha sappadaṭṭamēyaṁ jīvāvasu paramakāruṇiya ! || 65 ||
tō tavvayaṇāṇaṁtaramārōvēūṇa pavarasiviyāē । nīō sāhusayāsaṁ tayabhimuhaṁ bhaṇiyamēyaṁ ca ॥ 66 ॥
panavasi dayādhammaṁ jai sammaṁ muṇasi jiṇamayarahassaṁ । tā sāmi ! majjha mittaṁ jīvāvasu iya nisāmēuṁ ॥
naya kiṁpi muṇī jaṁpara jā tā jakkhēṇa avayariya pattē । bhaṇiyaṁ imēṇa mahavāsaṭhāṇakaṁkēlliṇō ḍālaṁ ॥
bhaggaṁ, tō ruṭṭēṇaṁ imassa ēyaṁ kayaṁ maē savvaṁ । muṇicaraṇarēṇutilayaṁ tā bhālē kuṇaha yassa ॥ 69 ॥
jēsujjhati mucca visaviyaṇāē viṇāvi jattēṇa । jamhā mahāṇubhāvāṇa daṁsaṇaṁ savvaduhaharaṇaṁ ॥ 70 ॥
ēsō mahāṇubhāvō nissaṁgō nimmamō nirāraṁbhō । maṁtataṁtāiviraō niraō nirayappahavibhaṁgē || 71 ॥
tō tēṇaṁ hiṭṭēṇaṁ kathaṁ tacaiva sōvi visamukō । uṭṭhēḍaṁ takkhaṇaṁ ciya suttaviva vimhaiō || 72 ||
saṁmānya bahu suvarṇavastrādikairvastubhiḥ । visr̥ṣṭaḥ sa pathikaḥ kāpaṭikaḥ punarnijē gr̥hē ||18||
dhr̥taḥ katyapi dināni saṁprati punaḥ prasthitaḥ svadēśē । gamayituṁ caitēna sahāhamatra saṁprāptaḥ ||19||
atrāpi śrutā vārtā yathā daṣṭaḥ sundarō viṣadharēṇa । tata ēṣa ihānītō mayēti sa bhaṇati suṣṭhu kr̥tam ॥ 60 ॥
kārpaṭikēna tathaiva ca prayuktaḥ pūrvavarṇitaprayōgaḥ । naca stōkō'pi viśēṣaḥ saṁjātastasya viṣaviṣayē ॥ 61॥
iti yad
viṣaśamanārthaṁ kriyatē'nyadapi tasya tat sarvam । bhavatyanarthaphalamēvāphalaṁ vā jāyatē kimapi ||2||
tasmādādīrṇāpūrṇō yāvatiṣṭhati kṣēmacandravaṇikpravaraḥ । tāvatkēnāpyāgatya nivēditamadr̥śaṁ tasmai ॥ 63 ॥
yathā cūtavr̥kṣasyādhō dr̥ṣṭō munipuṅgavō mayaikaḥ । nāsāgranyastadr̥ṣṭiratidharmiṣṭhaḥ paramayōgī ॥ 64 ॥
tatastasya pādamūlē kṣipyatāmēṣa bhaṇyatāmēvam । yathā sarpadaṣṭamētaṁ jīvaya paramakāruṇika ! || 65 ॥
tatastadvacanānantaramārōpya pravara śivikāyām । nītaḥ sādhusakāśaṁ tadabhimukhaṁ bhaṇitamētacca ॥ 66 ॥
prajñāpayasi dayādharma yadi samyagjānāsi jinamatarahasyam । tadā svāmin! mama mitraṁ jīvayēti niśamya ॥ 67॥
naca kimapi munirjalpati yāvattāvad yakṣēṇāvatīrya patrē | bhaṇitamanēna madvāsasthānakaṅkēllēḥ śākhā ॥68॥
tatō ruṣṭēnāsyaitat kr̥taṁ mayā sarvam । municaraṇarēṇutilakaṁ tasmād bhālē kurutaitasya ॥ 69 ॥
yēnaiṣa jhaṭiti mucyatē viṣavēdanayā vināpi yatnēna । yasmānmahānubhāvānāṁ darśanaṁ sarvaduḥkhaharaṇam ॥ 70 ॥
ēṣa mahānubhāvō nissaṅkī nirmamō nirārambhaḥ । mantratantrādiviratō niratō nirayapathāvabhaṅgē ॥71॥

pucchara kimēsa lōō miliō ēgattha, kiṁva kīlāō । nacaṇagēyappamuhāō tāō sahasōvasatāō ? ||
॥
tō kahiē vr̥ttaṁtē vittharaō sō muṇi namasēi । muṇiṇāvi dhammalābhiya dhammō kahiuṁ samādattō ॥ 74 ॥
bhō bhō bhavvā ! bhavasārammi bahukumayanīrabhariyammi । kicchēṇa lahai buḍḍō subōhinicchiḍabōhitthaṁ ।
labdhaṁti surasuhāī labdhaṁti nariṁdavidariddhīō । naya bhō subōhirayaṇaṁ labbhai micchattatamaharaṇaṁ ॥ 76 ॥
bahupunnapāvaṇijjaṁ rajjaṁpi labhijja cakkavaṭṭīṇaṁ । na uṇō subōhibahulābhasaṁgayaṁ narabhavaṁ vimalaṁ ॥ 77 ॥
suci subōhilābhō jattha jiṇō dēvayā vigayarāō । paṁcamahavvayadhārī gurūvi, jīvāitattāṇa ॥ 78 ॥
sammaṁ ca parinnāṇaṁ sammattaṁ taṁ ca biṁti jiṇavasahā । saṁkāidōsarahiyaṁ taṁ pālitā suhīhōha || 79 ॥
saṁkā puṭṭhiā kahiyā tēsiṁ savitrā muṇiṇā । annannadaṁsaṇāṇaṁ ahilāsō hōi puṇa kaṁkhā ||80||
sā sammattadharēhiṁ dūraṁ dūrēṇa hōi caiyavvā । niravajjarayaṇalābhē kō kāyamaṇī ahilasēi ? || 81 ॥
iccāivittharē sāhiyammi sammattamūlajiṇadhammē । vaṇikhēmacaṁda suṁdarapamuhā bahavō jaṇā tattha ॥ 82 ॥
muṇipāyakayara sammaṁ sammattamaha pavajjittā । vajjittā micchattaṁ niyaniyagēhēsu saṁpattā ||83 ||
pāliti niraiyāraṁ, aha annayā kōḍagēṇa cavalattā । bhikkhūṇa maḍhaṁ gaṁtuṁ taddhammaṁ suṁdarī sui || 84 ॥
mittēṇa vāriōvi hu na ṭhāi bhai ya kahaṁti ēēvi । jhāṇaṁ nāṇaṁ nivvāṇasāhaṇaṁ ēttha kimattaṁ ? ॥ 85 ॥
tō bhai khēmacaṁdō iṁdiyavasayāṇa jhāṇanāṇāī | gayamajjaṇatulāī ēsō ya imō samuvasō || 86 ॥
tatastēna hr̥ṣṭēna kr̥taṁ tathaiva sō'pi viṣamuktaḥ । utthāya tatkṣaṇamēva suptavyuttha iva vismitaḥ ॥72॥
pr̥cchati kimēṣa lōkō milita ēkatra, kiṁvā krīḍāḥ । nartanagēyapramukhāstāḥ sahasōpaśāntāḥ ? || 73 ॥
tataḥ kathitē vr̥ttāntē vistarataḥ sa muniṁ namasyati । munināpi dharmalābhamuktvā dharmaḥ kathayituṁ samārabdhaḥ ॥74॥
bhō bhō bhavyāḥ ! bhavasāgarē bahukumatanīrabhr̥tē । kr̥cchrēṇa labhatē magnaḥ subōdhiniśchidrayānapātram ॥75॥
labhyantē surasukhāni labhyantē narēndravr̥ndarddhayaḥ । na ca bhōḥ subōdhiratnaṁ labhyatē mithyātvatamōharaṇam ॥ 76 ॥
bahupuṇyaprāpaṇīyaṁ rājyamapi labhēta cakravartinām । na punaḥ subōdhi bahulābhasaṁgataṁ narabhavaṁ vimalam ॥77॥
sa ēva subōdhilābhō yatra jinō dēvatā vigatarāgaḥ । pañcamahāvratadhārī gururapi, jīvāditattvānām ॥ 78 ॥
samyak ca parijñānaṁ samyaktvaṁ tacca bruvanti jinavr̥ṣabhāḥ । śaṅkādidōṣarahitaṁ tatpālayantaḥ sukhībhavata ॥ 79॥
śaṅkā pūrvōddiṣṭaśa kathitā tēṣāṁ savistarā muninā । anyānyadarśanānāmabhilāṣō bhavati punaḥ kāṅkṣā ॥ 80॥
sā samyaktvadharairdūraṁ dūrēṇa bhavati tyaktavyā । niravadyaratnalābhē kaḥ kācamaṇīnabhilaṣati ? ॥81॥
ityādivistarē kathitē samyaktvamūla jinadharmē । vaṇikkṣēmacandrasundarapramukhā bahavō janāstatra ॥ 82 ॥
munipādapaṅkajasyāgrē samyak samyaktvamatha prapadya । varjayitvā mithyātvaṁ nijanijagēhēṣu saṁprāptāḥ ॥83॥.
pālayanti niraticāram, athānyadā kautukēna capalatvāt । bhikṣūṇāṁ maṭhaṁ gatvā taddharma sundaraḥ śr̥ṇōti ॥ 84॥
mitrēṇa vāritō'pi khalu na tiṣṭhati bhaṇati ca kathayanyētē'pi । dhyānaṁ jñānaṁ nirvāṇa sādhanamatra kimayuktam 1 85
tatō bhaṇati kṣēmacandra indriyavaśagānāṁ dhyānajñānē । gajamajjanatulyē ēṣa cāyaṁ samupadēśaḥ ॥ 86 ॥

supāsanāha variśrammi-
" maṇunnaṁ bhōyaṇaṁ bhucā maṇunnaṁ sayaṇāsaṇaṁ । maṇunnaṁsi agāraṁsi maṇunaṁ jhāyaē muṇī ||
mr̥dvī śayyā prātarutthāya pēyā madhyē bhaktaṁ pānakaṁ cāparā । drākṣākhaṇḍaṁ śarkarā cārdharātrē mōkṣaścāntē śākyaputrēṇa dr̥ṣṭa:"
aṇusōyappaṭṭhāṇaṁ imaṁ khu saṁsārakāraṇaṁ paramaṁ । iṁdiyajayammi tamhā sahalāī nāṇacaraṇāī || 87 ||
tā mitta ! tumaṁ bhulō rīrīkaṇaēsa tullakayamullō | vēruliyakāyatullattajaṁpirō taha hasijjihasi ||88 ||
ēvaṁ niruttarō sō kaōvi mittēṇa khēmacaṁdēṇaṁ । annannadaṁsaṇagaha asarahaṁ nō paricaya || 89 ॥
tō annayā kayāī nīō sūrīṇa pāyamūlammi । tāṇaṁ ca tēṇa kahiyaṁ tassa sarūvaṁ purā āsi || 10||
tō tēhiṁ kahaṁtērhi dhammaṁ, patthāvamāṇiuṁ bhaṇiyā । kaṁkhāē bahudausā kahā ya ēsā samārā ॥ 91 ॥
tathāhi;
vittasihaṁḍipasūyāvahāsiyaṁ vibuhavihiyamaṇatōsa । tidivaṁva gōvaijuyaṁ sirikaliyaṁ gayapuraṁ asthi ॥92॥
dariyārisalahapasarassa pāvagō tattha asthi atthīṇaṁ । dālidadārudahaṇikapaccalō bhūvaī rāyā ॥ 93 ॥
tassa samīvē kavi hu kēyavisayāō āgaō suhaḍō । bhuyamittabalī maggai sō lakkhaṁ varisavittīē ॥94॥
tō bhūvaiṇā bhaṇiō kā sattī, sō bhaṇai maha natthi । sattī kāvi hu, sukayaṁ tu asthi taṁ jēṇa diṭṭhō si ||
tō tassa vaggadhārī vinnavai narēsaraṁ paṇamiūṇa | maha pahuṇō guṇagaṇaguruṇō sattidugaṁ iyarajaṇadulahaṁ ॥96॥
hārēi na saṁgāmē taha buddhī kāvi sā, imō jīē । sattuṁ uppannavirōhakāraṇaṁpi hu pasāēi ||97||
tō dāūṇa pasāyaṁ kiṁcimmattaṁ samapiḍaṁ sinaṁ । viṁjhāyalavisamapaēsavāsiṇō samaravīrassa || 98 |
manōjña bhōjanaṁ bhuktvā manōjñaṁ śayanāsanam । manōjñē'gārē manōjñaṁ dhyāyati muniḥ ॥
anuśrōtaḥ prasthānamidaṁ khalu saṁsārakāraṇaṁ paramam । indriyajayē tasmāt saphalē jñānacaraṇē ॥ 87 ॥
tasmād
mittra ! tvaṁ skhalitō rīrīkanakayōḥ kr̥tatulyamūlyaḥ । vaiḍūryakā ca tulyatvajalpitā tathā hasiṣyasē ॥ 88 ॥
ēvaṁ niruttaraḥ sa kr̥tō'pi mittrēṇa kṣēmacandrēṇa ! anyānyadarśanagrahāsadgrahaṁ na parityajati ॥89॥
tatō'nyadā kadācid nītaḥ sūrīṇāṁ pādamūlē । tēbhyaśca tēna kathitaṁ tasya svarūpaṁ purāsīt ॥ 90 ॥
tatastaiḥ kathayadbhirdharmaṁ, prastāvamānīya bhaṇitāḥ । kāṅkṣāyā bahudōṣāḥ kathā caiṣā samārabdhā ॥ 91 ॥
vr̥ttaśikhaṇḍiprasūtāvabhāsitaṁ vibudhavihitamanastōṣam । tridivamiva gōpatiyutaṁ śrīkalitaṁ gajapuramāsīt ॥92॥
dr̥ptāriśalabhaprasarasya pāvakastatrāstyarthinām । dāridryadārudahanaikapratyalō bhūpatī rājā ॥ 93 ॥
tasya samīpē kō'pi khalu kētaka viṣayāgataḥ subhaṭaḥ । bhujamātrabalā mārgayati sa lakṣaṁ varṣavr̥ttyā ॥94॥
tatō bhūpatinā bhaṇitaḥ kā śaktiḥ sa bhaṇati mama nāsti । śaktiḥ kāpi khalu sukr̥taṁ tvasti tvaṁ yēna dr̥ṣṭōsi ॥
tatastasya khaḍgadhārī vijñapayati narēśvaraṁ praṇamya । mama prabhōrguṇagaṇagurōḥ śaktidvikamitarajana durlabham ॥96॥
hārayati na saṁgrāmē tathā buddhiḥ kāpi sā, ayaṁ yayā । śatrumutpannavirōdhakāraṇamapi khalu prasādayati ॥97||
16. kēyai, kha. kēvaya. ।

suṁdarakahā ।
143
pallīvaiṇō aipavarasūranibbhiccabhiccavaggassa । laddhajayasta raṇēsu uvari sō pēsiō rannā ॥ 99 ॥
āsāṇataramēva patthiō sō ṭhiō sasīmāē । tassa visajjai dūyaṁ sō taṁ gaṁtuṁ bhaṇai ēvaṁ || 100॥
sōhaḍasuhaḍō tuha uvari pēsiō naravarēṇa bhūvaiṇā । tō tarasa kuṇasu sēvaṁ jai icchasi appaṇō kusalaṁ ॥
sō bhai tujjha jīhāchēyaṁ na hu kāravēmi duutti । tō gaṁtuṁ iya pabhaṇasu sōhaḍaṁ majjha vayaṇēṇaṁ ॥ 102 ॥
ēsō hamāgaucciya tā pavisēuṁ kayaṁtavayaṇammi । jai mahasi tā paḍikkhasu ēttha ṭhiō caiva diṇadasagaṁ ॥
dūrṇa paḍavaṇē kahiē tō sōhaḍō taō caliō । pallivaīvi sasinnō miliyāī dōnivi balāī ||
tō sōhaḍēṇa bhaṇiyā niyasuhaḍā majjha piṭṭabhāyammi । parasinnapahāra। gōyara mmi bhō ciṭṭhaha niyaṁtā ॥ 105 ॥
sō pallivaī citai uvēhiō ēsa niyayasinēṇa । tō bhaṇiō caya satthaṁ ajjavi rakkhēmi tuha pāṇē ||
sō bhai tujjha pāṇā maha ruṭṭhē appaṇō cciya durakkhā । majjha harissa na gannaṁ tumhēhiṁ siyālalakkhēhiṁ ||
parihariya khattadhammaṁ tēṇa sasinēṇa tassa ēkssa । pahariumāraddhaṁ ēkakālamaikō havasagēṇa ॥ 108 ॥
mukāī paharaṇāī tēhiṁ sarīrāu tassa umphiḍiuṁ । jēhiṁ ciya mukkāī haṇaṁti tēsiṁ sarīrāī ॥ 109 ॥
iya niyapaharaṇajajjaradē hē bhaggami tassa sēnammi । uppāḍiya āṇīō pallivaī niyayasinnapi ॥ 110 ॥
paḍigāhiyaṁ ca savvaṁ paharaṇaāharaṇavāhaṇāīyaṁ । gaṁtūṇaṁ taṁ palli savvassaṁ tassa ghittūṇa ॥ 111 ॥
bhaṁjāviūṇa ghāē pallivaī kāriō paḍasarīrō । savvassēṇaṁ saha pēsiō ya naranāhapāsammi ॥ 112 ॥
5
tatō dattvā prasādaṁ kiñcinmātraṁ samarpya sainyam । vindhyācalaviṣamapradēśavāsinaḥ samaravīrasya ॥98॥
pallīpatēratipravaraśūranibhr̥tyabhr̥tyavargasya । labdhajayasya raṇēṣūpari sa prēṣitō rājñā ॥99॥
ādēśānantaramēva prasthitaḥ sa sthitaḥ svasīmni । tasmai visr̥jāti dūtaṁ sa taṁ gatvā bhaṇatyēvam ॥ 100 ॥
saubhaṭa subhaṭastavōpari prēṣitō naravarēṇa bhūpatinā । tatastasya kuruṣva sēvāṁ yadīcchasyātmanaḥ kuśalam ॥ 101 ॥
sa bhaṇati tava jihvācchēdaṁ na khalu kārayāmi dūta iti । tatō gatvēti prabhaṇa saubhaṭaṁ mama vacanēna ॥ 102 ॥
ēṣō'hamāgata ēva tāvat pravēṣṭuṁ kr̥tāntavadanē । yadi kāṅkṣāsa tadā pratīkṣasvātra sthita ēva dinadaśakam 103
dūtēna prativacanē kathitē tataḥ saubhaṭastataścalitaḥ । pallīpatirapi sasainyō militē dvē api balē ॥ 104 ॥
tataḥ saubhaṭēna bhaṇitā nijasubhaṭā mama pr̥ṣṭhabhāgē । parasainyaprahārāgōcarē bhōstiṣṭhata paśyantaḥ ॥ 105 ॥
sa pallīpatiścintayatyupēkṣita ēṣa nijasainyēna । tatō bhaṇitastyaja śastramadyāpi rakṣāmi tava prāṇān ॥ 106 ॥
sa bhaṇati tava prāṇā māya ruṣṭa ātmana ēva dūrakṣāḥ । mama harērna gaṇanā yuṣmākaṁ śr̥gālalakṣāṇām ॥ 107॥
parihr̥tya kṣattradharmaṁ tēna sasainyēna tamēkam । prahartumārabdhamēkakālamatikrōdhavaśagēna ॥ 108 ॥
muktāni praharaṇāni taiḥ śarīrāt tasyōdbhraśya । yairēva muktāni ghnanti tēṣāṁ śarīrāṇi ॥ 109 ॥
iti nijapraharaṇa jarjara dēhē bhagnē tasya sainyē । utpāṭyānītaḥ pallīpātirnijasainyē ॥110॥
parigrāhitaṁ ca sarvaṁ praharaṇābharaṇavāhanādikam । gatvā tāṁ pallīṁ sarvasvaṁ tasya gr̥hītvā ॥ 111 ॥
bhañjayitvā ghātān pallīpatiḥ kāritaḥ paṭuśarīraḥ । sarvasvēna saha prēṣitaśca naranāthapārśvē ॥ 112 ॥

supāsanāha-caritryammi-
vināviyaṁ ca kō maha āēsō saṁpayaṁti tō rannā । sō caiva gahīyavēlō pallivaī pēsiō viō ॥ 113 ॥
hakāriūṇa sōhaḍasuhaḍō saṁmāṇiō bahupayāraṁ । uvaladdhasamaravr̥ttaṁtavimhayāuliyahiyaṇa ||114 ||
puṭṭhō rannā kaha tuha jāyā accanyā imā saccī ? | tō sō sāhai jaha pahu ! saṁgā muḍḍāmarī vijjā ॥ 115 ॥
atthi maha mahāisayā dinnā sirijōgiṇā jayaṁtēṇa । sā sāhiyā vihīē tīē pabhāvō imō savvō ।
taṁ sōūṇaṁ rāyā ciṁtai samarammi tāva nivvaḍiō | buddhīēvi māhappaṁ niēmi iya citiuṁ tō sō ॥
muddiyasamuggamappiya ahannayā pāhuḍaṁ nariṁdēṇa । ujjēṇi rāyapāsamma pēsiō iya bhaūṇa ॥ 118 ॥
amhaṁ mahiṁdarāēṇa rāiṇā dūradēsabhāvāō । na virōhakāraṇaṁ kiṁpi tārisaṁ kiṁtu appāṇaṁ ॥ 119 ॥
sō ava bahu nimōtti vaḍḍhēi maccharō garuō । tā nahamaṁsappīī jaha saṁpajjaē taha karijjā |
āēsōti bhaṇēuṁ caliō pattō kamēṇa ujjēṇi । paḍihārasaiō sō pavisai naranāhaatthāṇē || 121 ।
niyanivaappiyamuddiyasamuggayaṁ ḍhōiūṇa nivapuraō । paṇamiya tadāviyaāsaṇammi uvavisai tō rannā ॥
ummuddiō samuggō tammajjhē lahusamuggayaṁ niyai । aha tammajjhē dahuṁ bhūicciya ciṁtai nariṁdō || 123 ||
bhālayalaghaḍiyabhiuḍī āyaṁbiralōyaṇō jahā majjha । dappaṁdhēṇaṁ tēṇaṁ mannē vihiō tirakārō ॥ 124 ॥
tā daṁsissāmi phalaṁ tassa imassa ya taduttakārissa । tō daṁsēuṁ bhūī jaṁpaṛa kiṁ dūya ! ēyaṁti ? || 125 ॥
sō bhai lakkhahōmō kāraviō naravarēṇa tumhāṇaṁ । tappunnavibhāgaṭṭhā bhūī saṁpēsiyā ēsā || 126 ||
tō manatō sō taṁtahati paḍhamōvayārahayahiyaō । hakāriya āsanē hatthaṁ paṭṭīē sē dēi || 127 ||
1
vijñāpitaṁ ca kō mamādēśaḥ sāṁpratamiti tatō rājñā । sa ēva gr̥hītavēlaḥ pallīpatiḥ prēṣyaḥ sthāpitaḥ ॥ 113 ॥
hakkārayitvā saubhaṭasubhaṭaḥ saṁmānitō bahuprakāram । upalabdhasamavr̥ttāntavismayākulitahr̥dayēna ॥ 114 ॥
pr̥ṣṭō rājñā kathaṁ tava jātā'tyadbhutēyaṁ śaktiḥ ? । tataḥ sa kathayati yathā prabhō ! saṁgrāmōḍḍāmarī vidyā ॥ 115 ॥
asti mama mahātiśayā dattā śrīyōgiṇā jayantēna । sā sādhitā vidhinā tasyāḥ prabhāvō'yaṁ sarvaḥ ।। 116 |
tat śrutvā rājā cintayati samarē tāvannirvartitaḥ । buddhērapi māhātmyaṁ paśyāmīti ciṁtayitvā tataḥ saḥ ॥ 117॥
mudritasamudgamarpayitvāthānyadā prābhr̥taṁ narēndrēṇa । ujjayinīrājapārśvē prēṣita iti bhaṇitvā ॥ 118 ॥
asmākaṁ mahēndrarājēna rājñā dūradēśabhāvāt । na virōdhakāraṇaṁ kimapi tādr̥śaṁ kintvātmānam ॥ 119 ॥
sa vayamapi ca bahu manyāmaha iti vardhatē matsarō guruḥ । tasmānnakhamāṁsaprītiryathā saṁpadyatē tathā kuryāḥ ॥ 120॥
ādēśa iti bhaṇitvā calitaḥ prāptaḥ kramēṇōjjayinīm । pratihārasūcitaḥ sa praviśati naranāthāsthānē ॥ 121 ॥
nijanr̥pārpitamudritasamudrakaṁ ḍhaukitvā nr̥papurataḥ । praṇamya taddāpitāsanē upaviśati tatō rājñā ॥ 122॥
unmudritaḥ samudrastanmadhyē laghusamudrakaṁ paśyati । atha manmadhyē dr̥ṣṭrā bhūtimēva cintayati narēndraḥ ॥ 123॥
bhālatalaghaṭita bhr̥kuṭirātāmralōcanō yathā mama । darpāndhēna tēna manyē vihitastiraskāraḥ ॥ 124 ॥
tatō darśayiṣyāmi phalaṁ tasyāsya ca taduktakāriṇaḥ । tatō darśayitvā bhūrti jalpati kiṁ dūta ! ētaditi ॥ 125 ॥
sa bhaṇati lakṣahōmaḥ kāritō naravarēṇa yuṣmākam । tatpuṇyavibhāgārthaṁ bhūtiḥ saṁprēṣitaiṣā ॥ 126 ॥

suṁdara kahā ।
- 145
bhaṇai ya bhaī maha baṁdhavassa, sō bhai savvakālaṁpi । ivhi paṇayaparammī bisēsaō tumha cittampi ||
tō sō kaivayadivasē dhariō tatthēva nivaiṇāṁ tattō । vatthāharaṇaturaṁgamapabhiī dāum̐ mahapasāyaṁ ॥ 129 ॥
niyaya pahāṇapurisēṇa saṁjuyaṁ apiūṇa hatthidugaṁ । taha rayaṇāharaṇaṁ pāhuḍammi ēyaṁ ca uvaiṁsiuṁ ॥ 130॥
jaha bhaṇiyavvō rāyā dēsō kōsō ya cauvvihaṁ sinnaṁ । niyagamiva majjhataṇayaṁ kajjē vāvāriyavvaṁti ॥ 131 ॥
rannā . visajjiō sō pattō ya kamēṇa gayapurē, ittō । saha sōhaḍēṇa puvi bhūvaiṇā pēsiō āsi ॥ 132॥
jō vissaṁbhāṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ ciya tēṇa vaiyarō savvō । parikahiō naravaiṇō sō puṇa tassāsi paccakkhō ||
aha sō mahiṁdaravaipahāṇapurisōvi sauṁha ḍēṇa samaṁ । paṇamai naranāhaṁ uciyaāsaṇē nivisiuṁ tattō ॥
taṁ niyapahupāhuḍamapiūṇa vayaṇa mahiṁdarāyassa । taha sāhai jaha bhaṇiyaṁ ēttō saṁmāṇiuṁ rannā ॥ 135 ॥
paḍipāhuḍaṁ samappiya visajjiō naravarēṇa iya tēsiṁ । paidiṇava vaḍḍhamāṇapparāyāṇaṁ jati diyahāī ॥ 136 ॥
raṇṇāvi buddhijuttaṁ pōrisamēyassa iya kalēūṇa । savvōdhi rajjabhārō nikkhittō sōhaḍē suhaḍē || 137 ॥
savvattha kayapamāṇō akhaliyaāṇō nariṁdalōēṇa । sō bhuṁjai rajjasiriṁ iō ya bhūvainaridassa || 138 ||
puvvakamāgayavērō aīvakhuddā narēsarakubērō । asthi arijipurīē sō taṁ uvacarai pacchannaṁ ॥ 139 ॥
uvayāraṁ tu paḍicchara imāē buddhīē sōhaḍō tassa । naravarabhūvaikajjaṁ viṇāsiyavvaṁ na tāva maē ॥ 940 ॥
kiṁtu imōvi hu garuō rāyā aṇuyattiō havai ēvaṁ । garupāṇaṇuvittī na niṣphalā hōi kaiyāvi ।। 141 ॥
tatō manyamānaḥ sa tat tathēti prathamōpacārahr̥tahr̥dayaḥ । āhūyāsanē hastaṁ pr̥ṣṭhē tasya dadāti ॥ 127॥
bhaṇati ca bhadraṁ mama bāndhavasya sa bhaṇati sarvakālamapi । idānīṁ praṇayaparē viśēṣatastava cittē ॥ 128॥
tataḥ sa katipayadivasān dhr̥tastatraiva nr̥patinā tataḥ । vastrābharaṇaturaṅgamaprabhr̥tiṁ dattvā mahāprasādam ॥ 129॥
nijapradhānapuruṣēṇa saṁyutamarpayitvā hastidvikam । tathā ratnābharaṇaṁ prābhr̥tē ētaccōpadiśya ॥ 130 ॥
yathā bhaṇitavyō rājā dēśa: kōśaśca caturvidhaṁ sainyam + nijakamiva madīyaṁ kāryē vyāpārayitavyamiti ॥ 131 ॥
rājñā visr̥ṣṭaḥ sa prāptaśca kramēṇa gajapurē, itaḥ । saha saubhaṭēna pūrvaṁ bhūpatinā prēṣita āsīt ॥132॥
yō viśrambhasthānaṁ prathamamēva tēna vyatikaraḥ sarvaḥ । parikathitō narapatayē sa punastasyāsītpratyakṣaḥ ॥ 133 ॥
atha sa mahēndranarapītapradhānapuruṣō'pi saubhaṭēna samam । praṇamati naranāthamucitāsanē niviśya tataḥ ॥ 134॥
tannijaprabhuprābhr̥tamarpayitvā vacanaṁ mahēndrarājasya । tathā kathayati yathā bhaṇitam, itaḥ saṁmānya rājñā ।। 135 ।।
pratipramr̥taṁ samarpya visr̥ṣṭō naravarēṇēti tayōḥ । pratidinapravardhamānapraṇayayōryānti divasāni ॥ 136 ॥
rājñāpi buddhiyuktaṁ pauruṣamētasyēti kalayitvā । sarvō'pi rājyabhārō nikṣiptaḥ saubhaṭē subhaṭē ॥ 137 ॥
sarvatra kr̥tapramāṇō'skhalitājñō narēndralōkēna । sa bhuṅgē rājyaśriyamitaśca bhūpatinarēndrasya ॥ 138 ॥
pūrvakramāgatavairō'tīvakṣudrō narēśvarakubēraḥ । astyariñjitpuryā sa tamupacarati pracchannam ॥ 129॥
upacāraṁ tu pratīcchatyanayā buddhyā saubhaṭastasya । naravarabhūpatikāryaṁ vināśayitavyaṁ na tāvanmayā ॥140॥
kintvayamapi khalu gurū rājā'nuvr̥ttō bhavatyēvam । guruṇāmanuvr̥ttirna niṣphalā bhavati kadāpi ॥ 141 ॥

146
supāsanāha cariammi-
tō bhūvaī kaiyāvi hu sammaṁ nāūṇa vaiyaraṁ ēyaṁ । citai aiduddha risō niggahajōggō yavassamimō ॥ 142 ॥
dāas ya visaṁ uggaṁ maō ya sō tēṇa tassa ākaṁkhā । ēkammivi paḍivakkhē ēvaṁ aidāruṇā jāyā ।। 143 ॥
tamhā daḍhasammatō hōuṁ ajjēsu sivasuhamaṇataṁ । kaṁkhāē viḍiō puṇa bhamihisi saṁsārakaṁtārē || 144||
iya muṇidēsaṇasavaṇā paḍibuddhā pāṇiṇō bahū tattha । ciṁtēi suṁdarī puṇa kimēsa galasōsaṇaṁ kuṇai 1 ॥ 145 ॥
savvēvi abhimayā majjha tāva savvē ya pūyaṇijjā ya । iya kayabuddhī mariḍaṁ bhamiō saṁsāravaṇagahaṇē ॥ 146 ॥
sammaṁ ca khēmacaṁdō sammattaṁ pāliuṁ niraiyāraṁ | sōhammē uvavannō kamēṇa pattō ya nivvāṇaṁ ॥ 147॥
॥ ityākāṅkṣāyāṁ sundarakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
tatō bhūpatiḥ kadāpi khalu samyagjñātvā vyatikaramētam । cintayatyatidurdharṣō nigrahayōgyaścāvaśyamayam ॥142॥
dāpayati ca viṣamugraṁ mr̥taśca sa tēna tasyākāṅkṣā । ēkasminnapi pratipakṣa ēvamatidāruṇā jātā ॥143॥
tasmād dr̥ḍhasamyaktvō bhūtvā'ya śivasukhamanantam । kāṅkṣayā vinaṭitaḥ punabhramiṣyasi saṁsārakāntārē || 144 ||
iti munidēśanāśravaṇāt pratibuddhāḥ prāṇinō bahavastatra । cintayati sundaraḥ punaḥ kimēṣa galaśōṣaṇaṁ karōti ? ||
sarvē'pyabhimatā mama tāvat sarvē ca pūjanīyāśca । iti kr̥tabuddhirmr̥tvā bhrāntaḥ saṁsāravanagahanē ॥146॥
samyak ca kṣēmacandraḥ samyaktvaṁ pālayitvā niraticāram । saudharma upapannaḥ kramēṇa prāptaśca nirvāṇam ॥ 147 ॥

sāhūṇa durguchāē jiṇadhammaphalammi saṁsaimaṇassa । duhadaṁdōlī jāyai jaha jāyā bhakkharadiyassa ॥ 1
tathāhi ;-
atthi iha bharahavāsē kāmiṇivayaṇaṁva rayaṇaramaṇīyaṁ । suhadhāmadīharacchaṁ nagaraṁ nāmēṇa girinagaraṁ ||2||
saṁtikiriyāsu kusalō duhāpi jannapiō diō atthi । sacchaṁdōvi paravasō nāmēṇaṁ vissabhūitti ॥ 3 ॥
tastratthi piyā ghariṇī saraṇī saraṇīva nēhasassassa । bhattāvi hu bhattārē nō aṇuyattēi bhattāraṁ ||4||
bhakkharabhāṇubhihāṇā duvēva pāṇapiyā suyā tāṇaṁ । navajōvvaṇābhirāmā ramaṁti tē kāṇaṇāī ||5||
ahannayā vasaṁtē uvasaṁtē gimhanivavalaṁ pattaṁ । ravitāvayavāōlighēmmēṇaṁ jaṇamabhibhavataṁ ॥ 6 ॥
tō naliṇahāracaṁdaṇapaṁkajaladāisāhaṇavalēṇaṁ । kahakahavi hu gimhabalaṁ ruṁbhēi jaṇō viyaṁbhataṁ ॥ 7 ॥
tā bhāṇubhakkharēhiṁ vaṇagahaṇāsannavattiṇi sarammi । kīlaṁtēhiṁ juvaī diṭṭhā nidaṁbharaṁbhavva ||8||
tō tī rūvasōhāē mōhiyā jāva kaṭṭhanicciṭṭhā । tē ṭhaṁti tāva tīēvi sadayaṁ saṁbhāsiyā ēvaṁ ||9॥
kē tubhē kiṁ jāyā niccēṭṭhā, tē bhāṁti tuha rūvaṁ । da adipucvaṁ ēgaggamaṇā palōyaṁtā ॥ 10 ॥
tō saviāraṁ tēsiṁ sōcā paccuttaraṁ taraladiṭṭhī | tāṇa hiyayāṇi hariuṁ caliyā kamalāṇi ucciṇiuṁ ||
tō kuviyantra turaṁtā laggā tappiṭṭaō taō sāvi । vaṁcēuṁ tadiṭṭhi katthavi līṇā niguṁjammi ||12||
tīē disāē tēvi hu gacchaṁtā ēvamēva bhulamaṇā । pāsaṁti muṇi ēṁgaṁ mayaṇaṁ saṁpattamuttiva ॥ 13 ॥
tō tamma divasa saṁpattē tammaṇāu ōsariō । mayaṇō hariṇō hariṇōvva tē taō garuyabhattīē ॥
sādhūnāṁ jugupsayā jinadharmaphalē saṁśayimanasaḥ । duḥkhadvandvālī jāyatē yathā jātā bhāskaradvijasya ॥ 1 ॥
astīha bharatavarṣē kāminīvadanamiva racanāramaṇīyam । sukhadhāmadīrgharathyaṁ ( vīkṣaṁ) nagaraṁ nāmnā girinagaram || 2 ||
śāntikriyāsu kuśalō dvidhā'pi yajña (janya) priyō dvijō'sti । svacchandō'pi paravaśō nāmnā viśvabhūtiriti ॥
tasyāsti priyā gr̥hiṇī saraṇiḥ saraṇiriva snēha sasyasya । bhaktāpi khalu bhartari nō anuvartatē bhartāram ||4|
bhāskarabhānvabhidhānau dvāvapi prāṇapriyau sutau tayōḥ । navayauvanābhirāmau ramātē tau kānanādiṣu ||5||
athānyadā vasanta upaśāntē grīṣmanr̥pabalaṁ prāptam । ravitāpalūtāvātā ligharmēṇa janamabhibhavat ॥ 6 ॥
tatō nalinahāracandanapaṅkajalārdrādisādhanabalēna । kathaṁkathamapi khalu grīṣmabalaṁ ruṇaddhi janō vijr̥mbhamāṇam ||
tadā bhānubhāskarābhyāṁ vanagahanāsannavartini sarāsē । krīḍadbhayāṁ yuvatirdr̥ṣṭā nirdambharambhēva ||8||
tatastasyā rūpaśōbhayā mōhitau yāvatkāṣṭhaniścēṣṭau । tau tiṣṭhatastāvattayāpi sadayaṁ saṁbhāṣitāvēvam ||9||
kau yuvāṁ kiṁ jātau niścaṣṭau tau bhaṇatastava rūpam । dr̥ṣṭādr̥ṣṭapūrvamēkāgramanasau pralōkamānau ||10||

tataḥ savikāraṁ tayōḥ śrutvā pratyuttaraṁ taraladr̥ṣṭiḥ । tayōrhr̥dayē hartuṁ calitā kamalānyuccētum ॥11॥
tataḥ kupitāviva tvaramāṇau lagnau tatpr̥ṣṭhatastataḥ sāpi । vañcayitvā taddr̥ṣṭiṁ kutrāpi līnā nikuñjē ||12||

atthi iha bharahavāsē nayaraṁ sōriyapuraṁti purapavaraṁ । duggaṁgasaṁgayaṁ bhūibhūsiyaṁ harasarīraṁ ||21||

dēhō'pi khalu yuṣmākaṁ nr̥palāñchanalāñchitō yathā pravarām । rājyaśriyamujjhitvā yuṣmābhirdakṣā prapannēti ॥ 17॥
tata ēvaṁvidhayauvanabharē taruṇījana prārthanīyē । kimutpannaṁ vairāgyakāraṇaṁ, tatō muniḥ kathayati ॥ 18 ॥

astīha bharatavarṣē nagaraṁ śauryapuramiti purapravaram । durgāṅgasaṁgataṁ bhūtibhūṣitaṁ haraśarīramiva ॥ 21 ॥
sūrō'pyanuprakaraḥ sōmō'pi khalu mr̥ga (mada ) kalaṅkaparimuktaḥ । dr̥ḍhadharmastatra nr̥pō bhāryā guṇasundarī tasyaṁ ॥22॥
guṇarājastayōḥ sutaḥ prāptō yauvanamitō vasantapurē | īśānacandrarājasya kanakavatī nāma varaduhitā ॥ 23॥

niyavacchālaṁkāraṁ karēsu iya tīē jaṁpiē kumarō । taṁ taha kāuṁ tuṭṭēṇa tīē kumarīkara niyayaṁ ॥ 41 ॥
sabvaṁgiyamābharaṇaṁ dinaṁ, ēttō ya tīē saṁlattaṁ । tumbhēhiṁ samaṁ iha asthi kiṁpi vattavvamētē ||42 ||
tattōya kumaradiṭṭīē cōiō ḍāō jō sacvō । tō vinnattō tīē kumarō, cinnavai iya kumarī ||43||
jīviyamāyattaṁ tumha kiṁtu maha nāha ! maṁdabhāgāē । tumha sarīrē saṁbhōgajōggayā kaivayadiṇaṁtē ||44 ||
bhōgaṁtarāyakāraṇavigamē hōhitti tujjha kahaṇatthaṁ । sahasā apattaṁ dēsiūṇa lōyāṇa majjhami ॥ 45 ॥
ajja sayaṁvaramālā nō pakkhittā, pabhāyasamayammi । khiviyantrā iya dūīvayaṇaṁ suṇiūṇa tayabhi muhaṁ ॥ 46 ॥
bhai guṇarāyakumarōjaivi hu aidukaraṁ imaṁ majjha । jaṁ tīi asaṁbhōgō tahavi hu āṇavai jaṁ kumarī ||47 ||
taṁ caiva māṇaṁ iya visajjiyā sō gayā ya tappāsaṁ । tavvattaṁttō sabbō kahiō kumarīē ēgaṁtē ॥ 48 ॥
tō bīyadi tīē sayaṁvarā maṁḍavampi takaṁṭhē । nivacakasamakkhaṁ ciya khittā kusumāṇa varamālā ॥49॥
savvaṁ nariṁdacakē sammāḍaṁ visajjiyaṁ rannā । guṇarāyakumārēṇaṁ pariṇīyā sā nivaṁgaruhā ॥50॥
kaivayadināvasāṇē pattō sōriyapurampi saha nīē । guruyaṇakaōvayārā mukkā sā annadhavalaharē ॥ 51 ॥
kumarōvi niyāvāsē pattō mittēhi parigaō tattha । dōguṁdagōvva dēvō kīlēi viccittakīlāhiṁ ॥ 52 ॥
tō dipi gaccha tanbhavaṇē ramai vivikīlāhi । tīē samaṁ pīīē diṇāṇi gacchaṁti kumarassa ॥ 53॥
||
naya tīē abhipāyaṁ lakkhara suviyakkhaṇōvi varakumarō । tattō ya sō visūrai kēṇa uvāēṇa sō nēō ॥
kiñca ।
nijavakṣō'laṁkāraṁ kuruṣvēti tayā jalpitē kumāraḥ । tat tathā kr̥tvā tuṣṭēna tasyai kumārīkr̥tē nijakam ॥41॥
sarvāṅgīṇamābharaṇaṁ dattaṁ, itaśca tathā saṁlaptam । yuṣmābhiḥ samamihāsti kimapi vaktavyamēkāntē ॥ 42 ॥
tataśca kumāradr̥ṣṭyā cōdita utthitō janaḥ sarvaḥ । tatō vijñaptastayā kumārō, vijñapayatīti kumārī ॥ 43 ॥
jīvitamāyattaṁ tava kintu mama nātha ! mandabhāgyāyāḥ । tava śarīrē saṁbhōgayōgyatā katipayadināntē ॥ 44 ॥
bhōgāntarāyakāraṇavigamē bhaviṣyatīti tava kathanārtham । sahasā'paṭutvaṁ darśayitvā lōkānāṁ madhyē ॥ 45 ॥
adya svayaṁvaramālā nō prakṣiptā, prabhātasamayē । kṣēptavyēti dūtīvacanaṁ śrutvā tadabhimukham ॥46॥
bhaṇati guṇarājakumārō yadyapi khalvatiduṣkaramidaṁ mama । yat tayā'saṁbhōgastathāpi khalvājñāpayati yatkumārī ॥
tadēva pramāṇamiti visr̥ṣṭā sā gatā ca tatpārśvam । tadvr̥ttāntaḥ sarvaḥ kathitaḥ kumāryā ēkāntē ॥ 48 ॥
tatō dvitīyadinē tayā svayaṁvarāmaṇḍapē tatkaṇṭhē | nr̥pacakrasamakṣamēva kṣiptā kusumānāṁ varamālā || 49 ॥
sarvaṁ narēndracakraṁ sammānya visr̥ṣṭaṁ rājñā । guṇarājakumārēṇa pariṇītā sā nr̥pāṅgaruhā ॥50॥
katipayadināvasānē prāptaḥ śauryapurē saha tayā । kr̥tagurujanōpacārā muktā sā'nyadhavalagr̥hē ॥11॥
kumārō'pi nijāvāsē prāptō mitraiḥ parigatastatra । daugunduka iva dēvaḥ krīḍati vicitrakrīḍābhiḥ ||12||
tataḥ pratidinamapi gacchati tadbhavanē ramatē vividha krīḍābhiḥ । tayā samaṁ prītyā dināni gacchanti kumārasya ||
na ca tasyā abhiprāyaṁ lakṣayati suvicakṣaṇō'pi varakumāraḥ । tataśca sa vidyatē kēnōpāyēna sa jñēyaḥ ॥ 54 ॥

bhakkhara diyakahā ।
kiṁ jōvvaṇēṇa kiṁ vā dhaṇēṇa kiṁ jīviēṇa rūvēṇa । jai mē sayaṁ na laggai ēsā ukkaṁṭhiyā kaṁṭhē ? ॥ 55 ॥
annamma dinē niyamaṁdiraṭṭhiyaṁ paṇabhiūṇa paḍihārō । vinnavai kumāraṁ jaha duvāra parisaṁṭiō purisō ॥56॥
siyacaṁdaṇakayatilaō siyavatthaniyaṁsaṇō kusumahatthō । ahilasai daṁsaṇaṁ tumha sāmi kō tattha āēsō ?
muṁca lahu iya bhaṇiē pavēsiō āsaṇammi dinnammi । uvaviṭṭhō ābhaṭṭō kattō bhaṇa kēṇa kajjēṇa ? ॥ 58 ॥
tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ mahāyasa ! jasaharanāmēṇa siddhaputtēṇa । maha dinnā varavijjā vihiyā mē puvvasēvāvi ॥ 59 ॥
vārasa varisāī, taō tujjha pasāēṇa sijjhihī sāvi । kumarēṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁ phalamēīē, sō bhaṇai ॥
nahayalagamaṇaṁ dhaṇakaṇayasaṁpayā kāmarūvakaraṇaṁ ca । lābhāiparinnāṇaṁ siddhāē havai vijjāē || 61 ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ kumarēṇa taō jaṁ kāyavvaṁ maē tayaṁ bhaṇasu । sō bhai ēgarāī maha uttarasāhagō hōsu || 62 ॥
paḍavannaṁ kumarēṇa parōvayārikkarasiyacittēṇa । parapatyaṇāē jamhā kiṁ kiṁ na kuṇaṁti sappurisā ? ॥63॥.
aha sō kafarnaō pattō kumārēṇa saha masāṇammi । rayaṇīyarasaṁkinē jagēhasamē mahābhīmē ||64 ॥
kiṇhaca uddasirayaṇī nisīhasamayammi, maṁḍala lihiyaṁ । pajjāliō ya jalaṇō tammajjhē khairakaṭṭhēhiṁ ॥ 65॥
rattakaṇavīracaṁdaṇaguggulamāīhiṁ jāva sō jāvaṁ । dēi tahiṁ kumarō puṇa karavālakarō purō ṭhāi ||66 ||
tāva sahasati kōvihu uttaraāsāē aṇuttaravirūvō । āgacchaṁtō diṭṭhō mahānihāuvva hakkāhiṁ ॥ 67 ॥
vihaḍatō girikūḍē kalayalaravēhiṁ bhariyanahaviva । palayānalasāricchō muhēṇa jālāō milaṁtō ॥ 68 ॥
dappubbhaḍa sappaphaḍākaḍappama uḍō sumaṁgalārūḍhō । ḍamaḍamiyaḍamaruyāḍōvaḍāmarō rōsaratacchō ॥ 69 ॥
kiṁ yauvanēna kiṁvā dhanēna kiṁ jīvitēna rūpēṇa । yadi mē svayaṁ na lagatyēṣōtkaṇṭhitā kaṇṭhē ? ॥ 55 ॥
anyasmin divasē nijamandira sthitaṁ praṇamya pratihāraḥ । vijñapayati kumāraṁ yathā dvāraparisaṁsthitaḥ puruṣaḥ ।। 56 ।।
sitacandanakr̥tatilakaḥ sitavastranivasanaḥ kusumahastaḥ | abhilapati darśanaṁ tava svāmin! kastatrādēśaḥ 1 ॥97॥
muñca ladhviti bhaṇitē pravēśita āsanē dattē । upaviṣṭa ābhāṣitaḥ kutō bhaṇa kēna kāryēṇa ? ||18||
tēna bhaṇitaṁ mahāyaśaḥ ! yaśōdharanāmnā siddhaputrēṇa । mahyaṁ dattā varavidyā vihitā mayā pūrvasēvāpi ॥ 59 ॥
dvādaśa varṣāṇi tatastava prasādēna sētsyati sāpi । kumārēṇa tatō bhaṇitaṁ kiṁ phalamētasyāḥ, sa bhaṇati ॥ 60 ॥
nabhastalagamanaṁ dhanakanakasaṁpat kāmarūpakaraṇaṁ ca । lābhādiparijñānaṁ siddhāyāṁ bhavati vidyāyām || 61 ॥
bhaṇitaṁ kumārēṇa tatō yat kartavyaṁ mayā tad bhaṇa । sa bhaṇatyēkarātrē mamōttarasādhakō bhava ॥ 62 ॥
pratipannaṁ kumārēṇa parōpakāraikarasikācētana । paraprārthanayā yasmāt kiṁ kiṁ na kurvanti satpuruṣāḥ 1 ॥ 63 ॥
atha sa kr̥tavidhikavacaḥ prāptaḥ kumārēṇa saha śmaśānē । rajanīcarasaṁkīrṇa yamagēhasamē mahābhīmē ॥64॥
kr̥ṣṇa caturdaśīrajanīniśīthasamayē, maṇḍalaṁ likhitam । prajvalitaśca jvalanastanmadhyē khadirakāṣṭhaiḥ || 65 ॥
raktakaravīracandanaguggulādibhiryāvat sa jāpam । dadāti tatra kumāraḥ punaḥ karavālakaraḥ purastiṣṭhati ॥ 66॥
tāvat saha sēti kō'pi hyuttarāśāyāmanuttaravirūpaḥ । āgacchan dr̥ṣṭō mahāniyāta iva hakkābhiḥ ||67 ||
vighaṭayan girikūṭān kalakalaravairbhr̥tanabhōvivaraḥ । pralayānalasadr̥śō mukhēna jvālā muñcan ॥ 68 ॥
