supāsanāha- carimamsi-
kuḍilakavilakēsō nāsiyāsēsavēsō aimasisamadēhō saddavikkhittamē hō ।
paṇayasuhanihāṇō mēhanāyābhihāṇō karakaliyakavālō khittavālō karālō ॥70॥
pattō sō aruḍō jaṁga rē rē aṇajja ! ajjavi ya । itthēva tumaṁ ciṭṭhasi aṇanunnāō maē dhiṭṭha ! ॥ 71 ॥
sāhēsi ēttha vijjaṁ maha pūyamakā umicchasi ya siddhiṁ । na havasi tā tumamihi tā iṭṭha sarasu rē dēvaṁ ||
sōviyataṇaō tumaē vēyāriō aviṇayassa । aṇuhavau phalaṁ caraō ahava kusaṁgō na kiṁ kuṇai ? ||
tavtrayaṇāyannaṇajāyakō va kumarēṇa pabhāṇiō ēvaṁ । rē rē nillajja ahamma ! ajja ruṭṭhō jamō tujjha ॥ 74॥
pāsaparisaṁṭiē mai imassa sakōpi kuṇai kiṁ vigyaṁ । iya ēvaṁ jaṁpatō pattō kumarō tayāsanē || 75||
pabhaṇai aṇajja ! kiṁ palaviēṇa jai asthi pōrisaṁ tujjha । abbhiṅasu mai saddhaṁ avaṇēmō jēṇa tuha gavvaṁ ।
amarisava sēṇa tō sō caliō tassaṁmuhaṁ asatthaṁ taṁ । daṭṭhē kumarō khaggaṁ millai dūrēṇa tō jhati ॥ 77 ॥৷
niviḍī kuṇai kaḍilaṁ sakēsapāsaṁ taō ya tēṇa samaṁ । jujjhatō hayahiyayaṁ kāuṁ taṁ kuṇai gayadappaṁ ॥ 78 ॥
tō vijjādēvī samāgayā tattha taṁ daddhuṁ । pabhaṇai kumāra ! siddhā sattikadhaṇassa tujjha ahaṁ ||79 ||
ki tuha kīrau sāhasa, kumarēṇaṁ pabhaṇiyā imaṁ dēvī । ēyassa tumaṁ sijjha saṁpāḍasu vaṁchiyaṁ atthaṁ ॥ 80 ॥
tuha sāhējjēṇaṁ ciya siddhā hamimassa, kiṁpi bhaṇa annaṁ । tō kaṇagavaī bhōgaṁtarāya hē sa pucchēi ॥ 81 ॥
sā uvaōgaṁ dāum̐ jaṁpai ēyaṁ sarvapi jāṇihisi । kāmiyarūvadharattēṇa taṁ ca tuha hōu maha vayaṇā ||82||
darpōṭasarpa phaṭā saṁghātamukuṭaḥ sumaṅgalārūḍhaḥ । ḍamaḍamita ḍamarukā ṭōpaḍāmarō rōṣaraktākṣaḥ ||69 ॥
kuṭilakapilakēśō nāśitāśēṣadvēyō'timapisamadēhaḥ śabdavikṣiptamētraḥ ।
praṇatasukhanidhānaṁ mēghanādābhidhānaḥ karakalitakapālaḥ kṣētrapālaḥ karālaḥ ॥71॥
prāptaḥ sō'tiruṣṭō jalpati rē rē nārya ! adyāpi ca । atraiva tvaṁ tiṣṭhasyananujñātō mayā dhr̥ṣṭa ! ||7|| 0
sādhayasyatra vidyāṁ mama pūjāmakr̥tvēcchasi ca siddhim । na bhavasi tāvattvamidānīṁ tasmādiṣṭaṁ smara rē dēvam ॥ 72 ॥
ēṣō'pi rājatanayastvayā pratāritō'vinayasya । anubhavatu phalaṁ varākō'thavā kusaṅgō na kiṁ karōti ? || 73 ॥
tadvacanākarṇana jātakōpakumārēṇa prabhaṇita ēvam । rē rē nirlajja ! adharma ! adya ruṣṭō yamastava ॥ 74 ॥
pārśvaparisasthitē mayyasya śakrō'pi karōti kiṁ vighnam । ityēvaṁ jalpan prāptaḥ kumārastadāsanē || 75 ॥
prabhaṇatyanāyē ! kiṁ pralapitēna yadyasti pauruṣaṁ tava । saṁgacchasva mayā sārdhamapanayāmi yēna tava garvam ॥ 76 ॥
amarṣavaśēna tataḥ sa cālitastatsaṁmukhamaśastraṁ tam । dr̥ṣṭvā kumāraḥ khaṅgaṁ muñcati dūrēṇa tatō jhaṭiti ॥77॥
nibiḍīkarōti kaṭībhavaṁ sakēśapāśaṁ tataśca tēna samam । yudhyamānō hatahr̥dayaṁ kr̥tvā taṁ karōti gatadarpam ॥ 78 ॥
itō vidyādēvī samāgatā tatra taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā । prabhaṇati kumāra ! siddhā satvaikadhanasya tavāham ||79||
kiṁ tava kriyatāṁ kathaya, kumārēṇa prabhaṇitēdaṁ dēvī । ētasya tvaṁ sidhya saṁpādaya vāñchitamartham ॥ 80 ॥
tava sāhāyyēnaiva siddhāhamasya kimapi bhaṇānyat । tataḥ kanakavatībhōgāntarāyahētuṁ sa pr̥cchati ॥ 81 ॥
sōpayōgaṁ dattvā jalpatyētatsvayamapi jñāsyasi । kāmitarūpadharatvēna tacca tava bhavatu mama vacanāt ॥ 82 ॥

bhakkharadiyakahā ।

tēṇaṁ mahāpasāē bhaṇiē dēvī gayā niyahāṇē | siddhēṇaṁ guṇarāō sappaṇayaṁ tō imaṁ bhaṇiō || 83 ॥
tumhāṇubhāvaō cciya samīhiyatthō maē samaṇupattō | tō āēsō dijjau nidēsakarassa maha kōi ||84||
bhai kumārō vilasaha icchāē ēsa tumha āēsō । sō bhai sumariyavvō katthai kajjē tahāvi ahaṁ ।।
i. bhaṇi sōvi gaō kumarō pakkhāliūṇa niyadēhaṁ । niyayāvāsammi gaō mōttūṇaṁ syaṇivatthāṇi ॥
kāū siṁgāraṁ kaṇagavaī maṁdirammi sō pattō । paccūsē vivihāhiṁ kahāhiṁ gamiūṇa khaṇamēgaṁ ॥ 87 ॥
niyabhavaṇē saṁpattō gamiḍaṁ divasaṁ gaō ya rayaṇīē | māṇusacakkhuagōyara rūvaṁ kāūṇa ēgāgī ॥ 88 ॥
kaṇagavaīē bhavaṇē khaggasahāō gihassa uvarimmi । jā ciṭṭhai kaṇagavaīvi tāva tatthēva saṁpattā ||89 ॥
dāsījuyalēṇa samaṁ bhaṇē hē suyaṇu ! kittiyā rayaṇī । dāsī bhaṇai nisīhō āgamavēlā vimāṇassa ||
tō tīi maggiō pahāṇasāḍaō khāliyaṁ niyaṁ aṁgaṁ । pasuēṇa lūhiya kayaṁgarāyā sunēvatthā ||11||
vivihālaṁkāradharā jā acchā tā vimāṇamaṇupattaṁ । tattha caḍiyāō tāō kumarōvi adissarūvadharō॥92॥
tō uttaradisihattaṁ maṇava sigdhaṁ avigghaō gaṁtuṁ । saratīrē ōinnaṁ vimāṇamaha naṁdaṇavaṇami ||93 ||
vijjāhararāyāvi hu diṭṭhō kumārēṇa cūyaṭṭimmi । nīhariya vimāṇāō kaṇagavaī tassa pāsamma || 94 ||
saṁpattā namijaṇaṁ tassa ya āṇāi tattha uvaviṭṭhā | thēvavēlāē pattā annāvi tini kumarīō ॥ 95 ॥
rairaṁbhārūvāō ubhaḍanavajōvvaṇābhirāmāō । uvaviṭṭhāō tāō khēyaranāhaṁ paṇamiṇa || 96॥
thēvēlā khayarō suibhūō niyasiyāmaladugūlō । pannattidēvibhavaṇē pattō namiūṇa pannati ॥ 97॥
tēna mahāprasādē bhaṇitē dēvī gatā nijasthānē । siddhēna guṇarājaḥ sapraṇayaṁ tata idaṁ bhaṇitaḥ ॥ 83॥
tavānubhāvata ēva samīhitārthō mayā samanuprāptaḥ । tata ādēśō dīyatāṁ nidēśakarasya mama kō'pi ॥84॥
bhaṇati kumārō vilasatēcchayaiṣa tavādēśaḥ । sa bhaṇati smartavyaḥ kutrāpi kāryē tathāpyaham ||89||
iti bhaṇitvā sō'pi gataḥ kumāraḥ prakṣālya nijadēham । nijāvāsē gatō muktvā rajanivastrāṇi ॥ 86 ॥
kr̥tvā śr̥ṅgāraṁ kanakavatīmandirē sa prāptaḥ । pratyūṣē vividhābhiḥ kathābhirgamayitvā kṣaṇamēkam ॥ 87 ॥
nijabhavanē saṁprāptō gamayitvā divasaṁ gataśca rajanyām । mānuṣacakṣuragōcararūpaṁ kr̥tvaikākī ॥ 88 ॥
kanakavatyā bhavanē khaḍgasahāyō gr̥hasyōpari । yāvattiṣṭhati kanakavatyapi tāvattatraiva saṁprāptā ॥89॥
dāsī yugalēna samaṁ bhaṇati hē sutanu ! kiyatī rajaniḥ । dāsī bhaṇati niśīthaṁ āgamavēlā vimānasya ॥90॥
tatastayā mārgitaḥ snānaśāṭakaḥ kṣālitaṁ nijamaṅgam । paṭṭāṁśukēna rūkṣayitvā kr̥tāṅgarāgā sunēpathyā ॥91॥
vividhālaṅkāravarā yāvadāstē tāvadvimānamanuprāptam । tatra caṭitē tē kumārō'pyadr̥śyarūpavaraḥ ॥92॥
tata uttaradibhimukhaṁ mana iva śīghramavighnatō gatvā । sarastīrē'vatīrṇa vimānamatha nandanavanē ॥93॥
vidyādhararājāpi khalu dr̥ṣṭaḥ kumārēṇa cūtasyādhaḥ । niḥsr̥tya vimānāt kanakavī tasya pārśvē ॥ 94 ॥
saṁprāptā natvā tasya cājñayā tatrōpaviṣṭā । stōkavēlayā prāptā anyā api tisraḥ kumāryaḥ ॥99॥
ratirambhārūpā udbhaṭanavayauvanābhirāmāḥ । upaviṣṭāstāḥ khēcaranāthaṁ praṇamya ॥ 96 ॥

supāsanāha- cariśrammi-
tēṇāraddhō jāvō ālihiyaṁ maṁḍalapi ghusiṇēṇa । bhūsannāṇunnāyā tinivi kumarīō namiūṇa || 98 ॥
ēkā sārai vīṇaṁ ēkā vannaṁ karēi mahurasaraṁ । ēkkā vāyai vaṁsa ēvaṁ tarhi tāhi vihiyami ||19||
kaṇagavaī naccaṇavārautti kaliūṇa kacchiyaṁ pattā । naccai sahāvabhāvaṁ vicittakaraṇaṁgahārēhiṁ ॥ 100॥
kaṇagavaīē sarahasapaṇaccaṇā tuṭṭiūṇa kiṁkaṇiyā । paḍiyā kumarapayaṁtē tēṇavi saṁgōvi ghariyā ॥ 101 ॥
tō raṁgunniē tīē savvattha sā gavidvāvi । nō diṭṭhā, savvāō visajjiyāō ya aha tēṇa ॥ 102 ॥
niyaniyavimāṇacaḍiyāu tāu savvāu niyaniyagihēsu । saṁpattāu khaṇēṇaṁ kumarō uṇa tavvimāṇā ।।
assaṁtō tī tagahadārāu uttarēūṇa । niyayāvāsammi gaō rayaṇīē caramapaharammi || 104 ॥
paccūsē udvittā takkālāvassayaṁ vihēūṇa । niyamaisāgaramaṁtissa appiyā kiṁkiṇī hatthē ॥ 105 ॥
bhaṇiō kaṇagavaī apijjasu majjha vayaṇaō cēva । tō tabbhavaṇammi gayā tē daṭuṁ uṭṭhaē sāvi ।। 106 ॥
sayamāsaṇaṁ samappai sayamavi uvavisai tassamīvammi । tō sārajūyaṁ ramiuṁ kumarīkumarēhiṁ pāraddhaṁ ॥ 107॥
hāraṁtama kumārē kaṇagavaī bhai kiṁpi sārēhi । tā kumarēṇa bhaṇiō maṁtī maisāgarō ēyaṁ ॥ 108 ॥
gahaṇayamappa, tō tēṇa apiyā kiṁkiṇī rayaṇaruirā । kaḍavaṭṭīō tīē karammi tō tīē sā daṭuṁ ॥
pañcabhināyā hā ! kattha pāviyā, pucchiō bhaṇai paḍiyā kiṁ । kattha paēsē pattā, sō bhaṇai jattha tē paḍiyā।
sā bhai na yāṇāmī, kumarō jaṁpēi ēsa mittī । bhūyabhavissaṁ jāṇai tā pucchasu jattha tē paḍiyā ||
1
stōkavēlayā khacaraḥ śucibhūtō nivasitāmaladukūlaḥ । prajñaptidēvībhavanē prāptō natvā prajñaptim ॥97॥
tēnārabdhō jāpa ālikhitaṁ maṇḍalamapi ghusaṇēna । bhrūsaṁjñānujñātāstisrō'pi kumāryō natvā ॥98 ॥
ēkā svārayati vīṇāmēkā varṇaṁ karōti madhurasvaram | ēkā vādayati vaṁśamēvaṁ tatra tābhirvihitē ॥99॥
. kanakavatī nartanavāra iti kalayitvā kacchikāṁ prāptā । nr̥tyati sahāvabhāvaṁ vicitrakaraṇāṅgahāraiḥ ॥ 100॥
kanakavatyāḥ sarabhasapranartanāt truṭitvā kiṅkiṇī । patitā kumārapādāntē tēnāpi saṁgōpya dhr̥tā ॥ 101 ॥
tatō raṅgōttīrṇayā tathā sarvatra sā gavēṣitāpi । nō dr̥ṣṭā, sarvā visr̥ṣṭāścātha tēna ॥ 102 ॥
nijanijavimānacaṭitāstāḥ sarvā nijanijagr̥hēṣu । saṁprāptāḥ kṣaṇēna kumāraḥ punastadvimānāt ॥ 103॥
adr̥śyamānastayā tadgr̥hadvārāduttīrya । nijāvāsē gatō rajanyāścaramapraharē || 104॥
pratyūṣē utthāya tatkālāvaśyakaṁ vidhāya । nijamatisāgaramantriṇō'rpitā kiṅkiṇī hastē ॥105॥
bhaṇitaḥ kanakavatyā arpayērmadvacanata ēva । tatastadbhavanē gatau tau dr̥ṣṭrōttiṣṭhati sāpi ॥ 106॥
svayamāsanaṁ samarpayati svayamapyupaviśati tatsamīpē । tataḥ śāradyūtaṁ ramayituṁ kumārīkumārāmyāṁ prārabdham ॥
jīyamānē kumārē kanakavatī bhaṇati kimapi sāraya । tadā kumārēṇa bhaṇitō mantrī matisāgara ētasyai ॥ 108 ॥
grahaṇakamarpaya, tatastēnārpitā kiṅkiṇī ratnarucirā । kaṭīpaṭṭatastasyāḥ karē tatastayā sā dr̥ṣṭvā ॥ 109 ॥
pratyabhijñātā hā ! kva prāpitā, pr̥ṣṭaḥ bhaṇati patitā kva : । kva pradēśē prāptā, sa bhaṇati yatra tē patitā ||
sā bhagati na jānāmi, kamārō jalpatyēṣa naimittikaḥ । bhūtabhaviṣyajjānāti tasmāttr̥ccha yatra tē patitā ॥

bhakkharadiyakahā ।
155
tō pucchai kaṇagavaī saciva, mē kahasu, tēṇabhippāyaṁ । nāūṇa kumarataṇayaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kallē kahissāmi ||
khillēḍaṁ khaṇamēgaṁ tahēva sō tō gaō niyayabhavaṇē । atthamiē diṇanāhō rayaṇīē paḍhamapaharammi ॥ 113 ॥
saṁpattō tanbhavaṇē puṇōvi sā patthiyā jahā puvviṁ । kumarōvi tahēva taō tatthēva gayāī savvāī ॥ 114 ॥
puvvakkamēṇa khayarēṇa jāvahōmāiyammi pāraddhē । āraddhaṁ picchaṇayaṁ kumarīhi tattha kaṇagavaī ॥ 115 ॥
vīṇa vāēi taōvakkhittamaṇāē tīē kumarēṇa । vāmacaraṇāō sigdhaṁ avahariyaṁ nēuraṁ tattō ॥ 116 ॥
tō picchaṇaē vitta bhaṇiyā dāsī halē ! gavēsēha । kēṇavi pacchanēṇaṁ avahariyaṁ nēuraṁ majjha ॥ 117 ॥
tō raṁgagaō lōō puṭṭhō dāsīē viṇayapaṇayāē । nō katthavi uvaladdhaṁ sudugavidvēpi taṁ tattha ॥ 118 ॥
puvvakamēṇa tattō niyaniyaṭhāṇammi tāī pattāī । kumarō vi. niyāvāsē suttō tattō pabhāyammi ॥ 119 ॥
āvasyaṁ vihē tattō maisāgarassa appē । taṁ nēuraṁ tahēva ya pattō bhajjā bhavaṇammi || 120 ॥
kumarō kaōvayārō uvaviṭṭhō sāvi tattha uvaviṭṭhā | pāraddhā tō gōṭṭhī samassaparipūraṇāīyā || 121 ॥
kumarēṇa paढ़iya
----
paḍupavaṇā hayapaumiṇa ! dalataralaṁ jīviyaṁ ca pēmmaṁ ca । jīvāṇaṁ juvvaṇadhaṇaṁ
(aō tīē suṇiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ )
taō tīē paḍhiyā pahēliyā;-
tumhā dhammaṁ kuha sammaṁ ॥ 122॥
i sikkhaviō sīsō jaīṇa rayaṇīē jujjai na gaṁtuṁ । tō kīsa bhaṇai ajjō mā saṁkasu dōvi tullāī ||
tataḥ pr̥cchati kanakavatī sacivaṁ, māṁ kathaya, tēnābhiprāyam । jñātvā kumārasya bhaṇitaṁ kalyē kathayiṣyāmi ॥
krīḍayitvā kṣaṇamēkaṁ tathaiva sa tatō gatō nijabhavanē । astamitē dinanāthē rajanyāḥ prathamapraharē ॥ 113 ॥
saṁprāptastadbhavanē punarapi sā prasthitā yathā pūrvam । kumārō'pi tathaiva tatastatraiva gatāḥ sarvē ॥ 114 ॥
pūrvakramēṇa khacarēṇa jāpahōmādikē prārabdhē । ārabdhaṁ prēkṣaṇakaṁ kumārībhistatra kanakavī ॥ 115 ॥
vīṇāṁ vādayati tatō'vakṣiptamanasastasyāḥ kumārēṇa । vāmacaraṇāt śīghramapahr̥taṁ nūpuraṁ tataḥ ॥ 116 ॥
tataḥ prēkṣaṇakē vr̥ttē bhaṇitā dāsī halē ! gavēṣaya | kēnāpi pracchannēnāpahr̥taṁ nūpuraṁ mama ॥117॥
tatō raṅgagatō lōkaḥ pr̥ṣṭō dāsyā vinayapraṇatayā । nō katrāpyupalabdhaṁ suṣṭhu gavēṣitamami tattatra ॥ 118 ॥
pūrvakramēṇa tatō nijanijasthānē tē prāptāḥ । kumārō'pi nijāvāsē suptastataḥ prabhātē ॥ 119 ॥
āvaśyakaṁ vidhāya tatō matisāgarasyāpayitvā । tannūpuraṁ tathaiva ca prāptō bhāryāyā bhavanē ॥ 120 ॥
kumāraḥ kr̥tōpacāra upaviṣṭaḥ sāpi tatrōpaviṣṭā । prārabdhā tatō gōṣṭhī samasyāparipūraṇādikā ॥ 121 ॥
kumārēṇa paṭhitam ;--
paṭupavanāhatapadmini ! dalataralaṁ jīvitaṁ ca prēma ca । jīvānāṁ yauvanadhanaṁ
( tatastayā śrutvā bhaṇitam )
tatastayā paṭhitā prahēliṁkā ;-
tasmād dharmaṁ kuru samyak ॥ 122 ॥

156
supāsanāha cariśrammi-
kumarēṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ rayaṇī divasō ya dōvi tullāī । tassa jaō sō dōhivi jahadviyaṁ niyai nāṇēṇa ॥
ēmāiviṇōēṇaṁ khaṇaṁ gamēūṇa tīē tō puṭṭhō । maisāgarō taē kiṁ jōisamavalōiyaṁ kiṁpi ? ॥ 125 ॥
āmaṁ, kiṁtu tuhannaṁ kiṁpi nadvaṁti pabhaṇiē bhaṇai । kiṁ taṁ, jaṁ taṁ jāṇasi iya bhaṇiē bhaṇē jāṇēmi ॥ 126॥
kiṁpuṇa kattha ya nahaṁ ahaṁ na yāṇāmi kahaha jai muṇaha । dōṇhavi paḍaṇadvāṇaṁ ēkkaṁciya tīē sō kahai || 127 ||
tō vimhiyā vicita kiṁkiṇiyā majjha katthai paḍiyā । iya nicchaō na āsī, taō ya paribhāviyaṁ ēyaṁ ॥
katthavi ihēva ya paḍiyā caḍiyā ēyassa tēṇa hatthammi । nēurapaḍaṇadvāṇaṁ ēsō tīēva parikahai ॥ 129 ॥
tā jōisēṇa jāṇai jai jāṇau kiṁtu kiṁkiṇī tattha । paḍiyā imassa hatthē caḍiyā kēṇappaōgēṇa ? |
naya gaṁtuṁ tattha imō mō taō sāhasikarasiyassa । maha bhattaṇō cciya imaṁ viyaṁbhiyaṁ hōjja tō bhaṇai ||
kiṁ nēuraṁpa tumhē hatthē caḍiyaṁ, bhaṇēi sō āmaṁ । sā bhaṇai maha samappaha tīē tō sō samappēi ॥ 132 ॥
tō sā pabhaṇai kumaraṁ sōhaṇamēyaṁ tu jai sayaṁ laddhaṁ । aha annāō pattaṁ maha paiṇā tā na laṭṭhayaraṁ ॥ 133 ॥
jaō ।
jalaṇapavēsēṇavi majjha natthi suddhitti jaṁpiē bhaṇai । kiṁ jalaṇapavēsēṇaṁ maha cittē visasu nissaṁkaṁ ॥
tattō ya sā vicitai maha paiṇō ēsa vaiyarō savvō । mannē paccakkhō cciya tā ajjappabhiri na tappāsē ॥
gaṁtavvaṁ, ṭhāyavvaṁ maṁdavvavaēsaō ihēva maē । vijjāharāhivaiṇō dāsīvayaṇāu kahiūṇaṁ ॥ 136 ॥
I
yadi śikṣitaḥ śiṣyō yatīnāṁ rajanyāṁ yujyatē na gantum । tataḥ kasmādbhaṇatyāryō mā śaṅkasva dvē api tulyē ॥ 123॥
kumārēṇa tatō bhaṇitaṁ rajanirdivasaśca dvāvapi tulyau । tasya yataḥ sa dvayōrapi yathāsthitaṁ paśyati jñānēna ॥ 124॥
ēvamādivinōdēna kṣaṇa gamayitvā tayā tataḥ pr̥ṣṭaḥ । matisāgarastvayā kiṁ jyautiṣamavalōkitaṁ kimapi ॥ 125 ॥
āma, kintu tavānyat kimapi naṣṭamiti prabhaṇitē bhaṇati । kiṁ tat, yattvaṁ jānāsīti bhaṇitē bhaṇati jānāmi ||
kintu kva ca naṣṭamahaṁ na jānāmi kathaya yadi jānāsi । dvayōrapi patanasthānamēkamēva tāṁ sa kathayati ॥ 127॥
tatō vismitā vicintayati kiṅkiṇī mama kutrāpi patitā । iti niścayō nāsīt, tataśca paribhāvitamētat ॥
kutrāpīhaiva ca patitā caṭitaitasya tēna hastē । nūpurapatanasthānamēṣa tasyā iva parikathayati ॥ 129 ॥
tasmājjyautiṣēṇa jānāti yadi jānātu kintu kiṅkiṇī tatra । patitāsya hastē caṭitā kēna prayōgēṇa ? || 130 ॥
na ca gantuṁ tatrāyaṁ kṣamastataḥ sāhasaikarasikasya । mama bharturēvēdaṁ vijr̥mbhitaṁ bhavēt tatō bhaṇati ॥131॥
kiṁ nūpuramapi yuṣmākaṁ hastē caṭitaṁ, bhaṇati sa āma । sā bhaṇati mahyaṁ samarpaya tasyai tataḥ sa samarpayati ॥
tataḥ sā prabhaṇati kumāraṁ śōbhanamētattu yadi svayaṁ labdham । athānyasmātprāptaṁ mama patyā tadā na sundarataram ॥
yataḥ ।
jvalanapravēśēnāpi mama nāsti śuddhiriti jalpitē bhaṇati । kiṁ jvalanapravēśēna mama cittē viśa niḥśaṅkam ॥
tataśca sā vicintayati mama patyurēṣa vyatikaraḥ sarvaḥ । manyē pratyakṣa ēva tasmādadyaprabhr̥ti na tatpārśvē ॥ 135 ॥
gantavyaṁ, sthātavyaṁ māndyavyapadēśata ihaiva mayā । vidyādharādhipatiṁ dāsavicanāt kathayitvā ॥ 136॥

bhakkharadiyakahā
157
ēvaṁ parikkhiē tassa māṇasē hōi kiṁpi jaṁ uciyaṁ । taṁ kāhāmi taō sā bīyadiṇē pēsaē dāsiṁ ॥
jāi kumārōvi tahiṁ tava dāsī ya vinnava tattha । vijjāhararāyaṁ jaha apaḍata ajja karāī ॥ 138 ॥
aha saṁbhaṁtō cita kiṁ sacca rōgiṇī imā jāyā । tā pucchai pannatti sā sāhai paḍusarīrā sā ।। 139 ॥
tō sō jaṁpai kuddhō tīē sarīraṁ ahaṁ paṛakarissaṁ । taṁ puṇa sumarasu ihaṁ dēvayamihi marasi pāvē ! || 140 ॥
puvvaṁ ca āsi kahiyē kaṇagavaīē imīē jaha kumarō । pacchannō tattha ṭiō muṇai imaṁ vaiyaraṁ savvaṁ ॥
tattō ya sā paryapara saraṇa sō maha kumāraguṇarāō । niddaya ! nidōsāē mārijjatīi pāva! taē । 142 ॥
tō vijjāhararāō pabhaṇaṛa sō kō visēsaō kahasu । bhaṇiō tō dāsīē suchu kathaṁ jaṁ tara puḍhaṁ 143
kumarassa cariyakahaṇēṇa tuha pavittēmi kaṇṇajuyalamahaṁ । dhavalai junhā añcatamaliṇavannēvi ya payatthē ॥ 144॥
majjha visēsēṇa puṇō juttaṁ tannāmagrahaṇamiha samaē । maraṇasamayammi jamhā sumarijjai dēvayaṁ iṭuṁ || 145 ॥
sō ciya iṭṭhō sō caitra dēvayā majjha sāmiṇīēvi । tā suṇasu suṇasu kupurisa ! supurisacariyaṁ kahijjaṁtaṁ ॥
jēṇa samakkhaṁ ciya naravaīṇa guṇarūvavikkamabalēṇa । sōhaggajayapaḍāyavva ahama ! maha sāmiṇī gahiyā ||
jēṇaṁ ciya garuyaguṇēṇa sayalasatthatthabhāviyamaṇēṇa । dūraḍiōvi nāō tumaṁpi kēvi paōgē || 148 ||
vēṇaṁ tumaṁ diṭṭhēvi na hōsi bhuvaṇammi sāhasaghaṇēṇa । tēṇa ahamattaṇō kīramāṇamicchāmi iha rakkhaṁ ||
āyantriūṇa ēvaṁ jāō tivalīta raṁgiyaniḍālō | vijjāharō harō iva pabhaṇai saṁharaṇajāyara sō ॥ 150 ॥
taṁ saraṇaṁ saramāṇā maraṇaṁ pāvēsi taṁ mahāpāvē ! । maha maṁḍalaggaaggī laggissa tassavi sarīrē ॥ 151 ॥
ēvaṁ parīkṣitē tasya mānasē bhavati kimapi yaducitam । tatkariṣyāmi tataḥ sā dvitīyadinē prēṣayati dāsīm ॥
yāti kumārō'pi tatra tathaiva dāsī ca vijñasyati tatra । vidyādhararājaṁ yathā'paṭutanuradya kanakavatī ॥138॥
atha saṁbhrāntaścintayati kiṁ satyaṁ rōgiṇīyaṁ jātā । tataḥ pr̥cchati prajñapti sā kathayati 'paṭuśarīrā sā' |
tataḥ sa jalpati kruddhastasyāḥ śarīramahaṁ paṭūkariṣyē । tvaṁ punaḥ smarēṣṭaṁ daivatamidānīṁ mriyasē pāpē ! ॥ 140 ॥
pūrva cāsītkathitaṁ kanakavatyā'syai yathā kumāraḥ । pracchannastatra sthitō jānātīmaṁ vyatikaraṁ sarvam ॥ 141 ॥
tataśca sā prajalpati śaraṇaṁ sa mama kumāraguṇarājaḥ । nirdaya ! nirdōṣāyā māryamāṇāyāḥ pāpa ! tvayā ॥ 142 ॥
tatō vidyādhararājaḥ prabhaṇatēi sa kō viśēṣataḥ kathaya । bhaṇitastatō dāsyā suṣṭhu kr̥taṁ yattvayā pr̥ṣṭham ॥143॥
kumārasya caritakathanēna tava pavitrayāmi karṇayugalamaham । dhavalayati jyōtsnā'tyantamalinavarṇānapi padārthān ॥
mama viśēṣēṇa punaryuktaṁ tannāmagrahaṇamiha samayē । maraṇasamayē yasmāt smaryatē daivatamiṣṭam ॥ 145 ॥
sa ēvēṣṭaḥ sa ēva dēvatā mama svāminyā api । tasmāt śr̥ṇu śr̥ṇu kupuruṣa ! supuruṣacaritraṁ kathyamānam ॥
yēna samakṣamēva narapatīnāṁ guṇarūpavikramabalēna । saubhāgyajayapatākēvādhama ! mama svāminī gr̥hītā ॥ 147 ॥
yēnaiva guruguṇēna sakalaśāstrārthabhāvitamanasā । dūrasthitō'pi jñātastvamapi kēnāpi prayōgēṇa ॥ 1.48 ॥
yēna tvaṁ dr̥ṣṭēnāpi na bhavasi bhuvanē sāhasaghanēna । tēnāhamātmanaḥ kriyamāṇāmicchāmīha rakṣām ॥ 149॥
ākarṇyatajjātastrivalī taraṅgitalalāṭaḥ । vidyādharō hara iva prabhaṇati saṁharaṇajātarasaḥ ॥ 150 ॥

158
supāsanāha carimammi -
ēvaṁ pabhaṇaṁtēṇaṁ tēṇaṁ āyaḍiō siyakivāṇō । dūrīhūō savvōvi pariyaṇō taṁ tahā dadatuṁ ।। 152 ।।
tō hasiūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ payuḍīhōūṇa tēṇa kumarēṇa । rē rē ! avijjakulahara ! vijjāhara ! kiṁ na lajjēsi ॥
kham umgīraṁtō itthavatthaṁ hayāsalōyāṇaṁ । paccakkhapicchirāṇaṁ tattaṇō paṁcabhūyāṇaṁ ? ॥ 154 ॥
kiñca ।
suttammattapattē vālē mahilāgaṇē ya jō purisō । paharēi mukkamajjāyasēharō sō ava || 155 ॥
tujjhavi uvari khagaṁ kaṭṭhētō kō na lajjai sayannō । itthiyaṇamajjhayārē jō suhaḍattaṁ payāsēsi ? ।। 156॥
kiṁpuṇa jaha taha duṭṭhāṇa niggahō khattiēhiṁ kāyavvō । tā na havasi tumamihiṁ bhaṇihisi vattā na mē kahiyā ||
ēvaṁ bhaṇiraṁ kumarō kōsāō kaḍūḍhaē taō khaggaṁ । sōvi gahiuggakhaggō valēi tassuvari kōvēṇa ॥ 158॥
āvaḍiō saṁgāmō kumarēṇa nihaṇiō sa duṭṭappā । tō hiṭṭāō tāō tinnivi kannāō tassaraṇaṁ ॥
pattāō bhaṇati tayaṁ amhē ēēṇa vayaṇabaddhāō । mōyāviyāu tumaē, tō kumarō bhāi kaha tassa ॥ 160 ॥
vayaṇacchalammi paḍiyā, ēgā tō kahai niyapiugihammi । kuṭṭimatalē lulaṁtī ēēṇa haḍhā niyā nē ||
umgīriō mamōvari jamajīhādīhataralakaravālō | maraṇabhayakaṁpirā haṁ bhaṇiyā ēēṇa pāvēṇa || 162॥
jai manasi maha vayaṇaṁ tō jīyaṁ tujjha iyarahā nēya । kiṁ taṁ kahēhi bhaṇiē tēṇa imaṁ sāhiyaṁ majjha ॥ 163 ॥
jaha pannattī vijjā pāraddhā sāhiuṁ maē tattha । jāvampri kīramāṇē chammāsē jāva paidiyahaṁ ॥ 164 ॥
samavayasamavannasa lakkhaṇāhi taruṇīhi rāyakannāhiṁ । vihiyavvaṁ picchaṇayaṁ puraō pattidēvī || 165 ॥
taṁ śaraṇaṁ sarantī maraṇaṁ prāpnōṣi tvaṁ mahāpāpē ! । mama maṇḍalāgrāgnirlagiṣyati tasyāpi śarīrē ॥ 151 ॥
ēvaṁ prabhaṇatā tēnākr̥ṣṭaḥ śitakr̥pāṇaḥ । dūrībhūtaḥ sarvō'pi parijanastaṁ tathā dr̥ṣṭvā ॥ 152 ॥
I
tatō hasitvā bhaṇitaṁ prakaṭībhūtēna tēna kumārēṇa । rē rē ! avidyākulagr̥ha ! vidyādhara ! kiṁ na lajjasē ॥ 153 ॥
khaṅgamudgiran strīvadhārthaṁ hatāśalōkēṣu । pratyakṣadarśanaśīlēṣu tathātmanaḥ pañcabhūtēṣu ॥ 154 ॥
suptōnmattapramattē bālē mahilājanē ca yaḥ puruṣaḥ । praharati muktamaryādaśēkharaḥ sō'draṣṭavyaḥ ॥ 155 ॥
tavāpyupari khaṅgaṁ karṣan kō na lajjatē sakarṇaḥ । strījanamadhyē yaḥ subhaṭatvaṁ prakāśayasi ? ॥ 156 ॥
kintu yathā tathā duṣṭānāṁ nigrahaḥ kṣattriyaiḥ kartavyaḥ । tasmānna bhavasi tvamadānī, bhaṇiṣyasi vārtā na mē kathitā ॥
ēvaṁ bhaṇitvā kumāraḥ kōṣāt karṣati tataḥ khaḍgam । sō'pi gr̥hītōgrakhaḍgō valatē tasyōpari kōpēna ॥ 158 ॥
āpatitaḥ saṁgrāmaḥ, kumārēṇa nihataḥ sa duṣṭātmā । tatō'dhastastāstisrō'pi kanyāstaccharaṇam ॥ 159 ॥
prāptā bhaṇanti taṁ vayamētēna vacanabaddhāḥ | mōcitāstvayā tataḥ kumārō bhaṇati kathaṁ tasya ॥ 160॥
vacanacchalē patitāḥ, ēkā tataḥ kathayati nijapitr̥gr̥hē । kuṭṭimatalē lōṭhantyētēna haṭhānītāraṇyē || 161 ॥
udgīrṇō mamōpari yamajihvādatirala karavālaḥ । maraṇabhayakampanaśīlāhaṁ bhaṇitaitēna pāpēna ॥ 162 ॥
yadi manyasē mama vacanaṁ tatō jīvitaṁ tavētarathā naiva । kiṁ tat kathaya bhaṇitē tēnēdaṁ kathitaṁ mama ॥ 163॥
yathā prajñaptividyā prārabdhā sādhayituṁ mayā tatra । jāpē kriyamāṇē ṣaṇmāsān yāvat pratidivasam ॥ 164 ॥

bhakkharadiyakahā |
156
tā ēkkā tāva tumaṁ paidiyahaṁ ējja maha vimāṇēṇa । taha purisasaṁgamōvi hu vihiyacvō maha aṇunnāē ॥
kahiyavvaṁ ca na kassavi ēyaṁ iya kāriyā ya savahasayaṁ । sikkhaviyāhaṁ vīṇaṁ annāuvi tinni kumarīō।।
mannāviyāṁ vayaṇaṁ jahēva haṁ taha kalāu sikkhatriyā । bhaṇiyaṁ ca tāṇa samuhaṁ jaha tumhāṇaṁ vimāṇāī ||
dēvī ahiṭṭiyāī jattha va tattha va nisāē ērhiti । ruhiya tāī sigyaṁ pannattīdēvibhavaṇāmi ॥169 ॥
āgaṁtavvaṁ tattha ya picchaṇayachaṇō khaṇaṁ vihēyavvō । ittiyadiṇāī sirasā paḍicchiyā tassa iya āṇā ||
kiṁtu na sīlabbhaṁsō tēṇa kaō amha iya guṇō tassa । tumha pasāēṇihiṁ saṁjāyaṁ sutthamamhāṇaṁ ॥ 171 ॥
tō kumarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ juttaṁ tumhāṇa saṁpayaṁ gaṁtuṁ । niyaniyajaṇayagihēsu jamhā bhayaṇīu maha tumhē || 172 ||
tāu bhaṇati kaha tattha vr̥ccimō tavtrimāṇarahiyāō ? | tō kumarasumaraṇēṇa vijjāsiddhō lahum̐ pattō ॥ 173 ॥
ārōviḍaṁ vimāṇē tāō sō nēi niyaniyagihēsu । taha kaṇagavaicēḍīsahiyaṁ kumaraṁpi taggē || 174 |
tō vijjāharamaraṇāivaiyaraṁ sāhiūṇa dāsīē । bhaṇiyaṁ nitrbhayahiyayā sammaṁ aṇuvattahi kumāraṁ ॥ 176 ॥
tō kaṇagavaī jaṁpai dubbalahiyayāē ittiyadiṇāṇi । tumhaṁ paricaraṇāē nāha ! maē vaṁciō appā ||
taha. atthi tassa baṁdhū aippayaṁḍōti kaṁpai maṇaṁ mē । mā bhāhi bhaṇai kumarō baṁdhudasaṁ sōvi lahuṁ lahihī ॥
tō nēhasārasarisaṁ khaṇaṁ gamēuṁ tahi ciya pattō । kaṇagavaīē sahiō ukkhittō gayaṇamaggami || 178 ||
tacchullabhāuṇā sō vittō jalahimmi divvajōēṇa | saṁpattaphalahakhaṁḍō uttinnō sattaraṁ tēṇa ।। 179 ॥
samavayaḥ samavarṇasalakṣaṇābhistaruṇībhī rājakanyābhiḥ । vidhātavyaṁ prēkṣaṇakaṁ purataḥ prajñaptidavyāḥ ॥ 165॥
tasmādēkā tāvattvaṁ pratidivasamēyā mama vimānēna । tathā puruṣasaṁgamō'pi khalu vidhātavyō mamānujñayā ॥ 166 ॥
kathayitatryaṁ ca na kasyāpyētāditi kāritā ca śapathaśatam । śikṣitā'haṁ vīṇāmanyā api tisraḥ kumāryaḥ ॥
mānitā vacanaṁ yathaivāhaṁ tathā kalāśca śikṣitāḥ । bhaṇitaṁ ca tāsāṁ saṁmukhaṁ yathā yuṣmākaṁ vimānāni ॥ 168 ॥
dēvyādhiṣṭhitāni yatra vā tatra vā niśi ēṣyanti । āruhya tāni śīghraṁ prajñaptidēvī bhavanē ॥ 169॥
āgantavyaṁ tatra ca prēkṣaṇakakṣaṇaḥ kṣaṇaṁ vidhātatryaḥ । iyaddināni śirasā pratīṣṭā tasyēyamājñā ॥ 170 ॥
kintu na śīlabhraṁśastēna kr̥tō'smākamiti guṇastasya । yuṣmākaṁ prasādēnēdānīṁ saṁjātaṁ sausthyamasmākam ॥
tataḥ kumārēṇa bhaṇitaṁ yuktaṁ yuṣmākaṁ sāṁprataṁ gantum । nijanijajanakagr̥hēṣu yasmādbhaginyō mama yūyam ॥ 172 ॥
tā bhaṇanti kathaṁ tatra vrajāmastadvimānarahitāḥ । tataḥ kumārasmaraṇēna vidyā siddhō laghu prāptaḥ ॥ 173॥
ārōpya vimānē tāḥ sa nayati nijanijagr̥hēṣu । tathā kanakavatīcēṭīsahitaṁ kumāramapi tahē ॥ 174॥
tatō vidyādharamaraṇādivyatikaraṁ kathayitvā dāsyā । bhaṇitaṁ nirbhayahr̥dayā samyaganuvartasva kumāram ॥ 175 ॥
tataḥ kanakavatī jalpati durbalahr̥dayayēyaddināni । tava paricaraṇāyāṁ nātha ! mayā vañcita ātmā ॥ 176॥
tathā'sti tasya bandhuratipracaṇḍa iti kampatē manō mē । mā bhaiṣīrbhaṇati kumārō bandhudaśāṁ sō'pi laghu lapsyasē ||
tataḥ snēhasārasadr̥śaṁ kṣaṇaṁ gamayitvā tatraiva prasuptaḥ । kanakavatyā sahita utkṣiptō gaganamārgē ॥ 178॥

supāsanāha-cariammi—
jalanihitami tattō tāvasakumarēṇa āsamapayammi । nīō tattha ya diṭṭhā kaṇagavaī tō kumārēṇa ॥ 180 ॥
puṭṭhā ya kahiṁ khittā tēṇaṁ, sā kahai pavvaē, tattō । pamuiyacittō pattō kulavaiṇō pāyamūlam ॥ 189 ॥
kumarō vaṁdaṇaputraṁ ālāvaṁ kiṁci tēṇa saha kāuṁ । uvaviṭṭhō tō bhaṇi kulavaṇā tumha bhajjēsā ? ॥ 182 ॥
tō bhaṇiyaṁ kumarēṇaṁ āmaṁ, tō kulavaī kahai ēvaṁ | jalanihitaḍamma diṭṭhā ubbaṁdhatī ihappāṇaṁ || 183 ||
paḍisiddhā amhēhiṁ kahiyaṁ ca imīē vallahō tujjha । milihī ihēva taiē diṇammi, jāyaṁ ca taṁ savvaṁ ॥ 184॥
bhayavaṁ ! aṇuggō mē vihiō tumhēhiṁ para hiyara ēhi । iccāi jaṁpiūṇaṁ pattō kumarō piyāpāsē || 185 ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ ya tēṇa suṁdari ! vihiṇō sacchaṁdacāriṇō cariyaṁ । ēyaṁ taṁ jaṁ satthē niṇijjai puvvamuṇikahiyē ।
viess saṁghaḍiyaṁpi hu puṇōvi saṁghaḍai vihaḍiyaṁ saṁtaṁ । saṁghaḍaṇavihaḍaṇāvāvaḍēṇa vihiṇā jaṇō naḍiō |
puvvabhavōvajjiyagaruyadukkayavasavattiṇō jaē jīvā । taṁ natthi kiṁpi dukkhaṁ saṁsārē jaṁna pāviti ॥ 188 |
sunnārannāī samāsayati caiūṇamiha kalattāī । ēēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ suṁdari ! muṇiṇō mahābhāgā ॥। 189 ।
bhōgāmisamma giddhā laddhā gihavāsaghaṇakalattēsu । amhārisā ahannā kiṁ suṁdari ! jaṁ na pāvaṁti ? || 190 ।
iccāi jaṁpiūṇaṁ kaṇagavaīṁ gahiya girinaī pattō । tō majjiuṁ jahicchaṁ bhujaṁti phalāī, aha dōvi ॥191॥
tatthēva pattāī rayaṇīē avahiyāī tēṇēva । khittāī puṇō rayaṇāyarammi puṇaravi ya miliyāī ॥ 192॥
kiṁ ajjautta ! ēyaṁ, kumarō pabhaṇēi suṁdari ! na kiṁpi । vihivilāsayaṁ vimōttuṁ ēsā tō bhaṇai kiṁ ēvaṁ ? |
tatkṣudrabhrātrā sakṣiptō jaladhau daivayōgēnaṁ । saṁprāptaphalakakhaṇḍa uttīrṇaḥ satvaraṁ tēna ॥ 179 ॥
jalanidhitaṭē tatastāpasakumārēṇāśramapadē । nītastatra ca dr̥ṣṭā kanakavatī tataḥ kumārēṇa ॥ 180 ॥
pr̥ṣṭā ca kva kṣiptā tēna, sā kathayati parvatē, tataḥ । pramuditacittaḥ prāptaḥ kulapatēḥ pādamūlē ॥ 189 ॥
kumārō vandanapūrvamālāpaṁ kiñcit tēna saha kr̥tvā । upaviṣṭastatō bhaṇitaḥ kulapatinā tava bhāṣā ॥ 182 ॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ kumārēṇāma, tataḥ kulapatiḥ kathayatyēvam । jalanidhitaṭē dr̥ṣṭōdhnantīhātmānam ॥ 183॥
pratiṣiddhā'smābhiḥ kathitaṁ cāsyai vallabhastava । mēliṣyatīhaiva tr̥tīyē dinē, jātaṁ ca tat sarvam ॥ 184 ॥
bhagavan ! anugrahō mē vihitō yuṣmābhiḥ parahitarataiḥ । ityādi jalpitvā prāptaḥ kumāraḥ priyāpārśvē ॥ 185 ॥
bhaṇitaṁ ca tēna sundari ! vidhēḥ svacchandacāriṇaścaritam । ētattad yacchāstrē śrūyatē pūrvamunikathitam ॥ 186 ।
vighaṭatē saṁghaṭitamapi khalu punarapi saṁghaṭatē vighaṭitaṁ sat । saṁghaṭanavighaṭanavyāpr̥tēna vidhinā janō naṭitaḥ ॥ 187 |
pūrvabhavōpārjitaguruduṣkr̥tavaśavartinō jagati jīvāḥ । tannāsti kimapi duḥkhaṁ saṁsārē yanna prāpnuvanti ॥ 188॥
śūnyāraṇyāni samāśrayanti tyaktvēha kalatrāṇi । ētēna kāraṇēna sundari ! munayō mahābhāgāḥ ॥ 189 ॥
bhōgāmiṣē gr̥ddhā lubdhā gr̥havāsadhanakalatrēṣu । asmādr̥śā adhanyāḥ kiṁ sundari ! yanna prāpnuvanti ? ॥ 190॥
ityādi jalpitvā kanakavatīṁ gr̥hītvā giriṇadīṁ prāptaḥ । tatō majjitvā yathēcchaṁ bhuñjātē phalāni, atha dvāvapi।
tatraiva prasuptau rajanyāmapahr̥tau tēnaiva । kṣiptau punā ratnākarē punarapi ca militau ॥192॥
kimāryaputra ! ētat, kumāraḥ prabhaṇati sundari ! na kimapi । vidhivilasitaṁ vimucyaiṣā tatō bhaṇati kimēvam ।

divvassa matthara pāḍiūṇa savvaṁ sarhati kāurisā । divvōvi tāṇa saṁkai jāṇaṁ tēō pariṣphura || 194॥
tā mā muyasu mahāyasa ! ucchāhaṁ bhuvaṇapasariyapayāva ! । iya majjhatthō taṁ jāva tāva annō pariṣphurai ||
taṁ kattha gayaṁ tuha nāha ! pōrisaṁ garuyasattuniṭavaṇaṁ । iyarēṇēva sahijjai jamiyaṁ dukkhāṇa richōlī ? ||
āyanniūṇa vayaṇaṁ kaṇagavaīē taō bhaṇai kumarō । divvassava adiṭṭhassa ariṇō iha karau kiṁ purisō ? ।।
iya bhaṇiuṁ rayaṇīē apamattō jāva ciṭṭhaē tāva । sō pattō tō dhariḍaṁ pāēṁ bhāmiu gaṇē ॥ 198 ॥
aphālissai dharaṇīē jāva tā tēṇa virasamārasiyaṁ । rakkhasu kumāra ! rakkhasu khamasu imē majjha avarāhē ॥
na puṇō ēvaṁ kā tujjhāhaṁ kiṁkarō taō tēṇa । mukkō dayāē khayarō dīṇēsu na dāruṇā garuyā ॥ 200 ॥

daivasya mastakē pātayitvā sarva sahantē kāpuruṣāḥ । daivamapi tēbhyaḥ śaṅkatē yēṣāṁ tējaḥ parisphurati ॥194॥
tasmād mā muñca mahāyaśaḥ ! utsāhaṁ bhuvanaprasr̥tapratāpa ! | iti madhyasthastvaṁ yāvattāvadanyaḥ parisphurati ॥ 195॥

ēvaṁ dinnāsīsā kaya saṁbhāsā ya tāvasijaṇēṇa । kumarēṇa samaṁ caliyā, vijjāsiddhaṁ sarai kumarō || 213 ॥
kēṇāvi kāraṇēṇa nahu pattō sō taō varamuttē । maggaṭhiō tāvasajuō caraṇēhiṁ caiva saṁcaliō ॥ 214॥
jāva simasanihāṇaṁ, pattō nagarassa bāhirujjāṇē । sūrappahābhihāṇō diṭṭhō sūrī bhavasarūvaṁ ||215 ||
bhaviyāṇa parūvaṁtō kumarēṇaṁ paṇamiuṁ taō ya khaṇaṁ । nisuō jiṇidadhammō bhāvēṇa ya pariṇaō tassa ।।
mahuraṁpi sūrivayaṇaṁ kaḍuyaṁ ciya avagayaṁ tamiyarīē । aipittapalittāṇaṁ mahurā kiṁ sakarā bhāi ? || 217||

।

kanakavatyapi khalu natvā tāpasanāthaṁ samaṁ parijanēna । kṣamayati tāpasīrviśēṣataścaraṇanihitaśirāḥ ॥ 208 ॥
tābhirapi bahalanirantarasnēhavaśa nirgatāśrudhārābhiḥ । vanatāpasībhirbhaṇitaṁ saduḥkhamētādr̥śaṁ vacanam ||209||
adyāsmābhirapi jñātai priyayōgaḥ kāraṇaṁ guruduḥkhānām । nivartamānē yattasmiñjāyatē nārakaṁ duḥkham || 210॥
tataḥ kiṁvēha bhaṇyatāṁ saṁsārē'tra sarvajīvānām । saṁyōgād viyōgō jāyatē tatō vraja sukhēna ॥ 219 ॥
priyadarśanadhana yaśōjīvitānāṁ sajjanasamāgamānāṁ ca । kaḥ saṁtōṣaṁ prāpnōtyēkaṁ muktvā jitarāgam ॥212॥
ēvaṁ dattāśīḥ kr̥tasaṁbhāṣā ca tāpasījanēna । kumārēṇa samaṁ calitā, vidyāsiddhaṁ smarati kumāraḥ ॥ 213॥
kēnāpi kāraṇēna na khalu prāptaḥ sa tatō varamuhūrttē । mārgasthitastāpasayutaścaraṇābhyāmēva saṁcalitaḥ ॥ 214॥

”
bhavikēbhyaḥ prarūpayan kumārēṇa praṇamya tataśca kṣaṇam । śrutō jinēndradharmō bhāvēna ca pariṇatastasya || 216॥
madhuramapi sūrivacanaṁ kaṭukamēvāvagataṁ taditarayā । atipittapradīptānāṁ madhurā kiṁ śarkarā bhāti ? || 217॥
tataḥ kanakavatī bhaṇitā sundari ! satyaṁ na sundara ēṣaḥ । saṁsārō duḥkhasārō viṣamaḥ karmaṇāṁ pariṇāmāt॥218॥
bahupratyavāyabhr̥tō gr̥havāsa indriyāṇi capalāni । atikuṭilā prēmagatiḥ kō jānāti kathamiva pariṇamati ? |
1 ka. kumarē piē ! na ।

bhakkhara diyakā
163.
kiṁpuṇa viyārabahulaṁ duṣaṁ nāha ! jāvvaṇāranaṁ । aivisamō visamasarō na jahicchaṁ māṇiyā bhōgā ||
bhōttr̥̄ṇa rāyalacchiṁ pacchā tō pucchiuṁ kamavi nāṇi । thaivammi āusēsē jaṁ uciyaṁ taṁ karissāmō ||
tataḥ kumāraḥ prāha;-
dullaṁghattaṁ jaṁ juvvaṇassa tēṇavi ya kāraṇēṇa buhā । ēyammi vayaṁ gahiuṁ aviyārā huti thēravva ॥ 223||
tathā cōktam ;-
tathā;
" manasi jarasābhibhūtā jāyantē yauvanē'pi vidvāṁsaḥ । mūḍhadhiyaḥ punaranyē bhavanti vr̥ddhatvayōgē'pi ॥"
kāurimāṇaṁ visamō visamasarō na uṇa dhīrapurisāṇa । maṁsammi khaggadhārā tinhā na uṇō ya vajjammi ||
na jahicchē iccāivi na suṁdaraṁ bhōgalāliō jīvō । saggēsuvi na ya tittō jalaṇō iva havvanivahēhi ॥
jāṇijjara avasamma suyaṇu ! bhōgēhiṁ nicchiō naraō । cattēhi tēhiṁ jāyai gamaṇaṁ saggāpavaggēsu ॥ 226 ॥
'bhōttūṇa rāyalacchiṁ' jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ tattha tīē giddhīē । hōi ahōgamaṇaṁ ciyanaya ittha suhaṁ jaō bhaṇiyaṁ ॥
" autsukyamātramavasādayati pratiṣṭhāṁ klēśastu labdhaparipālanavr̥ttirēva ।
naiva śramāpanayanāya yathā śramāya rājyaṁ svahastadhr̥tadaṇḍamivātapatram ॥
'nāṇi pucchiya' āussē sē jaṁ bhaṇasi taṁpi hu na juttaṁ । dhammēṇa viṇā suṁdari ! jīvaṁtāvi hu mayaccaiva ॥
yataḥ-
yasya dharmavihīnasya dinānyāyānti yānti ca । ma lōhakārabhastrēva śvasannapi na jīvati ॥
iyaṁ bhaṇiūṇaṁ namiūṇa jinavaraṁ milliūṇa taṁ bāhiṁ । gaṁtuṁ nagarassaṁtō jyavidvattēṇa davvēṇa ॥ 229||
kārāviūṇa bhōjaṁ pattō tatthēva jattha sā mukkā । kāūṇaṁ pāṇavitti tatthēva ṭhiyāī khaṇamēgaṁ ॥ 230॥
tasmādētāni sundari ! svayaṁ tyajāvaḥ pratrajāvō mārgam । pūrvapuruṣānucīrṇaṁ tatō bhaṇitaṁ tayaivamidam ॥ 220॥
kintu vikāra bahulaṁ durlaṅgha nātha ! yauvanāraṇyam । ativiṣamō viṣamaśarō na yathēcchaṁ mānitā bhōgāḥ ॥ 229 ॥
bhuktvā rājalakṣmī paścāt tataḥ pr̥ṣṭrā kamapi jñāninam । stōka āyuḥ śēṣē yaducitaṁ tat kariṣyāvaḥ ॥222॥
durlaṅghatvaṁ yad
yauvanasya tēnāpi ca kāraṇēna budhāḥ । ētasmin vrataṁ gr̥hītvā'vikārā bhavanti sthavirā iva ॥
kāpuruṣāṇāṁ viṣamō viṣamaśarō na punardhīrapuruṣāṇām । māṁsē khaḍgadhārā tīkṣṇā na punaśca vajrē || 224 ॥
I
na yathēcchamityādyapi na sundaraṁ bhōgalālitō jīvaḥ । svargēṣvapi na ca tr̥ptō jvalana iva havyanivahaiḥ ।। 225॥
jñāyatē'vasānē sutanu ! bhōgairniścitō narakaḥ । tyaktaistairjāyatē gamanaṁ svargāpavargayōḥ ॥ 226 ॥
'bhuktvā rājalakṣmīṁ ' yadbhaṇitaṁ tatra tasyāṁ gr̥jyā । bhavatyadhōgamanamēva nacātra sukhaṁ yatō bhaṇitam ॥ 227॥
"
jñāninaṁ pr̥ṣṭrā''yuḥ śēṣē ' yadbhaṇasi tadapi hi na yuktam । dharmēṇa vinā sundari ! jīvantāvapi hi mr̥tāvē"
iti bhaṇitvā nattrā jinavaraṁ muktvā tāṁ bahiḥ 1 gatvā nagarasyāntadyūtārjitēna dravyēṇa ॥ 229 ॥
kārayitvā bhōjyaṁ prāptastatraiva yatra sa muktā । kr̥tvā prāṇavr̥ttiṁ tatraiva sthitau kṣaṇamakam ॥ 230 ॥

supāsanāha caritrammi--
1
aha pēcchai kaṇagavaī sunnamaṇaṁ, hōjja kāraṇaṁ kimiha । sajaṇāṇa sumaraṇaṁvā paṁthēṇa va vāhiyā ahiyē ? ||
iya ciṁtaṁtō kumarō sarīracitaṁ karitu jā valiō । tō virahiṇiva pēcchai kaṇagavaī bahuviyārilaṁ ||232 ॥
ālihai cittakammaṁ kaṁṭhē ghōlēi paṁcamuggāraṁ । bāhajalabhariyanayaṇā hariṇivvaṁ nirikkhara disāō ||
vāmakarōvarisaṁṭhiyamuhapaṁkayamukadīhanīsāsā । abhaṇatacciya sāhai mayaṇaviyā uraṁ cittaṁ ॥ 234 ॥
kumarō cita kimimā karē iya viṣpalaṁbhaciṭṭhāō। kiṁ majjha khaṇaviōē kimannahā ahava kiṁ bahuṇā ।।
jai maṁ pikkhēūṇaṁ aṇālā hōhihī taō nr̥ṇaṁ । mai aṇurattā aha saṁvarissara tō na laṭṭhēti || 236 ||
iya āsannō hōuṁ appāṇaṁ tīē daṁsai taō sā । saṁvariyamayaṇaciṭṭhā abbhuddhivi saṁmuhā ēi || 237 ॥
uvavidvēṇaṁ puṭṭhā suṁdari ! dīsasi kimēvamuvviggā ? । kiṁ sumarasi sayaṇāṇaṁ sā jaṁpai kimiha sayaṇēhiṁ ? ॥
rannapi hōi vasimaṁ jattha jaṇō hiyayavallahō milai । piyavirahiyāṇa vasiṁmaṁpi hōi aḍavīi sāricchaṁ 239
kumarō cita viyaraphāravayaṇāī jaṁpaē ēsā । tā nūṇamanēhacciya lakkhijjai vayaṇarayaṇāhi || 240 ॥
jaō ।
|
vīsaṁbhaparavasēhivi parūḍhasambhāvapēmapasarammi । uvayārō kīrai māṇusammi kattō vaiyaṁ ēyaṁ ॥ 249 ॥
uvayārēhi parōcci ppii agghaṁti tē tarhi caiva । iyarammi pavattaṁtā pēmābhāvaṁ payāsaṁti ॥ 242 ॥
tō bhaviyavvaṁ iha kāraṇēṇa muṇiūṇa uḍiō kumarō । nidāmuddiyadiṭṭhīē tīē pattō vaṇassaṁtō ॥ 243॥
,
atha paśyati kanakavatīṁ śūnyamanasaṁ bhavētkāraṇaṁ kimiha । svajanānāṁ smaraṇaṁ vā pathā vā bādhitā'dhikam ? ॥
iti cintayankumāraḥ śarīracintāṁ kr̥tvā yāvadvalitaḥ । tatō virahiṇīmiva paśyati kanakavatī bahuvikāriṇīm ॥
ālikhati citrakarma kaṇṭhē ghūrṇayatē pañcamōdvāram । bāṣpajalabhr̥tanayanā hariṇīva nirīkṣatē diśaḥ ॥ 233॥
vāmakarōparisaṁsthitamukhapaṅkajamuktadīrghaniḥśvāsā | abhaṇantyēva kathayati madanavikārāturaṁ cittam ||234||
kumāraścintayati kimiyaṁ karōtīti vipralambhacēṣṭāḥ । kiṁ mama kṣaṇaviyōgē kimanyathāthavā kiṁ bahunā ? || 235 ॥
yadi māṁ prēkṣyānākulā bhaviṣyati tatō nūnam । mayyanuraktā'ya saṁvariṣyati tatō na sundaramiti ॥ 236 ॥
ityāsannō bhūtvā''tmānaṁ tasyai darśayati tataḥ sā । saṁvr̥tamadana cēṣṭā'bhyutthāya saṁmukhaiti ॥ 237॥
upaviṣṭēna pr̥ṣṭā sundari ! dr̥śyasē kimēvamudvignā । kiṁ smarāsa svajanānāṁ sā jalpati kimiha svajanaiḥ ? | 238|
araṇyamapi bhavati vasatiryatra janō hr̥dayavallabhō milati । priyavirahitānāṁ vasatirapi bhavatyavyā sadr̥śī ॥ 239 ॥
kumāṅkaścintayati vikārasphāravacanāni jalpatyēṣā । tasmānnūnamasnēhaiva lakṣyatē vacanaracanābhiḥ ॥ 240॥
yataḥ ।
viśrambhaparavaśairapi prarūḍhasadbhāvaprēmaprasarē । upacāraḥ kriyatē mānuṣē kutō vratamētat ? ॥ 249 ॥
upacāraiḥ para ēva gr̥hyatē rājanti tē tatraiva । itarasmin pravartamānāḥ prēmābhāvaṁ prakāśayanti ॥ 242 ॥
tatō bhavitavyamiha kāraṇēna jñātvōtthitaḥ kumāraḥ । nidrāmuṣitadr̥ṣṭyāṁ tasyāṁ prāptō vanasyāntaḥ ॥243॥
1 ka. kha. uva° । 2 kha. ga. vyayaṁ ।

makkhara diyakahā |
1
265
diṭṭhō ēgō purisō tēṇaṁ sō pucchiō jahā kumarō । kiṁ iha ciṭṭara, tēṇaṁ sō puḍhō ēsa kō kumarō ? ।।
sirivijayacaṁdarannō guṇacaṁdō nāma vissuō puttō । ēsōvi tē na nāō taha kahiyaṁ tēṇa purisēṇa ||
kāvi hu naravaradhūyā cihna samāgayā tahappāṁsē । majjhanē sō pattō ahaṁ tu kajjēṇa paṭṭaviō || 246 ॥
ēēṇa kāraṇēṇa pucchāmi tayaṁ, taō ya kumarēṇa । bhaṇiyaṁ siddhasamīhiyakajjō kumarō gaō ṭhāṇē ॥ 247 ॥
tō tē puṇō puṭṭhō kiṁ ghaḍiyā tassa, tēṇa sō bhaṇiō । ghaḍiyā na kēvalaṁ kiṁtu tēṇa nīyā niyaṁ bhavaṇaṁ ॥
daḍhamaṇuratō tī kumarō tō suṁdaraṁ imaṁ jāyē । iya bhaṇiuṁ nīhariō sa narō ujjāṇamajjhāō || 249 ॥
tō ciṁtas kumarō ritthu saṁsāravilasiyāṇamiha । ahaha ahō ! guvilāṇaṁ viratthu itthīsahāvā ||250 ||
na guṇēṇaṁ nēya rūvēṇa nōvayārēṇa nahu jiēṇāvi । ghippaṛa mahilāṇa maṇaṁ cavalaṁ pavaṇuddhuyadhayaṁva ॥ 259॥
niyahiyaya sarisamēsā jāva na āyarai tāva ēyamahaṁ । māulagagihē mōtaṇa niyayamahaṁ pasāhēmi || 252 ॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa kumarō gaō sayāsammi tīē, bhaṇiyā ya । ēhi lahuṁ gacchāmō tuhamāmaganiyaḍagāmammi ||
sāvi bhai paccūsē gacchassamahaṁ taō ya sā bhaṇiyā । laddhō saṁpai satthō tā na khamaṁ iha nilaṁbē ||
muttūṇa tattha cittaṁ caliyā kāraṇa tattha pattāī । pañcabhināyā tēhivi, kahiō avaharaṇavatō || 255 ॥
rayaṇīē taṁ sutaṁ mōtuṁ kumarō viṇiggaō ēttō । niyadhammagurusayāsē vihiṇā paḍivajjaē dikkha || 256 ||
paḍhiūṇa taō sutaṁ ēkallavihārapaḍimapaḍivannō । viharaṁtō iha pattō, sō ya ahaṁ, tēṇa kayamēvaṁ ॥ 257॥
kahiyaṁ tumhāṇa maē niyanivvēyassa kāraṇaṁ, tubhē । tā muttuṁ gihivāsa dahavāsaṁ kuṇaha pavvajjaṁ || 258 ॥
dr̥ṣṭa ēkaḥ puruṣastēna sa pr̥ṣṭō yathā kumāraḥ । kimiha tiṣṭhati, tēna sa pr̥ṣṭa ēṣa kaḥ kumāraḥ 1 ॥ 244 ॥
śrīvijayacandrarājasya guṇacandrō nāma viśrutaḥ putraḥ । ēṣō'pi tē na jñātastathā kathitaṁ tēna puruṣēṇa ॥ 245॥
kāpi khalu narapatiduhitā tiṣṭhati samāgatā tathā pārśvē । madhyāhnē sa prāptō'haṁ tu kāryēṇa prasthāpitaḥ ॥ 246 ॥
ētēna kāraṇēna pr̥cchāmi tvāṁ tataśca kumārēṇa । bhaṇitaṁ siddhasamīhitakāryaḥ kumārō gataḥ sthānē || 247 ||
tatastēna punaḥ pr̥ṣṭaḥ kiṁ ghaṭitā tasya tēna sa bhaṇitaḥ । ghaṭitā na kēvalaṁ kintu tēna nītā nijaṁ bhavanam ॥
dr̥ḍhamanuraktastasyāṁ kumārastataḥ sundaramidaṁ jātam । iti bhaṇitvā niḥsr̥taḥ sa nara udyāna madhyāt ॥ 249॥
tataścintayati kumārō dhigastu saṁsāravilasitānīha । ahaha ahō ! gupilān dhigastu strīsvabhāvān ॥ 250 ॥
na guṇēna naiva rūpēṇa nōpacārēṇa naiva jīvitēnāpi । gr̥hyatē mahilānāṁ manaścapalaṁ pavanōdbhutadhvaja iva ॥259॥
nijahr̥daya sadr̥śamēṣā yāvannācarati tāvadētāmaham । mātulakagr̥hē muktvā nijamarthaṁ prasādhayāmi ॥ 252॥
iti cintayitvā kumārō gataḥ sakāśē tasyāḥ, bhaṇitā ca । ēhi laghu gacchāvastvanmāmakanikaṭagrāmē ॥ 253॥
sāpi bhaṇati pratyūṣē gamiṣyāmyahaṁ tataśca sā bhaṇitā । labdhaḥ saṁprati sārthastasmānna kṣamamiha vilambitum ॥
muktvā tatra cittaṁ calitā kāyēna tatra prāptau । pratyabhijñātō tairapi kathitō'paharaṇavr̥ttāntaḥ ॥255॥
rajanyāṁ tāṁ suptāṁ muktvā kumārō vinirgata itaḥ । nijadharmagurusakāśē vidhinā pratipadyatē dīkṣām ॥256॥
paṭhitvā tataḥ sūtramēkākivihārapratimāpratipannaḥ । viharanniha prāptaḥ sa cāhaṁ tēna kr̥tamēvam ॥ 257॥

"

166
supāsanāha-cariammi
tō bhāgū bhai muṇi bhayavaṁ ! nivvēyahēyavō sulahā । dulahā tē puṇa tumamiva cayaṁti viulēvi jē bhōgē ।
aha bhakkharō paryaṁpai bhayavaṁ ! sā pātrakāriṇī kattha ? । āha muṇī jīē tumē rūpēṇāgarisiyā ittha || 260 ॥
saṁpattā maha pāsē, sō bhai kēṇa kāraṇēṇēsā । jūhabhaṭṭā hariṇivva carai ēgāgiṇī rannē ? || 261 ||
guṇacaṁdakumārammī tattha taō kiṁ imā na saṁghaḍiyā ? । bhaṇai muṇī saṁghaḍiūṇa vihaḍiyā sīlabhaṁsāō ॥
nikāliūṇa mukkā guṇacaṁdēṇaṁ taō bhramaṁtīha । maha didvigōyaragayā lajjāē ahōmuhī jāyā ॥ 263॥
paḍivōhiyā maē tō gihatthadhammō duvālasavihōvi । paḍivanō ēīē, pālēi sammattamūlaṁ taṁ || 264 ||
sayamālihiuṁ paḍimaṁ pūjai sattīē kamalakusumēhiṁ । tikālaṁ vihikaliyā vaṁdai niccapi bhattī || 265॥
kāsāra nijjharāisu nīraṁpi piēi phāsūyaṁ thōvaṁ । kusumapattāī muṁjai āhāramacittamēva imā || 266 ||
saṁvvapurisāṇa niyamō duvihaṁ tivihēṇa tīi paḍivannō । samaē lahihī dikkhaṁ mōkkhaṁpi bhavammi itthēva ||
tō bhō mahāṇubhāvā ! jadhammē ujjamaṁ kuṇaha tubbhē । aha na samatyā sammattamūlagi hidhammamāyaraha || 268 ॥
viraimamatyēhi sammattaṁ caiva tēhi paḍivanaṁ । anēvi kavi niyamē gahiuṁ niyaṭhāṇamaṇupattā ॥ 269 ॥
kuvvaṁti paidiṇaṁ ciya jiṇavaṁdaṇapūyaṇāijiṇadhammaṁ । aha annadiṇē bhaṇiō jēṭṭēṇaṁ baṁdhuṇā bhānū ॥ 270 ॥
baṁdhava ! na yāṇimucciya jiṇadhammatarussa kiṁ phalaṁ hōhī । jiṇadhammaṭhiyā muṇiṇō ya vaccha ! dīsaṁti suirahiyā ||
tō vicchāiyavayaṇō bhāṇū paḍibhaṇai baṁdhava ! na juttaṁ । iya citiuṁpi sammaṁ avagayavatthusahāvāṇaṁ ॥ 272 ॥
kathitaṁ yuvayōrmayā nijanirvēdasya kāraṇaṁ, yuvām । tasmānmuktvā gr̥hivāsaṁ duḥkhavāsaṁ kurutaṁ pravrajyām ॥258॥
tatō bhānurbhaṇati muniṁ bhagavan ! nirvēdahētavaḥ sulabhāḥ । durlabhāstē punaryūyamiva tyajanti vipulānapi yē bhōgān ॥
atha bhāskaraḥ prajalpati bhagavan ! sā pāpakāriṇī kva ? | āha muniryasyā yuvāṁ rūpēṇākr̥ṣṭāvatra ॥। 260॥
saṁprāptau mama pārśvē, sa bhaṇati kēna kāraṇēnaiṣā । yūtha bhraṣṭā hariṇīva caratyēkākinyaraṇyē ? ।। 261 ।।
guṇacandrakumārē tatra tataḥ kimiyaṁ na saṁghaṭitā ? । bhaṇati muniḥ saṁghaṭaya vighaṭitā śīlabhraṁśāt ॥ 262॥
niṣkāśya muktā guṇacandrēṇa tatō bhramantīha । mama dr̥ṣṭigōcaragatā lajjayā dhōmukhī jātā ॥ 263 ॥
pratibōdhitā mayā tatō gr̥hasthadharmō dvādaśavidhō'pi । pratipanna ētayā, pālayati samyaktvamūlaṁ tam ||264 ॥
svayamālikhya pratimāṁ pūjayati śaktyā kamalakusumaiḥ । trikālaṁ vidhikalitā vandatē nityamapi bhaktyā ॥ 265॥
kāsāranirjharādiṣu nīramapi pibati prāsukaṁ stōkam । kusumapatrāṇi bhuṅga āhāramacittamēvēyam ॥ 266 ॥
sarvapuruṣāṇāṁ niyamō dvividhaṁ trividhēna tayā pratipannaḥ । samayē lapsyatē dīkṣāṁ mōkṣamapi bhavē'traiva || 267 ||
tatō bhō mahānubhāvau ! yatidharma udyamaṁ kurutaṁ yuvām । atha na samarthōṁ samyaktvamūlagr̥hidharmamācaratam ॥ 268 ॥
viratyasamarthābhyāṁ samyaktvamēva tābhyāṁ pratipannam । anyānapi katyapi niyamān gr̥hītvā nijasthānamanuprāptau ॥
kurutaḥ pratidinamēva jinavandanapūjanādijinadharmam । athānyadinē bhāṇatō jyēṣṭhēna bandhunā bhānuḥ ॥270॥
bāndhava ! na jānīva ēva jinadharmatarōḥ kiṁ phalaṁ bhaviṣyati । jinadharmasthitā munayaśca vatsa ! dr̥śyantē śucirahitāḥ॥
tatō vicchāditavadanō bhānuḥ pratibhaṇati bāndhava ! na yuktam । iti cintayitumapi samyagavagatavastusvabhāvānām ॥

" niḥspr̥hō nādhikārī syānnākāmī maṇḍanapriyaḥ । nāvidagdhaḥ priyaṁ brūyāt sphuṭavaktā na vañcakaḥ ||
ēvaṁ ca durabbhāsā parivaḍihisi mūlaō ya sammattā । tattō viraiguṇāṇavi dūraṁ dūrēṇa taṁ hōsi ।। 275 ||
ēvaṁ ca guṇavimukō kāuṁ asamaṁjasāī bahuyāī । narayāighōradukkhē bhamihisi saṁsārakaṁtārē ||276 ॥
tā duvihaṁpi duguḷaṁ muṁcasu sammatta mē siharāō । mā parivaḍēsu baṁdhava ! dulaha miṇaṁ puṇavi jīvāṇaṁ ।। 277॥
ēvaṁpi bhannamāṇō na durguchaṁ muyai kahavi kammavasā । aha annadiṇē kēṇai nimaṁtiō bhōyaṇaṭṭāē । 278 ॥
tō giṭṭhō jā ciṭṭhai tāva tēṇa bhikkhaṭṭā । diṭṭhō muṇī paviṭṭhō malamaliṇī junnavatthō ya ॥ 279 ॥
taṁ daṭṭhē an taggihasāmī sayaṁ gahiyabhattō । paḍilāi muṇivasahaṁ taha darddha bhakkharō bhai || 280 ॥
tam gammi gihāō kamahō ! kaṭumitthamannāṇaṁ । tumhārisāvi ēvaṁ vivēiṇō iya aṇuta ॥ 289 ॥
kimimēṇaṁ sudēṇaṁ lōyavyavahārabāhirāsuiṇā । jalamalāvilataṇuṇā sayāvi jalasōyarahiēṇa ? || 282 ||
vaṇiṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁ amhāṇaṁ imāē ciṁtāē ? । gihamāgayassavassaṁ dāyavvā bhikkhuṇō bhikkhā।। 283 ।।
sāya bahumāṇaputraṁ dijjaṁtī bahuphalā havai aphalā । appaphalā vā iharā tō paḍasi kimiha annāṇaṁ ? |
śucirahitā yad munayō, bhaṇatha na samyagidamapi yadētān । suviśuddhabrahmacaryānmuktvā'nyasya kasya śaucam ? ||
malamalitadēhavastrā asnānaratā vimuktatāmbūlāḥ । na khalvaśucayō yadēpa paramō brahmavratōpāyaḥ || 274 ॥
vibhūṣā strīsaṁsargaḥ praṇītaṁ rasabhōjanam । narasya trikavaśinō viṣaṁ tālapuḍhaṁ yathā ॥
ēvaṁ ca durabhyāsāt paripatiṣyati mūlataśca samyaktvāt । tatō viratiguṇānāmapi dūraṁ dūrēṇa tvaṁ bhavasi ||
ēvaṁ ca guṇavimuktaḥ kr̥tvā'samañjasāni bahūni । narakādivōraduḥkhē bhramiṣyasi saṁsārakāntārē ||276 ॥
tasmād dvividhāmapi jugupsāṁ muñca, samyaktvamēruśikharāt । mā paripata bāndhava ! durlabhamidaṁ punarapi jīvānām ॥
ēvamapi bhaṇyamānō na jugupsāṁ muñcati kathamapi karmavaśāt । athānyadinē kēnacinnimantritō bhōjanārtham ॥
tatastadgr̥hōpaviṣṭō yāvattiṣṭhati tāvattēna bhikṣārtham । dr̥ṣṭō muniḥ praviṣṭō malamalinō jīrṇavastraśca ॥ 279॥
taṁ dr̥ṣṭrā'bhyuttiṣṭhati tadgr̥hasvāmī svayaṁ gr̥hītabhaktaḥ । pratilambhayati munivr̥ṣabhaṁ tathā dr̥ṣṭrā bhāskarō bhaṇati ॥
tasmin gatē gr̥hāt kaṣṭamahō ! kaṣṭamitthamajñānam । yuṣmādr̥śā apyēvaṁ vivēkina ityanutiṣṭhanti ॥ 281॥
kimanēna śūdrēṇa lōkavyavahāra bāhyāśucinā । jīrṇamalāvilatanunā sadāpi jalaśaucara hitēna ! ॥ 282 ॥
vaṇijā tatō bhaṇitaṁ kimasmākamanayā cintayā ? । gr̥hamāgatāyāvaśyadātavyā bhikṣavē bhikṣā || 283॥
sā ca bahumānapūrva dīyamānā bahuphalā bhavatyaphalā । alpaphalā vētarathā tataḥ prakaṭayasi kimihājñānam ? || 284 ॥

supāsanāha caritryammi
tō bhakkharēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ dijjau dāṇaṁ vaṇīmagajaṇassa । gēhāgayassa kiṁpuṇa sammāṇō māhaṇaṁ māttu ? || 285॥.
kijjatō maha hiyayaṁ tāvara tumhārisēhi suyaṇēhiṁ । vaṇiēṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ mā ēvaṁ bhada ! jaṁpēsu ॥ 286॥
jō carai vaṁbhacēraṁ taṁ ciya iha baṁbhaṇaṁ bhaṇati suī । jō itthipasaṁgaraō sō cciya muddō ya asuī ya॥ 287॥
saparāṇuggahakārī ēsō sammaṁ visuddhaguṇadhārī । nikaṁcaṇō ya amamō amaccharō kucchivalaō || 288 ||
bhadrēṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ kimaṇēṇaṁ vēyavihiyamaggassa । aṇabhinēṇa mahāyasa ! tō vaṇiō mōṇamallīṇō ।। 289 ॥
iya sāhūṇa duguḷaṁ kuṇamāṇō bhakkharō marēūṇa | ciṇiḍaṁ gurupāvacayaṁ uppannō paḍhamaḍhavī || 290 ॥
puvvabhavabaṁdhavō sē sammaṁ paripāliūṇa sammattaṁ । uppannō sōhammē bhāṇū taṁ niyai avahīē ॥ 299 ॥
nēhadayāvasavihuriyahiyaō gaṁtūṇa bhāṇuruvadharō । dūrē paramāhampiyadēvē kāūṇa bhai imaṁ ॥ 292 ॥
vaṁdhava ! ēyamavatthaṁ gayassa tuha kiṁ karēmi ahaminhi । tahavi bhaṇāmi visajjasu jiṇadhammadurguchaparamavisaṁ ॥
jēṇa iō ubvaṭṭō puṇōvi nō sahasi ērisamavatthaṁ । aha sō jaṁpara vaṁdhava ! khayammi kiṁ khivasi maha khāraṁ ।।
taṁ kila mēṁ paccārasi maha bhaṇiyaṁ jaṁ kayaṁ taē na purā । taṁ tuha imā avasthā, tā baṁdhuttēṇa maha hōu || 295 ॥
jāha jahāgayamahamavi bhaviyanvayaḍhōiyaṁ aṇuhavissaṁ । asuittasiō mā kayāvi maha hōu jiṇadhammō ||
tō sō tēṇa vilakkhō kaōvi hiyaēṇa sāṇukaṁpēṇa । sahāṇaṁ saṁpattō puṇō bhaṇissaṁti buddhī || 297 ॥
iyarōvi vivihaviyaṇaṁ sudāruṇaṁ tattha aṇubhavēūṇa । āukkhaēṇa jāō hariṇō davadavabhūmī ॥ 298 ॥
tatō bhāskarēṇa bhaṇitaṁ dīyatāṁ dānaṁ vanīpakajanāya । gēhāgatāya kintu sammānō brāhmaṇaṁ muktvā ॥ 285॥
kriyamāṇō mama hr̥dayaṁ tāpayati yuṣmādr̥śaiḥ sujanaiḥ । vaṇijā tatō bhaṇitaṁ maivaṁ bhadra ! jalpīḥ ॥ 286॥
yaścarati brahmacaryaṁ tamēvēha brāhmaṇaṁ bhaṇanti śucim । yaḥ strīprasaṅgarataḥ sa ēva śūdraścāśuciśca ॥ 287॥
svaparānugrahakāryēṣa samyag viśuddhaguṇadhārī । niṣkāñcanaścāmamō'matsaraḥ kukṣiśambalakaḥ ॥ 288 ॥
bhaṭṭēna tatō bhaṇitaṁ kimanēna vēdavihitamārgasya । anabhijñēna mahāyaśaḥ ! tatō vaṇig maunamālīnaḥ ॥ 289॥
iti sādhūnāṁ jugupsāṁ kurvāṇō bhāskarō mr̥tvā । citvā gurupāpacayamutpannaḥ prathamapr̥thivyām ||290॥
pūrvabhavabāndhavastasya samyak paripālya samyaktvam । utpannaḥ saudharmē bhānustaṁ paśyatyavadhinā ॥ 299 ॥
snēhadayāvaśavidhuritahr̥dayō gatvā bhānurūpadharaḥ । dūrē paramādhārmikadēvān kr̥tvā bhaṇatīdam ॥ 292 ॥
bāndhava ! ētāmavasthāṁ gatasya tava kiṁ karōmyahamidānīm । tathāpi bhaṇāmi visr̥ja jinadharmajugupsāparamaviṣam ॥
yēnēta udvr̥ttaḥ punarapi nō sahasē īdr̥śīmavasthām । atha sa jalpati bāndhava ! kṣatē kiṁ kṣipasi mama kṣāram ॥
tvaṁ kila māmupālabhasē mama bhaṇitaṁ yatkr̥taṁ tvayā na purā । tattavēyamavasthā, tasmādvandhutvēna mama bhavatu ॥ 295॥
yāhi yathāgatamahamapi bhavitavyatādau kitamanubhaviṣyāmi । aśucitvadūṣitō mā kadāpi mama bhavatu jinadharmaḥ ॥
tataḥ sa tēna vilakṣaḥ kr̥tō'pi hr̥dayēna sānukampēna । svasthānaṁ saṁprāptaḥ punarbhaṇiṣyāmīti buddhyā ॥ 297||
itarō'pi vividhavēdanāṁ sudāruṇāṁ tatrānubhūya । āyuḥkṣayēṇa jātō hariṇō davadugdhabhūmau ॥ 298 ॥

tatthavi chuhāpivāsāsīyāyavaviyaṇatāviyasarīrō । jā ciṭṭhaś tā diṭṭhō vāhēṇa haōya nikkaruṇaṁ ।। 299 ।।
jāō akāmanijjaravasaō dēvēsu ainihīṇēsu । tatthavi pattō māṇū bhakkhara bhavavilasiyaṁ kaha | | 300॥
tō sō jaṁpara taiyā sammattaṁ pāliūṇa taṁ jāō । dēvō vimāṇavāsī mahiḍhiō haṁ tu kāūṇa || 301 ||
tattha dugaṁchaṁ pattō ērisaaidusahadukkhadaṁdōliṁ । tahavi mahāyasa ! ēvaṁ aṇusāsasi maṁ ajōgaṁpi॥ 302 ॥
tā mai pāviḍēvi hu kuṣpaṁtēvi hu taē na paricattā । aṇukaṁpā, tō ēttō jiṇadhammō caitra maha saraṇaṁ ॥
iya paḍivanammita majjha kayatthō parissamō jāō । iya bhaṇiuṁ bhāṇusurō taṁ pucchiya ṭhāṇamaṇupattō ॥
aha sō citai imiṇā bhaṇiēṇavi narabhavē na aṇucinnō । jiṇadhammō suharammō avvō ! hā hāriō jammō ॥
jaha kahavi hu hajaṁ māṇusavārau, pāvisu pāvida pāvahavārau ।
jiṇavaradhammu karivi kammārau, na hōhissu kassavi kammāra ॥ 306 ॥
jō jiṇadhammu kahavi saṁpāviu, na ya jiṇavayaṇihiṁ appana bhāviu ।
sō pāyaguruvayarihiṁ pāviu, bhāmijjai saṁsārinivāriu ||307 ||
hauṁ hauṁ lahivi sudhammihiṁ juttara, māṇusajammu pamāi viguttau ।
tēṇa hua suravarakammaraṁḍa, ruṭu daivu ahava kiṁ mārau ? || 308 ||
i appāṇaṁ niṁda vaṁdai dēvē gurū ya bhattīē । aha āuyammi punnē caviḍaṁ caṁpāē uvavannō ॥ 309 ॥
īsaradattassa ō hōuṁ lahiūṇa saṁjamamuyāraṁ । pāviyakēvalanāṇō saṁpatō bhakkharō mōkkhaṁ ॥ 310 ॥
tatrāpi kṣutpipāsāśītātapavēdanātāpitaśarīraḥ । yāvattiṣṭhati tāvad dr̥ṣṭō vyādhēna hataśca niṣkaruṇam ||299॥
jātō'kāmanirjarāvaśatō dēvēṣvatinihīnēṣu । tatrāpi prāptō bhānurbhāskarabhavavilasitaṁ kathayati ॥ 300॥
tataḥ sa jalpati tadā samyaktvaṁ pālayitvā tvaṁ jātaḥ । dēvō vimānavāsī maharddhikō'haṁ tu kr̥tvā ॥ 302 ॥
tatra jugupsāṁ prāpta īdr̥śātiduḥ sahaduḥkhadvandvālim । tathāpi mahāyaśaḥ ! ēvamanuśāssi māmayōgyamapi ॥ 302 ॥
tasmād mayi pāpiṣṭhē'pi khalu kupyatyapi ca tvayā na parityaktā । anukampā, tata itō jinadharma ēva mama śaraṇam ॥
iti pratipannē tvayā mama kr̥tārthaḥ pariśramō jātaḥ । iti bhaṇitvā bhānusurastaṁ pr̥ṣṭrā sthānamanuprāptaḥ ॥ 204॥
atha sa cintayatyanēna bhaṇitēnāpi narabhavē nānucīrṇaḥ | jinadharmaḥ sukharamyō hanta ! hā ! hāritaṁ janma ||305॥
yadi kathamapi khalvahaṁ mānuṣyavāraṁ, prāpsyāmi pāvitaṁ pāpavārakam ।
'
jinavaradharma kr̥tvā karmavārakaṁ, na bhaviṣyāmi kasyāpi karmacārakaḥ ॥ 306 ॥
yēna jinadharmaṁ kathamapi saṁprāpya, na ca jinavacainairātmā bhāvitaḥ
sa pramādaguruvairibhiḥ pāpī, bhrāmyatē saṁsārē'nivāritaḥ ॥307॥
hā hā ! labdhvā sudharmairyuktaṁ, mānuṣyajanma pramādēna viguptam ।
tēna bhūtaḥ suravārakarmacārakō, ruṣyatu daivamathavā kiṁ mārayatu ? ||308||
ityātmānaṁ nindati vandatē dēvān gurūṁśca bhaktyā । athāyupi pūrṇē cyutvā campāyāmupapannaḥ ॥ 309 ॥

ummamgadēsaṇāṇa ummaggānadaṁsiyatthakārīṇaṁ । saṁsaggī duhajaṇayā jāya jaha bhīmakumarassa || 1 ||
tathāhi ; --
kavisīsayaviuladalē jiṇaharakēsara virāyamāṇammi । guṇiguṇagaṇagaṁdhaḍḍhē dharaṇīsarasīē kayasōhē || 2 ||
kamalammitra kamalapurē rāyā riukaraḍivihaḍaṇaparyaṁḍō । jayapayaḍapurisayārō harivva harivāhaṇō āsi || 3 ||
tassatthi piyā bīyācaṁda kalānikkalaṁkataṇulaiyā । dēvī mālaināmā mālaimālavva suguṇaḍḍhā ||4||
varamumiṇasūiyaṁ sā suyaṁ pasūyā sulakkhaṇōvēyaṁ । sapayāvakaṁtikaliyaṁ diṇayara vivaṁtra puvvadisā ||5||
puvvapurisakkamāgayanāmaṁ puttassa bārasāhammi । sammāṇiya savvajaṇaṁ dinaṁ bhīmati piyarē hi || 6 ||
aha kamasō sō ass kalākalāvēṇa dēhakatīhiṁ । siyapakkhasasaharō iva kayajaṇamaṇalōyaṇāṇaṁdō ||7||
buddhilamaṁtissa suō tassa ya sahapasukīliō mittō । buddhimayaraharanāmā jāō maṁtī samāṇavaō ॥8॥
aha annadiṇa niyamaṁdirāō kumarō pahāyasamayammi । buddhimayara harasahiō saṁpattō rāyapayamūlē ||9||
paṇamai nivapayakamalaṁ tēṇavi āliṁgiuṁ niucchaṁgē । khaṇamēkkaṁ saṁṭhaviō pacchā uciyāsaṇāsīṇō ॥ 10 ॥
naranāhacaraṇajuyalaṁ niyaē aṁkammi karivi sappaṇayaṁ । kamaladalakō malēhiṁ karēhiṁ saṁvāhaṇaṁ kuṇai || 11 || .
bhattibharanigbharaṁgō nisuṇai jaṇayassa sāsaṇaṁ jāvaṁ । tō ārāmaniuttō pattō vinnavai naranāhaṁ ॥ 12 ॥
dēviṁda viṁda vaṁdiyapayāraviṁdō'raviṁdamuṇinā hō । sīsagaṇasaṁparivuḍō pattō kusumāgarujāṇē ॥ 13 ॥
taṁ sōūṇaṁ rāyā harisavasavisappamāṇarōmaṁcō । dāūṇa mauḍavajjaṁ tassa samaggapi ābharaṇaṁ ||14||
unmārgadēśanānāmunmārganidarśitārthakāriṇām । saṁsaktirduḥkhajanikā jāyatē yathā bhīmakumārasya ॥ 1 ॥
kapiśīrṣakā vipuladalē jinagr̥ha kēsaravirājamānē । guṇiguṇagaṇagandhāḍhyē dharaṇī sarasyāḥ kr̥taśōbhē || 2 ||
kamala iva kamalapurē rājā ripukaraṭivighaṭanapracaṇḍaḥ । jagatprakaṭa puruṣakārō haririva harivāhana āsīt ॥3॥
tasyāsti priyā dvitīyācandrakalāniṣkalaṅka tanulatikā । dēvī mālatīnāmā mālatīmālēva suguṇāḍhyā ॥4॥
varasvapnasūcitaṁ sā sutaṁ prasūtā sulakṣaṇāpētam । sapratāpa kāntikalita dinakarabimbamiva pūrvadik ॥5॥
pūrvapuruṣakramāgatanāma putrasya dvādaśāhē । sammānya sarvajanaṁ dattaṁ bhīma iti pitr̥bhyām ॥6॥
atha kramaśaḥ sa vardhatē kalākalāpēna dēhakāntibhyām । sitapakṣaśaśadhara iva kr̥tajanamanōlōcanānandaḥ ॥ 7 ॥
buddhilamantriṇaḥ sutastasya ca sahapāṁśukrīḍitō mitram | buddhimakaragr̥hanāmā jātō mantrī samānavayāḥ ॥8॥
athānyadinē nijamandirāt kumāraḥ prabhātasamayē । buddhimakaragr̥hasahitaḥ saṁprāptō rājapādamūlē ॥9॥
praṇamati nr̥papādakamalaṁ tēnāpya। liṅgya nijōtsaṅgē । kṣaṇamēkaṁ saṁsthāpitaḥ paścāducitāsanāsīnaḥ ॥ 10 ॥
naranāthacaraṇayugalaṁ nijē'ṅkē kr̥tvā sapraṇayam । kamaladalakōmalābhyāṁ karābhyāṁ saṁvāhanāṁ karōti ॥ 11 ॥
bhaktibharanirbharāṅgaḥ śr̥ṇōti janakasya śāsanaṁ yāvat । tata ārāmaniyuktaḥ prāptō vijñapayati naranātham ॥12॥
dēvēndravr̥ndavanditapādāravindō'ravindamunināthaḥ । śiṣyagaṇasaṁparivr̥taḥ prāptaḥ kusumākarōdyānē ॥13॥
tat śrutvā rājā harṣavaśāvasarpadrōmāñcaḥ । dattvā mukuṭavarja tasmai samagramapyābharaṇam || 14॥

caliō vaṁda hē kumārasāmaṁtamaṁtipariyariō | paṁcavihābhigramēṇa sūrissa avaggahē pattō ॥ 15 ॥
harisaṁsupunnanayaṇō tattha ya apuvvasurabiṁbaṁva । uggatavatēyadittaṁ saṁtāvaharaṁ ca dīsaṁtaṁ ॥ 16 ॥
bhaviyakumuyāvavōhaṁ utpāiyapaurajaṇamaṇāṇaṁdaṁ । syaṇiyaraṁca apuvvaṁ kalaṁkabaṁkattaṇavimukkaṁ ॥ 17॥
nāṇacaraṇāinimmalaguṇarayaṇāūriyaṁ sugabhīraṁ । jalarāsiṁva apucvaṁ khārattajaḍattaparicattaṁ ॥ 18 ॥
sūriṁ daddhuṁ vaṁda piyāhiṇaputragaṁ naravariṁdō । sōvi hu sudhammalābhaṁ sē dēi sivēka lābhaṁ ||19||
nāsannē na ya dūrē ubaviṭṭhō naravaī saparivārō । guruṇāvi samāraddhā suvisuddhā dēkhaṇā tēsiṁ ||20||
tathāhi; --
gurukammasalilakallōlasaṁkulē āvaīmahāvattē । duhasayakacchavamacchara macchayapucchacchaḍāḍōvē ॥21॥
iṁdiyakasāyadūsiyamaṇavittipayaṁḍapavaṇaduttārē । kahavi maṇuyattarayaṇaṁ pāvai jīvō bhavasamudē ||22||
tatthavi kila vijayāṇaṁ sahisayaṁ dasa ya bharahaēvayā । iya khittasattarisayaṁ, paikhittaṁ paṁca khaṁḍāī ॥ 23॥
tēsu ajjāī ciya chaṭuṁ khaṁḍaṁ tu āriyaṁ hōi । paṇavīsaṁ ciya dēsā chavvīsaimaṁ tu dēsaddhaṁ ||24||
tatthavi rajjaṁtara sēladuggakāṇaṇanivāsiṇō micchā | dhammassa bāhiracciya sāmaggiabhāvaō pāyaṁ ||25||
dhammaṁdharāvi caṁḍālapāṇaṣpabhiī achippajāīsu । dhammō ēsahiṁ viralō ciya hōi saṁjōgō ||26||
chippāsuvi jāī ahammipāsaṁḍivāsiyakulēsu । uppannā saddhammō sagē na hu nisēvaṁti ||27||
sukulammavi uppannā kēvi hu jāyaṁti dēvībhacchā । daṭṭhēpi jē ajōggā dhammasvaṇaṁ kahaṁtāṇaṁ ? ॥ 28 ॥
calitō vandana hētōḥ kumārasāmantamantriparikaritaḥ । pañcavidhābhigamēna sūrēravagrahē prāptaḥ ॥ 15 ॥
harṣāśrupūrṇanayanastatra cāpūrvasūravimbamivaṁ । ugratapastējōdīptaṁ saṁtāpaharaṁ ca dr̥śyamānam ॥ 16॥
bhāvēkakumudāvabōdhamutpāditapracurajanamana ānandam । rajanikaramivāpūrva kalaṅkavakratvavimuktam ॥17॥
jñānacaraṇādinirmalaguṇaratnāpūritaṁ sugarbhārim । jalarāśimivāpūrvaṁ kṣāratvajaḍatvaparityaktam ॥18॥
sūriṁ dr̥ṣṭā vandatē tripradakṣiṇāpūrvakaṁ naravarēndraḥ । sō'pi khalu sudharmalābhaṁ tasmai dadāti śivaikasukhalābham ||
nāsannē naca dūra upaviṣṭō narapatiḥ saparivāraḥ । guruṇāpi samārabdhā suviśuddhā dēśanā tēṣām ||20||
gurukarmasalilakallōlasaṁkulē āpattimahāvartē । duḥkhaśatakacchapamatsaramatsya pr̥cchacchaṭāṭōpē ॥21॥
indriyakaṣāyadūṣitamanōvr̥ttipracaṇḍapavanadustārē । kathamapi manujatvaratnaṁ prāpnōti jīvō bhavasamudrē ॥22॥
tatrāpi kila vijayānāṁ ṣaṣṭiśataṁ daśa ca bharatairavatāni । iti kṣētrasaptatiśataṁ pratikṣētraṁ pañca khaṇḍāni ॥23॥
tēṣvanāryāṇyēva ṣaṣṭhaṁ khaṇḍaṁ tvārya bhavati । pañcaviṁśatirēva dēśāḥ ṣaḍviṁśaṁ tu dēśārdham ||24||
1
,
tatrāpi rājyāntara śailadurga kānananivāsinō mithyātvinaḥ । dharmasya bāhyā ēva sāmagryabhāvataḥ prāyaḥ || 25॥
dharmyadharāsvapi cāṇḍālapānaprabhr̥tiṣvaspr̥śyajātiṣu । dharmōpadēśakavirala ēva bhavati saṁyōgaḥ ||26||
spr̥śyāsvapi jātiṣvadharmipākhaṇḍivāsitakulēṣu । utpannāḥ saddharmōpadēśakān na khalu niṣēvantē ||27||
sukulē'pyutpannāḥ kē'pi khalu jāyantē dēhabībhatsāḥ । draṣṭumapi yē yōgyā dharmaśravaṇaṁ kathaṁ tēṣām ॥28॥

bhīmakumārakahā ।
173
vararuvadharāṇaṁpi hu bahuviduhavā hivihuriyaṁgāṇa | dhammasavaṇammi jāyai kahaṁ nu buddhīvi kē siṁpi ? ||29||
nirauvamaganbhanivāsajammadukkhā bhāyaṇaṁ hōuṁ । an ya jaṇiyapāvā bālacciya kēvi vihaḍaṁti ||30||
kiccā kicavivē buddhīvi na hōi maṁdahiyayāṇa । savaṇaggahadulahattaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ciya dhīrapurisēhiṁ ॥ 31 ॥
ālassamōhavaṁtā thaṁbhā kōhā pamāikivaṇattā । bhayasōgā annāṇāvakrakhēvakō ūhalāramaṇā ||32||
ēēhiṁ kāraṇēhiṁ ladghr̥ṇa sudullāhapi māṇussaṁ । na lahai suī hiyakariṁ saṁsāruttāraṇiṁ jīvō ॥ 33 ॥
micchābhinivēsaviḍaṁviyāṇa saddhāē pariṇaī kattō । tattatthāmayapāṇaṁ gālijjaṁtaṁpi vaimaṁtāṇaṁ ? ||34||
dulahō ya maṁdasattāṇa saṁjamō saṁjamammi vēraggō । jattō labbhai mōkkhō anaṁtabhavadukkha paḍivakkhō || 365॥
jāyā ya dhammasavaṇē jāva imā tumha paramasāmaggī | uttaraguṇēsu jattaṁ kāuṁ sahalaṁ imaṁ kuha || 36 ||
tā bhō dēvāṇupiyā ! duttarabhavasāyaraṁ samuttaraha । jai jiṇadikkhānāvaṁ āruhaha tumē lahuṁ cēva ||37||
aha asamatthā tatthavi sammaṁ sammattamūlagihidhammaṁ । paḍivajjaha jaha pāvaha pāraṁ bhavajalahiṇō kamasō ||38||
tō bhālayalanivēsiyakarakamalō naravarō bhaṇai sūriṁ । nāhaṁ nāha ! samatthō jadhammasamujjamē inhi ॥ 39 ॥
tā gihidhammō sammaṁ dijjau pasiūṇa jai ahaṁ jōggō । tō guruṇā varavihiṇā dinō sē'ṇuvvayāīō ||
savvavirahaṁ pavanā kēvi hu anē u dēsaō viraī । sammattamittamannē taha ya samitta kumārōvi ॥ 41 ॥
sammattaṁ paḍivajjai sammaṁ aiyārapaṁkanimmukaṁ । aha namijaṁ muṇināhaṁ parisā niyaṭhāṇamaṇupattā ॥42॥
vararūpadharāṇāmapi hi bahuvidhaduḥ khavyādhividhuritāṅgānām । dharmaśravaṇē jāyatē kathaṁ nu buddhirapi kēṣāmapi ? ||
niraya।pamagarbhanivāsajanmaduḥkhānāṁ bhājanaṁ bhūtvā । anyē ca janitapāpā bālā ēva kē'pi vighaṭantē ॥30॥
kr̥tyākr̥tyavivēkē buddhirapi na bhavati mandahr̥dayānām । śravaṇagrahadurlabhatvaṁ bhaṇitamēva dhīra puruṣaḥ ॥ 31 ॥
ālasyamōhavantāḥ stabdhāḥ krōdhinaḥ pramādikr̥paṇārtāḥ । bhayaśōkājñānāvakṣēpa kautūhalāramanasaḥ ॥ 32 ॥
ētaiḥ kāraṇairlabdhvā sudurlabhamapi mānuṣyam । na labhatē śrutiṁ hitakarī saṁsārōttāriṇīṁ jīvaḥ ॥33॥
mithyābhinivēśaviḍambitānāṁ śraddhāyāḥ pariṇatiḥ kutaḥ । tattvārthāmr̥tapānaṁ gālyamānamapi vamatām ? ॥34॥
durlabhaśca mandasattvānāṁ saṁyamaḥ saṁyamē vairāgyam । yatō- labhyaṁtē mōkṣō'nantabhavaduḥkhapratipakṣaḥ ||35||
jātā ca dharmaśravaṇē yāvadiyaṁ yuṣmākaṁ paramasāmagrī । uttaraguṇēṣu yatnaṁ kr̥tvā saphalāmimāṁ kuruta || 36॥
tasmād bhō dēvānupriyāḥ ! dustarabhavasāgaraṁ samuttarata । yadi jinadīkṣānāvamārōhata yūyaṁ ladhvēva ||37||
athāsamarthāstatrāpi samyak samyaktvamūlagr̥hidharmam । pratipadyadhvaṁ yathā prāpnuta pāraṁ bhavajaladhēḥ kramaśaḥ || 38 ॥
tatō bhālatalanivēśita karakamalō naravarō bhaṇati sūrim । nāhaṁ nātha ! samarthō yatidharmasamudyama idānīm ॥39॥
tasmād gr̥hidharmaḥ samyag dīyatāṁ prasadya yadyahaṁ yōgyaḥ । tatō guruṇā varavidhinā dattastasyāṇutratādikaḥ ॥40॥
sarvaviratiṁ prapannāḥ kē'pi khalvanyē tu dēśatō viratim । samyaktvamātramanyē tathā ca samittraḥ kumārō'pi ॥ 41 ॥
samyaktvaṁ pratipadyatē samyagaticārapaṅkanirmuktam । atha natvā munināthaṁ pariṣad nijasthānamanuprāptā ॥42॥

supāsanāha cariambhi --
kumarō ya kuṇai dhammaṁ dēvacaṇamāiyaṁ samittōvi । vaccai jaīṇa pāsē nisuṇai sammatta ārē || 43 ॥
aha annayā kumāraṁ niyamaṁdirasaṁṭhiyaṁ savihamittaṁ । sūriguṇē vannataṁ namiḍaṁ vinnava paḍihārō ||44 ||
dēva ! nararuṁḍamālāka liō kāvāliō vēliyadēhō । dāraṭiō tuha daṁsaṇamīhai tō muṁca iya bhaṇiē ।
tēṇa sō parimukō āsīvāyaṁ uvāyaṇaṁ kāuṁ । uvaviṭṭhō bhāi imaṁ kumāra ! lahu mē rahaṁ dēsu || 46 ||
tō bhūkhēvēṇa lahuṁ ōsariō pariyaṇō taō tēṇa । abhatthiō kumārō, bhaṇiyaṁ maha atthi varavijjā ।
bhuvaṇakkhōhaṇināmā vārasa varisāī puvvasēvā sē । vihiyā vihīra saṁpai uttarasēvaṁ karissāmi ||48॥
gaṁtuṁ ki causirayaṇīē masāṇamajjhabhāgammi | kāuṁ uttarasāhagamaha taṁ varasattasaṁpannaṁ ॥ 49 ॥
I
ajjadiṇāō dasa diṇammi kasiṇā caudasī hōhī । tā tuha sāhijjēṇaṁ sā sijjhai majjha nibrbhataṁ ॥
tō kumarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ēraṇa asārahayasarīrēṇa । jai kassavi uvayārō kīrai tā kiṁ na pajjattaṁ ? ॥51॥
iya tavvayaṇaṁ paḍivajjiūṇa kumarēṇa sō taō bhaṇiō । gaccha tumaṁ saṭṭhāṇaṁ sō pabhaṇai tujjha pāsamma || 52
ciṭṭhissamahaṁ supurisa ! tujjha aṇunnāē, bhaṇai kumarōvi । kimattaṁ jaṛa ciṭṭhasi ciṭsu jāēi sā rayaṇī ।
iya bhaṇiuṁ sō niccaṁ kumarasamīdē karēi sayaṇāī । daddūṇaṁ maṁtisuō pabhaṇai kimihēsa pāsaṁḍī ? ||54 ||
jaṁpa kumarō kajjēṇa, maṁtiputtō bhai ēyassa । kiṁ kajjēṇaṁ, jēṇaṁ saha ālāvōvi na hu juttō ॥ 55 ॥
mailai sammattamalaṁ imēṇa saha saṁthavō suthēvōvi । tā pasiya kumāra ! ēyaṁ ca dūraṁ kupāsaṁḍiṁ || 56 ॥
kumāraśca karōti dharma dēvārcanādikaṁ samittrō'pi । vrajati yatināṁ pārśvē śr̥ṇōti samyaktvāticārān ||43॥
athānyadā kumāraṁ nijamandirasaṁsthitaṁ savidhamittram । sūriguṇān varṇayantaṁ natvā vijñapayati pratihāraḥ || 44 |
dēva ! nararuṇḍamālākalitaḥ kāpālikō valitadēha: । dvārasthitastava darśana mīhatē tatō muñcēti bhaṇitē ॥ 45॥
tēna sa parimukta āśīrvādamupāyanaṁ kr̥tvā । upaviṣṭō bhaṇatīdaṁ kumāra ! laghu mē rahō dēhi ||46 ॥
tatō bhūkṣēpēṇa ladhvapasr̥taḥ parijanastatastēna । abhyarthitaḥ kumārō, bhaṇitaṁ mamāsti varavidyā ||47 ||
bhuvanakṣōbhaṇīnāmā dvādaśa varṣāṇi pūrvasēvā tasyāḥ । vihitā vidhinā saṁpratyuttara sēvāṁ kariṣyāmi ॥48॥
gatvā kr̥ṣṇacaturdaśī rajanyāṁ śmaśānamadhyabhāgē । kr̥tvōttarasādhakamatha tvāṁ varasattvasaṁpannam ॥49॥
adyadinād daśamē dinē kr̥ṣṇacartudaśī bhaviṣyati । tatastava sāhāyyēna sā sētsyati mama nirbhrāntam ||10||
tataḥ kumārēṇa bhaṇitamētēnāsārahataśarīrēṇa । yadi kasyāpyupakāraḥ kriyatē tarhi kiṁ na paryāptam ॥51॥
iti tadvacanaṁ pratipadya kumārēṇa sa tatō bhaṇitaḥ । gaccha tvaṁ svasthānaṁ sa prabhaṇati tava pārśvē ॥ 52॥
sthāsyāmyahaṁ supuruṣa ! tavānujñayā, bhaṇati kumārō'pi । kimayuktaṁ yadi tiṣṭhasi tiṣṭha yāvadēti sā rajaniḥ ॥
iti bhaṇitvā sa nityaṁ kumārasamīpē karōti śayanādi । dr̥ṣṭvā mantrisutaḥ prabhaṇati kimihaiṣa pākhaṇḍī ? ||
jalpati kumāraḥ kāryēṇa, mantriputrō bhaṇatyētasya । kiṁ kāryēṇa, yēna sahālāpō'pi na khalu yuktaḥ ॥ 55 ॥
malinayati samyaktvamalamanēna saha saṁstavaḥ sustōkō'pi । tasmātprasadya kumāra ! ētaṁ tyaja dūraṁ kupākhaṇḍinam ॥

savvaṁ ciya sulahamiṇaṁ rajjaṁ vijjā dhaṇaṁ ca dhannaṁ ca । ēkaṁ jayai dulahaṁ sammattaṁ cattaaiyāraṁ ||57 ||
jaha girivarāṇa mērū surāṇa iṁdō gahāṇa jaha caṁdō । dēvāṇaṁ jiṇacaṁdō taha sammattaṁ ca dhammāṇaṁ ॥ 58 ॥
sō jammō jō maṇuyattaṇammi, taṁ māṇusa jahi dhammō । sō dhammō jattha sayā sammattaṁ niccalaṁ hōi || 59 ॥
tastra puṇa niccattaṁ aiyārāṇaṁ vivr̥jjaṇaṁ, tamhā । daṁsaṇamittaṁpi imassa cayaha pāsaṁḍirudassa ॥ 60 ॥
dujjaṇasaṁgō jaivi hu muhamahurō bhāi kahamavi tahāvi । pariṇāmēṇuvahayakālakūḍa viriyaṁ visēsēi ॥ 61 ॥
buddhimayara harabhaṇiyaṁ sōuṁ kumarōvi bhaṇai ēvamiṇaṁ । dakkhinnakhinnamaraṇā paḍivannamiṇaṁ tahāvi maē ॥ 62 ॥
pavanē nivvahaṇaṁ ēyaṁ tu mahavvayaṁ supurisāṇa । niyataṇukalaṁkakāripi muyai ki sasaharō sasyaṁ ॥ 63 ॥
ahavā ।
kiṁ kuṇai kusaṁgō māṇusassa niyadhammakammasu divassa | visahara sirēvi vasiō kiṁ na maṇī garalamavaṇēi ? ॥
aha paṇa maṁtisuō jai paḍivannamma nivvahai kumārō । tō puvvaṁgīkayaniraiyārasammattamuvvahau ॥ 65॥
visaharamaṇī abhāvugadavvaṁ, jīvō u bhāvugaṁ, tamhā । sammaṁ citijjatō dihaṁtō ēsa jaṁ kiṁci ॥ 66 ॥
ēvaṁ paviōvi hu tēṇa kumārō aṇēgajuttīhiṁ । na cayai taṁ pāsaṁḍiṁ viḍaṁviō durabhimāṇēṇa || 67 ||
ēvaṁ ca vaṭṭamāṇē caudasirayaṇīnisīhasamayammi । kāvāliyabhaṇiēṇaṁ saṁvahium̐ laggaē kumarō || 68 ||
parihēī aimasiṇaṁ niyaṁsaṇaṁ niviḍavīragaṁṭhīē । baṁdhēi mallagaṁṭhīē kēsapāsa sakhaggō sō ॥ 69 ॥ |
vaṁciya pariyaṇamēgō karaṁkacayabhīsaṇē masāṇammi । kāvāliēṇa saddhiṁ saṁpattō sō khaṇadvēṇa ॥ 70 ॥
sarvamēva sulabhamidaṁ rājyaṁ vidyā dhanaṁ ca dhānyaṁ ca । ēkaṁ jagati durlabhaṁ samyaktvaṁ tyaktāticāram ||57॥
yathā giridharāṇāṁ mēruḥ surāṇāmindrō grahāṇāṁ yathā candraḥ । dēvānāṁ jinacandrastathā samyaktvaṁ ca dharmāṇām ॥
tajjanma yanmanujatvē, tanmānuṣyaṁ yatra dharmaḥ । sa dharmō yatra sadā samyaktvaṁ niścalaṁ bhavati ॥ 59 ॥
tasya punarniścalatvamaticārāṇāṁ vivarjanaṁ, tasmāt । darśanamātramapyasya tyaja pākhaṇḍirudrasya ||60 ||
durjanasaṅgō yadyapi khalu mukhamadhurō bhāti kathamapi tathāpi । pariṇāmēṇōpahatakālakūṭavīryād viśiṣyatē ॥ 61 ॥
buddhimakaragr̥habhaṇitaṁ śrutvā kumārō'pi bhaṇatyēvamidam । dākṣiṇyakhinnamatinā pratipannamidaṁ tathāpi mayā ॥62॥
pratipannē nirvahaṇamētattu mahāvrata supuruṣāṇām । nijatanukalaṅkakāriṇamapi muñcati kiṁ śaśadharaḥ śaśakam ? |
athavā |
,
kiṁ karōti kusaṅgō manuṣyasya nijadharmakarmasu dr̥ḍhasya । viṣadhara śirasyapyupitaḥ kiṁ na maṇirgaralamapanayati ? |
atha prabhaṇati mantrisutō yadi pratipannaṁ nirvahati kumāraḥ। tataḥ pūrvāṅgīkr̥tānāticārasamyaktvamudvahatu ॥ 65॥
viṣadharamaṇirabhāvukadravyaṁ, jīvastu bhāvukaṁ, tasmāt । samyak cintyamānō dr̥ṣṭāntaṁ ēṣa yatkiñcit ॥ 66 ॥
ēvaṁ prajñāpitō'pi khalu tēna kumārō'nēkayuktibhiḥ । na tyajati taṁ pākhaṇḍinaṁ viḍambitō durabhimānēna ॥ 67 ॥
ēvaṁ ca vartamānē caturdaśīrajaniniśīthasamayē । kāpālikabhaṇitēna saṁvōḍhuṁ lagati kumāraḥ ॥ 68 ॥ |
paridadhātyatimasr̥ṇaṁ vastraṁ nibiḍavīragranthinā । badhnāti mallagranthinā kēśapāśaṁ sakhaṅgaḥ saḥ ||69॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
lihiūṇa maṁḍala sō pūēḍaṁ maṁtadēvayaṁ kiṁpi । kumarassa sihābaṁdha kāuṁ samuṭṭhiō jāva ॥ 71 ॥
tō kumarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ niyasattaṁ caiva maha sihābaṁdha । pagayaṁ ciya kuṇasu tumaṁ nimbhayacittō mahābhāga ! ॥
kaṁḍhiyakaravālalalaṁtajīhābhīmō kavāliṇō pāsē । paṁcāṇaṇōvtra kumarō tō ciṭṭhā sāhasikarasō || 73॥
kumarāsiragahaṇasihibaṁdhaniyaḍamaha vihaḍiyaṁ sa dadrūṇaṁ । lēmi sira mimassa parakkamēṇa iya ṭhāviḍaṁ buddhiṁ ||
karakaliyagaruyakattī gayaṇasamaṁ kāumattaṇō rūvaṁ । kūvasamakannakuharō laggō dhaḍahaḍiumaiviḍaṁ ॥ 75 ॥
tataśca ।
naṁ kumma kaḍaḍiya piṭṭhi naṁ pavihau girivaru, naṁ surakaraḍihi raḍiu gahiru naṁ gajjiu jalaharu |
naṁ dharaṇiṁda phaṇākaḍappacaṁpiu dikkaraḍihiṁ, taḍayaḍaṁtu taḍidaṁḍu paḍiṅa naṁ girivarasiharihiṁ ॥76 ||
iya vihiya ciṁtahiṁ sura visara jasa thaḍahaḍiḍaṁ suṇēvi lahu ।
taha raṁbhapamuharamaṇihiṁ bhaṇiu rakkhi rakkhi maṁ tiyasapahu ! ॥77॥
sahai tāsu kari kattī taha ruhirāruṇiya, najjai jīhudāliya kiṁ jambhaḍataṇiya ।
kiha kattiyaphali tasu taṇu rēhai saṁkramiu, naṁ kumarahavahaṇatthaṁ duhiu taṇu nimmaviu ||78॥
tō tavviyaṁbhiyaṁ ciya pasiūṇa kumarō harivva karijūhaṁ । kuviō pauṇai khagaṁ namajīhāsa risamakkhu hiō ॥
jā tāva tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ rē rē rē bāla ! maha piḍē paḍiō । lēmi tuha uttamaṁgaṁ ahamihi taḍaphaḍatassa ||80||
jai puṇa maha maha vayaṇā sayamappisi matthayaṁ sahatthēṇa । chittuṁ tā taṁ jammaṁtaramvi suhabhāyaṇaṁ hōsi ॥ 81 ॥
vañcayitvā parijanamēkaḥ karaṅkacayabhīṣaṇē śmaśānē । kāpālikēna sārdhaṁ saṁprāptaḥ sa kṣaṇārdhēna ॥ 70 ॥
likhitvā maṇḍalaṁ sa pūjayitvā mantradaivataṁ kimapi । kumārasya śikhābandhaṁ kartuṁ samupasthitō yāvat ॥71॥
tataḥ kumārēṇa bhaṇitaṁ nijasattvamēva mama śikhābandhaḥ । prakr̥tamēva kuru tvaṁ nirbhayacittō mahābhāga ! ॥72॥
kr̥ṣṭakaravālalalajjihvābhīmaḥ kapālinaḥ pārśvē । pañcānana iva kumārastatastiṣṭhati sāhasikyarasaḥ ॥ 73 ॥
kumāra śirōgrahaṇaśikhibandhanigaḍamatha vighaṭitaṁ sa dr̥ṣṭā । lāmi śirō'sya parākramēṇēti sthāpayitvā buddhim ॥
karakalitagurukartarīkō gamanasamaṁ kr̥tvā''tmanō rūpam । kūpasamakarṇakuharō lagnō garjitumativikaṭam ॥75॥
nanu kūrmasya parāvartitaṁ pr̥ṣṭhaṁ nanu pavihatō girivaraḥ, nanu surakaraṭibhī raṭitaṁ gabhīrō nanu garjitō jaladharaḥ ॥
nanu dharaṇēndraḥ phaṇāsaṁghātacampitō dikkaraṭibhiḥ, taḍattastaḍiddaṇḍaḥ patitō nanu girivara śikharēṣu ॥
iti vismitāścintayanti suravisarā yasya garjāravaṁ śrutvā laghu ।
tathā rambhāpramukha ramaṇībhirbhaṇitaṁ rakṣa rakṣa māṁ tridaśaprabhō ! ॥77॥
rājati tasya karē katarī tathā rudhirāruṇitā, jñāyatē jihōddālitā kiṁ yamabhaṭīyā ।
kathaṁ kartarīphalakē tasya tanū rājati saṁkrāntaṁ nanu kumāravadhārthaṁ dvitīyatanurnirmāpitam ॥78॥
tatastadvijr̥mbhitamēva dr̥ṣṭrā kumārō haririva kariyūtham । kupitaḥ praguṇayati khanaṁ yamajihvā sadr̥śamakṣubhitaḥ॥79॥
yāvattāvattēna bhaṇitaṁ rē rē rē bāla ! mama piṭē patitaḥ । lāmi tavōttamāṅgamahamidānīṁ capalāyamānasya ॥ 80 ॥

tō ēvaṁ jaṁpatō. bhaṇiō kumarēṇa rē kupāsāṁḍa ! | caṁḍālaḍuṁvaciṭṭhiya ! niṭṭhiyakallāṇa ! annāṇa ! ||82 ॥
vissāsiyāṇa jēsi taē kavālēhiṁ viraiyā mālā | tāṇavi varaṁ khālēmi ajja vittuṁ tuha kavālaṁ ॥83॥
tō kattiyāē ghāō mukō kumarē ya tēṇa, kumarōvi । khaliḍaṁ khaggēṇa jhaḍatti tassa khaṁdhaṁ samārūḍhō ॥ 84 ॥
citai ya sō iyāṇi khaggēṇa duhā karēmi ēyassa | pāvassa kaṁṭhadēsaṁ kiṁpuṇa maha kaiyavēṇāvi || 85 ||
sēvamimōpaḍivō bahusa tijuō ya kahavi jai dhammē । ṭhāi pabhāvai tō pavayapi iya ciṁti kumarō ॥
nihaṇai muṭṭhīhi tayaṁ sirammi, tāḍēi khagga javaēṇa । kāvāliōvi jā taṁ ginhai hatthēhiṁ tā kumarō ||
jhatti tasvaṇamajjhē pavisai karagahiyataralakaravālō | girikuharagaō paṁcāṇaṇōvva tarhi sō virāēi ||
tō kharanaharapahārihiṁ parai kumaru tarhi, jimba sūyaru didādihi kharakhara khaṇai mahiṁ ।
saraḍiṇa ḍapaṭṭiṇa jimva kari kaḍu raḍai, timba kannaṁtarayaṇaviharu su āraḍai || 89 ||
tō hatthē gahiraṁ kumarō kannāu kaṭṭiu kahavi । tēṇa dhariūṇa caraṇē tattō ucchāliō gayaṇē ॥ 90 ॥
tō nivaḍatō tō kkhaṇidēvīē divvajōgēṇaṁ । karasaṁpuḍē karēuṁ nīō niyamaṁdira saṁtō ॥ 91 ॥
jaṁ niyauccattēṇaṁ ōhāvara tuhiṇasēlasiṁgaṁpi । aivitthārēṇa puṇō jiṇēi bhavapi aviṇō || 12 ||
jatya ya aruṇacchāyaṁ niēvi nisi paumarāyakiraṇēhi । amarīja gōsakiccaṁ kuṇaṁti paccūsa sakāē |
jattha phalihōtralē saṁkataṁ niēvi niyayapaḍibiṁbaṁ । īsāē naḍaṁti piē amarīō savattikā ॥ 94 ॥
yadi punarmahyaṁ mama vacanātsvayamarpayasi mastakaṁ svahastēna । chittvā tadā tvaṁ janmāntarē sukhabhājana bhavasi ॥81॥
tata ēvaṁ jalpan bhaṇitaḥ kumārēṇa rē kupākhaṇḍin ! । cāṇḍālaśvapacacēṣṭita ! niṣṭhitakalyāṇa ! ajñāna ! ॥82॥
viśvāsitānāṁ yēṣāṁ tvayā kapālairviracitā mālā । tēṣāmapi vairaṁ kṣālayāmyadya gr̥hītvā tava kapālam ॥83॥
tataḥ
kartaryā ghātō muktaḥ kumārē ca tēna, kumārō'pi । skhalayitvā khanēna jhaṭiti tasya skandhaṁ samārūḍhaḥ॥84॥
cintayati ca sa idānīṁ khaṅgēna dvidhā karōmyētasya । pāpasya kaṇṭhadēśaṁ kintu mama kaitavēnāpi ॥ 85 ॥
sēvāmayaṁ pratipannō bahuśaktiyutaśca kathamapi yadi dharmē । tiṣṭhati prabhāvayati tadā pravacanamapīti cintayitvā kumāraḥ ॥
nihanti muṣṭibhyāṁ taṁ śirasi, tāḍayati khagaṁ javēna । kāpālikō'pi yāvattaṁ gr̥hṇāti hastābhyāṁ tāvatkumāraḥ ॥ 87 ॥
jhaṭiti tacchravaṇamadhyē praviśati karagr̥hītataralakaravālaḥ । girikuharagataḥ pañcānana iva tatra sa virājatē ॥ 88 ॥
tataḥ kharanakharaprahāraiḥ praharati kumārastatra yathā śūkarō dr̥ḍhadaṁṣṭrābhyāṁ kharakharaṁ khanati mahīm ।

tatō hastēna gr̥hītvā kumāraḥ karṇātkr̥ṣṭvā kathamapi । tēna dhr̥tvā caraṇē tata ucchālitō gaganē ॥90॥
tatō nipatan prāptō yakṣiṇīdēvyā daivayōgēna । karasaṁpuṭē kr̥tvā nītō nijamandirasyāntaḥ ॥91॥
yad nijōccatvēnākrāmati tuhinaśailaśr̥ṅgamapi । ativistārēṇa punarjayati bhavanamapyahipatēḥ ॥92॥

supāsanāhacariyammi-
ēvaṁvihammi tammi sahasā kumarō niēi attāṇaṁ । uvaviddhaṁ varasīhāsaṇammi maṇirayaṇajaḍiyammi ॥95॥
vimyicittō tattō jā ciṁta niyamaṇē kimēti । tō jōḍiyakarakamalā tadpuraō jakkhiṇī hōuṁ ॥ 96 ॥
bhai mahāyasa ! ēsō viṁjhō nāmēṇa pavvaō tuṁgō | tannāmēṇa nāmaṁ aḍavīivi tihuyaṇa siddhaṁ ॥ 97॥
afirantari ēyaṁ vēḍavviyaṁ ca maha bhavaṇaṁ । kīlatthamittha nivasāmi jakkhiṇī nāma kamalakkhā ॥
niyasurayaṇapaḍiyariyā ciṭṭhāmi sayāvi iha saicchāē । ajjaṁ cēva puṇō haṁ aṭṭhāvyapavvayammi gayā॥99॥
ittō ya calatīē diṭṭhō si tumaṁ nahammi pakkhittō । kāvāliēṇa tēṇaṁ jhiliō ya maē payattēṇa ।। 100॥
sue mhasaradhōraṇī ghāēhiṁ pīḍiyasarīrā । tuha saraṇamāgayā haṁtā supurisa ! rakkha maṁ rakkha ॥। 101 ॥
ēsō maha parivārō savvōvi hu tujjha kiṁkarō hōhī । kuṇasu pasāyaṁ bhuṁjasu visayasuhaṁ iha maē saddhiṁ ।। 102 ॥
taṁ jakkhiṇīē vayaṇaṁ sōuṁ daravihasiēṇa kumarēṇaṁ । bhaṇiyaṁ ahō ! niyacchaha aisahō mayaṇasarapasarō ॥
citā dūricciya ēsō amhārilō abuhalōō । picchaha vibuhajaṇōvi hu ēvaṁ vinaḍijjai imēṇa ||
ēēṇaṁ abhibhūyā jīvā na muṇaṁti kiṁpi hiyamahiyē । nisuṇaṁti nēya dhammaṁ kajjākajjaṁ na yāti ॥ 105 ॥
na gaṇaṁti avajasamiṇa juttājuttaṁpi nō viyāṇaṁti । visayavimōhiyacittā jīvā kayamajjapāṇavva ॥ 106॥
kamaliṇidalagayajalalavasarisahavisaya suhakāraṇi aivirasaha |
na gaṇa jaṇu tarhi pēraṁta himagirisarisa duhōhu paḍata ॥ 107॥
aiduṭṭiyamahurasaṇōvam visayasuhu uvarbhujaṁtara jīu na yāṇēi ēu duhu ।
ēvaṁvidhē tasmin sahasā kumāraḥ paśyatyātmānam । upaviṣṭaṁ varasiṁhāsanē maṇiratnajaṭitē ||15||
vismitacittastatō yāvaccintayati nijamanasi kimētaditi । tatō yōjitakarakamalā satpuratō yakṣiṇī bhūtvā ॥
bhaṇati mahāyaśaḥ । ēṣa vindhyō nāmnā parvatastuṅgaḥ । tannāmnā nāmāṭavyā api tribhuvanaprasiddham ॥97॥
vindhyagirisamīpagatamētad vaikrayikaṁ ca mama bhavanam । krīḍārthamatra nivasāmi yakṣiṇī nāma kamalākṣā ||98 ॥
nijasurajanaparikaritā tiṣṭhāmi sadāpīhī svēcchayā । adyaiva punarahamaṣṭāpadaparvatē gatā ॥99॥
itaśca valamānayā dr̥ṣṭō'si tvaṁ nabhasi prakṣiptaḥ । kāpālikēna tēna gr̥hītaśca mayā prayatnēna ॥ 100॥
idānīṁ manmathaśaradhārēṇyā ghātaiḥ pīḍitaśarīrā । tava śaraṇamāgatā'haṁ tasmātsupuruṣa ! rakṣa māṁ rakṣa ॥ 101 ॥
ēṣa mama parivāra : sarvō'pi hi tava kiṅkarō bhaviṣyati । kuruṣva prasādaṁ bhuṅkṣva viṣayasukhamiha mayā sārdham ॥
tad
yakṣiṇyā vacanaṁ śrutvēṣadvihasitēna kumārēṇa । bhaṇitamahō ! paśyatātiduḥ sahō madanaśaraprasaraḥ ॥ 103॥
tiṣṭhatu tāvad dūra ēvaiṣō'smādr̥śō'budhalōkaḥ । paśyata vibudhajanō'pi khalvēvaṁ vinaṭyatē'nēna ॥104॥
ētēnābhibhūtā jīvā na jānanti kimapi hitamahitam । śr̥ṇvanti naiva dharmaṁ kāryakāryaṁ na jānanti ॥ 105 ॥
na gaṇayantyapayaśa idaṁ yuktāyuktamapi nō vijānanti । viṣayavimōhitacittā jīvāḥ kr̥tamadyapānā iva ।। 106 ॥

tasmin pariṇāmaprāptē pīḍyatē varcaḥ pratyayaṁ punarapi । tasya ca vigamē punaḥ kṣudhā pīḍyatē bāḍham ॥ 113 ॥

supāsanāha- cariśrammi-
tāmaha bhattī paramā tumammi, jō sāmi ! tujjha puṇa pujjō । jiṇanāhō sō saraṇaṁ āsaṁsāraṁpi maha hōu ।।
iya jāva garuyasaṁvēgabhāva pasaratabhattipavbhārā । anaṁpi kiṁpi bhaṇihī tā nisuṇēūṇa mahurajhuṇi ॥ 121 ॥
aibaṁdhurabaṁdhasamiddhasiddhasiddhaṁtasāravayaṇāṇa । pucchara bhīmakumārō kē iha kuvvaṁti sajjhāyē ? || 122 ||
tō bhai jakkhiṇī nāha । ittha vijhagirigakhyaguhamajjhē । ciṭṭhēti mahāmuṇiṇō ca māsāō ya pāraṁti ॥
tā tāṇa tavassīṇaṁ kuvvaṁtāṇaṁ visisajjhāyaṁ । subbai ahamahuraguṇī taṁ sōūṇaṁ bhaṇai kumarō || 124||
sēyamaṇabhā buṭṭī marummi ēyaṁ tamajja kamalasaraṁ । jaṁ itthavi majjha susāhusaṁgamō punnajōē || 125 ॥
tā ahamihiṁ ciya rayaṇisēsamēēsa pāyamūlammi | gaṁtuṁ gamēmi tō jakkhiṇīē puraō payaṭṭāē॥ 126 ॥
ittō iṁtō kumarō pāyamavadhārautti bhaṇirīē । maggaṁ dētīē sō pattō sāhuāsanē ॥ 127 ॥
sāvi hu sapariyaṇā haṁ vaṁdissaṁ sāhuṇōti bhaṇiūṇa | saṁpattā niyaṭhāṇē jhāyai kumarassa uvaēsē || 128 ॥
kumarēṇa guhavāhi diṭṭhō sūrī muṇīhiṁ pariyariō । vivihāsaṇajuttēhi sajjhāyajjhāṇaniraēhiṁ ॥ 129॥
tattha kayavāhū daṭṭhē kēī uvikkhaē kumarō | dhammatthakayakilēsā vayaṁti u kahati imē ॥ 130 ॥
kēvi puṇa gāē ukkhaviē kaha sahati udghaṭṭiyā । naṁ saggaṁ gaṁtumaṇā sikkhaṁti nahaṁgaṇuppāyaṁ ॥ 131 ॥
iya dukkaratavacaraṇēsa vāvaḍaṁ picchiūṇa muṇisaṁghaṁ । paṁcavihābhigamēṇaṁ saṁpattō gurusamīvammi ॥ 132 ॥
ciṁtara kimēsa sōmattaṇēṇa lōāṇa lōyaṇāṇaṁdō । rāhukayatthaṇabhīōvva sasaharō rannamallīṇō ? ॥ 133 ॥
tasmāttava prasādēna mamāpi janmāntarē na khalu durlabhaḥ । niḥśēṣaduḥkhavimuktō mōkṣō viṣayāṁstyajantyāḥ ॥ 119 ॥
tasmād mama bhaktiḥ paramā tvayi yaḥ svāmin ! tava punaḥ pūjyaḥ । jinanāthaḥ sa śaraṇamāsaṁsāramapi mama bhavatu ||
iti yāvad gurusaṁvēgabhāvaprasadbhaktiprāgbhārā । anyadapi kimapi bhaṇiṣyati tāvat śrutvā madhuradhvanim ॥121॥
atibandhurabandhasamr̥ddhasiddhasiddhāntasāravacanānām । pr̥cchati bhīmakumāraḥ ka iha kurvanti svādhyāyam ॥ 122 ॥
tatō bhaṇati yakṣiṇī nātha ! atra vindhyagiriguruguhāmadhyē । tiṣṭhanti mahāmunayaścaturmāsīṁ ca pārayanti ॥ 123॥
tasmāttēṣāṁ tapasvināṁ kurvatāṁ viśiṣṭasvādhyāyam । śrūyatē'timadhuradhvanistat śrutvā bhaṇati kumāraḥ ॥ 124॥
sēyamana bhrā vr̥ṣṭirmarāvētat tadadya kamalasaraḥ । yadatrāpi mama susādhusaṁgamaḥ puṇyayōgēna ॥ 125 ॥
tasmādahamidānīmēva rajaniśēṣamētēṣāṁ pādamūlē । gatvā gamayāmi tatō yakṣiṇyāṁ purataḥ pravr̥ttāyām ॥ 126 ॥
itō yan kumāraḥ pādamavadhārayatviti bhaṇanaśīlāyām । mārga dēśayantyāṁ sa prāptaḥ sādhvāsannē || 127॥
sāpi khalu saparijanā'haṁ vandiṣyē sādhūniti bhaṇitvā । saṁprāptā nijasthānē dhyāyati kumārasyōpadēśān ॥
kumārēṇātha guhāyā bahirdr̥ṣṭaḥ sūrirmunibhiḥ parikaritaḥ । vividhāsanayuktaiḥ svādhyāyadhyānanirataiḥ ॥ 129॥
tatra kr̥tōrdhvabāhūn dr̥ṣṭā kāṁścidupēkṣatē kumāraḥ । dharmārthakr̥taklēśā vrajantyūrdhvaṁ kathayantīmē ॥130॥
kē'pi punarēkapādē utkṣiptē kathaṁ rājantyurdhvasthitāḥ । nanu svargaṁ gantumanasaḥ śikṣantē nabhō'ṅgaṇōtpātam ॥131॥
iti duṣkaratapaścaraṇēṣu vyāpr̥taṁ dr̥ṣṭrā munisaṁgham । pañcavidhābhigamēna saṁprāptō gurusamīpē ॥132॥
cintayati kimēṣa sōmatvēna lōkānāṁ lōcanānandaḥ । rāhukadarśanabhīta iva śaśavarō'raṇyamālīnaḥ ॥ 133 ॥

bhīmakumārakahā ।
181
rōmaṁcakaṁcuijjatasavvagattō vihīē muṇināhaṁ । tō vaṁdai bhattīē sēsēvi hu muṇivarē kumarō || 134 ||
uvalammalābhō suddhē dharaṇīyammi uvavisiuṁ । khaṇamāyanniya dhammaṁ muṇivaiṇō parikahaṁtassa ।। 135 ॥
vimhiyāhiyaō laddhūṇa avasaraṁ sāyaraṁ paṇamiṇa । bhaṇai muṇīsara ! ēsā acaṁtaṁ bhīsaṇā aḍaī ||
kaha tubhē bhayarahiyā asahāyā nirakhaṇā sayā tisiyā । iha nivasaha, majjha imaṁ garuyaṁ paḍihāi acchariyaṁ ॥
iya kumarajaṁpiē jāva kiṁpi kila munivaī paḍibhaṇēi । tā pēcchai nahamaggē āgacchaṁtiṁ bhuyaṁ kumarō ।। 138 ॥
aster kinhā sā avayaramāṇī nahāu paḍihāi । dūraṁ palaṁbamāṇā nahayalalacchīē vēṇivva ॥ 139 ॥
aithirathōrā garuyā palaṁbamāṇā dharāē paḍilaggā । najjai sā kālabhuyaṁgiṇivva dūī jamabhassa || 140 ॥
rattaṁdaṇēṇa littā aika ḍhiṇā taralabhīsaṇāgārā । najjai lalamāṇā jamabhaḍēṇa pagaḍīkayā jīhā ॥ 141 ॥
aha sā vimyajaṇaṇī samāgayā jhatti tappaēsapi । pēcchaṁtāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ muṇikumarāṇaṁ abhīrūṇaṁ ॥ 142 ॥
āgaṁtūṇa taō sā sahasā kumarassa saṁtiyaṁ khagaṁ । gahium̐ muṭṭhīhiṁ diḍaṁ puṇōvi pacchāmuhaṁ baliyā ||
taṁ picchiūṇa kumarēṇa citiyaṁ kassa saṁtiyā ēsā । ērisarūvā bāhā kiṁ karihī maha kivāṇēṇa ? ||
kiñca ।
tamahaṁ picchāmi sayaṁ gaṁtūṇaṁ jassa saṁtiyā ēsā । tō kōuyarasavasaō namiū muṇivaī payaō ॥ 145 ॥
tō uṭṭiuṁ kumārō sīhōvva samucchalai nahamaggē । muṇijaṇajaṇiyacchariō tīē bāhāē ārūḍhō ।। 146॥
aikasiṇabhuyārūḍhō vaccatō nahayalammi sō kamasō । kāliyapiṭṭhārūḍhasta viṇhuṇō līlamuvvahai || 147॥
rōmāñcakañcukāyamānasarvagātrō vidhinā muninātham । tatō vandatē bhaktyā śēpānapi munivarān kumāraḥ ॥ 134॥
upalabdhadharmalābhaḥ śuddhē dharaṇītalē upaviśya । kṣaṇamākarṇya dharmaṁ munipatēḥ parikathayataḥ ॥ 135 ॥
vismitahr̥dayō labdhvā'vasaraṁ sādaraṁ praṇamya । bhaṇati munīśvara ! ēṣā'tyantaṁ bhīṣaṇā'ṭavī ॥ 136॥
kathaṁ yūyaṁ bhayarahitā asahāyā niraśanāḥ sadā tr̥ṣitāḥ । iha nivasatha, mamēdaṁ guru pratibhātyāścaryam ॥ 137॥
iti kumārajalpitē yāvaskimapi kila munipatiḥ pratibhaṇati । tāvatpaśyati nabhōmārga āgacchantī bhujāṁ kumāraḥ ॥
atidīrghā kr̥ṣṇā sā'vatarantī nabhasaḥ pratibhāti । dūraṁ pralambamānā nabhastalalakṣmyā dēṇīva ॥ 139॥
atisthirasthūlā gurvī pralambamānā dharāyāṁ pratilagnā । jñāyatē sā kālabhujaṅginīva dūtī yamabhaṭasya ॥ 140 ॥
raktacandanēna liptā'tikaṭhinā taralabhīṣaṇākārā । jñāyatē lalantī yamabhaṭēna prakaṭīkr̥tā jilhā ॥ 141 ॥
atha sā vismayajananī samāgatā jhaṭiti tatpradēśē । paśyatāṁ tēṣāṁ munikumārāṇāmabhīrūṇām ॥142॥
āgatya tataḥ sā sahasā kumārasya satkaṁ khaṅgam । gr̥hītvā muṣṭibhyāṁ dr̥ṣṭaṁ punarapi paścānmukhaṁ valitā ॥ 143॥
tad dr̥ṣṭvā kumārēṇa cintitaṁ kasya satka ēṣaḥ । īdr̥śarūpō bāhuḥ kiṁ kariṣyati mama kr̥pāṇēna ॥144॥
tamahaṁ paśyāmi svayaṁ gatvā yasya satka ēṣaḥ । tataḥ kautukarasavaśatō natvā munipatiṁ prayataḥ || 149॥
tata utthāya kumāraḥ siṁha iva samucchalati nabhōmārgē । munijanajanitāścaryastasmin bāhāvārūḍhaḥ ॥146॥
atikr̥ṣṇabhujārūḍhō vrajannabhastalē sa kramaśaḥ । kāliyapr̥ṣṭhārūḍhasya viṣṇōrlīlāmudrahati ॥ 147 ॥
