182
supāsanāha caritryasmi --
thirathōra bāhuphalahayamāruḍhō viulanahayalasamudaṁ । bhinnavahaṇōvva vaṇiō taramāṇō bhāi varakumarō ॥ 148 ॥
bahutaruvaragirigaṇagirinaīō jā vañcai palōyatō । nivbhayacittō bhīmō tā pēcchai kāliyābhavaṇaṁ ॥
ruhirōhēṇa vittiṁ sāpavāhēṇa paramavībhacchaṁ । rattakusumōkyāraṁva paḍiyavahumaṁsakhaṁḍēhiṁ ॥ 150 ॥
iya ērisassa bhavaṇassa ganbhaharayammi saṁṭhiyā diṭṭhā | bhīmakumārēṇa naramuṁḍamaṁḍiyā kāliyāpaḍimā ||
vigarālanayaṇavayaṇā mahisārūḍhā ya bhairavasarīrā । naraaṁtamālahārā vīsakarā paharaṇasaṇāhā || 152||
ērisaruvāē kāliyāē puraō ya saṁṭhiō diṭṭhō । sō puvvakavaḍakārī krūrō kāvāliō chiṭṭō || 153 ॥
taha vāmakaraṇaṁ tēṇaṁ kāvāliēṇa duṭṭhēṇa । ēgō suṁdarapurisō diṭṭhō kēsēsu parigahiō ॥ 154 ॥
jīē puṇa bāhāē kumarō āgacchaē samārūḍhō । sā tassa kupāsaṁḍissa saṁtiyā dāhiṇā vāhā ॥ 155॥
taṁ kēsaparigahiyaṁ daṭṭhē kumarēṇa ciṁtiyaṁ ēyaṁ । kiṁ ēsō pāviṭṭō kāhī karadhariyapurisassa ? || 156 ||
tā pacchannō hōuṁ ahayaṁ ēyassa ciṭṭiyaṁ tāva । picchāmi taō pacchā jaṁ hōhī taṁ karistāmi ॥ 157॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa kumarō tassa jhuāō jhaḍatti uttariḍaṁ । tassēva piṭṭhidēsassa piṭṭaō saṁṭhiō nihuō ॥ 158 ॥
bhīmakumarassa khagaṁ ghēttr̥ṇa samāgayā bhuyā jāva । vāmakaradhariyapurisō bhaṇiō kāvāliēṇa imaṁ ।। 159 ॥
sarasu kiṁpi niyaiṭṭhadēvayaṁ jaṁ ahaṁ imēṇasiṇā । ghēttuṁ tuha sirakamalaṁ pūyaṁ kālīē viraissaṁ ॥ 160 ॥
sō bhai sayalajayajīvabaṁdhavō jinavarō maē tāva । savvāvatthagaēṇavi sumarēyanvō na annōti ॥ 169॥
kiṁtu taccaraṇasēvī puvvapurisakamāgaō sāmī । sahapaṁsukīliō paṇayavacchalō jīviyāōvi ॥ 162 ॥
rē
sthirasthūlabāhuphalakamāruḍhō vipulanabhastalasamudram | bhinnavāhana itra vaṇik taran bhāti varakumāraḥ ॥ 148 ॥
bahutaruvaragirigaṇagirinadīryāvad vrajati pralōkamānaḥ । nirbhayacittō bhīmastāvatpaśyati kālikābhavanam॥149॥
rudhiraughēna viliptaṁ vāpravāhēna paramabībhatsam । raktakusumōpacāramiva patitabahumāṁsakhaṇḍaiḥ ॥ 150 ॥
itīdr̥śasya bhavanasya garbhagr̥hē saṁsthitā dr̥ṣṭā । bhīmakumārēṇa naramuṇḍamaṇḍitā kālikāpratimā ॥ 151 ॥
vikarālanayanavadanā mahiṣārūḍhā ca bhairavaśarīrā । narāntramālāhārā viṁśatikarā praharaṇasanāthā ॥152॥
īdr̥śarūpāyā: kālikāyāḥ purataśca saṁsthitō dr̥ṣṭaḥ । sa pūrvakapaṭakārī krūraḥ kāpālikō dhr̥ṣṭaḥ ॥ 153॥
tathā vāmakaratalēna tēna kāpālikēna duṣṭēna । ēkaḥ sundarapuruṣō dr̥ṣṭaḥ kēśēṣu parigr̥hītaḥ ॥ 154 ॥
yasmin punarvāhau kumāra āgacchat samārūḍhaḥ । sa tasya kupākhaṇḍinaḥ satkō dakṣiṇō bāhuḥ ॥ 155 ॥
taṁ kēśaparigr̥hītaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā kumārēṇa cintitamētat । kimēṣa pāpiṣṭhaḥ kariṣyati karadhr̥tapuruṣasya ? ॥156॥
tasmāt pracchannō bhūtvā'hamētasya cēṣṭitaṁ tāvat । paśyāmi tataḥ paścād yad bhaviṣyati tatkariṣyāmi ॥197॥
iti cintayitvā kumārastasya bhujātō jhaṭityuttīrya । tasyaiva pr̥ṣṭhadēśasya pr̥ṣṭhataḥ saṁsthitō nibhr̥taḥ ॥158॥
bhīmakumārasya khaṅgaṁ gr̥hītvā samāgatā bhujā yāvat । vāmakaravr̥tapuruṣō bhāṇataḥ kāpalikēnēdam ॥159॥
rē smara kimapi nijēṣṭadaivataṁ yadahamanēnāsinā । gr̥hītvā tava śiraḥ kamalaṁ pūjāṁ kālyā viracayiṣyāmi ॥ 160॥
sa bhaṇati sakalajagajjīvabāndhavō jinavarō mayā tāvat । sarvāvasthāgatēnāpi smartavyō nānya iti ॥161॥

jēṇa ahaṁ anmahiō diṭṭhō, kāvāliyassa pāvassa । maha vāraṁtassavi jō vissasiō patthiō tēṇa ॥
nīō katthaī sō cēva māṇasē majjha phurai tā havau । sō ciya bhīmakumārō saraṇaṁ,
cciya bhīmakumārō saraṇaṁ, tō bhaṇai pāsaṁḍī ॥
rē rē sō tuha sāmī puvvipi palāiō maha bhaēna । annaha tassa sirēṇa pūyaṁtō kāliya dēvi ।। 165 ।।
tayabhāvē tappūyā tujjha sirēpi tāva kāyavvā । tō kaha tujjha sarannō sō hōhī mūḍha ! kāurisō ? ॥ 166 ॥
kiñca ।
rē rē sō tujjha pahū kahiō maha kāliyāē dēvīē | viṁjhagiriguhāsannē siyabhikkhūṇaṁ sayāsammi ॥ 167 ॥
ēyaṁ khaggaṁpi maē samāṇiyaṁ tassa lakkhaṇōvēyaṁ । ēēṇaṁ ciya khaggēṇa tujjha rē chijjihī sīsaṁ ॥ 168 ॥
tā kaha sō tuha nāhī āgaṁtuṁ rakkhihī tumaṁ ēttha ? | jaṛa kāliṁ sumaraṁtō tō rakkhatō ahaṁ caiva ॥ 169 ॥
ubhayālāvaṁ sōuṁ kumarō ciṁtara sadukkhasāmarisaṁ । buddhimayara haramaṁti hā ! kaha pāvō viḍaṁbē ? ॥ 170 ॥
tattō hakka rē rē nigiṭṭa pāvi hi ! tumamēva । kāuṁ kīṇāsabaliṁ karēmi parinibbuē suyaṇē || 171 ॥
aha sō mati mōtuṁ valiō kumarassa, tēṇa tō tassa । dārakavāḍapahārēṇa pāḍiyaṁ hatthaō khagaṁ ॥ 172॥
ghēttuṁ kēsēsu dharāē pāḍiō dāumurutalē caraṇaṁ । jā kaṭissai sīsaṁ tā kālī aṁtarē hōuṁ ॥ 173 ॥
jaṁpai mā mā māratu ēyaṁ maha vacchalaṁ chaliyalōyaṁ । jō narasirakamalēhiṁ raēi maha vaṁchiyaṁ pūyaṁ ॥ 174॥
ēēṇa kira sirēṇa aṭṭhattarasayamaṇūṇagaṁ hōhī । narasirakamalāṇa, ahaṁ tattō ēyassa paccakkhā || 175॥
hōuṁ kira sijjhissaṁ tāva tumaṁ āgaō si nivataṇaya ! । tuha pōrisēṇa tuṭṭhā maggasu jaṁ kiṁpi paḍihāra ||
kintu taccaraṇasēvī pūrvapuruṣakramāgataḥ svāmī । sahapāṁśukrīḍitaḥ praṇatavatsalō jīvitādapi ॥ 162 ॥
yēnāhamadhikō dr̥ṣṭaḥ, kāpālikasya pāpasya । mama vārayatō'pi yō viśvasitaḥ prārthitastēna ॥ 163॥
nītaḥ kvāpi sa ēva mānasē mama sphurati tasmād bhavatu । sa ēva bhīmakumāraḥ śaraṇaṁ, tatō bhaṇati pākhaṇḍī ॥
rē rē sa tava svāmī pūrvamapi palāyitō mama bhayēna । anyathā tasya śirasā'pūjayiṣyaṁ kālikāṁ dēvīm ॥ 165॥
tadabhāvē tatpūjā tava śirasāpi tāvatkartavyā । tataḥ kathaṁ tava śaraṇyaḥ sa bhaviṣyati mūṛha ! kāpuruṣa ! 1 ॥ 166॥
rē rē sa tava prabhuḥ kathitō mama kālikyā dēvyā । vindhyagiriguhāsannē sitabhikṣūṇāṁ sakāśē ॥ 167॥
ēṣa khaḍgō'pi mayā samānītastasya lakṣaṇōpētaḥ । ētēnaiva khaḍgēna tava rē chētsyatē śiraḥ ॥168॥
tasmātkathaṁ sa tava nātha āgatya rakṣiṣyati tvāmatra ? | yadi kālīmasmariṣyastatō'rakṣiṣyamahamēva ॥ 169 ॥
ubhayālāpaṁ śrutvā kumāraścintayati saduḥkhasāmarṣam | buddhimakaragr̥hamantriṇaṁ hā ! kathaṁ pāpō viḍambayati ? ॥
tatō hakkayati rē rē nikr̥ṣṭa pāpiṣṭha bhraṣṭa ! tvāmēva । kr̥tvā kīnāśabaliṁ karōmi parinirvr̥tān sujanān ॥ 179॥
atha sa mantriṇaṁ muktvā valitaḥ kumārāya tēna tatastasya । dvārakapāṭaprahārēṇa pātitō hastataḥ khagam ।। 172।
gr̥hītvā kēśēṣu dharāyāṁ pātitō dattvōrutalē caraṇam । yāvatkarṣiṣyati śīrṣa tāvatkālyantarē bhūtvā ॥ 173॥
jalpati mā mā mārayaitaṁ mama vatsalaṁ chalitalōkam । yā naraśiraḥ kamalai racayati mama vāñchitāṁ pūjām ||
ētēna kila śirasā'ṣṭōttaraśatamanūnakaṁ bhaviṣyati । naraśiraḥ kamalānām, ahaṁ tata ētasya pratyakṣā ॥ 175॥

184
supāsanāha cariammi-
tō kumarēṇa bhaṇiyā tuṭṭā jai dēsi icchiyaṁ majjha । maṇavaikāēhiṁ tumaṁ jīvavahaṁ tā vivajjēhi ॥ 177॥৷
tavasīlēhivi ya lōē tujjha kā hōjja dhammasaṁpattī । ēsō ciya tuha dhammō muṁcasu tasaghāya duvvasaṇaṁ ।। 178 ॥
jēṇa ।
appāṇaṁ na lahai pāyavō jahā mūlapasaraparihīṇō । taha dhammō jīvāṇaṁ na hōi nūṇaṁ dayāē viṇā || 179 ॥
tāmā ghāyāvaha apaṇō purō pāṇiṇō viṇā kajjaṁ । majjēṇa ya mā tusasu visidvajaṇagara hiṇijjēṇa ||
kajjēva pāṇavahaṁ kariṁti kāriti tē mahāpācā । jē uṇa kajjēṇa viṇā tēsiṁpi hu tē sirōmaṇiṇō ॥
kāvā liyāhāravivajjiyāē ki tujjha jīvavahaṇēṇaṁ । puvvabhavammivi na kaō jiṇadhammō jīvadayarammō ||
tēṇa tu saṁjāyā aikivvisiyā kudēvajōṇīē । tā caya jīvavahaṁ tuha bhattāvi kuṇaṁti jēṇa dayaṁ ॥ 183 ||
taha sadaṁsaṇamūlaṁ dhammaṁ sadahasu jiṇavariṁdēhi । sahiyaṁ tappaḍimāṇa ya jahasattīō kuṇasu bhartti ॥ 184 ॥
tammaggasaṁṭhiyāṇa ya saṁnijjhaṁ kuṇasu savvakajjēsu । jēṇa narattaṁ ladhuṁ aṇatasōkkhaṁ lahasi mōkkhaṁ ।। 185॥
tō kālī paṇa ajjapabhii savvaṁpi jīvarā simahaṁ । niyajīvaṁva gaṇissaṁ iya bhaṇiumadaṁsaṇaṁ pattā ||
ittō laddhāvasarō kumaraṁ paṇamēi buddhimayaraharō । asujalāvilanayaṇō taṁ daḍhamāliṁgaē sōvi ॥ 187 ||
dāruṇapariṇāmamissa pāviṇō taṁ viyāṇamāṇōvi । sajjaṇasēhara ! kaha pāḍiō piḍē dujjaṇēṇimiṇā ? |
buddhimayara haramaṁtī bhaṇai rayaṇīē paḍhamapaharammi | kumara ! tuha vāsabhavaṇē saṁpattā bhāriyā jāva ।। 189 ॥
bhūtvā kila sētsyāmi tāvattvamāgatō'si nr̥patanaya ! | tava pauruṣēṇa tuṣṭā mārgaya yatkimapi pratibhāti ।। 176 ।
tataḥ kumārēṇa bhaṇitā tuṣṭā yadi dadāsīpsitaṁ mahyam । manōvacaḥ kāyaistvaṁ jīvavadhaṁ tadā vivarjaya || 177 ॥
tapaḥ śīlābhyāmapi ca lōkē tava kā bhavēd dharmasaṁpatti: ? । ēṣa ēva tava dharmō muñca saghāta durvyasanam ॥ 178॥
yēna ।
ātmānaṁ na labhatē pādapō yathā mūlaprasaraparihīṇaḥ । tathā dharmōṁ jīvānāṁ na bhavati nūnaṁ dayayā vinā ॥ 179 ॥
tasmād mā ghātayātmanaḥ puraḥ prāṇinō vinā kāryam । madyēna ca mā tuṣya viśiṣṭajana garhaṇīyēna ॥ 180॥
kāryēṇāpi prāṇavadhaṁ kurvanti kārayanti tē mahāpāpāḥ । yē punaḥ kāryēṇa vinā tēṣāmapi khalu tē śirōmaṇayaḥ ॥
kāvalikāhāravivarjitayā kiṁ tava jīvavadhēna । pūrvabhavē'pi na kr̥tō jinadharmōṁ jīvadayāramyaḥ || 182||
tēna tvaṁ saṁjātā atikilbiṣakā kudēvayōnau । tasmāttyaja jīvavadhaṁ tava bhaktā api kurvanti yēna dayām ॥
tathā saddarśanamūlaṁ dharmaṁ śraddhēhi jinavarēndraiḥ । sahitaṁ tatpratimānāṁ ca yathāśakti kuru bhaktim || 184 ॥
tanmārgasaṁsthitānāṁ ca sāṁnidhyaṁ kuru sarvakāryēṣu । yēna naratvaṁ labdhvā'nantasaukhyaṁ labhasē mōkṣam ॥185॥
tataḥ kālī prabhaṇatyadyaprabhr̥ti sarvamapi jīvarāśimaham । nijajīvamiva gaṇayiṣyāmīti bhaṇitvā'darśanaṁ prāptā ॥
itō labdhāvasaraḥ kumāraṁ praṇamati buddhimakaragr̥haḥ । aśrujalāvilanayanastaṁ dr̥ḍhamāliṅgati sō'pi ॥ 187॥
"gaṇapariṇāmamasya pāpinastvaṁ vijānānō'pi । sajjanaśēkhara ! kathaṁ pātitaḥ piṭē durjanēnānēna ? ॥188॥
- bhaṇati rajanyāḥ prathamapraharē । kumāra ! tava vāsabhavanē saṁprāptā bhāryā yāvat ॥ 189 ॥

bhīmakumārakahā ।
185
tattha na diṭṭhā tubhē tīē tō vimhiyāē jāmillā । puṭṭhā bhaṇati chaliyā jaggaṁtā hā ! kahaṁ amhē ? ||
tō savvattha gaviṭṭhōva jā navi diṭṭhō tumaṁ taō rannō । kahiyaṁ kēṇavi kumarō hariō nisi paḍhamapaharammi |!
āyanniūṇa ēvaṁ vayaṇaṁ sīhāsaṇāō naranāhō । mucchānimīliyacchō sahasā dharaṇīyalē paḍiō । । 192 ॥
māipamuhō jaṇaṇījaṇōvi taha caiva mucchiō savvō । caṁdaṇarasēṇa sittō tō kahavi sacēyaṇō jāō ।।
jā vilaviḍaṁ payattō rāyā jaṇaṇījaṇō samatiyaṇō । tāva sahasatti pattā majjhavayā itthiyā ēkā ॥
kaṁpaṁtakarakarālā bhāsuravayaṇā dhuṇaṁtasirakamalā । bhaṇai nariṁdēṁ uṭṭhasu maha pūyaṁ kuṇasu bhattī ।। 195 ।।
ahayaṁ tuha kuladēvī samāgayā tujjha puttaattīē । mā taṁ nariṁda ! khēyaṁ kuṇasu, suō tujjha avahariō ||
pāsaṁḍiyāhamēṇaṁ uttarasāhagamisēṇa rayaṇīē । kāūṇaṁ saṁgāmaṁ kumarassa siraṁ kila gahēhī || 197 ||
tā jakkhiṇidēvīē nīō niyamaṁdirammi iccāi । kahiuṁ bhaṇiō kahivi dihiṁ ēi vibhūīē । 198 ॥
iya sā kahiūṇa gayā vayaṇaṁ saṁvāiuṁva tīē ahaṁ । sauṇanirikkhaṇahēḍaṁ jāva gaō nayaravāhimmi ॥ 199॥
tāva sahasati vāmērāsu ṭhāuṁ disāsu bāhara । khukhuttayasadēṇaṁ tittirāṇaṁ jugaṁ jhati ॥ 200 ॥
suṇaōvi hu savaḍīē gaṁtūṇaṁ dāhiṇēṇa caraṇēṇa । kaṁḍūyai uttimaṁgaṁ ramaṇīyuccē ṭhiō ṭhāṇē ॥ 201 ||
āgāsajōgiṇīē nisuō sadōvi vāmapāsammi । sāmā vāmā laviḍaṁ tārā caḍiyā sukhīradumē ॥ 202 ॥
iccāisauṇasauṇōharaṁjiō jāva kila valissāmi । tō gayaṇagaṇimiṇā ukkhiviḍaṁ ahamihāṇīō ||
tatra na dr̥ṣṭā yūyaṁ tayā tatō vismitayā yāmikāḥ । dr̥ṣṭā bhaṇanti cchalitā jāgratō hā ! kathaṁ vayam ? ॥ 190 ॥
tataḥ sarvatra gavēṣitō'pi yāvannaiva dr̥ṣṭastvaṁ tatō rājñē । kathitaṁ kēnāpi kumārō hr̥tō niśi prathamapraharē ॥ 191 ॥
ākaṇyaitad vacanaṁ siṁhāsanād naranāthaḥ । mūrcchanimīlitākṣaḥ sahasā dharaṇītalē patitaḥ ॥192॥
mālatīpramukhō jananījanō'pi tathaiva mūcchitaḥ sarvaḥ । candanarasēna siktastataḥ kathamapi sacētanō jātaḥ ॥ 193॥
yāvadvilapituṁ pravr̥ttō rājā jananījanaḥ samantrijanaḥ । tāvat sahasēti prāptā madhyavayāḥ strī ēkā ॥194॥
kampamānakarakarālā bhāsuravadanā dhunvacchiraḥ kamalā । bhaṇati narēndramuttiṣṭha mama pūjāṁ kuru bhaktyā ॥ 195॥
ahaṁ tava kuladēvī samāgatā tava putrārtyāṁ । mā tvaṁ narēndra ! khēdaṁ kuru, sutastavāpahr̥taḥ ॥ 196॥
pākhaṇḍikādhamēnōttarasādhakamiṣēṇa rajanyām । kr̥tvā saṁgrāmaṁ kumārasya śiraḥ kila grahīṣyati ॥ 197॥
tāvad yakṣiṇīdēvyā nītō nijamandira ityādi । kathayitvā bhaṇitaṁ katibhirapi dinairēṣyati vibhūtyā ॥ 198 ॥
iti sā kathayitvā gatā vacanaṁ saṁvādayitumiva tasyā aham । śakunanirīkṣaṇa hētōryāvadvatō nagarād bahiḥ ॥ 199 ॥
tāvatsahasēti vāmētarayōḥ sthitvā diśōrvyāharati । khukhutrayaśabdēna tittirayōryugaṁ jhaṭiti ॥ 200॥
śunakō'pi khalu svasani gatvā dakṣiṇēna caraṇēna । kaṇḍūyatyuttamāṅgaṁ ramaṇīyōcē sthitaḥ sthānē || 201 ॥
ākāśayōginyāḥ śrutaḥ śabdō'pi vāmapārśvē । śyāmā vāmā lapitvā tārā caṭitā sukṣīradrumē ॥ 202॥
ityādisaguṇaśakunaiaugharañjitō yāvatkila valiṣyē । tatō gaganagatēnānēnōtkṣipyāhamihānītaḥ ॥203॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
bahupunnapāvaṇijjāṇa mēlijaṁḍaṁ tuha caraṇakamalāṇaṁ । tuhavirahavihuriō haṁ nivvaviō jhatti tō kumara ! || 204 |
paramuvayārī ēsō tā saṁpaiṇuggahaṁ maha vihēḍaṁ । uvaisaha dhammamēyassa sō ta bhai uvaviṭṭō || 205॥
maha dēvīē disaṁtēṇa caiva dhammō athammacariyassa | succiya saraṇaṁ tadēsaō ya maha hōu jiṇanāhō || 206|
aparaṁ ca ।
avayākhvayāraparasta buddhimayarahara ! tuha paē vaṁdē । guṇamaṇirōhaṇagiriṇō dāsō haṁ puṇa kumārassa || 207
jāvēvaṁ tē jaṁpaṁti tāva uiē ravimmi tattha taō । pattō karīva jakkhō sattaṁgapaiḍiō sōvi || 208॥
kumaraṁ karē karēuṁ niyapaṭṭīē ṭhavēi maṁti ca । kāliyabhavaṇāu taō uppaiō gayaṇamammi || 209 ॥
tattō kumarō jaṁpara ahaha ahō ! savvamacalōyasmi । ērisakarivararayaṇaṁ kiṁ dīsai kiṁva uppayara ? || 210
buddhimaya haramaṁtī pabhaṇai jiṇavayaṇabhāviyamaīō । taṁ natthi saṁvihāṇaṁ kumāra ! jaṁ bhavai nēha bhavē ।।211
kiṁtu tuhapunnapagarisaparipēriyasuravarō imō kōvi । tā jāu jattha tattha va natthi bhayaṁ ihasayāsāō ।। 212
iya japatāṇa khaṇēṇa tāṇa hatthī nahāu avayariḍaṁ । ēkkammi sunnanagarē gōuradārasmi tē mōtuṁ ॥293॥
katthavi gaōha kumarō maṁti mōttaṇaṁ nayarabāhimmi । nivbhayacittō pavisara ēgāgī nayaramajjhammi || 214 |
varasatyapaddhaiṁ piva sasuvannaṁ pajarabimalalaṁkāraṁ । sōvannavaṇiyahaṭṭi annēvi hu tattha haṭṭa gihē ॥ 215||
pēcchaṁtō jā vacai sunnē rannivva tō tarhi niyai । narasiṁhāgāradharaṁ kiṁpi accanbhuyaṁ jīvaṁ ॥ 216 ॥
tasu duha dāḍhaha aṁtari rasaṇā lahalahai, naṁ sārayaghaṇamajjhi taḍicchaḍa jhalahalai |
tēṇaccaṁtarasaṁta ruirataṇu ēgu naru, vayaṇi gahiu pabhaṇaṁta mēṁ maha pāṇa haru ।।217॥
bahupuṇyaprāpaṇīyāni mēlayitvā tava caraṇakamalāni । tvadvirahavidhuritō'haṁ nirvāpitō jhaṭiti tataḥ kumāra ! |
paramōpakāryēṣa tasmātsaṁpratyanugrahaṁ mayi vidhāya । upadiśa dharmamētasya sa tatō bhaṇatyupaviṣṭaḥ ||20||
mama dēvīṁ diśataiva dharmō'dharmacaritasya । sa ēva śaraṇaṁ taddēśakya mama bhavatu jinanāthaḥ || 206 ||
apakārōpakāraparasya buddhimakaragr̥ha ! tava pādau vandē । guṇamaṇirōhaṇa girērdāsō'haṁ punaḥ kumārasya ॥207॥
yāvadēvaṁ tē jalpanti tāvaduditē ravaiau tatra tataḥ । prāptaḥ karīva yakṣaḥ saptāṅgapratiṣṭitaḥ sō'pi ॥ 208 ॥
kumāraṁ karē kr̥tvā nijapr̥ṣṭhē sthāpayati mantriṇaṁ ca । kālikābhavanāt tata utpatitō gaganamārga ॥ 209॥
tataḥ kumārō jalpatyahaha ahō ! sarvamartyalōkē । īśakarivararatnaṁ kiṁ dr̥śyatē kiṁvōtpatati ? ॥21॥
buddhimakaragr̥hamantrī prabhaṇati jinavacanabhāvitamatēḥ । tannāsti saṁvidhānaṁ kumāra ! yad bhavati nēha bhavē ॥ 211{}
kintu tvatpuṇyaprakarṣapariprēritasuravarō'yaṁ kō'pi । tasmād yātu yatra tatra vā nāsti bhayamasya sakāśāt ॥
iti jalpatōḥ kṣaṇēna tayōrhastī nabhasō'vatīrya । ēkasmin śūnyanagarē gōpuradvārē tau muktvā ॥213॥
।
kvāpi gatō'tha kumārō mantriṇaṁ muklā nagarād bahiḥ । nirbhayacittaḥ praviśatyēkākī nagaramadhyē ॥ 214॥
varaśāstrapaddhatimiva sasuvarṇā pracuravimalālaṅkārām । sauvarṇavaṇigvīśrīmanyānyapi ca tatra haṭṭagr̥hāṇi ॥ 215 ॥
paśyan yāvad vrajati śūnyē'raṇya iva tatastasminpaśyati । narasiṁhākāravaraṁ kimapyatyadbhutaṁ jīvam ॥ 216 ॥

187
taṁ daṭṭhē kumarō dēvayamaidāruṇaṁ imaṁ kiṁpi । iya ciṁtiya taṁ saviṇayamiya patthai muṁca purisamimaṁ ॥218॥
ummīliyacchijuyalēṇa tēṇa tā pulaiūṇa kumaramuhaṁ । sō purisō vayaṇāō mōtuṁ payahiō ṭaviō ||
maṇiyaṁ ca ahō ! supasannavayaṇa ! millēmi kaha mahaṁ ēyaṁ । ajja maē chuhiēṇaṁ jaṁ laddhō ēsa bhakvaṁti ? ॥
kumarō bhāi tumaṁ kayavikkiyarūvō surōvva lakkhiyasi । tō kaha tuha bhakrakhamiṇaṁ jamakavalāhāriṇō dēvā ? ||
ahō jaṁvā taṁtrā karē, juttaṁ na tumha puṇa ēyaṁ । vilavaṁtāṇa sadukkhaṁ jīvāṇaṁ māraṇaṁ vivahā ! || 222 ||
jahavā havā jīvē jō baṁdhai vaha mārai rasaṁtē । sō dussahaduhadaṁdōlikavaliō bhamai bhavagahaṇē ॥223॥
tō sō paḍijaṁpara saccamiṇaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ tara savvaṁ । kiṁpuṇa duharichōlī imiṇā taha daṁsiyā majjha || 224 ||
tō punvabhavamma jaha sayavāraṁpi māriē ṇimiṇā । vijjhāi na kōhaggī ittō ciya jīvamāṇassa | | 225 ||
kāuṁ katthaṇāō bahuyāō dusahadukkhajaṇaṇīō । mārissāmi imaṁ, tō kumarō taṁ bhai bhō bhadda ! ||
avayārisu jai kōvō tuha tā kiṁ na kuṇasi kōvammi । sayalapurisatthavigdhē nibbigghē dukkha hēummi ? ||
tā muṁcasu dīṇamiṇaṁ karuṇārasapaccayaṁ ciṇasu dhammaṁ । jēṇannabhavē mōkkhaṁ pāvasi niṭṭhāviu kammaṁ ॥228॥
iya bahu vinnaviōvi huna jāva sō kahavi millaē purisaṁ । tō kumarō ciṁtai sāmabhēyadāṇāṇimō'sajjhō ||
kōhāvō tō sahasā piliūṇa taṁ kumarō । niyapaṭṭhīē ṭhāvai purisaṁ kuviō taō sōvi ॥ 230 ॥
dhāvai pasāriyamuhō giliuṁ kumaraṁ taō kumārēṇa । dhariḍaṁ khurammi matthayauvariṁ bhāmē mārō ॥231॥
tasya dvayōrdayōrantō rasanā lālalyatē, nanu śāradaghanamadhyē taḍicchaṭā jājvalyatē ।
tēnātyantaṁ rasan ruciratanurēkō narō, vadanē gr̥hītaḥ prabhaṇan mā mama prāṇān hara ॥ 217॥
tatastad dr̥ṣṭvā kumārō daivatamatidāruṇamidaṁ kimapi । iti cintayitvā taṁ savinayamiti prārthayatē muñca puruṣamim ।।
unmīlitākṣiyugalēna tēna tatō dr̥ṣṭrā kumāramukham । sa puruṣō vadanānmuktvā pādayōradhastātsthāpitaḥ ॥219॥
bhaṇitaṁ cāhō ! suprasannavadana ! muñcāmi kathamahamētam । adya mayā kṣudhitēna yallabdha ēṣa bhakṣyamiti ? ॥ 220 ॥
kumārō bhaṇati tvaṁ kr̥tavaikriyarūpaḥ sura iva lakṣyasē । tataḥ kathaṁ tava bhakṣyamidaṁ yadakavalāhāriṇō dēvāḥ ? ||
abudha yadvā tadvā karōti, yuktaṁ na tava punarētat । vilapatāṁ saduḥkhaṁ jīvānāṁ māraṇaṁ vibudha ! ||222||
yathā vā tathā vā jīvān yō badhnāti hanti mārayati rasataḥ । sa duḥsahaduḥkhadvandvālīkavalitō bhramati bhavagahanē ||
tataḥ sa pratijalpati satyamidaṁ jalpitaṁ tvayā sarvam । kintu duḥkhapaṅgiranēna tathā darśitā mama ॥ 224॥
itaḥ pūrvabhavē yathā śatavāramapi māritēnānēna । vidhyati na krōdhāgnirita ēva jīvataḥ ॥ 225 ॥
kr̥tvā kadarthanā bahūduḥ sahaduḥkhajananīḥ । mārayiṣyāmīmaṁ, tataḥ kumārastaṁ bhaṇati bhō bhadra ! || 226 ॥
apakāriṣu yadi kōpastava tadā kiṁ na karōṣi kōpē । sakalapuruṣārthavighnē nirvighnē duḥkhahētau ? ॥ 227॥
tasmānmuñca danimimaṁ karuṇārasapratyayaṁ cinu dharmam । yēnānyabhavē mōkṣaṁ prāpnōṣi niṣṭhāpya karma ॥ 228॥
iti bahu vijñapitō'pi khalu na yāvatsa kathamapi muñcati puruṣam । tataḥ kumāraścintayati sāmabhēdadānānāmayamasādhyaḥ ॥
krōdhāviṣṭō dhr̥ṣṭastataḥ sahasā prērya taṁ kumāraḥ । nijaṣpr̥ṣṭhē sthāpayati puruṣaṁ kupitastataḥ sō'pi ॥ 230 ॥

supāsanāha cariṣyasmmi-
tō sō sumō hōuṁ niggaṁtuṁ kumarahatthamajjhāō । adissōṁ kumaraguṇōharaṁjiō ṭāi tatthēva ॥ 232 ॥
tammi u adissamāṇē kumarō aha tassa nāyaranarassa । bhuyadaṁḍavilaggō kōugēṇa pavisēi rāyaulaṁ ॥
māyaṁgasaṁgayāō susuttajuttāō samayaghaḍiyāō । jattha kuviṁdakuḍīōva gayasālāō niyai kumarō ||
kattha ya tarusāhāō ghaṇavallisamāulāō tuṁgāō । hayasālāu niyaṁtō vaccai kumarō sunissaṁkō ||
vibuhāṇa maīō iva bahumatthasamanniyāō vimalāō । āuhasālāō varāō tattha gacchai niyacchaṁtō ॥
ērisarūvaṁ tō rāyaaṁgaṇaṁ uccasaṁ palōyaṁtō । kumarō narēṇa sahiō saṁpattō rāyabhavaṇammi ||237||
bahuruvanimmatriē suvicittacittayammi sattatalē । vimhayarasavasahiyaō pāsāē jā samārūḍhō || 238 ॥
tō tattha thaṁbhaviṇikuṭṭiyāhiṁ pavarāhiṁ sālahaṁjīhiṁ । jōḍiyakarāhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ sāgayamiha bhīmakumarassa ||
tattō turiyaīē ōyariḍaṁ thaṁbhauvaribhāgāō । kaṇayamayamāsaṇaṁ tassa tāhiṁ dinaṁ sabahumāṇaṁ ॥ 240 ॥
tō kumarō tēṇa narēṇa saṁjuō jāva tattha uvaviṭṭhō । tā lahu nahāu pattā majjaṇasāmaggiyā savvā ||
tō sālahaṁjiyāhiṁ payaṁpiya parihiu imaṁ pōttiṁ । kumarō karēu pahāṇaṁ kāuṁ amhōvari pasāyaṁ ॥ 242 ॥
tō kumarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ maha mittō nagaraparisarujāṇē । ciṭṭhai lahu hakkāraha tō tāhi sōvi āṇīō ||
buddhimayara haramaṁtī majjaṇayaṁ kāriḍaṁ kumārēṇaṁ । saha tāhiṁ taō bhōyaṇavihiṁ ca aha jāva pallēkē || 244 |
ṭhaviō vihiyahiyaō kumarō ciṭṭhēi attaṇō puraō । tā kaṁtilaṁ dēvaṁ picchaṛa calakuṁḍalāharaṇaṁ ||245||
dhāvati prasāritamukhō galituṁ kumāraṁ, tataḥ kumārēṇa । dhr̥tvā khurē mastakōpari bhramayitumārabdhaḥ ॥231॥
tataḥ sa sūkṣmō bhūtvā nirgatya kumārahastamadhyāt । adr̥śyaḥ kumāra guṇaugharañjitastiṣṭhati tatraiva ॥ 232॥
tasmiṁstvadr̥śyamānē kumārō'tha tasya nāgaranarasya । bhujadaṇḍavilagnaḥ kautukēna praviśati rājakulam ||233॥
mātaṅgasaṁgatāḥ susūtrayuktāḥ samakaghaṭitāḥ । yatra kuvindakuṭīvi gajaśālāḥ paśyati kumāraḥ ॥ 234॥
kva ca taruśākhā ghanavallīsama | kulāstuṅgāḥ । hayaśālāḥ paśyan vrajati kumāraḥ suniḥśaṅkaḥ ||235॥
vibudhānāṁ matīriva bahuśa (śā) strasamanvitā vimalāḥ । āyudhaśālāḥ varāstatra gacchati paśyan ॥236॥
īdr̥śarūpaṁ tatō rājāṅgaṇamudvasaṁ pralōkamānaḥ । kumārō narēṇa sahitaḥ saṁprāptō rājabhavanē ॥ 237॥
bahurūpanirmāpitē suvicitracitra kē saptatalē । vismayarasavaśahr̥dayaḥ prāsādē yāvat samārūḍhaḥ ॥238॥
tatastatra stambhavinikuṭṭitābhiḥ pravarābhiḥ śālabhañjabhiḥ । yōjitakarābhirbhaṇitaṁ svāgatamiha bhīmakumārasya ॥
tatastvaritagatyā'vatīrya stambhōparibhāgāt । kanakamayamāsanaṁ tasya tābhirdattaṁ sabahumānam ॥ 240 ॥
tataḥ kumārastēna narēṇa saṁyutā yāvattatrōpaviṣṭaḥ । tāvallaghu nabhasaḥ prāptā majjanasāmagrikā sarvā ॥ 241 ॥
tataḥ śālabhañjībhiḥ prajalpitaṁ paridhāyēdaṁ śāṭakam । kumāraḥ karōtu snānaṁ kr̥tvā'smākamupari prasādam ||
tataḥ kumārēṇa bhaṇitaṁ mama mitraṁ nagaraparisarōdyānē । tiṣṭhati laghu hakkārayata tatastābhiḥ sō'pyānītaḥ ॥
buddhimakaragr̥hamantrī, majjanakaṁ kārayitvā kumārēṇa saha tābhistatō bhōjanavidhiṁ cātha yāvatpalyaṅkē ॥ 244॥
sthāpitō vismitahr̥dayaḥ kumārastiṣṭhatyātmanaḥ purataḥ । tāvatkāntimantaṁ dēvaṁ paśyati calakuṇḍalābharaṇam ॥

tō jōḍiyakarajuyalēṇa jaṁpiyaṁ tēṇa bhīmakumarassa । tuha asamavikamēṇa tuṭṭō hūṁ magga tā kiṁci ॥ 246॥
kumarēṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ jai tuṭṭō taṁ si majjha tā kahasu । kō si tumaṁ kimimaṁ paṭṭaṇaṁ ca kahamuvvasaṁ jāyaṁ ? ॥
dēvēṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ nisuṇasu bhō kumara ! jaṁ tara puḍhaṁ । kaṇayapuraṁ puramēyaṁ kaṇayara hō nāma iha rāyā | 248|
jō rakkhiō tara sō, ēyassa purōhiō ahaṁ caṁḍō । savvasta jaṇassuvariṁ ruṭṭhō ciṭṭhāmi nipi । 249 |
ittō savvāṇavi purajaṇāṇa jāō aīva vēsō haṁ । nō ittha kōvi hu maē phiṭṭāmittōvi saṁjaṇiō | 250 |
sōvi naravariṁdō payaīē kannadubbalō kurō । saṁkāēva avarāhassa kuṇai aidāruṇaṁ daṁḍaṁ || 251 ||
aha annayā kayāī kēṇāvi hu majjha asahamāṇēṇa । aliyaṁ parikahiyamiṇaṁ jaha cukō ēsa ḍaṁbīē || 252 ॥
phālaṁ magatōvi hu tō haṁ aviyāriūṇa ēēṇa । ēyaṁ na annā hōi kahavi, ēvaṁ bhaṇatēṇaṁ ॥ 253॥
viṭāviḍaṁ siṇēṇaṁ chaṁṭāvēūṇa pauratēllēṇa । jālāviō rasaṁtō tattō pāṇēhiṁ paricattō ॥ 254 ॥
bhaviyanvayāvasēṇaṁ jāō hamakāmanijjarāē ihaṁ । nāmēṇaṁ savvagilōtti rakkhasō sumariḍaṁ vēraṁ ।। 255 ||
itthāgaṁtūṇa maē sōvi tirōhiō pauralōō । taha visarisarūvadharēṇa naravarō ēsa saṁgahiō || 256॥
karuṇāē'ṇannapō risapagarisarayaṇāyarēṇa taha tumaē । mōyāvaṁtēṇa imaṁ camakkiyaṁ māṇasaṁ majjha || 257 ||
tattō ahissēṇaṁ ēsa samaggōvi tumha uvayārō । bhattīē divvasattīē viraiō majjāīō || 258 ||
tumhaṇuvittīē tahā ēsōvi hu payaḍiō maē lōō । tā jā niyai kumarō tā picchai sayalapuralōyaṁ ॥
iya ēvaṁ bahatē kumarō picchai surēhiṁ thuvvaṁtaṁ । gayaṇēṇa । gacchaṁtaṁ mōhariḍaṁ cāraṇamuṇidaṁ ॥ 260 ॥
tatō yōjitakarayugalēna jalpitaṁ tēna bhīmakumārasya । tavāsamavikramēṇa tuṣṭō'haṁ mārgaya tasmātkiñcit ॥ 246 ॥
kumārēṇa tatō bhaṇitaṁ yadi tuṣṭastvamasi tadā kathaya । kō'si tvaṁ kimidaṁ pattana ca kathamudvasaṁ jātam ? ||
dēvēna tatō bhaṇitaṁ śr̥ṇu bhōḥ kumāra ! yattvayā pr̥ṣṭam । kanakapuraṁ puramētat kanakarathō nāmēha rājā ॥ 248॥
।
yō rakṣitastvayā saḥ, ētasya purōhitō'haṁ caṇḍa: । sarvasya janasyōpari ruṣṭastiṣṭhāmi nityamapi || 249॥
itaḥ sarvēṣāmapi purajanānāṁ jātō'tīva dvēṣyō'ham | nō atra kimapi khalu mayā mārgamittramapi saṁjanitam 250
ēṣō'pi naravarēndraḥ prakr̥tyā karṇadurbala krūraḥ । śaṅkayāpyaparādhasya karōtyatidāruṇaṁ daṇḍam ॥259॥

athānyadā kadācitkēnāpi hi mamāsahamānēna । alīkaṁ parikathitamidaṁ yathā bhraṣṭa ēṣa śvapacyām ॥ 252॥
dhairya mārgayannapi khalu tatō'hamavicāryaitēna । ētannānyathā bhavati kathamapiṁ, ēvaṁ bhaṇatā ॥ 253 ॥
vēṣṭayitvā sinēna sēcayitvā pracuratailēna । jvālitō rasaṁstataḥ prāṇaiḥ parityaktaḥ ॥254॥
bhavitavyatāvaśēna jātō'hama kāmanirjarayēha | nāmnā sarvagila iti rākṣasaḥ smr̥tvā vairam ॥255॥

supāsanāha ca
buddhimayara haramaṁtī jattha ṭhiō āsi kumaraparimukō । tattha muṇidō paramāsanammi suraviraiyammi ṭhiō ॥
tāhē kumaravaṇaṁ savvagilō rakkhasō imaṁ bhaṇiō । hē rakkharsida ! ēsō majjha gurū āgaō tattha || 262 ॥
ēyassa caraṇajuyadaṁsaṇēṇa sahalīkarēmu appāṇaṁ । iya bhaṇiē rakkhēṇaṁ payaṁpiyaṁ hōu ēvaṁti || 263 ||
buddhimayara haramaṁtī kaṇagarahō kumarasavvagilapamuhā । savvēvi bhattimatā saṁpattā muṇisayāsamma || 264 ॥
kaṇayakamalō viṭṭhō suranarakhayariṁdasaṁdhuṇijjaṁtō । mōhariū muṇināhō paṇaō bhattīē savvēhiṁ ॥ 265 ॥
amayarasēṇava sittēṇa tēṇa savvēṇa purajaṇēṇāvi । āgaṁtu bhattibharēṇa paṇamiō tattha muṇināhō || 266॥
tattō muṇirāēṇaṁ āḍhattā dhammadēsaṇā tēsiṁ । jaha kōhaggahagahiō jīvō paribhama bhavagaṇē || 267॥
tathāhi ;-
kōhapasattō jīvō pāvāī kuṇaṛa viviharūbāī । vahabaṁdhamāraṇāīṇi nirayagaigamaṇajōgāī || 268 ||
kōhāūriyadēhō kajjākajjaṁ na picchaē kiṁpi । juttājuttaṁ na muṇai tahēva hēēyaraṁ vatyuṁ ॥ 269 ॥
cappaī ;
jahi uppajjai jalaṇu taṁ nicchiyaṁ tā ḍahai, pāsaṭṭi phuliṁgihiṁ ḍahai navā ḍahai ।
jasu puṇu kōhu su apparaṁ avaruvi jaṇu ḍahiu, hāṇi karēi parataha jiṇavari iya kahiu ॥ 270 ॥
rōsiṇa akkhāṇu ju viyarai avarajaṇi, sō tēṇavi paribhaviyai ḍajjhai attumaṇi ।
tō taṁ sō iha lōivivairiu bhaṇi haṇa, āli ju dinnai pāvu ayāṇau na taṁ gaṇai || 271 ॥
ityēvaṁ vartamānē kumāraḥ paśyati suraiḥ stūyamānam । gaganēnāgacchantaṁ mōharipuṁ cāraṇamunīndram ॥ 260 ॥
buddhimakaragr̥hamantrī yatra sthita āsītkumāraparimuktaḥ । tatra munīndraḥ padmāsanē suraviracita sthitaḥ || 261।।
tadā kumāravarēṇa sarvagilō rākṣasa idaṁ bhaṇita: । hē rākṣasēndra ! ēṣa mama gururāgatastatra ॥ 262 ॥
ētasya caraṇayugadarśanēna saphalīkurma ātmānam । iti bhaṇitē rakṣasā prajalpitaṁ bhavatvēvamiti ॥ 263 ॥
buddhimakaragr̥hamantrī kanakarathaḥ kumārasarvagilapramukhāḥ । sarvē'pi bhaktimantaḥ saṁprāptā munisakāśē ॥ 264 ||
kanakakamalōpaviṣṭaḥ suranarakhacarēndrasaṁstūyamānaḥ । mōharipurmunināthaḥ praṇatō bhaktyā sarvēḥ ॥ 265 ॥
amr̥tarasēnēva siktēna tēna sarvēṇa purajanēnāpi । āgatya bhaktibharaṇa praṇatastatra munināthaḥ ॥ 266॥
tatō munirājēnārabdhā dharmadēśanā tēṣām । yathā krōdhagrahagr̥hītō jīvaḥ paribhramati bhavagahanē ||267॥
krōdhaprasaktō jīvaḥ pāpāni karōti vividharūpāṇi । vadhabandhamāraṇadīni nirayagatigamanayōgyāni ॥ 268 ॥
krōdhāpūritadēhaḥ kāryākāryaṁ na paśyati kimapi । yuktāyuktaṁ na jānāti tathaiva hēyētaraṁ vastu ॥ 269 ॥
catuṣpadī;--
yatrōtpadyatē jvalanastad niścitaṁ tāvaddahati, pārśvasthitaṁ sphuliṅgairdahati navā dahati ।
yasya punaḥ krōdhaḥ sa ātmānamaparamapi janaṁ dagdhvā hāniṁ karōti paratrāpi jinavarēṇēti kathitam॥ 270 ॥

rōsānaliṇa palittu muhuttiṇa ḍahai naru, niyadhammaha bhaṁḍāru susaṁṭhiu jō suciru ।
rōsapisāiṇa gahiu na bhuṁjai na ya suyai, aivallaha dhaṇu māṇusu viṇu dōsiṇa muyai || 272 ||
jaha kuṁḍalakēūra kiḍa vihasaṇavihūsiṅa, viṇayavihūṇau sōha na pāvai naru kahavi ।

taha paṁḍiu dāyāru tavassī jai tahavi, na lahai sugāimaggu sarōsiru naru kahavi || 273 ||
rōsāiṭṭhō jīvō taṁ taṁ kajjaṁ kuṇēi mūḍhamaṇō । jēṇajjiṇē pāvaṁ bhavē bhavē bhamai dukkhattō || 274 ||
iya muviṇa sōuṁ savvagilō uhiuṁ paṇamiūṇa | muṇināhaṁ paṛa jaṁpara niyattiō haṁ akajjāō | 275 ॥
pahuṇā hēlāē cciya, ahavā na taē, imēṇa kumarēṇa । jēṇa tuhapāyapaṁkayapaṇamaṇapaṇō kaō ēvaṁ | 276 ।
kumarapabhāvēṇaṁ citra nimgahiō purajaṇē maē kōvō | kaṇagarahammi saṁpai puṇa nāha! tuhappabhāvēṇa ॥ 277॥
bhaṇai muṇī uvayāraṁ nāuṁ tuha kōhapariṇaī ēvaṁ । uvadaṁsiyā maē, sō na annahā mōhapayaḍī || 278 ॥
aibhīmaṁ micchataṁ jaṁ sammattēvi tappabhāvēṇa । aiyārāṇa payārā huti duraṁtā jiyaṁtāṇaṁ || 279 ||
paralōē dukkhōhaṁ dukkhōhaṁ taṁ jaṇaṁti puṇa ēē । jēṇakaṁtā jīvā lahu bahu mannaṁti maraṇāī || 280 ||
iya muṇivayaṇaṁ sōuṁ jā kumarō bhaṇai nāha ! ēvamiṇaṁ । tā gaḍayaḍaṁ kuṇaṁtō sabhāgaō gayavarō tattha । 281 ।
tō khuhiyā sā parilā mattagaiṁdassa daṁsaṇē sahasā । taṁ kumarō dhīravium̐vappukārēi karirāyaṁ ॥ 282 ॥
tō sō saṁkōēḍa karēṁ karī takkhaṇēṇa uvasaṁtō । dipayāhiṇa karēuṁ muṇivaiṇō parisasahiyassa ||283 |
rōṣēṇābhyākhyānaṁ yō vitaratyaparajanē, sa tēnāpi paribhūyatē dātē ātmamanasi ।
tatastaṁ sa iha lōkē'pi vairiṇaṁ bhaṇitvā hanti, āli yadudīryatē pāpamajñāyakō na tadguṇayati ॥ 272 ॥
rōṣānalēna pradīptō muhūrtēṇa dahati narō, nijadharmasya bhāṇḍāgāraṁ susaṁsthitō yaḥ suciram |
rōṣapiśācēna gr̥hītō na bhuṅgē na svapiti, ativallabhaṁ dhanaṁ manuṣyaṁ vinā dōṣēṇa muñcati ॥272 ||
yathā kuṇḍalakēyūrakiraṭivibhūṣitō vinayavihīnaḥ śōbhāṁ na prāpnōti naraḥ kathamapi ।
tathā paṇḍitō dātā tapasvī yadi tathāpi, na labhatē sugatimārga sarōṣō naraḥ kathamapi ॥ 273॥
rōṣādiṣṭō jīvastattat kāryaṁ karōti mūḍhamanāḥ । yēnārjayati pāpaṁ bhavē bhavē bhramati duḥkhārtaḥ ॥ 274॥
iti munivacanaṁ śrutvā sarvagila utthāya praṇamya । munināthaṁ prati jalpati nivartitō'hamakāryāt ॥ 275॥
। ॥
pramuṇā hēlayaiva, athavā na tvayā, anēna kumārēṇa । yēna tvatpādapaṅkajapraṇamanapraguṇaḥ kr̥ta ēvam ॥ 276 ॥
kumāraprabhāvēṇaiva nigr̥hītaḥ purajanē mayā kōpaḥ । kanakarathē saṁprati punarnātha ! tvatprabhāvēṇa ॥ 277 ॥
bhaṇati munirupakāraṁ jñātvā tava krōdhapariṇatirēvam । upadarśitā mayā, sa nānyathā mōhaprakr̥tiṣu ॥ 278 ॥
atibhīmaṁ mithyātvaṁ yatsamyaktvē'pi tatprabhāvēṇa । aticārāṇāṁ prakārā bhavanti durantā jīvatām ॥279॥
paralōkē duḥkṣōbhaṁ duḥkhaiaughaṁ taṁ janayanti punarētē । yēnākrāntā jīvā laghu bahu manyantē maraṇāni ॥ 280 ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
vaṁdai bhattī muṇiṁ tattō saṁhariya hatthiṇō ruvaṁ । sō paccakkhō jakkhō jāō calakuṁḍalāharaṇō ॥ 284॥
tattō sō muṇivaṇā bhaṇiō taṁ kumaramaṇusarēūṇa । niyapaḍipōttayamēyaṁ samāgaō gayavarō hōuṁ ॥ 285॥
iha āṇīō puvviṁ ēsō kaṇagaraharāya rakkhaṭṭhā | saṁpai niyanayaraṁ para nēuṁ ēyaṁ tuhucchāhō || 286 ॥
tō jakkhēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ēvamiṇaṁ nāha! majjha ēsa nivō । kaṇagarahō puvvabhavammi nattuō āsi maha jēṇa ||
kiśca ।
vinnaviyavvamimaṁ puṇa puvvaṁ aṁgīkaēvi sammattē । pāsaṁḍiyasaṁsaggī aggīva niraggalā laggā ॥ 288 ॥
maha maṇabhavaṇē tēṇa daḍḍhā sammattarayaṇavarariddhī । haddhī jāōṇiddhī vaṁtarajōṇīē jakkhō haṁ ॥ 289॥
kāuṁ pasāyamihi ārōvaha majjha nāha ! sammattaṁ । kaṇagarahara kkhasāīhiṁ bhaṇiyama mhaṁpi ii hōu || 290 ॥
tō muṇiṇā sammattaṁ dinaṁ nivajakkharakkhasāīṇaṁ । kumarēṇa puṇō bhaṇiyaṁ majjha visōhiṁ pahu ! payaccha ||
jēṇa maē lahiūṇaṁ kahavi kulaggēṇa nāha! sammattaṁ । pāsaṁḍikusaṁgēṇaṁ puṇōvi vihiyaṁ saaiyāraṁ ।। 292॥
tappaṁkēṇaṁ maliṇaṁ nimmalapacchittadāṇa salilēṇa । majjha maṇaṁ pakkhālasu muṇiṇāvi tahēva taṁ vihiyaṁ । 293 |
tō nimmalasammattō kumarō muṇipāyavaṁdaṇaṁ kāuṁ । kaṇagaraharāyabhavaṇē rakkhasamāīhi saha pattō ॥ 294 ॥
kaṇagarahōviya rāyā amaccasāmaṁta maṁtiparikaliō । paṇamiya bhaṇai kumāraṁ savvamiṇaṁ tumha māhappaṁ । । 295॥
jaṁ jīvijjai jā rajjasaṁpayā jaṁ ca ēsa puralōō। jaṁ ēyassa ya lacchīvicchaḍḍō jaṁ ca sammattaṁ ॥ 296 ॥
tō ēsa jaṇō tuha kumara ! kiṁkarō jaharihammi kajjammi । taha vāvāriyavvō aṇuggahīō jahā hōi ।। 297॥
tataḥ sa saṁkōcya karaṁ tatkṣaṇanōpaśāntaḥ । triḥ pradakṣiṇāṁ kr̥tvā munipatēḥ pariṣatsahitasya ॥ 283॥
vandatē bhaktvā muniṁ tataḥ saṁhr̥tya hastinō rūpam । sa pratyakṣō yakṣō jātaścalakuṇḍalābharaṇaḥ ॥ 284 ॥
tataḥ sa munipatinā bhaṇitastvaṁ kumāramanusr̥tya । nijapratipautrakamētaṁ samāgatō gajavarō bhūtvā ॥ 285 ॥
ihānītaḥ pūrvamēṣa kanakaratharājarakṣārtham । saṁprati nijanagaraṁ prati nētumētaṁ tavōtsāhaḥ ॥ 286 ॥
1
tatō yakṣēṇa bhaṇitamēvamidaṁ nātha ! mamaiṣa nr̥paḥ । kanakarathaḥ pūrvabhavē naptā''sīd mama yēna ॥ 287 ॥
vijñapayitavyamidaṁ punaḥ pūrvamaṅgīkr̥tē'pi samyaktvē । pākhaṇḍisaṁsaktiragnirivārgalā lagnā ॥ 288 ॥
mama manōbhavanē, tēna dagdhā samyaktvaratnavararddhiḥ । hā dhig jātō'nr̥ddhirvyantarayōnau yakṣō'ham ॥ 289 ॥
kr̥tvā prasādamidānīmārōpaya mama nātha ! samyaktvam । kanakaratharākṣasādibhirbhaṇitamasmākamapīti bhavatu ॥ 290 ॥
tatō muninā samyaktvaṁ dattaṁ nr̥payakṣarākṣasādīnām । kumārēṇa punarbhaṇitaṁ mama viśuddhiṁ prabhō ! prayaccha ॥291॥
yēna mayā labdhvā kathamapi kulagnē nātha ! samyaktvam । pākhaṇḍikusaṅgēna punarapi vihitaṁ sāticāram ॥ 292॥
tatpaṅkēna malinaṁ nirmalaprāyaścittadānasalilēna । mama manaḥ prakṣālaya munināpi tathaiva tad vihitam || 293॥
tatō nirmalasamyaktvaḥ kumārō munipādavandanaṁ kr̥tvā । kanakaratharājabhavanē rākṣasādibhiḥ saha prāptaḥ ॥ 294 ॥
kanakarathō'pi ca rājā'mātyasāmantamantriparikalitaḥ । praṇamya bhaṇati kumāraṁ sarvamidaṁ tava māhātmyam ॥ 295॥
yajjīvyatē yā rājyasaṁpad yacaiṣa puralōkaḥ । yadētasya ca lakṣmīvistarō yacca samyaktvam ||296॥

kumāraḥ prāha; --
jammaṇamaraṇāī jahā annōnnanibaṁdhaṇaṁ bhavagayāṇaṁ । taha saṁpayāvayāō kā gaṇaṇā annahēussa ? || 298 ॥
vāvārō puṇa ēsō tumha sukulunbhavāṇa savvāṇa । na pamāō kāyavvō jiṇadhammē sudurlabhē ॥ 299 ॥
sōyarattaṁ sāhammiēsa sēvā ya sāhuvaggassa | jiṇasāsaṇē pabhāvaṇamapavittī pāvaṭhāṇēsu ॥ 300 ॥
tuma sayā vihēyā tō kumaraṁ tē bhāṁti thēvadiṇē । iha ciṭṭhaha jiṇadhammē jēṇamha pavīṇayā hōī || 301 ||
itra sōūṇaṁ tāṇaṁ kumarōjā kiṁpi dēi paḍivayaṇaṁ । tā ḍamaḍamaṁtaḍamaruyagurusaddattasiyanivalōyā ||302 ||
vāsā kālīkāvāliyaṁsajuyā tarhi pattā | kumaramabhivāiūṇaṁ uvavidvā kumarapāsammi || 303 ॥
bhaṇai ya kumāra ! tajhyā āṇijjaṁtassa tujjha iha kariṇā । ōhīē maē nāyaṁ jaha ēsa hiō kumārassa ||
tō haṁ taha caiva ṭhiyā nivyahiyayā paryapi nō caliyā । iṇhi puṇa tuha jaṇaō jaṇaṇī sayaṇō purajaṇō ya ॥
aṇavarayaṁ ruyamāṇō puṇō puṇō sumariūṇa tujjha guṇē । kajjavasēṇa gayāē tattha maē kiṁci saṁṭhaviō ॥
vihiyā ya tāṇa puraō maē pannā jahā diṇadugaṁtē । bhīmakumārō niyamā āṇēyavvō maē ēttha | | 307॥
kahiyē ca jahā kumarēṇa ṭhāviō bahujaṇō jiṇamayammi । mārijjatōva ya rakkhiō tahā bahū lōō ||
buddhimaraharasahiō cii kusalēṇa kaṇayapuranayarē । tā paramaharisaṭhāṇē khēyaṁ mā kuha tumbhēvi ॥ 309 ॥
iya suṇiya usuṣamaṇō kumarō kira kuṇai jāva patthāṇaṁ । tāva paḍapaḍahabhērībhaṁbhāiravō samucchaliō |
gayaṇayalē tattō puṇa vimāṇamālāṇa majjhimavimāṇē । hāravirāiyavacchā kuṁḍalaullihiyagaṁḍayalā ॥ 311 ॥
tata ēṣa janastava kumāra ! kiṅkarō yathā kāryē । tathā vyāpārayitavyō'nugr̥hītō yathā bhavati ॥ 297 ॥
janmamaraṇē yathā'nyōnyanibandhanaṁ bhavagatānām । tathā saṁpadāpadē, kā gaṇanā'nyahētōḥ ? ||298 ॥
vyāpāraḥ punarēṣa yuṣmākaṁ sukulōdbhavānāṁ sarvēṣām । na pramādaḥ kartavyō jinadharmē suṣṭhudurlabhē ॥ 299॥
sōdaratvaṁ sādharmikēṣu sēvā ca sādhuvargasya । jinaśāsanē prabhāvanamapravr̥ttiḥ pāpasthānēṣu ॥ 300 ॥
yuṣmābhiḥ sadā vidhēyā tataḥ kumāraṁ tē bhaṇanti stōkadināni । iha tiṣṭhata jinadharmē yēnāsmākaṁ pravīṇatā bhavati ॥
iti śrutvā tēṣāṁ kumārō yāvatkimapi dadāti prativacanam । tāvaḍḍamaḍamaḍamaruguruśabdatrastanr̥palōkā ॥ 302 ॥
viṁśatibhujā sā kālī kāpālikasaṁyutā tatra prāptā । kumāramabhivādyōpaviṣṭhā kumārapārśvē ॥ 303 ॥
bhaṇati ca kumāra ! tadā''nīyamānē tvayīha kariṇā । avadhinā mayā jñātaṁ yathēṣa hitaḥ kumārasya || 204॥
tatō'haṁ tathaiva sthitā nirvr̥tahr̥dayā padmapi nō calitā । idānīṁ punastava janakō jananī svajanaḥ purajanaśca ॥ 305 ॥
anavarataṁ rudan punaḥ punaḥ smr̥tvā tava guṇān । kāryavaśēna gatayā tatra mayā kiñcitsaṁsthāpitaḥ ॥ 306 ॥
vihitā ca tēṣāṁ puratō mayā pratijñā yathā dinadvayāntē । bhīmakumārō niyamādānētavyō mayātra ॥ 307 ॥
kathitaṁ ca yathā kumārēṇa sthāpitō bahujanō jinamatē । māryamāṇō'pi ca rakṣitastathā bahulakaḥ ॥ 208 ॥
buddhimakaragr̥hasahitastiṣṭhati kuśalēna kanakapuranagarē । tasmātparamaharṣasthānē khēdaṁ mā kuruta yūyamapi ॥ 309 ||
iti śrutvōtsukamanāḥ kumāraḥ kila karōti yāvatprasthānam । tāvatpaṭupaṭahamērībhambhādivaḥ samucchalitaḥ ||

supāsanāha cariammi-
diṭṭhā ya saṁnisannā dēvī dasadisipaṇāsiyatamōhā। tō saṁbhaṁtō kimimaṁti jaṁpirō uṭṭaō rakkhō || 312 ||
kkhōva gaḍaḍatō karē karēūṇa mōggaraṁ garuyaṁ । uṭṭhēi kāliyāvi hu karakaṭṭiyakattiyakara(lā।। 313 ॥
kumarō ya asaṁtō jā ci tāva garuyasadēhiṁ । jaya jīva naṁda naṁdaṇa harivāhaṇanivaiṇō kumara ! ।। 314 ||
iya bhaṇamāṇā dēvā dēvīō samāgayā kumarapāsaṁ । sāhiti jakkhiṇīē kamalakkhā ē samāgamaṇaṁ ।। 315॥
tattō sāvi khaṇēṇaṁ muttu vimāṇaṁ kumāracaraṇajugaṁ । namiūṇaṁ uvaviṭṭhā kumaraṁ vinnavai vyakusalā || 316 ॥
sampattaṁ maha dāu viṁjhagiriguhāē muṇisagāsammi । tajhyā tumaṁ mahāyasa ! ṭhiō sipattā pabhāyammi ||
tatthāhaṁ saha niyapariyaṇēṇa, saphalīkaō maē jammō । muṇipāyavaṁdaṇēṇaṁ tumha pasāēṇa bhattīē ॥ 398 ॥
diṭṭhā na tattha tubbhē puṭṭā muṇiṇō na diti paḍivayaṇaṁ । tō āulacittāē dāum̐ avahīē utra ōgaṁ ||
kārijjatā majjaṇavihimiha diṭṭhā taō saukaṁṭhā । caliyā khaliyā kālaṁ kiyaṁtamavi garuyakajjēṇa ॥
aha jakkhēṇa vimāṇaṁ biubvēūṇa pathaṇiō kumarō । āruhaha jaō sigdhaṁ gaṁtavvaṁ kamalapurana yarē ।। 321 ॥
tō uṭṭhaō kumārī saṁbōūṇa kaṇagaraharāyaṁ । ārūḍhō suvimāṇē saṁjutō maṁtiputtrēṇa || 322||
gacchaṁtassa ya dēvā gāyaṁtā kēvi kēvi naccatā । gayagajji hayahiṁsaṁ ca tappuraō kēvi kuvvaṁtā || 323 ॥
kalayalatūraravēṇa ya bahiraṁtā sayalanahayalābhōyaṁ । kumarēṇa saha pattā kamalapurāsannagāmammi || 324 ||
tō kumarō jiṇabhavaṇē gaō taō jakkharakkhasāīhiṁ । saha vaṁdiuṁ jiṇidaṁ dāvai sa mahatyamittōya ||
gaganatalē tataḥ punarvimānamālānāṁ madhyamavimānē । hāravirājitavakṣāḥ kuṇḍalō likhitagaṇḍatalā ||311॥
dr̥ṣṭā ca saṁniṣaṇṇā dēvī daśadikpraṇāśitatamaōvā । tataḥ saṁbhrāntaḥ kimidamiti jalpitrutthitaṁ rakṣaḥ || 312॥
yakṣō'pi jāgarjat karē kr̥tvā mudgaraṁ gurum । uttiṣṭhati kālikāpi khalu karakr̥ṣṭakartarīkarālā ||313 ॥
kumāraścāsaṁbhrāntō yāvattiṣṭhati tāvad guruśabdaiḥ । jaya jīva nanda nandana ! harivāhananr̥patēḥ kumāra ! ||314 ||
iti bhaṇantā dēvā dēvyaḥ samāgatāḥ kumārapārśvam । kathayanti yakṣiṇyāḥ kamalākṣāyāḥ samāgamanam ॥315॥
tataḥ sāpi kṣaṇēna muktvā vimānaṁ kumāracaraṇayugam । natvōpaviṣṭā kumāraṁ vijñapayati vacaḥ kuśalā ||316॥
samyaktvaṁ mama dattvā vindhyagiriguhāyāṁ munisakāśē । tadā tvaṁ mahāyaśaḥ ! sthitō'si prāptā prabhātē ॥ 317॥
tatrāhaṁ saha nijaparijanēna, saphalīkr̥taṁ mayā janma | munipādavandanēna tava prasādēna bhaktyā ||318 ॥
dr̥ṣṭā na tatra yūyaṁ pr̥ṣṭā munayō na dadati prativacanam । tata ākulacittayā dattvā'varupayōgam ॥319॥
kāryamāṇā majjanavidhimiha dr̥ṣṭāstataḥ sōtkaṇṭhā । calitā skhalitā kālaṁ kiyantamapi gurukāryēṇa ॥ 320 ॥
atha yakṣēṇa vimānaṁ vikr̥tya pramaṇita ḥ kumāraḥ । ārōhata yataḥ śīghraṁ gantavyaṁ kamalapuranagarē ॥321॥
tata utthitaḥ kumāraḥ saṁbōdhya kanakaratharājam । ārūḍhaḥ suvimānē saṁyuktō mantriputrēṇa ॥322॥
gacchataśca dēvā gāyantaḥ kē'pi kē'pi nr̥tyantaḥ । gajagarjiṁ hayahēṣāṁ ca tatpurataḥ kē'pi kurvantaḥ ॥ 323॥
kalakalatūraravēṇa ca badhirayantaḥ sakalanabhastalābhōgam । kumārēṇa saha prāptāḥ kamalapurāsannagrāmē ॥ 324 ॥
tataḥ kumārō jinabhavanē gatastatō yakṣarākṣasādibhiḥ । saha vanditvā jinēndraṁ dāpayati sa mahārthamitaśca ॥

ḍhakkā kahuḍakāvukāsaṁbukakara ḍipabhiīṇaṁ । āujjāṇamatucchō ucchaliō gahiranigghōsō || 326 ||
kamalapurē atthāṭṭhiēṇa āyaniō nariṁdēṇa । sō sasurāsuramaṁthijjamāṇajalarāsiravagahirō ॥ 327॥
tō rāyā maṁtiyaṇaṁ puccha kiṁ ajja kassavi muṇissa । uppannaṁ varanāṇaṁ jaṁ suvvai amaratūrakhō || 328 ॥
jā maṁtiyaṇō īhāpōhaṁ kāūṇa kiṁpi kila kahihī । taggāmabhōiēṇaṁ rāyā baddhāviō tāva || 329॥
dēva ! kumārō pattō maha gāyē dēvadēvipariyariō । jiṇabhavaṇē pāraddhō mahasavō tēhiṁ ramaṇijjō ॥ 330 ॥
tō savvaṁ ābharaṇaṁ niyaṁgalaggaṁ kirīḍaparihīṇaṁ । dāuṁ tassāiṭṭhō paḍihārō bhaṇasu savrvvapi ॥ 339॥
sāmaṁtāīlōyaṁ jēṇaṁ saṁvahai kumarapaccōṇī । kāyavvā paccūsē tahēva tēṇāvi taṁ vihiyaṁ ॥ 332 ॥
kāraviya sōhaṁ sapariyaṇō narapaī gaō samuhaṁ । āgacchaṁtō kumarō miliō maggammi naravaiṇō 333
uttariya vimāṇāō pāē paṇamēi puhaināhassa | jaṇaṇīpamuhajaṇassa ya annāṇavi kāuṁ karaṇijjaṁ 334
niyapi āēsēṇaṁ ārūḍhō karivarammi tō kumarō । maṁtisuraṇavi vihiyaṁ uciyaṁ savvasta lōyassa 335
pacchāsamma kariṇō ahasō ārōviō kumārēṇa । pattō piuṇā saddhiṁ dhavalaharē maṁgalasaēhiṁ ॥ 336॥
bhututtarammi paripucchiēṇa kumarassa sāhiyaṁ cariyē । jaṁ jaha vattaṁ taṁ taha naravaṇō maṁtitaṇaēṇa ||337॥
pariṇāviō ya bahuyā bahuā kumarō niyammi rajjammi। aha sittō ya nivēṇaṁ gahiyā ya sayaṁ tu jiṇadikkhā ||
bhīmanariṁdō jāō jiṇasāsaṇa unnaī karēūṇa | saṁpāviyapavvajjō pattō payamuttamuttamayaṁ ॥ 339 ॥
iya yēvōvi hu saṁgō pāsaṁḍīṇaṁ ihēba dukkhakarō । avihiyapacchittō uṇa narayā isu dēi duhajālaṁ ||340 ॥
ḍhakkāḍakkahuḍukkābukkāsaṁbukkakaraviprabhr̥tīnām । ātōdyānāmatuccha ucchalitō gabhīranirghōṣaḥ || 326 ॥
kamalapurē āsthānasthitēnākarṇitō narēndrēṇa । sa sasurāsuramathyamānajalarāśiravagabhīraḥ ॥ 327॥
tatō rājā mantrijanaṁ pr̥cchati kimadya kasyāpi munēḥ । utpannaṁ varajñānaṁ yat śrūyatē'maratūraravaḥ || 328 ॥
yāvad mantrijana īhāpōhaṁ kr̥tvā kimapi kila kathayiṣyati । tāmabhōgikēṇa rājā vardhitastāvat ॥ 329॥
dēva ! kumāraḥ prāptō mama grāmē dēvadēvīparikaritaḥ । jinabhavanē prārabdhō mahōtsavastai ramaṇīyaḥ ||330॥
tataḥ sarvamābharaṇaṁ nijāṅgalagnaṁ kirīṭaparihīṇam । dattvā tasmā ādiṣṭaḥ pratihārō bhaṇa sarvamapi ॥ 331॥
sāmantādilōkaṁ yēna saṁvahati kumārapratigamanam । kartavyaṁ pratyūṣē tathaiva tēnāpi tad vihitam ||332 ||
kārayitvā haṭṭaśōbhāṁ saparijanō narapatirgataḥ saṁmukham । āgacchan kumārō militō mārgē narapatēḥ ॥ 333॥
uttīrya vimānāt pādau praṇamati pr̥thivīnāthasya । jananīpramukhajanasya cānyēṣāmapi kr̥tvā karaṇīyam ॥ 334 ॥
nijapitrādēśēnārūḍhaḥ karivarē tataḥ kumāraḥ । mantrisutēnāpi vihitamucitaṁ sarvasya lōkasya ॥ 335 ॥
paścādāsanē kariṇō'tha sa ārōpitaḥ kumārēṇa । prāptaḥ pitrā sārdhaṁ dhavalagr̥hē maṅgalaśataiḥ ॥236॥
bhuktōttaraṁ paripr̥ṣṭēna kumārasya kathitaṁ caritam । yad yathā vr̥ttaṁ tattathā narapatayē mantritanayēna ||337||
pariṇāyitaśca bahūrvadhūḥ kumārō nijē rājyē । atha siktaśca nr̥pēṇa gr̥hītā ca svayaṁ tu jinadīkṣā ||338||
bhīmanarēndrō jātō jinaśāsanōnnatiṁ kr̥tvā । saṁprātipratrajyaḥ prāptaḥ padamuttamōttamam ॥ 339 ॥

bhīmakumārēṇa pattaṁ dukkhaṁ pāsaṁḍisaṁthavōtthaṁ taṁ । jaṁ puṇa suhamaṇuhūyaṁ sammattaphalaṁ ti taṁ muha || 341 ||
1
॥ iti pākhaṇḍisaṁstavē bhīmakumārōdāharaṇaṁ samāptam ॥
iti stōkō'pi khalu saṅgaḥ pākhaṇḍinā mihaiva duḥkhakaraḥ । avihitaprāyaścittaḥ punarnarakādiṣu dadāti duḥkhajālam॥
bhīmakumārēṇa prāptaṁ duḥkhaṁ pākhaṇḍisaṁstavōtthaṁ tat । yatpunaḥ sukhamanubhūtaṁ samyaktvaphalamiti tajjānīta ॥ 341 ॥

tathāhi ;-
sappurisajammabhūmī sayayapavarddhatadhammasāmaggi | vijayaṁva suppasiddhaṁ vijayapuraṁ puravaraṁ, tattha ||2||
duvvāra vērivahuhiyayadārudāvānalō nalō nāma । sajjabhuyavajjapaṁjara niyaliyasirisāriō rāyā ॥ 3 ॥
vaṇarāivtra virāya jasta sarīrē sayāvi bararāī । sacchāyā daṁtavaṇōvasōhiyā sauṇasēvaṇiyā ||4|
gaṁbhīramaṇamahōya himahallirullāsasayalasasimuttī । tassatthi piyā sōhaggamaṁjarī pēmakulabhavaṇaṁ ||5||
kayaduṭṭhalōyavilaō jaṇamaṇatulaō subuddhivaranilaō । nāmēṇa maṁtitilaō maṁtī nayatilayatarūmalaō ||
niravajjakajjajahavaḍḍhaṭha viyasāmappamukkhanīipahō । sō cēva tassa rajjē kayappamāṇō ya savvattha ||7||
aha annayā kathāī rāyā āhēḍayammi saṁcaliō । turayārūḍhō maṁtīvi patthiō saha nariṁdē ||8||
tā jāva gayā ranē sinnaṁ savrvvapi pasariyaṁ tattha । maṁtitilaēṇa saddhiṁ rāyā majjhēṇa rannassa || 9 ||
jā gacchai tā picchai ēka hariṇaṁ sudīhadaḍhasiṁgaṁ । ārōviūṇa cāvaṁ haṇihī taṁ jāva bāṇēṇa ॥ 10 ॥
tā hariṇō bhai imaṁ jujjai khattassa tujjha kiṁ ēyaṁ । vasaṇāsattō muṁcasi maha jaṁ ēvaṁ tumaṁ vāṇaṁ ? |
nō khattasa atthaṁ pariyāṇasi jaṁ khayāu tāyaṁti । sayalaṁpi jaṇaṁ taha khattiyā ya tē caiva vaccaṁti ॥ 12 ॥
jē ubhayakulavisuddhā khattiyakulakēuṇō mahāsattā । avahatthiyariussavi paharaṁti na, jē puṇō mūḍhā ||
vajjiyaavarāhāṇaṁ varāhahariṇāiyāṇa paharaṁtā । gayapaharaṇāṇa pāvā dūrē tē khattiyattassa ||14||
pākhaṇḍipraśaṁsā puṣṇāti pāpaṁ janayati saṁtāpam । yathā mantritilakamantriṇaḥ sarvathā tyajata tasmādētām ॥ 1 ॥
satpuruṣajanmabhūmiḥ satatapravartamāna varmasāmāgrē । vijayamiva suprasiddhaṁ vijayapuraṁ puravaraṁ, tatra ॥2॥
durvāravairivadhūhr̥dayadārudāvānalō nalō nāma । sajjabhujavajrapañjaranigaḍitaśrīśa rikō rājā ॥3॥
vanarājīva virājati yasya śarīrē sadāpi vararājñī । sacchāyā dantavanōpaśōbhitā saguṇa (śakuna ) sēvanīyā ॥4॥
gambhīramanōmahōdadhimahōllāsasakalaśaśimūrttiḥ । tasyāsti priyā saubhāgyamañjarī prēmakulabhavanam ||5||
kr̥taduṣṭa lōkavilayō janamanastōlaka : subuddhivaranilayaḥ । nāmnā mantritilakō mantrī nayatilakatarumalayaḥ ॥
niravadyakāryayathāvr̥ddhasthāpitasāmapramukhanītipathaḥ । sa ēva tasya rājyē kr̥tapramāṇaśca sarvatra || 7 ||
athānyadā kadācid rājā''khēṭakē saṁcalitaḥ । turagārūḍhō mantryapi prasthitaḥ saha narēndrēṇa ॥8॥
tau yāvad gatāvaraṇyē sainyaṁ sarvamapi prasr̥taṁ tatra । mantri tilakēna sārdhaṁ rājā madhyēnāraṇyasya ॥9॥
yāvad gacchati tāvatpaśyatyēkaṁ hariṇaṁ dīrghadr̥ḍhaśr̥ṅgam । ārōpya cāpaṁ haniṣyati taṁ yāvad bāṇēna ॥ 10॥
tāvad hariṇō bhaṇatīdaṁ yujyatē kṣattrasya tava kimētat । vyasanāsaktō muñcasi mayi yadēvaṁ tvaṁ bāṇam ? ॥ 11 ॥
nō kṣattraśabdārtha parijānāsi yat kṣatāt trāyantē । sakalamapi janaṁ tathā kṣatriyāśca ta ēvōcyantē ॥12॥
ya ubhayakulaviśuddhāḥ kṣattriyakulakētavō mahāsattvāḥ । apahastitaripōrapi praharanti na yē punarmūḍhāḥ ॥ 13॥
varjitāparādhānāṁ varāhahariṇādikānāṁ praharantaḥ । gatapraharaṇānāṁ pāpā dūrē tē kṣatriyatvasya ॥14॥

cukā bhaṁḍārē kiṁ tuha aṁtēurē purē sivirē ? | gayasaraṇē haṇasi jahā tahēva dhī khattiyattaṁ tē ॥ 15 ॥
tathā cāha;
hariṇa caraṁti varṇatari hi avihiyaparasaṁtāva । tāhivi kaha bāhaṁti kara sajjaṇa ! saralasahāva ||16||
icāi nisuṇiūṇaṁ rāyāmaccaṁ bhaṇēi acchēraṁ । jaṁ pasuṇōvi hu jaṁpati nivbhayā māṇusagirāē || 17॥
maṁtitilaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ dēva ! imō dāṇavō va dēvō vā । kēṇāvi kāraṇēṇaṁ kayamigavēsō samōinō || 18 ||
tā gaccha turiya turiyaṁ turayaṁ mā khaṁca muṁca mukalayaṁ । picchaha kiṁ kuṇai imōtti tō nivō taha samāyarai ॥
uccaccapayāhiṁ gaccha hariṇōvi piṭṭaō rāyā । tā jāva majjha bhāgē vaṇassa tā picchara tattha ॥ 20 ॥
uttattakaṇayavannaṁ palaṁvabāhuṁ sudaṁsaṇaṁ sōmaṁ । kaṁdaṣpaṁpi adappaṁ kuṇamāṇaṁ dēhasōhāē ||21||
muṇimēgaṁ ēgaṁ nirūddhavayaṇaṁ vimuktaṇucidvaṁ । nāsagganisiyadihiṁ jhāyaṁta kiṁpi paramatthaṁ ||22||
tā hariṇēṇa bhaṇiyā vaṁdaha bhō bhō imaṁ mahābhāgaṁ । muṇimavayariḍaṁ turiyaṁ turayāō tō nivāmaccā ॥ 23॥
vaṁdati bhattimaṁtā sōvi hu tēsiṁ payacchai atucchaṁ । varadhammalābhavayaṇaṁ jagaṇaṁ sivasukkhalābhassa ||24||
vaviṭṭhā dharaṇīē jātē tō tattha sinnamaṇupattaṁ । muṇiṇāvi samāraddhā tēsiṁ sadēsaṇā ēvaṁ ||25||
tathāhi;
--
jīvō aṇāipaikhaṇabajjhatudayaṁta kammasaṁtāṇō । paribhamai duhasayāvattaduggamē bhavasamudammi ||26||
tattha tasēyarajīvāṇa dukkhamuppāiūṇa narayammi । aṇuhava vivihasatyābhighāyasaṁjaṇiyaviyaṇāō।।27॥
tiriyattaṇēvi vāhaṇaḍahaṇaṁkaṇakannakappaṇāīṇi । aṇuhavai vivihadukkhāī khuṣpivāsāparistō ||28||
|
kiṁ bhraṣṭā bhāṇḍāgārē kiṁ tavāntaḥpurē purē śibirē ? । gataśaraṇān haṁsi yathā tathaiva dhik kṣatriyatvaṁ tē ॥ 15 ॥
hariṇāścaranti vanāntarē hi avihitaparasaṁtāpāḥ । tathāpi kathaṁ bādhyantē kuru sajjana ! saralasvabhāvam ॥ 16॥
ityādi śrutvā rājāmartya bhaṇatyāścaryam । yat paśavō'pi khalu jalpanti nirbhayā manuṣyagirā ॥ 17 ॥
mantritilakēna bhaṇitaṁ dēva ! ayaṁ dānavō vā dēvō vā । kēnāpi kāraṇēna kr̥tamr̥gavēṣaḥ samavatīrṇaḥ ॥ 18 ॥
tasmād gaccha tvaritaṁ tvaritaṁ turaṁga mā karṣa muñca svatantram । paśya kiṁ karōtyayamiti tatō nr̥pastathā samācarati ॥
uccōccajhampābhirgacchati hariṇō'pi pr̥ṣṭhatō rājā । tāvadyāvanmadhyabhāgē vanasya tadā paśyati tatra ॥ 20 ॥
uttaptakanakavarṇē pralambabāhuṁ sudarśanaṁ sōmam । kandarpamapyadarpaṁ kurvāṇaṁ dēhaśōbhā ॥21॥
munimēkamēkāntē niruddhavacanaṁ vimuktatanutrēṣṭam । nāsāgranyastadr̥ṣṭiṁ dhyāyantaṁ kimapi paramārtham ||22||
tadā hariṇēna bhaṇitau vandēthāṁ bhō bhō imaṁ mahābhāgam । munimavatīrya tvaritaṁ turagāt tatō nr̥pāmātyaiau ||23||
vandētē bhaktimantau sō'pi khalu tayōḥ prayacchatyatuccham । varadharmalābhavacanaṁ jananaṁ śivasaukhyalābhasya ॥24॥
upaviṣṭau dharaṇyāṁ yāvattau tatastatra sainyamanuprāptam । munināpi samārabdhā tēṣāṁ sadēśanaivam ||25||
jīvō'nādipratikṣaṇabadhyamānōdayatkarmasaṁtānaḥ । paribhramati duḥkhaśatāvartadurgamē bhavasamudrē ||26||
tatra basētara jīvānāṁ duḥkhamutpādya narakē । anubhavati vividhaśastrābhighātajanitavēdanāḥ ॥ 27 ॥

māṇusammivi dāridavāhidō haggadukkha saṁtattō । visayāsānaḍiō aṇuvaladdhavisaō gamai kālaṁ ॥ 29 ॥
aha kavi lahai siē tassēvāē vivaḍhaē ahiyaṁ । visayahilāsō, tittī ya nēya, tēsiṁ asaṁpattī ॥30॥
hōi kayāi avassaṁ tō subharaṁtō nisēviē puvi । araīi tīi ghippaṛa jīi na nirdapi pāvē ||31||
dēvatva mahadviyaiṭīīsā duṇēi iyarēvi | abhiyōgiya kivvisiyā puṇa bhaṁḍaṁ caiva dukkhāṇa ||32||
tathā ca tē śōcanti :-
ēgaguruṇī sayāsē tavama cinaṁ maē imēṇāvi । haddhī ! majjha pāō phaliō ēyassa apamāō ||33||

tathā;-
dēvattaṇi tullēvi paru jaṁ āṇavai sarōsu । kiṁ kijjai tasu vairiyaha dhammapamāyaha dō ||34||
tiriyanarasurabhavēsuṁ visayāsēvāē jō suhābhāsō । sōvi apatthaṁ pacchā ditō gurudukkhadaṁdōli ||35||
ēvaṁ ca niraṁtara duhaparaṁparāparigayammi saṁsārē । jiṇadēsiē karatē bhaṇiyamaṇuha bhavakatē || 36 ||
bhai nivō ēvamiṇaṁ kiṁtu visēsēṇa kāraṇaṁ tumha । vēraggē jaṁ jāyaṁ taṁ sāhaha, tō muṇī kahai ||37||
asthi nagaraṁ pasiddhaṁ siddhapuraṁ nāma tattha naranāhō । nāmēṇa bhuvaṇasārō bhajjā tassatthi kaṇayasirī ||
atiabhihāṇō tassa atthi maisāgarōti varamaṁtī । dāhiṇadēsāō ahannayāgaō tattha samudāō ।।
gaṁdhavtriyaāujjiyanaccaṇimāīṇa tassa atthāṇē । paḍihāramūiō tēṇa kāuṁ pēkkhaṇayamāraddhaṁ ||40||
apuvyapēkkhakkhaṇahēḍaṁ kaṁcuimuhēṇa naranāhō । aṁtēurēṇa vinnāviō tayaṁ tēṇaṇunnāyaṁ ||41 ||
1
tiryaktvē'pi vāhanadahanāṅkanakarṇakartanādīni । anubhavati vividhaduḥkhāni kṣutpipāsāpariśrāntaḥ ॥ 28 ॥
mānuṣyē'pi dāridryavyādhidaurbhāgyaduḥkhasaṁtaptaḥ । viṣayāśānaṭitō'nupalabdhaviṣayō gamayati kālam ॥ 29 ॥
atha kathamapi labhatē viṣayāṁstatsēvayā vivardhatē'dhikam । viṣayābhilāṣaḥ, tr̥ptiśca naiva, tēṣāmasaṁprāptiḥ ॥30॥
bhavati kadācidavaśyaṁ tataḥ smaranniṣēvitān pūrvam । aratyā tayā gr̥hyatē yayā na nidrāmapi prāpnōti ॥31॥
।
dēvatvē'pi maharddhikaddhaya dunōtītarē'pi । abhiyōgika kilviṣikā : punarbhāṇḍamēva duḥkhānām ||32||
ēkagurōḥ sakāśē tapō'nucīrṇa mayā'nēnāpi । hā dhig ! mama pramādaḥ phalita ētasyāpramādaḥ ॥ 33॥
dēvatvē tulyē'pi parō yadājñāpayati sarōṣaḥ । kiṁ kriyatē tasya vairiṇō dharmapramādō dōṣaḥ ॥ 34 ॥
tiryagnarasurabhavēṣu viṣayāsēvāyāṁ yaḥ sukhābhāsaḥ । sō'pyapathyaṁ paścād dadad guruduḥ khadvandvālīm ||35||
ēvaṁ ca nirantaraduḥkhaparamparāparigatē saṁsārē । jinadēśitē kr̥tāntē bhaṇitamanutiṣṭhata bhavakr̥tāntē ॥ 36 ॥
bhaṇati nr̥pa ēvamidaṁ kintu viśēṣēṇa kāraṇaṁ yuṣmākam । vairāgyē yajjātaṁ tatkathayata, tatō muniḥ kathayati ॥
asti nagaraṁ prasiddhaṁ siddhapuraṁ nāma tatra naranāthaḥ । nāmnā bhuvanasārō bhāryā tasyāsti kanakaśrīḥ ॥ 38 ॥
avitathābhidhānastasyāsti matisāgara iti varamantrī । dakṣiṇadēśādathānyadā''gatastatra samudāyaḥ ||39||
gāndharvikātōdikanartanyādīnāṁ tasyāsthānē । pratihārasūcitastēna kartuṁ prēkṣaṇakamārabdham ||40||
apūrva prēkṣaṇēkṣaṇa hētōḥ kañcukimukhēna naranāthaḥ । antaḥ purēṇa vijñapitastat tēnānujñātam ॥41॥

tō javaṇiyachiḍēhiṁ picchai aṁtēuraṁpi picchaṇayaṁ । vāravilāsiṇisatyō atthāṇatyō puṇō niyaḥ ॥ 42 ॥
tathāhi, -

surasuṁdarisamarūvāhiṁ laḍahalīlāvilāsakaliyāhiṁ । nāṇāpagāralaṁkāraphārasiṁgārasārāhiṁ ॥ 43 ॥
kasiṇaghaṇakuṁtaluppīlaka liyadhammillakusumadāmāhiṁ । mayaṇādiparimaluggāragāravagghaviya sōhāhiṁ ॥ 44 ॥
mairāmayamaulāviyapahōlirāyaṁvalōyaṇillāhiṁ । aviralapayaṭṭaghaṇa sēyabiṁdudaṁturiyabhālāhi ||45 ||
vāraviyāhi rāyā saṁvādijjaṁtalaliyakamakamalō । vīijjatō avarāhi naravarō cāmarakarāhiṁ ॥ 46 ॥
safar atthāṇē jā cihna pēkkhaṇammi akkhittō । tā sahasā paḍihārō samāgaō kuṇai vinnatti ॥
dēva ! duvārē cihna aganimittajāṇaō baḍuō । putthiyahatthō siyanivasaṇō ya pahudaṁsaṇā sā ॥ 48 ॥
kō ārasō mu, māsu ca tassa kō'vasarō । dēvāṇa dulhammivi atucchapicchaṇayachaṇakālē ? |
maisāgarasacivēṇaṁ tō vitta niyō imaṁ jhatti | dēva ! pasāyaṁ kāuṁ millāsu baṁbhaṇaṁ ēyaṁ ॥ 50 ॥
aganimittadharō dharāē nahu kōvidīsaē pāyē । pēcchaṇayaṁ puṇa dīsai diṇē diṇē tuha pasāēṇa ॥ 51 ॥
tō bhaṇiyaṁ naravaiṇā muṁcasu paḍihāra ! vaṁbhaṇaṁ ēvaṁ | āēsōti bhaṇittā mukkō sō tēṇa pattō ya ॥
maṁtuccāraṇapuvvaṁ siyakkhaē matthaē narridassa । appē ubaviṭṭō uciyadvāṇammi sō bahuō || 53 ||
sūḍasamattīē taō ābhaṭṭō naravarēṇa sō ēvaṁ । sayakālaṁ tē kusalaṁ sō jaṁpara nāha ! nō kusalaṁ ॥ 54 ॥
mama tumhāṇaṁ annassa vāvi ihanayaravāsilōyassa | nāṇēṇa maē nāyaṁ aṁtamuhutaṁtarāparaō || 55||
1
tatō yavanikāchidraiḥ paśyatyantaḥ puramapi prēkṣaṇakam । vāravilāsinīsārtha āsthānasthaḥ punaḥ paśyati ॥42॥
surasundarī samarūpābhiḥ sundaralīlāvisāsakalitābhiḥ । nānāprakārālaṅkārasphāraśr̥ṅgārasārābhiḥ ॥43॥
kr̥ṣṇaghanakuntalasaṁghātakalitadhammillakusumadāmābhiḥ । mr̥ganābhiparimalōdgāra gaiauravapūrṇaśōbhābhiḥ ॥ 44 ॥
madirāmadamukulitapraghūrṇanaśīlātāmralōcanābhiḥ । aviralapravr̥ttavana svēdavindudanturitabhālābhiḥ ॥ 45 ॥
vāravanitābhī rājā saṁvāhya mānalalitakramakamalaḥ । vījyamānō'parābhirnaravaraścāmarakarābhiḥ ॥46॥
upaviṣṭa āsthānē yāvattiṣṭhati prēkṣaṇa ākṣiptaḥ । tāvatsahasā pratīhāraḥ samāgataḥ karōti vijñaptim ॥47॥
dēva ! dvārē tiṣṭhatyaṣṭāṅganimittajñāyakō baṭukaḥ । pustikāhastaḥ sitanivasanaśca prabhudarśanāśayā ॥ 48 ॥
ka ādēśō mucyatē, mā muñca vagdhi tasya kō'vasaraḥ । dēvānāṁ durlabhē'pyatuccha prēkṣaṇakakṣaṇakālē ? ॥ 49 ॥
matisāgarasacivēna tatō vijñaptō nr̥pa idaṁ jhaṭiti । dēva ! prasādaṁ kr̥tvā mōcaya brāhmaṇamētam ॥ 50 ॥
aṣṭāṅganimittadharō dharāyāṁ naiva kōpi dr̥śyatē prāyaḥ । prēkṣaṇakaṁ punardr̥śyatē dinē dinē tava prasādēna ॥ 51 ॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ narapatinā muñca pratihāra ! brāhmaṇamētam । ādēśa iti bhaṇitvā muktaḥ sa tēna prāptaśca ॥ 52॥
mantrōccāraṇapūrva sitākṣatān mastakē narēndrasya । arpayitvōpaviṣṭa ucitasthānē sa baṭukaḥ ॥53॥
prastāva samāptau tata ābhāṣitō naravarēṇa sa ēvam । sadākālaṁ tē kuśalaṁ sa jalpati nātha ! nō kuśalam ||14|
mama yuṣmākamanyasya vāpīha nagaravāsilōkasya । jñānēna mayā jñātamantarmuhūrtāntarāparataḥ ॥55 ॥

?
tō taṁ paṛa jaṁpēi puhaivaī garuyaṇakkhabharabhariō । kiṁ gayaṇaṁ nivaḍēhī gahacakajuyaṁpi iha nayarē ? ||56 ||
kiṁvā aigaruagiriṁ kōvi surō pāḍihī purassuvariṁ । palayānalasāricchō ahavā jalaṇō ihuṭṭhiī ! ||
ahaha ! asaṁbaddhapalāvirassa bahuyassa pēccha maha puraō । jīhāē caṁcalattaṁ tō maṁtī bhaṇai pasiūṇa ॥ 58 ॥
ēsō ci pucchijjara dēvākusalassa kāraṇaṁ kiṁpi । kimimēhiṁ aṇakkhēhiṁ viyappabahulēhi bhaṇiēhi ? ॥
tō bhai nivō bhaṇa bhadda ! kāraṇaṁ akusalē purajaṇassa । jaṁpara dēva ! suṇijjau maṇaṁ pasanna karēūṇaṁ ॥ 60 ॥
naravara ! varōvi divvaṁ dēvannū sakkaē na rakkhēḍaṁ । jaṁ bhāvi suhaṁ asuhaṁ taṁ ciya sō kahai aviyappaṁ । । 61 ॥
tā mā rusa majjha jahadiṭṭhē bhāvi parikahaṁtassa । iya bhaṇiuṁ dēvannū nibbhayacittō kahai ēvaṁ || 62॥
musalappamāṇaghaṇadhāradhōraṇīē dharāē taha kahavi । dhārādharō pabuddhiṁ kāhī dhīrāṇa ghuṇiyasi ॥ 63 ॥
akaliyaguruthalagattōrusāladēvaulamāladhavalaharaṁ । ēkajalaṁ ciya hōhī nayaraṁ gurunīranihisarisaṁ ॥ 64 ॥
isa tassa kahaṁtassavi parivattiya uttarō ṭhiō pavaṇō । kaccōlayamuhamēttaṁ samunnayaṁ mēhakhaṁḍaṁ ca ॥ 65 ॥
tō bhai vaṁbhaṇō bhō uttaraō niyaha abhayaṁ lōyā ! | pacchāissara ēvaṁ samaggagayaṇagaṇaṁ kamasō ॥ 66 ॥
tatō atthāṇatthō lōō savvōvi ṭhāi uḍḍhamuhō । uppaiuṁ pitra gayaṇē tavvayaṇassēva bhayabhīō || 67॥
jaha jaha paṇa pasarai taha taha pasarēi mēghakhaṁḍaṁpi । gayaṇagaṇaparisakaṇamahamahamigayāiva kuṇaṁti || 68 ॥
bhariyagirikaṁdarōdaradharaviivarō jhatti thaṇiyasadōvi | phōḍatō vaṁbharḍa ṭikaraḍiravōna vitthariō || 69॥
pasaraṁtataḍayaḍārāvabhariyabhuvaṇaṁtarā taḍidaṁḍī | surakuṁbhikuṁbhuvarisāyakuṁbha āharaṇa kiraṇavva ॥ 70 ॥
tatastaṁ prati jalpati pr̥thivīpatirgururōpabharabhr̥taḥ । kiṁ gaganaṁ nipatiṣyati grahacakrayutamapīha nagarē ? ॥ 56 ॥
kiṁvā'tigurugiriṁ kō'pi sura: pātayiṣyati purasyōpari । pralayānalasadr̥śō'thavā jvalana ihōtthāsyati ? ॥ 57 ॥
ahaha ! asaṁbaddhapralapiturbaṭukasya paśya mama purataḥ । jihvāyāścañcalatvaṁ tatō mantrī bhaṇati prasa || 58 ॥
ēṣa ēva pr̥cchayatāṁ dēvākuśalasya kāraṇaṁ kimapi । kimēbhī rōṣairvikalpabahulairbhaṇitaiḥ 1 ॥19॥
tatō bhaṇati nr̥pō bhaṇa bhadra ! kāraṇamakuśalē purajanasya | jalpati dēva ! śrūyatāṁ manaḥ prasannaṁ kr̥tvā ॥ 60॥
naravara ! varō'pi daivaṁ daivajñaḥ śaknōti na rakṣitum । yaddhāvi śubhamaśubhaṁ tadēva sa kathayatyavikalpam ॥ 61 ॥
tasmād mā ruṣya mama yathādr̥ṣṭaṁ bhāvi parikathayataḥ । iti bhaṇitvā daivajñō nirbhayacittaḥ kathayatyēvam ॥ 62॥
musalapramāṇavanadhārāghōraṇyā dharāyāṁ tathā kathamapi । dhārādharaḥ pravr̥ṣṭiṁ kariṣyati dhīrāṇāṁ dhūnitaśirāḥ ॥ 63 ॥
akalitagurusthalagataruśāladēvakulamālāghavalagr̥ham । ēkajalamēva bhaviṣyati nagaraṁ gurunīranidhisadr̥śam ॥ 64 ॥
iti tasmin kathayatyapi parivr̥ttyōttaraḥ sthitaḥ pavanaḥ । caṣakamukhamātraṁ samunnataṁ mēghakhaṇḍaṁ ca ॥65॥
tatō bhaṇati brāhmaṇō bhō uttarataḥ paśyatābhrakaṁ lōkāḥ ! । pracchādayiṣyatyētatsamagragaganāṅgaṇaṁ kramaśa: ॥ 66 ॥
tata āsthānasthō lōkaḥ sarvō'pi tiṣṭhatyūrdhvamukhaḥ । utpatitumiva gaganē tadvacana iva bhayabhītaḥ ॥67॥
yathā yathā pavanaḥ prasarati tathā tathā prasarati mēghakhaṇḍamapi । gaganāṅgaṇapariṣvaṣkaṇamahamahamikayēva kurvanti ॥
bhr̥tagirikandarōdaradharāvivarō jhaṭiti stanitaśabdō'pi । sphōṭayan brahmāṇḍaṁ dikkaradikha iva vistr̥taḥ ॥ 69 ॥

kiñca ।
supāsanāha cariammi
taḍidaṁḍāvara nivbharaṁvaraṁ takkhaṇē jayaṁ jāyē । palayānalajaḍilavilōlajālamālākavaliyaṁva ॥ 71 ॥
iya naravaipamuhajō jaṇiyacchariō khaṇaṁ nirikkhaṁtō । jā cihna tā laggō varisēuṁ musaladhārāhi ||
'tō takkhaṇēṇa taha kahavi pasariō pauranīrapurōvi । jaha bōliuṁ payaṭṭō palaē jalahivva naralōyaṁ ॥ 73॥
tō jāō purakhōhō khuhiō tā naravaīvi ciṁtēi । kimakālē saṁjāō ahaha ahō ! palayakālō'yaṁ ? |
ēvaṁ ciṁtaṁtassavi atthāṇasahā ēvi pāviyaṁ salilaṁ । uṭṭhēuṁ tō caḍiō sattamabhūmī mahināhō || 75 ॥
maisāyarēṇa sahiō baḍuēṇa ya tāva tattha puralōyaṁ । akaṁdabharakaṁtaṁ vilavaṁtaṁ nisuṇaē ēvaṁ || 76 ||
hā vaccha vaccha ! gacchasu pāṇē gahium̐ gurummi dēvaulē । mā maṁ paḍikkha nīraṁ upasarai palayajalahivva ॥
annā ya bhaṇai nārī vaccha ! tumaṁ sarasu jiṇanamukkāraṁ । āhāraṁ paccakkhasu sāgāraṁ aṇasaṇaṁ kāuṁ ॥ 78॥
iya karuṇaṁ vilavaṁta jaṇaṁ suṇēūṇa dukkhaō rāyā । jā ciṭṭhai tā nīraṁ sattamabhūmīē saṁpattaṁ ॥ 79 ॥
taṁ picchiuṁ nariṁdō pabhaṇai maṁtissa saṁmuhaṁ ēyaṁ । amhāṇa akayadhammāṇa āgayaṁ saṁpayaṁ maraṇaṁ ॥ 80 ॥
sukayaṁ na kayaṁ parihīṇamājyaṁ āvaī palōēḍaṁ । pāsāyasiṁgasaṁṭhiyaddhaunna maha dhuvvaē hiyayaṁ ॥ 81 ॥
visayāsattēṇa maē ittiyakālō muhāi gamiō jaṁ । na kaō jiṇidadhammō sāvayakulasaṁbhavēṇāvi ॥82॥
ēmēva gaō jammō asāra saṁsārakāraṇarayassa । paccāsanē maraṇē ahamihi kiṁ karissāmi ? || 83 ॥
hā hā ! ō for fha vihalamaṇuyattaṇaṁ gamatēṇa । niyapuvvapurisamērā bhaggā bhaggāsaēṇa maē ||84||
prasarattaṭataṭārāvabhr̥tabhuvanāntarastaḍiddaṇḍaḥ । surakumbhikumbhō pariśātakumbhābharaṇakiraṇa iva ॥ 70 ॥
taḍiddaṇḍāḍambaranirbharāmbaraṁ tatkṣaṇē jagajjātam । pralayāna lajaṭilīvalōlajvālāmālā kavalitamiva ॥ 71 ॥
iti narapatipramukhajanō janitāścaryaḥ kṣaṇaṁ nirīkṣamāṇaḥ । yāvattiṣṭhati tāvallagnō varṣituṁ musaladhārābhiḥ ॥72॥
tatastatkṣaṇēna tathā kathamapi prasr̥taḥ pracuranīrapūrō'pi । yathā'tikramituṁ pravr̥ttaḥ pralayē jaladhiriva naralōkam ॥
tatō jātaḥ purakṣōbhaḥ kṣubhitastasmānnarapatirapi cintayati । kimakālē saṁjātō'haha ahō ! pralayakālō'yam ? ॥
ēvaṁ cintayatō'pyāsthānasabhāyāmapi prāptaṁ salilam । utthāya tataścaṭitaḥ saptamabhūmyāṁ mahīnāthaḥ ॥75॥
matisāgarēṇa sahitō baṭukēna ca tāvattatra puralōkam । ākrandabharākrāntaṁ vilapantaṁ śr̥ṇōtyēvam ॥76॥
hā vatsa vatsa ! gaccha prāṇān gr̥hītvā gurau dēvakulē । mā māṁ pratīkṣasva nīramupasarati pralayajaladhiriva ॥77॥
anyā ca bhaṇati nārī vatsa ! laṁ smara jinanamaskāram । āhāraṁ pratyākhyāhi sākāramanaśanaṁ kr̥tvā ॥ 78 ॥
iti karuṇaṁ vilapantaṁ janaṁ śrutvā duḥkhitō rājā । yāvattiṣṭhati tāvannīraṁ saptamabhūmō saṁprāptam ॥79॥
tad dr̥ṣṭvā narēndraḥ prabhaṇati mantriṇaḥ saṁmukhamētat । asmākamakr̥tadharmaṇāmāgataṁ sāṁprataṁ maraṇam ||80||
sukr̥taṁ na kr̥taṁ parihīṇamāyurāpadaṁ pralōkya । prāsādaśr̥ṅgasaṁsthitadhvaja iva mama dhūyatē hr̥dayam ॥ 81 ॥
viṣayāsaktēna mayaitāvatkālō sudhā gamitō yat । na kr̥tō jinēndradharmaḥ śrāvakakulasaṁbhavēnāpi ॥82॥
ēvamēva gataṁ janmāsārasaṁsārakāraṇaratasya । pratyāsanē maraṇē'hamidānīṁ kiṁ kariṣyāmi ? ॥ 83॥

sāvajjarajjakajjē aṇajjamajjāyamāyaraṁtēṇa । hā ! savvasaṁgacāō na kaō visaēsa giddhē || 85 ||
kōḍī vaḍīyā vērulīyamaṇī ya kāyakhaṁḍēṇa । citāmaṇī uvalēṇaṁ kappatarū thōharēṇava ॥ 86 ॥
hā ! hāriō maē jaṁ dukkhasarūvāṇa dukkhahēūṇa । visayāṇa sēvāē gamiō jammō akayadhammō ॥ 87॥
kiṁ kuṇiyō ki sarimō kiṁ bhaṇimō saṁkaḍammi āvaḍiē ? | ia pabhaṇatassa tahiṁ nīraṁ pattaṁ suvēgēṇa ||
tā jā namōkāraṁ maṇammi citēi tāva vōhitthaṁ । abhimuharmitaṁ picchai ummiṭṭagayaṁva amassaṁ ॥89॥
sattamabhūmīē varaṁḍiyāē vēgēṇa taṁ samāvaḍiyaṁ । maisāgarēṇa tattō bhaṇiyaṁ āruhau iha dēvō ॥ 90 ॥
jaṁ dēvamimāu āīja nityāriḍaṁ surō kōvi । ēvaṁ ḍhōyai punnōdaēṇa paripēriō tumha ||11||
iya suṇiuṁ naranāhō āruhaṇatthaṁ mahatyavōhitthē । jā ukkhivēi caraṇaṁ varaṁḍiyāṭhaviyavāmapaō || 92 ॥
tāva na jalaṁ na mēṁhō naya bōhitthaṁ na vijjugajjīō । sutthāvatthaṁ tu paraṁ pāsa pamuiyamaṇaṁ lōyaṁ ॥ 93॥
katthavi saṁgīyaravaṁ katthavi pāraddhavivihakalaha । katthavi payaḍiyanahaṁ tō rāyā vihiō bhai || 94 ॥
kiṁ aṇaṇubhūyapucvaṁ ēvaṁ accanbhuyaṁ gaṇayapavara ! | sī bhaṇai ahaṁ niva ! iṁdajāliō na uṇa jōisiō ||
tattō vimyaparavasahiyaō rāyā suvannakōḍidugaṁ । vatthāī annapi hu dāviya bahuyaṁ visajjēi ॥ 96 ॥
maisāgarapamuhajaṇaṁ avarōhasamanniyaṁ bhavaviratō । bhāi nariṁdō dihaṁ viyaṁbhiyaṁ iṁdayālassa ? ॥97॥
dihaṁ savvaṁpi imaṁ tumha pasāēṇa tēvi jaṁpaṁti । aiaccabhuyamēyaṁ kēṇavi na kayāvidiṭṭhati ॥ 98 ॥
hā hā ! hatō'smīdānōṁ viphalamanujatvaṁ gamayatā । nijapūrvapuruṣamaryādā bhagnā bhagnāśayēna mayā ॥ 84 ॥
sāvadyarājyakāryē'nāryamaryādāmācaratā । hā ! sarvasaṅgatyāgō na kr̥tō viṣayēṣu gr̥ddhēna ॥ 85 ॥
kōṭirvarāṭikayā 'vaiḍūryamaṇiśca kācakhaṇḍēna | cintāmaṇirupalēna kalpataruḥ snuhyēva ॥ 76 ॥
hā ! hāritō mayā yad duḥkhasvarūpāṇāṁ duḥkhahētūnām । viṣayāṇāṁ sēvāyāṁ gamitaṁ janmākr̥tadharma ॥ 87 ॥
kiṁ kurmaḥ kiṁ sarāmaḥ kiṁ bhaṇāmaḥ saṁkaṭē āpatitē । iti prabhaṇatastatra nīraṁ prāptaṁ suvēgēna ॥ 88 ॥
tadā yāvannamaskāraṁ manasi cintayati tāvad yānapātram । abhimukhamāyat paśyatyunmr̥ṣṭagajamivāmanuṣyam ॥ 89 ॥
saptamabhūmērvaraṇḍikāyāṁ vēgēna tat samāpatitam । matisāgarēṇa tatō bhaṇitamārōhatviha dēvaḥ ॥90॥
yad dēvamasyā āpadō nistārayituṁ suraḥ kō'pi । ētākatē puṇyōdayēna pariprēritō yuṣmākam ॥ 91 ॥
iti śrutvā naranātha ārōhaṇārtha mahārthayānapātrē । yāvadutkṣipati caraṇaṁ varaṇḍikāsthāpitavāmapādaḥ ॥92॥
tāvanna jalaṁ na mēghō naca yānapātraṁ na vidyudgarjayaḥ । susthāvasthaṁ tu paraṁ paśyati pramuditamanasaṁ lōkam ॥ 93 ॥
kvāpi saṁgītaravaṁ kvāpi prārabdhavividhakalahaṭṭam । kvāpi prakaṭitanāṭyaṁ tatō rājā vismitō bhaṇati ॥ 94 ॥
kimananubhūtapūrvamētadatyadbhutaṁ gaṇakapravara ! । sa bhaṇatyahaṁ nr̥pa ! indrajālikō na punajyōtiṣikaḥ ॥ 95 ॥
tatō vismayaparavaśahr̥dayō rājā suvarṇakōṭidvikam । vastrādyanyadapi ca dāpayitvā baṭukaṁ visr̥jati ॥96॥
matisāgarapramukhajanamavarōdhasamanvitaṁ bhavaviraktaḥ । bhaṇati narēndrō dr̥ṣṭaṁ vijr̥mbhitamindrajālasya ? ॥97॥
dr̥ṣṭaṁ sarvamapīdaṁ tava prasādēna tē'pi jalpanti । atyadbhutamētatkēnāpi na kadāpi dr̥ṣṭamiti ॥ 98 ॥

tō bhai naravariṁdō jārisamimamidajālaviṣphuriyaṁ । tārisamiha saṁsārē savvaṁ bahudukkhabhaṁḍārē ॥ 99 ॥
rūvaṁ thāmaṁ pēmaṁ tārunnaṁ saṁpayā ya āuṁ ca । pavaṇapahalliradambhaggalaggajalabiṁdutaralataraṁ ॥ 100 ॥
tathāhi;
kuṭṭāivāhivihuriyana sānapa muhaaṁguraṁgāṇa | pajjunasamāṇavi rūvasaṁpayā hōī bībhacchā ॥ 101 ॥
vāhipivāsāchuha susiyaruhira maṁsāidhāusaṁtāṇā । māruatulabalāvi hu kaṭṭhēṇuṭuṁti ṭhāṇāō ॥ 102 ॥
pēmāṇavi bhajjāka siṭṭirahutilayasīyapabhiīṇa । kō na muṇai dāruṇapariṇaīṇa sōūṇa vittaṁtē ॥ 103 ॥
tārunnānaṁpi hu vivihavilāsullasaṁtasālilaṁ । ujjhai jaradavajālāvalīē vihalaṁ annāṇaṁ ॥ 104 ॥
kisalayadalaggasaṁlaggajalalabullāsa vilasirasirīē । kō vīsasai sirīē asaīēva dōsaparāē ? || 105 ||
aṇavaśyakamalasaṁvaraṇalaganālaggakaṁṭayavva sirī । katthaī payaṁ nivēsai na nivbharaṁ ajjavi khapi । 106 ।
saṁpannamūladaḍhadaṁḍakōsamaṁḍalaviyāsapauraṁpi । divasavasāṇē kamalaṁba muyai maṇusaraṁ lacchī ॥ 107 ॥
iya diyara muttī bahuvihasaṁkētiladdhavasarāē। ēyāra kō na taviō jayammi lacchīē sacchaṁda ? | 108 |
paisamayagalatē āyammi nirukamēvi thirabuddhī । jēsi tērsi vijjūē dukkarā nō thirattāsā ॥ 109 ॥
iya muṇiūṇa asāraṁ savvaṁ saṁsāravilasiyamiyāṇi । visayasuhābhāsē caṁcalampi kō haṁta ! paḍibaṁdhō ? ||
ittiyakāla mē muhāi gamiyā narāisāmaggī । puvvapurisāṇucinē saṁpai maggammi laggissaṁ ॥ 111 ॥
iya bhaṇiuṁ harivikamakumaraṁ rajjē ṭhavēvi suhalaggē । dāūṇa dhaṇaṁ dhammē jāō samaṇō sa ēsa ahaṁ ।। 112 ।।
tatō bhaṇati naravarēndrō thādr̥śamidamindrajāla visphuritam । tādr̥śamiha saṁsārē sarva bahuduḥ khabhāṇḍāgārē ||99 ॥
rūpaṁ sthāma prēma tāruṇyaṁ saṁpañcāyuśca । pavanapracaladarbhāgralagnajalabindutaralataram ॥100॥
kuṣṭhādivyādhividhuritanāsānakhapramukhāṅgōpāṅgānām । pradyumnasamānāmapi rūpasaṁpad bhavati bībhatsā ॥ 101 ॥
vyādhipipāsākṣucchuṣkarudhiramāṁsādidhātusaṁtānā । mārutatulyabalā api khalu kaṣṭēnōttiṣṭhanti sthānāt ॥102॥
prēmṇāmapi bhāryākāṣṭhaśrēṣṭharaghutilaka sītāprabhr̥tīnām । kō na jānāti dāruṇa pariṇatīnāṁ śrutvā vr̥ttāntān ? ॥
tāruṇyāraṇyamapi khalu vividhavilāsōllasacchālakam । dahyatē jarādavajvālāvalyā viphalamadhanyānām ॥ 104 ॥
kiśalayadalāgrasaṁlagna jalalavōllāsavilasitaśriyam । kō viśvasiti śriyamasatīmiva dōṣapracurām ॥ 105 ॥
anavaratakamala saṁvaraṇalagnanālāyakaṇṭhakēva śrīḥ । kvacitpadaṁ nivēśatē na nirbharamadyāpi kṣaṇamapi ॥ 106 ॥
saṁpannamūladr̥ḍhadaṇḍakōśamaṇḍalavikāsa pracuramapi । divasāvasānē kamalamiva muñcati manujēśvaraṁ lakṣmīḥ ॥ 107॥
iti dinakaramūva bahuvidhasaṁkrāntilabdhaprasarayā । ētayā kō na tāpitō jagati lakṣmyā svacchandam ? 108
pratisamayagalatyāyuṣi nirupakramē'pi sthirabuddhiḥ । yēṣāṁ tēṣāṁ vidyutō duṣkarā nō sthiratvāśā ॥ 109 ॥
iti jñātvā'sāraṁ sarvaṁ saṁsāravilasitamidānīm । viṣayasukhābhāsē cañcalē kō hanta ! pratibandhaḥ 1 ॥ 110 ॥
tasmādētāvatkālaṁ mayā mudhā gamitā narādisāmagrī । pūrvapuruṣānucīrṇē saṁprati mārgē lagiṣyāmi ॥ 111 ॥

niyaaṇuhūyaṁ javi hu sāhijjaṁtaṁ jaṇēi lahuyattaṁ । tumhārisē su naravara ! taṁ ciya guṇakāraṇaṁ hōi ॥ 113 ॥
tō kammiṁdhaṇa analēṇimiṇā cariēṇa nalanariṁdassa । ujjōiyāu jhīṇaṁ maṇāu annāṇasaṁtamasaṁ ॥ 114 ॥
tō bhai mahāsattāṇa vāha ! tumhārisāṇa turhati । nivalacchibaṁdhasaṁbaṁdhabaṁdhaṇāṇīha jai tahavi ॥ 115 ॥
ghaṇakammaniviḍabaṁdhaṇavaddhāṇaṁ vigayasuddhasaddhāṇaṁ । amhārisamuddhāṇaṁ dūrē saddhammabuddhīvi ॥ 116 ॥
dūratarēṇaṁ sugurūṇa saṁgamō kiṁtu nāha ! aigaruyaṁ । mannē samajjiyaṁ ciya punnaṁ pāvapi pugvabhavē ॥ 117 ॥
tē tuha pāyakamalaṁ kamalasaraṁ piva marummi paṇaēṇa । laddhaṁ migasāhijjā sakkēmi na sēviuṁ kīvō ॥ 118 ॥
uktaṁ caḥ-
"" mahadbhiḥ pāpātmā viralamapi saṅgaṁ na labhatē, viyōgaṁ prāpnōti kṣaṇamapi na taiḥ puṇyasahitaḥ ।
,
ataḥ kiñcit pāpaṁ sukr̥tamapi śaṅkē svaviṣayē bhavadbhiḥ saṁsargaḥ kathamatha kathaṁ caiṣa virahaḥ ? || "
ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē dhammassa jassa maha asthi jōggayā sāmi ! | tavvisaē āēsō maha dijjau tō muṇō āha ||
arahaṁtō ciya dēvō jīvāipayatthasatya saddahaṇaṁ । ahigayatattō ya gurū ii sammattaṁ payatē ॥ 120 ॥
jāvajjīvaṁ saṁkākakhāpāmukkhadōsaparimukaṁ । bhō naravara ! paripālasu jai sivasōkkhaṁ lahu mahasu || 121 ॥
tō maṁtiṇā samaṁ ciya paḍivannaṁ taṁ vihīē naravaiṇā । puṇaravi savisēsaṁ ciya pannaviē tassarūvammi || 122॥
bhai nivō maha kalāṇakulaharaṁ kō imō migō nāha ! | kahai gurū tuha mittaṁ putrabhavē māhaṇō āsi ॥
sō mariūṇaṁ jakkhō annāṇatavēṇimō sappannō । punvabhavabhāsāō pīī tuha daṁsaṇē jāyā || 124 ॥
bhagabhāvō jāō imassa maha daṁsaṇāō iha niccaṁ । kāūṇa hariṇarūṁ tō imiṇā vavasiyaṁ ēyaṁ ॥ 125॥
I
iti bhaṇitvā harivikramakumāraṁ rājyē sthāpayitvā śubhalagnē । dattvā dhanaṁ dharmē jātaḥ śramaṇaḥ sa ēṣō'ham ॥
nijānubhūtaṁ yadyapi khalu kathyamānaṁ janayati laghutvam । yuṣmādr̥śēṣu naravara ! tadēva guṇakāraṇaṁ bhavati ॥ 113॥
tataḥ karmēndhanānalēnānēna caritēna nalanarēndrasya । udyōtitāt kṣīṇaṁ manasō'jñānasaṁtamasam ॥ 114 ॥
tatō bhaṇati mahāsattvānāṁ nātha ! yuṣmādr̥śānāṁ truṭyanti । nr̥palakṣmībandhasaṁbandhabandhanānīha yadi tathāpi 119
ghanakarmanibiḍabandhanabaddhānāṁ vigataśuddhaśraddhānām । asmādr̥śamugdhānāṁ dūrē saddharmabuddhirapi ॥ 116 ॥
dūrataraṁ sugurūṇāṁ saṁgamaḥ kintu nātha ! atiguru । manyē samarjitamēva puṇyaṁ pāpamapi pūrvabhavē ॥117॥
tēna tava pādakamalaṁ kamalasara iva marau praṇayēna । labdhaṁ mr̥gasāhāyyācchaknōmi na sēvituṁ klībaḥ ॥ 118 ॥
ēvaṁ ca sthitē dharmasya yasya mamāsti yōgyatā svāmin ! | tadviṣaya ādēśō mama dīyatāṁ tatō munirāha ||
arhannēva dēvō jīvādipadārthasārthaśraddhānam । adhigatatattvaśca gururiti samyaktvaṁ prayatnēna ॥120॥
yāvajjīvaṁ śaṅkākāṅkṣāpramukhadōṣaparimuktam । bhō naravara ! paripālaya yadi śivasaukhyaṁ laghu kāḥ ॥ 121 ॥
tatō mantriṇā samamēva pratipannaṁ tad vidhinā narapatinā । punarapi saviśēṣamēva prajñāpitē tatsvarūpē ॥122॥
bhaṇati nr̥pō mama kalyāṇakulagr̥haṁ kō'yaṁ mr̥gō nātha ! । kathayati gurustava mittraṁ pūrvabhavē brāhmaṇa āsīt ॥
samr̥tvā yakṣō'jñānatapasā'yaṁ samutpannaḥ । pūrvabhavābhyāsāt prītistava darśanē jātā ॥ 124 ॥

tō jakkhō paccakkhō hōūṇaṁ bhaṇai muṇivaraṁ ēvaṁ । paḍivannaṁ sammattaṁ maēvi tuha pāyamūlammi || 126 ||
annaṁpi dhammavisayaṁ sikkhaṁ saṁpāviḍaṁ muṇisayāsē । namiūṇa niyaṭṭāṇē vaccai jakkhō nalanivōvi ॥ 127 ॥
aha rāyā jiṇapaḍimaṁ kārēḍaṁ pūyaē tikālaṁpi । jiṇapatrayaṇammi ucchappaṇāu kārē vivihāō ॥ 128 ॥
sakkārai sammāṇai sāhujaṇaṁ kuṇai taha ya tavvayaṇaṁ । taha sāhammiyalōyaṁ mannai baṁdhuṁva puttaṁva ॥ 129 ॥
maṁtīvi maṁtitilaō ēvaṁ ciya kuṇai jiṇamayaṁ dhammaṁ । nalanaravaiṇā sayayaṁ mannijjatō gamai kālaṁ ॥ 130 ॥
aha maṁtitilayamaṁtī kayāi bahuvāddivihuriyasarīrō । paccakkhāō vijjēhi ujjaō dhammamaggampi 131
parivāyagavēsadharēṇikkēṇaṁ taha kahām̐pa paḍiyariō । jaha jāō nīrōgō vahai taō pakkhavāyaṁ sē ॥ 132 ॥
bhōyṇavatthāīhiṁ uvayarai ya sō ya kahai niyadhammaṁ । appaḍikūlaṁtō dhuttāē jiṇadēsiyaṁ maggaṁ ॥ 133 ॥
aha vaḍḍhatē paṇaē nēi samaṁ bhappaṇā naravaissa । taṁ atthāṇē pucchara taō nariṁdō kamēti ? || 134 ||
sō bhai ērisō tārisī imō garuyaguṇagaṇagdhaviō । bhaṇai nariṁdō ēyappa saṁsaṇē malaya sē sammaṁ ||
havi huna pakkhavāyaṁ sō muyai paryapaē tahā ēyaṁ । saṁtaguṇakittaṇāō sampattē mayalā kaha ṇu ? ॥
iya ēvaṁ bahatē puiṭhāṇāō āgaō lēhō । naranāhacārapurisēhiṁ pēsiō rāyapa| sammi ॥ 137 ॥
iha nāha ! iō purisō parivāyagavēsadhāraō ēgō । vantrēṇa sāmavannō varuṇa paṇatīsavacchariō ॥ 138 ॥
vijjō taha vāyālō paṭṭhaviō tuhaghāyaṇanimittaṁ । nīlēṇa rāiṇā, taggahammi jattō vihēvva ॥ 139 ॥
bhadrakabhāvō jātō'sya mama darśanādiha nityam । kr̥tvā hariṇarūpaṁ tatō'nēna vyavasitamētat ॥ 125 ॥
tatō yakṣaḥ pratyakṣō bhūtvā bhaṇati munivaramēvam । pratipannaṁ samyaktvaṁ mayāpi tava pādamūlē || 126 ॥
anyāmapi dharmāviṣayāṁ śikṣāṁ saṁprāpya munisakāśē । natvā nijasthānē vrajati yakṣō nalanr̥pō'pi ॥ 127 ॥
atha rājā jinapratimāṁ kārayitvā pūjayati trikālamapi । jinapravacanē utsarpaṇāḥ kārayati vividhāḥ ॥ 128 ॥
satkārayati sammānayati sādhujanaṁ karōti tathā ca tadvacanam । tathā sādharmikalōkaṁ manyatē bandhumiva putramiva ॥
mantryapi mantritilaka ēvamēva karōti jinamataṁ dharmam । nalanarapatinā satataṁ mānyamānō gamayati kālam ॥ .
atha mantritilakamantrī kadācid bahuvyādhividhuritaśarīraḥ । pratyākhyātō vaidyairudyatō dharmamārgē ॥ 131 ॥
parivrājakavēṣadharaṇaikēna tathā kathamapi pratikr̥taḥ । yathā jātō nīrōgō vahati tataḥ pakṣapātaṁ tasya ॥ 132॥
bhōjanavastrādibhirupacarati ca sa ca kathayati nijadharmam । apratikūlayan dhūrttatayā jinadēśitaṁ mārgam ॥133॥
atha vardhamānē praṇayē nayati samamātmanā narapatim । tamāsthānē pr̥cchati tatō narēndraḥ kimētaditi : ।। 134 ॥
sa bhaṇatīdr̥śastādr̥śō'yaṁ guruguṇagaṇapūrṇaḥ । bhaṇati narēndra ētatpraśaṁsanē malinayasi samyaktvam ॥135॥
tathāpi khalu na pakṣapātaṁ sa muñcati prajalpati tathaitat । sadguṇakīrtanāt samyaktvē malinatā kathaṁ nu ? ॥ 136 ॥
ityēvaṁ vartamānē pr̥thivīsthānādāgatō lēkhaḥ । naranāthacārapuruṣaiḥ prēṣitō rājapārśvē ॥137॥
iha nātha ! itaḥ puruṣaḥ parivrājakavēṣadhāraka ēkaḥ । varṇēna śyāmavarṇō vayasā pañcatriṁśadvatsarikaḥ ॥ 138 ॥
vaidyastathā vācālaḥ prasthāpitastvadghātananimittam । nīlēna rājñā, tanahē yatnō vidhātavyaḥ ॥ 139 ॥

tō ēgaṁtē rāyā lēhāyariyaappiyaṁ tayaṁ lēhaṁ । vāēūṇaṁ sammaṁ phāḍēuṁ kuṇai khaṁḍāī ॥ 140 ॥
aha rāyāēsēṇaṁ atthāṇāō sa jāva mallēhi । vāhāō vāliūṇaṁ āḍhattō cārayaṁ nēuṁ ॥ 141 ॥
tā kaṁka lōhamayakattiyā taō nivaḍiyā dharaṇivaṭṭē । dihā jaṇēṇa rāyassa appiyā jhatti mallēhiṁ ||
tō bhai naravariṁdō kaṁ rē ! ēyaṁ, bhaṇēi sō tattō । jaṁ kiṁpi muṇai dēvō bhaṇai amaccaṁ taō rāyā ॥
maha atthāṇē āṇasi payaḍasi tullaṁ guṇēhiṁ sāhūṇaṁ । jiṇavayaṇabhāviyāṇaṁ ēvaṁ ēvaṁ durāyāraṁ ? || 144 ॥
kiśca ।
parapāsaṁḍipasaṁsaṁ jiṇapaḍikuddhaṁ tara kuṇatēṇa । niyasammattaṁ maha jīviyaṁ ca iha dōvi gamiyāī ॥ 145 ॥
iya bahuyaṁ taṁ nibrbhacchiūṇa sikkhākaē ya ēyassa । ṭhāvai annaṁ lēi ya savyastaṁ kiṁpi mōttr̥ṇa ॥ 146 ॥
tō citiu amaccō paḍikūlaṁtassa majjha jiṇavayaṇaṁ । yēvamiṇa, muṇipāsē tō paḍivajjittu pacchittaṁ ॥
paḍivajja gihidhamma pālai sammaṁ duvālasavirhapi । taṁ nāumappai nivō khamāviḍaṁ tassa savvassaṁ ॥ 148॥
ittōvi vāyagōvi hu nalarāyaṁ bhaṇai bhāvaō ihiṁ । paḍivannō jiṇadikkhaṁ jaṁ juttaṁ hōi taṁ kuṇasu ॥
bhāi nariṁdō mallē bāhujyaṁ sajjiḍaṁ muyaha ēyaṁ । bhāi maraṁtō ēvaṁ ēsō mukkī maē tahavi ।। 150 ।
aha ciṁta naranāhō sikkhaviyanvō sa tāva nīlanivō । jāyai bahujīvavahō sayaṁ ca taṁ viggahaṁtāṇaṁ ||
puvvi kathamigarūvaṁ tō taṁ jakkhaṁ maṇē karēūṇa । pōsahasālāra karēi aṭṭamaṁ sō taō jakkhō || 152 ॥
tadabhipāyaṁ nāuṁ nīlanivaṁ tassa daṁsaē baddhaṁ । bhaṇai ya ēsa sa nīlō jō ahimara pēsaō tujjha 153
tata ēkāntē rājā lēkhācāryārpitaṁ taṁ lēkham । vācayitvā samyak sphāṭayitvā karōti khaṇḍāni ॥ 140 ॥
atha rājādēśēnāsthānāt sa yāvanmallaiḥ । bāhū vālayitvā''rabdhaścārakaṁ nētum ॥ 141 ॥
tāvatkaṅkalōhamayakartarī tatō nipatitā dharaṇipaṭṭē । dr̥ṣṭā janēna rājñō'rpitā jhaṭiti mallaiḥ ॥142॥
tatō bhaṇati naravarēndraḥ kiṁ rē ! ētat, bhaṇati sa tataḥ । yatkimapi jānāti dēvō bhaṇatyamartya tatō rājā ॥
mamāsthānē ānayasi prakaṭayasi tulyaṁ guṇaiḥ sādhūnām । jinavacanabhāvitānāmēvamēṣa durācāraḥ ? || 144॥
parapākhaṇḍipraśaṁsāṁ jinapratikūlāṁ tvayā karvatā । nijasamyaktvaṁ mama jīvitaṁ cēha dvē api gamitē ॥ 145 ॥
iti
bahu taṁ nirbhartsya śikṣākr̥tē caitasya । sthāpayatyanyaṁ lāti ca sarvasvaṁ kimapi muktvā ॥ 146 ॥
tataścintayitvā'martyaḥ pratikūlayatō mama jinavacanam । stōkamidam munipārśvē tataḥ pratipadya prāyaścittam ॥
pratipadyatē gr̥hidharmaṁ pālayaṁti samyagdvādaśavidhamapi । tajjñātvā'rpayati nr̥paḥ kṣamayitvā tasya sarvasvam ॥148॥
itō'pi dhātakō'pi khalu nalarājaṁ bhaṇati bhāvata idānīm । pratipannō jinadīkṣāṁ yad yuktaṁ bhavati tatkuru ॥
bhaṇati narēndrō mallān bāhuyugaṁ sajjayityā muñcataitam । bhaṇati mriyamāṇa ēvamēṣa muktō mayā tathāpi ॥ 150 ॥
atha cintayati naranāthaḥ śikṣayitavyaḥ sa tāvannīlanr̥paḥ । jāyatē bahujīvavadhaḥ svayaṁ ca taṁ vigr̥hṇatām ॥ 151 ॥
pūrvaṁ kr̥tamr̥garūpaṁ tatastaṁ yakṣa manasi kr̥tvā । pauṣadhaśālāyāṁ karōtyaṣṭamaṁ sa tatō yakṣaḥ || 152 ॥
tadabhiprāyaṁ jñātvā nīlanr̥paṁ tasmai darśayati baddham । bhaṇati caiṣa sa nīlō yō'bhimaraprēpastava ॥ 153 ॥

tō bhai taṁ nariṁdō saṁpai kiṁ tujjha hōu, sō bhaṇai । diṭṭhammi tujjha payapaṁkayammi jaṁ hōi ta hōu ||
tō chōḍēḍaṁ baṁdhē sammāṇēūṇa bhaṇiya taṁ jakkhaṁ । saṭṭāṇē saṁpattaṁ suhēṇa kārai khaṇadvēṇa ।। 155॥
aha nikaṭayamēyaṁ rajjaṁ pālaṁtayassa naravaiṇō | sāhammiyasammāṇaṇaparassa jiṇadhammanirayassa ॥ 156 ॥
jōgattaṁ saṁpattaṁ puttaṁ rajjammi ṭhaviukāmassa । dikkhābhimuhassujjāṇapālaō vinnavai ēvaṁ ॥ 157 ॥৷
guṇarayaṇāyarasūrī samōsaḍhō dēva ! naṁdaṇujjāṇē । kayasajjaṇamaṇaharisō punnakarisōvva dēvarasa || 158 ॥
tassa kayapīīdāṇō'ṇugammamāṇō nariṁdarvidēhiṁ । gaṁtu vaṁdai vihiṇā rāyā sūriṁ saparivāraṁ ।। 159॥
kiṁ sōcciya saccainasēharō ēsa ii vicitatō । ālatō sūrīhiṁ kiṁ pariyāṇasi mahārāya ! ? ।। 160 ।।
tō nissaṁsayahiō sirakayakarakamalasaṁpuḍhō bhai | jaṇaṇī sacciya dhannā jīi pasūō tumaṁ sāmi ! ॥
laddhapasaraṁpi tahā bhuvaṇattayasuhaḍavinaḍaṇasahaṁpi । hēlāicciya bhaggaṁ jēṇa taē nāha ! mōhabalaṁ ।। 162 ||
aha mahayā saṁdēṇaṁ sūrī parikahai tīē parisāē । sāmaggīi imāē nibaṁdhaṇaṁ amha ēsa nivō || 163 ||
nivanīla pēsiō vāyagōtti kaliūṇa gāhiō rannā । paḍiyā ya kattiyā maha pāsāō tō maē bhaṇiya ।।
bhāvapaḍivanna jiṇamayadikkhō haṁ taṁ suyaṁ nariṁdēṇa । jāṇatēṇavi ēvaṁ palāvamittaṁ vimukō haṁ ।। 165 ॥
bhuvaṇacchērayasucariyaraṁjiahiyaēṇa taṁ tahēva maē । sugurūparyaṁtē vihiyaṁ hiyaṁ ca taṁ ēvamātrannaṁ ॥ 166 ॥
iya sōuṁ accanyavēraggarasāulāē parisāē । sūrīhi parikahiō aṇēgabhaṁgīhi jiṇadhammō ॥167॥
vāsiyacīrē suva māṇasēsu raṁgō tahā kahavi laggō । jaha pavvajjābhimuddō pāyaṁ jāō jaṇō savvō ।। 168॥
tatō bhaṇati taṁ narēndraḥ saṁprati kiṁ tava bhavatu, sa bhaṇati । dr̥ṣṭē tava pādapaṅkajē yadbhavati tadbhavatu ॥ 154॥ .
tatō mōcayitvā bandhān saṁmānya bhaṇitvā taṁ yakṣam । svasthānē saṁprāptaṁ sukhēna kārayati kṣaṇārdhēna ॥155॥
atha niṣkaṇṭakamētadrājyaṁ pālayatō narapatēḥ । sādharmika sammānanaparasya jinadharmaniratasya ॥ 156 ॥
yōgyatvaṁ saṁprāptaṁ putraṁ rājyē sthāpayitukāmasya । dīkṣābhimukhasyōdyānapālakō vijñapayatyēvam ॥197॥
guṇaratnākarasūriḥ samavasr̥tō dēva ! nandanōdyānē । kr̥tasajjanamanōharṣaḥ puṇyōtkarṣa iva dēvasya ॥ 158 ॥
tasmai kr̥taprītidānō'nugamyamānō narēndravr̥ndaiḥ । gatvā vandatē vidhinā rājā sūriṁ saparivāram ॥ 159 ॥
kiṁ sa ēva satyapratijñaśēkhara ēṣa iti vicintayan । ālaptaḥ sūribhiḥ kiṁ parijānāsi mahārāja ! ? ॥ 160 ॥
tatō niḥsaṁśayahr̥dayaḥ śiraḥ kr̥takarakamalasaṁpuṭō bhaṇati । jananī saiva dhanyā yayā prasūtastvaṁ svāmin! ॥ 169 ॥
labdhaprasaramapi tathā bhuvanatrayasubhaṭavinaṭanasahamapi । hēlayaiva bhagnaṁ yēna tvayā nātha ! mōhabalam || 162॥
atha mahatā śabdēna sūriḥ parikathayati tasyāṁ pariṣadi । sāmagryā asyā nibandhanamasmākamēṣa nr̥paḥ ॥ 163 ॥
nr̥panīlaprēṣitō ghātaka iti kalayitvā grāhitō rājñā । patitā ca kartarī mama pāśrvāttatō mayā bhaṇitam ॥ 164 ॥
bhāvapratipannajinamatadīkṣō'haṁ tat śrutaṁ narēndrēṇa । jānatāpyētat pralāpamātraṁ vimuktō'ham ॥ 165॥
bhuvanāścaryasucaritarañjita hr̥dayēna tattathaiva mayā । sugurupādāntē vihitaṁ hitaṁ ca tadēvamāpannam ॥ 166 ॥
iti śrutvā'tyadbhutavairāgyarasākulāyāṁ parṣadi । sūribhiḥ parikathitō'nēkamaṅgibhirjinadharmaḥ ॥ 167 ॥

vinnavai jahā suguru ! iya tuha cariēṇa dēsaṇāē ya । sajjō dhittumaṇāṇavi pavvajjaṁ asthi paḍivaṁdhō।।
buḍḍhāī pirāī kassavi annassa lahuyavaccāī | annassa vivabharaṇī avacacitāriṇī annō || 170॥
iya sōuṁ bhai nivō dhaṇēṇa saṁvahai jittiēṇaṁ jō । tammattaṁ tassa ahaṁ dēmi taō sō jaṇō bhaṇai ॥
vāḍhaṁ aṇuggahō ēsa amha, vinnavai surimaha rāyā । jaī dikkhājōggō haṁ bhavāmi pauṇō lahupitaō ।।
sūrī pabhaṇai dikkhāmaṇōrahaṁ suyabalēṇa tuha nāuṁ । ahamittha āgaō tā sijjhara maṇavaṁdviyaṁ tumha |
tō baṁdiūṇa sūriṁ rāyā pattō niyammi bhavaṇammi । ṭhāvara rajjē jōggaṁ kumaraṁ amaraṁ akāpi ॥ 174॥
pavvai umaṇaṁ ca jaṇaṁ paḍahayaugghōsaṇāē vāharijaṁ । dāūṇa kimavi daviṇaṁ annaṁ ahiṇavanariṁdāō ||
aṁgīkārēūṇaṁ tapparipālaṇarihāṇa savisēsaṁ । paripālaṇamakhilaṁpi hu taṁ dikhāē kuṇai pauṇaṁ ।। 176॥
tēhiṁ samaṁ taha aṁtēurēṇa annēhiṁ pavarapurisēhiṁ । paḍivannō pavvajjaṁ pālēḍaṁ taṁ ca aṇavajjaṁ ॥ 177॥
parivajjiya bhattāī saṭṭhi samahiḍiō samāhīē । savvaṭṭē saṁpattī ihēva bharahammi sijjhii || 178 ||
maṁtitilaōvi maṁtrī samaṁ nariṁdēṇa gahiyapavvajjō । upapannō sōhammē sijjhissai paṁcamammi bhavē ।। 179 ॥
॥ iti pākhaṇḍipraśaṁsāyāṁ mantritilakakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
vāsitacīvarēṣviva mānasēṣu raṅgastathā kathamapi lagnaḥ । yathā pratrajyābhimukhaḥ prāyō jātō janaḥ sarvaḥ ||
vijñapayati yathā sugurō ! iti tava caritēna dēśanayā ca । sadyō grahītumanasāmapi pravrajyāmasti pratibandhaḥ ॥
vr̥ddhau pitarau kasyāpyanyasya laghvapatyāni । anyasya vidhavabhaginī apatyacintaṇa anyaḥ ॥ 170 ॥
iti śrutvā bhaṇati nr̥pō dhanēna saṁvahati yāvatā yaḥ । tamātraṁ tasmā ahaṁ dadāmi tataḥ sa janō bhaṇati ॥
bāḍhamanugraha ēṣō'smāsu, vijñapayati sūrimatha rājā । yadi dīkṣāyōgyō'haṁ bhavāmi praguṇō ladhvapi tataḥ ॥ 172॥
sūriḥ prabhaṇati dīkṣāmanōrathaṁ śrutabalēna tava jñātvā । ahamatrāṁgatastasmāt sidhyatu manōvāñchitaṁ tava ॥ 173 ॥
tatō vanditvā sūriṁ rājā prāptō nijē bhavanē । sthāpayati rājyē yōgyaṁ kumāramamaramakāmamapi ॥174॥
pravrajitumanasaṁ ca janaṁ paṭahōddhōṣaṇayā''hūya । dattvā kimapi draviṇamanyadabhinavanarēndrāt ॥ 175॥
aṅgīkārya tatparipālanārhāṇāṁ saviśēṣam । paripālanamakhilamapi khalu taṁ dīkṣāyāṁ karōti praguṇam ॥ 176॥
taiḥ samaṁ tathā'ntaḥ purēṇa (nyaiḥ pravarapuruṣaiḥ । pratipannaḥ pravajyāṁ pālayitvā tāṁ cānavadyam ॥ 177॥
parivarjya bhaktāni ṣaṣṭiṁ samadhiṣṭhitaḥ samādhinā । sarvārthē saṁprāpta ihaiva bharatē sētsyati ॥ 178॥
mantritilakō'pi mantrī samaṁ narēndrēṇa gr̥hītapratrajyaḥ । utpannaḥ saudharmē sētsyati pañcamē bhavē ॥ 179॥
