citāmaṇī maṇīṇaṁ kappatarū taruvarāṇa jaha pavarō । taha sammattaṁ vr̥ttaṁ pavaraṁ savvāṇavi guṇāṇa ॥ 1 ॥
pakkhīṇa pakkhirāō surāṇa iṁdō gahāṇa jaha caṁdō । taha sammattaṁ pavaraṁ bhaṇiyaṁ savvāṇavi guṇāṇa ॥2॥
amayaṁ jahā rasāṇaṁ narāṇa cakkī muṇīṇa gaṇanāhō । taha daṁsaṇaṁ pasatthaṁ jāṇaha savvāṇavi guṇāṇa ॥ 3 ॥
jaṁ sammattavittā niravajjaṁ pāliūṇa jaikiriyē । gēvijjapi hu pattā puṇōvi bhumirā bhavamapāraṁ ॥4॥
narayāsu dukkhāī sarhati aidūsahāī iha jīvā । na ya tēsi sivagamaṇaṁ mōttuṁ sammatta saṁpatti ||5||
sammattaṁ puṇa pattā aṁtamuhuttaṁpi jaṁti mōkhammi | āsāyaṇavahulāvi hu avaḍḍhapariyamajjhampi || 6 ||
tō aiyāravimukaṁ dhannā pālaṁti kēi sammattaṁ । dhannāṇamavi dhannayarā jē taṁ jaṇayaṁti annēsiṁ ||7||
॥ samāptaṁ sāticāraṁ samyaktvadvāram ॥
cintāmaṇirmaṇīnāṁ kalpatarustaruvarāṇāṁ yathā pravaraḥ । tathā samyatvamuktaṁ pravaraṁ sarvēṣāmapi guṇānām ॥ 1 ॥
pakṣiṇāṁ pakṣirājaḥ surāṇāmindrō grahāṇāṁ yathā candraḥ । tathā samyaktvaṁ pravaraṁ bhaṇitaṁ sarvēṣāmapi guṇānām ॥2॥
amr̥taṁ yathā rasānāṁ narāṇāṁ cakrī munīnāṁ gaṇanāthaḥ । tathā darśanaṁ praśastaṁ jānīta sarvēṣāmapi guṇānām ||3||
yatsamyaktvaviyuktā niravadyaṁ pālayitvā yatikriyām । graivēyakamapi hi prāptāḥ punarapi bhramiṇō bhavē'pārē ||4||
narakādiṣu duḥkhāni sahantē'tidussahānīha jīvāḥ । na ca tēṣāṁ śivagamanaṁ muktvā samyaktvasaṁprāptim ||5||
samyaktvaṁ punaḥ prāptā antarmuhūrtamapi yānti mōkṣē । āśātanabahulā api hyapārdhaparivartamadhyē || 3 ||
'tatō'ticāravimuktaṁ dhanyāḥ pālayanti kēcitsamyaktvama । dhanyānāmapi dhanyatarā yē tajjanayantyanyēṣām ||7||

adhunā'ṇuvratādiparipālanātīcāraguṇadōṣān sadr̥ṣṭāntān spaṣṭaṁ niṣṭaṅkayannāha;
jāvajjīvaṁ jīvaṁ thūlaṁ saṁkappaō niravarahaṁ । maṇavaikāēhiṁ sayā na hōī nō haṇāvē ॥ 1 ॥
jō āraṁbha mōtuṁ, sō iha vijayacaṁda kumarōvva । aviulaṁ rajjasiriṁ lahiuṁ sivasaṁpayamuvē || 2 ||
tathāhi ;-
asthi iha bharahavāsē nayaraṁ nāmēṇa maṁgalapuraṁti । dharaṇivilayāē tilayaṁ maṁgalanilayaṁ nahayalaṁba ||3||
tatthasthi nivō riukaraḍikaraḍataḍa pāḍaṇikkasōḍīrō । sīhō iva jayasīhō cāīṁṇa sayā phusiyalīhō || 4 ||
tassatthi pavarabhajjā ruvēṇa raivva dhariyaguṇalajjā | sīlēṇa jaṇiyacōjjā pīimaī nāma mayavajjā ॥5॥
niyapahupaḍiyabhattī visālakittī visuddha maṇavittī । mainijjiyasuramaṁtī tassa ya maisāyarō maṁtī || 6 ||
pī mahāhiṁ bhajjāhiṁ samaniō visayasōkkhaṁ । aṇuhavara suravaī iva accharasāhiṁ saha samāvi ||7||
aha. annayā kayāī atthāṇagayassa tassa naranaiṇō । matthakayasiddhatyō putthiyahatthō suvīsatthō ||8||
gayaṇāō avayariō siyavasaṇadharō sarōyadalanayaṇō । purisō sasisamavayaṇō purō ṭhiō naṁ sayaṁ mayaṇō ||
tō rannā uṭṭhēuṁ āsaṇadāṇāiviṇayapaḍivattiṁ । kāūṇaṁ paripuṭṭhō kusalapatti bhai sōvi ॥ 10॥
kusalamalē mama naravara ! pasatyatityāṇa vaṁdaṇarayassa | saṁpaṛa jiṇidarvibē sammēē vaṁdiuṁ caliō ॥ 11 ॥
ōinō taṁ daddhuṁ sāhammiyapīiparavasō ēttha । pabhaṇai sāhasa kajjaṁ sajjō sāhēmi jēṇa tayaṁ ॥ 12 ॥
narapatiruvāca;
•
suyaṇāṇa daṁsaṇaṁ ci kallāṇaṁ jaṁ ihōyaraṁtēṇa । taṁ sāhiyamēva taē paōaṇēṇaṁ kimanēṇaṁ 1 ॥ 13 ॥
yāvajjīvaṁ jīvaṁ sthūlaṁ saṁkalpatō niraparādham । manōvacaḥ kāyaiḥ sadā na hanti nō ghātayati ॥ 1॥
ya ārambhaṁ muktvā sa iha vijayacandrakumāra iva । ativipulāṁ rājyaśriyaṁ labdhvā śivasaṁpadamupaiti ॥2॥
astīha bharatavarṣē nagaraṁ nāmnā maṅgalapuramiti । dharaṇivanitāyāstilakaṁ maṅgalanilayaṁ nabhastalamiva ॥ 3 ॥
tatrāsti nr̥pō ripukaraṭikaraṭataṭapāṭanaikaśauṇḍīraḥ । siṁha iva jayasiṁhastyāgināṁ sadā mr̥ṣṭarēkhaḥ || 4 ||
tasyāsti pravarabhāryā rūpēṇa ratiriva dhr̥taguṇalajjā । śīlēna janitāścaryā prītimatī nāma madavarjā ॥ 5 ॥
nijaprabhuprakaṭitabhaktirviśālakīrtirviśuddhamanōvr̥ttiḥ । matinirjitasuramantrī tasya ca matisāgarō mantrī ॥ 6 ॥
prītimatīpramukhābhirbhāryābhiḥ samanvitō viṣaya saukhyam । anubhavati surapatirivāpsarōbhiḥ saha sadāpi ॥ 7 ॥
athānyadā kadācidāsthānagatasya tasya narapatēḥ । sstakakr̥ta siddhārthaḥ pustikāhastaḥ suviśvastaḥ ||8|
gaganādavatīrṇaḥ sitavasanadharaḥ sarōjadalanayanaḥ । puruṣaḥ śaśisamavadanaḥ puraḥ sthitō nu svayaṁ madanaḥ || 9 ||
tatō rājñōtthāyāsanadānādivinayapratipattim । kr̥tvā paripr̥ṣṭaḥ kuśalapravr̥ttiṁ bhaṇati sō'pi ॥ 10 ॥
kuśalamalaṁ mama naravara ! praśastatarthānāṁ vandanaratasya । saṁprati jinēndrabimbāni sammētē vandituṁ calitaḥ ॥
avatīrṇastvāṁ dr̥ṣṭvā sādharmikaprītiparavaśō'tra । prabhaṇati kathaya kārya sadyaḥ sādhayāmi yēna tat ॥ 12 ॥
sujanānāṁ darśanamēva kalyāṇaṁ yadihāvataratā । tatsādhitamēva tvayā prayōjanēna kimanyēna ? || 13 ॥

supāsanāhacariyammi-
itthaṁtarammi maisāgarēṇa guruviṇayapucvayaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ । jai kulakumuyāṇaṁdō naravaṇō naṁdaṇī hōī || 14 ||
tō laṭhṭhē saṁjāyai sahalaṁ tuha daṁsapi amhāṇaṁ । tō bhaṇiyaṁ siddhēṇaṁ sijjhaṁtu maṇōrahā tumha ||15|
abhimaṁtiūṇa tē pr̥yaphalaṁ apiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ca । pīimaīē dijjasu jaha puttō hōi lahu tīē ||16||
salt jaṁpiṇaṁ uppaiō nahayalammi sō siddhō । dēvīē phala asiyaṁ jāō puttōvi samayammi || 17||
ddhāvaṇa bahuvityarēṇa kāūṇa vijayacaṁdōtti । māsammi gaē nāmaṁ paṭṭiyaṁ rāyabharaṇīhi || 18 ||
terraneharō va kalāsu dēhē ya uvacayaṁ lahai । tō sayalakalākusalō jāō 'thēvēhivi dihi ||
aha annayā turaṁgamāhaṇahēuṁ gaēṇa kumarēṇa । diṭṭō muṇī niviṭṭō tavatayaṁgō jiyāgaṁgō ||20|
nāmēṇaṁ muṇicaṁdō caunāṇī bhavigakumuyavaṇacaṁdō । namiūṇaṁ sō jaṁpara laddhāsīsō visēsē ||21||
dēvagurummatattaṁ kahēsu maha nāha! bahuyapunahiṁ । pattō tamiha mahāyasa ! marupahiēṇēva kamalasaraṁ ||22||
himahāra hasiyasiyadasaṇakiraṇarichōlivicchuriyavayaṇō । aha pabhaṇai sō sāhū rāyasuyaṁ suṇasu uvauttō. ॥
tadyathā;-
sōpasaru jasu vayaṇi ṇa vijjai, kāmiṇilaḍahakaḍakkhatikkhasatthihiṁ ju na bhijjai ।
juna karhipi kari karai kiṁpi paharaṇu raṇaraṁgau, jiṇi diṭṭhēṇavi galai pāu bhavasa saṁvari ||24||
sō tumha dēva jiṇavaru saraṇu bhavabhayadutthagalatthiyahaṁ, ājammu jammajaravajjiyau bīyarāja sivapatthiyahaṁ ।
jasu na gharaṇi maṇaharaṇi saraṇi niru nirayanivāsaha, jasu na khittu halamusalasatthu citavi gharavāsaha ||
'atrāntarē matisāgarēṇa guruvinayapūrvakaṁ bhaṇitam । yadi kulakumudānandō narapatērnandanō bhavati ॥ 14 ॥
tataḥ sundaraṁ saṁjāyatē saphalaṁ tava darśanamapyasmākam । tatō bhaṇitaṁ siddhēna sidhyantu manōrathā yuṣmākam ॥
abhimantrya tēna pūgaphalamarpayitvā bhaṇitaṁ ca । prītimatyai dīyatāṁ yathā putrō bhavati laghu tasyāḥ ॥ 16 ॥
ityādi jalpitvōtpatitō nabhastalē sa siddhaḥ । dēvyā phalamaśitaṁ jātaḥ putrō'pi samayē ॥17॥
vardhana bahuvistarēṇa kr̥tvā vijayacandra iti । māsē gatē nāma pratiṣṭhitaṁ rājabhaginībhiḥ ॥ 18 ॥
sitapakṣaśaśadhara iva kalāsu dēhē cōpacayaṁ labhatē । tataḥ sakalakalākuśalō jātaḥ stōkairapi dinaiḥ ॥ 19 ॥
athānyadā turaṅgamavāhanahētōrgatēna kumārēṇa । dr̥ṣṭō muniniviṣṭastapastanvaṅgō jitānaṅgaḥ ॥20॥
nāmnā municandraścaturjñānō bhavikakumudavanacandraḥ । natvā sa jalpati labdhāśīrviśēṣēṇa ॥ 21 ॥
dēvagurudharmatattvaṁ kathaya mama nātha ! bahupuṇyaiḥ । prāptastvamiha mahāyaśaḥ ! marūpathikēnēva kamalasaraḥ ||22||
himahārahasitasitadaśana kiraṇa paṅkivicchuritavadanaḥ । atha prabhaṇati sa sādhū rājasutaṁ śr̥ṇupayuktaḥ ॥23॥
duṣṭāṣṭādaśadōṣaprasarō yasya vacanē na vidyatē, kāminīramyakaṭākṣatakṣṇi śastrayōṁ na bhidyatē ।
yō na kvāpi karē karōti kimapi praharaṇaṁ raṇaraṅgitaḥ, yēna dr̥ṣṭēnāpi galati pāpaṁ bhavaśatasaṁvargitam ॥ 24 ॥
sa yuṣmākaṁ dēvō jinavaraḥ śaraṇaṁ bhavabhaya dauḥ syyanāśārthināmājanma janmajarāvarjitō vītarāgaḥ śivaprasthitānām ।
yasya na gr̥hiṇī manōharaṇī saraṇirniścitaṁ nirayanivāsasya, yasya na kṣētraṁ halamusalaśastraṁ cintāpi gr̥havāsasya ॥

vijayacaṁdakahā |

jasu na daviṇadhaṇakaṇasamiddhisaṁbaṁdhu samuddharu, ju navi jīvadayapamuhapavaru vaḍa khaṁḍai duddharu ।
samasanumittu chajjīvahi bhavasāgaraduttarataraṇu, sai vihivihāra karaṇujjamiḍa hōu suguru tumhaha saraṇu ||
jahiṁ sacarācarajīvarakkha aṇavaraya vihijjai, aliyakaliu jarhi kahivi navi ya vayaṇuvi jaṁpijjai ||
aft parakī adinnu tiguvi maṇasā na lijjai, jattha paratthīsatthu rayaṇibhōyaṇuvi caijjai ||27|
sō dhammurammu bhavabhayaharaṇu saraṇu asaraṇaha hōu tuhu ।
jiṇanāhaka hiu jayajīvahi sāsayasirivi ju dēi suhu ||28||
imāi muṇiṇa dhammō kahiō savittharō tattha । kumarēṇa paḍivannaṁ sammattaṁ taha imē niyamā ॥ 29 ॥
avarāhavajjiyāṇaṁ saṁppēṇaṁ tasāṇa pāṇavahaṁ । jāvajjīvaṁ maṁsaṁ paṁcuṁvarimāi vajjēmi ||30||
tya aṁgīkaniyamō niyagihapattō karēi jiṇadhammaṁ । aha annayāvahariō haraṇa vivarīyasikkhēṇa ॥ 31 ॥
triusisvīē paḍiō naḍiō taṇhāē kaṁḍagayapāṇō । parisaṁtaturayavayaṇāō jhatti avaṇēi jā kaviyaṁ ॥
tō sahasā sō kō pāṇēhiṁ dujjaṇōti kaliūṇa | mucchānimīlayacchō paḍiō kumarōvi dharaṇīē ||
jā ci tā diṭṭhō puliṁdamihuṇēṇa kiṁcisaccihō । sīyapavaṇēṇa jāō salilaṁ sannā patthitō ॥ 34 ॥
tattōya puliṁdī kuōvi himasisiranīramāṇēuṁ । sittō uṭṭhēūṇaṁ piyai jalaṁ tamalamamayaṁ ॥ 35 ॥
tattōya mahuṁ maṁsaṁ uvaṇīyaṁ tēhi bhōyaṇanimittaṁ । na ya bhakkhara kahavi tayaṁ kumarō paḍivananiyamadhurō ॥
mahuṁ maṁsaṁ mōttūrṇa phalakaṁdāī na vijjaē ittha । iya kahiēvi na asai tō tāī gayāī taṁ mōtuṁ ॥ 37॥
yasya na draviṇadhanakaṇasamr̥ddhisaṁbandhaḥ samudraḥ, yō nāpi jīvadayāpramukhapravaraṁ vrataṁ khaṇḍayati durdharam ।
samaśatrubhittraḥ ṣaḍjīvahitō dustarabhavasāgarataraṇaḥ sadā vivivihāra karaṇōdyatō bhavatu sugururyuṣmākaṁ śaraṇam ||
yatra sacarācarajīvarakṣā'navarataṁ vidhīyatē, alīkakalitaṁ yatra kvāpi nāpi ca vacanamapi jalpyatē ।
yatra parakīya madattaṁ tr̥ṇamapiṁ manasā na lāyatē, yatra parastrīsātha rajanibhōjanamapi tyajyatē ॥ 27 ॥
sa dharmō ramyō bhavabhayaharaṇaḥ śaraṇamaśaraṇānāṁ bhavatuṁ yuṣmākam |
jinanātha kathitō jagajjīvahitaḥ śāśvataśriyamapi yō dadāti sukham ||28||
ityēvamādirmuninā dharmaḥ kathitaḥ savistarastatra । kumārēṇa pratipannaṁ samyaktvaṁ tathēmē niyamāḥ ||29||
aparādhavarjitānāṁ saṁkalpēna trasānāṁ prāṇavatram । yāvajjīvaṁ māṁsaṁ pañcōdumbarādi varjayāmi ||30||
• ityaṅgīkr̥taniyamō nijagr̥haprāptaḥ karōti jinadharmam । athānyadā'pahr̥tō hayēna viparītaśikṣēṇa ॥ 31 ॥
vikaṭāṭavyāṁ patitō naṭitastr̥ṣṇayā kaṇṭhagataprāṇaḥ । pariśrāntaturagavadanājjhaṭityapanayati yāvatkavikām ॥
tataḥ sahasā sa muktaḥ prāṇairdurjana iti kalayitvā । mūcchānimīlitākṣaḥ patitaḥ kumarō'pi dharaṇyām ॥33॥
yāvattiṣṭhati tāvad dr̥ṣṭa: pulindamithunēna kiñcitsacēṣṭaḥ । śītapavanēna jātaḥ salilaṁ saṁjñayā prārthayamānaḥ ||
tataśca pulindyā kutō'pi himaśiśiranīramānīya । sikta utthāya pibati jalaṁ tadalamamr̥tamiva ॥35॥
tataścaṁ madhu māṁsamupanītaṁ tābhyāṁ bhōjananimittam । na na bhakṣayati kathamapi tatkumāraḥ pratipannaniyamadhuryaḥ ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
tēsiṁ apattiyaṁtō chuhāē paripīḍiō arannasmi । sō bhamai nēya pāvai tahāvihaṁ mūlakaṁdāī ||38||
jaha taha kavi mayāṇaṁ maṁsāī migāiyāṇa sulahāī । labbhaṁti mahūṇi ya kiṁtu tēsu na maṇaṁpi sō kuṇai ||
jātā navamadivasē migayāgayagayapurē sanaravaiṇō । sinnaṁ pasariyamittō kumaraṁ picchē sō rāyā ॥ 40 ॥
taruchāyāēṁ nivi susihaṁ, sōvi taṁ nivaṁ nāuṁ । abhuṭṭiya paṇamēī rannā nāō jahā tisiō ॥ 41 ॥
pālikaravāu nīraṁ pāēuṁ pucchiō kaō ēttha । kumarōvi kahai savvaṁ rāyā tō appaē turayaṁ ॥ 42 ॥
niyaāsavārasahiyē pēsai jatthacchaē niyāvāsō । kayamajjaṇō ya bhuṁjai rāyaniōgēṇa sō tattha ॥ 43 ॥
tō bīyadi rāyā kumara āhēḍayatthamaḍavīē । turayārūḍhaṁ āuhapāṇi saha apaṇō nēi ||44 ||
caudisipasariyaniyaāsavāravārēṇa khēḍiḍaṁ khuḍiē । miyasasayasūyarāī garuyaragattāē khiviūṇa || 45॥
ēkadisā rāyā kumarō vīyāē ṭhāviō tēṇa । nīharamāṇē jīvē vidhai bāṇēhiṁ naranāhō ||46 ||
aha kumaradisāhutaṁ paṇō vaccataē niēūṇa । rāyā bhaṇai kumāraṁ haṇasu imē mā uhi || 47||
tō bhai vijayacaṁdō nāhaṁ jīvē haṇāmi gayadōsē । tumhaṁpi na juttamiṇaṁ nayasārapahuttajuttāṇa || 48 ॥
tō ciṁta naranāhō kāvi apuvvā imassimā bhaṇiī। tō taṁ pabhaṇai kiṁ taṁ na hōsi naṇu khattiyakumārō ? ||
sō bhai naravarēsara ! haṇaṁti jīvē viṇāvarāhaṁ jē । tē sōyariyapamuhā khattiyaputtati tumha mayā ||50 ॥
tō tassa vayaṇaviṇayāiēhi hiyayammi raṁjiō rāyā । taccittaparikkhatthaṁ visēsaō kuṇai ēvaṁti ॥ 51 ॥
I
madhu māṁsaṁ muktvā phalakandādi na vidyatē'tra । iti kathitē'pi nāśnāti tatastau gatau taṁ muktvā ॥ 37 ॥
tayōrasaṁghaṭitaḥ kṣudhā paripīḍitō'raṇyē । sa bhramati naiva prāpnōti tathāvidhaṁ mūlakandādi ||38||
yathā tathā kathamapi mr̥tānāṁ māṁsāni mr̥gādikānāṁ sulabhāni । labhyantē madhūni ca kintu tēṣu na manō'pi sa karōti ॥
yāvat tāvad navamadivasē mr̥gayāgatagajapurēśanarapatēḥ । sainyaṁ prasr̥tamitaḥ kumāraṁ paśyati sa rājā ॥40॥
I
tarucchāyāyāṁ niviṣṭaṁ śuṣkauṣṭhaṁ, sō'pi taṁ nr̥paṁ jñātvā । abhyutthāya praṇamati rājñā jñātō yathā tr̥ṣitaḥ ॥ 41 ॥
pālikaravāda nīraṁ pāyayitvā pr̥ṣṭaḥ kutō'tra । kumārō'pi kathayati sarvē rājā tatō'rpayati turagam ॥ 42॥
nijāśvavārasahitaṁ prēṣayati yatrāstē nijāvāsaḥ । kr̥tamajjanaśca bhuṅgē rājaniyōgēna sa tatra ॥43॥
tatō dvitīyadinē rājā kumāramākhēṭakārthamaṭavyām । turagārūḍhamāyudhapāṇi sahātmanā nayati ॥ 44 ॥
caturdikprasr̥ta nijāśvavāravārēṇa khēṭayitvā tuḍitān । mr̥gaśaśaśūkarādīn gurutaragartē kṣiptvā ॥ 45 ॥
ēkadiśi rājā kumārōdvitīyasyāṁ sthāpitastēna । niḥsaratō jīvān vidhyati bāṇairnaranāthaḥ ॥ 46 ॥
atha kumāradigabhimukhaṁ paśūn vrajatō dr̥ṣṭvā । rājā bhaṇati kumāraṁ jahīmān mōpēkṣasva ||47||
tatō bhaṇati - vijayacandrō nāhaṁ hanmi gatadōṣān । yuṣmākamapi na yuktamidaṁ nayasāraprabhutvayuktānām ||48|
tataścintayati naranāthaḥ kāpyapūrvā'syēyaṁ bhaṇitiḥ । tatastaṁ prabhaṇati kiṁ tvaṁ na bhavasi nanu kṣatriyakumāraḥ ।
sa bhaṇati naravarēśvara ! ghnanti jīvān vināparādhaṁ yē । tē śaukarikapramukhāḥ kṣatriyaputrā iti yuṣmākaṁ matāḥ ॥
tatastasya vacanavinayādikairhr̥dayē rañjitō rājā । taccittaparīkṣārthaṁ viśēṣataḥ karōtyavāmīti ॥ 51 ॥

kiṁ ēttō lajjaṇayaṁ uttamapurisāṇa jīvalōgammi । jaṁ paharijjai dīṇē palāyamāṇē pattē vā ? ॥ 59 ॥

natthi
after sukkhu saṁsāra kiṁpi dadhamma payahi, paṁcaha divasaha rēsi rāya ! mēṁ māri yahi ||65 ||
iyaēvamāi amaō ēhiṁ vayaṇēhiṁ karuṇasārēhiṁ । avaḍaṁ mōhavisa nivōtri vihiō dayāhārō ॥66॥
saddhammavayaṇaviṇayāitōsiō naravaī vijayacaṁdaṁ । niyataṇayaṁ pitra khāmēumapaṇā dēi sappaṇayaṁ ||37||
niyapaṇaiṇī puttaṁ paramiṇināmāē paṭṭadēvīē । savvāṇaṁ pañcakakhaṁ juvarāyapayammi saṁṭhavai ||68 ||
bhāī pāraddhīē pāvasamiddhīra hōu maha niyamō । tuha kumara ! dhammabaṁdhava ! pabhāvaō paramakāruṇiya ! |
niyanayaraṁ saṁpattō kumāralaṁbhēṇa harisiō rāyā । kārāvara kārāmōyaṇāi vr̥ddhāvaṇayamaputraṁ ॥ 70 ॥
pihupāsāyavarḍasagamēgaṁ taha turayarahavarāīyaṁ । rāyā dēi kumārassa sōvi lihiūṇa vinnati ॥71॥
pēsara niyasavvasarūnagōyaraṁ turiyapurisapāsamma । niyavirahadutthiyāṇaṁ sutthatthaṁ jaṇaṇijaṇayāṇaṁ ॥72॥
aha annayā kayāvi hu pāsammi pariṭṭiē kumārampi । rayaṇīē addharatē rāyā nidāē vigamapi ॥ 73 ॥
nisuṇai karuṇayarasaraṁ nayaravahi itthiyāē, tō bhaṇai । suddhiṁ lahāviūṇaṁ kumāra ! maha kahasu lahu tattō ॥
āēsōtti bhaṇittā khaggasahāō viniggaō vāhi । laṁbittā pāyāraṁ vijjukkhittēṇa karaṇēṇa ॥ 75 ॥
tājā masāṇaṁ sarāṇusārēṇa vaccaī kuparō । pajjaliyajalaṇakuṁḍē khimāṇaṁ maṁsakhaṁḍāī || 76 ||
jōiyamēyaṁ pēcchai salakkhaṇitthīē ūrumaṁsāī । ukkattaṁtaṁ siyakattiyāē virasaṁ rasaṁtīē || 77 ||
arthō'sārō'sthirō bandhustanū rōgēṇa klāntā, āyāti jarārākṣasī durantā janmaiti tvaramāṇam ।
nāsti saukhyaṁ saṁsārē kimapi dayādharmē pravartasva pañca divasāni tiṣṭhasi rājan ! mā māriṁ pravartaya ॥ 65 ॥
ityēvamādyamr̥tōpamairvacanaiḥ karuṇāsāraiḥ | apanīya mōhaviṣaṁ nr̥pō'pi vihitō dayādhāraḥ ॥ 66 ॥
,
saddharmavacanavinayāditōṣitō narapatirvijayacandram । nijatanayamiva kṣamayitvā''tmanā dadāti sapraṇayam ॥67॥
nijapraṇayinyai putraṁ padminīnāmāyai paṭṭadēvyai । sarvēṣāṁ pratyakṣaṁ yuvarājapadē saṁsthāpayati ॥ 68 ॥
bhaṇati pāparddhēḥ pāpasamr̥ddhērbhavatu mama niyamaḥ । tava kumāra ! dharmabāndhava ! prabhāvataḥ paramakāruṇika ! ॥69॥
nijanagaraṁ saṁprāptaḥ kumāralābhēna harṣitō rājā । kārayati kārāmōcanādi vardhanakamapūrvam ॥70॥
pr̥thuprāsādāvataṁsakamēkaṁ tathā turagarathavarārādikam । rājā dadāti kumārāya sō'pi likhitvā vijñaptim ॥ 71 ॥
prēṣayati nijasarvasvarūpagōcarāṁ tvaritapuruṣapārśvē । nijavirahaduḥ sthitayōḥ sausthyārthaṁ jananījanakayōḥ ॥72॥
athānyadā kadāpi khalu pārśvē paristhitē kumārē । rajanyāmardharātrē rājā nidrāyā vigamē ||73 ||
śr̥ṇōti karuṇatarasvaraṁ nagarādvahiḥ striyāḥ, tatō bhaṇati । śuddhiṁ lambhayitvā kumāra ! mama kathaya laghu tataḥ ||
ādēśa iti bhaṇitvā khaḍgasahāyō vinirgatō bahiḥ । laṅghitvā prākāraṁ vidyatkṣiptēna karaṇēna ॥ 75 ॥
tatō yāvat śmaśānāntē svarānusārēṇa vrajati kumāraḥ । prajvalitajvalanakuṇḍē kṣipantaṁ māṁsakhaṇḍāni ॥ 76॥
yōginamēkaṁ paśyati salakṣaṇastriyā ūrumāṁsāni । utkr̥tantaṁ śitakartaryā virasaṁ rasandhyāḥ ||77 ||

tō karuṇārasarasiō kumarō pabhaṇē rē kimārō | caṁḍālāṇaviṇuciō ramaṇivahō liṁgiēṇāvi 1 ।। 78 ।।
aha bhīōvi huṁ pabhaṇaṛa mā vigdhaṁ kuṇasu suṇasu mahatrayaṇaṁ । varalakkhaṇadhara nārīnarāṇa ūrūṇa maṁsāṇa॥79॥
aōttarakhaṁḍasaēhiṁ maṁtapūēhi huyavahē huṇiē । sijjhēi cēḍayavarō siddhaṇṇāō maha sa inhi ॥ 80 ॥
jai puṇa jāyai vigghaṁ tō maṁ mārēi ēsa nirbhitaṁ । bhaṇai kumārō tahavi hu varāiyaṁ muṁca lahu ēyaṁ ॥ 81 ॥
niyaūrūṇaṁ kapiya jēṇa samappēmi maṁsakhaṁḍāī | tō sō tōsavasagaōbhaṇai imaṁ sāhu sāhasiya ! ॥82॥
tuha sarisāṇa alaṁbhē nigviṇamēyaṁ maē samāyariyaṁ । tā mukkacciya ēsā kuṇasu lahuṁ jaṁ taēbhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 83 ॥
aha sāhasikarasiō kumarō ūrūṇa maṁsakhaṁḍāī | karakēliyakatti ukkattiūṇa jōgissa appēi ॥ 84 ॥
tā jāva tassa siddhō ḍayarāyā bhaṇēi tō kumaraṁ । tuha sāhijjēṇaṁ ciya ēyassa vasaṁ ahaṁ pattō ॥ 85 ॥
tā tujjha ēsa cēḍō ahaṁ tu tuha cēḍayassa cēḍōtti | sumarēyavvō kajjē sāhasaghaṇadhaṇiya ! iya vōttuṁ ॥ 86 ॥
jāō sō assō jōīvi ha tavvaṇēsaṇēūṇa । saṁrōhaṇīēṁ gāruḍamaṁta dāu ca tasta gaō ॥87॥ !
hu
kumarōvi bālakaliō akhaliyalaliō taō samucaliō । pattō nivassa pāsē daṁsai kannaṁ, taō rannā ॥
puḍā kaha kumarēṇaṁ āṇīyā, kahai sā jahādihaṁ । tō kumaraṁ ārōviya aṁkammi sagagyaṁ bhaṇai ॥ 89 ॥
māṇikēhi uvalaṁ kaha ēyaṁ khilliyaṁ taē baccha ! | 'suddhiṁ lahāviūṇaṁ kahasu' tti paryapiravi maē ? ॥90॥
taṁ caiva majjha pāṇā taṁ saraṇabhimasta majjha lōyassa । nayaraṁ raṭuṁ ca imaṁ tuha kusalē kusalamubbahai ॥ 91 ॥
tataḥ karuṇārasarasitaḥ kumāraḥ prabhaṇati rē kimārabdhaḥ । cāṇḍālānāmapyanucitō ramaṇīvadhō laiṅgikēnāpi ? ॥

aṣṭōttaraśatakhaṇḍairmantrapūtai hutavahē hutē । sidhyati cēṭakavaraḥ siddhaprāyō mama sa idānīm ||80||
yadi punarjāyatē vighnastatō māṁ mārayatyēṣa nirbhrāntam । bhaṇati kumārastathāpi hi varākīṁ muñca laghvētām ॥ 81 ॥
nijōrvōḥ
: klr̥ptvā
yēna samarpayāmi māṁsakhaṇḍāni । tataḥ sa tōṣavaśagatō bhaṇatīdaṁ sādhu sāhasika ! ॥ 82 ॥
tava sadr̥śānāmalābhē nirghr̥ṇamētanmayā samācaritam । tasmānmuktaivaiṣā kuru laghu yattvayā bhaṇitam ॥ 83 ॥
atha sāhasaikarasikaḥ kumāra ūvōrmīsakhaṇḍāni । karaka litakartarīka utkr̥tya yōginē'rpayati ॥ 84॥
tāvadyāvattasya siddhaṭakarāja bhaṇati tataḥ kumāram । tava sāhāyyēnaivaitasya caśamahaṁ prāptaḥ || 85 ||
tasmāttavaiṣa cēṭō'haṁ tu tava cēṭasya cēṭa iti । smartavyaḥ kāryē sāhasaghanaghanika ! ityuktvā ॥ 86 ॥
jātaḥ sō'dr̥śyōyōgyapi khalu tadvraṇānapanīya | saṁrōhaṇyā gāruḍamantraṁ dattvā ca tasmai gataḥ ॥87॥
kumārō'pi bālākalitō'skhalita lalitastataḥ samuccalitaḥ । prāptō nr̥pasya pārśvē darśayati kanyāṁ tatō rājñā ॥
pr̥ṣṭā kathaṁ kumārēṇānītā, kathayati sā yathādr̥ṣṭam । tataḥ kumāramārōpyāṅkē sagadaṁ bhaṇati ॥ 89 ॥
māṇikyairupalaḥ kathamēṣa krītastvayā vara ! | 'śuddhiṁ lambhayitvā kathaya' iti prajalpitē'pi mayā ? ॥90॥
tvamēva mama prāṇāstvaṁ śaraṇamasya mama lōkasya । nagaraṁ rāṣṭraṁ cēdaṁ tava kuśalē kuśalamudvahati ॥91॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
na ya aṁgaṁgībhāvēṇa pariṇaē'nannasarisajiṇadhammē । juttaṁ maṇuyattaṁ sivasu hakkhamaṁ saṁsaē khiviṁu ॥ 92 ॥
ahavā juttājuttaṁ jāṇai vacchō tahāvi nō tumaē । iya kāyantraṁ maha patthaṇāē kaiyāvi, tō kumarō ॥ 93 ॥
kāūṇa aṁjali matyayammi jaṁpai pamāṇamāēsō । aha bhagai nivō kannē kā si tumaṁ kahaba basaṇamimaṁ ? ।। 94 ॥
sā nabhiḍaṁ bhaṇai ihaṁ kamalāyara sēṭṭhiṇō ahaṁ dhūyā | kamalasirī nāmēṇaṁ ramamāṇī uvavaṇastō ||95 ||
diṭṭhā tēṇa taō maṁ karēṁ gahēūṇa gayaṇamuppaiō | pattō masāṇamajjhaṁ vinnattamiō paraṁ putraṁ ॥ 96 ||
tuhadusahaviraha huyavahajālōlipalīviyāī hiyayāī । pātu nivvuī sidvisayaṇa galsa iva bhaṇiuṁ ॥ 97॥
nibhicabhicasahiyā viṇivēsiyamāṇasā kumārammi । tamittaṇaṁ kannā paṭṭaciyā piugihē rannā || 98 ॥
taṁdaṇaṁ sahasā rāhuni iṁduṇō vivaṁ । siṭṭimuhaṁ viṣphuriyaṁ sāyaramavagr̥hium̐ tattō ॥ 99 ॥

I
1
savisēsaṁ sammāṇiya tē nivabhicē bisajjaē siṭṭī | jaṇaṇīpamuhajaṇēṇavi harisēṇāliṁgiḍaṁ bhaṇiyā ||100॥
vacchē ! tuhavirahānalasaṁtattamaṇēhiṁ dīṇavayaṇēhiṁ । cajjāmāvi hu rayaṇī jāyasahassōbamā gamiyā ॥ 101 ॥
rōmaṁcaciyagattā paḍatī kumaraguṇagaṇukarisaṁ । savvaṁ taṁ vittaṁtaṁ paripuḍā siṭṭiṇō kahai ||102||
tō avagataccittataṁ siṭṭī bhāi tēṇa tu vacchē !। sakuṭuṁbapariyaṇassavi maha jīviyanivvisēsāē ||
rakkhaṁtēṇaṁ pāṇē jaṁ vihiyaṁ tassa natthi paḍiyārō । tō dāyavvāvassaṁ tassa tumaṁ hōu iya tāva || 104 ॥
rayaṇapaḍipuṇṇathālaṁ pabhayasamayammi ḍhōiuṁ tattō । siṭṭī kayappaṇāmō saṁthuṇai narēsaraṁ ēvaṁ ॥ 105 ॥
dhannō sō ēsa jaṇō supunnapuṁjōyba nāha ! jassa tumaṁ । duriyāva haraṇasaṁpayasaṁpāyaṇajaggirō sayayaṁ ॥ 106 ॥
na cāṅgāṅgībhāvēna pariṇatē'nanyasadr̥śajinadharmē । yuktaṁ manujatvaṁ śivasukhakṣamaṁ saṁśayē kṣēptum ॥ 92 ॥
athavā yuktāyuktaṁ jānāti vatsastathāpi nō tvayā । iti kartavyaṁ mama prārthanayā kadāpi tataḥ kumāraḥ ॥ 93 ॥
kr̥tvā'ñjaliṁ mastakē jalpati pramāṇamādēśaḥ । atha bhagati nr̥paḥ kanyāṁ kā'si tvaṁ kathaṁ vā vyasanamidam ? ॥ 94 ॥
sānatvā bhaṇatīha kamalākara śrēṣṭhinō'haṁ duhitā । kamalaśrīrnāmnā ramamāṇōpavanasyāntaḥ || 99||
dr̥ṣṭā tēna tatō māṁ karē gr̥hītvā gaganamutpatitaḥ । prāptaḥ śmaśānamadhyaṁ vijñapitamitaḥ paraṁ pūrvam ॥ 96 ॥
tvaduḥ saviraha hutavaha jvālālīpradīpitāni hr̥dayāni । prāpnuvantu nirvr̥tiṁ śrēṣṭhisvajana vargasyēti bhaṇitvā ॥
nirbhr̥tyabhr̥tyasahitā vinivēśitamānasā kumārē । tanumātrēṇa kanyā prasthāpitā pitr̥gr̥hē rājā ||28||
tāṁ dr̥ṣṭvā sahasā rāhuvimuktamivēndōrbimbam । śrēṣṭhimukhaṁ visphuritaṁ sādaramavagu tataḥ ॥ 99 ॥
saviśēṣaṁ sammānya tān nr̥pabhr̥tyān visr̥jati śrēṣṭhī । jananīpramukhajanēnāpi harṣēṇāliṅgaya bhaṇitā ॥ 100 ॥
vatsē ! tvadvirahānalasaṁtaptamanōbhidarnivadanaiḥ । caturyāmāpi khalu rajaniryāmasahasōpamā gamitā ॥ 101 ॥
rōmāñcāñcitagātrā prakaṭayantī kumāraguṇagaṇōtkarṣam । sarvaṁ taṁ vr̥ttāntaṁ paripr̥ṣṭā śrēṣṭhinaṁ kathayati ॥ 102 ॥
tatō'vagatataścittastāṁ śrēṣṭhī bhaṇati tēna tava datsē ! । sakuṭumba parijanasyāpi mama jīvitanirviśēṣāyāḥ ॥ 103 ॥
rakṣatā prāṇān yadvihitaṁ tasya nāsti pratikāraḥ । tatō dātavyā'vaśyaṁ tasmai tvaṁ bhavatviti tāvat ॥ 104 ॥
ratnaparipūrṇasthālaṁ prabhātasamayē ḍhaukitvā tataḥ । śrēṣṭhī kr̥tapraṇāmaḥ saṁstauti narēśvaramēvam ॥105॥

dhannāvinnatā hu |ta ēēṇa puttarayaṇēṇa । dēvāṇa ya maṇuyāṇaṁ ca cittacamakāracariēṇa || 107 ||
vinnaviyavvaṁ tu imaṁ tumaē niyadiṭṭigōyaraṁ pattā । majjha dayāē dhūyā maha gēhē pavēsiyā jhati ॥ 108 ॥
sā ya kumāraṁ kāū māṇasē tatthaṁ nāha ! saṁpattā | iya vipalaṁbhiyāē visaē kō tīi āēsō ? ॥
tō hasiuṁ bhaṇai nivō ēsā kumaravarōhagēhammi। jāvajjīvaṁ nivasau samapiyā suthiralaggami ॥ 110 ॥
bhaṇi mahāpasāyaṁ kayasammāṇō samuḍiō siddhī । aha annayā kumārō turaē vāhitaō vāhi ॥ 111 ॥
nisura akaṁdarakhaṁ bahunaranārīṇa tūraravamuhalē । vicchai ya sumuladugūlamalaya saṁchāiyaṁ itaṁ ॥ 112 ॥
jaṁpāṇaṁ, tō jaṁpara nāūṇaṁ tūrasaravisēsēṇa । ahidā kannēsā, kiṁ jīvati hissati ॥ 113 ॥
tō niyapurisa saṁpēsiūṇa kumarō kahāvara tāṇa | mā maḍayē ḍahaha imaṁ jā pauṁjāmi tamahaṁ ॥ 114||
tō amaṭṭitullaṁ ēyaṁ suṇiūṇa vimhiyā jāva । citi tāva kumarō turiyaṁ tassaṁtiyaṁ pattō ॥ 115 ॥
tattō gāruḍamaṁtēṇa salilamabhimaṁtiūṇa jahavihiṇā । sattaculuēhi pahayā sā uṭṭa amaya sittavva ॥ 116॥
daṭṭuṁ puraō kuparaṁ rūvēṇa suraṁva mayaṇasaraviddhā । kō ēsō kasmaō kiṁca imaṁ pucchiō tīē | | 117॥
taṁ caitra palōyaṁtī jā ciṭṭha aṇimisā taō maṁtī | nayasārī tīē piyā kumaraṁ pai japaē ēvaṁ ॥ 118 ॥
dhannā sā puṇṇukarisanimmiyā tihuyaṇēvi tuha jaṇaṇī । jīṛa pamūō si tumaṁ dīddharaṇikadulaliō ||
dhana kamalasirī jīsē'vatthaṁ imaṁ pavanāē । pāṇaparittāṇakara saraṇaṁ taṁ caiva saṁjāō || 120॥
dhanyaḥ sa ēṣa janaiḥ supuṇyapuñja iva nātha ! yasya tvam । duritāpaharaṇasaṁpatsaṁpādana jāgaritā satatam ॥ 106 ॥
dhanyānāmapi dhanyatamaḥ prabhō ! tvamētēna putraratnēna । dēvānāṁ ca manujānāṁ ca cittacamatkāracaritēna ॥ 107 ॥
vijñapayitavyaṁ tvidaṁ tvayā nijadr̥ṣṭigōcaraṁ prāptā । mayi dayayā duhitā mama gēhē pravēśitā jhaṭiti ॥ 108॥
sā ca kumāraṁ kr̥tvā mānasē tatra nātha ! saṁprāptā । iti vipralambhitāyā. viṣayē kastasyā ādēśa: ॥ 109॥
tatō hasitvā bhaṇati nr̥pa ēṣā kumārāvarōdhagēhē । yāvajjīvaṁ nivasatu samarpitā susthira lagnē ॥ 110॥
bhaṇitvā mahāprasādaṁ kr̥tasammānaḥ samutthitaḥ śrēṣṭhī । athāndā kumārasturagān vāhayan bahiḥ ॥ 111 ॥
śr̥ṇōtyākrandarakhaṁ bahunaranārīṇāṁ tūraravamukharam । paśyati ca sumūlya dukūlamallakasaṁcchāditamāyat ॥ 112 ॥
śavayānaṁ, tatō jāti jñātvā tūrasvaraviśēṣēṇa । ahidr̥ṣṭā kanyaivā, kiṁ jīvantīṁ vakṣyanti ? ॥ 113॥
tatō nijapuruṣaṁ saṁprēvya kumāraḥ kathāpayati tān । mā mr̥takaṁ dahatēdaṁ yāvatprayujē mantramaham ॥ 114॥
tatō'mr̥tavr̥ṣṭitulyamētat śrutvā vismitā yāvat । tiṣṭhanti tāvatkumārastvaritaṁ tasyāntikaṁ prāptaḥ ॥ 119॥
tatō gāruḍamantrēṇa salilamabhimantrya yathāvidhi । saptaculukaiḥ prahr̥tā sōttiṣṭhatyamr̥tasitēva ॥ 116 ॥
dr̥ṣṭvā purataḥ kumāraṁ rūpēṇa surabhiva madanaśaravidvā । ka ēṣa kasya sutaḥ kiñcidaṁ pr̥ṣṭastathā ॥ 117 ॥
tamēva pralōkamānā yāvatiṣṭhatyanimiṣā tatō mantrī | nayasārastasyāḥ pitā kumāraṁ prati jalpatyēvam ॥ 118 ॥
dhanyā sā puṇyōtkarvanirmitā tribhuvanē'pi tava jananī । yayā prasūtō'si tvaṁ dīnōddharaṇakadurlalitaḥ ॥ 119॥
dhanyatarā kamalaśrīryasyā avasthāmimāṁ prapannāyāḥ । prāṇaparitrāṇakr̥tē śaraṇaṁ tvamēva saṁjātaḥ ॥120॥

supāsanāha-yariammiṁ -
tō lajjōṇayavayaṇō maṁrti āpucchium̐ gaō kumarō । tēhi dhiya tūrēhiṁ vaddhāvaṇayapi vajrjatē ॥ 121 ॥
afe for art uvagijjētēsu maṁgalasaēsa । vaddhāvitēsu paikamaṁ tu annanalōē || 122 || -
savvāivi sāmaggīi tīē dhūyāē taha ya saṁjuttō । saṁpattō naravaimaṁdirammi nayasāramaṁtivarō ॥ 123 ॥
rāyā taṁ taha daṭṭhē jāva vikkē kiṁ kimēyati । paḍihārasaiō tō paṇamai maṁtī nivapayāī ॥ 124 ॥
uciyāsaṇē niviṭṭō ābhaṭṭhō naravarēṇa aha bhaṇai । rōmaṁcakaṁcuijjatasavvagattō puṇō namiuṁ ॥ 125 ॥
maraṇasabhā jaṁ kira natthi āvaī taṁpi tuha suputrēṇa । kayamannahā narēsara ! vayaṇaṁ aisayanihāṇēṇa ||
iya ukkhiviḍaṁ savvaṁ vittaṁtaṁ vittharēṇa taṁ kahiuṁ । vinnavai majjha dhūyā saṁpai kumārāu dūrammi || 127 ॥
ahilasai nēya ṭhāuṁ asarīrasarappahārabhayabhīyā । jaha tīē bhayaṁ na havai kuṇasu pasāyaṁ tahā sāmī ! ॥
rāyā taṁ paḍivajjiya sōhaṇalaggammi guruvibhūīē । kamalāvimalasirīṇaṁ pāṇī gāhāvaē kumaraṁ ।। 129 ॥
visayahamaṇubhavatō tō tāhi samaṁ gamēi diyahāī । jiṇadhammaṁ kuvrvatō dhuvvatō divaṁdēhaṁ ॥ 130॥
aha annayā nariṁdō āryakakaṁtaviggahō sahasā । taṁ ahisiṁca rajjē sayaṁ ca savvannubhaṇiēṇa ।। 131 ।
tēṇaṁ uvadvēṇaṁ paṁcanamōkkārasumaraṇāpuvviṁ । samabhāvabhāviyappā vihiṇā pāṇē paricaya || 132 ||
aha parā annadinē sīhaduvārammi uccasadēhiṁ । sāhulihatthā pukārayaṁti musiyamha musiyamha ।। 133 ।।
tō naravaṇā sōuṁ hakārēūṇa kāraṇaṁ puṭṭhā | sāhati adiṭṭhō kōvi takarō musai jagatē ||134 ||
tō tajjai nayarārakkhiyaṁ nivō sōvi bhaṇai pahu ! cōrō । diṭṭhīē gōyarē kōvi nēi kimahaṁ karēmi taō ? |
tatō lajjāvanatavadanō mantriṇamabhipr̥cchaya gataḥ kumāraḥ । tairava tūrairvardhana kē vādyamānē ॥ 121 ॥
"tairēva vadanairupagīyamānēṣu maṅgalaśatēṣu । vardhayatsu pratikramaṁ tvanyānyalōkēṣu ॥ 122॥
sarvayāpi sāmagryā tayā duhitrā tathā ca saṁyuktaḥ । saṁprāptō narapatimandirē nayasāramantrivaraḥ ॥ 123॥
rājā taṁ tathā dr̥ṣṭvā yāvad vitarkayati kiṁ kimētaditi । pratihārasūcitastataḥ praṇamati mantrī nr̥papādau ॥ 124 ॥
ucitāsanē niviṣṭa ābhāṣitō naravarēṇātha bhaṇati । rōmāñcakañcukāyamāna sarvagātraḥ punarnatvā ॥ 125 ॥
maraṇasamā yatkila nāstyāpat tadapi tava suputrēṇa । kr̥tamanyathā narēśvara ! vacanamatiśaya nidhānēna ॥ 126 ॥
ityutkṣipya sarva vr̥ttāntaṁ vistarēṇa taṁ kathayitvā । vijñapayati mama duhitā saṁprati kumārād dūrē || 127||
abhilaṣati naiva sthātumaśarīraśaraprahārabhayabhītā । yathā tasyā bhayaṁ na bhavati kuruṣva prasādaṁ tathā svāmin ! |
rājā tat pratipadya śōbhanalagnē guruvibhūtyā | kamalāvimalāśrayōḥ pāṇī grāhayati kumāram ||129 ॥
viṣayasukhamanubhavaṁstatastābhyāṁ samaṁ gamayati divasāni | jinadharmaṁ kurvan stūyamānō bandivr̥ndaiḥ ॥ 130 ॥
athānyadā narēndra ātaṅkākrāntavigrahaḥ sahasā । tamabhiṣiñcati rājyē svayaṁ sarvajñamaṇitēna ॥ 131 ॥
tēnōpadiṣṭēna pañcanamaskārasmaraṇapūrvam । samabhāvabhāvitātmā vidhinā prāṇān parityajati ॥132॥
atha paurā anyadinē siṁhadvārē uccaśabdaiḥ । vastrahastāḥ pūtkārayanti muṣitāḥ smō muṣitāḥ smaḥ || 133॥
tatō narapātanā śrutvā hakkārayitvā kāraṇaṁ pr̥ṣṭāḥ । kathayantyadr̥ṣṭaḥ kō'pi taskarō muṣṇāti jāgrataḥ ॥ 134 ॥

sō kōvi uvāō natthi dēva ! gahaṇē na tassa jō vihiō । bhaṇai nivā saṁpayamavi itthēva ahaṁ tamāṇēmi ॥
tō cēḍayāō takkhaṇamāṇāvēūṇa patthaō bāhaṁ । baddhaṁ daṁsai tēsi taṁ cōraṁ pucchara tahēyaṁ ॥137॥
kaha na musaṁtō dīsasisa bhai ōsōyaṇīē vijjāē । sōvāviūṇa lōyaṁ musēmi sicchāē gharasāraṁ ||
rāyā jaṁpara mōsaṁ ēsi appē, bhagai sō dēva ! । jēṇa ahaṁ āṇīō mōsaṁ savvaṁpi tēṇēva ॥ 139॥
jaṁ āsi maē hariyaṁ bhaṁḍāyārammi tumha taṁ ṭhatriyaṁ । āūṇa maē cciya saddhiṁ tattō ya āgaṁtuṁ ॥ 140 ॥
bhāṁḍāriō paivs suvannavatthāivatthusaṁghāō । bhaṁḍāgāraṁ tappaṁgaṇaṁ ca savvaṁpi pūraṁtō ॥ 141 ॥
sahasā dīsara, dēvō tattha pamāṇaṁ, taō nivō bhaṇai । vaṇiyāṇa appaha imaṁ tō bhaṇiyā tēvi niyaniyayaṁ ।।
gahiuṁ bhāṁti tihuyaṇaacchērayacariyahariyajayaduriya ! | amhaṁ punnōdayajīviēṇa taṁ jīva cirakālaṁ |
aha paṁcagapaṇāmaṁ kāūṇaṁ niggaēsu paurēsu । jaṁpara sō vijjāsiddhatakarō jōḍiuṁ hatthē || 144 ||
tuha pahu ! pasariyaubhaḍapayāvapavaṇēṇa akatūlaṁba । ukkhiviya ihāṇīō vivasō suhakammajōēṇa ॥ 145 ॥
dihaṁ ca sayalakallāṇakulaharaṁ tumha caraṇakamalajuyaṁ । ittō jaṁ maha jōgaṁ tēṇa pasāyaṁ kuṇau dēvō ॥ 146 ॥
rāyāvi bhai kallāṇakulaharaṁ hōsu ēsa āēsō । savvannubhāsiyāī suṇiūṇaṁ aṇuhiṇaṁ ca ॥ 147॥
bhai maha disasu tāī rāyā tō kahai duvihajiṇadhammaṁ । aha suyapuvvaṁ ēvaṁ majjha purā iya vicitaṁ tō ||
saṁjāyaja itaraṇa puvyabhavanmatthasariyasuttatthō । paḍivajjai pavvajjaṁ dēvayajavaṇīyamuṇiliṁgō || 149||
tatastarjayati nagarārakṣikaṁ nr̥paḥ sō'pi bhaṇati prabhō ! cauraḥ । dr̥ṣṭēgōṁcarē kō'pi naiti kimahaṁ karōmi tataḥ ||
sa kō'pyupāyō nāsti dēva ! grahaṇē na tasya yō vihitaḥ । bhaṇati nr̥paḥ sāṁpratamapyatraivāhaṁ tamānayāmi ॥ 136॥
tataścēṭakāt tatkṣaṇamānāyya prasthatō bāhau । baddhaṁ darśayati tēbhyastaṁ cauraṁ pr̥cchati tathaitat ॥ 137 ॥
kathaṁ na muṣṇan dr̥śyasē, sa bhaṇatyavasvāpanyā vidyayā । svāpayitvā lōkaṁ muṣṇāmi svēcchayā gr̥hasāram ॥138॥
rājā jalpati mōṣamēbhyō'rpaya, bhaṇati sa dēva ! । yēnāhamānītō mōṣaḥ sarvō'pi tēnaiva ॥139॥
ya āsīnmayā hr̥tō bhāṇḍāgārē tava sa sthāpitaḥ । ānīya mayaiva sārdhaṁ tataścāgatya ॥ 140 ॥
bhāṇḍāgārikaḥ prajalpati suvarṇavastrādivastusaṁvātaḥ । bhāṇḍāgāraṁ tatprāṅgaṇaṁ ca sarvamapi pūrayan ॥ 141 ॥
sahasā dr̥śyatē, dēvastatra pramāṇam, tatō nr̥pō bhaṇati । vaṇigbhyō'rpayēmaṁ tatō bhaṇitāstē'pi nijanijam ॥
gr̥hītvā maṇanti tribhuvanāścaryacaritahr̥tajagadurita ! | asmākaṁ puṇyōdayajīvitēna tvaṁ jīva cirakālam ॥
atha pañcāṅgapraṇāmaṁ kr̥tvā nirgatēṣu parēṣu । jalpati sa vidyāsiddhataskarō yōjayitvā hastau ॥ 144 ॥
tava prabhō ! prasr̥tōdbhaṭapratāpapavanēnārkatūlamiva । utkṣipyē hānītō vivaśaḥ śubhakarmayōgēṇa || 145 ।।
dr̥ṣṭaṁ.ca sakalakalyāṇakulagr̥haṁ tava caraṇakamalayugam । itō yad mama yōgyaṁ tēna prasādaṁ karōtu dēvaḥ ॥146॥
rājāpi bhaṇati kalyāṇakulagr̥haṁ bhavēṣa ādēśaḥ । sarvajñabhāṣitāni śrutvā'nuṣṭhāya ca ॥ 147॥
bhaṇati mē diśa tāni rājā tataḥ kathayati dvividhajinadharmam । atha śrutapūrvamētanmayā purēti vicintayan ||
saṁjātajātismaraṇaḥ pūrvabhavābhyastaspr̥tasūtrārthaḥ । pratipadyatē pravrajyāṁ dēvatōpanītamuniliṅgaḥ ॥ 149 ॥

supāsanāhacariyammi-
aha rāyā rōmaṁciyagattō siṁhāsaṇāu uṭṭhēuṁ । ti payāhiṇīkarēuṁ paṇamiya paramāra bhattīē ॥ 150 ॥
uciyāsaṇē nivēsiya pucchara kaha nāha ! tihuyaṇacchariyaṁ । iya pahuṇā āyariyaṁ, jāīsaraṇāu tō kahai ॥
āpucchiya naranāhaṁ vihariya abhujjaō gaō mōkkhaṁ । rāyā ya tattha dēsē pabhāvaē jiṇamayaṁ dhammaṁ ॥ 152 ॥
tathā;-
jasaṁmaddēṇa viṇā hōu vasē maha sacakaparacakaṁ । iya paribhāviya āisai cēḍayaṁ rāyavāḍīē || 153॥
ḍiṁḍīrapiṁḍapaṁḍurapuṁḍarīyaṁ taṁ dharēsu majjuvariṁ । gayaṇaṭṭiyadivyarūvō tēṇāvi kaē jahādiṭṭhē || 154 ||
tō cōravaiyarē taha imammi kahiyammi cārapurisēhi । sīmālā naravaiṇō savvē tē sēvamāvannā ॥ 155 ॥
itthaṁ savvattha samatthapatthivā matthaēṇa tahasāṇaṁ । sōūṇa tappabhāvaṁ dharaṁti dhīrāva viṇaṇa || 156॥
pasariyavayāvadusahō avasāriyadariyasattutamavisarō । vitthariyakamalakōsō hayadōsō sahai sō sūrō ।। 157॥
maṁgalauranayarāō samāgaō cauravayaṇaabhihāṇō । jayasīharāyapēsiyaduō aha annayā tassa || 158 ॥
atthāṇasabhāē saṁṭiyassa sirivijayacaṁdarāyassa । daṁsai rāyāēsaṁ paḍihārapavēsiō sōvi || 159॥
uṭṭhēūṇaṁ rāyā dōhivi hatthēhiṁ givhiūṇa tayaṁ । ārōviūṇa sīsē ṭhāviya siṁhāsa tattō ॥ 160 ॥
vimyiyiṇa samaṁ atthāṇagaēṇa savvalōēṇa | paṁcagaṁ paṇivāyaṁ kāuṁ ghittūṇa vāēi || 161 ॥
tadyathā; --
I
sirimaṁgalauranayarāō jayasīhanarāhivō suvikkhāō । sirihatthiṇauranayarē payāvaakaṁtanivacakaṁ ॥
sirivijayacaṁda nivaī sāyaramavagr̥hiuṁ paṇayasāraṁ । hiyayagayaṁ sambhāvaṁ sagaggayaṁ kiṁpi payaḍēi ॥ 163 ॥
atha rājā rōmāñcitagātraḥ siṁhāsanādutthāya । triḥ pradakṣiṇīkr̥tya praṇamya paramayā bhaktyā ॥ 150 ॥
ucitāsanē nivēśya pr̥cchati kathaṁ nātha ! tribhuvanāścaryam । iti prabhuṇācaritaṁ, jātismaraṇāttataḥ kathayati ॥
āpr̥cchyaṁ naranāthaṁ vihr̥tyābhyudyatō gatō mōkṣam । rājā ca tatra dēśē prabhāvayati jinamataṁ dharmam ॥ 152 ॥
janasaṁmardēna vinā bhavatu vaśaṁ mama svacakraparacakram । iti paribhāvyādiśati cēṭakaṁ rājavāṭyām ॥154॥
ḍiṇḍīra piṇḍapāṇḍurapuṇḍarakiṁ tvaṁ ghara mamōpari । gaganasthitādivyarūpastēnāpi kr̥tē yathādiṣṭē ॥ 154॥
tataścaiauravyatikarē tathā'sminkathitē cārapuruṣaiḥ । sīmasthā narapatayaḥ sarvē tē sēvāmāpannāḥ ॥ 155॥
itthaṁ sarvatra samarthapārthivā mastakēna tasyājñām । śrutvā tatprabhāvaṁ dharanti dhīrā api vinayēna ॥ 156 ॥
prasr̥tapratāpa dussahō'pasāritadr̥ptaśatrutamōvisaraḥ । vistr̥ta kamalā (la) kōśō hatadōṣō rājati saśū (sū ) raḥ ॥ 157॥
maṅgalapuranagarāt samāgataścaturavacanābhidhānaḥ । jayasiṁharājaprēṣitadūtō'thānyadā tasya ॥198॥
āsthānasabhāyāṁ saṁsthitasya śrīvijayacandrarājasya । darśayati rājādēśaṁ pratihārapravēśitaḥ sō'pi ॥। 159 ।
utthāya rājā dvābhyāmapi hastābhyāṁ gr̥hītvā tam । ārōpya śīrṣē sthāpayityā siṁhāsanē tataḥ ॥ 160 ।
vismita hr̥dayēna samamāsthānagatēna sarvalōkēna । pañcāṅgaṁ praṇipātaṁ kr̥tvā gr̥hītvā vācayati ॥ 169 ॥
śrīmaṅgalapuranagarājjayasiṁha narādhipaḥ suvikhyātaḥ । śrīhastināpuranagarē pratāpa kāntanr̥pacakram ॥ 162॥

vijayacaṁda kahā |
223
jāyaṁti āvayaṁ pāviuṁpi garuyā visālariddhillā | khīṇōvi hōi jalahī mahalahalaṁtakallōlō ॥164॥
āvaigayāvi garuyā hāsahāṇaṁ na hōṁti lōyassa । baṁdhapavannāvi gayā siriṁ gayā rāyabhavaṇēsu || 165 ||
visamaśvatthagaēṇavivaccha ! taē kiṁkarīkayasurēṇa । saccaviyamimaṁ savvaṁ rajjasiriṁ aṇuhavaṁtēṇa ॥ 166 ॥
kiṁtu suṇaṁtastavi tujjha rāyasiradhariyasāsaṇasamiddhiṁ । īsāiva savaṇāṇaṁ nayaṇāī naīti maha hiyayaṁ ॥ 167 ॥
kiñca ।
turayāvahārapuvvaṁ savvattha gavēsiōvi nō diṭṭhō । tō tuhavirahahuyāsō pajjaliō maha majjā ।। 168 ||
daḍḍhaṁ tēṇa taō taṁ suhapallaviyaṁ ghaṇāsakusumillaṁ । nimmalapunnaphalaṭaṁ vivēyavarabhūruhasamiddhaṁ ।। 169 ॥
kiñca ।
tujjha viōē niva! nivaipurajaṇō jaṇavaō jaṇaṇivaggō । jaṁ kahiuṁpi na tīrai duhamaṇuhavai ajjavi ya ।।
tuhavirahakāyarāē jaṇaṇīē nayaṇavāripūrēṇa । palamajalaō ayaṁḍē varisaviō dukkhataviyā ॥ 171 ॥
saṁpa puṇa āhī vāhī taha āhiā maha sarīrē । jaha taṁ cayaṁti pāṇā tā lahu daṁsēhi appāṁ ।। 172 ॥
iya lēhaṁ vāyaṁtō sagaggayaṁ lōyaṇaṁsakusumēhiṁ । jaṇayaniyahattha lihiyakkharēsu pūyaṁva nimvaī || 173॥
bhai ya kira jaṇayāī jāēhiṁ suēhiṁ huṁti suhiyāī । taṁ vivarīyaṁ jāyaṁ mai jāē majjha jaṇayāṇa ॥
tō nayasārappamuhaṁ maṁtijaṇaṁ pucchiūṇa sumuhuttē । vimalasirī puttaṁ sulōyaṇaṁ ṭhāviu rajjē || 175 ॥
rajjassa bāharī taha nayasāraṁ ṭhāvium̐ mahāmaṁti । saṁjhāē patthāṇē ṭhiō bahiṁ sōhaṇamuhuttē ॥ 176 ॥
!
śrīvijayacandranr̥patiṁ sādaramavaguhya praṇayasāram । hr̥dayagataṁ sadbhāvaṁ sagadaṁ kimapi prakaṭayati ॥ 163॥
jāyanta āpadaṁ prāpyāpi guravō viśālarddhayaḥ । kṣīṇō'pi bhavati jaladhiścalanmahākallōlaḥ ॥ 164 ॥
āpatā api guravō hāsyasthānaṁ na bhavanti lōkasya । bandhaprapannā api gajāḥ śriyaṁ gatā rājabhavanēṣu ॥
viṣamāvasthāgatēnāpi vatsa ! tvayā kiṅkarīkr̥tasurēṇa । satyāpitamidaṁ sarva rājyaśriyamanubhavatā ॥ 166॥
kintu śr̥ṇvatō'pi tava rājaśirōghr̥taśāsanasamr̥ddhim । īrṣyayēva śravaṇayōrnayanē nāṭayatō mama hr̥dayam || 167॥
turagāpahārapūrvaṁ sarvatra gavēṣitō'pi nō dr̥ṣṭaḥ । tatastvadvirahahutāśaḥ prajvalitō mama manaudyānē || 168॥
dagdhaṁ tēna tatastat sukhapallavitaṁ ghanāśākusumakam । nirmalapuṇyaphalāḍhyaṁ vivēkavara bhūruhasamr̥ddham ॥ 169 ॥
tava viyōgē nr̥pa ! nr̥patipurajanō janapadō jananīvargaḥ । yatkathayitumapi na śakyatē duḥkhamanubhavatyadyāpi ca ॥
tvadvirahakātarayā jananyā nayanavāripūrēṇa । pralayajaladō'kāṇḍē varṣitō duḥkhataptayā ॥ 171 ॥
saṁprati punarādhinā vyādhistathāhitō mama śarīrē । yathā tattyajanti prāṇāstasmāllaghu darśayātmānam ॥ 172॥
iti lēkhaṁ vācayan sagadgadaṁ lōcanāśrukusumaiḥ । janakanijahastalikhitākṣarēṣu pūjāmiva nirmāpayati ॥173॥
bhaṇati ca kila janakāni jātaiḥ sutairbhavanti sukhitāni । tadviparītaṁ jātaṁ mayi jātē mama janakayōḥ ॥ 174॥
tatō nayasārapramukhaṁ mantrijanaṁ pr̥ṣṭvā sumuhūrtē । vimalaśriyāḥ putraṁ sulōcanaṁ sthāpayitvā rājyē ॥ 175 ॥
rājyasya vāhakaṁ tathā nayasāraṁ sthāpayitvā mahāmantriṇam । saṁdhyāyāṁ prasthānē sthitō bahiḥ śōbhanamuhūrtē ॥

supāsanāha caritryasmi --
aṁtēurēṇa sahiō kaivayara haturayakarisaharusēhiṁ । saṁcaliō cālatō sallasahassāī lōyarasa || 177||
niyapatthāṇayavaiyaramāiṭṭhō naravarēṇa parikahai । tavvēlaṁ ciya jayasīhanivaiṇō cēḍaō gaṁtuṁ ॥ 178 ॥
taṁ sōuṁ sō sahasā mukō rōgēhi amayasittōvva । māi na aṁgē jaṇaṇīvi pariyaṇō jaṇavayajaṇōya ॥
saṁmāṇiūṇa tēṇaṁ visajjiō vijayacaṁdanaravaiṇō । taṁ sō sāhai tattō ya ūsuyattaṁ pariccaiuṁ ॥ 180 ॥
caisyapayaḍiyamaggō gāmāgaranagaraparimaṁḍiyaṁ vasuhaṁ । vōlatō sō vaccai ṭhāṇē ṭhāṇē paḍicchatō || 181 ॥
rāyāṇamuvāyaṇamaṇēgagaṇarāyarāyavivāī । ṭhāvaṁtō bhajatō dappamaṇagāṇa suhaḍāṇa ॥ 182॥
painagaraṁ paigāmaṁ pāyē jinamaṁdirāī pūryatō । jinnāi uddharaṁtō sammāṇaṁtō samaṇadhammē || 183 ||
nigrapiucauraṁga camūsaṁcārapavittabhūmibhāgāē । saṁpattō sīmāē kamēṇa dēmasta sō tattō ॥ 184 ॥
cēyamuṇa ēvaṁ jayasiṁhanarāhiba bhaṇāvēi । jaha kāūṇa pasāyaṁ maha paccōṇī na kāyavvā || 185 ॥
aikisadēhattāō maggasamēṇa puṇōvi bhavisu । rōganti taō tēci taṁ paḍivajjit naram ||186 ॥
sōhāfrist at sacivāu nāyarajaṇāṇaṁ । tēhivi niyamattīē pārō sō savitthaō || 187 ||
tathāhi;
1
ṭhāṇadvāṇanivēsiyasiyacāmaravatthakusumaramaṇīyaṁ । ramaṇīyarayaṇamālāviraiyavaravaṁḍurāmālaṁ ॥ 188 ॥
mālaṭṭālayagurusālamaṁcaārūḍhapōḍhara maṇijaṇaṁ । jaṇasaṁkularatthāmuhapurasuṁdarivihiyavaragēyaṁ ॥ 189 ॥
gēyāṇumagalagguggasubhaganaccaṁtanaccaṇī ōhaṁ । ōhā viyasurasuṁdarisuṁdaripārakalahaṅkaṁ ॥ 190॥
antaḥpurēṇa sahitaḥ katipayarathaturagakarisahasraiḥ । saṁcalitaścālayan śalyasahasrāṇi lōkasya || 177 ॥
nijaprasthānavyatikaramādiṣṭō naravarēṇa parikathayati । tadvēlamēva jayasiṁhanr̥patayē cēṭakō gatvā ॥ 178 ॥
tat śrutvā sa sahasā muktō rōgairamr̥tasikta iva । māti nāṅkē jamanyapi parijanō janapadajanaśca ॥ 179 ॥
sammānya tēna visr̥ṣṭō vijayacandranarapatayē । tat sa kathayati tataścōtsukatvaṁ parityajya ॥ 180 ॥
cēṭakaprakaṭitamārgōṁ grāmākaranagaraparimaṇḍitāṁ vasudhām । atikrāman sa vrajati sthānē sthānē pratīcchan ॥
rājādīnāmupāyanamanēkagaṇarājarāja vimbāni । sthāpayan bhañjan darpamanēkēṣāṁ subhaṭānām ॥182॥
pratinagaraṁ pratigrāmaṁ prāyō jinamandirāṇi pūjayan । jīrṇānyuddharan sammānayan śramaṇadharmiṇaḥ || 1832 ||
nijapitr̥caturaṅgacamūsaṁcāra pavitrabhūmibhāgāyām । saṁprāptaḥ sīmni kramēṇa dēśasya sa tataḥ ॥ 184 ॥
cēṭakamukhēnaitajjayasiṁha narādhipaṁ bhāṇayati । yathā kr̥tvā prasādaṁ mamābhigamanaṁ na kartavyam ॥ 185 ॥
atikr̥śadēhatvād mārgaśramēṇa punarapi prabhaviṣṇuḥ । rōga iti tatastēnāpi tatpratipadya nagarē || 186 ॥
haṭṭaśōbhādēśō dattaḥ sacivād nāgarajanānām । tairapi nijaśaktyā prārabdhaḥ sa savistaram ॥ 187॥
sthānasthānanivēśitasitacāmaravastra kusumaramaṇīyam । ramaṇīyaratnamālāviracitavaravandanamālam ॥ 188॥
mālāṭṭālakaguruśālamañcārūḍhaprauḍharamaṇījanam | janasaṁkularathyāmukhapurasundarīvihitavaragēyam ॥ 189॥
gēyā nu mārgalagnōgrasubhaganr̥tyannartanyōtram | adhaskr̥tasurasundarīka sundarīprārabdha kalahāsam ॥ 190 ॥

haṭṭagharadāraviraiyamuttāhalara ṇusatthiyapabaṁdhaṁ । baṁdhavahasuṁkaparimukkalōyaāsīsara muhalaṁ ॥। 191 ।।
iya para mūsavabhūyaṁ pavisiya nayaraṁ nivō vijayacaṁdō । jahasīhamahārāyaṁ paṇamai jaṇaṇipi sakalattō ॥ 192॥
niyatrirahataviyadēhaṁ harisaṁsujalēṇa nivvavatōvva । āliṁgiya nivasataṁ dharāē siṁhāsanē u || 193॥
anōnnamamaṁdāṇaṁdamaṁdirā jāva ṭhaṁti khaṇamēgaṁ । rōmaṁcaṁciyagattā tā samayanivēyaō paḍhāi || 194 ||
avagāhiūṇa jalahiṁ lahiuṁ udayāyalamma agmudayaṁ । viyasāviyakamalavaṇō sabbuvariṭiō ravī jaya ||
samayāṇugayaṁ vayaṇaṁ sarisaṁ nivavijaya kuṁdacariyassa । paḍhiyaṁti kaṇayalakkhaṁ dāvai baṁdissa naranāhō ||
ēttō ya sāvarahi vittaṁ jiṇaharēsu savrvvasu । ṇhavaṇabalipūyapabhiī niṣpannaṁ jaṁ jahā i ॥ 197॥
āsanē jiṇabhavaṇē dēvē vaṁdati dōvi naranāhā । bhaṁḍāriya bhaṇati ya avi aṭṭāhiyādivasē ॥ 198 ॥
maggati sāvayā jaṁ davvaṁ ghaṇasā raghusiṁṇamāīyaṁ । dāvaṁti ya jaṁ kiṁcivi tattha vilaṁba na kāyavvō । 199 ॥
samayamahōyahi sūrīṇa pāyakamalaṁ namasiuṁ iṁti । niyabhavaṇē bhuṁjati ya sapariyaṇā paramapīīē || 200 ||
aha patthā kahiō suyattatō nivassa puḍhēṇa । maighaṇasacivaṇa taō jayasiṁhanivō bhaṇai tanayaṁ ॥ 201 ॥
tai vaccha ! puhaipālaṇabharadharaṇadhuraṁdharammi niścitō । puvvapurisāṇucinnaṁ saṁpai maggaṁ pavajjāmi || 202 ॥
tō vijayacaṁdarāyā uḍaṁ jaṇayapāyavīdammi | viṇivēsiuttimaṁgō sagaggayaṁ bhaṇai pasiūṇa ॥ 203 ॥
risāī kavi nāyakamalarēṇūra majjha bhālayalaṁ । tāya ! pavittīkāūṁ uciyapi imaṁ vihēyavvaṁ ॥ 204॥
ēvamasaga paramavi puttaṁ saṁvōhiūṇa juttīhi । pīimaīē sahiō kaivayasāmaṁtatijuō ॥205॥
haṭṭagr̥hadvāraviracitamuktāphalarēṇusvastikaprabandham । bandhavadhaśulkaparimuktalōkāśīrabamukharam ॥191॥
iti paramōtsavabhūtaṁ praviśya nagaraṁ nr̥pō vijayacandraḥ । jayasiṁhamahārājaṁ praṇamati jananīmapi sakalatraḥ ॥192॥
nijaviraha taptadēhaṁ harṣāśrujalēna nirvāpayanniva । āliṅgya nivasantaṁ dharāyāṁ siṁhāsanē sthāpayati ॥ 193॥
anyōnyamamandānandamandirāṇi yāvattiṣṭhanti kṣaṇamēkam । rōmāñcāñcitagātrāstāvatsamayanivēdakaḥ paṭhati । । 194 ॥
avagāhya jaladhiṁ labdhvōdayācalē'bhyudayam । vikāsitakamala (lā) vanaḥ sarvasyōparisthitō ravirjayati ॥ 195॥
samayānugataṁ vacanaṁ sadr̥śaṁ nr̥pavijayacandracaritasya । paṭhitamiti kanakalakṣaṁ dāpayati bandinē naranāthaḥ ॥ 196॥
itaśca śrāvakairvijñāpitaṁ jinagr̥hēṣu sarvēṣu । snapanabalipūjāprabhr̥ti niṣpannaṁ yad yathēṣṭam ॥197॥
āsannē jinabhavanē dēvān vandētē dvāvapi naranāthau । bhāṇḍāgārikaṁ bhaṇataśca aṣṭāpyaṣṭāhikādivasān ॥ 198 ॥
mārgayanti śrāvakā yad dravyaṁ ghanasāraghusr̥ṇādikam । dāpayanti ca yat kiñcidapi tatra vilambō na kartavyaḥ ॥
samayamahōdadhisūrīṇāṁ pādakamalaṁ namastvitaḥ । nijabhavanē bhuñjatē ca saparijanau paramaprītyā |200||
atha prastāvē kathitaḥ sutavr̥ttāntō nr̥pāya pr̥ṣṭēna । matidhanasacivēna tatō jayasiṁhanr̥pō bhaṇati tanayam ॥ 209 ॥
tvayi vatsa ! pr̥thivīpālanabharadharaṇadhurandharē niścintaḥ । pūrvapuruṣānucīrṇa saṁprati mārga prapadyē ॥ 202 ॥
tatō vijayacandrarāja utthāya janakapādapīṭhē । vinivēśitōttamāṅgaḥ sagadgadaṁ bhaṇati prasadya ॥203॥
varṣāṇi katyapi nijapādakamalarēṇvā mama bhālatalam । tāta ! pavitrīkr̥tyōcitamapīdaṁ vidhātavyam ॥204॥

ucchapaṇāpurassaramaṇavajjāyariyā(mūlammi । giṇhavi dikkhaṁ vihiṇā naranāhīṁ mōkkhamaṇupattō ॥ 206॥
sirivijayacaṁdarāyā pathāu pālēi parabhanīīē । jiṇabhavaṇabhūsiya visayamappaṇō kuṇai savrvvapi ॥207॥
nēya maṁdēṇaṁ maraī kōī tiriō ahava maṇuō vā । sārīṇa caiva mārō daṁḍō chattāṇa tavvisaē || 208 ॥
ami caudasīē amāvasāē ya punimāēvi । giṇhēi pōsahaṁ sō paramaṁ vēraggamāvannō ॥ 209 ॥
taha kahavi karaṁ giṇhai jaha taṁ dinaṁ muṇaṁti na pacāō । sāvayajaṇaṁ tu savvaṁ akaraṁ ciya savvā kuṇai ||
kallāṇāidiṇēsuṁ savvatthavi sāvaēhiṁ jiṇabhavaṇē । jiṇamajjaṇaṁ kārai sayapi samayammi jāi tahiṁ ||
iya baccatē kālē kamalasirī pasavara puttaṁ । nāmēṇa vijayasēṇaṁ kalāpahiṁ sudhammiṭṭhē || 212 ||
aha annayā nariṁdō pāsāyasirammi kamalasirisaṁhiō । jā acchā tā pēcchā paccāsannammi pāsāē ||
vuḍḍhanaramihuṇamēgaṁ raikalahaparavva paḍiyadasaṇaṁ । accataṁ jaṁpataṁ nillajjaṁ sajjiyāgaṁga || 214 ||
kaṁpaṁtasavvagataṁ taṇusirabhūpaliyarōmacihuracayaṁ । avana miyapiṭṭadēsaṁ ghulaṁtamuhalāladupicchaṁ ॥ 215 ॥
taṁ daṁsiya bhai piyaṁ visayapivāsā na jāva amhēvi । ēvaṁ vinaḍai suṁdari ! tā muccau rucau tuhēyaṁ ॥
dēvī paṇa visayā sēvāē jarā kimēsimā ṇīyā । jaṁ dēvō iya jaṁpa, kaṁpai ēēṇa maha hiyayaṁ ॥ 227॥
kayasukayadukkayāṇaṁ ēvaṁ citra aṁtaraṁ maṇussāṇaṁ । visayāṇaṁ saṁpattī ēgēsiṁ nēya annēsiṁ ||218 ||
kiñca |
ēvamasaha paramapi putraṁ saṁbōdhya yuktibhiḥ । prītimatyā sahitaḥ katipayasāmantamantriyutaḥ ॥ 205 ॥
utsarpaṇā purassara manavadyācāryapādamūlē । gr̥hītvā dīkṣāṁ vidhinā naranāthō mōkṣamanuprāptaḥ ॥ 206 ॥
śrīvijayacandrarājaḥ prajāḥ pālayati paramanītyā | jinabhavanabhūṣitaṁ viṣayamātmanaḥ karōti sarvamapi ॥ 207 ||
na ca māndhēna mriyatē kō'pi tiryagathavā manujō vā । śārīṇāmēva mārō daṇḍaśchatrāṇāṁ tadviṣayē ॥ 208 ॥
aṣṭamyāṁ caturdaśyāmamāvāsyāṁ ca pūrṇimāyāmapi । gr̥hṇāti pauṣadhaṁ sa paramaṁ vairāgyamāpannaḥ ||209 ||
tathā kathamapi karaṁ gr̥hṇāti yathā taṁ dattaṁ jānanti na prajāḥ । śrāvakajanaṁ tu sarvamakaramēva sarvathā karōti ॥
kalyāṇādidinēṣu sarvatrāpi śrāvakairjinabhavanē । jinamajjanādi kārayati svayamapi samayē yāti tatra ॥ 299 ॥
iti jati kālē kamalaśrīḥ prasūtē putram । nāmnā vijayasēnaṁ kalāprakr̥ṣṭaṁ sudharmiṣṭham ॥ 212 ॥
athānyadā narēndraḥ prāsādaśirāsē kamalaśrī sahitaḥ । yāvadāstē tāvat paśyati pratyāsannē prāsādē ॥ 213 ॥
vr̥ddhanaramithunamēkaṁ ratikalahaparavaśaṁ patitadaśanam । atyantaṁ jalpannirlajjaṁ sajjitānaṅgam ॥214॥
kampamānasarvagātraṁ tanuḥśirōbhrūpalitarōmacihuracayam । avanatapr̥ṣṭhadēśaṁ ghūrṇamānamukhalālādurdarśam ॥ 215 ॥
taddarśayitvā bhaṇati priyāṁ viṣayapipāsā na yāvadasmānapi । ēvaṁ vināṭayati sundari ! tāvanmucyatāṁ rucyatāṁ tavaivata ||
dēvī prabhaṇati viṣayāsēvayā jarā kimanayōrānītā । yadēva iti jalpati, kampata ētēna mama hr̥dayam ॥ 217||

૨૭
savvēvi dukkhabhīrū savvēvi suhēsiṇō phuḍaṁ jīvā । tā ēyāvatthamayaṁ miṇamiṇaṁ iya payaṭṭataṁ । । 219॥
visayāsēvāē muhaṁ sāhai payaḍaṁ tahāvi nāhasta । kaha daṭṭumimaṁ jāyā visaēsu parammuhā buddhī ? || 220 ॥
narapatiruvāca
|
daṁsaṇanāṇamaṇataṁ viriyamaṇataṁ tahā suhamaṇataṁ । paramatthēṇa sarūvaṁ jīvāṇa imaṁ, tahāvi imē ॥ 222 ॥
visayapivāsāpāmā patthiyā iha bhavē aṇāimmi | saṁpāyaṇatthamēsi visayāṇa sahaṁti dukkhāī ॥ 222 ॥
jāyaṁti puṇa tahākima isē kayā ikassāvi | dālidaduhaṭṭāṇaṁ annēsiṁ jāi puṇa jammō ॥ 223 ॥
tēsi paribhōgē kaḍkaṁḍyantra suhalēsaṁ । bhuṁjatō vahu mannai visayapivāsaṁ payati ।। 224 ।।
aha kavi dhaṇābhāvē pagaṇivirahēṇa huṁti nō visayā । tō taccitāsalliyahiyaō dukkhaṁ gamai kālaṁ ।।
uktaṁ ca
"aprāptāḥ saṁkalpaiḥ prāptā darpēṇa cintayā virahē । varayanti jvarayanti kraśayanti prāṇinaṁ viṣayāḥ ॥ "
naya samai bisayata hā ciraṁpi saṁsēviētu visaēsu । aisayamaṇōharē suvi visēsaō baḍḍhaē giddhī || 226॥
uktaṁ ca;
--
"
" na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānāmupabhōgēna śāmyati । haviṣā kr̥ṣṇavamēva bhūya ēvābhivardhatē ॥
visayapivāsāya imā rāgō aṇukūlaēsu visaēsu । paḍikūlēsuṁ dōsō jīvāṇaṁ mōhavasayāṇaṁ ॥ 227॥
rāgadōsā ya puṇō kampasa nibaṁdhaṇaṁ dhuvaṁ huṁti । kammōdaēṇa jīvō pāvai dukkha bhavē ghōraṁ ||228||
ēvaṁ visayapivāsā ihaparalōunbhavāṇa dukkhāṇa | paramaṁ kāraṇamēsā ya jōnvaṇē maṁdasatēhiṁ ॥ 229||
nō nijjēuṁ sakkā, imaṁ tu vuḍapi mihuṇamēyāē । ēvaṁ viyāvahulaṁ vihiyē tō tēṇimaṁ bhaṇiyē ॥ 230 ॥
sarvē'pi duḥkhabhīravaḥ sarvē'pi sukhaiṣiṇaḥ sphuṭaṁ jīvāḥ । tasmādētadavasthāgataṁ mithunamidamiti pravartamānam ॥ 219॥
viṣayāsēvāyāṁ sukhaṁ kathayati prakaṭaṁ tathāpi nāthasya । kathaṁ dr̥ṣṭrēdaṁ jātā viṣayēṣu parāṅamukhā buddhiḥ || 220 ॥
darśanajñānamanantaṁ vīryamanantaṁ tathā sukhamanantam । paramārthēna svarūpaṁ jīvānāmidam, tathāpī mē ॥221॥
viṣayapipāsāpāmā kadarthitā iha bhavē'nādau । saṁpādanārthamēṣāṁ viṣayāṇāṁ sahantē duḥkhāni ॥ 222 ॥
jāyantē punastathāvidhakarmaṇa imē kadāpi kasyāpi । dāridryaduḥkhārtānāmanyēṣāṁ yāti punarjanma || 223 ॥
tatastēṣāṁ paribhēāgē kaṇḍūkaṇḍūyana iva sukhalēśam | bhuñjānō bahu manyatē viṣayapipāsāṁ pravartamānām॥ 224 ॥
atha kathamapi dhanābhāvē praṇayinīvirahēṇa bhavanti nō viṣayāḥ । tatastaccintāśalyitahr̥dayō duḥkhaṁ gamayati kālam ॥
naca śāmyati viṣayatr̥ṣṇā ciramapi saṁsēvitēṣu viṣayēṣu | atiśaya manōharēṣvapi viśēṣatō vardhatē gr̥ddhiḥ ॥ 226 ॥
viṣayāpipāsā cēyaṁ rāgō'nukūlēṣu viṣayēṣu । pratikūlēṣu dvēṣō jīvānāṁ mōhavaśagānām ॥ 227॥
rāgadvēṣau ca punaḥ karmaṇō nibandhanaṁ dhruvaṁ bhavataḥ । karmōdayēna jīvaḥ prāpnōti duḥkhaṁ bhavē ghōram ॥ 228 ॥
ēvaṁ viṣayapi sēhaparalōkōdbhavānāṁ duḥkhānām । paramaṁ kāraṇamēṣā ca yauvanē ma dasattvaiḥ ॥ 229 ॥ .
nō nirjētuṁ śakyēdaṁ tu vr̥ddhamapi mithunamatayā । ēvaṁ vikārabahulaṁ vihitaṁ tatastēnēdaṁ bhaṇitam ||230||

jiṇavayaṇagabbhiyaṁ vijayacaṁda piyayamapayaṁpiyaṁ ēyaṁ । sōūṇaṁ kamalasirī sappaṇayaṁ bhaṇai vayaṇamiṇaṁ ॥
jaṁ muharayāē piyayama ! paryaṁpiyaṁ appiyaṁ maē tumha । taṁ pasiūṇa khamijjau kuṇimō dhammujjamaṁ paramaṁ ॥
tō vijayacandarāyā jēsukhaṁ vijayarāyanāmāṇaṁ । ṭhaviḍaṁ rajjē giṇhai vihīē dikkhaṁ sugurumūlē ॥ 233॥
kamalasirīpabhirhi tēuriyāhi taha ya maṁtīhiṁ । sāmaṁtēhivi hici sahiō aimahavibhūīē || 234॥
gahiūṇa duvihasikvaṁ varisaṁtē kēvalīvi hōūṇa । sāsaya sōkkhaṁ pattō sammēē pavtrayavarammi || 235||
॥ iti sthūlaprāṇātipātaniraticāraprathamāṇuvrataphaladr̥ṣṭāntē vijayacandranarēśvarakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
jinavacanagarbhitaṁ vijayacandra priyatamaprajalpitamētat । śrutvā kamalaśrīḥ sapraṇavaṁ bhaṇati vacanārmadam ॥231॥
yad mukharatayā priyatama ! prajalpitamapriyaṁ mayā yuṣmābhiḥ । tatprasadya kṣamyatāṁ kurmō dharmōdyamaṁ paramam ॥ 232॥
tatō vijayacandrarājō jyēṣṭhataṁ vijayarājanāmānam । sthāpayitvā rājyē gr̥hṇāti vidhinā dīkṣāṁ sugurumūlē||
kamalaśrīprabhr̥tibhirāntaḥpurikībhistathā ca mantribhiḥ । sāmantairapi kaiścitsahitō'timahāvibhūtyā ॥ 234॥
gr̥hītvā dvividhaśikṣā varṣānti kēvalyapi bhūtvā । śāśvatasaukhyaṁ prāptaḥ sammētē parvatavarē ॥ 235 ॥

niravēkkhō duṭṭapaṇō tiriyāīṇaṁ karēi jō baṁdha । sō pāvai baṁdhavahaṁ jaha pattaṁ baṁdhurāēṇa ॥ 1 ॥
tathāhi: -
atthi puraṁ pōrāṇaṁ paumiṇisaṁḍaṁva paḍamiṇīsaṁḍaṁ । suvicittapattakaliyaṁ paumāvāsaṁ suvāṇiyayaṁ ॥2॥
tatyatthi asthijaṇavaṁdviyatyasaṁpāḍaṇikadullaliō | dhaṇaucca ghaṇō sēṭṭhī bhajjā tassatthi baṁdhumaī || 3 ||
tāṇaṁ ca parōpparanēhanivbharaṁ visayasōkkhanirayāṇaṁ । caccai kālō akaliyaduhāṇa dhaṇadhannakaliyāṇa |
kēvalamavaccadukkhaṁ sallai hiyaē parōpparaṁ tāṇaṁ । kiṁ vihavēṇamhāṇaṁ kulakēusuputtara hiyāṇaṁ ? ॥ 5 ॥
iya ciṁtājuttāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ vaccēti vāsarā virasā । aha annayā kayāī bandhumaī niyavaraduvārē ॥ ॥
jā ciṭṭhai tā pēcchai kassai gāhāvaissa gahavaiṇī । dhūlibhuruṁḍiyaputtērhi parigayā citaē tattō ॥ 7॥
dhannā ēsā mahilā jā ēvaṁ attaē ramāvēi । aimaṁjumammaṇullāvirīē vāṇīē suhāē ॥ 8 ॥
ēkkē gharaṛa kaḍīē bīyaṁ hatthaṁgulīē saṁlaggaṁ । tajhyāō ya cautthaṁ ruṭaṁ saṁbhāsa ēvaṁ ॥ 9 ॥
āgaccha vaccha ! aṁbā jaṁ jaṁpa taṁ karēha kiṁ bahuṇā ? । ginhasu aṁśyajaṁbuyaphalāī jaṇaṇīē ditīē ॥
iya bahuḍiṁbhajuyāē cariyaṁ daṭṭaṇa tīē mahilāē । appāṇaṁ niṁdatī pattā gēhassa majjhami ||11||
ciṁtē ahaṁ jaṇiyā ēkkacciya maṁdabhāiṇī vihiṇā । ēkkaṁpi puttabhaṁḍa jīē pasūrya na pāvāē ॥12॥
jammō niratthau tīē jīē mahilāē mammaṇulavirō। ramiūṇa dhūlidhavalō puttō nāruhai aṁkammi || 13 ||
annannakajjavaiyara ravikiraṇakayatthiyaṁ hiyayakumuyaṁ । ūsarai navari maṇuyāṇa taṇayamuhayaṁdasaccavaṇē ॥ 14 ॥
nirapēkṣō duṣṭamanāstiryagādīnāṁ karōti yō bandham । sa prāpnōti bandhavadhaṁ yathā prāptaṁ bandhurājēna ॥1॥
asti puraṁ purāṇaṁ padminīpaṇḍamiva padminīṣaṇḍam | suvicitrapā ( 1 )trakalitaṁ padmāvāsaṁ suvāṇija (pānīya) kam ॥
tatrāstyarthijana vāñchitārthasaṁpādanaikadurlalitaḥ । dhanada iva dhanaḥ śrēṣṭhī bhāryā tasyāsti bundhumatī ॥ 3 ॥
tayōśca parasparasnēhanirbharaṁ viṣaya saukhyaniratayōḥ । vrajati kālō'kalitaduḥkhayōvarnadhānyakalitayōḥ ॥ 4 ॥
kēvalarūpatyaduḥkhaṁ śalyati hr̥dayē parasparaṁ tayōḥ । kiṁ vibhavēnāvayōḥ kulakētusuputrarahitayōḥ ? || 9 ||
iti cintāyuktayōstayōrvrajanti vāsarā virasāḥ । athānyadā kadācid bandhumatī nijagr̥hadvārē || 6 ॥
yāvattiṣṭhati tāvatpaśyati kasyāpi gāthāpatēgr̥hapatnīm । dhūlidhūsarita putraḥ parigatāṁ cintayati tataḥ ॥ 7 ॥
dhanyaiṣā mahilā yaivamātmajān ramayati । atimañjumanmanōllāpanaśīlayā vāṇyā sukhadayā ॥ 8 ॥
ēkaṁ dharati kaṭyāṁ dvitīyaṁ hastāṅgulau saṁlagnam | tr̥tīyācca caturtha ruṣṭaṁ saṁbhāṣata ēvam ॥ 9 ॥
āgaccha vatsa ! ambā yajjalpati tatkuru kiṁ bahunā | gr̥hāṇāmrajāmbavaphalāni jananyā dadatyā ॥10॥
iti bahuḍimbhayuktāyāścaritaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā tasyā mahilāyāḥ । ātmānaṁ nindantī prāptā gēhasya madhyē ॥ 11॥
cintayatyaha' janitaikaiva mandabhāginī vidhinā । ēkamapi putrabhāṇḍaṁ yayā prasūtaṁ na pāpayā ॥ 12 ॥
janma nirarthakaṁ tasyā yasyā mahilīyā manmanōllapitā । rantvā dhūlidhavalaḥ putrō nārōhatyaṅkē ॥ 13 ॥
anyānyakāryavyatikarara vikiraṇakadarthitaṁ hr̥dayakumudam । ullasati kēvalaṁ manujānāṁ tanayamukha candradarśanē ॥ 14 ॥

dōgaccaṁpi na najjai na gaṇijjai āvaīvi aigaruī । hiyayassa nivvuikarō jāṇa suā guṇagaṇāhārō ||
iya taṇayābhāvasamubbhavēṇa asuhēṇa dūmiyā saṁtī । diṭṭhā siṭṭiṇaṇaṁ parammuhā sayalakajjēsu || 16 ||
himadakamaliṇī iva dīsasi kiṁ suyaṇu ! pucchiē tēṇa । sā kahai tassa puttābhāvadahaṁ tō ghaṇō bhaṇai ||
mā hōsu ūsuyamaṇā dhaṇiyaṁ bhattīē dhagayajakkhamahaṁ । ārāhiūga vihigā tuha puttaṁ dāvaissāmi ||18||
sattadiṇabhiṁtaraō tā mā pamayacchi ! khēyamuvvahasu । iya vr̥ttuṁ saṁjhāē dhaṇasiddhī iuṁ jakkhaṁ || 19||
parimukkasayalakajjō tabhavaṇē ṭhāi nirasaṇō tāva । jā sattamiyā rayaṇī tā jakkhō bhaṇai paccakkhaṁ ॥ 20 ॥
hōhī tuha lahu puttō, mahāpasāutti bhaṇiya namiūṇa । jakkhassa pāyakamalaṁ saṁpattō niyagihē siṭṭī || 21 ||
jakkhāēsaṁ savvaṁ kahē bhajjāēṁ sā ya saṁtuṭṭhā | baṁdhai gaṁṭhi bhaṇai ya ēvaṁ ciya hōu ēyaṁti ||22||
tō pacchimammi jāmē dhumaī pāsaē sumiṇayammi । niyavayaṇē pavisaṁta nāraṁgaṁ jaṇiyagururaṁgaṁ ||23||
uṭṭhēu sā sāhai pāiṇō tattō vimasiuṁ sammaṁ । tēṇavi taṇaō hōhitti sāhiyaṁ sā ya parituṭṭhā ||24||
tadivasajāyagabbhā pasavai samaē maṇōramaṁ puttaṁ । pattammi bārasāhē dinaṁ nāmaṁ imaṁ tassa ||25||
jaṇaēhi baṁdhurāōti lacchivicchaḍaō taō kamasō । ahigayakalākalāvī saṁpattō jōvvaṇaṁ sōvi ॥
aha kēvi kajjēṇaṁ dhaṇasēṭṭhī baṁdhurāya parikaliō । saṁpattō ujjāṇē jaṇamaṇaāṇaṁdaṇabhihāṇē ||27||
tō pēcchai tattha muṇi dēsataṁ sugaipañcalaṁ dhammaṁ । bhavvāṇa hiyaṭṭhāē uvaviṭṭhō sōvi nisuṇē ||28||
tadyathā:-
daurgatyamapi na jñāyatē na gaṇyata āpadapyatigurvī | hr̥dayasya nirvr̥tikarō yēṣāṁ sutō guṇagaṇādhāraḥ ॥ 15 ॥
iti tanayābhāvasamudbhavanāsukhēna dāvitā santī 1 dr̥ṣṭā śrēṣṭhidhanēna parāṅmukhā sakalakāryēṣu || 16 ||
himadagdhakamalinīva dr̥śyasē kiṁ sutanuṁ ! pr̥ṣṭē tēna । sā kathayati tasmai putrābhāvaduḥkhaṁ tatō dhanō bhaṇati ॥17॥
mā bhavōtsukamanā bāḍhaṁ bhaktyā dhanadayakṣamaham । ārādhya vidhinā tubhyaṁ putra dāpayiṣyāmi ॥ 18 ॥
saptadinābhyantaraṁ tasmānmā pramadākṣiṁ ! khēdamudvaha । ityuktvā saṁdhyāyāṁ ghanaśrēṣṭhī pūjayituṁ yakṣam ॥ 19 ॥
parimuktasakalakāryastadbhavanē tiṣṭhati niraśanastāvat । yāvatsaptamī · rajanistadā yakṣō bhaṇati pratyakṣam ॥20॥
bhaviṣyati tava laghu putrō mahāprasāda iti bhaṇitvā natvā । yakṣasya pādakamalaṁ saṁprāptō nijagr̥hē śrēṣṭhī ॥ 21 ॥
yakṣādēśa sarvaṁ kathayati bhāryāyāḥ sā ca saṁtuṣṭā । badhnāti granthi bhaṇati caivamēva bhavatvētaditi ॥ 22॥
tataḥ paścimē yāṁmē bandhumatī paśyati svapnē । nijavadanē praviśad nāraṅgaṁ janitagururaṅgam ||23||
utthāya sā kathayati patyē tatō vimr̥śya samyak । tēnāpi tanayō bhaviṣyatīti kathitaṁ sā ca parituṣṭa | ॥ 24 ॥
taddivasa jātagarbhā prasūtē samayē manōramaṁ sutram । prāptē dvādaśāhē dattaṁ nāmēdaṁ tasya ॥ 25 ॥
janakābhyāṁ bandhurāja iti lakṣmīvistaratastataḥ kramaśaḥ । adhigatakalākalāpaḥ saṁprāptō yauvanaṁ sōḍāvē ॥ 26 ॥
atha kēnāpi kāryēṇa dhanaśrēṣṭhī bandhurājaparikalitaḥ । saṁprāpta udyānē janamanaānandanābhidhānē ||27॥
tataḥ paśyati tatra muni diśantaṁ sugatipratyalaṁ dharmam । bhavyānāṁ hitārthamupaviṣṭaḥ sō'pi śr̥ṇōti ॥ 28॥

bandhurājakahā ।
bāhattarikalakusalavitē nara muṁkkhagaṇi, sayalakalahaṁ supavitta na dayakala jāhaṁ maṇi ।
saṁjamakala taha tavakala varavinnāṇakala, jē iya kalā hu na yāṇahiṁ tē nara naṇu vigala ||29||
chadaṁsaṇa channavai pāsaṁḍaī, avarupparuvi na maccharu chaḍḍaī |
tāhaṁ na dūsai kōi ahiṁsā, tō tamaṇuha ma kuṇaha hiṁsā ||30||
jō saddhammāmā gai kuhammu naru, pacchattāvadavēṇa su ḍajjhai jēmba taru |
,
jō die kiraviṇu minhai kāyamaṇi, sō jāṇaga jāṇāviu bahu tappēṛa maṇi ॥ 31 ॥
na jaḍakalā na vakkalacīraī, na maṁḍaṇū naṁ khālaṇu nīraī ।
ēyāī sōhi karaṁti na pāvahūṁ, jaha daya thāvarajaṁgamajīvahaṁ ॥ 32 ॥
239
iccāidayāguṇagaṇamāyanēuṁ murṇidāsamma | vihiṇā tasavahaviraī paḍivannā baṁdhurāēṇa ||33||
jō ēyaṁ paḍivajjai vajjai sō baṁdhapamuhaaiyārē । iya kahiē muṇitrayaṇā paḍivajjai tēvi taha cēva ॥ 34 ॥
dhaṇasēṭṭhiṇā pavana sāvayadhammō duvālasavihōvi । paṇamēuṁ munināhaṁ saṭṭhāṇaṁ jaṁti tē dōvi ||35||
jīvadayaṁ kuvvatō savisēsaṁ baṁdhurāyavaṇipavarō । paṁcahi bhajjāhiṁ samaṁ kīlai dōguṁdugasurōvva ॥ 36 ॥
aha anayā kayāī kēṇaī mittēga sāhiyaṁ tassa । jaha ajja jōganaṁdī ujjāṇē jōgiō pattō ||37|
jō niyaguṇagaṇadhavala bahumullamahalamōttiyasarīē । kaṁṭhagayāē rēhai himavaṁtagirivva gaṁgāē ||38||
tādavva ēsō agaacchērayāṇa kulabhavaṇaṁ । daṭṭhavvadaṁsaṇaṁ ciya nayaṇāṇa phalaṁ buhā viṁti ||39||
dvāsaptatikalākuśalā api tē narā mūrkhagaṇē, sakalakalāsu supavitrā na dayākalā yēṣāṁ manasi ।
saṁyamakalā tathā tapaḥkalā varavijñānakalā, yē iti kalāḥ khalu na jānanti tē narā nanu vikalāḥ ॥ 29 ॥
ṣaḍ darśanāni ṣaṇṇavatiḥ pākhaṇḍāni, parasparamapi na matsaraṁ muñcanti ।
tēṣāṁ na dūṣayati kō'pyahiṁsāṁ, tatastāmanutiṣṭhata mā kuruta hiṁsām ||30||
yaḥ saddharmāśayā gr̥hṇāti kudharma naraḥ, paścāttāpadavēna sa dahyatē yathā taruḥ ।
yō vaiḍūryaṁ vikrīya gr̥hṇāti kācamaṇi, sa jñāyakō jñāpayitā bahu tapati manasi ॥ 31 ॥
naṁ jaṭākalāpō na valkalacīvarāṇi, na maṇḍanaṁ na kṣālanaṁ nīrēṇa ।
,
ētāni śuddhiṁ kurvanti na pāpānāṁ yathā dayā sthāvarajaṅgamajīvānām ॥32॥
ityādidayāguṇagaṇamākarṇya munīndrapārśvē । vidhinā trasavadhaviratiḥ pratipannā bandhurājēna ||33||
ya ētāṁ pratipadyēta varjayēt sa bandhapramukhāticārān । iti kathitē munivacanātparivarjayati tānapi tathaiva ॥
dhanaśrēṣṭhinā prapannaḥ śrāvakadharmōṁ dvādaśavidhō'pi । praṇamya munināthaṁ svasthānaṁ yātastau dvāvapi ॥ 35॥
jīvadayāṁ kurvan saviśēṣaṁ bandhurājavaṇikpravaraḥ । pañcabhirbhāryābhiḥ samaṁ krīḍati daugundukasura iva ॥ 36 ॥
athānyadā kadācitkēnacid mitrēṇa kathitaṁ tasmai । yathā'dya yōganandyadyānē yōgī prāptaḥ ||37||
yō nijaguṇagaṇadhavalō bahumūlyamahāmauktikamālayā । kaṇṭhagatayā rājati himavagiririva gaṅgayā ||38||

baṁdhurājakahā ।
233
bhamirhati bhavaṁ ghōraṁ tē vahabaṁdhādukkhaparataṁtā । thaivōvi hu vayabhaṁgō jaṇēi garuyāī dukhāim̐ || 54 ||
iya piuṇā bhannatō mannatō sō tirṇava tavvayaṇaṁ । taha caiva payaṭṭaṁtō ōhaṭṭaṁtō na maṇayapi ॥ 55 ॥
rāyāmaccāīhiṁ nāūṇa supāḍihēraparikaliyaṁ । sāmēṇaṁ bhaṇiōvi hu na kuṇai kannēvi tanvayaṇa ॥56॥
aha vivēlāitō bhadhaṇavvaiyarammi kalahaṁtō । gahiō baṁdhāviya cēḍagāō labdhaṁ dhaṇaṁ kiṁpi ॥ 57 ॥
dāyavvamatthi annaṁpi kiṁpi sō bhāi tumha jaṁ ēttha । tassa ya sa khaggaṁ ginhaha ēyaṁti sō bhaṇiuṁ ॥
kōsāō āyaṭṭiya khaggaṁ daṁsaṇamisēṇa sahasatti । ēkkēṇaṁ ghāēṇaṁ dō khaṁḍai baṁdhurāyaṁ sō ।। 59 ।।
niyabhiccasahāō sō tāsēuṁ bandhurāyabhiccajaṇaṁ । niyayāvāsammi gaō tattha sakhtrē talārēṇa ॥ 60 ॥
vinna naravaiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ jaha ēttiyassa sō jōggō | annāyaparō tamhā gavasaṇā iha na kāyavvā ॥ 61 ॥
vinnattē
tō paṁcagaō gamihī gaī bahupayārāsu । visatō ghaṇadukkhaṁ baṁdhaṇavahamāraṇāīyaṁ ॥ 62 ॥
siṭṭhī hu vivaṁ sattasu khittēsu pakkhivēūṇa । suguruṇa pāyamūlē giṇhai dikkhaṁ sabhajjōvi ॥ 63 ॥
gahiūṇa duvihasikkhaṁ aṁtē saṁlēhaṇaṁ vihēūṇa | saṁpattō sōhammē kamēṇa mōkkhaṁpi gacchahihī ॥ 64 ॥
॥ iti prāṇātipātaviratiprathamāticāravipākē bandhurājakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
bhuvanaguruṇōpadiṣṭaṁ jīvadayānirmalaṁ vrataṁ gr̥hītvā । bhañjanti jantusaṁtāpanēna yē mandabuddhayaḥ ||13||
bhramiṣyanti bhavaṁ ghōraṁ tē vadhabandhādiduḥkhaparatantrāḥ । stōkō'pi khalu vratabhaṅgō janayati gurūṇi duḥkhāni ॥
iti pitrā bhaṇyamānō manyamānaḥ sa tr̥ṇamiva tadvacanam । tathaiva pravartamānō'sapan na manāgapi ॥ 55 ॥
rājāmatyādibhirjñātvā suprātihāryaparikalitam । sāmnā bhaṇitō'pi khalu na karōti karṇē'pi tadvacanam ॥ 56 ॥
atha nr̥pavēlā''yuktō labhyadhanavyatikarē kalahayan । gr̥hītō bandhayitvā cēṭakād labhyaṁ dhanaṁ kimapi ॥ 57 ॥
dātavyamastyanyadapi kimapi sa bhaṇati tubhyaṁ yadatra । tasya ca saṭṭē khaṅgaṁ gr̥hāṇaitamiti sa bhaṇitvā ॥58॥
kōśa ādākr̥ṣya khaṅgaṁ darśanamiṣēṇa sahasēti । ēkēna ghātēna dvidhā khaṇḍayati bandhurājaṁ saḥ ॥ 59 ॥
nijabhr̥tyasahāyaḥ sa trāsayitvā bandhurājabhr̥tyajanam । nijāvāsē gatastatra svarūpē purarakṣēṇa ॥ 60 ॥
vijñāpitē narapatinā bhaṇitaṁ yathaitāvataḥ sa yōgyaḥ । anyāyaparastasmād gavēṣaṇēha na kartavyā ॥ 61 ॥
tataḥ pañcatvagatō gamiṣyati kugatiṣu bahuprakārāsu । viṣahamānō ghanaduḥkhaṁ bandhanavadhamāraṇādikam ॥62॥
dhanaśrēṣṭhyapi khalu vibhavaṁ saptasu kṣētrēṣu prakṣipya । sugurūṇāṁ pādamūlē gr̥hṇāti dīkṣāṁ sabhāryō'pi ॥63॥
gr̥hām̐tvā dvivivaśikṣāmantē saṁlēkhanāṁ vidhāya । saṁprāptaḥ saudharmē kramēṇa mōkṣamapi gamiṣyati ॥ 64 ॥

jō liṭṭhalauḍadaṁḍāiēhi jīvāṇa tāḍaṇaṁ kuṇai । nissaṁkō kuddhamaṇō diōvva sō bhamai bhīmabhavē ॥
tathāhi;
asthi bharahammi vāsē kusumapuraṁ puramaṇaṁgasāricchaṁ । sirinaṁdaṇaṁ samayaraṁ aviggahaṁ khāisālilaṁ ||2||
tammi niat nivatilaō malaō dāridadāvataviyāṇaṁ । raisuṁdarī kalattaṁ sukalattaṁ tassa sukalattaṁ ||3||
taha maṁtī maijalahī tassatthi purōhiō ya sirikaṁṭhō । sē bhajjā ya jasōyā putō tāṇatthi sirivacchā ||
sō anya kayāī piuṇā avamāṇiō jaḍappagaī । kaṁcanapurammi pattō kaṇavittiṁ kuṇai paḍhēī ya ||5||
vijjāmammi tahavi hu na kiṁci āgacchaī paḍhaṁtassa । tō nivvinnō bāḍhaṁ pāḍhaṁ mōtuṁ dahasarīrō || 6 ||
ōlaggiuṁ pavattō bhōyaṇavittīya sūragihavaiṇō । tassa suēṇaṁ saddhiṁ kampivi gāmammi saṁcaliō ॥7॥
picchaṁti ya tē maggē muṇīṇa jayalaṁ pahē parissaṁtaṁ । naggōharuvakhahiḍā uvahiṁ phāyasē ||8||
taṁ ca namiūṇa dōvi hu uvaviṭṭhā aha bhaṇēi bhattīē । tayabhimuhaṁ sūrasuō pahu ! dhammō kiṁphalō hō ? ||
tō sajalajalaharuddāmagahirasaddēṇa tāṇa taṁ kahai । tammajjhē jiṭṭamuṇī taccittaṇukūlaṇatthaṁ jaṁ ॥ 10 ॥
tathāhi ;-
mōkkhaphalō duhadalaṇō āvaikālēvi dinnasāhijjō । hiyaicchiyakajjakarō havai sumittōvva jiṇadhammō ॥
sārīramāṇasāṇa dukkhāṇaṁ mōyagō maṇāṇaṁdō । bhavajalahijāṇavattaṁ savvattha jayāvahō dhammō || 12 |
dālidavāhiparamōsava sōharaṁgakaṁḍayaṁ paramaṁ । maṇacitiyatthasaṁpāḍaṇammi ciṁtāmaṇī dhammō ॥ 13 ॥
vinnāṇanāṇajaṇaō baṁdhū nīsēsajaṁtuvaggassa । bīsāsakaraṇapaḍuō paramapayaṭṭāvaō dhammō ॥ 14 ॥
yō lēpṭulakuṭadaṇḍādikairjīvānāṁ tāḍanaṁ karōti । niḥśaṅkaḥ kruddhamanā dvija iva sa bhramati bhīmabhavē ॥ 1 ॥
asti bharatē varṣē kusumapuraṁ puramanaṅgasadr̥śam । śrīnandanaṁ sa-ma-karama vigrahaṁ khāti (di) śāli ॥2॥
tasmin nr̥pō nr̥patilakō malayō dāridryadāvataptānām । ratisundarī kalatraṁ sukalatvaṁ tasya śukalaptam ॥3॥
tathā mantrī matijaladhistasyāsti purōhitaścaḥ śrīkaṇṭhaḥ । tasya bhāryā ca yaśōdā putrastayōrasti śrīvatsaḥ ॥4॥
sō'nyadā kadācitpitrā'pamānitō jaḍaprakr̥tiḥ । kāñcanapurē prāptaḥ kaṇavr̥ttiṁ karōti paṭhati ca ॥5॥
vidyāmaṭhē tathāpi khalu na kiñcidāgacchati paṭhataḥ । tatō nirviṇṇō bāṁḍha pāṭhaṁ muktvā dr̥ḍhaśarīraḥ ॥ 6 ॥
avalagituṁ pravr̥ttō bhōjanavr̥ttyā sūragr̥hapatēḥ । tasya sutēna sārdhaṁ kasminnapi grāmē saṁcalitaḥ ||7||
paśyataśca tau mārgē munīnāṁ yugalaṁ pathi pariśrāntam । nyagrōdhavr̥kṣasyāca upaviṣṭaṁ prāsukapradēśē ॥8॥
tacca natvā dvāvapyupaviṣṭāvatha bhaṇati bhaktyā । tadabhimukhaṁ sūrasutaḥ prabhō ! dharmaḥ kiṁ phalō bhavati ? ॥9॥
tataḥ sajalajaladharōddāmagabhīraśabdēna tayōstaṁ kathayati । tanmadhyē jyēṣṭhamunistaccittānukūlanārthaṁ yat ॥10॥
mōkṣaphalō duḥkhadalana āpatkālē'pi dattasāhāyyaḥ । hr̥dayēpsitakāryakarō bhavati sumittramiva jinadharmaḥ ॥11॥
śārīramānasayōrduḥkhayōmōṁcakō manaānandaḥ । bhavajaladhiyānapātraṁ sarvatra jayāvahō dharmaḥ ॥12॥
dāridryavyādhiparamaiṣadhamiva saubhāgyakāṇḍaḥ paramaḥ । manaścintitārthasaṁpādanē cintāmaṇirdharmaḥ ॥13॥

dōsāyaraṇanivittī sukuluppattī suhāṇa saṁpattī | sattubalassa vivattī jāyai paramēṇa dhammēṇa ॥ 15 ॥
sayalajaṇapatthaṇijjā suhayā sacchaṁdagāmiṇī viulā । viyarai samujjalaṁgī kittī dhammēṇa savva ॥ 16 ॥
iya kahiuṁ dhammaphalaṁ bhaṇiyā tē dōvi sāhuṇā bhō bhō ! । jiṇavarabhaṇiyaṁ dhammaṁ kuṇaha payattēṇa paidiyahaṁ ||
siricchrēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sō dhammō kērisō, muṇī kahai । jiṇabhaṇiyasadahāṇaṁ jīvadayā aṇuhāṇaṁ ॥ 18 ॥
aha jiganāhasarūvaṁ sugurusarūvaṁ jiyāitattāī । kahiūṇa jīvadayāmūlattaṁ kahai dhammassa ||19||
tadyathā;
" paṭhitaṁ śrutaṁ ca śāstraṁ guruparicaraṇaṁ ca gurutapaścaraṇam । ghanagarjitamiva vijalaṁ viphalaṁ sakalaṁ dayāvikalam ।।"
iccāisavapaṁcaṁ jaidhammaṁ kahiya kahai gihidhammaṁ । tō sivicchō jaṁpara āyannaha majjha vinnati || 20 |
na hami nirava jī saṁkappaō ahaṁ dhūlē । jāvajjīvaṁ tā maha kuṇaha pasāyaṁ vayēṇimiṇā ||21||
tō muṇiṇā sē kahiyā baṁdhāī paṁca ittha aiyārā । ēēvi na kāyavtrā paḍhamavayaṁ rakkhamāṇēṇa ॥ 22 ॥
āmaṁti tēṇa bhaṇiē sūrasuēṇavi tahēva paḍivanē । vihiṇā paḍhamamaṇuvvayamārōvai tāṇa muṇināhō ||23||
tō baṁdiūṇa muṇiṇō caliyā tē dōvi jattha gaṁtavthaṁ । muṇiṇōvi jahābhimayaṁ pagayā pagaēṇa kajjēṇa ॥
kariūṇaṁ taṁ jattaṁ pattā tē puṇavi kaṁcanapurammi । kisikammamāiyāī kariti kammāī vivihāī || 25 ||
aha sūrēṇa vivāhō pāraddhō niyasuyāē vittharaō । saha īsarēṇa kēṇavi tīē āharaṇahēuṁ ca ॥ 26 ॥
suttai bahuṁ suvannaṁ māṇikāī ca mōttiyāī ca । aha lahubaṁdhū sūrassa kēsavō citaē ēvaṁ ||27||
vijñānajñānajanakō bandhurniḥ śēṣajantuvargasya । viśvāsakaraṇapaṭuḥ paramapadasthāpakō dharmaḥ ॥ 14 ॥
dōṣācaraṇanivr̥ttiḥ sukulōtpattiḥ sukhānāṁ saṁpattiḥ । śatrubalasya vipattirjāyatē paramēṇa dharmēṇa ॥ 15 ॥
sakalajanaprārthanīyā subhagā svacchandagāminī vipulā । vicarati samujjvalāṅgī kīrtirdhamēṇa vēśyēva ॥ 16॥
iti kathayitvā dharmaphalaṁ bhaṇitau tau dvāvapi sādhunā bhō bhōḥ ! | jinavarabhaṇitaṁ dharma kuruta prayatnēna pratidivasam ॥
śrīvatsēna bhaṇitaṁ sa dharmaḥ kīdr̥śō, muniḥ kathayati । jinamaṇitaśraddhānaṁ jīvadayāyā anuṣṭhānam ॥18॥
atha jinanāthasvarūpaṁ sugurusvarūpaṁ jīvāditattvāni । kathayitvā jīvadayāmūlatvaṁ kathayati dharmasya ॥ 19॥
ityādisaprapañcaṁ yatidharmaṁ kathayitvā kathayati gr̥hidharmam । tataḥ śrīvatsō jalpatyākarṇayata mama vijñaptim ॥20॥
na hanmi niraparādhān jīvāt saṁkalpatō'haṁ sthūlān । yāvajjīvaṁ tasmānmama kuruta prasādaṁ tēnānēna ॥21॥
tatō muninā tasya kathitā bandhādayaḥ pañcātrāticārāḥ । ētē'pi na kartavyāḥ prathamatrataṁ rakṣatā ||22||
āmēti tēna bhaṇitē sūrasutēnāpi tathaiva pratipannē । vidhinā prathamamaṇutratamārōpayati tayōrmunināthaḥ ||23||
tatō vanditvā munī calitau tau dvāvapi yatra gantavyam । munī api yathābhimataṁ pragatau prakr̥tēna kāryēṇa ॥ 24॥
kr̥tvā tāṁ yātrāṁ prāptau tau punarapi kāñcanapurē । kr̥ṣikarmādikāni kurutaḥ karmāṇi vividhāni ||25|
atha sūrēṇa vivāhaḥ prārabdhō nijasutāyā vistarataḥ । sahēśvarēṇa kēnāpi tasyā ābharaṇahētōśca ॥ 26 ॥
sūtrayati bahu suvarṇa māṇikyāni ca mauktikāni ca । atha laghubandhuḥ sūrasya kēśavaścintayatyēvam ॥27॥

jaṁ ēsa iha vaissai taṁ savvaṁ majjha jāi vihavāō । tamhā hōmi vibhinnō paḍhamaṁpi vivāhakālāō ||28||
tō sūraṁ sō pabhaṇai baṁdhava ! jaṁ kiṁpi ēi maha bhāgē । taṁ dēha, bhaṇai sūrō kiṁ ēvaṁ bucca vaccha ! ||29|
kasya punnēhiṁ sirī bahai miliyāṇa najjai na ittha । hōjja puḍhībhūyāṇaṁ sā kassavi kavi dālidaṁ ।
tō tassava ābhārō kaḍḍēyavvōvarēṇa savvōvi । suyaṇattasaṁṭhiēṇaṁ ēvaṁ ciya vahau tā vaccha ! ||31||
tō aus haal maha dāli hōhiī viuttassa । jai, tōvi na patthistaṁ kiṁpi ahaṁ dēhi maha bhāgaṁ ।।
iya kāuṁ nibaṁdha baṁdhusayāsāu lēi viśvaddhaṁ । sirivacchaṁpi ha lōbhaviya nē tō appaṇī pāsē ||33|
paidivasa ciya vaḍḍhar viśvō sūrarasa, kēsavastra puṇō । taha khīṇō jaha bhōyaṇamittaṁ kicchēṇa saṁpaḍai ||
ditastava nō giues sūrassa imō dhaṇā thēpi । iya tampi khīṇavivammi āgaō pāusō kasō ||
tathāhi; --

hu
gajjaṁtagahira ghaṇagaruyagayaghaḍāḍōvapayaḍiyapayāvō । uttharai gimhanihaṇikavikamō pāusō rāyā ||36||

iya pāusēṇa kaṇiyāriūṇa varisaṁtamēghadhārāhiṁ । nivvaviyaṁ bhuvaṇayalaṁ mōttaṇaṁ virahihiyayāī || 38 |

tataḥ sūraṁ sa prabhaṇati bāndhava ! yatkimapyēti mama bhāgē । tad dēhi, bhaṇati sūraḥ kimēvamucyatē vatsa ! ॥
kasya ca puṇyaiḥ śrīrvartatē militānāṁ jñāyatē nātra । bhavētpr̥thagbhūtānāṁ sā kasyāpi kathamapi dāridryam ||30||

tatō bhaṇati kēśavō mama dāridryaṁ bhaviṣyati viyuktasya । yadi, tatō'pi na prārthayiṣyē kimapyahaṁ dēhi mama bhāgam |

pratidivasamēva vardhatē vibhavaḥ sūrasya, kēśavasya punaḥ । tathā kṣīṇō yathā bhōjanamātraṁ kr̥cchrēṇa saṁpadyatē ॥34॥

supāsamāha - variyami-
dō sārabalihāvi hu tērhi uddāliyā taō sagaḍaṁ । vāhēi bhāḍaēṇaṁ sirivacchō avaragōṇēhiṁ ॥ 57 ॥
aha anadinē juttō sō galiō gaḍḍayammi bhariyammi ghaṇadhūlīkhōṇīē khurēvi ukkhaṇai na kahapi ॥ 58 ॥
sagaḍāō uttariuṁ tō sō ārāhiṁ vidhaē haṇai । tōtayalauḍayaḍaṁgālivalāīhiṁ nikkaruṇaṁ ॥ 59 ॥
aha mōḍēu laggō pucchaṁ jā tēṇa galibaladēṇa । lattāē haō gāḍhaṁ mammammi maō gaō narayaṁ ॥ 60 ॥
tō sūrasuō citara haddhī ēsō pamāyavasavattī । vayamayalaṇāu nūṇaṁ bhamihī ēsō bhavanē ॥ 61 ॥
majjhavi aladdhapuvvaṁ laddhuṁ ēyaṁ sudhammasāmaggiṁ । kugaīē nivaḍatō appā nōviksiḍaṁ jutō ॥62॥
sugaī puṇa mutticciya sā puṇa saṁpunnacaraṇaō cēva । taṁ puṇa ṁ sugurūṇa samāgamēṇa, gavissāmitā ēē ॥
ēvaṁ sō saṁtō kō pāhiṁ āupajjatē । akhaṁḍiyapaḍhamavaō pattō īsāṇakappammi ॥ 64 ॥
sirivacchanāra ōvi hu paramāhammiyamuhāu nisuṇēuṁ । sumarēūṇaṁ ca tahā paḍhamāṇuvvaya akamaṇaṁ ॥ 65 ॥
pasariyapacchāyāvō paricita hā ! maē aṇajjēṇa । amayalavammi nihittō kaha muṭṭhī kālakūḍassa 1 ॥
laddhūṇa savvasaṁjamasāmaggimaṇuvvayaṁ maē paḍhamaṁ । ēkaṁ ciya paḍivannaṁ taṁpi hu jāṇaṁtaēva ॥ 67॥
bhagaṁ akamaṇa pavaraamarattakāraṇaṁ paramaṁ । sivasuhasaṁpattiphalaṁ kamēṇa inhi tu pāvō hai ||68 ||
ēyamavatthaṁ pattō karēmi kiṁ dukkhasāyara nibuḍḍō । tā saccamiṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kēhivi vihēhi purisēhiṁ ॥ 69॥
"ihaiva narakavyādhēścikitsāṁ na karōti yaḥ । gatō nirauṣadhaṁ sthānaṁ sa rujaḥ kiṁ kariṣyati ? ॥”
ēvaṁ sō appāṇaṁ niṁdatō jiṇavarappaṇīyaṁ ca । dhammaṁ bahu mannatō vāsasahassāī dasa gabhiuṁ ॥ 70 ॥
itaśca kapilamūṣakakaccarabahujhillī śalabhaprabhr̥tibhiḥ । kēśavakr̥ṣirvinaṣṭā vyavahāra kaistatō dhr̥taḥ ॥56॥
dvau sārabalīvardāvapi khalu taigr̥hītau tataḥ śakaṭam । vāhayati bhāṭakēna śrīvatsō'paragavābhyām ||17|
athānyadinē yuktaḥ saṁ galiḥ śakaṭē bhr̥tē । ghanadhūlikṣōṇyāṁ khurānapyutkhanati na kathamapi ||18||
śakaṭāduttīrya tataḥ sa ārābhirvidhyati hanti । tōtralakuṭayaṣṭilēṣṭūpalādibhirniṣkaruṇam ||19||
atha mōṭayituṁ lagnaḥ pucchaṁ yāvattēna galibalīvardēna । pādēna hatō gāḍhaṁ marmaṇi mr̥tō gatō narakam ॥60॥
tataḥ surasutaścintayati hā viśēṣa pramādavaśavartī । vratamalinīkaraṇānnūnaṁ bhramiṣyatyēṣa bhavāraṇyē ॥ 61॥
mamāpyalabdhapūrvī labdhvatāṁ sudharmasāmagrīm । kugatau nipatannātmā nōpēkṣituṁ yuktaḥ ॥ 62॥
sugatiḥ punarmuktirēva sā punaḥ saṁpūrṇacāritrata ēva । tatpunaḥ sugurūṇāṁ samāgamēna, gavēṣayiṣyāmi tasmādētān ॥
ēvaṁ sa vyavasyan muktaḥ prāṇairāyuḥparyantē । akhaṇḍita prathamatrataḥ prāpta īśānakalpē ॥ 64 ॥
śrīvatsanārakō'pi khalu paramādhārmikamukhāt śrutvā । smr̥tvā ca tathā prathamāṇutrātikramaṇam ||65||
prasr̥tapaścāttāpaḥ pariracintayati hā ! mayā'nāryēṇa । amr̥talavē nihitaḥ kathaṁ muṣṭiḥ kālakūṭasya ? ॥66॥
labdhvā sarvasaṁyama sāmagrīkamaṇuvrataṁ mayā prathamam । ēkamēva pratipannaṁ tadapi khalu jānataiva ॥ 67 ॥
bhagnamatikrāmatā pravarāmaratvakāraṇaṁ paramam । śivasukhasaṁpattiphalaṁ kramēṇēdānīṁ tu pāpō'ham ||68 ||
ētāmavasthāṁ prāptaḥ karōmi kiṁ duḥkhasāgaranimagnaḥ । tasmātsatyāmituṁ bhaṇitaṁ kairapi vibudhaiḥ puruṣaiḥ ॥69॥

tathāhi ; ---
mahimahilāmuhatilayaṁva lacchinilayaṁ puraṁ iha pasiddhaṁ । vijiyavipakkhanariṁdō rāyā tatthatthi kurucaṁdō ॥2॥
tassatthiṁ piyā gōrīva saṁbhuṇō sīlasāliṇī līlā | rāhaḍanāmā maṁtī surajjakajjē sayā sajjō ॥ 3 ॥
aha annayā nariṁdō rāhaḍamaṁḍaliyamāilōēṇa । parivāriō samaṁtā atthāṇasahāē vō ||4||
jā ci tā diṭṭhō ēgō vijjāharō nahayalāō । āgacchaṁtō karakaliyakhaggaphalaō sabhajjō ya||5||
saṁpatō atthāṇē pabhaṇai naranāhapaṇayapayakamalaṁ । kurucaṁdarāya ! nisuṇasu vinnatti majjha pasiūṇa ||6||
aṇamēgaṁ majjha piyā rakkhēyavvā taē payattēṇa । jāva ahaṁ saṁgāmaṁ karēmi gaṁtūṇa saha riuṇā || 7॥
annattha katthavi ahaṁ ēyaṁ mōttuṁ caēmi nahu tēṇa । tuha pāsamma muēmi paranārisahōyara ! nariṁdē ! ||8||
parakajjakaraṇarasiyā dīsaṁti mahīē paviralanariṁdā | tumhārisā mahāyasa ! purisōttamaguṇagaṇōvēyā ॥9॥
savvassaṁ maha ēsā pāṇapiyā paṇaiṇī imā tamhā । rakkhēyavvā tumaē iya bhaṇiuṁ tō gaō khayarō ॥ 10 ॥
dinnāsamma aha sā uvaviṭṭhā khayarapaṇaiṇī jāva । tā gayaṇāō sahasā pharayasaṇāhā bhuyā paḍiyā ||
tāhē uḍḍhamuhāṇaṁ savvāṇa jaṇāṇa tammi atthāṇē । digahiyamaṁḍalaggā duiyabhuyā nivaḍiyā jhati ॥ 12 ॥
tattō khēvēṇa viṇā paḍiyaṁ gayaṇagaṇāu sirakamalaṁ । maṇimauḍadipamāṇaṁ majjhahadidirvivaṁ ॥ 13 ॥
gurukōvāruṇadāruṇapasāriyacchaṁ aīva duṣpicchaṁ । tivalībhaṁgurabhālaṁ niṭhuradaṁtaggadaṭṭhōhaṁ ॥14||
galakambalakarṇādīnāṁ chēdanaṁ yaḥ karōti jīvānām । sa rāhaḍa iva prāpnōti bhavabhūmaṇaduḥkhāni bhīmāni ॥ 1 ॥
mahīmahilāmukhatilakamiva lakṣmīnilayaṁ puramiha prasiddham । vijitavipakṣanērēndrō rājā tatrāsti kurucandraḥ ॥2॥
tasyāsti priyā gaurīva śambhōḥ śīlaśālinī līlā | rāhaḍanāmā mantrī surājyakāryē sadā sajjaḥ ॥3॥
athānyadā narēndrō rāhaḍamāṇḍalikādilōkēna । parivāritaḥ samantādāsthānasabhāyāmupaviṣṭaḥ || 4 ||
yāvattiṣṭhati tāvad dr̥ṣṭa ēkēō vidyādharō nabhastalāt । āgacchan karakalitakhaḍgaphalakaḥ sabhāryaśca ॥5॥
saṁprāpta āsthānē prabhaṇati naranāthapraṇatapādakamalam । kurucandrarājan ! śr̥ṇu vijñaptiṁ mama prasadya ॥ 6 ॥
kṣaṇamēkaṁ mama priyā rakṣitavyā tvayā prayatnēna । yāvadahaṁ saṁgrāmaṁ karōmi gatvā saha ripuṇā ||7|
anyatra kvāpyahamētāṁ mōktuṁ śaknōmi naiva tēna । tava pāvēṁ muñcāmi paranārīsahōdara ! narēndra ! ||8||
parakāryakaraṇarasikā dr̥śyantē madyāṁ praviralanarēndrāḥ । yuṣmādr̥śā mahāyaśaḥ ! puruṣōttamaguṇagaṇōpētāḥ ॥9॥
sarvasvaṁ mamaiṣā prāṇapriyā praṇayinīyaṁ tasmāt । rakṣitavyā yuṣmābhiriti bhaṇitvā tatō gataḥ khacaraḥ ॥ 10 ॥
dattāsanē'tha sōpaviṣṭā khacarapraṇayinī yāvat । tāvad gaganāt sahasā pharakasanāthā bhujā patitā ॥ 11 ॥
tadōrdhvamukhēṣu sarvēṣu janēṣu tasminnāsthānē । dr̥ḍhagr̥hītamaṇḍalāgrā dvitīyabhujā nipatitā jhaṭiti ॥ 12 ॥
tataḥ kṣēpēṇa vinā patitaṁ gaganāṅgaṇācchiraḥ kamalam । maṇimukuṭadīpyamānaṁ madhyāhr̥dinēndrabimbamiva ॥ 13॥
gurukōpāruṇadāruṇaprasāritākṣamatīva durdarśam । trivalībhaṅgurabhālaṁ niṣṭhuradantāpradaṣṭauṣṭham ॥ 14॥

rāhaḍamaṁtikahā ।

tē samaṁ ciya paḍiya pahārasayajajjaraṁ dharḍapi taō । taṁ taha da maṁḍaliyavayaṇā khayarī bhaṇai rāyaṁ ॥ 15 ॥
ēsō maha pāṇapiō riuṇā vāvāiō na saṁdēhō । tā tassa viōē haṁ nō pāṇē dhāriḍaṁ sakkā ॥ 16 ॥
tā kāūna pasāyaṁ sigyaṁ maha dēhi bhāya ! dārūṇi । piyavirahadahaṇadaḍḍhaṁ dahēmi dēhaṁ puṇō jēṇa ||17||
tāhē rannā bhaṇiyaṁ bhagiṇī taṁ majjha tā imaṁ rajjaṁ । tuha saṁtiyaṁti maṁcasu pāṇaparicāyabuddhipi ॥ 18 ॥
tō
puga bhaṇiyaṁ tīra ēvaṁ citra ittha tumha baṁdhuca । jaṁ iḍavirahadukkhiyamaṇā mē dēsi kahāṇi ॥ 19 ॥
puṇaravi vahuppayāraṁ bhaṇiyā rannā na juttamiya kāuṁ । appāṇammivi pīḍā bihiṇā vihiyā havai suhayā ||
dharasu mahavyayabhāraṁ hāraṁ sivaramaṇimaṇaharanuyāraṁ । jiṇasu kasāē siddhaṁtajāvaō suhanihipisāē ॥ 21 ॥
parihara kudiddhisēvaṁ dēvaṁ mannētu vigayarāgamalaṁ । samatiṇamaṇiṇō muṇiṇō guruṇō, jīvāitattāī ||22||
iya bhaṇiyāvi na mannai vayaṇaṁ puhaīsarasta sā khayarī । khayaraguṇē uccariḍaṁ puṇō puṇō ruyai tō rannā ||23||
dāvāviāī tīsē caṁdaṇakaṭṭhāī viraiūṇa ciyaṁ । aha sā khaparī niyapagattāī jhatti ghittr̥ṇaṁ ॥ 24 ॥
huyahajālaciyā ciyāē sā tīē jā kira paviṭṭhā | tō kurucaṁdanarāhivapuraō sō āgaō khayarō |
karakaliyapharayakhaggō naranāhaṁ pagamiūṇa vinnavai । pahu ! paranārisahōyaramatthaya cūḍāmaṇi ! nariṁda ! |
tujjha pahāvēṇa maē nihaō sattū gariṭṭhabalakaliō । saraṇāgayajaṇavacchala ! maha daiyaṁ mē samappēsu ॥
saṁpai niyanayara para gacchissaṁ jēṇa jaṇamaṇāṇaṁda ! | āṇānidēsakarō ēsa jaṇō tujjha sayakālaṁ ||28||
tō khuhiō naranāhō cita kiṁ uttaraṁ payacchēmi । tō pakkhittā diṭṭhī rannā maṁtissa vayaṇammi ||29||--
tēna samamēva patitaṁ prahāraśatajarjaraṁ kabandhamapi tataḥ । tattathā dr̥ṣṭvā mukulitavadanā khacarī bhaṇati rājānam ॥ 15 ॥
ēṣa mama prāṇapriyō ripuṇā vyāpāditō na saṁdēhaḥ । tasmāttasya viyōgē'haṁ nō prāṇān dhārayituṁ śaktā ॥ 16 ॥
tasmāt kr̥tvā prasādaṁ śīghraṁ mama dēhi bhrātaḥ ! dārūṇi । priyavirahadahanadagdhaṁ dahāmi dēhaṁ punaryēna ॥ 17 ॥
tadā rājñā bhaṇitaṁ bhaginī tvaṁ mama tasmādidaṁ rājyam । tava satkamiti muñca prāṇaparityāgabuddhimapi ॥ 18॥
tataḥ punarbhaṇitaṁ tayaivamēvātra yuṣmākaṁ bandhutvam । yadiṣṭavirahaduḥkhitamanasō mē dadāsi kaṣṭāni ||19||
punarapi bahuprakāraṁ bhaṇitā rājñā na yuktamiti kartum । ātmanyapi pīḍā vidhinā vihitā bhavati sukhadā ॥ 20 ॥
dhara mahāvratabhāraṁ hāraṁ śivaramaṇīmanōharamudāram । jaya kaṣāyān siddhāntajāpataḥ sukhanidhipiśācān ॥21॥
parihara kudr̥ṣṭisēvāṁ dēvaṁ manyasva vigatarāgamalam । samatr̥ṇamaṇīn munīn gurūn, jīvāditattvāni ॥ 22 ॥
iti bhaṇitāpi na manyatē vacanaṁ pr̥thivīśvarasya sā khacarī । khacaraguṇānuccārya punaḥ punā rōditi tatō rājñā ॥ 23॥
dāpitāni tasyai candanakāṣṭhāni viracayya citām । atha sā khacarī nijapatigātrāṇi jhaṭiti gr̥hītvā ॥24॥
hutavahajvālācitāyāṁ citāyāṁ sā tasyāṁ yāvatkila praviṣṭā । tataḥ kurucandranarādhipapurataḥ sa āgataḥ khacaraḥ ॥
karakalitapharakakhaṅgō naranārthaṁ praṇamya vijñapayati । prabhō ! paranārīsahōdaramastakacūḍāmaṇē ! narēndra ! ॥26॥
tava prabhāvēṇa mayā nihataḥ śatrurgariṣṭhabalakalitaḥ । śaraṇāgatajanavatsala ! mama dayitāṁ mē samarpaya ॥ 27 ॥
saṁprati nijanagaraṁ prati gamiṣyāmi yēna janamanaānanda ! | ājñānirdēśakara ēṣa janastava sadākālam ||28||

tō maṁtiṇā jahaṭṭiyavr̥ttaṁtē sāhiē samaggēvi । tā kasiṇīkayavayaṇō khayarō vinnava naranāhaṁ ||30|
amayaṁpi visaṁ jāyaṁ caṁdōvi hu muyai jalaṇajālōli । māyaṁḍōvi hu payaḍai ahaha ! akaṁḍēvi tamapaḍalaṁ ।
tumhārisāvi jai paricayaṁti pāgayajaṇavva majjāyaṁ । tā nāha ! samuddēhivi nūṇamamuddēhiṁ hōyavvaṁ ॥ 32 ॥
ahamēsō paccakkhō sā maha aṁgāī paṇaiṇī ghēttuṁ । caḍiyā ciyāē, aliyaṁpi buccaē kiṁci ghaḍamāṇaṁ ||
।
aṁtēurēṇa chuhiūṇa maha piyaṁ bhaṇasi sāhiyaṁ jalaṇaṁ । jaṁ buccijjai si paranārisōyarō āyara si ēyaṁ ।
tā niyajasapasuraṁ tihuyapi ujjōyamāṇamimamēvaṁ । mā kuṇasu kalaṁkēḍaṁ tullaṁ caṁdrēṇa jayanāha ! ||35||
tā aṣpasu maha daiyaṁ kuṇasu dayaṁ jā tuṭṭai mahāsā । aha tuṭṭacciya āsā sahasēva gayaṁva pāṇēhiṁ ||36||
taṁ saccaṁ mannatō taddukkhaduhāulō naravariṁdō । kiṁkāyavyavimūḍhō chūḍhōvva jalatajalaṇammi ||37||
aikasiṇīkayavayaṇō ahōmuhō jā na kiṁpi paḍibhaṇai । tāva khayarō paryapai saccaciya sā mayā kiṁnu ? ॥
tahavi hu rāyā cigs niruttarō jāva khēya tāva | jaṁpai mayāvi ēsā jīvau tujjhapahāvēṇa ||39||
pabhaṇai āgaccha piē ! paraduhaduhiō suhaṁ lahau sāmī । iya bhaṇiē jāva nivō ūsasiō īsi tā sahasā ।।
uddāmamaddalālīkaṁsāliyatilimakaṁsiyahuḍukā । ḍakkābōkkāṇa vō viyabhiō rāyapaṁgaṇa ॥ 41 ॥
tammajjhaṭhiyā chaṁdānusāraō bhāvanivbharaṁ khayarī । puraō paṇaccamāṇī paṇamai naranāhapayakamalaṁ ॥ 42 ॥
tuha kō yatthamitthaṁ vihiyaṁ mē khayaraiṁdiyālēṇa । iya kahiuṁ naravaiṇō picchaṇayaṁ tēṇa pāraddhaṁ ॥43॥
tataḥ kṣubhitō naranāthaścintayati kimuttaraṁ prayacchāmi । tataḥ prakṣiptā dr̥ṣṭī rājñā mantriṇō vadanē ॥ 29 ॥
tatō mantriṇā yathāsthitavr̥ttāntē kathitē samagrē'pi । tataḥ kr̥ṣṇīkr̥tavadanaḥ khacarō vijñapayati naranātham ॥30॥
amr̥tamapi viṣaṁ jātaṁ candrō'pi khalu muñcati jvalanajvālālīm ।
mārtaṇḍōspi khalu prakaṭayatyahaha ! akāṇḍē'pi tamaḥpaṭalam ॥31॥
yuṣmādr̥śā api yadi parityajanti prākr̥tajanā iva maryādām । tadā nātha ! samudrairapi nūnamamudrērbhavitavyam ॥ 32॥
aimēṣa pratyakṣaḥ sā mamāṅgāni praṇayinī gr̥hītvā । caṭitā citāyām, alīkamapyucyatē kiñcid ghaṭamānam ||
antaḥpurē kṣiptvā mama priyāṁ bhaṇasi sādhitaṁ jvalanam । yaducyatē'si paranārīsahōdara ācarasyētat || 34॥
tasmānnijayaśaḥprasarēṇa tribhuvanamapyudyōtamānamidamēvam । mā kuru kalaṅkayitvā tulyaṁ candrēṇa jagannātha |||35||
tasmādarpaya mamaṁ dayitāṁ kuru dayāṁ yāvat truṭyati mamāśā । atha truṭitaivāśā sahasaiva gatamiva prāṇaiḥ ॥ 36॥
tat satyaṁ manyamānastadduḥkhaduḥkhākulō naravarēndraḥ । kiṁkartavyavimūḍhaḥ kṣipta iva jvalajjvalanē ॥37॥
atikr̥ṣṇīkr̥tavadanō'dhōmukhō yāvanna kimapi pratibhaṇati । tāvatkhacaraḥ prajalpati satyamēva sā mr̥tā kiṁnu ? |
tathāpi khala rājā tiṣṭhati niruttarō yāvatkhēcarastāvat । jalpati mr̥tāpyēṣā jīvatu tava prabhāvēṇa ||39||
prabhaṇatyāgaccha priyē ! paraduḥkhaduḥkhitaḥ sukhaṁ labhatāṁ svāmī । iti bhaṇitē yāvannr̥pa ucchūsita īpattāvatsahasā ॥
uddāmamardalālīkāṁsālikatilimakāṁsikahuḍukkānām । ḍakkābukkānāṁ ravō vijr̥mbhitō rājaprāṅgaṇakē ॥41॥
tanmadhyasthitā chandō'nusāratō bhāvanirbharaṁ khacarī । purataḥ pranr̥tyantī praṇamati naranāthapādakamalam ॥42॥
