tō rāyā puralōō maṁtiyaṇō maṁḍalīyamāīyā । vimyihiyayā jaṁpati ahaha ! acchariyamacchariyaṁ ॥44॥.
tō rāyā bhaṇai tayaṁ kiṁ khayara ! imaṁti kahasu sambhāvaṁ । na bhavāmi ahaṁ khayarō narapuṁgava ! iṁdiyālīō ||
iya jayaṁtē tēsiṁ sapariyaṇō naravaīvi tōsēṇa । savvaṁgiyamābharaṇaṁ kaḍagāī dēi, ittō ya ॥ 46 ॥
patthāvōti muṇittā sahasā gayaṇagaṇāō avayariō । cāraṇamuṇī mahappā caunāṇī tāṇa puṇṇēhiṁ ॥ 47॥
sapariggahō ya rāyā abhuṭṭāṇaṁ karēi paṇamai ya । uvaṇamiyaṁ sīhāsaṇamaha tattha muṇimmi uvavidvē ॥ 48 ॥
saṁvariyaṁ pēcchaṇayaṁ muṇiṇāvi ya dēsaṇā samāraddhā | saṁvēyavivēyakarī suṇaṁti savvē tamuvattā ||49||
tathāhi ;-
jaha ēsa iṁdiyālī daṁsai khaṇanassarāī ruvāī | taha kammasuttahārō suttai jīvāṇavatthāō ||50||
paḍhamaṁ ciya bālattaṁ tattō kumarattajuvvaṇattāī । tattō ya buḍḍhabhāvaṁ kayāi paṁcatta saṁpattī ॥ 51 ॥
hu
dēvapi kuṇai tiriyaṁ maṇuyaṁ vā,
tiriyaṁ maṇuyaṁ vā, māṇarvapi nēraiyaṁ । dēvaṁ vā maṇuyaṁ vā tiriyaṁ vā, tiriyamavi ēvaṁ ॥ 52 ॥
nēraiyaṁpi hu tiriyaṁ naraṁ ca, paṁcidiyapi ēgiṁdī । iya ghaḍaṇavihaḍaṇāhiṁ viṇaḍai bhruvaṇaṁ asēsaṁpi ॥53॥
bālatva kiṁpi karēi kuṭṭi jari khaī vāvi । kumaratēvi hu pattē gharā gharaṁ bhāmai bhikkhaṁ ॥ 54 ॥
juvvaṇavaṇammi pattaṁ ḍaṁsāvara duṭṭakāmasappēṇa । jaha appamavēyaṁtō paḍai sō duriyagattāē || 55 ||
valipaliyagaliyasōhaṁ kuṇai ya vuḍḍhattaṇassa samayammi । vaṁkīkayakāyalayaṁ hāsakaraṁ tucchataruṇīṇa ॥ 56 ॥
tō bhō savvajaṇāṇaṁ savvāvatthāsu natthi thēvaṁpi । suhamasuhaṁ puṇa dīsa paccakkhaṁ caiva jīvāṇa ॥ 57॥
taba kautukārthamitthaṁ vihitaṁ mayā khacarēndrajālēna । iti kathayitvā narapati prēkṣaṇakaṁ tēna prārabdham ॥ 43 ॥
tatō rājā puralōkō mantrijanō maṇḍalikādikāḥ । vismitahr̥dayā jalpanti ahaha ! āścaryamāścaryam ॥ 44 ॥
tatō rājā bhaṇati taṁ kiṁ khacara ! idamiti kathaya sadbhāvam । na bhavāmyahaṁ khacarō narapuṅgava । aindrajālikaḥ ॥
iti jalpatē tēṣāṁ saparijanō narapatirapi tōṣēṇa । sarvāṅgīṇamābharaṇaṁ kaṭakāni dadāti itaśca ॥ 46 ॥
prastāva iti jñātvā sahasā gaganāṅgaṇādavatīrṇaḥ । cāraṇamunirmahātmā caturjñānastēṣāṁ puṇyaiḥ ॥47॥
saparigrahaśca rājā'bhyutthānaṁ karōti praṇamati ca । upanamitaṁ siṁhāsanamatha tatra munāvupaviṣṭē ॥48॥
saṁvr̥taṁ prēkṣaṇakaṁ munināpi ca dēśanā samārabdhā । saṁvēgavivēkakarī śr̥ṇvanti sarvē tāmupayuktāḥ ||49||
yaṁthaiṣa indrajālī darśayati kṣaṇanaśvarāṇi rūpāṇi । tathā karmasūtradhāraḥ sūtrayati jīvānāmavasthāḥ ||10||
prathamamēva bālatvaṁ tataḥ kumāratvayauvanē । tataśca vr̥ddhabhāvaṁ kadācitpañcatvasaṁpattiḥ ॥51॥
,
dēvamapi karōti tiryañcaṁ manujaṁ vā, mānavamapi nairayikam । dēvaṁ vā manujaṁ vā tiryañcaṁ vā, tiryañcamadhyēvam ॥
nairayikamapica tiryañca naraṁ ca pañcēndriyamapyēkēndriyam । iti ghaṭanavighaṭanābhyāṁ vinaṭati bhuvanamaśēṣamapi ॥
bālatvē'pi kamapi khalu karōti kuṣṭhinaṁ jvariṇaṁ kṣayiṇaṁ vāpi । kumāratvē'pi hi prāptē gr̥hād gr̥haṁ bhramayati bhikṣām ||
yauvanavanē prāptaṁ daṁśayati duṣṭakāmasarpaṇa । yathā''tmānamavidan patati sa duritagartē ॥55॥
valipalitagalitaśōbhaṁ karōti ca vr̥ddhatvasya samayē । vatrīkr̥takāyalataṁ hāsyakaraṁ tucchataruṇīnām ॥ 56॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
1
sā kammakkhaḍampi jayaha jiṇadēsiyam dhammammi । jēṇa kayatthaṇatraṇadutthavajjiyaṁ lahaha siddhattaṁ ॥ 58 ॥
sō puṇa jīvadayacciya sēsā saccāiyā baī tassā । taṁ savvaōvi kāuṁ asamatyō kuṇai dēsēṇa ॥ 59 ॥
aha paṇamiūṇa vinnava naravarō rāhaḍō taha apraccō । puvvapurisakamēṇavi sammattaṁ aha pahu ! asthi ||
pāṇāvāyaviraiṁpa dēsaō dēha amha pasiūṇa । bhaṇai suṇī hōu imaṁ kiṁpuṇa ēē ihaiyārā || 61 ||
baṁdhavahaṁ chavicchēyaṁ aibhāraṁ bhattapāṇavōcchēyaṁ । duṭṭamaṇaēhi ēē vajjēyavvā payatēṇa ||62 ||
tō vihiṇā paḍivannaṁ paḍhamavayaṁ nivamacaṭṭhēhiṁ । avarēhivi avarāī vīyavayāīṇi gahiyāṇi ॥ 63॥
tō muṇivarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ gacchāmō patthuyammi kajjammi । paḍivanavayavisēsē visēsaō ujjamēyavvaṁ ॥ 64॥
iya bhaṇijaṁ uppaiō tamāladalasāmalammi gayaṇammi । rāyāvi kuṇai dhammaṁ rajjadhuraṁ rāhaḍē ṭhaviḍaṁ ॥65॥
tō rāhaḍōva ēkē ṭhāvēi payammi maṁḍalīyāṇa । annāṇa payasaṁ karēi niyayāē icchāē ॥66॥
ēvaṁ ca vaṭṭamāṇō diṇē diṇē caḍai garupa abhimāṇē । thēvēvi hu avarāhē aigarūyaṁ kuṇai sō daṁḍa || 67॥
kēsipi hu karacaraṇē annēsiṁ puṇa saunāsauḍē । anēsi kappāvara nikaruṇō mūlaō kanē || 68 ||
uppāḍāvara nayaṇē dasaṇē pāḍāvaē ya annēsiṁ । kēsiṁ ca sayāsāō giṇhāvara ugadaṁḍē sō || 69 ||
vasaṇacchēyaṁ kāra jinyaṁ kappāvaē ya annēsiṁ । ēvaṁ ca rasē caḍiō avarāhavivajjiyāpi ॥ 70 ॥
ārōviḍaṁ alīyaṁ avarāhaṁ niyadhaṇaṁ aditāṇa । annēsiṁ bhayahēu kappāvara aṁguraṁgāī ॥ 71 ॥
tatō mōḥ sarvajanānāṁ sarvāvasthāsu nāsti stōkamapi । sukhamasukhaṁ punardr̥śyatē pratyakṣamēva jīvānām ॥57॥
tasmāt karmakṣayahētau yatadhvaṁ jinadēśitē dharmē । yēna kadarthanaghanadauḥsthyavarjitaṁ labhadhvaṁ siddhatvam ॥18॥
sa punarjīvadayaiva śēṣāḥ satyādikā vistarastasyāḥ । tāṁ sarvatō'pi kartumasamarthaḥ karōti dēśēna || 59॥
atha praṇamya vijñapayati naravarō rāhaḍastathā'martyaḥ । pūrvapuruṣakramēṇāpi samyaktvamāvayōḥ prabhō ! asti ॥ 60 ॥
prāṇātipātaviratimapi dēśatō dēkhāvayōḥ prasadya । bhaṇati munirbhavatvidaṁ kintvēta ihāticārāḥ ॥ 61 ॥
bandhavadhaṁ ṣaḍvicchēdō'tibhārō bhaktapānatryucchēdam । duṣṭamanōbhirētē varjayitavyāḥ prayatnēna ॥ 62 ॥
tatō vidhinā pratipannaṁ prathamavrataṁ nr̥pāmartyaśrāddhaiḥ । aparairapyaparāṇi dvitīyatratādīni gr̥hītāni ॥63॥
tatō munivarēṇa bhaṇitaṁ gacchāmaḥ prastutē kāryē । pratipannatrataviśēṣē viśēṣata udyantatryam ||64 ||
iti bhaṇitvōtpatitastamāladalaśyāmalē gaganē । rājāpi karōti dharma rājyadhurāṁ rāhaḍē sthāpayitvā ॥ 65 ॥
tatō rāhaḍō'pyēkānū sthāpayati padē maṇḍalikānām । anyēṣāṁ padabhraṁśaṁ karōti nijayēcchayā ।। 66 ॥
ēvaṁ ca vartamānō dinē dinē caṭati gurvabhimānē । stōkē'pi khalvaparādhē'tiguruṁ karōti sa daṇḍam ॥ 67 ॥
kēṣāmapi khalu karacaraṇānanyēṣāṁ punaḥ sauṣṭhanāsāpuṭam । anyēṣāṁ chēdayati niṣkaruṇō mūlataḥ karṇān ॥ 68 ॥
utpāṭayati nayanāni daśanān pāṭayati cānyēṣām । kēṣāṁ ca sakāśād grāhayatyugradaṇḍān saḥ ॥ 69 ॥
1
vasanacchēdaṁ kārayati jihvāṁ chēdayati cānyēṣām । ēvaṁ ca rasē cāṭatō'parādhavivarjitānāmapi ॥ 70 ॥
ārōpyālīkamaparādhaṁ nijadhanamadadatām । anyēṣāṁ bhayahētōśchēdayatyaṅgōpāṅgāni ॥71॥

ēvaṁ ca kutō sō lōyāṇaṁ jāṇiūṇa naravaiṇā । bhaṇiō rāhaḍamaṁtī mā kuṇa ii dāruṇaṁ pāvaṁ ।। 72 ।।
● jāṇatāṇa assaṁ vayassa bhaṁgō na ēttha aiyārō । sō hōi aṇābhōgāikāraṇā tō tayaṁ cayaha ॥73॥
hālāhala visapiyaṇaṁ varaṁ khu churiyāē haṇaṇamuyarasta । pavvayasiharāu varaṁ appā mukō nirālaṁbō ||74॥

।।
labdhaṁti vivimaṇikaṇayarayaṇabhavaṇōvabhōyasaṁjuttā । riddhivisēsā na uṇō kapi dhammō dayārūvō || 76॥

tattō vi hu uvvaṭṭō bhami saṁsārasāyarē ghōrē । ladhuṁ puṇōvi dhammaṁ anaṁtasammaṁ sivaṁ lahihī ॥ 79 ॥

tattō avaravidēhē hōūṇa kayaṁgalāē naranāhō । pattō nivvāṇasuhaṁ pajjaṁtē laddhajidikkhō ॥ 81 ॥
vayaaiyārō dukkhāṇa kāraṇaṁ vajjaṇaṁ tu puṇa tassa । avilaṁvēṇaṁ sivasuhajaṇayaṁ tā cayaha ēyaṁpi ॥ 82 ॥
॥ iti prāṇātipātatr̥tīyāticārē rāhaḍamantrikathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
ēvaṁ ca kurvan sa lōkānāṁ jñātvā narapatinā । bhaṇitō rāhaḍamantrī mā kurviti dāruṇaṁ pāpam ॥72॥
jānatāmavaśyaṁ vratasya bhaṅgō nātrāticāraḥ । sa bhavatyanābhōgādikāraṇāt tatastaṁ tyaja ॥ 73 ॥
hālāhalāviṣapānaṁ varaṁ khalu kṣurikayā hananamudarasya । parvataśikharād varamātmā muktō nirālambaḥ ॥74॥
jvālājālakarālē jvalanē varaṁ viśēd niviśēta । khaṅgōgradhārōpari na punarpraśēta nijaniyamam ॥79॥ .
labhyantē vividhamaṇikanakaratna bhavanōpabhōgasaṁyuktāḥ । r̥ddhiviśēṣā na punaḥ kathamapi dharmō dayārūpaḥ ॥76॥

tatō'pi khadvr̥ttō bhrāntvā saṁsārasāgarē ghōrē । labdhvā punarapi dharmamanantaśarma śivaṁ lapsyatē ॥ 79 ॥
kurucandrō'pi khalu rājā paryantē'naśanaṁ vidhāya । prāptasamādhimaraṇaḥ saudharmē suravarō jātaḥ ॥80॥

vratāticārō duḥkhānāṁ kāraṇaṁ varjanaṁ tu punastasya । avilambēna śivasukhajanakaṁ tasmāttyajataitam ॥82॥

nikaruṇō jō jīvē abhārārōvaṇēṇa pīḍēi । sō iha pēccabhavēmuvi sulasō iva lahai dukhāī ॥ | 1 ||
tathāhi;-
1
nibhavaṇapavaranāhi uyārapāyāranēmipariyariyaṁ । bharaharahacakabhūyaṁ nagaraṁ nāmēṇa cakapuraṁ ||2||
tami raṇaraṁgamallō rāyā niścapi cāyadullaliō । līlāvilāsakaliyā laliyā nāmēṇa tassa piyā ||
tatthathi susasēṭṭī nivapuradiṭṭhī sayā ahammiṭṭī । ainiviḍamicchadiṭṭī gayatuṭṭī kamaladaladiṭṭhī ॥4॥
savvaisuvi kajjēsuṁ naravaṇō niyamaṇava nibbhiccō । bhiccō mittaṁ maṁtī samagaṁ ciya suyai bhujai ya ॥5॥
aha annayā nariṁdō atthāṇasahāē ciṭṭhaē jāva । tā purapavarō lōō sāhulihatthō tarhi pattō || 6 ||
sāhasiēṇa kēṇavi ā chammāsāu paṭṭaṇaṁ ēyaṁ । jagataṁpi musijjai sāmiya ! pāēṇa pairayaṇi ॥ 7॥
kassavi bhajjā vararuvasāliṇī kannagā u annassa । rayaṇakaṇayāiyāṇaṁ saṁkhāvi na tēṇa hariyāṇa ॥8॥
tō ārakairaṇaṁ niyai nivō bhaṇai paṇamiḍaṁ sōvi । savvaṁciya saccamiṇaṁ jaṁ jaṁpara purajaṇō dēva !॥9॥
tā kiṁ agōyarō tujjha takarō naravarēṇa iya bhaṇiē । sō bhaṇai dēva ! ēyaṁ kimannahā amuvikkhēmi ? ||
gayaṇēṇaṁ āgaṁtu bahujaṇauppāḍaṇijjamavi vatyuṁ । ēmāgīvi hu ghēttuṁ gaccha sō jhatti uppaiḍaṁ ||11||
iya ēvaṁ bhaṇatammi tammi kēṇāvi bhaṇiyamajjēva । taṁ giṇhasu iya sōuṁ rāyā paribhāvaē ēvaṁ || 12॥
divvā bhāsā ēsā na annahā hōi tā ahaṁ nūṇaṁ । kayaujjamō lahissaṁ ajaṁ ciya taṁ mahācōraṁ ॥ 13 ॥
bhai ya purapahāṇē niyadutthaṁ majjha parikahaṁtēhiṁ । kāyavvaṁ kayamittō maha ciṁtā ittha kajjammi || 14 ||
।
niṣkaruṇō yō jīvānatibhārārōpaṇēna pīḍayati । sa iha prētyabhavēṣvapi sulama iva labhatē duḥkhāni ॥1॥
nr̥pabhavanapravaranābhi udāraprākāranēmiparikaritam । bharatarathacakrabhūtaṁ nagaraṁ nāmnā cakrapuram ॥2॥
tasmin raṇaraṅgamallō rājā nityamapi tyāgadurlalitaḥ । līlāvilāsakalitā lalitā nāmnā tasya priyā ॥ 3 ॥
tatrāsti sulasaśrēṣṭhī nr̥papuradr̥ṣṭiḥ sadā'dharmēṣṭiḥ । atinibiḍamithyādr̥ṣṭirgata tuṣṭiḥ kamaladaladr̥ṣṭiḥ || 4 ॥
sarvēṣvapi kāryēṣu narapatērnijamana iva nirbhr̥tyaḥ । bhr̥tyō mitraṁ mantrī samakamēva svapiti bhuṅktē ca ॥5॥
athānyadā narēndra āsthānasabhāyāṁ tiṣṭhati yāvat । tāvatpurapravarō lōkō vastrahastastatra prāptaḥ || 6 ||
sāhasikēna kēnāpyā ṣaṇmāsāt pattanamētat । jāgradapi muṣyatē svāmin ! prāyēṇa pratirajani ||7||
kasyāpi bhāryā vararūpaśālinī kanyakā tvanyasya । ratnakanakādikānāṁ saṁkhyāpi na tēna hr̥tānām ||8||
tata ārakṣikavadanaṁ paśyati nr̥pō bhaṇati praṇamya sō'pi । sarvamēva satyamidaṁ yajjalpati purajanō dēva ! ॥9॥
tadā kimagōcarastava taskarō naravarēṇēti bhaṇitē । sa bhaṇati dēva । ētaṁ kimanyathā'hamupēkṣē ? || 10 |
gaganēnāgatya bahujanōtpāṭanīyamapi vastu । ēkākyapi khalu gr̥hītvā gacchati sa jhaṭityutpatya ॥ 11 ॥
ityēvaṁ prabhaṇati tasmin kēnāpi bhaṇitamadyaiva । taṁ gr̥hāṇēti śrutvā rājā paribhāvayatyēvam ॥ 12॥
divyā bhāṣaiṣā nānyathā bhavati tasmādahaṁ nūnam । kr̥tōdyamō lapsyē'dyaiva taṁ mahācauram ||13||

sulasasiṭṭhikahā ।
247
iya bhaṇiuṁ sammāṇiya visajjaē naravarō nayaralōyaṁ । citai ya divvavayaṇaṁ 'ajjaṁ ciya giṇhasu' taō ya ।।
paccāsaṇē nūṇaṁ hōyavvaṁ tassa saṁnivēsēṇaṁ । vaṁciya pariyaṇamittō nisi nīsariō asisahāō ||16||
tō maṇasīkaya uttaradisissa sē jhatti bhairavā vāmā । kilakiliyā maggēṇaṁ tēṇaṁ ciya tō payaṭṭō sō ॥ 17 ॥
aha jā gāuyadugaṁ gaṁtuṁ vaḍaviḍaviṇō ṭhiō hiṭṭā । tō katthūriyavaṇasāraparimalō tassa nāsā ॥ 18 ॥
tassa paviṭṭhō tō tayaṇusāraō kōttharaṁ palōēi । jā tāva tammi nisuṇai ālāvē vivihabhaṁgīhiṁ ॥ 19॥
ramaṇīṇaṁ suisuhaē,
vaccatō tayaṇusāraō tattō । pēcchai varapāsāyaṁ rayaṇujjōiya disāvalayaṁ ॥ 20॥
tassaṁ bhavaṇassa dārammi pavisamāṇēṇa rāiṇā diṭṭhā। ēgā pavarā taruṇī viyaḍaniyaṁbā visālacchī ॥
āharaṇamaṇimaūhōharaṁjiyā jiyaaṇaṁgapāṇapiyā । sīivi diṭṭhō rāyā nayaṇāṇa mahūsavaṁ ditō ||22||
nijjiyaaṇaṁgarūvaṁ rāyaṁ daṭṭūṇa tattha sā juvaī । cittalihiyavva niru thaṁbhiyavva thakkā khaṇaṁ ēkaṁ ॥ 23 ॥
tō kicchēṇaṁ kahakahavi tīē vayaṇāō niggayā vāyā । hā ramaṇilōyaṇāṇaṁda ! kattha taṁ āgaō ittha ? |
tā gaccha gaccha turiyaṁ jāva na ajjavi sa ēi pāviṭṭhō । jassa imō pāsāō dinavisāō ya amhāṇaṁ ॥
raṇaraṁgamalarāyā pucchara taṁ bāliyaṁ imaṁ bhavaṇaṁ । kassa taṇayaṁ sa kō vā ciṭṭhā kaha saṁpayaṁ kahasu ? || 26॥
ēyāō kassa va saṁtiyā navajōvvaṇāu ramaṇīō । ēkkāō karuṇasaraṁ gāyaṁti rūyaṁti annāō ? ||27||
bhaṇiyaṁ tīē ēyaṁ pāyālagihaṁ bhaṇijjaē suhaya ! । ēyassa sāmiō puṇa piṁgacchō nāma cōrutti ॥ 28॥
3
bhaṇati ca purapradhānāni nijadausthyaṁ māṁ parikathayadbhiḥ । kartavyaṁ kr̥tamitō mama cintātra kāryē ॥14॥
iti bhaṇitvā samānya visr̥jati naravarō nagaralōkam । cintayati ca divyavacanaṁ 'adyaiva gr̥hāṇa' tataśca ॥ 15 ॥
pratyāsannē nūnaṁ bhavitavyaṁ tasya saṁnivēśēna । cañcayitvā parijanamitō niśi niḥsr̥tō'si sahāyaḥ ॥ 16 ॥
tatō manasikr̥tōttaradiśastasya jhaṭiti bhairavī vāmā | kilakilitā mārgēṇa tainēva tataḥ pravr̥ttaḥ saḥ ॥17॥
atha yāvatkrōśadvikaṁ gatvā vaṭaviṭapinaḥ sthitō'vaḥ । tataḥ kastūrikāghanasāraparimalastasya nāsāyām ॥ 18॥
tasya praviṣṭastatastadanusārataḥ kōṭaraṁ pralōkayati । yāvat tāvattasmin śr̥ṇōtyālāpān vividhabhaṅgibhiḥ || 19||
ramaṇīnāṁ śrutisukhadān, bajaṁstadanusāratastataḥ । paśyati varaprasādaṁ ratnōdyōtitadigvalayam ॥20॥
tasya bhavanasya dvārē praviśatā rājñā dr̥ṣṭā । ēkā pravarā taruṇī vitatanitambā viśālākṣī || 21॥
ābharaṇamaṇimayūkhaugharañjitā jitānaṅgaprāṇapriyā । tayāpi dr̥ṣṭō rājā nayanayōmahōtsava dadat ॥22॥
nirjitānaṅgarūpaṁ rājānaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā tatra sā yuvatiḥ । citralikhitēva niścitaṁ stambhitēva sthitā kṣaṇamēkam ॥ 23 ॥
tataḥ kr̥cchrēṇa kathaṁkathamapi tasyā vadanād nirgatā vākū । hā ramaṇīlōcanānanda ! kvatvamāgatō'tra ? ||24||
tasmād gaccha gaccha tvaritaṁ yāvannādyāpi sa ēti pāpiṣṭhaḥ । yasyāyaṁ prāsādō dattaviṣādaścāsmākam ॥ 25 ॥
raṇaraṅgamallarājaḥ pr̥cchati tāṁ bālikāmidaṁ bhavanam । kasya saṁbandhi sa kō vā tiṣṭhati kathaṁ sāṁprataṁ kathaya ? ॥
ētāḥ kasya vā satkā navayauvanā ramaṇyaḥ । ēkāḥ karuṇasvaraṁ gāyanti rudantyanyāḥ ? ||27||
bhaṇitaṁ tayaitat pātālagr̥haṁ bhaṇyatē subhaga ! । ētasya svāmī punaḥ piṅgākṣō nāma caura iti ॥28॥

supāsanāha-cariammi-
sōvi aīva paḍō dujjēō khēparāsurāṇaṁpi । niyabhuyavalēṇa musiūṇa āṇa pavaravatthūṇi ॥ 29 ॥
taha jāu jāu ramayaṁti niyamaṇaṁ tāu tāu ramaṇīō । āūṇaṁ milai ihaī pāyālabhavaṇammi ||30 ॥
ciṭṭha saṁtāvitō juvaijaṇaṁ diṇamaṇimmi uiyammi | rāīē puṇa vāhi nīhariuṁ musaī paralōyaṁ ॥ 31 ॥
tammiya bāhimmi gaē jai katthai jāi kāi nīhariuṁ । taṁ tattha gayaṁ jāṇai tattō āṇai viḍaṁbai ya ॥
tō cita puhaivaī ēsō sō jēṇa paṭṭaṇaṁ musiyaṁ । mahataṇayaṁ, tā inhi picchāmi imassa māha ||33||
iya ēvaṁ ciṁtaṁtassa tassa tatthēva thēvavēlāē । sō piṁgacchō cōrō samāgaō khaggaggakarō ||34||
raṇaraṁgamalarāyassa aggamahisiṁ mahaṁtasadēṇa । pukāritaṁ khaggaṁ uggīriya bhāyamāṇō ya ||35||
aha sahasā naravaiṇā sō cōrō hakkiuṁ imaṁ bhaṇiō | rē purisāhama ! khaggaṁ uggīrasi uvari itthīṇaṁ ? ॥
The jāsi inhi rāyaviruddhāī karivi kammāī । mōttuṁ imaṁ palāyasu aha sajjō hōsu jujjhami ||37||
iya tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇa ciṁtiyaṁ tēṇa purisacōrēṇa । ērisaaigr̥hagi kahamitya samāgaō ēsō ? ॥38॥
aha tēṇa nivō bhaṇiō pāva ! paviṭṭō mamāvarōhammi । kēṇavi kiṁ dukkhēṇaṁ nicinnō jīviyāsāē ? ॥ 39 ॥
majjha karavāladhārā jala titthē nivvavēsi appāṇaṁ । kiṁ kuviō kayaṁtō dēi cavēḍaṁ kavōlammi 1 ॥40॥
tā tuha ajja kō kuviō nahu ittha niggamōvāō । sūyārasālapaḍiō sasauvva tumaṁ viṇassihasi ।।
tō bhaṇiō sō rannā cōrō bhaṇiūṇa majjha taṁ vajjhō । taṁ vivarīyaṁ jāyaṁ sasaēhiṁvi lauḍayā gahiyā ||
sō'pyatīva pracaṇḍō durjēyaḥ khēcarāsurāṇāmapi । nijabhujabalēna muṣitvā''nayati pravaravastūni ॥ 29 ॥
tathā yā yā ramayanti nijamanastāstā ramaṇīḥ । ānīya muñcatīha pātālabhavanē ||30||
tiṣṭhati saṁtāpayan yuvatijanaṁ dinamaṇāvuditē । rātrau punarbahirniḥsr̥tya muṣṇāti puralōkam ॥31॥
- tasmiṁśca bahirgatē yadi kvacidyāti kācinniḥsr̥tya । tāṁ tatra gatāṁ jānāti tata ānayati viḍambayati ca ॥ 32॥
tataścintayati pr̥thivīpatirēṣa sa yēna pattanaṁ muṣitam । madīyaṁ tasmādidānīṁ paśyāmyasya māhātmyam ॥33॥
ityēvaṁ cintayatastasya tatraiva stōkavēlayā । sa piṅgākṣaścauraḥ samāgataḥ khaḍgavargakaraḥ ||34||
raṇaraṅgamallarājasyāgramahiṣīṁ mahāśabdēna । pūtkurvantīṁ khaḍgamudīrya bhēṣayaṁśca ॥ 35॥
atha sahasā narapatinā sa caurō hakkavitvēdaṁ bhaṇitaḥ | rē puruṣādhama ! khaḍgamudguṇāsyupari strīṇām ? |
tasmāt ka yāsīdānīṁ rājaviruddhāni kr̥tvā karmāṇi । muktvēmāṁ palāyasvātha sajjī bhava yuddhē ||37||
iti tadvacanaṁ śrutvā cintitaṁ tēna puruṣacaurēṇa । īdr̥śātigūḍhagr̥hē kathamatra samāgata ēṣaḥ ? ॥ 38 ॥
atha tēna nr̥pō bhaṇitaḥ pāpa ! praviṣṭō mamāvarōdhē । kēnāpi kiṁ duḥkhēna nirviṇṇō jīvitāśāyām ||39||
mama karavāladhārājalatīrthē nirvāpayasyātmānam । kiṁvā kupitaḥ kr̥tāntō dadāti capēṭāṁ kapōlē ? ॥40॥
tasmāttatvādya kr̥tāntaḥ kupitō naivātra nirgamōpāyaḥ । sūdakāraśālāpatitaḥ śaśaka iva tvaṁ vinaṅkṣyasi॥41॥
tatō bhaṇitaḥ sa rājñā caurō bhaṇitvā mama tvaṁ vadhyaḥ । tadviparītaṁ jātaṁ śaśakairapi lakuṭikā gr̥hītā ॥ 42 ॥

tō taṁ rannō vayaṇa sōuṁ kōvānalēja pajjaliō । sō piṁgacchō cōrō pahāviō rāyasaṁmuhaō || 43 ॥
aruṇaṁ tēvi liō tikkhakhaggaguruvāō । rāyāvi dakkhayāē taṁ vaṁciya gēhiya vāhā ॥ 44॥
uhālē khaggaṁ pāyapahārēṇa pāḍivi dharāē । taṁ pacchāmuhavāhaṁ baṁdhai takaṇayasuttēṇa ॥ 45 ॥
aha taṁ dahuṁ cōraṁ baddhaṁ savvāu tāu ramaṇīō । harisabharanivbharubbhinnavahalapulayāō jāyāō || 46 ||
saṁti vivibhāvē vidyārabahulāō kāmanaḍiyāō । gāḍhaṁpi hu dhammilla chōḍēvi puṇōvi baṁdhati ||47 ||
tō savvivikāmiṇa maṇi harisiya, naṁ niyavallahamilaṇuka risiya ।
pararamaṇīyaṇavihuṇiya rāyaha, daṁsahiṁ nēharasōkaru rāyaha ॥ 48 ॥
raatūṇa tāō dēvaṁ ālavara jāva kira rāyā । tō āyannai hayahisiyāī gayagajjiyāī ca ॥ 49 ॥
taṁ sōuṁ naranāhō savimhaō ṭhāi bhāi tō dēvī । āṇijjaṁtīē maē aṇēgahā palaviyaṁ maggē ॥50॥
vikkhiriyāī taha muttiyāī muddā ya rayaṇarujhāō । tō tēhiṁ ciṁdhēhiṁ maha aṇumaggēṇa tumha balaṁ ॥ 51 ॥
āgayamēyaṁ manē tuhavirahadavānalēṇa ujjhataṁ । nivvāvijjau turiyaṁ niyasaṁgama amaya sēēṇa ||52 ||
tō tāō ramaṇīō aggē kāuṁ tava dēvi ca । taha gahiyabaddhacōrō kamaō nīharai naranāhō ॥53॥
askuttharadāra viṇiggayāu aha daṭuṁ tāō ramaṇīō । jaṁpaṁti maṁtipamuhā kimimā pāyāla kannāō ||54॥
kiṁvā suraṁgaṇāō pāyālē pāsiūṇa kayacōjjā । niggacchati imāō, ēvaṁ jaṁpati jā tāva ॥55॥
tatastadrājñō vacanaṁ śrutvā kōpānalēna prajvalitaḥ । sa piṅgākṣadharaḥ pradhāvitō rājasaṁmukhataḥ ॥43॥
atiruṣṭēna tēnāpi ghaṭitastīkṣṇasvagaguruvātaḥ । rājāpi dakṣatayā taṁ vañcayitvā gr̥hītvā bāhau ॥ 44 ॥
uddālaya khaṅgaṁ pādaprahārēṇa pātayitvā dharāyām । taṁ paścānmukhabāhuṁ badhnāti tatkanakasūtrēṇa ॥ 45 ॥
atha taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā cauraṁ baddhaṁ sarvāsta ramaṇyaḥ । harṣabharanirbharōdbhinnabahala pulakā jātāḥ ॥ 46 ॥
darśayanti vividhabhāvān vikārabahulāḥ kāmanaṭitāḥ । gāḍhamapi khalu dhammillaṁ chōṭayitvā punarapi badhnanti ॥
tataḥ sarvā api kāminyō manasi harṣitāḥ, nanu nijavallabhamēlanōtkarṣitāḥ ।
pararamaṇījanavidhunitaṁ rājānaṁ darśayantyaḥ snēharasōtkaraṁ rājantē ॥ 48 ॥
avadhīrya tā dēvīmālapati yāvatkila rājā । tata ākarṇayati hayahēṣitāni gajagarjitāni ca ॥49॥
tat śrutvā naranāthaḥ savismayastiṣṭhati bhaṇati tatō dēvī । ānīyamānayā mayā'nēkadhā pralapitaṁ mārgē ॥ 5 ॥
vikīrṇāni tathā mauktikāni mudrāśca ratnarucirāḥ । tatastaiścidvairmamānumārgēṇa yuṣmākaṁ balam ॥51॥
āgatamētad manyē tvadviradavānalēna dayamānam । nirvāpyatāṁ tvaritaṁ nijasaṁgamāmr̥ta sēkēna ॥52॥
tatastā ramaṇīragrē kr̥tvā tathaiva dēvīṁ ca । tathā gr̥hītabaddhacauraḥ kramatō niḥsarati naranāthaḥ ||13||
vaṭakōṭaradvāravinirgatā atha dr̥ṣṭvā tā ramaṇīḥ । jalpanti mantripramukhāḥ kimimāḥ pātālakanyāḥ 1 ॥ 54 ॥
kiṁvā surāṅganāḥ pātālaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā kr̥tāścaryāḥ । nirgacchantīmāḥ, ēvaṁ jalpanti yāvattāvat ॥ 55॥

nahariō naranāhō harivva girikaṁdarāō dararahiō । dadūṇa haṭṭhā tē taṁ paṇamaṁti dēvi ca ॥ 56 ॥
bhaṇaṁti nāha ! dēvīharaṇaṁ nāūṇa tumha pathamūlaṁ । jā aṇusarimō tā nēya picchima dēvapāēvi ॥57॥
dēvīē avaharaṇaṁ vīsariyaṁ tō adaṁsaṇē tumha । kiṁkāyantravimūḍhā jā ciṭṭhāmō giyaciṭṭhā ||18||
ārakkhiṇa tattō āgaṁtuṁ sāhiyaṁ jahuttaraō । kēṇavi gayaṇacarēṇa nijjai dēvī palavāṇā ॥ 59 ॥

tō tēsi naravaṇā niyaniggamaṇāra tāṇa milaṇaṁtaṁ । kahiūṇaṁ vr̥ttaṁtaṁ bhaṇiō tulasī jahā tumhē || 6 3
jō jāṇijjai sāmī jassa, samappēha tassa taṁ savvaṁ । bhūmigiṭṭiyavatthaṁ sē millēha bhaṁḍārē ॥ 64 ॥ ॥
ēyāō vāliyāō niyaniyagēhēsu jaha pahuppaṁti । taha kuṇaha, taō maṁtī tassāēsaṁ lahuṁ kuṇaḥ || 65 ||
karikhaṁdhasamārūḍhō nayarābhimuhaṁ taō nivō caliō । cōrōvi aṁgarakkhāṇa apiḍaṁ cāliō samagaṁ ॥ .
maggē gacchaṁtēṇaṁ jaganaṁ daṇakēvalī kêṇayakamalē । aivilē ubaviṭṭō diṭṭhō dhammaṁ payāsatō ||67 ||
hatthīōōyariḍaṁ pattō muṇipāya paṁkayassaṁtē । ti pakkhiṇīkarē baṁdara rāyaḥ vi varavihiṇā || 68 ||
sāmaṁtāī lōō sōhu paṇamiūṇa uvavihō । cōrōvi vinavāva naranāhamapi muṇināhaṁ ॥ 69 ॥
I
niḥsr̥tō naranāthō haririva girikandarātō dararahitaḥ । dr̥ṣṭvā hr̥ṣṭatuṣṭāstē taṁ praṇamanti dēvīṁ ca ॥ 56 ॥
prabhaṇanti nātha ! dēvīharaṇaṁ jñātvā yuṣmākaṁ pādamūlam । yāvadanusarāmastāvannaiva paśyāmō dēvapādānapi ॥ 17 ॥
dēvyā apaharaṇaṁ vismr̥taṁ tatō'darśanē yuṣmākam । kiṁkartavyavimūḍhā yāvattiṣṭhāmō vigatacēṣṭāḥ || 58 ॥
ārakṣikēṇa tata āgatya kathitaṁ yathōttarataḥ । kēnāpi gaganacarēṇa nīyatē dēvī pralapantī ॥19॥
tatastadarśitamārgēṇa nirgatā mauktikādivastūni । ū kuṣṭāḥ paśyanta āgatā atra ||60||
purataścābhijñānaṁ na paśyāmō dinakarasyōdayē'pi । sthitā ihaiva viṣaṇṇāstatō dr̥ṣṭaṁ yuṣmākaṁ pādakamalam ॥ 61 ॥

icchāmi baṁdiuṁ tō rannā āgāviō paṇamiūṇa । muṇivaramuvavihō sō sulasōvi samāgaō tattha ॥

paḍhau bahuṁ kuṇau tavaṁ sahau duhaṁ vasau varṇāniguṁjēsu । jassa na jīvēsu dayā savvaṁ ciya niṣphalaṁ tassa ॥

athavā samyaktvamavandhyakāraṇamuttarōttaraguṇānām । tadēva durlabhaṁ tatō bhaṇati naravaraḥ kiṁsvarūpamidam ? ॥79॥
tataḥ samyaktvasvarūpē savistarē varṇitē munipatinā । bhaṇati nr̥pa ārōpayata samyaktvaṁ mayi yāvajjīvam ||80||
tatō jalpati munināthaḥ saphalaṁ na bhavati bhadra ! ētadapi । rahitaṁ jīvadayayā viśiṣṭaphalasādhanābhāvāt ॥ 81 ॥
paṭhatu bahu karōtu tapaḥ sahatāṁ duḥkhaṁ vasatu vananikuñjēṣu । yasya na jīvēṣu dayā sarvamēva niṣphalaṁ tasya ॥82॥
dharatu śirasi jaṭābhāraṁ karōtu hutāśasya tarpaṇaṁ haviṣā । luñcatu vā ciharacayaṁ tyajatu prāṇānapi tīrthē ॥ 83॥
।

252
supāsanāha-caritrmammi -
hava va vakaladhārī nirahārī baṁbhacēravayadhārī । jai jīvahaṇaṇakārī niratyayaṁ tassa tā savvaṁ ॥ 84 ॥
ēyaṁ dhammarahassaṁ ēyaṁ tattaṁ tilōyasāramiṇaṁ । jaṁ jīvāṇa ahiṁsā vahāiaiyāraparimukkā ||85||
ii dēsaṇaṁ suṇēuṁ rāyā sulasēṇa saha vayaṁ paḍhamaṁ । girahai sammatta juyaṁ asamatyō savvariē ||86||
cōrōvi savvavirahaṁ paḍivajjai taha bahū jaṇō annō । jiṇabhavaṇarvivapūyaṁ tattha ya vigahāē parihāraṁ ॥ 87॥
kōvi aṇuvvayamēgaṁ annē savvāī kōvi pavvajjaṁ । paḍivajjai aha savvē namiuṁ vaccaṁti ṭhāṇēsu ॥ 88 ॥
raṇaraṁgamalarāyā paḍadāṇēṇa niyayadēsammi | ghōsāvaē amāriṁ kārāgārāī sōhēi ||89 ||
rahajattāu pavattai savvattha pabhāvaē tahā titthaṁ । sāhammiyavacchalaṁ karēi sāraṁ sugihidhammē ||90 ॥
jōkōvi ubhayasaṁjhaṁ paḍikama paḍhēi guṇai suṇaī ya। jiṇasiddhatarahassaṁ taha jiṇabhavaṇēsu nicaṁpi ॥ 91 ॥
pahavaṇaccaṇaāra ttiyalēkkhayamāī karēi jō vihiṇā । savvassavi sakuṭuṁbassa tassa raṇaraṁgamalaniva ॥ 92॥
bhōaṇavatthāsaṇavāhaṇāī saṁpāḍaē asēsaṁpi । dhammavvayassa hē davvaṁ dāvāvara pauraṁ ||93 ||
pāyaṁ sāvayalōō na karai na kāravēi vaṇijāī । gurudēvāṇaṁ sēvaṁ karēi niñcapi nicitō || 94 ||
jē bhūrivivajuttā tēsiṁpi sayāvi kuṇai sammāṇaṁ । paṁcapara miṭṭhimittēṇa sāvayā jēvi tēsiṁpa || 95||
haṭṭa gharāṇaṁ na karō kayāṇagaṁ jaṁ ca ēkagaḍḍīē । āṇiti niṁti tassa ya sukaṁ mukaṁ nariṁdē ||96 ||
aha sō mittō sulasō cukkō aṁtēurīē naravaṇō । savvassaṁ vittr̥ṇaṁ mukō tahavi hu nariṁdē ॥ 97 ॥
dhikkārijjai ya jaṇēṇa tassa daṭṭhē muhaṁpi, sayalajaṇō । annattō avalōyai sōvi hu vittīya vicchēē ||
bhavatu vā valkaladhārī nirāhārī brahmacaryavratadhārī । yadi jīvahananakārī nirarthakaṁ tasya tadā sarvam ॥ 84॥
ētad dharmarahasyamētat tattvaṁ trilōkīsāramidam । yajjīvānāmahiṁsā vadhādyaticāraparimuktā ॥ 85 ॥
iti dēśanāṁ śrutvā rājā sulasēna saha vrataṁ prathamam । gr̥hṇāti samyaktvayutamasamarthaḥ sarvavirata ॥ 86 ॥
caurō'pi sarvaviratiṁ pratipadyatē tathā bahurjanō'nyaḥ । jinabhavanabimbapūjāṁ tatra ca vikathāyāḥ parihāram ||87॥
kō'pyatratamēkamanyē sarvāṇi kō'pi pravrajyām । pratipadyatē'ya sarvē natvā vrajanti sthānēṣu ॥ 88 ॥
raṇaraṅgamallarājaḥ paṭahakadānēna nijadēśē । ghōṣayatyamāriṁ kārāgārāṇi śōdhayati ॥ 89 ॥
rathayātrāḥ pravartayati sarvatra prabhāvayati tathā tarthim । sādharmika vātsalyaṁ karōti sāraṁ sugr̥hidharmē ॥90॥
yaḥ kō'pyubhayasandhyaṁ pratikrāmati paṭhati guṇayati śr̥ṇōti ca । jina siddhāntarahasyaṁ tathā jinabhavanēṣu nityamapi ॥
snapanārcanārātrikalēkhyakādīn karōti yō vidhinā । sarvasyāpi sakuṭumbasya tasya raṇaraṅgamallanr̥paḥ ॥92॥
bhōjanavastrāsanavāhanādi saṁpādayatyaśēṣamapi । dharmatratasya hētōrdravyaṁ dāpayati pracuram ॥93॥
prāyaḥ śrāvakalōkō na karōti na kārayati vāṇijyādi । gurudēvayōḥ sēvāṁ karōti nityamapi niścintaḥ ॥94॥
yē bhūrivibhavayuktāstēṣāmapi sadāpi karōti sammānam । pañcaparamēṣṭhimātrēṇa śrāvakā yē'pi tēṣāmapi ॥ 95 ॥
haṭṭagr̥hāṇāṁ na karaḥ krayāṇakaṁ yaccaikaśakaṭyā | ānayanti nayanti tasya ca śulkaṁ muktaṁ narēndrēṇa ॥ 96 ॥
atha sa mittraṁ sulasō bhraṣṭō'ntaḥ purē narapatēḥ । sarvasvaṁ gr̥hītvā muktastathāpi khalu narēndrēṇa ॥97॥

sulasasiṭṭhikahā ।

hi sagaḍē karēs vāṇijjayaṁpi sayamēva । tassavi na hōi sukaṁ tō sē ārōvara pauraṁ ॥ 99 ॥
tattha kayāṇagamēvaṁ bhārakaṁtāṇaṁ sagaḍavasahāṇaṁ । jāṇai sa nēyanihuṁ aiyārassavi na vīhēi ॥ 100 ॥
satta pahāṇā gōṇā ahannayā tēṇa thalasamāruhaṇē । hakkijjētā caḍiuṁ laggā tuṭṭā taō yaciraṁ ॥ 101 ॥
aṇubhaviūṇa mayā tē kiṇi annē tahēva vāhē । tēsuvi maē annē, ēvaṁ sē baccaē kālō || 102 ||
mukadaviṇassa chuṭṭai bahuyassa tahāvi imō na gōṇāṇaṁ । mullassa kuṇai ganna naya asthi dayāē pariṇāmō ॥
tō ēvaṁ gōṇāṇa bahuṇā kālēna sō varāyāṇaṁ । bahuyāṇaṁ jaṇiūṇaṁ ghōraṁ pīḍaṁ vivartti ca ॥ 104 ॥
tattō apaḍikatō rujjhāṇaṭṭiō marēūṇa । taccāē puḍhavīē paramāū nāraō jāō || 105 ||
uvvaṭṭiūṇa tattō ghōraṁ sahiuṁ ciraṁ bhavē dukkhaṁ । puvvōvaladdhasammattabhāvaō jiṇamayaṁ laddhaṁ ॥ 106 ॥
sukulamma kuṁḍanayarē khattiyavaṁsammi jaṇapasiddhammi । sammaṁ ca pāliūṇaṁ mōkkhammi kamēṇa saṁpattō ॥ 107॥
ēvaṁ aibhārārōvaṇēṇa vayamaiyaraṁti jē paḍhamaṁ । iya dukkhabhāyaṇaṁ tē havaṁti tō jayaha taccāē ॥ 108 ॥
raṇaraṁgamallarāyāvi nikkalaṁka aṇuvvayaṁ paḍhamaṁ । pālēḍaṁ niyarajjē ṭhaviūṇaṁ suṁdarakumāraṁ ॥ 109 ॥
rayaṇamayaṁ jiṇapaḍiṁma suibhūō pūiūṇa bhattīē । vaṁdatō paricattō āusamattīē pāṇēhiṁ ॥ 110 ॥
sahasārē iṁdattaṁ pattō tattō cuō ya iha bharahē । rahadhīrapurē puttō hōūṇaṁ dhammarāyassa ॥ 111 ॥
paḍhamava pavvaiō aṇavajjaṁ pāliūṇa pavvajjaṁ । vihuṇiyakammakalaṁkō pattō ṭhāṇaṁ nirābāhaṁ ॥ 112 ॥
॥ iti prāṇātipātaprathamāṇuvratē caturthātīcārē'tibhārārōpaṇōdāharaṇē sulasaśrēṣṭhikathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
dhikkāryatē ca janēna tasya dr̥ṣṭvā mukhamapi, sakalajanaḥ । anyatō'valōkatē sō'pi khalu vr̥ttēvicchēdē ॥98॥
ēkēna śakaṭēna karōti vāṇijyakamapi svayamēva । tasyāpi na bhavati śulkaṁ tatastasminnārōpayati pracuram ||99||
tatra kayāṇakamēvaṁ bhārākrāntānāṁ śakaṭavr̥ṣabhānām । jānāti sa naivāniṣṭamaticārādapi na bibhēti ॥ 100 ॥
sapta pradhānāni gāvō'thānyadā tēna sthalasamārōhaṇē | prēryamāṇāścaṭituṁ lagnāstruṭitāstataścāciram ॥ 101 ॥
anubhūya mr̥tāstē krītvā'nyāṁstathaiva vāhayati । tēṣvapi mr̥tēṣvanyān ēvaṁ tasya vrajati kālaḥ ॥ 102 ॥
śulkadraviṇasya chuṭyatē bahōstathāpyayaṁ na gavām । mūlyasya karōti gaṇanāṁ na cāsti dayāyāḥ pariṇāmaḥ ॥
tata ēvaṁ gavāṁ bahunā kālēna su varākāṇām । bahūnāṁ janayitvā ghōrāṁ pīḍāṁ vipattiṁ ca ॥ 104॥
tatō'pratikrāntō raudradhyānasthitō mr̥tvā । tr̥tīyasyāṁ pr̥thivyāṁ paramāyurnārakō jātaḥ ॥ 105 ॥
udvr̥tya tatō ghōraṁ sahitvā ciraṁ bhavē duḥkham । pūrvōpalabdhasamyaktvabhāvatō jinamataṁ labdhvā ॥106 ॥
sukulē kuṇḍanagarē kṣattriyavaṁśē janaprasiddhē । samyak ca pālayitvā mōkṣaṁ kramēṇa saṁprāptaḥ ॥ 107 ॥
ēvamatibhārārōpaṇēna vratamaticaranti yē prathamam । iti duḥkhabhājanaṁ tē bhavanti tatō yatadhvaṁ tattyāgē ॥ 108॥
raṇaraṅgamallarājō'pi niṣkalaṅkamaṇutrataṁ prathamam । pālayitvā nijarājyē sthāpayitvā sundarakumāram ॥ 109॥
ratnamayīṁ jinapratimāṁ śucibhūtō pūjayitvā bhaktyā । vandamānaḥ parityakta āyuḥ samāptau prāṇaiḥ ॥ 110 ॥
sahasrāra indratvaṁ prāptastataścyutaścēha bharatē । rathavīrapurē putrō bhūtvā dharmarājasya ॥ 111 ॥
prathamavayasi pravrajitō'navadyāṁ pālayitvā pravrajyām । vidhunitakarmakalaṅkaḥ prāptaḥ sthānaṁ nirābādham ॥ 112 ॥

atthāṇatyasamutthaṁ bucchēyaṁ bhattapāṇagāīṇaṁ । kutō jīvāṇaṁ sīhōntra bhai bhavagahaṇē ॥ 1 ॥
tathāhi--
jaladhijalamēhalāē vilasirasurasarivavāhahārāē । mahimahilāē muhaṁ piva kusumapuraṁ asthi varanayaraṁ ||2||
tattha nariṁdō pasiarakāmiṇīvayaṇakamalahimapasarō । nāmēṇa hēmacaṁdō caṁdō iva suyaṇakumuyāṇa ॥3॥
rūvaviṇijjiyaraṁbhā vihiyā raṁbhā sayāvi sukaēsu । tassatthi piyā raṁbhā raṁbhāthaṁbhōrū gayā || 4 ||
tāṇatthi satthasatthōhapāragō dhāragō guṇagaṇāṇa | taṇaō vuhajaṇapaṇaō nāmēṇaṁ suvaṇamallōtti ||5||
sahapaṁkīliō kīliuvva hiyaēṇa saha kumārassa । sirisēhara maṁtisuō sīhō nāmēṇa sē mittaṁ ॥ 6 ॥
aha juvvaṇammi pattō kumarō kaiyāvi rāyapāsamma । jā ciṭṭhai uvavihō tā paḍihārō tarhi pattō ||7||
vinava dēva ! bāhi purisō ēgō pahussa payakamalaṁ । daṭuṁ icchai naya sō appā kahai kōvi ahaṁ ॥ 8 ॥
bhai nariṁdō maṁca mukō pacō naridadidvipahaṁ । tō hasiuṁ bhaṇai nivō gōvasi kiṁ karaha ! appāṇaṁ ? ॥ 9 ॥
tō sō daṁḍapaṇāmaṁ kāuṁ paḍibhaṇai karahaō tujjha । avayāraṇayaṁ kijjau sāmiya ! sahiyaya sirōmaṇiṇō ॥
ō pāṇigahaṇa mahūsamma sugahīyanāmadhēyāē । mahapahugurubhaiṇīē taiyā raṁbhāē dēvīē ॥ 11 ॥
sirisirisēṇassa narāhivassa diṭṭhī kumārabhāvammi । dhārayamāṇō pāuāō ōlakkhiō ēvaṁ ॥ 12 ॥
nāmapi na vīsariyaṁ rāyā tō bhaṇai pāuyā majjha । ṭhaviyāō kaṇayasayaṁ vittr̥ṇaṁ apiyā ēvaṁ ।। 13॥
uvayārī kaha vīsarāsa majjha iya bhaṇivi dāhiṇō hatthō । pāyalaggassa dinō piṭṭhīē, pucchiō taha ya || 14 ||
arthānarthasamutthaṁ vyucchēdaṁ bhaktapānakādīnām । kurva jīvānāṁ siṁha iva bhramati bhavagahanē ॥ 1 ॥
jaladhijalamēkhalāyā vilasitasurasaritpravāhahārāyāḥ । mahīmahilāyā mukhamiva kusumapuramasti varanagaram ||2||
tatra narēndraḥ pratipakṣakāminīvadanakamalahimaprasaraḥ । nāmnā hēmacandracandra iva sujanakumudānām ||3||
rūpavinirjitarambhā vihitārambhā sadāpi sukr̥tēṣu । tasyāsti priyā rambhā rambhāstambhōrūrgatadambhā ॥4॥
tayōrasti śāstraśastraughapāragō dhārakō guṇagaṇānām । tanayō budhajanapraṇatō nāmnā bhuvanamalla iti ॥5॥
sahapāṁśukrīḍitaḥ kīlita iva hr̥dayēna saha kumārasya । śrīśēkhara mantrisutaḥ siṁhō nāmnā tasya mitram ||6||
atha yauvanaṁ prāptaḥ kumāraḥ kadāpi rājapārśvē । yāvat tiṣṭhatyupaviṣṭastāvatpratihārastatra prāptaḥ ॥ 7॥
vijñapayati dēva ! bahiḥ puruṣa ēkaḥ prabhōḥ pādakamalam । draṣṭumicchati na ca sa ātmānaṁ kathayati kō'pyaham ॥ 8॥
bhaṇati narēndrō muñca muktaḥ prāptō narēndradr̥ṣṭipatham । tatō hasitvā bhaṇati nr̥pō gōpayasi kiṁ karabha ! ātmānam ? ||
tataḥ sa daṇḍapraṇāmaṁ kr̥tvā pratibhaṇati karabhr̥tastava । avatāraṇakaṁ kriyatāṁ svāmin ! sahr̥dayaśirōmaṇēḥ ॥ 10 ॥
āḥ pāṇigrahaṇamahōtsavē sugr̥hītanāmadhēyāyāḥ । matprabhugurubhaginyāstadā rambhāyā dēvyāḥ ॥ 11 ॥
śrīṣēṇasya narādhipasya dr̥ṣṭaḥ kumārabhāvē । dhārayamāṇaḥ pādukā upalakṣita ēvam ॥ 12 ॥
nāmāpi na vismr̥taṁ rājā tatō bhaṇati pādukē mama । sthāpitē kanakaśataṁ gr̥hītvā'rpitē ēvam ॥ 13॥
upakārī kathaṁ vismaryasē mamēti bhaṇitvā dakṣiṇō hastaḥ । pādalagnasya dattaḥ pr̥ṣṭhē, pr̥ṣṭastathā ca ॥ 14॥

।।
kusalaṁ sirisēṇanarāhivassa sō bhai kāmiē titthē । pēmāmayasaṁpannē tumha vasaṁtassa hiyayammi ॥ 15 ॥
kusalaṁ ciya pahuṇō kāraṇaṁ tu maha pēsaṇē imaṁ tattha । nāmēṇa rayaṇamālā asthi
tattha । nāmēṇa rayaṇamālā atthi suyā tassa kiṁ bahuṇā ? ॥
ramaṇīyaṁ ramaṇīyaṁ vihiṇō ramaṇīyaṇaṁ ghaḍatassa । āsaṁsāraṁ mannē vinnāṇappagarasō vālā ॥17॥
sāvi hu kayappannā rāhāvēhaṁ karēi jō kōi । sō cciya maha hōi varō rāyā vā rāyakumarō vā ॥ 18॥
rāyā puṇa bahu mannai tīi varaṁ bhuvaṇamallakumaravaraṁ । tahavi na kumarīvayaṇaṁ paḍikūlai iya vicitaṁ tō ॥ 19॥
kittiyamitta rāhāvēhō kumarassa bhuvaṇamallassa | tō kumaradaṁsaṇūsuyamaṇēṇa sirisēṇanaravaiṇā || 20॥
pahu ! tuha pāyasūlambhi pēsiō nivbilaṁbamaha kumarō । niyadaṁsaṇāmaēṇaṁ diṭṭhi nivvava sāmissa ||21||
tō avalō rāyā gaṇayamuhaṁ sō ya bhaṇai kumarassa । ajjaṁ citra saṁjhāē jattā savvatthasiddhikara ॥ 22 ॥
tō rāyā paricita kallāṇaparaṁparā kumārassa । ēsā, jaṁ āsannaṁ laddhaṁ lagaṁ samaggaguṇaṁ ||23||
yata uktam;
" laghūtthānānyavighnāni saṁbhavāt sādhanāni ca । kathayanti guruṁ siddhiṁ kāraṇānyēva karmaṇām ॥”
aha sēṇāva sāmaṁtamuhamāṇavara pariyaṇaṁ sāraṁ । kumarēṇa samaṁ gamaṇē saṁvāhatthaṁ tu caṁpāē ||24||
itthaṁtarasmi vāruṇiāsāpāsāyamāvisa sūrō | kumarēṇa samaṁ gamaṇē saṁvāhatthaṁ tu capāē ||25||
viṣkuriyakiraṇaruirō nakkhattagaṇō vihāi gayaṇammi | kumarasahacaliyarayaṇīparihiyalaṁkārabhāruvva ॥ 26॥
aha maṁgalakō kuladēvayajaṇaṇijaṇayapabhiīṇi । pujjāī namaṁsēuṁ jaṇayāō pāviḍaṁ sikkha || 27 ॥
maṇapavaṇasa uṇapariyaṇaaṇukūlattēṇa laggasamayammi । cauraṁgavalasamēō kumarō saṁcalai nayarāō ||28||
kuśalaṁ śrīṣēṇanarādhipasya sa bhaṇati kāmitē tīrthē । prēmāmr̥tasaṁpannē tava vasatō hr̥dayē ॥ 15॥
kuśalamēva prabhōḥ kāraṇaṁ tu mama prēṣaṇē idaṁ tatra । nāmnā ratnamālā'sti sutā tasya kiṁ bahunā ? ॥ 16 ॥
ramaṇīyaṁ ramaṇīyaṁ vidhē ramaṇījanaṁ ghaṭayataḥ । āsaṁsāraṁ manyē vijñānaprakarṣō bālā ॥ 17 ॥
sāpi khalu kr̥tapratijñā rādhāvēdhaṁ karōti yaḥ kō'pi । sa ēva mama bhavati varō rājā vā rājakumārō vā ॥ 18 ॥
rājā punarbahu manyatē tasyā varaṁ bhuvana mallakumāravaram । tathāpi na kumārīvacanaṁ pratikūlayatīti vicintayan ॥
kiyanmātraṁ rādhāvēdhaḥ kumārasya bhuvanamallasya । tataḥ kumāradarśanōtsukamanasā śrīṣēṇanarapatinā ||20||
prabhō ! tava pādamūlē prēṣitō nirvilambamatha kumāraḥ । nijadarśanāmr̥tēna dr̥ṣṭiṁ nirvāpayatu svāminaḥ ॥21॥
tatō'valōkatē rājā gaṇakamukhaṁ sa ca bhaṇati kumārasya । adyaiva saṁdhyāyāṁ yātrā sarvārthasiddhikarā ॥ 22 ॥
tatō rājā paricintayati kalyāṇaparamparā kumārasya । ēṣā, yadāsannaṁ labdhaṁ lagnaṁ samagraguṇam ॥23॥
atha sēnāpatisāmantapramukhamājñapayati parijanaṁ sāram । kumārēṇa samaṁ gamanē saṁvāhārthaṁ tu campāyām ॥24॥
atrāntarē vāruṇyāśāprāsādamāviśati sūraḥ । kumārēṇa samaṁ gamanē saṁvāhārthē tu campāyām ||25||
visphuritakiraṇarucirō nakṣatragaṇō vibhāti gaganē | kumārasahacalitarajaniparihitālaṅkārabhāra iva ॥ 26 ॥
atha kr̥tamaṅgalakr̥tyaḥ kuladēvatājananī janakaprabhr̥tīni । pūjyāni namasthitvā janakāt prāpya śikṣām ||27||

256
supāsanāhacariyammi-
turayakhurakhaṇiyadhūlīmisēṇa khōṇī nahammi saṁlaggā । kumaraguṇēsuvarattā pattā sinnassa chattattaṁ ॥ 29 ॥
bahugāmāgaranaganagara khēḍakavaḍasamā ulaṁ vasuhaṁ । magganarāhivabahuvihiyasāgaō laṁghiu kumarō ||30||
siddhatyapurāsanē saṁpatō jātra tāva tapahuṇā । pēsiyavarapurisēhiṁ vinattō tumha āvāsō ||31||
khīrasaṁrassāsanē taitthāgamaṇēṇa kijjau pasāō । tō kayauciyālāvō āvāsai tattha gaṁtr̥̄ṇa ॥ 32 ॥
jēṇa citra tattha kajjaṁ siddhatthapurāhivēṇa taṁ savvaṁ । annaṁpi kumara sivirēṁssa appiyaṁ, ahaṁ kumārōvi ॥33॥
ramaṇīya ubavaṇāī savvattō vimhaēṇa jā niyai | siddhatthapura disāō tā picchai channagayaṇāī ||34||
ḍiṁḍīrapiṁḍaparipaṁḍurāī iṁtāī puṁḍarīyāī । hayaghaṭṭāī va tahā kariṇō karēṇuyāī ya ||35||
tō siddhatthapurāhivapurisē pucchara kimēyamēyaṁti ? । tē vinnaviṁti sammaṁ na muṇēmō kiṁtu sayamēva ||36||
sirimūladēvadēvō āgacchai ittha natthi saṁdēhō । jaṁ kumarāgamavattāyannaṇasamayā muhuttaṁpi ||37||
mannai dēvō saṁvaccharaṁva iya jāva tē paryaṁpaṁti । tā vilasirapaḍihārō paḍihārō vinnava ēvaṁ ||38|| -
siddhatthapuranariṁdō uttinō karivarāu caraṇēhiṁ । iṁtō ittō dīsaha āyanēūṇa iva kumarō ॥39॥
siṁhāsaṇaṁ vimōttuṁ saṁmuhamaha ēi jāva kira gaṁtuṁ । tō parimiyaparivārō pattō sō jhatti tatthēva ॥ 40 ॥
tō daṭṭūṇa kumāraṁ ruvēṇaṁ muttimaṁta mitra mayaṇaṁ । mucchā nimīliyacchō sahasatti mahīyalē paḍiō || 41 ||
tō hāhāramuhalē atthāṇajaṇē sasaṁbhramaṁ kumarō। caṁdaṇarasa sēyāīuvayāraṁ karēi kārai ya ॥42॥
manaḥ pavanaśakuna parijanānukūlatvēna lagnasamayē । caturaṅgabalasamētaḥ kumāraḥ saṁcalati nagarāt ॥ 28 ॥
turagakhurakhanitadhūlīmiṣēṇa kṣōṇī nabhasi saṁlagnā । kumāraguṇēṣūparaktā prāptā sainyasya cchatratvam ||29||
bahuprāmākaranaganagara khēṭa karbaṭasamākulāṁ vasuvām । mārganarādhipabahuvihitasvāgatō laṅghayitvā kumāraḥ ॥ 30 ॥
siddhārtha purānē saṁprāptō yāvat tāvat tatprabhuṇā । prēṣitavarapuruṣairvijñaptō yuṣmākamāvāsaḥ ॥31॥
kṣīrasarasa āsannē tatrāgamanēna kriyatāṁ prasādaḥ । tataḥ kr̥tōcitālāpa āvasati tatra gatvā ॥32॥
yēnaiva tatra kāryaṁ siddhārthapurādhipēna tat sarvam । anyadapi kumāraśibirasyārpitam, atha kumārō'pi ॥33॥
ramaṇīyōpavanādīn sarvatō vismayēna yāvat paśyati । siddhārthapura diśastāvat paśyati cchannagaganāni ॥ 34॥
ḍiṇḍīra piṇḍaparipāṇḍurānyāyanti puṇḍarīkāṇi । hayavaṭṭāni ca tathā kariṇaḥ karēṇvādiśca || 35॥
tataḥ siddhārthapurādhipapuruṣān pr̥cchati kimētadētaditi । tē vijñapayanti samyag na jānīmaḥ kintu svayamēva ॥
śrīmūladēvadēva āgacchatyatra nāsti saṁdēhaḥ । yat kumārāgamavārtā karṇēna samayād muhūrtamapi ||37||
manyatē dēvaḥ saṁvatsaramivēti yāvat tē prajalpanti । tāvad vilasitr̥pratihāraḥ pratihārō vijñapayatyēvam ॥ 38 ॥
siddhārthapuranarēndra uttīrṇaḥ kāravarāccaraṇābhyām | āyantritō dr̥śyata ākarṇyati kumāraḥ ||39||
siṁhāsanaṁ vimucya saṁmukhamathaiti yāvatkila gatvā । tataḥ parimitaparivāraḥ prāptaḥ sa jhaṭiti tatraiva ॥ 40 ॥
tatō dr̥ṣṭrā kumāraṁ rūpēṇa mūrtimantamiva madanam । mūrcchānimīlitākṣaḥ sahasati mahītalē patitaḥ ॥ 41 ॥
1 ka. tarurasā । 2 ga. āga । 3 gaṁ u maha pa° ।

aha laddhacēyaṇaṁ taṁ khaṇēṇa bhāsaṇē nivēsēuṁ । paripucchē kumārō kiṁ bāhara tumha aṁgammi ? ||43||
aha ummīliyanayaṇō avalōiya kiṁpi caliradiṭṭhīē | kaṁḍuai vāmakannaṁ nāhipaēsaṁ parimusēi ॥ 44 ॥
lajjaṁ nāḍai naya dēi uttaraṁ pucchiōvi kumarēṇa । vāmapayaṁguṭṭēṇaṁ ōṇayavayaṇō hi dharaṇi ॥ 45 ॥
iya tassa ciṭṭhiyaṁ pāsiūṇa ciṁtai savimhayaṁ kumarō । samayaṇaramaṇiviyārā kiṁ kāraṇamittha dīsaṁti ? ॥
ēvaṁ ca viyatō suṇai jhuṇī sajalaghaṇasamuddāmaṁ । tō bhaṇai amayavuṭṭīkalāṇaṁ kassa vayaṇamiṇa ? ||47॥
tō kaha maṁtiputtō ēsa jhuṇī abhayasūriaisaiṇō । . tō tēṇa nivēṇa samaṁ kumarō pattō tarhi turiyaṁ ॥ 48 ॥
kaṁca giriṁva unnaisamanniyaṁ sayalalōyamajjhatthaṁ । thirayāsaṁjayamatulaṁ jaccasuvannacchavicchāyaṁ ॥ 49 ॥
varapavahaṇaṁva bhavajalahipaḍiyajaṁtūṇa tāraṇasamatthaṁ । hāraṁva suguṇakaliyaṁ paṇamaṁti kumāranaravaiṇō ||50 ॥
muṇināhacaraṇakamalaṁ maṁtī sīhōvi kumarapāṇapiō । sāmaṁtāī ya tahā ubaviṭṭhā uciyaṭhāṇēsu ॥ 51 ॥
।
tō tāṇa hiyadvā dhammaṁ vāgarai abhayasūrīvi । jīvō aṇāinihaṇō aṇāikayakammasaṁbaṁdha ||22||
rāgassa va dōsassa va vasagō pāvāī kuṇai vivihāī । ghāi pāṇinivahaṁ aliyaṁ japēī khudamaṇō ॥ 53 ॥
avaharai parassa dhaṇaṁ ṭhuddhō saṁtēvi varakalattammi । vilasai paranārīhiṁ ihaparalōyāṇa niravikkhō ॥ 54॥
bahujīva vidhāyakarē āraṁbhē kuṇai kāravēi tahā । aṇumannai annakaē tanniuṇajaṇaṁ pasaṁtī || 55 ||
micchābhimāṇanaḍiō karēi ēvaṁ aṇēgahā pāvaṁ । tassōdayamma avasō vina ḍijjai ghōranaraēsu ॥ 56॥
tatō hāhāravamukhara āsthānajanē sasaṁbhramaṁ kumāraḥ । candanarasasēkādyupacāraṁ karōtiṁ kārayati ca ॥ 42॥
atha labdhacētanaṁ taṁ kṣaṇēna bhadrāsanē nivēśya | paripr̥cchati kumāraḥ kiṁ bādhatē yuṣmākama ? || 43 ॥
athōnmīlitanayanō'valōkya kimapi calitr̥dr̥ṣṭyā । kaṇḍūyati vāmakarṇa nābhipradēśaṁ parimuṣṇāti ॥ 44 ॥
lajjāṁ naṭayati na ca dadātyuttaraṁ pr̥ṣṭō'pi kumārēṇa । vāmapādāṅguṣṭhēnāvanatavadanō likhati dharaṇim ॥45॥
iti tasya cēṣṭitaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā cintayati savismayaṁ kumāraḥ । samadanaramaṇīvikārāḥ kiṁ kāraṇamatra dr̥śyantē ? ॥46॥
ēvaṁ ca vitarkayan śr̥ṇōti dhvaniṁ sajalaghanasa muddāmam । tatō bhaṇatyamr̥tavr̥ṣṭikalyāṇaṁ kasya vacanamidam ? ॥47॥
tataḥ kathayati mantriputra ēṣa dhvaniramaya sūryatiśayinaḥ । tatastēna nr̥pēṇa samaṁ kumāraḥ prāptastatra tvaritam॥48॥
kāñcanagirimivōnnatisamanvitaṁ sakalalōkamadhyastham । sthiratāsaṁyutamatulaṁ jātyasuvarṇaccha vicchāyam ॥49॥
varapravahaṇamiva bhavajaladhipatitajantūnāṁ tāraṇasamartham । hāramiva suguṇakalitaṁ praṇamataḥ kumāranr̥patī ॥50॥
munināthacaraṇakamalaṁ mantrī siṁhō'pi kumāraprāṇapriyaḥ । sāmantādayaśca tathōpaviṣṭā ucitasthānēṣu ॥ 51 ॥
tatastēṣāṁ hitārthaṁ dharma vyākarōtyabhayasūrirapi । jīvō'nādinidhanō'nādikr̥takarmasaṁbandhaḥ ॥ 52॥
rāgasya vā dvēṣasya vā vaśagaḥ pāpāni karōti vividhāni । ghātayati prāṇinivahamalīkaṁ jalpati kṣudramanāḥ ॥
apaharati parasya dhanaṁ lubdhaḥ satyapi varakalatrē । vilasati paranārībhirihaparalōkayōrnirapēkṣaḥ ॥ 54 ॥
bahujīvavighātakarānā''rambhān karōti kārayati tathā । anumanyatē'nyakr̥tāṁstannipuṇajanaṁ praśaṁsan ॥ 55॥
mithyābhimānanaṭitaḥ karōtyēvamanēkadhā pāpam । tasyōdayē'vaśō vinaṭyatē ghōranarakēṣu ॥ 16 ॥

258
supāsanāha cariammi-
Tatiant area saṁciṇiya pāvamaighōraṁ । tiriēsa sahai dukkhaṁ puṇōvi naraēsa tiriē || 57॥
ēvaṁ duharichōliṁ visatō dīṇamāṇasō avasō । jugasamilānāēṇaṁ lahēi kahakahavi maṇubhataṁ ॥ 58 ॥
tatthavi pātra jīvō puvvajjiyadukayapariṇaivasēṇa । vahabaṁdhaṇamaraṇāī dhaṇāvahārāivasaṇāī ॥ 59 ॥
dāridarōga dōhaggasōgaba huāvaīhiṁ parikaliō | ciṁtāsaṁtāvēṇaṁ dukulatēṇaṁ paribbhūō ॥ 60 ॥
tō ciṁtēi niyamaṇē annabhavē kiṁ maē kayaṁ pāvaṁ । jēṇēsō haṁ vihiō vihiṇā dukkhāṇa guruvāṇī || 61 ॥
tattō dhamma kā mahammaṁ puṇōvi kumaīsu । vinaḍijjaiṇēgavihaṁ pāvai kōvi hu kudēvattaṁ ॥ 62 ॥
tattha thē vaṁtarabhāvēvi kiṁkarāpi kiṁkarō kōi । hōi naḍijjai tatthavi tērsi āṇāē aṇavarayaṁ ॥ 63 ॥
dāsāvi māṇusattē sāmīhitō lahaṁti bhattāī । tō tē tērsi āṇaṁ bahu mannatāvi hu kuṇati ॥ 64 ॥
abhiōgiyadēvā puṇa lahaṁti na hu kiṁpi sāmipāsāō । āṇāikamaṇē uṇa tē tāḍijjati tēhiṁ tahā ॥
jaha vēyaṇābhibhūyā nārayavāsāō nārayanva taō । bahu mannaṁti bhavaṁtaragamaṇaṁ, annē puṇō kēi ॥ 66 ॥
ajjhavasāyavisēsā idvisēsaṁpi kiṁpi saṁpattā । daṭhṭhē mahiṭṭiṭṭha īsākavaliyamaṇā taha ya ॥ 67॥
rāgadō saṭṭā na lahaṁti raī maī ca jiṇadhammē । rudajjhāṇōvagayā cuyā ya pāvaṁti tō kugaī ॥68॥
tō rāgadōsāṇaṁ asēsadukkhōhakhāṇibhūyāṇaṁ । ujjamaha niggahammī sō puṇa jiṇadhammasēvāē || 69 ||
dhammōvi yaduvigappō javammō taha gitthavammō ya । jaidhammō dasabhēō sāvagadhammō duvāla sahā ॥ 70 ॥
rāgadvēṣavaśārtastatrāpi saṁcitya pāpamatighōram । tiryakṣu sahatē duḥkhaṁ punarapi narakēṣu tiryakṣu ||17||
ēvaṁ duḥkhapaṅkti viṣamāṇō dīnamānasō'vaśaḥ । yugaśamyānyāyēna labhatē kathaṁkathamapi manujaśvam ||18||
tatrāpi prāpnōti jīvaḥ pūrvōpārjitaduṣkr̥tapariṇativaśēna । vadhabandhanamaraṇāni dhanāpahārādivyasanāni ॥ 59 ॥
dāridryarōgadaurbhāgyaśōkabahnāpadbhiḥ parikalitaḥ । cintāsaṁtāpēna duṣkulatvēna paribhūtaḥ ||60 ||
tataścintayati nijamanasyanyabhavē kiṁ mayā kr̥taṁ pāpam । yēnaiṣō'haṁ vihitō vidhinā duḥkhānāṁ gurukhāniḥ ? |
tatō dharmamatyā kr̥tvā'dharma punarapi kumatiṣu । vinaṭya tē'nēkavidhaṁ prāpnōti kō'pi khalu kudēvatvam ॥ 62॥
tatra ca vyantarabhāvē'pi kiṁkarāṇāmapi kiṁkaraḥ kō'pi । bhavati nayyatē tatrāpi tēṣāmājñayā'navaratam ॥ 63 ॥
dāsā api manuṣyatvē svāmibhyō labhantē bhaktādīn । tatastē tēṣāmājñāṁ bahu manyamānā api khalu kurvanti । 64
ābhiyōgikadēvāḥ punarlabhantē na khalu kimapi svāmipārśvāt । ājñātikramaṇē punastē tāḍyantē taistathā ॥ 65 ॥
yathā vēdanābhibhūtā nārakavāsād nārakā iva tataḥ । bahu manyantē bhavāntaragamanam, anyē punaḥ kēcit ॥ 66 ॥
adhyavasāyaviśēṣādr̥ddhiviśēṣamapi kamapi saṁprāptāḥ । dr̥ṣṭvā maharddhir̥ddhimīrṣyā kaṁvalitamanasastathā ca ॥67॥
rāgadvēṣavaśāta na labhantē rati matiṁ ca jinadharmē । raudrabhyānōpagatāścyutāśca prāpnuvanti tataḥ kugatim ॥ 68 ॥
tatō rāgadvēṣayōraśēṣaduḥkhaubakhānibhūtayōḥ । udyacchata nigrahē sa punarjinadharmasēvayā ||39||
dharmō'pi ca dvivikalpō yatidharmastathā gr̥hasthadharmaśca । yativarmō daśabhēdaḥ śrāvakadharmō dvādaśadhā ॥70॥
1 ga. savisa° । 2 ka. ga. dukala । 3 ka.vi ।

sīhakahā ।
256
asamatyō jammē tā sammaṁ kuṇau dēsēviraiṁpi । tatthavi asamatthō taṁpi dēsaō kuṇau, tēṇāvi ॥71॥
pattasudēvattasumāṇusattasammattasuddhadhammō । agbhāsavasāō nihayarāgaddōsō ahakkhāyaṁ ॥72॥
laḍhūṇa caritaṁ ghāikammammmūliūṇa saṁpattō । kēvalanāṇaṁ tattō pāvai ṭhāṇaṁ nirābāhaṁ ॥ 73 ॥
1
iya nisuṇiūṇa kumarō sūriṁ vinnava majjha gihidhammē । paḍhamavayaṁ kahasu tahā tadōsē, sūriṇāvi taō ॥
vahabaṁdhāivisuddhaṁ kahiyē vitthāriūṇa paḍhamavayaṁ । paḍivannaṁ kumarēṇaṁ sacivasuēṇaṁpi sīhēṇa || 75 ||
sammattēṇa samēyaṁ samayavihāṇēṇa paramasaddhāē । tō puṭṭhō kumarēṇaṁ sūrī tantrayaranivacariyaṁ ॥ 76 ॥
kaha ēsōṁ mēṁ da mucchāē nivaḍiō, kahaṁ kuṇai । ramaṇīmayaṇatriyārē purisōvi, tō kahai sūrī ॥77॥
siṁhapurē āsi tumaṁ puvvabhavē naravarō rayaṇasārō । bhajjā ya mayaṇarēhā daḍhanēhā āsi tujjha piyā ||
ēmēva kavi tī tumaṁ viratō, imā taha ccēva । tara aṇurattāvi darda darddha avamāṇamaidusaha ॥ 79 ॥
ubvaṁdhēūṇa mayā siddhatyapurammi suṁdara nivassa । ajjhavasāyavisēsā jāyā dhūyā'ṇavaccassa ॥80॥
mūlē nakkhattammī naranāhō tīi janmasamayammi । bhaviyavvayāvasāō sahasā paṁcattamaṇupattō ॥ 81 ॥
ēī puttattaṁ sumaamacēṇa pāyaḍaṁtēṇa । ahisittā rajjammī itthittaṁ gōviyaṁ ca dr̥ḍhaṁ ॥82॥
mariūṇa rayaṇasārō upannō taṁ samāgaō ēttha । puvyabhavabhāsāō tai diṭṭhē pasariē mōhē || 83 ||
kiṁ maha pīī ēvaṁ imammi iya vimarisappayarisammi | jāē jāīsaraṇē taṁ jāyaṁ jaṁ tara puḍhaṁ ॥ 84 ॥
asamarthō yatidharmē tadā samyak karōtu dēśaviratimapi । tatrāpyasamarthastāmapi dēśataḥ karōtu, tēnāpi ॥ 71 ॥
prāptasudēvatvasumanuṣyatvasamyaktvaśuddhayatidharmaḥ । abhyāsavaḥñcād nihatarāgadvēṣō yathākhyātam ॥72॥
labdhvā cāritraṁ ghātikarmōnmūlya saṁprāptaḥ । kēvalajñānaṁ tataḥ prāpnōti sthānaṁ nirābādham ॥73॥
iti śrutvā kumāraḥ sūriṁ vijñapayati mama gr̥hidharmē । prathamatrataṁ kathaya tathā taddōṣān, sūriṇāpi tataḥ ॥74॥
vadhabandhādiviśuddhaṁ kathitaṁ vistārya prathamavratam । pratipannaṁ kumārēṇa saciva sutēnāpi siṁhēna ॥75॥
samyaktvēna samētaṁ samayavidhānēna paramaśraddhayā । tataḥ pr̥ṣṭaḥ kumārēṇa sūristannagaranr̥pacaritam ॥76॥
kathamēṣa māṁ dr̥ṣṭvā mūrcchayā nipatitaḥ, kathaṁ karōti । ramaṇīmadanavikārān puruṣō'pi tataḥ kathayati sūriḥ ॥
siṁhapurē āsīstvaṁ pūrvabhavē naravarō ratnasāraḥ । bhāryā ca madanarēkhā dr̥ḍhasnēhā''sīt tava priyā ॥78॥
ēvamētra kathamapi tasyāṁ tvaṁ viraktaḥ, iyaṁ tathaiva । tvayyanuraktāpi dr̥ḍhaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā'pamānamatiduḥsaham ॥79॥
udbadhya mr̥tā siddhārthapurē sundaranr̥pasya । adhyavasāyaviśēṣājjātā duhitā'napatyasya ॥80॥
mūlē nakṣatrē naranāthastasyā janmasamayē । bhavitavyatāvaśāt sahasā pañcatvamanuprāptaḥ ॥ 81 ॥
ētasyāḥ putratvaṁ sumatyamartyēna prakaṭayatā । abhiṣiktā rājyē strītvaṁ gōpitaṁ ca dr̥ḍham ॥82॥
mr̥tvā ratnasāra utpannastvaṁ samāgatō'tra । pūrvabhavābhyāsāt tvayi dr̥ṣṭē prasr̥tē mōhē ॥ 83 ॥
kiṁ mama prītirēvamasminniti vimarṣaprakarṣē । jātē jātismaraṇē tajjātaṁ yat tvayā pr̥ṣṭam ॥ 84 ॥
1 ga. gēhidhammaṁpi ।

supāsanāha cariammi-
tō mugāō jāē caraṇamōhaviramammi । sā niyarajjaṁ kumarē ṭhatriṇaṁ lēi paccajjaṁ ॥ 85 ॥
siddhatyapurē gaṁtuṁ sacivē sumaimmi uviya rajjabharaṁ । kumarō caliō puraō paṁthē pattō ya aḍavīē ।
jā bhāra hiyakahā iva bhīmajjuṇanaulasa uṇisōhillā । khittapuhaicva bhaddayakari sayauvasōhiyā rammā ||
titthēsaravasahī iva nāṇāvihasāva ēhiṁ parikaliyā । sarasavisālasarōvara sirīva ghaṇapuṁḍarīillā ||88 ||
ēvaṁvihāḍavī kumarō gaṁtr̥̄ṇa niyavalasamēō । dasajōyaṇāṇa aṁtē āvāsai varuṇanaitīrē ॥ 89 ॥
kaivapurisasamēō pattō kōūhalēṇa vaṇagahaṇaṁ । avalōyatō picchā vijjāhara raiyajiṇabhavaṇaṁ ॥ 90 ॥
ainimmalaphalihasilāviṇimmiyaṁ sasaharassava vimāṇaṁ । rāhussa saṁbhamāō ōinnaṁ vasumaīvīḍhē ॥ 91 ॥
tatya ya saṁkaṁtāī taḍasaṁṭhiyataruvarāṇa kusumāī । paricuṁvaṁti ya bhamarā pīḍiyavayaṇā lahu valati ||12||
tammi jiṇēsarabhavaṇē savimhayaṁ jāva pavisa kumārō । kayaubhaḍasiṁgāraṁ tō piccha dēviniuraṁvaṁ ॥93॥
kāōvi tahi puṁjaya puṁcha chaumēṇa niyayapāvarayaṁ । avaṇitīō iva sāraviṁti jiṇamaṁdiraṁgaṇayaṁ ॥ 94 ॥
annāō jidhammē rāyamamāyatayēva hiyayammi । kuṁkumacchaḍayamisēṇaṁ ṭhavaṁti jiṇabhavaṇāṁgaṇaē ॥95॥
ēkkā ya tattha vālā acaṁtasurya kusumamālāhiṁ । nāṇāvicchittīhiṁ pūai gavbhahara jiṇavivaṁ ॥ 96 ॥
ēvaṁvihasuravilayāulammi bhavaṇammi saṁṭhiyaṁ divaṁ । sōmmaṁ kaṁcanavanaṁ bivaṁ siririsahasā missa || 97 ॥
taṁ daṇaṁ gurubhattipavarasamuppannavahalarōmaṁcō । mauliyakarakamalajuōṁ thuṇiūṇa jisa muvi
॥98 ॥
tatō munipativacanāt saṁjātē caraṇamōhavirāmē । sā nijarājyaṁ kumārē sthāpayitvā lāti pravajyām ||85||
siddhārthapurē gatvā sacivē sumatau sthāpayitvā rājyabharam । kumāraścalitaḥ purataḥ pathi prāptaścāṭavyām ||86 ॥
yā bhāratīyakathēva bhīmārjunanakulaśakuniśōbhāvatī । kṣētrapr̥thivīva bhadrakakariśata ( karpaka) upaśōbhitā ramyā |
tīrthēśvaravasatiriva nānāvidhaśvāpadaiḥ (śrāvakaiḥ) parikalitā । sarasa viśālasarōvara śrīriva ghanapuṇḍarīkā ॥ 88॥
ēvaṁvidhāṭavyāṁ kumārō gatvā nijabalasamētaḥ । daśayōjanānāmantē āvāsayati varuṇā nadītīrē ॥89॥
katipaya puruṣasamētaḥ prāptaḥ kutūhalēna vanagahanam । avalōkamānaḥ paśyati vidyādhararacitajinabhavanam ॥90॥
atinirmalasphaṭikaśilāvinirmitaṁ śaśadharasyēva vimānam । rāhōḥ saṁbhramādavatīrṇa vasumatīpīṭhē ॥ 91 ॥
tatra ca saṁkrāntāni taṭasaṁsthitatasvarāṇāṁ kusumāni । paricumbanti ca bhramarā: pīḍitabadanā laghu valantē ॥ 92 ॥
tasmiñjinēśvarabhavanē savismayaṁ yāvatpraviśati kumāraḥ । kr̥tōdbhaṭaśr̥ṅgāraṁ tāvatpaśyati dēvīnikurambam ||23||
kā api tatra rajaḥ prōñchanacchadmanā nijapāparajaḥ । apanayantya iva samāracayanti jinamandirāṅgaṇakam ॥94॥
anyā jinadharmē rāgamamāntamiva hr̥dayē । kuṅkumacchaṭāmiṣēṇa sthāpayanti jinabhavanaprāṅgaṇakē ||95||
ēkā ca tatra bālā'tyantasugandhakusumamālābhiḥ । nānāvicchittibhiḥ pūjayati garbhagr̥ha jinabimbam ॥ 96 ॥
ēvaṁvidhasuravanitākulē bhavanē saṁsthitaṁ dr̥ṣṭam | saumyaṁ kāñcanavarṇaṁ vimbaṁ śrī r̥ṣabhasvāminaḥ ||97||
tad dr̥ṣṭvā gurubhaktipravarasamutpannabahala rōmāñcaḥ । mukulitakarakamalayutaḥ stutvā jinēśamupaviśati ॥ 98 ॥

sīhakahā ।
261
tāō asurabahūō paidiṇakiccāī tattha kāūṇa । picchaṇayaṁ ārattiyamaṁgaladīva iyaṁ savvaṁ ॥ 99 ॥
niyaniyaṭhāṇē gayā kumarōvi samuṭṭiūṇa jiṇabhavaṇaṁ । jā jōyai savvaṁttō tā pacchimadārabāhimmi ||
pīṇapayō harasuhayā navakuvalayanayaṇapīvara sirīyā । varahaṁsagayā vāvī diṭṭhā kumarēṇa ramaṇivva ॥ 101 ॥
taṁ picchiūṇa kumarō sīyalamahurēṇa nimmalajalēṇa । guruvayaṇēṇava sōhai appāṇaṁ maggarayamaliṇaṁ ॥ 102 ॥
jalapāṇaṁ kāū uvavihō jāva tīi taḍidēsē । tā vānarīē sahiō padaṁgamō āgaō ēgō ॥103॥
ahiṇavahaddivanō guṁjāhalārabhūsiyasarīrō । sallaisāhāhatthō tārāsahiōvva suggīvō ॥ 104 ॥
kumarasirapavaramaṇiṇō tattō kumarassa bhuvaṇamallassa । kāūṇaṁ paṇivāyaṁ paryapaṇa maṇuyavāṇī || 105 ॥
asaraṇasaraṇṇa dayaguṇapavanna ai asamavihiyadakkhinna । parauvayārarasannaya suṇēhi maha kumara ! vinnatti ॥
iha aḍavīē majjhē kumāra ! nivasāmi savvakālēpi । ēsā ya vānarī pahu ! maṇaiṭṭā bhāriyā majjha || 107 ||
ēsā majjha sarīraṁ ēsāvi dhaṇaṁ ca jīviyaṁ ēsā । ēyāē virahiō khalu kharṇapi na khamō ahaṁ ṭhāuṁ ॥
kiṁpuṇa iha aḍavīē saṁyāvi maha vānarēsu sāmittaṁ । taṁ puṇa varṇatarē maha gayassa kajjataravasē || 109 ||
dudvēṇa vānarēṇaṁ ahiṭṭiyaṁ taṁ ca niggahēumahaṁ । jaivi samatthō tahavi hu ēsā aikāyara tēṇa ॥ 110 ॥
mai nēharā dēi jujjhiuṁ nēya kahavi pikkhaṁtī । ēgāgiṇiṁ ca ēvaṁ mōtuṁ sakkēmi nēya ahaṁ ॥ 111 ॥
lōya mahasakarō saṁpa punnōdayapagarisēṇa । diṭṭhō tumaṁ mahāyasa ! muttō dhammōcca pañcakhaṁ ॥ 112 ॥
tō tuha chāyāēṁ nivasau niruvadavā imā tāva । jā tassa dunnayaphalaṁ ahamuvadaṁsēmi gaṁtr̥ṇa ।। 113 ॥
tā asuravadhvaḥ pratidinakr̥tyāni tatra kr̥tvā । prēkṣaṇakamārātrikamaṅgaladīpādikaṁ sarvam ॥ 99 ॥
nijanijasthānēṣu gatāḥ kumārō'pi samutthāya jinabhavanam । yāvat paśyati sarvatastāvat paścimadvārabahiḥ ॥
pīnapayōbha (gha) rasubhagā navakuvalayanayanapīvaraśrīkā । varahaṁsagatā vāpī dr̥ṣṭā kumārēṇa ramaṇīva ॥ 101 ॥
tāṁ dr̥ṣṭvā kumāraḥ śītalamadhurēṇa nirmalajalēna । guruvacanēnēva śōdhayatyātmānaṁ mārgarajōmalinam ॥102॥
jalapānaṁ kr̥tvōpaviṣṭō yāvat tasyāstaṭīdēśē । tāvad vānaryā sahitaḥ plavaṁgama āgata ēkaḥ || 103 ||
abhinavaharidrāvarṇō guñjā phalahārabhūṣitaśarīraḥ । salakīśākhāhastastārāsahita iva sugrīvaḥ ॥ 104 ॥
kumāraśiraḥpravaramaṇēstataḥ kumārasya bhuvanamallasya । kr̥tvā praṇipāta prajalpati manujavāṇyā ॥ 105 ॥
aśaraṇaśaraṇya ! dayāguṇaprapanna ! ayi ! asamavihitadākṣigya ! | parōpakārarasajña ! śr̥ṇu mama kumāra ! vijñaptim ॥
ihāvyā madhyē kumāra ! nivasāmi sarvakālamapi । ēṣā ca vānarī prabhō ! manaiṣṭā bhāryā mama ॥ 107 ॥
ēṣā mama śarīramēṣaiva dhanaṁ ca jīvitamēṣā । ētayā virahitaḥ khalu kṣaṇamapi na kṣamō'haṁ sthātum ॥ 108॥
kintvihāṭavyāṁ sadāpi mama vānarēṣu svāmitvam । tat punarvanāntarē mama gatasya kāryāntaravaśēna ॥ 109 ॥
duṣṭēna vānarēṇādhiṣṭhitaṁ taṁ ca nigrahītumaham । yadyapi samarthastathāpi khalvēpā'tikātaratvēna ॥110॥
,
mayi snēhanirbharā dadāti yōddhuṁ naiva kathamapi prēkṣamāṇā । ēkākinīṁ caitāṁ mōktuṁ śaknōmi naivāham ॥ 111 ॥
lōcanamahōtsavakaraḥ saṁprati puṇyōdayaprakarṣēṇa । dr̥ṣṭastvaṁ mahāyaśaḥ ! mūrtī dharma iva pratyakṣam ॥ 112 ॥

262
supāsanāha carimmi-
iya bhaṇiūṇa parvagō viṇiggaō tattha piyayamaṁ mōttuṁ । tō kumarō paricita dīsaha accabhūyaṁ ēyaṁ 114
sāhāmigōvi ēsō māṇusabhāsāē jaṁ paryapēṛa । maipubviyā ya vittī kahavā pasuṇōvi ya imassa ? ॥115॥
aha khaṇamēgaṁ gamiuṁ bhaṇiō kumarō pavaṁgamapiyāē । aivaliō sōsattū mārissai majjha maṇadaiyaṁ 116
tō tassa maraṇavattā maha ēi na savaṇagōyaraṁ jāva । tā jīviya caissaṁ iya bhaṇiuṁ paḍai vāvī । | 117॥
tō kumarō paricita hā ! mahasaraṇāgayāē ēīē । na hu maraṇamuvakkhēḍaṁ juttaṁ iya tīi paṭṭīē ॥ 118 ॥
pariyaṇaaparinnāyābhipāō taraṇasattisaṁjuttō । tīē kaḍḍhaṇahēḍaṁ jhapa jā dēi kumarōvi ॥ 119 ॥
tāva na sāvānariyā naya vāvī nēya pāṇiyaṁ tattha । kōmalatūlisaṇāhē appāṇaṁ niyai pallēkē || 120 ॥
kumarassa bhicavaggō ahiō takkhaṇēṇa tahāṇaṁ । kiṁkāyavyavimūḍhī saṁpattō niyayasiviram ॥ 121 ॥
sāhai sacivāīṇaṁ, tēvi hu kariturayarahavarāīyaṁ । paguṇaṁti balamasēsa kāriti ya saṁtikammāī ॥ 122 ॥
kumarōvi tattha bhavaṇaṁ picchai baraphalihabhittimaṇijālaṁ । jālagavakkhataranīharaṁ tavaradhūvadhūmasihaṁ ॥ 123 ॥
dhūmasi hāmavalīkijja māṇaaiviulavimalagayaṇayalaṁ । gayaṇayalagaruyasaṁlaggadhayavaḍāḍōyakamaṇīyaṁ ॥ 124 ॥
kamaṇīyacalirasuravahu saṁgha ukkhaḍiyakaḍayamaṇiniyaraṁ । maṇiniyarajaḍiyalaṁvaṁtadāmakiraṇōhadippataṁ ॥ 125 ॥
dippaṁtakaṇayathaṁ mōhaghaḍiyavarasālahaṁjiyārammaṁ । rammamahivīḍhaviraiyasugaṁdhasiyapupphapayarōhaṁ ॥ 126 ॥
pupphapayarō hamayaraṁdaddhaguṁjaṁtabhamirabhamara ulaṁ । bhamirabhamaraula aimahurasaddavahiriyadisābhōyaṁ ॥ 127॥ !
tatastava bhujacchāyāyāṁ nivasatu nirupadravēyaṁ tāvat । yāvattasya durnayaphalamahamupadarśayāmi gatvā ॥ 113 ॥
iti bhaṇitvā plavaṁgō vinirgatastatra priyatamāṁ muktvā । tataḥ kumāraḥ pariracintayati dr̥śyatē'tyadbhutamētat ॥
śākhāmr̥gō'pyēṣa manuṣyabhāṣayā yatprajalpati । matipūrvikā ca vr̥ttiḥ kathaṁ vā paśōrapi cāsya ? ॥ 115 ॥
atha kṣaṇamēkaṁ gamayitvā bhaṇitaḥ kumāraḥ plavaṁgamapriyayā । atibalitaḥ sa śatrurmārayiṣyati mama manōdayitam ||
tatastasya maraṇavārtā mamaiti na śravaṇagōcaraṁ yāvat । tāvajjīvitaṁ tyakṣyāmīti bhaṇitvā patati vāpyām ॥
tataḥ kumāraḥ paricintayati hā ! maccharaṇāgatāyā ētasyāḥ । na khalu maraṇamupēkṣituṁ yuktamiti tasyāḥ pr̥ṣṭhē ॥ 118 ॥
parijanāparijñātābhiprāyastaraṇaśaktisaṁyuktaḥ । tasyāḥ karṣaṇahatō mpāṁ yāvaddadāti kumārō'pi ॥ 119 ॥
tāvanna sā vānarī na ca vāpī naiva pānīyaṁ tatra । kōmalatūlasinātha ātmānaṁ paśyati palyaṅkē ॥ 120॥
kumārasya bhr̥tyavargō'tiduḥkhitastatkṣaṇēna tatsthānam । kiṁkartavyavimūḍhaḥ saṁprāptō nijaśibirē || 121॥ .
kathayati sacivādīnāṁ tē'pi khalu karituragarathavarādikam । praguṇayanti balamaśēṣaṁ kārayanti ca śāntikarmāṇi ॥
kumārō'pi tatra bhavana paśyati varasphaṭikabhittimaṇijālam । jālagavākṣāntaraniḥ saradvaradhūpadhūmaśikham ॥ 123॥
dhūmaśikhāmalinīkriyamāṇātivipulavimalagaganatalam । gaganatala gurusaṁlagnadhvajapaṭāṭōpakamanīyam ॥ 124॥
kamanīyacalitr̥suravadhūsaṁghatuḍitakaṭakamaṇinikaram । maṇinikarajastilambamānadāmakiraṇaughadīpyamānam ॥ 125॥
dapyamānakanakastambhaughaghaṭitavaraśālabhañjikāramyam । ramyamahīpīṭhaviracitasugandhasitapuṣpaprakaraugham ॥ 126॥
puṣpapraka raughamakarandalubdhaguñjaddbhramitr̥bhramarakulam । bhramitr̥bhramarakulātimadhuraśabdabadhiritadigābhōgam ॥ 127॥

sīhakahā ।
263
iya ērisamma bhavaṇē diṭṭhō kumarēṇa kuṁḍalāharaṇō । ēgō dēvō puraō āharaṇapahāhiṁ cicaiō || 128॥
sō dēvō bhai ō mā annaṁ kiṁpi idda viyappēsu । kāraṇavasēṇa bhō kumara ! āṇīō iha maē taṁ si ॥ 129 ॥
tō taṁ pai sō jaṁpara kō dēsō ēsa kō pahū ēttha । kō si tumaṁ kimahaṁ puṇa ihāṇiō kahaha majjha imaṁ ? ॥
iya nisuṇiūṇa dēvō paḍijaṁpara kumara ! jaṁ taē bhaṇiyaṁ । taṁ nisuṇaha savisēsaṁ sāhippaṁta imaṁ ihi ॥ 131 ॥
ēyaṁ kīlābhavaṇaṁ vivviraṁ niyayapaṇaiṇīsahiō । kīlāmi ahaṁ niścaṁ amiyagaī nāma asurō haṁ ॥
ēyassa sāmisālō, ahannayā rēvayammi saṁcaliō । cāraṇamuṇikēvaliṇō namasaṇatthaṁ vibhūīē || 133 ॥
niyadēvīē samēō jāhē vaccāmi thēvabhūbhāgaṁ । tā picchāmi masāṇē uvavihaṁ jōgiaṁ ēgaṁ ॥ 134 ॥
rattadaṇakayatilayaṁ parihiyabhigacammacēḍayara udaṁ । suvicittiyamatthaya ṭōpiāī pacchāiya siragaṁ ॥ 135॥
kasiṇasarī savataṇucamma vihiavarajōgapaṭṭiābaṁdhaṁ । millata huṁkāraṁ aigarūaṁ dāruṇaṁ tattha ॥ 136 ॥
tasya puraō diṭṭhō suṭṭa huā huyavahō mahājālō । vāmē pāsammi puṇō ciṭṭhā varabāliyā ēgā ॥ 137॥
aha taṁ picchittu maē dēvī bhaṇiyā piē! paḍikkhēḍaṁ । khaṇamēkkaṁ pikkhāmō kiṁ vavasai ēsa pāsaṁḍī ॥ 138 ॥
ēvaṁ ca kaē kēnnaṁ taṁ ruyamāṇi sa pāvapāsaṁḍī । saṁṭhāvai maṁḍalaē caccai rattaṁdaṇēṇa taō ॥ 139 ॥
rattakaṇavīramālē avalaṁviya tīē kaṁṭhadēsammi । kira aggīē khivissai tō sō mē tajjiō ēvaṁ ॥ 140 ॥
rē rē pāvig ! tumaṁ ērisamasamaṁjasaṁ jaṇaviruddhaṁ । mama puraō kāūṇaṁ vaccasi kira kattha taṁ mūḍha ! || 141 ॥
itīdr̥śē bhavanē dr̥ṣṭaḥ kumārēṇa kuṇḍalābharaṇaḥ । ēkō dēvaḥ purata ābharaṇaprabhābhirmaṇḍitaḥ ॥ 128 ॥
sa dēvō bhaṇati tatō mā'nyatkimapīha vikalpasva । kāraṇavaśēna bhōḥ kumāra ! ānīta iha mayā tvamasi ॥
tatastaṁ prati sa jalpati kō dēśa ēṣa kaḥ prabhuratra । kō'si tvaṁ kimahaṁ punarihānītaḥ kathaya mamēdam 1 || 130 ॥
iti śrutvā dēvaḥ pratijalpati kumāra ! yattvayā bhaṇitam । tacchr̥ṇu saviśēṣaṁ kathyamānamidamidānīm ॥131॥
ētat krīḍābhavanaṁ vikr̥tya nijapraṇayinīsahitaḥ । krīḍāmyahaṁ nityamamitagatirnāmāsurō'ham ॥ 132॥
ētasya svāmisāraḥ, athānyadā raivatē saṁcalitaḥ । cāraṇamunikē valinō namasyanārthaṁ vibhūtyā ॥ 133॥
nijadēvyā samētō yadā vrajāmi stōkaṁ bhūbhāgam । tadā paśyāmi śmaśāna upaviṣṭaṁ yōginamēkam ॥ 134॥
raktacandanakr̥tatilakaṁ parihitamr̥gacarmacēṭakaraudram । suvicitritamastakōṣṇīṣēna pracchāditaśirō'yam ॥ 135 ॥
kr̥ṣṇasarṣapatanucarmavihitavarayōgapaṭṭikābandham । muñcantaṁ huṅkāramatiguruṁ dāruṇaṁ tatra ॥ 136॥
tasya ca puratō dr̥ṣṭaḥ suṣṭhu hutō hutavahō mahājvālaḥ । vāmē pārśvē punastiṣṭhati varabālikaikā ॥137॥
atha taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā mayā dēvī bhaṇitā priyē ! pratīkṣya । kṣaṇamēkaṁ prēkṣāvahē kiṁ vyavasyatyēṣa pākhaṇḍī ॥ 138 ॥
ēvaṁ ca kr̥tē kanyāṁ tāṁ rudatīṁ sa pāpapākhaṇḍī । saṁsthāpayati maṇḍalakē carcati raktacandanēna tataḥ ॥ 139 ॥
raktakaṇavīramālāmavalambya tasyāḥ kaṇṭhadēśē | kilāgnau kṣēpsyati tataḥ sa mayā tarjita ēvam ॥140॥
rē rē pāpiṣṭha ! tvamīdr̥śamasamañjasaṁ janaviruddham । mama purataḥ kr̥tvā vrajasi kila kva tvaṁ mūṛha ! ॥ 141 ॥

supāsanāha caritrammi--
nillajja ! kiṁ na lajjasi ēyāṇaṁ niyayapaṁcabhūyāṇaṁ । ihaparalōyaviruddhaṁ jēṇākajjaṁ samāyarasi ? || 142 ॥
iya mama vayaṇaṁ sōuṁ taṁ bālaṁ cayai sō palāyaṁtō । karuṇāē parimukō, dēvīē samapiyā kannā || 143॥
saṁpunnalakkhaṇaṁ taṁ dhāriti rūvasaparyaṁ divyaṁ । ucchaṁgē kāūṁṇaṁ jaṁpai dēvī, ahaṁ jāyā ॥ 144 ॥
dēvī hu sappasavā, bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē na ēttha saṁdēhō । lāvannāmayasiṁdhū kahaṁ imā māṇusī hōi 1 ॥ 145 ॥
iya japatōpattō kēvaliyāsammi, taṁ ca namiūṇa । uvaviṭṭhō hiyayagayaṁ saṁdēhaṁ jāṇiuṁ sōvi ॥ 146 ॥
hariāūriyavarapaṁca yannaghōsōvamēṇa saddēṇa । ēyāē vāliyāē cariyē kahiṁ samādattō ॥ 147॥
tathāhi; —
bhara sta yamaṁgalāē nayarīē āsi dhaṇasiṭṭhī । tassavi ya bālavihavā tagayā jayasuṁdarī nāma ।।
tīsē ya baṁdhuṇō paṁca tē āṇāē tīē va ṁti । jiṭṭhassaṁ puṇō gharaṇī na vahai tīi saha samma ॥ 149 ॥
taṁ pariṇāvai annaṁ kannaṁ taha puvvabhāriyāi kathaṁ । jaṁ vā taṁ vā dūsai dubbayaṇēhi ya dai dēhaṁ ॥ 150 ॥
akōsai bhāujjāiyāvi ēvaṁ ca tāu vati । vatī jjhāṇē samagaṁ vijjūē daḍhāō ।। 151 ।।
vagghittaṁ pattāō parōpparaṁ diṭṭigōyaragayāō । puvvavērāṇubaṁdhā jujjhiya taiyaṁ gayā puḍhavi || 152 ||
uccaṭṭiūṇa tattō pariṇāmavisēsaō gayaurammi | bhāujjāyā jāyā bhajjā sūrassa naravaṇō || 153 ||
gantīē nagaṁdā dhūyattāē imā samāvannā । uvvaṭṭiya narayāō pariṇāmavisēsaō taha ya ॥ 154 ॥
bhavabhāsāō appī kuṇai sāvi gavbhammi । taha tappāḍaṇahēuṁ sayā uvāē kuiṇēgē || 155 ॥
nirlajja ! kiṁ na lajjasē ētēṣāṁ niyatapañcabhūtānām । ihaparalōkaviruddhaṁ yēnākārya samācarasi ? ॥142॥
iti mama vacanaṁ śrutvā tāṁ bālāṁ tyajati sa palāyamānaḥ । karuṇayā parimuktaḥ, dēvyai samarpitā kanyā ॥ 143 ॥
saṁpūrṇalakṣaṇāṁ tāṁ dhārayantīṁ rūpasaṁpadaṁ divyām । utsaṅgē kr̥tvā jalpati dēvī, ahaṁ jātā ॥ 144 ॥
dēvyapi khalu saprasavā bhaṇitaṁ ca mayā nātra saṁdēhaḥ । lāvaṇyāmr̥tasindhuḥ kathamiyaṁ mānuṣī bhavēt ॥145॥
iti jalpan prāptaḥ kēvalipārśvē, taṁ ca natvā । upaviṣṭō hr̥dayagataṁ saṁdēhaṁ jñātvā sō'pi ॥ 146 ॥
daryāpūritavarapāñcajanyaghōṣōpamēna śabdēna । ētasyā bālikāyāścaritaṁ kathayituṁ samārabdhaḥ ॥ 147 ॥
bharata ihaiva kr̥tamaṅgalāyāṁ nagaryāmāsīd dhanaśrēṣṭhī । tasyāpi ca bālavidhavā tanayā jayasundarī nāma ॥ 148॥
tasyāśca bandhavaḥ pañca ta ājñāyāṁ tasyā vartantē । jyēṣṭhasya punargr̥hiṇī na vartatē tayā saha samyak ॥ 149 ॥
taṁ pariṇāyayatyanyāṁ kanyāṁ tathā pūrvabhāryayā kr̥tam । yadvā tadvā dūṣayati durvacanaiśca dahati dēham ॥ 190॥
ākrōśati bhrātr̥jāyāpyēvaṁ ca tē vartētē । vartamānē ca dhyānē samakaṁ vidyutā dagdhē ॥ 151 ॥
vyāghrītvaṁ prāptē parasparaṁ dr̥ṣṭigōcaragatē । pūrvavairānubandhād yuddhvā tr̥tīyāṁ gatē pr̥thivīm ॥ 192॥
udvr̥tya tataḥ pariṇāmaviśēṣatō gajapurē । bhrātr̥jāyā jātā bhāryā śūrasya narapatēḥ ॥153॥
garbhē tasyā nanāndā duhitr̥tayēyaṁ samāpannā । uddhr̥tya narakāt pariṇāmaviśēṣatastathā ca ॥ 154 ॥
pūrvabhavābhyāsādaprītiṁ karōti sāpi garbhē । tathā tatpāṭana hētōḥ sadōpāyān karōtyanēkān ॥ 115 ॥

tēṇaṁ ca khiyamāṇī jalaṇē asurēṇa mōiyā imiṇā । tā thēvaṁpi na appā appēyavtrō kasāyāṇaṁ ॥ 160 ॥

jē savvā asakā parihariu tēvi dēsaō ca । paritaṇuyaṁti kasāē, gurukammā jē ya ēyaṁpi ॥ 162॥

tā itō tuha pāyā maha saraṇaṁ cattasavvasaṁgāhaṁ । jaha hōmi taha pasāyaṁ karēsu maha paramakāruṇiya ! || 165॥
tō jaṁpara muṇināhō niruvakamamatthi tujjha bhōgaphalaṁ । ajjavi kammaṁ, gihidhammamēva paḍivajja tā inhiṁ ॥
sā jaṁpa savvannū jāṇai juttaṁ paraṁ imō majjha । kaha sammaṁ nivvahihī avirayaasurāṇa majjhammi ? || 167॥
bhai muṇī kāliṁjara aḍavīē risahanāhajiṇabhavaṇē । pikkhihisi bhuvaṇamallaṁ rāyamuyaṁ, tassa āyattā ॥
hōuṁ sāvayadhammaṁ sammaṁ pāliya kamēṇa pavvajjaṁ । paḍivajjiya tēṇa samaṁ lahihisi ṭhāṇaṁ nirābāhaṁ ॥ 169 ॥
sōūṇa vaiyaramimaṁ parisāē tattha kēvi pavvajjaṁ । anē sāvayadhammaṁ sammattaṁ sammamannē u || 170 ||
patitastathāpi na garbhō nirupakramāyurbhāvatastataḥ । samayē jātā dr̥ṣṭā tatastasyāḥ sā mānasaṁ dahati ॥156॥
sūtikarmakaryē draviṇaṁ dattvā mr̥tēti prakaṭayya । mōcayati cchannaṁ, tayā nijāyai duhitrē ॥157॥
taddivaprasūtāyai samarpitā vardhitā ca sā, itaḥ । dr̥ṣṭā ḍimbhaiḥ samaṁ krīḍantī yōginā tatra ॥ 158॥
atirudravidyāsādhanahētōrmārgayatā varakanyām । tatō lōbhayitvā nītā sahātmanā prētabhūmau ॥ 119 ॥
tēna tra kṣipyamāṇā jvalanē'surēṇa mōcitā'nēna । tasmāt stōkamapi nātmā'rpayitavyaḥ kaṣāyēbhyaḥ || 160॥
tēbhyaśca bhavanti dūrē parihr̥taparigrahā gatārambhāḥ । yaddhētau samagrē nūnaṁ na nivartatē kāryam ॥161 ॥
yē sarvathā'śaktāḥ parihartuṁ tē'pi dēśatastyaktvā । paritanūyanti kaṣāyān, gurukarmāṇō yē caitadapi ॥ 162॥
kartumasamarthā ēva tē'pi khalu tattyāgakārakēṣu dr̥ḍham । bahumānāt prāpnuvanti yōgyatām, iti munīndrē ॥ 163 ॥
jalpati karmakṣayē jātiṁ smr̥tvā bālikā bhaṇati । sarvō'pi khalu vr̥ttāntō jātō mama nātha ! pratyakṣaḥ ॥164॥
tasmāditastava pādā mama śaraṇaṁ tyaktasarvasaṅgā'ham । yathā bhavāmi tathā prasādaṁ kuruṣva mayi paramakāruṇika ! |
tatō jalpati muninātha nirupakramamasti tava bhōgaphalam । adyāpi karma, gr̥hidharmamēva pratipadyasva tasmādidānīm ॥
sā jalpati sarvajñō jānāti yuktaṁ, paramayaṁ mama । kathaṁ samyag nirvakṣyatyaviratāsurāṇāṁ madhyē 1 ॥ 167 ॥
bhaṇati muniḥ kāliñjarāvyāmr̥ṣabhanāthajinabhavanē । prēkṣiṣya sē bhuvanamallaṁ rājasutaṁ, tasyāyattā ॥ 168 ॥

iti tē sāṭōpā yāvad bhavanti rāṇvanti tāvatpaṭhyamānam । asurasyānujñayā caritaṁ kumārasya dēvaiḥ ॥191॥
nr̥pahēmacandrakulakumudacandra ! śrībhuvana mallakumāravara ! | avitathābhidhāna ! sattvapradhāna ! varajñāna ! jīva ciram ॥
parōpakāraparāyaṇapuruṣēṣu labhatē tava kō rēkhām । paśumātrasyāpi kāryē gaṇayasi prāṇāṁstr̥ṇasamānān ॥ 193॥
ēvaṁ ca nijaprabhōḥ kulaguṇōttanaṁ śr̥ṇvatām । vismitamanasāṁ sahasā dr̥ṣṭērgōcaraṁ prāptaḥ ॥194॥
tasmin vimānē kumāraḥ, tatō rōmāñcañcukāyamānāḥ । bhūnihitabhālaphalakā uttīrṇēna vimānāt ॥ 195॥
utthāpyōtthāpya bāḍhamāliṅgitāḥ kumārēṇa । tasyādēśāt taiḥ praṇatō dēvaḥ sadēvīkaḥ ॥ 196 ॥
upaviṣṭāśca yathōcitamasurēṇa kumāragurupuruṣabhyaḥ । kathitaḥ sa vr̥ttāntaḥ, varamuktājālaracitē ॥ 197॥

vatyābharaṇāī samapiūṇa kumarasya pariyaṇō savyō । sammāṇiō jahāciyabādhāī kumārassa || 199||
vatthālaṁkārēhiṁ sammāūṇa tīi ucchaṁgē । appiya vijayapaḍāyaṁ sappaṇayaṁ bhaṇai tuha ēsā ॥ 200॥
ittō dhūyā, iyaēvamāi kāūṇa saṁpayāṇavihiṁ । vijayavaḍāyē pabhaṇai vacchē! suṇa majjha vayaṇamiṇa | 201 |
“nirvyājā dayitē nanāndr̥ṣu natā śraśrūṣu bhaktā bhava, snigdhā bandhuṣu vatsalā parijanē smērā sapatnīṣvapi । .
patyurmittrajanē sanarmavacanā khinnā ca tadudvēṣiṣu, strīṇāṁ saṁvananaṁ natabhru ! tadidaṁ vītauṣadhaṁ bhartr̥ṣu ||
abhyutthānamupāgatē gr̥hapatau tadbhāṣaṇē namratā, tatpādārpitadr̥ṣṭirāsanavidhēstasyōpacaryā svayam |
suptē tatra śayīta tatprathamatō jahyāca śayyāmiti, prācyaiḥ putri ! nivēditāḥ kulavadhūsiddhāntadharmā abhī |'
tatō vijayapaḍāyā pāsuṁ paṇamiuṁ bhaṇai ēvaṁ । savvaṁpi taṁ karissaṁ tāēṇaṁ jaṁ samāiṭuṁ || 202 ||
aha dēvīṇaṁ paṇagaṁ tīē āēsakārayaṁ mōtuṁ । duhiyāē aṇunnāō kumarēṇa ya vihiyasammāṇō || 203 ||
sahāṇaṁ saṁpatō amigaī dāviḍaṁ vijayaḍhakaṁ । kumarōvi hu saṁcaliō pattō ya kamēṇa capāē || 204 ||
sirisēṇanarridōvi hu paccōṇīē samāgaō daṭṭhē । vijayapaḍāyākumariṁ pariyariyaṁ tāhiṁ amarīhiṁ ॥205॥
kumarāgamaṇanitrē agapurisaṁ pucchai savimhayaṁ tattō । kumarapaṭṭī kāō amarīō iha vimāṇammi ? || 206 ॥
tō siṁ vr̥ttaṁ savvaṁ parikahai sōvi, tō rāyā । harisappayarisaparisappamāṇahiyaō vicitēi || 207||
tammi kulē uppattī sō viṇaō taṁ kalāsu kōsallaṁ । sō kōvi punnapanbhārapagarisa asthi ēssa ||
jēṇa 'nivakumaracakaṁ avaganēūṇa nūṇa sayamēva । mahakannārayaṇapaṇaṁ aṇavāhaṁ vidhaī rāhaṁ ॥ 209 ||
tā avaravarāsaṁkāsaṁbhava majjha māṇasaṁ inhiṁ । niṇhuyaviyappajālaṁ avalaṁbaḍa nivvuī paramaṁ ॥ 290 ॥
||
upavēṁśitaścatuṣkēṁ kumārō bhr̥tā ca tasya dēvyā । muktāphalaiḥ śēṣā, asurēṇa kumārakarakamalē ॥198॥
vastrābharaṇāni samarpya kumārasya parijanaḥ sarvaḥ । sammānitō yathōcitamambādhātrī kumārasya ॥ 199 ॥
vastrālaṅkāraiḥ sammānya tasyā utsaṅgē । arpayitvā vijayapatākāṁ sapraṇayaṁ bhaṇati tavaiṣā ॥ 200॥
itō duhitā, ityēvamādi kr̥tvā saṁpradānavidhim । vijayapatākāṁ prabhaṇati vatsa ! śr̥ṇu mama vacanamidam ||
tatō vijayapatākā pādayōḥ praṇamya bhaṇatyēvam । sarvamapi tatkariṣyē tātēna yatsamādiṣṭam ॥ 202॥
atha dēvīnāṁ pañcakaṁ tasyā ādēśakārakaṁ muktvā । duhitrā'nujñātaḥ kumārēṇa ca vihitasammānaḥ ॥203॥
svasthānaṁ saṁprāptō'mitagatirdāpayitvā vijayaḍhakkām । kumārō'pi khalu saṁcalitaḥ prāptaśca kramēṇa campāyām ॥
śrīṣēṇanarēndrō'pi khalu svāgatasamārōhēṇa samāgatō dr̥ṣṭvā । vijayapatākākumārīṁ parikaritāṁ tābhiramaśībhiḥ ||
kumārāgamananivēdakapuruṣaṁ pr̥cchati savismayaṁ tataḥ । kumārapr̥ṣṭhē kā amarya iha vimānē ? ॥ 206 ॥
tatastāsāṁ vr̥ttāntaṁ sarvaṁ parikathayati sō'pi tatō rājā । harṣaprakarṣaparisarpaddhayō vicintayati ॥207॥
tasmin kula utpattiḥ sa vinayastat kalāsu kauśalam । sa kō'pi puṇyaprāgbhāraprakarṣō'styētasya ॥ 208 ॥
yēna nr̥pakumāracakramavagaṇayya nūnaṁ svayamēva । matkanyāratnapaṇamanābādhaṁ vidhyēd rādhām ॥ 209॥

paisamayapaṭṭiyapaṇayanivbharā dōvi kumaranaravaiṇō । uciyapaḍivattipuvvaṁ pattā kumarassa arihammi ||
āvāsē kajjō cipapayatthaparipūriyammi, aha rāyā | saṁpatō dhavalaharē vijayapaḍāyaṁ samaṁ nēuṁ ॥ 212 ॥
saṁṭhāvara kannatē rammi kārai ya tīi uvadhāraṁ । rāhāmaṁḍavamasamaṁ sajjāvara puvvanimmaviyaṁ ॥ 293॥
aha rāhāvēhadiṇē kumarō hakāriō naridēṇa । varavatthāharaṇāī asuraviinnāī parihēuṁ ॥ 214 ||
karivarārūḍhō saṁcaliō sayalaniyabalasamēō । pattō ya tattha tattō karivarakhaṁghāō ōyariō ||
maṁcō varisaṁṭhāviyasiṁhāsa ṇapariniviharāyasuē। rāyasuyamauḍacūḍāmaṇippahā jālajaḍilillē ॥ 216 ॥
nayaṇūsavabhūē tattha maṁḍavē surasahāē sakkōvva । niyayapahā ōhāmiyanivacakō nivisa kumarō || 217॥
sirisēṇarāyapāsaṭṭiyā ya taṁ pikkhiuṁ rayaṇamālā | vimhiyāhiyā kumaraṁ pariyāṇiya pariyaṇamuhāō ॥
cita varabhāvē ahigayama ēyārisē purisarayaṇē । rāhāvēhapainnā buddhī hā divva ! kaha dinnā ? || 219 ||
ahavā kiṁ ēvaṁ sōiēṇa jai kahavividha rāhaṁ । annō ēvaṁ mōttuṁ tā maha maraṇaṁ paraṁ saraṇaṁ ||220 ||
ittō ya maṁḍavē tammi ṭhāviō gurudiḍhō kaṇayathaṁbhō । tassōvari saṁṭhaviyā ahōmuhā kaṇayaputtaliyā || 221 ॥
tī ahō viyāī rayaparibhamirāī aṭu cakāī | kōīci vāmaṁ bhabhirāī dāhiṇaṁgēṇa kāpi ॥ 222॥
simahōbhūmī ṭhaviyā kuṁḍī ya tēllapaḍipunnā । tattha paḍivibiyaṁta rāhārūvaṁ niēūṇa ॥ 223 ॥
vidhēyanvā thiramāṇasēṇa vāmacchitāriyā tīē । thaivaṁpi pamāṇavi aniyaṁtēṇa uvarihuttaṁ ||224||
1
tasmādaparavarāśaṅkāsaṁbhrāntaṁ mama mānasamidānīm । nihnutavikalpajālamavalambatāṁ nirvr̥tiṁ paramām ॥ 290॥
pratisamayapravartitapraṇayanirbharau dvāvapi kumāranarapatī । ucitapratipattipūrvaṁ prāptau kumārasyārhē ॥211॥
āvāsē kāryōcitapadārthaparipūritē, atha rājā । saṁprāptō dhavalagr̥hē vijayapatākāṁ samaṁ nītvā ॥ 212 ॥
saṁsthāpayati kanyāntaḥpurē kārayati ca tasyā upacāram । rādhāmaṇḍapamasamaṁ sajjayati pūrvanirmārpitam ॥ 213॥
atha rādhāvēdhadinē kumārō hakkāritō narēndrēṇa । varavastrābharaṇānyasuravitīrṇāni paridhāya ॥ 214॥
karivaraskandhārūḍhaḥ saṁcalitaḥ sakalanijabalasamētaḥ । prāptaśca tatra tataḥ karivaraskanvādavatīrṇaḥ ॥ 215॥
mañcōparisaṁsthāpitasiṁhāsanapariniviṣṭarājasutē । rājasutamukuṭacūḍāmaṇiprabhājālajaṭilitē ॥ 216 ॥
nayanōtsavabhūtē tatra maṇḍapē surasabhāyāṁ śakra iva । nijaprabhātōlitanr̥pacakō niviśatē kumāraḥ ॥ 217 ॥
śrīṣēṇarājapārśvasthitā ca taṁ prēkṣya ratnamālā । vismitahr̥dayā kumāraṁ parijñāya parijanamukhāt ॥218॥
cintayati varabhāvē'dhigata ētādr̥śē puruṣaratnē । rādhāvēdhapratijñābuddhirhā daiva ! kathaṁ dattā ? ॥219॥
athavā kimēvaṁ śōcitēna yadi kathamapi vidhyati rāvām । anya ētāṁ muktvā tadā mama maraṇaṁ paraṁ śaraṇam ॥
itaśca maṇḍapē tasmin sthāpitō gurudr̥ḍhaḥ kanakastambhaḥ । tasyōpari saṁsthāpitā'dhōmukhā kanakaputrikā ॥ 221॥
tasyā avaḥ sthāpitāni rayaparibhramitr̥ṇyaṣṭa cakrāṇi । kānicid vāmaṁ bhramitr̥ṇi dakṣiṇāṅgēna kānyapi ॥

tathā ।
||
ityāgayāṇa muṇiuṁ savvēsiṁ khattiyāṇa nāmāī । bhujjēsuṁ lihiūṇaṁ mimmayagōlēsu khittāī || 226 ॥
kaṇayakalasē visālē ṭhaviyāī saṁti tāī kaṁtē । amhaṁ purōhiyammī nīsarai gōlaō jassa || 227॥
sōrāhāvēmmī vavasāyaṁ kuṇau jaha iya vavatthā । tattha purōhiyahatthē paḍhamaṁ ciya gōlaē caḍiē || 228||
nāmammi vāiē tattha tassa puttō aujjhanivapahuṇō । mayaraddhayakumarō uṭṭiūṇa cāvaṁ karē karai ॥ 229 ॥
kuṁḍaliyacāvadaṁḍēṇa tēṇa dhaṇuvēyagavviyamaṇēṇaṁ । puvvabhaṇiēṇa vihiṇā mukō bāṇō diḍhamaṇēṇa ॥ 230॥
arayammi suvittāsaṁjiyammi muṇimāṇasēva uphiḍiuṁ । savvattha laddhapasarō bhaggō mayaraddhayassa sarō ||
rāhāvēhavihīē vilāraṁbhēhiṁ khattiyavarēhiṁ । mayaraddhayavva lakkhē bhaggē anēhivi bahū || 232 ||
kahiyāvasarammiṁ purōhiṇa siribhuvaṇamallakumarēṇa । sajjīkayakōyaṁḍē jhatti samārōviyasarēṇa || 233 ||
āyaṭṭiyakōyaṁḍēṇa paṁḍunaranāhanaṁdaṇērṇava । uvariṭṭiyarāhāvā matāriyā jhatti parividdhā || 234॥
aha jayatālāmuhalē jaṇammi ujjīviyaṁtra appāṇaṁ । mannatī mālaṁ khivai bāliyā kumarakaṁṭhammi || 235॥
atrāntarē paṭhitaṁ bhaṭṭēna;
rāhāvēhavarappainnasāyara burḍutauṁ, kannārayaṇu tilōyataruṇivaraguṇasaṁjuttaraṁ ।
jasu uttāraṇi rāyacakku savvuvi paḍibhaggauṁ, taṁ uttāriya jēṇa jhatti, tasu payauṁ laggauṁ ||236 ||
vēddhavyā sthiramānasēna vāmākṣitārikā tasyāḥ । stōkamapi pramādēnāpyapaśyatō paryabhimukham ॥224॥
tadā śrīṣēṇēna narapatinā jalpitaṁ yathā bhō bhōḥ ! । yō rādhāmimāṁ vidhyati sa kanyāyā asyā varaḥ ॥ 225 ॥
atrāgatānāṁ jñātvā sarvēṣāṁ kṣattriyāṇāṁ nāmāni । bhūrjēṣu likhitvā mr̥ṇamayagōlakēṣu kṣiptāni ॥226॥
kanakakalaśē viśālē sthāpitāni santi tāni karṣati । asmākaṁ purōhitē niḥsarati gōlakō yasya ॥ 227॥
sa rādhāvēdhē vyavasāyaṁ karōtu yathēti vyavasthā । tatra purōhitahastē prathamamēva gōlakē caṭitē ॥ 228॥
nāmani vācitē tatra tasya putrō'yōdhyānr̥paprabhōḥ । makaradhvajakumāra utthāya cāpa karē karōti ॥ 229॥
kuṇḍalitacāpadaṇḍēna tēna dhanurvēdagarvitamanasā । pūrvabhaṇitēna vidhinā muktō bāṇō dr̥ḍhamanasā ॥ 230 ॥
arakē suvr̥ttāsañjitē munimānasa ivōdraśya । sarvatra labdhaprasarō bhagnō makaradhvajasya śaraḥ ॥ 239 ॥
rādhāvēdhavidhau viphalārambhaiḥ kṣattriyavaraiḥ । makaradhvajēnēva lakṣyē bhagnē'nyērapi bahubhiḥ || 232 ॥
kathitāvasarē purōhitēna śrībhuvanamalakumārēṇa । sajjīkr̥takōdaṇḍēna jhaṭiti samārōpitaśarēṇa || 233॥
ākarṣita kōdaṇḍēna pāṇḍunaranāthanandanēnēva । uparisthitarādhāvāmatārikā jhaṭiti parividdhā || 234 ॥
atha jayatālā mukharē jana ujjīvitamivātmānam । manyamānā mālāṁ kṣipati bālikā kumārakaṇṭhē || 235॥

vinnāṇu agacchu atuccha maṁi jasu parakajjisu dhīraha । tasu pāya namasahu khattiyahu bhuvaṇamallavara vīraha ||
rōmaṁcakaṁcuijjatasavvagattō nariṁdasirisēṇō । mauḍavikajjāharaṇaṁ savvaṁ sē dēva bhaṭṭas || 238 ||
annōvi rāyalōō saṁtaguṇukittaṇaṁ kumārassa । taha caiva kuṇai sabvō, guṇēsu kō maiccharaṁ vahaī || 239 ॥
sirisēṇanariṁdēṇaṁ rāyāṇō taha ya rāyaputtā ya । kayasammāṇā annē niyaniyaṭhāṇēsu saṁpattā ॥ 240॥
phagguṇasipapaṁcamigurudiṇammi vihiyaṁ sumaṁgalasaēhiṁ । kumarēṇa rayaṇamālāvijayapaḍāyāṁṇa pariṇayaṇaṁ ।
rannā kayapaḍivattī kumarō nīharai caṁpanayarīō । dōhivi bhajjāhiṁ samaṁ ārūḍhō varavimāṇammi || 242 ॥
laṁghaṁtō bahunaganagarārāmavarakhēḍa kabbaḍāīṇi । thōvadiṇēhiṁ pattō kusumapurāsannagāmammi || 243 ॥
paccōṇīē rāyā aṁtēuraparigaō tarhi pattō । kumarōvi saha vahūhiṁ ōyariūṇaṁ vimāṇāō || 244॥
payapaṁkayāī paṇamai piūṇa saṁbhāsiuṁ paṇaivaggaṁ । nayarammi taō pavisai ūsavabhūyammi savvattō ॥ 245 ॥
bhutattarammi savvaṁ kahiyaṁ siṁhēṇa kumaramittēṇa । rannō jaṁ jaha vittaṁ tā jāva ihāgaō kumarō ॥ 246 ॥
bīyadi tō rāyā kumaraṁ ahisiṁciūṇa rajjammi । siriabhayasūripāsē girahai pavvajjamaṇavajjaṁ । 247|
aha hēmacaṁda sāhū paḍhiēsa samaggaaṁguvaṁgēsu । ṭhaviō niyamūripaē viharai vasuhāē vihipuvvaṁ ॥ 248 ॥
jiṇasāsaṇa ucchappaṇadappaṇahatthāē tavasirivahūē । parikaliōvi hu jō baṁbhayāricūḍāmaṇī bhaṇiō ||
dēsē sugaimaggaṁ bhavvāṇa bhayaṁ ca kumayacārīṇaṁ । dēsaṇapaḍaharavēṇaṁ abhayaṁ jīvāṇa jō dēi ॥ 250 ॥
vijñānamagarvamatucchā matiryasya parakāryēṣu dhīrasya । tasya pādau namasyāmi kṣatriyasya bhuvanamallavaravīrasya ॥ 237॥
rōmāñcakañcukāyamānasarvagātrō narēndraśrīṣēṇaḥ । mukuṭāvivajabharaṇaṁ sarvē tasmai dadāti bhaṭṭāya || 238||
anyō'pi rājalōkaḥ sadguṇōtkīrtanaṁ kumārasya । tathaiva karōti sarvaḥ, guṇēṣu kō matsaraṁ vahēt ? ॥ 239 ॥
śrīṣēṇanarēndrēṇa rājānastathā ca rājaputrāśca । kr̥tasammānā anyē nijanijasthānēṣu saṁprāptāḥ ॥ 240 ॥
phālguna sitapañcamīgurudinē vihitaṁ sumaṅgalaśataiḥ । kumārēṇa ratnamālāvijayapatākayōḥ pariṇayanam ॥241॥
rājñā kr̥tapratipattiḥ kumārō nissarati campānagarītaḥ । dvābhyāmapi bhāryābhyāṁ samamārūḍhō varavimānē ॥ 242॥
laṅghamānō bahunaganagarārāmavarakhēṭakarbaṭādīni । stōkadinaiḥ prāptaḥ kusumapurāsannagrāmē ॥243॥
svāgatōtsavēna rājā'ntaḥ puraparigatastatra prāptaḥ । kumārō'pi saha vadhūmyāmavatīrya vimānāt ॥ 244॥
pādapaṅkajāni praṇamati pitrōḥ saṁbhāṣya praṇayivargam । nagarē tataḥ praviśatyutsavabhūtē sarvataḥ ॥ 245 ॥
bhuktōttarē sarvaṁ kathitaṁ siṁhēna kumāramittrēṇa । rājñē yad yathā vr̥ttaṁ tāvadyāvadihāgataḥ kumāraḥ ॥ 246॥
dvitīyadinē tatō rājā kumāramabhiṣicya rājyē । śrīabhayasūripārśvē gr̥hṇāti pravrajyāmanavadyām ॥247॥
atha hēmacandrasādhuḥ paṭhitēṣu samagrāṅgōpāṅgēṣu । sthāpitō nijasuripadē viharati vasudhāyāṁ vidhipūrvam ॥ 248॥
jinaśāsanōtsarpaṇādarpaṇahastayā tapaḥ śrīvadhvā । parikalitō'pi khalu yō brahmacāricūḍāmaṇī bhāṇataḥ ॥ 249 ॥
dēśayati sugatimārgaṁ bhavyānāṁ bhayaṁ ca kumaticāriṇām । dēśanāpaṭaharavēṇābhayaṁ jīvānāṁ yō dadāti ॥ 290॥
1 chappaya chaṁda । 2 ga. gāmava° ।

www.jainelibrary.org=== lakshmangani01output-279-to-279.json ==========================
૨૭૨
supāsanāha cariammi-
varakaṇayakalasasadaṁḍabhāsuraṁ sāsaṇaṁ jiṇidassa । sāsa mittēṇa kuṇati jassa puhaīsarā jhati ॥ 259 ॥
rahattapattasōhaṁ aṭṭāhiyamahimavihiyakhalakhōhaṁ । niṇasāsaṇaṁ samaggaṁ jāyaṁ tattō niruvasaggaṁ ॥ 252 ॥
iya hēmacaṁdasūrī sūrō iva tabakarēhiṁ dippaṁtō । vihugaṁtō mōhatamaṁ nariṁda maṁḍaliyamāīṇaṁ ॥ 253 ॥
viharai vasuhāē, bhuvaṇamallarāyāvi rajjamaṇavarayaṁ । taha pālai jaha suyaṇā gayaṁpi kālaṁ na yāṇaṁti ॥
cattō sō dēsō dujjaṇēhi bhīēhiṁ jattha sō gayā । garuḍāhiṭṭiyaṭhāṇaṁva sappaniyarēṇa dūrēṇa || 255 ||
aha annayā ya sīhō naravaiṇā ṭhāviō aṁmacapaē । jō iha siṁhasavō maṇuyamigāṇaṁ samaggāṇaṁ || 256।।
kārāvara kārāmaṁdirāī parāī sō apuvvāī । puvvēsu amāyaṁtē aṇavarayadharijjamāṇajaṇē || 257 ||
avarāhāsaṁkāē dhariyā jē tattha niśvarāhāvi । tēsiṁ vārai bhattaṁ pāṇaṁ ca viyāraparimukō || 258॥
tattha ya pāṇañcāōṁ jāyara kēsipi chuhakilaṁtāṇaṁ । tanhāē phuḍiyanayaṇā annē purṇa jaṁti paṁcataṁ ॥ 259 ॥
taṁ asamaṁjasacariyaṁ nāūṇaṁ naravarō bhaṇai siṁha । kiṁ bhavajalahitaraṁḍaṁ paḍhamacayamēvamaiyarasi ? || 260 ॥
tā kōvina guttī dhariyacvō bhō ! taē niravarāhō । thēvē avarāhēvi hu vārēyavvaṁ na bhattajalaṁ ।। 261 ||
aha sō taṁ nivaṇaṁ sōuṁ bhaṇiuṁ 'pamāṇamā ēsō' । jahapucviṁ bahaṁtō vahai taha caiva niccapi ॥ 262॥
taṁ ca pariyāṇi bhaṇiō rannā kahaṁ tava tumaṁ । vaṭṭasi, viramasi nō vāriōvi, ēvaṁ uvikkhāē ||
majjhavi aiyarasi vayaṁ, tō sō paṁḍibhaṇai jaha na aiyarai । taha kijjau apijjau muddā annassa kassāvi ||
bhai nivōta muddē imaṁ muyaṁtammi natthi maha asuha । jaṁ cayasi niyamamudaṁ taṁ puṇa vāḍhaṁ dahai hiyayaṁ । 265 ।।
varakanakakalaśasaddaṇḍabhāsuraṁ śāsanaṁ jinēndrasya । śāsanamātrēṇa kurvanti yasya pr̥thivīdharā jhaṭiti ॥259॥
rathayātrāprāptaśōbhamaṣṭāhikāmahimavihitakhalakṣōbham । jinaśāsanaṁ samagraṁ jātaṁ tatō nirupasargam ॥ 252॥
iti hēmacandrasūri : sūra iva tapaḥ karairdīpyamānaḥ । vidhūnayan mōhatamō narēndra maṇḍalikādīnām ॥253॥
viharati vasudhāyāṁ, bhuvanamallarājō'pi rājyamanavaratam । tathā pālayati yathā sujanā gatamapi kālaṁ na jānanti ||
tyaktaḥ sa dēśō durjanairbhītairyatra sa rājā । garuḍādhiṣṭhitasthānamiva sarpanikarēṇa dūrēṇa ॥255॥
athānyadā ca siṁhō narapatinā sthāpitō'martyapadē । ya iha siṁhasvarūpōṁ manujamr̥gāṇāṁ samagrāṇām ॥ 256 ॥
kārayati kārāmandirāṇi pracurāṇi sōḍapūrvāṇi । pūrvēṣvamātya'navarata dhriyamāṇajanē ॥ 257॥
।
aparādhāśaṅkayā dhr̥tā yē tatra niraparādhā api । tēṣāṁ vārayati bhaktaṁ pānaṁ ca vicāraparimuktaḥ ॥298॥
tatra ca prāṇatyāgō jāyatē kēṣāmapi kṣutklāntānām । tr̥ṣṇayā sphuṭitanayanā anyē punaryānti pañcatvam ॥
tadasamajjasacaritaṁ jñātvā naravarō bhaṇati siṁham । kiṁ bhavajaladhitaraṇḍaṁ prathamatratamēvamaticarasi ? ॥ 260॥
tasmātkō'pi na guptau dhartatryō bhōḥ ! tvayā niraparādhaḥ । stōkē'parādhē'pi khalu vāriyatavyaṁ na bhaktajalam ।।
atha sa tannr̥pavacanaṁ śrutvā bhaṇitvā 'pramāṇamādēśaḥ ' । yathāpūrvaṁ vartamānō vartatē tathaiva nityamapi ॥262॥
tacca parijñāya bhaṇitō rājñā kathaṁ tathaiva tvam । vartasē, viramasi nō vāritō'pi, ēvamupēkṣayā ॥ 263 ॥
mamāpyaticarasi vrataṁ, tataḥ sa pratibhaṇati yathā nāticarati । tathā kriyatāmarpyatāṁ mudrā'nyasmai kasmāyapi ॥ 264 ॥

sīhakahā ।
273
tā jai ēyaṁ mudaṁ muṁcasi tā muṁca natthi iha dōsō । saggāpavaggadārāī tubbha jaṁ muddaē ēsā || 266 ॥
vayamudaṁ tu cayatō lahihisi saṁsārasāyarē ghōrē । duhadaṁdōlimaṇataṁ kālaṁ tā cayasu mā, ēvaṁ ॥ 267 ॥
aṇusāsijjatō sō mudda muttūṇa nivasamīvammi । niyagēhaṁ saṁpattō aṇaṇunnāō nariṁdē || 268 ||
aha sāvayadhammarayasta sumaiṇō sumaināmasacivassa । taṁ muddamapiūṇaṁ rāyāvi hu kuṇai jiṇadhammaṁ ॥ 269 ॥
jiṇasāsaṇaṁ pabhāvai rahajattāīhi vivihaūhiṁ । sāhammiyamappaguṇaṁdhi mannaē appaṇō tullaṁ ॥ 270 ॥
aha sīhēṇaṁ pubbiṁ paṭṭiyagāmammi tuṭṭadēvvatthaṁ । paṭṭailō naravālō puvviṁ jō āsi guttīē ॥ 271 ॥
khittō chuhāē naḍiō mariūṇaṁ vaṁtaśē samuppannō । sō, sumariyapuvvabhavēṇa tēṇaṁ sīhō nahē dhariuṁ ॥ 272 ॥
ubbhāviyaṁ ca vēraṁ paccakkhaṁ paurapauralōyassa । sō māriō rasaṁtō uppannō paḍhamaḍhavī || 273 ||
bhafmī bhavam tattō kicchēṇaṁ pāviḍaṁ puṇavi bōhi । lahihī sivaṁṣi, taṁ puṇa tabbhavasammattalābhaphalaṁ ॥
aha hēmacaṁdasūrī kamēṇa viharaṁtaō tarhi pattō । tō bhuvaṇamallarāyā vaṁdai sakalattaō gaṁtuṁ ॥ 275 ॥
taddēsaṇadāvānalakammiṁdhaṇadahaṇalaṭṭhavēraggō । puttaṁ rajjē mayaṇaṁ ṭhaviūṇaṁ rayaṇamālāēṁ || 276 ||
paḍivajjiya pavvajjaṁ vijayapaḍāyāē saha vibhūīē । mukkagurukampakavaō saṁpattō sāsayaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ ॥ 277 ॥
॥ bhaktapānavyavacchēdē siṁhamantridr̥ṣṭāntaḥ samāptaḥ । tatsamāptau samāptaṁ sāticāraṁ prathamamaraṇuvratam ॥
bhaṇati nr̥pastvayi mudrāmimāṁ muñcati nāsti mamāsukham । yattyajasi niyamamudrāṁ tatpunarvāḍhaṁ dahati hr̥dayam ॥
tasmādyadyētāṁ mudrāṁ muñcasi tadā muñca nāstīha dōṣaḥ । svargāpavargadvārāṇi tava yanmudrayatyēṣā ॥ 266॥
vratamudrāṁ tu tyajalasya sē saṁsārasāgarē ghōrē । duḥkhapaṅgimanantaṁ kālaṁ tasmānmuñca mā, ēvam ॥ 267 ॥
anuśiṣyamāṇaḥ samudrāṁ muktvā nr̥pasamīpē । nijagēhaṁ saṁprāptō'nanujñātō narēndrēṇa || 268 ||
atha śrāvakadharmaratāya sumatayē sumatināmasacivāya । tāṁ mudrāmarpayitvā rājāpi khalu karōti jinadharmam ॥
jinaśāsanaṁ prabhāvayati rathayātrādibhirvivivahētubhiḥ । sādharmikamalpaguṇamapi manyata ātmanastulyam ॥270॥
atha siṁhēna pūrva padragrāmē truṭitadravyārtham । padēśō narapālaḥ pūrvaṁ ya āsīda guptau ॥271 ॥
kṣiptaḥ kṣudhā naṭitō mr̥tvā vyantaraḥ samutpannaḥ । saḥ, smr̥tapūrvabhavēna tēna siṁhō nabhasi dhr̥tvā ॥ 272 ॥
udbhāvitaṁ ca vairaṁ pratyakṣaṁ pracurapauralōkasya । sa māritō rasannutpannaḥ prathamapr̥thivyām ॥ 273 ॥
bhramiṣyati bhavē tataḥ kr̥cchrēṇa prāpya punarapi bōdhim । lapsyatē śivamapi tatpunastadbhava samyaktvalābhaphalam ॥
atha hēmacandrasūriḥ kramēṇa viharaṁstatra prāptaḥ । tatō bhuvanamallarājō vandatē sakalatrakō gatvā ||275 ||
taddēśanādāvānalakarmēndhanadahanaramyavairāgyaḥ । putraṁ rājyē madanaṁ sthāpayitvā ratnamālāyāḥ ॥276॥
pratipadya pravajyāṁ vijayapatākayā saha vibhūtyā । muktagurukarmakavacaḥ saṁprāptaḥ śāśvataṁ sthānam || 277 ||
1 kha dakṣiṇatthaṁ ।
